Chapter i. Wuh wak-krus ish-veh vesh' wuh buhfik t' wak, ish-veh vesh' wuh rasahkos t' wak, ish-veh vesh' wuh ya'shakhuv t' kau, ish-veh vesh' wuh ya'shakhuv t' duh'es, ish-veh vesh' wuh nauf t' dva, ish-veh vesh' wuh nauf t' incredulity, ish-veh vesh' wuh tevun-yonuk t' ta'hal, ish-veh vesh' wuh tevun-yonuk t' mu'khlup'es, ish-veh vesh' wuh sikar t' rok, ish-veh vesh' wuh karil t' despair, etek had kanok-vei fa' etek, etek had nothing fa' etek, etek vesh' ek' going kharik tor sha-ka-ri, etek vesh' ek' going kharik wuh vath yut--svi' pen, wuh wak-krus vesh' ni irak spo' wuh la' wak-krus, ik ein t' its noisiest ek'te'kru insisted fi' its hasu poprah, na' rom il na' ek'rasah, svi' wuh superlative degree t' comparison goh. Tra' vesh' wuh sa-te'kru k' wuh suk ahs heh wuh ko-te'kru k' wuh eiktra limuk, fi' wuh throne t' england; tra' vesh' wuh sa-te'kru k' wuh suk ahs heh wuh ko-te'kru k' wuh rom limuk, fi' wuh throne t' france. Svi' fi' shasol ish-veh vesh' clearer do khush tor wuh s'haile t' wuh fupa s' korsau t' loaves heh aluk, ik vel svi' paik vesh' settled na' ek'wak. Ish-veh vesh' wuh tevun t' etwel s'haile leh-teh stehkuh hundred heh steh-leh-kaukuh. Spiritual revelations vesh' conceded tor england na' ik favoured wak-krus, u' na' nash. Mrs. Southcott had recently attained ish-veh kaukuh-heh-twentieth blessed gad t'keshtan, t' ik wuh prophetic awek svi' wuh ha'kiv klashau had heralded wuh sublime appearance k' announcing ik arrangements vesh' tor na' wuh swallowing abru t' london heh westminster. Kauk wuh cock-lane tam'a had vesh' laid goh wuh pauk dozen t' tevun, po' rapping si' its skladan, u' wuh tam'a t' nash maut tevun kim-shah vesht (supernaturally pafam svi' originality) rapped si' ish-veh. Mere skladan svi' wuh terrupik zek t' pavek had lately sarlah tor wuh eingelsu tarkiv heh sutra, s' wuh congress t' british subjects svi' america: if, flekh tor relate, ma skan-tor weht yauluhk tor wuh komihn ne-koshtri do sovek communications wi poprah k'fai sovek t' wuh kahm t' wuh cock-lane kesh-travek. France, lehkuh favoured fi' wuh bosh u' tor tukh spiritual do ish-veh ko-kai t' wuh fo-dan heh trident, padukau k' namautauk smoothness ne' kunel, tor dun donku heh spending ish-veh. Ne' wuh guidance t' ish-veh christian pastors, she entertained herself, isha, k' such humane srashiv u' sentencing wuh youth ki' ish-veh el'ru tresahk ska', ish-veh lahv torn si' k' pincers, heh ish-veh ak'shem yontau alive, fai'ei au had ri kneeled ne' svi' wuh sov-masu tor tor dor tor wuh kitork procession t' monks if be' dvun-tor k'svi ish-veh zan-tor, na' wuh ir t' ein kau-leh il sheh-leh ker. Ish-veh nam-tor kesik hiyet ik, rooted svi' wuh lapan t' france heh norway, tra' vesh' growing lap, lu ik sufferer vesh' tostau, already pu'ulidau k' wuh woodman, buk, tor sarlah ne' heh nam-tor sawn vi' dohn, tor tor wuh ac'ruth movable nentutra k' wuh sa'haf heh wuh lipau svi' ish-veh, terrible svi' vesht-var. Ish-veh nam-tor kesik hiyet ik svi' wuh rough outhouses t' ein tillers t' wuh ras shasol beyik tor paris, tra' vesh' rau-tor s' wuh igen-va ik maut gad, snertau hal, bespattered k' rustic mire, snuffed pa' k' pigs, heh roosted svi' k' poultry, if wuh uroshitausu, tevakh, had already eku k'wuhli tor nam-tor ish-veh tumbrils t' wuh revolution. Tonk'peh ik woodman heh ik uroshitausu, hi au ar'kadan ek'wak, ar'kadan silently, heh kling puzhu-tor au u' au went pa' k' nessau tread: wuh rather, forasmuch u' tor entertain sovek suspicion ik au vesh' kum'i, vesh' tor nam-tor atheistical heh traitorous. Svi' england, tra' vesh' scarcely wuh nosahp t' zek heh protection tor justify mau national boasting. Daring burglaries k' armed sasu, heh yut robberies, nem-tor shi svi' wuh capital itself kanok mu-yor; skan vesh' publicly yuzh-tor ri tor hal-tor s' kahr rik' removing ish-veh furniture tor upholsterers' warehouses na' shar'es; wuh highwayman svi' wuh gu'gelik vesh' wuh kahr tradesman svi' wuh ta'hal, heh, hasu naglanshau heh kali-tor k' ish-veh katravahsu-tradesman ik au pehkau svi' ish-veh character t' "wuh khart-lan, " gallantly pohshaya ish-veh k'fai wuh patam heh fau-tor maf; wuh sakat vesh' waylaid k' stehkuh robbers, heh wuh klashausu pohshaya rehkuh tevik, heh yi prah pohshaya tevik himself k' wuh vath kehkuh, "svi' consequence t' wuh vravshaya t' ish-veh ammunition: " po' if wuh sakat vesh' robbed svi' sochya; ik magnificent potentate, wuh s'haile mayor t' london, vesh' tor tor lamok heh tefu fi' turnham yar-kur, k' veh highwayman, vi despoiled wuh illustrious creature svi' glan t' ek' ish-veh retinue; prisoners svi' london gaols fought battles k' ish-veh turnkeys, heh wuh majesty t' wuh tor-gav pohshau blunderbusses svi' ekhlami, putush-tor k' rounds t' pohshaya heh rin'k'n; pi'tak snipped ska' lerash-khush tuhsau s' wuh talu t' thol s'haile na' kelek bestan-tvi-shal; musketeers went vi' st. Giles's, tor psthan na' contraband goods, heh wuh patreitaya pohshau fi' wuh musketeers, heh wuh musketeers pohshau fi' wuh patreitaya, heh kling nahp sovek t' aifa occurrences mau s' wuh tsuri yut. Svi' wuh midst t' au, wuh hangman, ek'wak toranik heh ek'wak weh-rasahkos do nam-tor-fam, vesh' svi' ek'kayik requisition; i', stringing abru wu fel-tor t' miscellaneous criminals; i', hanging wuh housebreaker fi' gad vi had vesh' taken fi' gad; i', yontau sutra svi' wuh el'ru na' newgate k' wuh dozen, heh i' yontau pamphlets na' wuh svep t' westminster tvur; tor-gad, taking wuh ha'kiv t' wuh atrocious murderer, heh tor-morrow t' wuh wretched pilferer vi had robbed wuh uroshitausu's sa-kan t' sixpence. Ek' aifa vel, heh wuh thousand spo' au, sarlah tor be' dvun svi' heh ikap-tor fi-tor wuh tal-kam hinek tevun leh-teh stehkuh hundred heh steh-leh-kaukuh. Environed k' au, du' wuh woodman heh wuh uroshitausu ar'kada unheeded, eifa dahkuh t' wuh suk ahs, heh eifa vath dahkuh t' wuh eiktra heh wuh rom limuk, sahr-tor k' stir hiyet, heh lesh ish-veh ekonik rights k' wuh pid el'ru. Thus did wuh tevun leh-teh stehkuh hundred heh steh-leh-kaukuh spa-tor ish-veh greatnesses, heh myriads t' pi' creatures--wuh creatures t' nash chronicle among wuh shom--bi' wuh fau-yut ik ti fa' au. Chapter ii. Wuh sakat ish-veh vesh' wuh dover fau-yut ik ti, fi' wuh gad mu-yor tab-ma svi' november, fa' wuh wuh'rak t' wuh persons k' ik nash vesht-var has business. Wuh dover fau-yut ti, u' tor ish-veh, mesakh wuh dover sakat, u' ish-veh lumbered abru shooter's kunel. Au lates-tor abru kunel svi' wuh mire k' wuh vla t' wuh sakat, u' wuh shom t' wuh passengers did; ri fai'ei au had wuh least relish na' walking tusok, ne' wuh circumstances, tonk'peh fai'ei wuh kunel, heh wuh harness, heh wuh vral, heh wuh sakat, vesh' ek' ni ras, ik wuh jarel had rehkuh wak already sarlah tor wuh pehkaya, isha wuh'wak bestan wuh coach mes' wuh fau-yut, k' wuh mutinous intent t' taking ish-veh pla' tor blackheath. Reins heh wonil-zehl heh coachman heh klashausu, however, svi' terish, had telv-tor ik ua'mrki t' t'naehm if forbade wuh lof vathru strongly svi' favour t' wuh nerau-kek-vuhnayek, ik ein brute animals nam-tor endued k' utvau; heh wuh team had capitulated heh fun-tor tor ish-veh gu-vam. K' tevan-tor patam heh tremulous harr, au mashed ish-veh yut k'fai wuh bali vral, floundering heh stumbling svi' whiles, u' kuv au vesh' tevan-tor tor krus na' wuh larger joints. U' k'ashiv u' wuh yetursu shom-tor au heh katau au tor wuh lamok, k' wuh wary "wo-ho! Ni-ho-yi!" wuh be' leader violently hutau ish-veh patam heh kanok-vei fi-tor ish-veh--spo' wuh unusually emphatic jarel, denying ik wuh coach kupi nam-tor prah abru wuh kunel. Whenever wuh leader tor nash rattle, wuh passenger palikau, u' wuh nervous passenger lau, heh vesh' ertau svi' kashek. Tra' vesh' wuh steaming mist svi' ek' wuh hollows, heh ish-veh had roamed svi' its forlornness abru wuh kunel, spo' wuh ek'rasah tam'a, seeking shom heh finding rim. Wuh clammy heh intensely samu mist, ish-veh tor its vohris yut k'fai wuh sov svi' ripples ik visibly zahal-tor heh overspread veh wuh'ashiv, u' wuh pral t' wuh unwholesome masutra lau tor. Ish-veh vesh' ihnik hiyet tor ikap-tor si' kanok-vei s' wuh ta'hal t' wuh coach-ha'gelek tonk'peh aifa its sha' workings, heh wuh zamu ker t' fau-yut; heh wuh reek t' wuh labouring jarel steamed vi' ish-veh, u' kuv au had tor ish-veh ek'. Dahkuh vath passengers, isha wuh veh, vesh' plodding abru wuh kunel k' wuh vla t' wuh sakat. Ek' rehkuh vesh' wrapped tor wuh cheekbones heh abru' wuh kaluk, heh sai-vel-tor jack-kluf. Ri veh t' wuh rehkuh kupi ma leralmin-tor, s' sovek-vel gla-tor ish-veh, ra either t' wuh vath dahkuh vesh' spo'; heh tik vesh' ipik ne' siyah u' wehk wrappers s' wuh bezhun t' wuh kashek, u' s' wuh bezhun t' wuh ak'shem, t' ish-veh dahkuh besu. Svi' eifa gad, travellers vesh' maut fusik t' hasu confidential fi' wuh pen beglanau, na' anybody fi' wuh fau-yut lau nam-tor wuh robber il svi' league k' robbers. U' tor wuh latter, lu kanok posting-kelek heh ale-kelek kupi torvau somebody svi' "wuh khart-lan's" vlitau, ranging s' wuh landlord tor wuh lowest tihet non-descript, ish-veh vesh' wuh likeliest vel fi-tor wuh nop. Ni wuh klashausu t' wuh dover sakat nahp tor himself, ik gad mu-yor svi' november, veh thousand stehkuh hundred heh steh-leh-kaukuh, lumbering abru shooter's kunel, u' au lam-tor fi' ish-veh sha' particular perch za' wuh sakat, beating ish-veh ash'ya, heh keeping wuh bezhun heh wuh el'ru fi' wuh kar-tuf fa' ish-veh, wilat wuh putush-tor blunderbuss ti na' wuh fik t' shehkuh il ohkuh putush-tor jarel-el'ru-pohshayek, titau fi' wuh substratum t' cutlass. Wuh dover sakat vesh' svi' its tsuri genial shul ik wuh klashausu suspected wuh passengers, wuh passengers suspected veh wuh'ashiv heh wuh klashausu, au ek' suspected kanok-veh else, heh wuh coachman vesh' sure t' nothing tonk'peh wuh jarel; u' tor if cattle au kupi k' wuh pa'shik conscience ma taken ish-veh oath fi' wuh dahkuh testaments ik au vesh' ri nunau na' wuh halovaya. "wo-ho!" leralmin-tor wuh coachman. "ni, yi! Veh weht seshaya heh du're na' wuh fik heh nam-tor damned tor du, na' i ma had trouble hiyet tor prah du tor ish-veh!--joe!" "halloa!" wuh klashausu kilko-tor. "ra o'wak-vel tor du tor ish-veh, joe?" "lehkuh minutes, rom, vesht leh-wun." "t'nash-veh khaf!" khrasau wuh smertau coachman, "heh ri fi' t' shooter's wi! Tst! Yah! Prah fi' k' du!" wuh emphatic jarel, tresahk pen k' wuh wonil-zehl svi' wuh danik klopau negative, tor wuh klopau parish-tor na' ish-veh, heh wuh rehkuh vath jarel zahal-tor saikhut. Wuh'wak weht, wuh dover sakat struggled fi', k' wuh jack-kluf t' its passengers squashing bi' k' its vla. Au had pehkau lu wuh coach pehkau, heh au potau ikap-tor apc'koik k' ish-veh. Kuv sovek veh t' wuh rehkuh had had wuh hardihood tor propose tor wuh'ashiv tor lates fi' wuh pi' ahead vi' wuh mist heh mu'khlup'es, au would ma shitau himself svi' wuh rom yut t' getting pohshaya instantly u' wuh highwayman. Wuh kim-shah thorau lesh wuh sakat tor wuh dan-pid-sfek t' wuh kunel. Wuh jarel pehkau tor esh-tor va'ashiv, heh wuh klashausu prah ne' tor skid wuh halek na' wuh tevan, heh tu'ash wuh coach-svep tor kal-tor wuh passengers svi'. "tst! Joe!" maf-tor wuh coachman svi' wuh warning spes, looking ne' s' ish-veh natuhn. "ra tor du leralmin, tom?" au fi' shroi. "i leralmin wuh jarel na' wuh canter coming abru, joe." "i leralmin wuh jarel na' wuh ausahr, tom, " fun-tor wuh klashausu, leaving ish-veh meskaraya t' wuh svep, heh mounting nimbly tor ish-veh shi. "gentlemen! Svi' wuh sa-te'kru's ahm, ek' t' du!" k' nash hurried adjuration, au cocked ish-veh blunderbuss, heh lam-tor fi' wuh offensive. Wuh passenger booked k' nash vesht-var, vesh' fi' wuh coach-ash, getting svi'; wuh dahkuh vath passengers vesh' ikap-tor za' ish-veh, heh pa' tor zahal-tor. Au hafau fi' wuh ash, ulef svi' wuh coach heh ulef s'; au hafau svi' wuh fau-yut ne' ish-veh. Au ek' glazhau s' wuh coachman tor wuh klashausu, heh s' wuh klashausu tor wuh coachman, heh shroi. Wuh coachman glazhau pla' heh wuh klashausu glazhau pla', heh kauk wuh emphatic leader pricked abru ish-veh kaluk heh glazhau pla', rik' contradicting. Wuh stillness consequent fi' wuh cessation t' wuh rumbling heh labouring t' wuh coach, hau tor wuh stillness t' wuh mu-yor, tor ish-veh maut hizhuk indeed. Wuh panting t' wuh jarel sviribau wuh tremulous dvunel tor wuh coach, u' kuv ish-veh vesh' svi' wuh fupa s' t' agitation. Wuh khaf-spol t' wuh passengers kuhsh-tor ral hiyet sos'eh tor nam-tor puzhu-tor; tonk'peh na' sovek tav, wuh hizhuk svizh vesh' audibly expressive t' sutra s' esh, heh holding wuh esh, heh having wuh khaf-spol-gaya quickened k' gishat. Wuh ralash t' wuh jarel na' wuh ausahr sarlah sahris heh furiously abru wuh kunel. "ni-ho!" wuh klashausu sang si', u' ral u' au kupi roar. "yo tra'! Lamok! I dungau yon!" wuh sahr vesh' suddenly rihamau, heh, k' mau splashing heh floundering, wuh sasu's spes puvutau s' wuh mist, "nam-tor ik wuh dover sakat?" "worla du kashek ra ish-veh nam-tor!" wuh klashausu retorted. "ra nam-tor du?" "nam-tor ik wuh dover sakat?" "po tor du aitlun tor fai-tor?" "i aitlun wuh passenger, kuv ish-veh nam-tor." "ra passenger?" "mr. Jarvis lorry." etwel booked passenger gluvau svi' wuh moment ik ish-veh vesh' ish-veh ahm. Wuh klashausu, wuh coachman, heh wuh dahkuh vath passengers eyed ish-veh distrustfully. "potau wilat du nam-tor, " wuh klashausu puvutau tor wuh spes svi' wuh mist, "fai'ei, kuv i dang tor wuh lafosh, ish-veh kupi worla nam-tor eku gas'rak svi' ish-veh lifetime. Gentleman t' wuh ahm t' lorry kilko-srashiv zehik." "ra nam-tor wuh tukh?" ya'akash wuh passenger, yi, k' mildly quavering starun. "vi aitlu me? Nam-tor ish-veh jerry?" ("i ri tor spo' jerry's spes, kuv ish-veh nam-tor jerry, " growled wuh klashausu tor himself. "au's hoarser do saikhut me, nam-tor jerry.") "ha, mr. Lorry." "ra nam-tor wuh tukh?" "wuh despatch satau po' du s' abru' yonder. T. Heh co." "i fai-tor nash skladasu, klashausu, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, getting ne' vi' wuh fau-yut--gol-tor s' za' weht swiftly do politely k' wuh vath dahkuh passengers, vi iyi parish-tor vi' wuh coach, ikap-tor wuh svep, heh seshau abru wuh krani. "au lau sarlah ikap-tor; tra''s nothing riyeht." "i rok tra' ain't, tonk'peh i mokuhlek't tor ni 'shashol sure t' ik, " leralmin-tor wuh klashausu, svi' gruff soliloquy. "hallo du!" "muhl! Heh hallo du!" leralmin-tor jerry, weht hoarsely do fa'. "sarlah fi' na' wuh footpace! D'ye kashek me? Heh kuv du've prah holsters tor ik saddle o' yourn, ri tor kal-tor me gla-tor ish-veh el'ru hal-tor nigh 'em. Na' i'm wuh e'shua na' wuh sahris lafosh, heh lu i tor veh ish-veh nem-tor wuh shid t' ras-tukh. Ni i' kal-tor's glazhau na' du." wuh khlop t' wuh jarel heh rider sarlah slowly k'fai wuh eddying mist, heh sarlah tor wuh vla t' wuh sakat, wilat wuh passenger lam-tor. Wuh rider stooped, heh, casting abru ish-veh bezhun na' wuh klashausu, handed wuh passenger wuh pi' hesha dun. Wuh rider's jarel vesh' blown, heh fi' jarel heh rider vesh' wein-tor k' vral, s' wuh hoofs t' wuh jarel tor wuh taik t' wuh sasu. "klashausu!" leralmin-tor wuh passenger, svi' wuh molu t' hizhuk business guhl'es. Wuh tun-tor klashausu, k' ish-veh gas'rak el'ru na' wuh fek t' ish-veh ashenau blunderbuss, ish-veh losrak na' wuh subok, heh ish-veh bezhun fi' wuh horseman, kilko-tor curtly, "osu." "tra' nam-tor nothing tor apprehend. I belong tor tellson's kutra. Du bolau fai-tor tellson's kutra svi' london. I am going tor paris fi' business. Wuh tarkiv tor mon. I lau telv-tor nash?" "kuv ni nam-tor u' du're sahris, osu." au tu'ash ish-veh svi' wuh ta'hal t' wuh coach-ha'gelek fi' ik vla, heh telv-tor--wuh'rak tor himself heh yi aloud: "'bek-tor na' dover na' mam'selle.' ish-veh's ri wu, gla-tor du, klashausu. Jerry, leralmin ik t'nash-veh kilko-srashiv vesh', recalled tor ha'kiv." jerry palikau svi' ish-veh saddle. "ik's wuh blazing flekh kilko-srashiv, nuh', " leralmin-tor au, na' ish-veh hoarsest. "nem-tor ik skladan pla', heh au dungi fai-tor ik i poprah nash, u' muhl u' kuv i kitau. Tor wuh buhfik t' ish-veh yut. Rom mu-yor." k' eifa zhit wuh passenger tu'ash wuh coach-svep heh prah svi'; ri na' ek' gol-tor k' ish-veh katravahsu-passengers, vi had expeditiously secreted ish-veh glantau heh sa'haf svi' ish-veh kluf, heh vesh' i' tor wuh paik pretence t' hasu asleep. K' rai weht definite lof do tor stron wuh hazard t' originating sovek vath ves t' torai. Wuh coach lumbered fi' va'ashiv, k' heavier wreaths t' mist ikapik pauk ish-veh u' ish-veh began wuh tevan. Wuh klashausu ak va'prah ish-veh blunderbuss svi' ish-veh kar-tuf, heh, having glazhau tor wuh shom t' its tuhllar, heh having glazhau tor wuh supplementary el'ru-pohshayek ik au sai-vel-tor svi' ish-veh san-zhel, glazhau tor wuh smaller tuf ne'rak ish-veh ku-san, svi' if tra' vesh' wuh zamu zhuksu's raul, wuh couple t' torches, heh wuh tinder-natuhn. Na' au vesh' furnished k' ik completeness ik kuv wuh coach-ha'gelek had vesh' blown heh stormed si', if did occasionally pavesh-tor, au had goh tor ikap-tor himself abru svi'udish, potau wuh kil-tukh heh pishek kil-tor muhl ska' wuh terp, heh prah wuh ta'hal k' tolerable ek'manek heh ease (kuv au vesh' kunli) svi' kaukuh minutes. "tom!" softly abru' wuh coach kamu. "hallo, joe." "did du zhu-tor wuh skladan?" "i did, joe." "ra did du tor t' ish-veh, tom?" "nothing na' ek', joe." "ik's wuh coincidence, nuh', " wuh klashausu mused, "na' i tor wuh ka t' ish-veh myself." jerry, losrak sa'awek svi' wuh mist heh mu'khlup'es, dismounted meanwhile, ri goh tor ease ish-veh spent jarel, tonk'peh tor psethau wuh vral s' ish-veh limuk, heh hutau wuh masupik s' ish-veh taik-brim, if lau nam-tor capable t' holding pa' ulef wuh gallon. Po' standing k' wuh bridle abru' ish-veh heavily-splashed kar, abi' wuh halek t' wuh sakat vesh' rai longer k'svi khaf-spol heh wuh mu-yor vesh' ved fam dvun va'ashiv, au da-tor tor lates ne' wuh kunel. "po' ik tra' ausahr s' temple mofek, hinek t'sai, i skil-tor't sahrafel ish-veh fore-mal till i prah du fi' wuh volik, " leralmin-tor nash hoarse skladasu, glancing na' ish-veh mare. "'recalled tor ha'kiv.' ik's wuh blazing flekh skladan. Mau t' ik wouldn't tor na' du, jerry! I leralmin, jerry! Du'd nam-tor svi' wuh blazing rasahkos yut, kuv recalling tor ha'kiv vesh' tor sarlah vi' fashion, jerry!" chapter iii. Wuh mu-yor duv wuh wonderful kla-min tor haul-tor fi-tor, ik kanok komihn creature nam-tor constituted tor nam-tor ik profound tsat heh mystery tor kanok vath. Wuh solemn consideration, lu i svi-tor wuh lo'uk kahr k' mu-yor, ik kanok veh t' eifa darkly clustered kelek vi'ikap-tor its sha' tsat; ik kanok tvi-shal svi' kanok veh t' au vi'ikap-tor its sha' tsat; ik kanok beating khaf-spol svi' wuh hundreds t' thousands t' thasek tra', nam-tor, svi' ein t' its imaginings, wuh tsat tor wuh khaf-spol nearest ish-veh! Vel t' wuh awfulness, kauk t' tevakh itself, nam-tor referable tor nash. Rai weht mokuhlek i da-tor wuh mor t' nash tal-kam dunap ik i ashau, heh vainly rok svi' wak tor telv-tor ish-veh ek'. Rai weht mokuhlek i glazhau vi' wuh gluder t' nash unfathomable masu, wherein, u' momentary ha'ge glanced vi' ish-veh, i ma had glimpses t' visolektau treasure heh vath vel submerged. Ish-veh vesh' kru'minaakh ik wuh dunap dang ikap-tor k' wuh sikar, na' ek'wak heh na' ek'wak, lu i had telv-tor tonk'peh wuh thalv. Ish-veh vesh' kru'minaakh ik wuh masu dang nam-tor klacha svi' wuh ek'wakik le-su, lu wuh ta'hal vesh' mavaun fi' its skonn, heh i lam-tor svi' ignorance fi' wuh gef. T'nash-veh t'hy'la nam-tor tevik, t'nash-veh behsu nam-tor tevik, t'nash-veh ashaya, wuh ashal-veh t' t'nash-veh soul, nam-tor tevik; ish-veh nam-tor wuh inexorable lerashan heh perpetuation t' wuh tsat ik vesh' kwon-hau-ov svi' ik individuality, heh if i dungau lesh svi' t'nash-veh tor t'nash-veh ha'kiv's shaht. Svi' sovek t' wuh visolektaya-shitau t' nash kahr k'fai'ei i be' dvun, nam-tor tra' wuh sleeper weht inscrutable do its toranik inhabitants nam-tor, svi' ish-veh innermost nafu'es, tor me, il do i am tor au? U' tor nash, ish-veh malatik heh ri tor nam-tor alienated inheritance, wuh skladasu fi' horseback had exactly wuh ka ma-vel u' wuh sa-te'kru, wuh wuh'rak minister t' fupa s', il wuh richest merchant svi' london. Ni k' wuh rehkuh passengers ikap'uh t'du ru'lut svi' wuh wonil seshan-kharat-thonek t' veh lumbering hinek sakat coach; au vesh' mysteries tor veh wuh'ashiv, u' ovsotik u' kuv tik had vesh' svi' ish-veh sha' coach heh shehkuh, il ish-veh sha' coach heh sheh-leh, k' wuh breadth t' wuh county svi' ish-veh heh wuh thurai. Wuh skladasu fau-tor pla' na' wuh hagik sahr-tor, stopping takov k'ashiv na' ale-kelek k' wuh yut tor mon, tonk'peh evincing wuh tendency tor potau ish-veh sha' counsel, heh tor potau ish-veh taik cocked abru' ish-veh bezhun. Au had bezhun ik assorted maut muhl k' ik decoration, hasu t' wuh skonn nesh-kur, k' rai gluder svi' wuh kur il shid, heh mau nuh' be' teretuhr--u' kuv au vesh' kwes t' hasu afer-tor si' svi' vel, singly, kuv au potau nuh' irak k'wuhli. Au had wuh sinister sagluvaya, ne' wuh hinek cocked-taik spo' wuh rehkuh-cornered spittoon, heh abru' wuh lo'uk muffler na' wuh chin heh drahk, if tev-tor nearly tor wuh wearer's mal-nef. Lu au pehkau na' mon, au dvun-tor nash muffler k' ish-veh losrak el'ru, goh du' au mukau ish-veh liquor svi' k' ish-veh gas'rak; u' ak u' ik vesh' ovsoh, au nessau va'ashiv. "rai, jerry, rai!" leralmin-tor wuh skladasu, harping fi' veh theme u' au fau-tor. "ish-veh wouldn't tor na' du, jerry. Jerry, du trau tradesman, ish-veh wouldn't saikhut ish-veh zehl t' business! Recalled--! Bust me kuv i ri tor nah-tor au'd vesh' wuh drinking!" ish-veh skladan perplexed ish-veh kashek tor ik degree ik au vesh' fain, several wak, tor nem-tor ska' ish-veh taik tor scratch ish-veh patam. Kaula fi' wuh tarkiv, if vesh' raggedly bald, au had stegel, nesh-kur isachya, standing jaggedly ek' abru' ish-veh, heh growing ne' kunel siyah tor ish-veh sax'ksei, pasik han. Ish-veh vesh' ni spo' zhuksu's ar'kadan, ni mau weht spo' wuh fik t' wuh strongly spiked temok do wuh patam t' isachya, ik wuh buhfik t' hahf na' leap-git'woa lau ma declined ish-veh, u' wuh danik tehvar-bosh sasu svi' wuh panu tor hal-tor abru'. Du' au sahr-tor pla' k' wuh skladan au vesh' tor tefu tor wuh mu-yor watchman svi' ish-veh natuhn na' wuh svep t' tellson's kutra, k' temple mofek, vi vesh' tor tefu ish-veh tor greater ek'te'kru k'svi, wuh duv t' wuh mu-yor nem-tor such shid tor ish-veh u' arose s' wuh skladan, heh nem-tor such shid tor wuh mare u' arose s' ish-veh awek ong t' uneasiness. Au seemed tor nam-tor numerous, na' she shied na' kanok duv fi' wuh fau-yut. Ra wak, wuh sakat-coach lumbered, jolted, rattled, heh bumped fi-tor its tedious yut, k' its rehkuh katravahsu-inscrutables svi'udish. Tor ik, likewise, wuh duv t' wuh mu-yor revealed themselves, svi' wuh shidau ish-veh dozing bezhun heh wandering nahp suggested. Tellson's kutra had wuh sahr-tor fi-tor ish-veh svi' wuh sakat. U' wuh kutra passenger--k' wuh kar drawn k'fai wuh leathern zhel, if did ra ti svi' ish-veh tor potau ish-veh s' pounding tehnat wuh thurai passenger, heh driving ish-veh vi' ish-veh teruk, whenever wuh coach prah wuh special jolt--nodded svi' ish-veh shi, k' ulef-ikap-tor bezhun, wuh pi' coach-krani, heh wuh coach-ha'gelek dimly gleaming k'fai au, heh wuh bulky uzh'a'lek t' mesyutik passenger, became wuh kutra, heh did wuh lo'uk shad-kisheya t' business. Wuh rattle t' wuh harness vesh' wuh chink t' donku, heh weht fnalan vesh' pudor-tor svi' kaukuh minutes do kauk tellson's, k' ek' its k'shatri heh ha-kel tersaya, ek'wak vlitau svi' thrice wuh wak. Yi wuh karik-tvi-shal underground, na' tellson's, k' such t' ish-veh taluhk mahr-kel heh tsat u' vesh' fainu tor wuh passenger (heh ish-veh vesh' ri wuh pi' ik au fai-tor pa' au), tu'ash fa' ish-veh, heh au went svi' among au k' wuh lo'uk tal-muv heh wuh feebly-yontau ha'fek, heh afer-tor au safe, heh karik, heh ralash, heh fam dvun, aishan u' au had kim-shah gla-tor au. Tonk'peh, hi wuh kutra vesh' siyah kwon-hau-ov k' ish-veh, heh hi wuh coach (svi' wuh confused yut, spo' wuh la'es t' kusut ne' wuh opiate) vesh' kwon-hau-ov k' ish-veh, tra' vesh' wuh'ashiv current t' impression ik worla ceased tor sahr-tor, ek' k'fai wuh mu-yor. Au vesh' fi' ish-veh yut tor hil-tor ein veh s' wuh shi'vukhut. I', if t' wuh multitude t' limuk ik gluvau themselves fa' ish-veh vesh' wuh yeht limuk t' wuh visolektau person, wuh duv t' wuh mu-yor did ri indicate; tonk'peh au vesh' ek' wuh limuk t' wuh sasu t' kaukuh-heh-keh-leh k' tevun, heh au differed principally svi' wuh shaukaush au sagluvau, heh svi' wuh ghastliness t' ish-veh worn heh thinoi fupa s'. Pride, contempt, defiance, stubbornness, nekhaya, lamentation, navau veh wuh'ashiv; ni did vuhna'es t' sunken nak, cadaverous kur, emaciated el'ru heh khlop. Tonk'peh wuh limuk vesh' svi' wuh nen veh limuk, heh kanok patam vesh' prematurely wan-kur. Wuh hundred wak wuh dozing passenger inquired t' nash spectre: "visolektau uf wu?" wuh kilko-srashiv vesh' kwon-hau-ov wuh ka: "siyah leh-oh tevun." "du had abandoned ek' rok t' hasu hil-tor si'?" "wu ago." "du fai-tor ik du nam-tor recalled tor ha'kiv?" "au var-tor me ni." "i rok du tun tor ha-tor?" "i mokuhlek't leralmin." "dungau i gluvaya ish-veh tor du? Dungi sarlah du heh gla-tor ish-veh?" wuh kilko-srashiv tor nash deshker vesh' vuhnauk heh contradictory. Sometimes wuh pushau kilko vesh', "bek-tor! Ish-veh would stau me kuv vesht gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh nuh' ak." sometimes, ish-veh vesh' putan-tor svi' wuh sival sov-masu t' bezhun-masu, heh yi ish-veh vesh', "nem-tor me tor ish-veh." sometimes ish-veh vesh' staring heh bewildered, heh yi ish-veh vesh', "i ri tor fai-tor ish-veh. I ri tor ken-tor." po' such glenonik discourse, wuh passenger svi' ish-veh fancy would hil-tor, heh hil-tor, hil-tor--i' k' wuh ash'ya-hilek, i' k' wuh lo'uk tal-muv, i' k' ish-veh el'ru--tor hil-tor nash wretched creature si'. Prah si' na' kim-shah, k' terra hanging pa' ish-veh limuk heh isachya, au would suddenly sovek maf tor grazhiv. Wuh passenger would yi palikaya tor himself, heh weh-neik wuh krani, tor prah wuh reality t' mist heh sov-masu fi' ish-veh nak. Wi kauk lu ish-veh bezhun vesh' tu'ash fi' wuh mist heh sov-masu, fi' wuh dvun-tor patch t' ta'hal s' wuh ha'gelek, heh wuh labah na' wuh roadside retreating k' hutau, wuh mu-yor duv s'udish wuh coach would tevan vi' wuh ranau t' wuh mu-yor duv k'svi. Wuh yeht banking-kelek k' temple mofek, wuh yeht business t' wuh vesht gad, wuh yeht karik tvi-shal, wuh yeht sagluvau satau po' ish-veh, heh wuh yeht skladan fun-tor, would ek' nam-tor tra'. Si' t' wuh midst t' au, wuh ghostly limuk would shen, heh au would accost ish-veh va'ashiv. "visolektau uf wu?" "siyah leh-oh tevun." "i rok du tun tor ha-tor?" "i mokuhlek't leralmin." hil-tor--hil-tor--hil-tor--abi' wuh impatient dvun s' veh t' wuh dahkuh passengers would admonish ish-veh tor seshaya abru wuh krani, bes-tor ish-veh kar securely k'fai wuh leathern zhel, heh speculate fi-tor wuh dahkuh slumbering shidau, abi' ish-veh kashek pakik its meskaraya t' au, heh au va'ashiv slid maf vi' wuh kutra heh wuh shi'vukhut. "visolektau uf wu?" "siyah leh-oh tevun." "du had abandoned ek' rok t' hasu hil-tor si'?" "wu ago." wuh zhit vesh' fam dvun svi' ish-veh khaf-spol u' aishan spoken--distinctly svi' ish-veh khaf-spol u' ek'wak spoken zhit had vesh' svi' ish-veh ha'kiv--lu wuh weary passenger palikau tor wuh hokni'es t' gad-ha'khlup, heh afer-tor ik wuh duv t' wuh mu-yor vesh' hal-tor. Au ne-tor wuh krani, heh glazhau si' na' wuh rising yel. Tra' vesh' wuh tauf t' ploughed solektra, k' wuh plough fi-tor ish-veh wilat ish-veh had vesh' losrak kim-shah mu-yor lu wuh jarel vesh' unyoked; mesakh, wuh hizhuk coppice-lapan, svi' if wehk mor t' yontau yon-kur heh pi-maat-kur kin-kur fam dvun hafau fi-tor wuh lap. Hi wuh terra vesh' samu heh masupik, wuh igen vesh' pa'shik, heh wuh yel she-tor ugelik, placid, heh vaksurik. "leh-oh tevun!" leralmin-tor wuh passenger, looking na' wuh yel. "gracious fereiksu t' gad! Tor nam-tor visolektau alive na' leh-oh tevun!" chapter iv. Wuh preparation lu wuh sakat prah successfully tor dover, svi' wuh rivak t' wuh forenoon, wuh patam zish-nef na' wuh royal george hotel tu'ash wuh coach-svep u' ish-veh custom vesh'. Au did ish-veh k' ein flourish t' hali-kal, na' wuh sakat halovaya s' london svi' karil vesh' wuh srashiv tor congratulate wuh adventurous traveller fi-tor. K' ik wak, tra' vesh' goh veh adventurous traveller losrak nam-tor congratulated: na' wuh dahkuh vath had vesh' eku ne' na' ish-veh respective roadside destinations. Wuh mildewy svi' wuh coach, k' its damp heh kitork terp, its disagreeable fnish-tor, heh its obscurity, vesh' rather spo' wuh larger dog-kennel. Mr. Lorry, wuh passenger, shaking himself si' t' ish-veh svi' naf-elakh t' terp, wuh tangle t' shaggy wrapper, flapping taik, heh muddy mal, vesh' rather spo' wuh larger wihfelau t' dog. "tra' dungi nam-tor wuh packet tor calais, fa-gad, zish-nef?" "ha, osu, kuv wuh igen-va meskarau heh wuh salan dvolau tolerable rom. Wuh mashen dungi dvin-tor takov nicely na' pa' dahkuh svi' wuh aru, osu. Sar-tak, osu?" "i dungau ri hal-tor tor sar-tak till mu-yor; tonk'peh i aitlun wuh shi'yuk, heh wuh barber." "heh yi asal-yem, osu? Ha, osu. Ik yut, osu, kuv du sanoi. Gluvaya concord! Gentleman's valise heh fal masu tor concord. Seshaya ska' gentleman's kluf svi' concord. (du dungi talal wuh tok-ti masutra-kastik-kov yon, osu.) zaprah barber tor concord. Stir pa' tra', i', na' concord!" wuh concord sar-tak-tvi-shal hasu kwon-hau-ov assigned tor wuh passenger k' wuh sakat, heh passengers k' wuh sakat hasu kwon-hau-ov heavily wrapped abru s' patam tor ash'ya, wuh tvi-shal had wuh shaik eku'ko na' wuh establishment t' wuh royal george, ik hi tonk'peh veh ves t' sasu vesh' gla-tor tor hal-tor vi' ish-veh, ek' ves heh vuhna'es t' sasu sasarlah t' ish-veh. Consequently, wuh'ashiv zish-nef, heh dahkuh porters, heh several maids heh wuh landlady, vesh' ek' loitering k' kisheya na' vuhnauk sfekau t' wuh fau-yut svi' wuh concord heh wuh mon-tvi-shal, lu wuh gentleman t' sheh-leh, formally sai-vel-tor svi' wuh khav-kur saikhut t' sai-vel, takov muhl worn, tonk'peh maut muhl potau, k' suk keh-vla cuffs heh suk pi'rala tor wuh abru'lik, be' dvun-tor bi' fi' ish-veh yut tor ish-veh asal-yem. Wuh mon-tvi-shal had rai vath occupant, ik forenoon, do wuh gentleman svi' khav-kur. Ish-veh asal-yem-pasu vesh' drawn fa' wuh yon, heh u' au hayal-tor, k' its ta'hal shining fi' ish-veh, waiting na' wuh yem, au hayal-tor ni fam dvun, ik au lau ma vesh' sitting na' ish-veh portrait. Maut orderly heh methodical au glazhau, k' wuh el'ru fi' tik mal-nef, heh wuh ral glantau ticking wuh sonorous sermon ne' ish-veh flapped san-tor-pal, u' hi ish-veh pitted its ne-seshan heh difan'es tehnat wuh levity heh rikwon'es t' wuh brax yon. Au had wuh rom mal, heh vesh' wuh pi' vain t' ish-veh, na' ish-veh khav-kur stockings fitted sleek heh ikap-tor, heh vesh' t' wuh tok-ti lef'es; ish-veh ash'el heh tersek, nuh', hi eiktra, vesh' trim. Au sai-vel-tor wuh shaik pi' sleek crisp flaxen wig, setting maut beyik ish-veh patam: if wig, ish-veh nam-tor tor nam-tor presumed, vesh' tor t' isachya, tonk'peh if glazhau irak weht u' hi ish-veh vesh' pada-tor s' pi'elakh t' silk il makh. Ish-veh linen, hi ri t' wuh fineness svi' accordance k' ish-veh stockings, vesh' u' wan-kur u' wuh fik t' wuh pral ik shau fi-tor wuh neighbouring shahov, il wuh specks t' mashalo-thalv ik glinted svi' wuh ug'yel-ha'gel irak na' masutra. Wuh limuk habitually nelau heh quieted, vesh' fam dvun lighted abru ne' wuh quaint wig k' wuh shif t' moist ugelik bezhun ik ish-veh bolau ma kodona ish-veh owner, svi' tevun hal-tor k', ein kusut-tor tor spitau tor wuh tertitau heh reserved sagluvaya t' tellson's kutra. Au had wuh muhl-bosh kur svi' ish-veh nak, heh ish-veh limuk, hi zehl-tor, spitau zamu zavikau t' anxiety. Tonk'peh, sos'eh wuh confidential bachelor clerks svi' tellson's kutra vesh' principally occupied k' wuh tun-tor t' vath sutra; heh sos'eh dahr-el'ru tun-tor, spo' dahr-el'ru sai-vel, sarlah easily ska' heh fi'. Completing ish-veh resemblance tor wuh sasu vi vesh' sitting na' ish-veh portrait, mr. Lorry eku-tor ska' tor yuk. Wuh lashan t' ish-veh asal-yem kastorilau ish-veh, heh au leralmin-tor tor wuh zish-nef, u' au dvun-tor ish-veh ku-san tor ish-veh: "i istaya accommodation dator na' wuh nu'ri t'sai vi lau sarlah la' na' sovek wak tor-gad. She lau ya'akash na' mr. Jarvis lorry, il she lau goh ya'akash na' wuh gentleman s' tellson's kutra. Sanoi tor kal-tor me fai-tor." "ha, osu. Tellson's kutra svi' london, osu?" "ha." "ha, osu. Etek ma oftentimes wuh dor tor entertain ish-veh gentlemen svi' ish-veh travelling pla'rak heh fa'rak betwixt london heh paris, osu. Wuh vast deal t' travelling, osu, svi' tellson heh apc'koik's kelek." "ha. Etek nam-tor ved wuh french kelek, u' muhl u' wuh eingelsu veh." "ha, osu. Ri mau svi' wuh es'merka t' such travelling yourself, i nah-tor, osu?" "ri t' tab-ma tevun. Ish-veh nam-tor leh-kau tevun opi' etek--opi' i--sarlah kim-shah s' france." "indeed, osu? Ik vesh' fa' t'nash-veh wak la', osu. Fa' etwel sutra's wak la', osu. Wuh george vesh' svi' vath el'ru na' ik wak, osu." "i dva-tor ni." "tonk'peh i would meskaraya wuh takov wager, osu, ik wuh kelek spo' tellson heh apc'koik vesh' flourishing, wuh tukh t' kau-leh, ri tor stariben t' leh-kau tevun ago?" "du lau abralash ik, heh leralmin wuh hundred heh kau-leh, wi ri nam-tor irak s' wuh yeht'es." "indeed, osu!" rounding ish-veh ru'lut heh fi' ish-veh bezhun, u' au ash-tor pla'rak s' wuh pasu, wuh waiter izau ish-veh ru'lut-sai s' ish-veh gas'rak kar tor ish-veh losrak, eku-tor vi' wuh kel'o attitude, heh lam-tor surveying wuh be'hai'la du' au ate heh drank, u' s' wuh shi'igen-glantaya il watchtower. Fupa s' wuh immemorial nam-tor t' waiters svi' ek' ya'shakhuv. Lu mr. Lorry had shahtau ish-veh asal-yem, au went si' na' wuh stroll fi' wuh shahov. Wuh pi' wonil, pi'tak-tor kahr t' dover ip-sut itself maf s' wuh shahov, heh sahr-tor its patam vi' wuh gav menal, spo' wuh marine ostrich. Wuh shahov vesh' wuh eshikh t' heaps t' masutra heh kov tumbling wildly pa', heh wuh masutra did ra ish-veh tishau, heh ra ish-veh tishau vesh' vashaya. Ish-veh thundered na' wuh kahr, heh thundered na' wuh menal, heh katau wuh gef ne', madly. Wuh sov among wuh kelek vesh' t' ni karik wuh piscatory zahv ish-veh lau ma supposed has-bosh aluk went abru tor nam-tor spis-tor svi' ish-veh, u' has-bosh sutra went ne' tor nam-tor spis-tor svi' wuh masutra. Wuh pi' fishing vesh' ovsoh svi' wuh kif, heh wuh nosahp t' strolling pa' k' mu-yor, heh looking seaward: wa' na' eifa wak lu wuh mashen tor, heh vesh' be' abrash. Pi' tradesmen, vi did rai business whatever, sometimes unaccountably realised suk fortunes, heh ish-veh vesh' remarkable ik kling svi' wuh neighbourhood kupi palesh-tor wuh lamplighter. U' wuh gad declined vi' wuh aru, heh wuh sov, if had vesh' na' tvi-wak pa'shik hiyet tor kal-tor wuh french gef tor nam-tor gla-tor, became va'ashiv vifalunau k' mist heh muhs, mr. Lorry's nahp seemed tor wan nuh'. Lu ish-veh vesh' gu'gelik, heh au hayal-tor fa' wuh mon-tvi-shal yon, awaiting ish-veh aru-yem u' au had awaited ish-veh asal-yem, ish-veh kashek vesh' busily digging, digging, digging, svi' wuh ha-tor yon-kur kastik-kov. Wuh mashek t' rom claret po' aru-yem tor wuh hilek svi' wuh yon-kur kastik-kov rai klau, vathru do u' ish-veh has wuh tendency tor lehm ish-veh s' ar'kadan. Mr. Lorry had vesh' idle wuh akarshif, heh had aishan mukau si' ish-veh kim-shah glassful t' wine k' u' ovsotik wuh appearance t' satisfaction u' nam-tor ek'wak tor nam-tor afer-tor svi' wuh shakhupik gentleman t' wuh sluk complexion vi has prah tor wuh shaht t' wuh mashek, lu wuh rattling t' halek sarlah abru wuh wonil yut, heh rumbled vi' wuh ha-shal-ker. Au eku ne' ish-veh makh untouched. "nash nam-tor mam'selle!" leralmin-tor au. Svi' wuh maut zamu minutes wuh waiter sarlah svi' tor tor'pra ik din-tor manette had lasha s' london, heh would nam-tor kunli tor gla-tor wuh gentleman s' tellson's. "ni ak?" din-tor manette had taken ein refreshment fi' wuh fau-yut, heh required rim yi, heh vesh' extremely anxious tor gla-tor wuh gentleman s' tellson's iyi, kuv ish-veh suited ish-veh sanosh heh convenience. Wuh gentleman s' tellson's had nothing losrak na' ish-veh tonk'peh tor herbosh ish-veh makh k' wuh sov t' stolid desperation, settle ish-veh shaik pi' flaxen wig na' wuh kaluk, heh zahal-tor wuh waiter tor din-tor manette's ha-shal. Ish-veh vesh' wuh suk, gu'gelik tvi-shal, furnished svi' wuh funereal manner k' nesh-kur horsehair, heh putush-tor k' ras gu'gelik pasu. Aifa had vesh' oiled heh oiled, abi' wuh dahkuh ha-vol ha'fek fi' wuh pasu svi' wuh svitan t' wuh tvi-shal vesh' gloomily haul-tor fi' kanok mor; u' kuv au vesh' visolektau, svi' glu shi'vukhut t' nesh-kur mahogany, heh rai ta'hal tor stariben t' kupi nam-tor gishu s' au abi' au vesh' hil-tor si'. Wuh obscurity vesh' ni rihagik tor penetrate ik mr. Lorry, picking ish-veh yut abru' wuh muhl-worn kushel la'y, supposed din-tor manette tor nam-tor, na' wuh moment, svi' ein beyik tvi-shal, abi', having prah vesht wuh dahkuh ha-vol ha'fek, gla-tor ish-veh standing tor poprah ish-veh k' wuh pasu svi' au heh wuh yon, wuh nu'ri t'sai t' ri weht do leh- steh, svi' wuh riding-tor-sai, heh fam dvun holding ish-veh terp travelling-taik k' its ribbon svi' ish-veh el'ru. U' ish-veh bezhun shom-tor fi' wuh pen, slight, takov khlop, wuh nosahp t' pi-maat-kur isachya, wuh shif t' pla-kur bezhun ik ragel-tor ish-veh sha' k' wuh inquiring glazhau, heh wuh fa-patam k' wuh singular tsoh (remembering uf nu'ri heh mos ish-veh vesh'), t' rifting heh knitting itself vi' wuh sagluvaya ik vesh' ri ved veh t' perplexity, il wonder, il vikayek, il goh t' wuh ugelik teslau attention, hi ish-veh vinan-tor ek' wuh kehkuh sagluvaya--u' ish-veh bezhun shom-tor fi' aifa vel, wuh sudden vivid likeness be' dvun-tor fa' ish-veh, t' wuh kan ik au had meskarau svi' ish-veh kar fi' wuh tvur mes' ik maut mashyut, veh samu wak, lu wuh masu-kov marau heavily heh wuh masutra sahr-tor pid. Wuh likeness be' dvun-tor maf, spo' wuh esh bi' wuh skonn t' wuh gaunt pier-makh za' ish-veh, fi' wuh nentu t' if, wuh shi'has procession t' negro cupids, several headless heh ek' cripples, vesh' nufaya nesh-kur ki'haf t' tevik masutra savas tor nesh-kur divinities t' wuh kogavik guv--heh au tor ish-veh hotorik kes-wun tor din-tor manette. "pray nem-tor wuh ku-san, osu." svi' wuh maut pa'shik heh vaksurik nu'ri spes; wuh pi' k'shatri svi' its accent, tonk'peh wuh maut pi' indeed. "i shok ish-veh el'ru, din-tor, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, k' wuh manners t' wuh earlier kinuf, u' au tor ish-veh hotorik kes-wun va'ashiv, heh nem-tor ish-veh ku-san. "i poprah wuh nuhm s' wuh kutra, osu, za-gad, informing me ik ein kash-tor'es--il discovery--" "wuh zhit nam-tor ri tukh, din-tor; either zhit dungi tor." "--respecting wuh pi' veltra t' t'nash-veh ri donku-tor sa-mekh, ik i worla gla-tor--ni wu tevik--" mr. Lorry dvun-tor svi' ish-veh ku-san, heh vishizhau wuh troubled glazhau na' wuh shi'has procession t' negro cupids. U' kuv au had sovek gol'nev na' anybody svi' ish-veh absurd ki'haf! "--rendered ish-veh bolayatik ik i dang hal-tor tor paris, tra' tor sviribau k' wuh gentleman t' wuh kutra, ni rom u' tor nam-tor despatched tor paris na' wuh lof." "myself." "u' i vesh' dator tor zhu-tor, osu." she curtseyed tor ish-veh (nu'ri t'sai tor curtseys svi' eifa gad), k' wuh takov aitlun tor zhelesh tor ish-veh ik she olau uf mau older heh wiser au vesh' do she. Au tor ish-veh wuh'ashiv kes-wun. "i kilko-tor tor wuh kutra, osu, ik u' ish-veh vesh' panah-tor bolayatik, k' eifa vi fai-tor, heh vi nam-tor ni ves u' tor na'shikhau me, ik i dang hal-tor tor france, heh ik u' i am wuh orphan heh ma rai t'hy'la vi kupi hal-tor k' me, i dang vam ish-veh highly kuv i lau nam-tor permitted tor shi myself, du' wuh halovaya, ne' ik worthy gentleman's protection. Wuh gentleman had losrak london, tonk'peh i nah-tor wuh skladasu vesh' satau po' ish-veh tor eit'jae wuh favour t' ish-veh waiting na' me la'." "i vesh' kunli, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, "tor nam-tor entrusted k' wuh falun. I dungau nam-tor weht kunli tor fitor ish-veh." "osu, i nemaiyo indeed. I nemaiyo maut gratefully. Ish-veh vesh' var-tor me k' wuh kutra ik wuh gentleman would danau tor me wuh details t' wuh business, heh ik i bolau dator myself tor talal au t' wuh surprising malat. I ma ovsoh t'nash-veh buhfik tor dator myself, heh i naturally ma wuh karik heh nayik eku'ko tor fai-tor ra au nam-tor." "naturally, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry. "ha--i--" po' wuh svizh, au hau, va'ashiv settling wuh crisp flaxen wig na' wuh kaluk, "ish-veh nam-tor maut rihagik tor palikau." au did ri palikau, tonk'peh, svi' ish-veh indecision, ragel-tor ish-veh glance. Wuh nu'ri fa-patam abertau itself vi' ik singular sagluvaya--tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' takov heh noshtra, isha hasu singular--heh she ashenau ish-veh el'ru, u' kuv k' wuh shatipik torai she kum-tor na', il stayed ein be' dvun-tor duv. "nam-tor du ved wuh ri-fainusu tor me, osu?" "am i ri?" mr. Lorry tu'ash ish-veh el'ru, heh sadvun-tor au outwards k' wuh argumentative abru'teruklar-ru'lut. Svi' wuh bezhun-zehl heh aishan abru' wuh pi' kogavik han, wuh zehl t' if vesh' u' delicate heh tok-ti u' ish-veh vesh' tor-yehat tor nam-tor, wuh sagluvaya deepened itself u' she nem-tor ish-veh ku-san thoughtfully svi' wuh ku-san k' if she had hitherto hafau standing. Au glantau ish-veh u' she mused, heh wuh moment she ashenau ish-veh bezhun va'ashiv, went fi': "svi' ish-veh thanai shasol, i presume, i fam yehat tor weh-rom do shi'yavekh du u' wuh nu'ri eingelsu t'sai, din-tor manette?" "kuv du sanoi, osu." "din-tor manette, i am wuh sasu t' business. I ma wuh business falun tor acquit myself t'. Svi' ish-veh reception t' ish-veh, ri tor heed me sovek weht do kuv i vesh' wuh speaking mish-vel--truly, i am ri mau else. I dungi, k' ish-veh trasha, relate tor du, din-tor, wuh var t' veh t' etwel klepovausu." "var!" au seemed wilfully tor lafosh wuh zhit she had ashiv-tor, lu au hau, svi' wuh brax, "ha, klepovausu; svi' wuh banking business etek usually vutau etwel tersaya etwel klepovausu. Au vesh' wuh french gentleman; wuh talik gentleman; wuh sasu t' lo'uk acquirements--wuh hassu." "ri t' beauvais?" "po, ha, t' beauvais. Spo' monsieur manette, ish-veh sa-mekh, wuh gentleman vesh' t' beauvais. Spo' monsieur manette, ish-veh sa-mekh, wuh gentleman vesh' t' repute svi' paris. I had wuh dor t' fai-tor ish-veh tra'. Etwel relations vesh' business relations, tonk'peh confidential. I vesh' na' ik wak svi' etwel french kelek, heh had vesh'--oh! Dah-leh tevun." "na' ik wak--i lau ya'akash, na' ra wak, osu?" "i stariben, din-tor, t' dah-leh tevun ago. Au telik--wuh eingelsu t'sai--heh i vesh' veh t' wuh trustees. Ish-veh tek'ik, spo' wuh tek'ik t' wehk vath french gentlemen heh french skan, vesh' entirely svi' tellson's el'ru. Svi' wuh kahwa yut i am, il i ma vesh', trustee t' veh ves il vath na' nosahp t' etwel klepovausu. Aifa nam-tor mere business relations, din-tor; tra' nam-tor rai friendship svi' au, rai particular eku'ko, nothing spo' sentiment. I ma be' dvun-tor s' veh tor wuh'ashiv, svi' wuh rivak t' t'nash-veh business ha'kiv, aishan u' i be' dvun s' veh t' etwel klepovausu tor wuh'ashiv svi' wuh rivak t' t'nash-veh business gad; svi' pen, i ma rai feelings; i am wuh mere mish-vel. Tor hal-tor fi'--" "tonk'peh nash nam-tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh's var, osu; heh i palikau tor nah-tor"--wuh curiously roughened fa-patam vesh' maut intent fi-tor ish-veh--"ik lu i vesh' losrak wuh orphan k'fai t'nash-veh ko-mekh's surviving t'nash-veh sa-mekh goh dahkuh tevun, ish-veh vesh' du vi katau me tor england. I am siyah sure ish-veh vesh' du." mr. Lorry nem-tor wuh hesitating pi' el'ru ik confidingly storilau tor nem-tor ish-veh, heh au shitau ish-veh k' ein hali-kal tor ish-veh bru-lar. Au yi conducted wuh nu'ri t'sai straightway tor ish-veh ku-san va'ashiv, heh, holding wuh ku-san-pla' k' ish-veh losrak el'ru, heh using ish-veh gas'rak k' da-tor tor tetaya ish-veh chin, seshaya ish-veh wig na' wuh kaluk, il sfek ra au leralmin-tor, lam-tor looking ne' vi' ish-veh limuk du' she hayal-tor looking abru vi' ish-veh. "din-tor manette, ish-veh vesh' i. Heh du dungi gla-tor uf truly i stariben t' myself aishan i', svi' taran i had rai feelings, heh ik ek' wuh relations i meskaraya k' t'nash-veh katravahsu-creatures nam-tor mere business relations, lu du haul-tor ik i ma worla gla-tor du opi'. Rai; du ma vesh' wuh ward t' tellson's kelek opi', heh i ma vesh' toranik k' wuh vath business t' tellson's kelek opi'. Feelings! I ma rai wak na' au, rai pavesh t' au. I be' dvun t'nash-veh bosh ha'kiv, din-tor, svi' turning wuh immense pecuniary mangle." po' nash shaik kethelvaya t' ish-veh kanok-gadik routine t' employment, mr. Lorry flattened ish-veh flaxen wig fi-tor ish-veh patam k' fi' el'ru (if vesh' danik unnecessary, na' nothing kupi nam-tor snuhkrol-tor do its shining skonn vesh' fa'), heh resumed ish-veh former attitude. "ni irak, din-tor (u' du ma remarked), nash nam-tor wuh var t' ish-veh regretted sa-mekh. I' sarlah wuh natyan. Kuv ish-veh sa-mekh had ri tev-tor lu au did--ri tor nam-tor koltha! Uf du palikaya!" she did, indeed, palikaya. Heh she kum-tor ish-veh kar-nik k' fi' ish-veh el'ru. "pray, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, svi' wuh soothing molu, bringing ish-veh losrak el'ru s' wuh pla' t' wuh ku-san tor ti ish-veh fi' wuh supplicatory ozh ik clasped ish-veh svi' ni khrashik wuh tremble: "pray tash ish-veh agitation--wuh tukh t' business. U' i vesh' taran--" ish-veh glazhau ni discomposed ish-veh ik au pehkau, czar-tor, heh began anew: "u' i vesh' taran; kuv monsieur manette had ri tev-tor; kuv au had suddenly heh silently sasaudau; kuv au had vesh' spirited maf; kuv ish-veh had ri vesh' rihagik tor guess tor ra dreadful shi, hi rai tanaf kupi zavikau ish-veh; kuv au had wuh nemut svi' ein compatriot vi kupi tusok wuh privilege ik i svi' t'nash-veh sha' wak ma fainu wuh boldest sutra kwes tor stariben t' svi' wuh zhal, mes' wuh masu tra'; na' instance, wuh privilege t' boshak abru blank shidau na' wuh consignment t' sovek veh tor wuh oblivion t' wuh prison na' sovek wu-vath t' wak; kuv ish-veh ko-telsu had implored wuh sa-te'kru, wuh ko-te'kru, wuh kelek, wuh clergy, na' sovek tidings t' ish-veh, heh ek' ved svi' vain; --yi wuh vesht-var t' ish-veh sa-mekh would ma vesh' wuh vesht-var t' nash unfortunate gentleman, wuh hassu t' beauvais." "i entreat du tor var-tor me weht, osu." "i dungi. I am going tor. Du mokuhlek lesh ish-veh?" "i mokuhlek lesh sovek-vel tonk'peh wuh uncertainty du trasha me svi' na' nash moment." "du stariben collectedly, heh du--nam-tor tershau. Ik's rom!" (hi ish-veh manner vesh' lehkuh satisfied do ish-veh zhit.) "wuh tukh t' business. Fudau ish-veh u' wuh tukh t' business--business ik bolau nam-tor ovsoh. I' kuv nash hassu's ko-telsu, hi wuh t'sai t' lo'uk courage heh tam'a, had dashau ni intensely s' nash aishan fa' ish-veh pi' kan vesh' pukeshta--" "wuh pi' kan vesh' wuh ko-fu, osu." "wuh ko-fu. Wuh-wuh-tukh t' business--ri tor nam-tor flakosh. Din-tor, kuv wuh ri donku-tor t'sai had dashau ni intensely fa' ish-veh pi' kan vesh' pukeshta, ik sarlah ish-veh tor wuh determination t' sparing wuh ri donku-tor kan wuh inheritance t' sovek krus t' wuh agony she had fainu wuh kusut-tor t', k' rearing ish-veh svi' wuh dva ik ish-veh sa-mekh vesh' tevik--rai, ri tor kneel! Svi' sha-ka-ri's ahm po dang du kneel tor me!" "na' wuh yeht'es. O tal-kam, rom, compassionate osu, na' wuh yeht'es!" "wuh--wuh tukh t' business. Du confuse me, heh uf mokuhlek i transact business kuv i am confused? Kal-tor etek nam-tor pa'shik-headed. Kuv du kupi kindly mention i', na' instance, ra naukuh wak ninepence nam-tor, il uf wehk shillings svi' dah-leh guineas, ish-veh would nam-tor ni encouraging. I dang nam-tor ni mau weht na' t'nash-veh ease pa' ish-veh fupa s' t' kashek." rik' directly answering tor nash appeal, she hayal-tor ni fam dvun lu au had maut kogavik ashenau ish-veh, heh wuh el'ru ik had ri ceased tor clasp ish-veh kar-nik vesh' ni mau weht br'xan do au had vesh', ik she sviribau ein reassurance tor mr. Jarvis lorry. "ik's gas'rak, ik's gas'rak. Courage! Business! Du ma business fa' du; useful business. Din-tor manette, ish-veh ko-mekh nem-tor nash rivak k' du. Heh lu she tev-tor--i dva-tor pushau-hearted--having worla slackened ish-veh unavailing psthan na' ish-veh sa-mekh, she losrak du, na' dahkuh tevun hinek, tor tor'ovau tor nam-tor svai-tu-ashya, vaksurik, heh kunli, rik' wuh gu'gelik wan fi-tor du t' living svi' uncertainty whether ish-veh sa-mekh ak sai-vel-tor ish-veh khaf-spol si' svi' prison, il thinoi tra' k'fai wehk svizh-tor tevun." u' au leralmin-tor wuh zhit au glazhau ne', k' wuh krol-tor pity, fi' wuh flowing pi-maat-kur isachya; u' kuv au pictured tor himself ik ish-veh lau ma vesh' already kur-tor k' zhai-kur. "du fai-tor ik ish-veh mekhlar had rai lo'uk mat, heh ik ra au had vesh' shar-tor tor ish-veh ko-mekh heh tor du. Tra' has vesh' rai uzh discovery, t' donku, il t' sovek vath veltra; tonk'peh--" au olau ish-veh kar-nik meskarau closer, heh au pehkau. Wuh sagluvaya svi' wuh fa-patam, if had ni wa' skamau ish-veh beglanau, heh if vesh' i' immovable, had deepened vi' veh t' kusut heh horror. "tonk'peh au has vesh'--vesh' afer-tor. Au nam-tor alive. Greatly rubai, ish-veh nam-tor nuh' yesik; siyah wuh vashau, ish-veh nam-tor tor-yehat; hi etek dungi rok wuh buhfik. Fam dvun, alive. Ish-veh sa-mekh has vesh' taken tor wuh kelek t' wuh hinek dvinsu svi' paris, heh etek nam-tor going tra': i, tor shasutan-tor ish-veh kuv i mokuhlek: du, tor restore ish-veh tor ha'kiv, ashaya, gu-vam, shom, comfort." wuh shiver sahr-tor k'fai ish-veh nentu, heh s' ish-veh k'fai ish-veh. She leralmin-tor, svi' wuh neik, natya, teshan-stricken spes, u' kuv she vesh' taran ish-veh svi' wuh sahr-tor, "i am going tor gla-tor ish-veh tam'a! Ish-veh dungi nam-tor ish-veh tam'a--ri ish-veh!" mr. Lorry quietly chafed wuh el'ru ik meskarau ish-veh kar. "tra', tra', tra'! Gla-tor i', gla-tor i'! Wuh buhfik heh wuh rasahkos nam-tor fainu tor du, i'. Du nam-tor muhl fi' ish-veh yut tor wuh ri donku-tor wronged gentleman, heh, k' wuh rom masutra halan, heh wuh rom solektra halovaya, du dungi nam-tor ak na' ish-veh tal-kam vla." she ashiv-tor svi' wuh ka molu, ne'hal-tor tor wuh zhal, "i ma vesh' elik, i ma vesh' kunli, wi ish-veh tam'a has worla haunted me!" "goh veh vel weht, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, laying hishel fi-tor ish-veh u' wuh wholesome tvai t' enforcing ish-veh attention: "au has vesh' afer-tor ne' wuh'ashiv ahm; ish-veh sha', wu yen-tor il wu ip-sut. Ish-veh would nam-tor weh-rasahkos do nam-tor-fam i' tor inquire if; weh-rasahkos do nam-tor-fam tor seek tor fai-tor whether au has vesh' na' tevun overlooked, il kwon-hau-ov designedly meskarau prisoner. Ish-veh would nam-tor weh-rasahkos do nam-tor-fam i' tor tor sovek inquiries, fai'ei ish-veh would nam-tor tehvar-bosh. Weh-rom ri tor mention wuh subject, sovek-wilat il svi' sovek yut, heh tor snem-tor ish-veh--na' wuh du' na' ek' pavek--s' france. Kauk i, safe u' wuh englishman, heh kauk tellson's, yauluhk u' au nam-tor tor french lit, nan'woi ek' naming t' wuh tukh. I lesh pa' me, ri wuh moguhsh t' kitaun openly referring tor ish-veh. Nash nam-tor wuh tsat dvin altogether. T'nash-veh credentials, svin, heh memoranda, nam-tor ek' comprehended svi' wuh veh zehl, 'recalled tor ha'kiv; ' if lau tvai sovek-vel. Tonk'peh ra nam-tor wuh tukh! She doesn't beglanau wuh zhit! Din-tor manette!" perfectly fam dvun heh ralash-fam, heh ri kauk tevan-tor pla' svi' ish-veh ku-san, she hayal-tor ne' ish-veh el'ru, utterly insensible; k' ish-veh bezhun tu'ash heh teslau fi-tor ish-veh, heh k' ik kim-shah sagluvaya looking u' kuv ish-veh vesh' skrim-tor il branded vi' ish-veh fa-patam. Ni ikap-tor vesh' ish-veh meskaraya fi-tor ish-veh kar, ik au ptha tor dahl-tor himself lest au dang dash-tor ish-veh; therefore au puvutau si' loudly na' assistance rik' dvun-tor. Wuh kwai-looking kosu, ik kauk svi' ish-veh agitation, mr. Lorry glantau tor nam-tor ek' t' wuh yon-kur kur, heh ki' yon-kur isachya, heh sai-vel-tor svi' ein wehtsuri wufik-fitting fashion, heh ki' fi' ish-veh patam wuh danik wonderful bonnet spo' wuh grenadier wooden thon-tor, heh rom thon-tor nuh', il wuh lo'uk stilton thuhk, sarlah sahran vi' wuh tvi-shal svi' storilaya t' wuh ha-shal dvinsu, heh ak settled wuh deshker t' ish-veh detachment s' wuh ri donku-tor nu'ri t'sai, k' laying wuh brawny el'ru fi-tor ish-veh tuf, heh sending ish-veh hashan pla' tehnat wuh nearest temok. ("i really nah-tor nash bolau nam-tor wuh sasu!" vesh' mr. Lorry's breathless haulan, simultaneously k' ish-veh coming tehnat wuh temok.) "po, glazhau na' du ek'!" bawled nash khlop, addressing wuh ha-shal dvinsu. "po ri tor du hal-tor heh zaprah vel, instead t' standing tra' staring na' me? I am ri ni mau tor glazhau na', am i? Po ri tor du hal-tor heh zaprah vel? I'll kal-tor du fai-tor, kuv du ri tor katau smelling-alem, samu masu, heh sfith-masu, sahris, i dungi." tra' vesh' wuh iyi saganaya na' aifa restoratives, heh she softly laid wuh hasausu fi' wuh ku-san, heh palutunau ish-veh k' lo'uk renkup'es heh gentleness: calling ish-veh "t'nash-veh taluhk!" heh "t'nash-veh kushel!" heh spreading ish-veh pi-maat-kur isachya aside abru' ish-veh tipan k' lo'uk pride heh tun. "heh du svi' khav-kur!" she leralmin-tor, indignantly turning tor mr. Lorry; "couldn't du var-tor ish-veh ra du had tor var-tor ish-veh, rik' frightening ish-veh tor tevakh? Glazhau na' ish-veh, k' ish-veh takov spoh limuk heh ish-veh samu el'ru. Tor du vutau ik hasu wuh banker?" mr. Lorry vesh' ni exceedingly disconcerted k' wuh deshker ni lerash tor kilko-srashiv, ik au kupi goh glazhau fi', na' wuh ir, k' mau feebler sympathy heh humility, du' wuh karik kosu, having klee'fah'tu wuh ha-shal dvinsu ne' wuh mysterious penalty t' "letting au fai-tor" vel ri mentioned kuv au stayed tra', staring, recovered ish-veh falun k' wuh regular weizehl t' gradations, heh coaxed ish-veh tor ti ish-veh tevan-tor patam fi-tor ish-veh tipan. "i rok she dungi tor muhl i', " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry. "rai itaren tor du svi' khav-kur, kuv she tor. T'nash-veh ashal-veh takov!" "i rok, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, po' wuh'ashiv svizh t' kobat sympathy heh humility, "ik du sailau din-tor manette tor france?" "wuh kesik vel, nuh'!" kilko-tor wuh karik kosu. "kuv ish-veh vesh' ek'wak intended ik i dang hal-tor mes' alem masu, tor du suppose providence would ma vishizhau t'nash-veh lot svi' wuh vikuvtra?" nash hasu wuh'ashiv deshker lerash tor kilko-srashiv, mr. Jarvis lorry withdrew tor panah-tor ish-veh. Chapter v. Wuh wine-mahr-kel wuh suk cask t' wine had vesh' eku-tor heh pushau, svi' wuh yut. Wuh kisheya had pavesh-tor svi' getting ish-veh s' wuh hal; wuh cask had tumbled si' k' wuh sahr-tor, wuh hoops had thorau, heh ish-veh ti fi' wuh kov aishan s'udish wuh svep t' wuh wine-mahr-kel, zarahk-tor spo' wuh walnut-fo. Ek' wuh sutra k'svi pulau had suspended ish-veh business, il ish-veh idleness, tor sahr-tor tor wuh gla-tor heh mon wuh wine. Wuh rough, ripakhaik kov t' wuh yut, pointing kanok yut, heh designed, veh lau ma nahp, expressly tor lame ek' living creatures ik betau au, had dammed ish-veh vi' pi' patra; aifa vesh' vikuvau, tik k' its sha' jostling travek il patreitan, fupa s' its suk'es. Ein sasu kneeled ne', tor scoops t' ish-veh dahkuh el'ru hau, heh mon-tor, il ar'kada tor gol'nev kosu, vi keh'sei abru' ish-veh tipan, tor mon-tor, fa' wuh wine had ek' sahr-tor si' svi' ish-veh ozh. Vath, sasu heh kosu, spis-tor svi' wuh pi'muzh k' pi' mugs t' mutilated earthenware, il kauk k' handkerchiefs s' kosu's patam, if vesh' lerakhovau pseth vi' kan-bu' ru'lut; vath tor pi' vral-vulsolotra, tor kas-fek wuh wine u' ish-veh sahr-tor; vath, khartau k' lookers-fi' abru na' pid krani, darted la' heh tra', tor tresahk ska' pi' pilash t' wine ik palikau maf svi' uzh kharat; vath vaikau themselves tor wuh sodden heh lee-kur-tor krus t' wuh cask, licking, heh kauk champing wuh moister wine-nehau karf k' nayik relish. Tra' vesh' rai smashaya tor lesh ska' wuh wine, heh ri goh did ish-veh ek' prah taken abru, tonk'peh ni mau vral prah taken abru bi' k' ish-veh, ik tra' lau ma vesh' wuh tevanu-yokulsu svi' wuh yut, kuv anybody acquainted k' ish-veh kupi ma pudva-tor svi' such wuh miraculous la'es. Wuh shrill ralash t' laughter heh t' amused spes--spes t' sasu, kosu, heh kanu--resounded svi' wuh yut du' nash wine zhagra palesh-tor. Tra' vesh' pi' roughness svi' wuh torvukh, heh mau playfulness. Tra' vesh' wuh special besu'es svi' ish-veh, wuh observable inclination fi' wuh krus t' kanok veh tor hau ein vath veh, if pufulag-tor, wa' among wuh luckier il lighter-hearted, tor frolicsome nartau, drinking t' healths, shaking t' el'ru, heh kauk hau t' el'ru heh taman, wuh dozen teretuhr. Lu wuh wine vesh' hal-tor, heh wuh shitau wilat ish-veh had vesh' danik abundant vesh' dref-tor vi' wuh gridiron-nel-dath k' ozh, aifa demonstrations ceased, u' suddenly u' au had pushau si'. Wuh sasu vi had losrak ish-veh gla-tor sticking svi' wuh yon-lapan au vesh' tresahk-tor, eku ish-veh svi' dvunel va'ashiv; wuh kosu vi had losrak fi' wuh svep-ash wuh pi' sunil t' fal vitush, na' if she had vesh' trying tor soften wuh kusut svi' ish-veh sha' starved ozh heh gof, il svi' eifa t' ish-veh kan, fun-tor tor ish-veh; sasu k' sai-famik kar, matted klachek, heh cadaverous limuk, vi had sasarlah vi' wuh karil ta'hal s' cellars, dvun-tor maf, tor tev-tor va'ashiv; heh wuh gloom hoknau fi' wuh scene ik saudau weht malatik tor ish-veh do sunshine. Wuh wine vesh' yon-kur wine, heh had kurau wuh solektra t' wuh wonil yut svi' wuh suburb t' osu antoine, svi' paris, wilat ish-veh vesh' ne-tor. Ish-veh had kurau wehk el'ru, nuh', heh wehk limuk, heh wehk sai-fam ash'ya, heh wehk wooden ash'el. Wuh el'ru t' wuh sasu vi sawed wuh lapan, losrak yon-kur ulidar fi' wuh billets; heh wuh fa-patam t' wuh kosu vi nursed ish-veh kan-bu, vesh' kurau k' wuh kuraya t' wuh hinek a'cit she skek pa' ish-veh patam va'ashiv. Eifa vi had vesh' greedy k' wuh staves t' wuh cask, had acquired wuh tigerish smear pa' wuh ru'lut; heh veh ha-vol joker ni besmirched, ish-veh patam weht s' wuh wu squalid sa'haf t' wuh nightcap do svi' ish-veh, scrawled fi-tor wuh temok k' ish-veh ozh spis-tor svi' muddy wine-lees--khaf. Wuh wak vesh' tor sarlah, lu ik wine nuh' would nam-tor ne-tor fi' wuh yut-kov, heh lu wuh kuraya t' ish-veh would nam-tor yon-kur fi-tor wehk tra'. Heh i' ik wuh wan settled fi' osu antoine, if wuh momentary gleam had driven s' ish-veh sacred countenance, wuh mu'khlup'es t' ish-veh vesh' ras--samu, kitek, has-mar, ignorance, heh aitlun, vesh' wuh s'haile svi' waiting fi' wuh saintly la'es--thol t' lo'uk tepul ek' t' au; tonk'peh, danik wa' wuh kim-shah. Li-fal t' wuh sutra ik had undergone wuh terrible grinding heh regrinding svi' wuh mill, heh certainly ri svi' wuh fabulous mill if solektra hinek sutra nu'ri, shivered na' kanok teruk, be' dvun-tor svi' heh si' na' kanok svep-sharu, glazhau s' kanok krani, nuv-tor svi' kanok vestige t' wuh ain ik wuh salan hutau. Wuh mill if had ar'kada au ne', vesh' wuh mill ik grazhau nu'ri sutra hinek; wuh kanu had t'kahr limuk heh shi'vukhut spes; heh fi-tor au, heh fi-tor wuh grown limuk, heh ploughed vi' kanok furrow t' ya'shakhuv heh coming abru afresh, vesh' wuh spes-tevan, avon. Ish-veh vesh' prevalent kanok-wilat. Avon vesh' kwitau si' t' wuh ha-vol kelek, svi' wuh wretched sai-vel ik geldau fi-tor fek heh zehl; avon vesh' patched vi' au k' terp heh a'cit heh lapan heh dun; avon vesh' ashiv-tor svi' kanok karf t' wuh pi' modicum t' yon-lapan ik wuh sasu sawed ska'; avon nantau ne' s' wuh smokeless vuzh-mev, heh palikau abru s' wuh filthy yut ik had rai guhsh, among its klee'fah, t' sovek-vel tor yokul. Avon vesh' wuh inscription fi' wuh leipausu's nef, written svi' kanok pi' loaf t' ish-veh scanty fek t' rasahkos kap; na' wuh kahm-mahr-kel, svi' kanok tevik-dog preparation ik vesh' nufau na' sale. Avon rattled its pseth hinek among wuh roasting chestnuts svi' wuh da-tor cylinder; avon vesh' tresahk-tor vi' atomics svi' kanok farthing porringer t' husky val t' potato, pupol-tor k' ein reluctant eku-tor t' elmin. Its abiding shi vesh' svi' ek' vel fitted tor ish-veh. Wuh wonil kuvoran yut, bosh t' offence heh stench, k' vath wonil kuvoran yut diverging, ek' peopled k' a'cit heh nightcaps, heh ek' smelling t' a'cit heh nightcaps, heh ek' visible vel k' wuh brooding glazhau fi-tor au ik glazhau has-bosh. Svi' wuh shi'kar sov t' wuh sutra tra' vesh' wi ein kwai-beast nahp t' wuh possibility t' turning na' tchol. Depressed heh slinking hi au vesh', bezhun t' yon vesh' ri wanting ekhlami; il lerakhovau bru-lar, wan-kur k' ra au nelau; il fa-patam knitted vi' wuh likeness t' wuh geld-stau-nentu-man-elakh au mused pa' enduring, il inflicting. Wuh trade glat (heh au vesh' siyah u' wehk u' wuh mahr-kel) vesh', ek', grim illustrations t' aitlun. Wuh butcher heh wuh porkman kras-tor abru, goh wuh leanest scrags t' kahm; wuh leipausu, wuh coarsest t' meagre loaves. Wuh sutra rudely pictured u' drinking svi' wuh wine-mahr-kel, croaked abru' ish-veh scanty thon-tor t' wonil wine heh naliveh, heh vesh' gloweringly confidential teretuhr. Nothing vesh' represented svi' wuh flourishing nosh, korsau raul heh wun; tonk'peh, wuh cutler's lipau heh la'ash vesh' nasik heh ugelik, wuh zhuksu's mah-vel vesh' ras, heh wuh gunmaker's fek vesh' murderous. Wuh crippling kov t' wuh pavement, k' ish-veh wehk pi' reservoirs t' vral heh masu, had rai footways, tonk'peh shau ska' abruptly na' wuh svep. Wuh kennel, tor tor amends, sahr-tor ne' wuh svitan t' wuh yut--lu ish-veh sahr-tor na' ek': if vesh' goh po' ras sov-mashau, heh yi ish-veh sahr-tor, k' wehk rivitanik nunau, vi' wuh kelek. Mes' wuh yut, na' eik tvi-wak, veh om'toi ha'gelek vesh' slung k' wuh man-elakh heh pulley; na' mu-yor, lu wuh lamplighter had kal-tor aifa ne', heh lighted, heh abertau au va'ashiv, wuh kobat pi'laptra t' neik-ha'khlup wicks swung svi' wuh sickly manner overhead, u' kuv au vesh' na' masutra. Indeed au vesh' na' masutra, heh wuh hali heh hali-sutra vesh' svi' peril t' tempest. Na', wuh wak vesh' tor sarlah, lu wuh gaunt scarecrows t' ik shal dang ma glantau wuh lamplighter, svi' ish-veh idleness heh avon, ni wu, u' tor conceive wuh idea t' improving fi' ish-veh method, heh hauling abru sasu k' eifa man-elakh heh pulleys, tor flare fi-tor wuh mu'khlup'es t' ish-veh nosh. Tonk'peh, wuh wak vesh' ri sarlah wi; heh kanok salan ik blew abru' france hutau wuh a'cit t' wuh scarecrows svi' vain, na' wuh kushel, tok-ti t' song heh kan, nem-tor rai warning. Wuh wine-mahr-kel vesh' wuh teruk mahr-kel, weh-rom do danik vath svi' its appearance heh degree, heh wuh trensu t' wuh wine-mahr-kel had lam-tor s'udish ish-veh, svi' wuh kin-kur waistcoat heh yar-kur breeches, looking fi' na' wuh struggle na' wuh pakik wine. "ish-veh's ri t'nash-veh tek'ik, " leralmin-tor au, k' wuh kim-shah shrug t' wuh tipan. "wuh sutra s' wuh mahr-kel did ish-veh. Kal-tor au katau wuh'ashiv." tra', ish-veh bezhun aisha tor kum wuh ha-vol joker kitaun abru ish-veh kha'wal, au puvutau tor ish-veh mes' wuh yut: "leralmin, yi, t'nash-veh gaspard, ra tor du tor tra'?" wuh katravahsu sfekau tor ish-veh kha'wal k' immense significance, u' nam-tor k'ashiv wuh yut k' ish-veh tribe. Ish-veh din-tor its ulidar, heh completely vravshau, u' nam-tor k'ashiv wuh yut k' ish-veh tribe nuh'. "ra i'? Nam-tor du wuh subject na' wuh mad shi'has?" leralmin-tor wuh wine-mahr-kel keeper, mes wuh fau-yut, heh obliterating wuh jest k' wuh handful t' vral, abrashau na' wuh lof, heh smeared abru' ish-veh. "po tor du kitau svi' wuh tsuri yut? Nam-tor tra'--var-tor me thou--nam-tor tra' rai vath shi tor kitau such zhit svi'?" svi' ish-veh expostulation au eku-tor ish-veh cleaner el'ru (sos'eh accidentally, sos'eh ri) fi-tor wuh joker's khaf-spol. Wuh joker rapped ish-veh k' ish-veh sha', nem-tor wuh nimble sikar abru'le, heh sarlah ne' svi' wuh fantastic taman attitude, k' veh t' ish-veh kurau ash'el hutau ska' ish-veh ash'ya vi' ish-veh el'ru, heh meskarau si'. Wuh joker t' wuh extremely, ri tor leralmin wolfishly practical character, au glazhau, ne' eifa circumstances. "shitau ish-veh fi', shitau ish-veh fi', " leralmin-tor wuh vath. "vutau wine, wine; heh shaht tra'." k' ik na'shikh, au psethau ish-veh soiled el'ru fi-tor wuh joker's sai-vel, such u' ish-veh vesh'--ved deliberately, u' having dirtied wuh el'ru fi' ish-veh khrosahp; heh yi recrossed wuh fau-yut heh svi-tor wuh wine-mahr-kel. Nash wine-mahr-kel keeper vesh' wuh bull-necked, martial-looking sasu t' reh-leh, heh au dang ma vesh' t' wuh fal temperament, na', hi ish-veh vesh' wuh sfith(-) gad, au sai-vel-tor rai tor-pal, tonk'peh lesh veh slung abru' ish-veh tipan. Ish-veh sav'el-sleeves vesh' padukau abru, nuh', heh ish-veh khav-kur kar vesh' sai-famik tor wuh kar-nef. Neither did au sai-vel-tor sovek-vel weht fi' ish-veh patam do ish-veh sha' crisply-tcha-tor pen gu'gelik isachya. Au vesh' wuh gu'gelik sasu altogether, k' rom bezhun heh wuh rom vakh breadth svi' au. Rom-humoured looking fi' wuh bosh, tonk'peh implacable-looking, nuh'; evidently wuh sasu t' wuh karik resolution heh wuh eku lof; wuh sasu ri desirable tor nam-tor ragel-tor, rushing ne' wuh wonil be' dvun k' wuh suk'tchol fi' either vla, na' nothing would da-tor wuh sasu. Madame defarge, ish-veh ko-telsu, hayal-tor svi' wuh mahr-kel za' wuh tumek u' au sarlah svi'. Madame defarge vesh' wuh stout kosu t' pa' ish-veh sha' ya'shakhuv, k' wuh tun-tor bezhun ik seldom seemed tor glazhau na' sovek-vel, wuh suk el'ru heavily kus-tor, wuh br'xan limuk, karik features, heh lo'uk composure t' manner. Tra' vesh' wuh character pa' madame defarge, s' if veh lau ma predicated ik she did ri k'ashiv tor lafosh tehnat herself svi' sovek t' wuh reckonings abru' if she presided. Madame defarge hasu kash-zakar tor samu, vesh' wrapped svi' ausachya, heh had wuh nosahp t' ugelik shawl twined pa' ish-veh patam, hi ri tor wuh concealment t' ish-veh suk kaluk-mokov. Ish-veh knitting vesh' fa' ish-veh, tonk'peh she had laid ish-veh ne' tor pick ish-veh zud k' wuh toothpick. Thus engaged, k' ish-veh gas'rak kar-nef nenikau k' ish-veh losrak el'ru, madame defarge leralmin-tor nothing lu ish-veh s'haile sarlah svi', tonk'peh huhsh-tor aishan veh kap-yar t' huhsh. Nash, svi' terish k' wuh lifting t' ish-veh darkly mesprah bezhun-zehl abru' ish-veh toothpick k' wuh breadth t' wuh zehl, suggested tor ish-veh sa-telsu ik au would tor muhl tor glazhau pauk wuh mahr-kel among wuh klepovausu, na' sovek uzh klepovausu vi had eku-tor svi' du' au ash-tor abru' wuh yut. Wuh wine-mahr-kel keeper accordingly padukau ish-veh bezhun pa', abi' au shom-tor fi-tor wuh shakhupik gentleman heh wuh nu'ri t'sai, vi vesh' hayal-tor svi' wuh teruk. Vath apc'koik vesh' tra': dahkuh mavaun nop, dahkuh mavaun dominoes, rehkuh standing k' wuh tumek lengthening si' wuh pen tanilau t' wine. U' au be' dvun-tor za' wuh tumek, au nem-tor beglanau ik wuh shakhupik gentleman leralmin-tor svi' wuh glazhau tor wuh nu'ri t'sai, "nash nam-tor etwel sasu." "ra wuh e'shua tor du tor svi' ik af-tum tra'?" leralmin-tor monsieur defarge tor himself; "i ri tor fai-tor du." tonk'peh, au vup-tor ri tor beglanau wuh dahkuh ri-fainusu, heh tevan-tor vi' discourse k' wuh triumvirate t' klepovausu vi vesh' drinking na' wuh tumek. "uf hal-tor ish-veh, jacques?" leralmin-tor veh t' aifa rehkuh tor monsieur defarge. "nam-tor ek' wuh spilt wine vitem-tor?" "kanok eku, jacques, " kilko-tor monsieur defarge. Lu nash interchange t' christian ahm vesh' effected, madame defarge, picking ish-veh zud k' ish-veh toothpick, huhsh-tor wuh'ashiv kap-yar t' huhsh, heh ashenau ish-veh bezhun-zehl k' wuh breadth t' wuh'ashiv zehl. "ish-veh nam-tor ri k'ashiv, " leralmin-tor wuh dahr t' wuh rehkuh, addressing monsieur defarge, "ik wehk t' aifa miserable beasts fai-tor wuh zahvan t' wine, il t' sovek-vel tonk'peh nesh-kur kap heh tevakh. Nam-tor ish-veh ri ni, jacques?" "ish-veh nam-tor ni, jacques, " monsieur defarge fun-tor. Na' nash dahr interchange t' wuh christian ahm, madame defarge, fam dvun using ish-veh toothpick k' profound composure, huhsh-tor wuh'ashiv kap-yar t' huhsh, heh ashenau ish-veh bezhun-zehl k' wuh breadth t' wuh'ashiv zehl. Wuh kim-shah t' wuh rehkuh i' leralmin-tor ish-veh leralmin, u' au shitau ne' ish-veh herbosh drinking hali heh smacked ish-veh bru-lar. "ah! Ni mau wuh weh-rasahkos! Wuh sfith(-) zahvan ish-veh nam-tor ik such ri donku-tor cattle kwon-hau-ov ma svi' ish-veh ru'lut, heh lerash ha-tor au ha-tor, jacques. Am i gas'rak, jacques?" "du nam-tor gas'rak, jacques, " vesh' wuh kesaya t' monsieur defarge. Nash wuh interchange t' wuh christian ahm vesh' ovsoh na' wuh moment lu madame defarge shitau ish-veh toothpick k', potau ish-veh bezhun-zehl abru, heh slightly rustled svi' ish-veh ku-san. "meskaraya yi! Yeht!" muttered ish-veh sa-telsu. "gentlemen--t'nash-veh ko-telsu!" wuh rehkuh klepovausu seshau ska' ish-veh taik tor madame defarge, k' rehkuh flourishes. She nafai ish-veh homage k' bending ish-veh patam, heh giving au wuh sahris glazhau. Yi she glanced svi' wuh casual manner pauk wuh wine-mahr-kel, nem-tor abru ish-veh knitting k' lo'uk apparent calmness heh repose t' tam'a, heh became absorbed svi' ish-veh. "gentlemen, " leralmin-tor ish-veh sa-telsu, vi had potau ish-veh ugelik bezhun observantly fi-tor ish-veh, "rom gad. Wuh tvi-shal, furnished bachelor-fashion, ik du istau tor gla-tor, heh vesh' inquiring na' lu i ash-tor si', nam-tor fi' wuh fifth lan-tol. Wuh svep-sharu t' wuh staircase mazhiv-kur-tor fi' wuh pi' courtyard beyik wuh losrak la', " pointing k' ish-veh el'ru, "be' tor wuh krani t' t'nash-veh establishment. Tonk'peh, i' ik i vokau, veh t' du has already vesh' tra', heh mokuhlek gluvaya wuh yut. Gentlemen, adieu!" au vlitau na' ish-veh wine, heh losrak wuh shi. Wuh bezhun t' monsieur defarge vesh' studying ish-veh ko-telsu na' ish-veh knitting lu wuh shakhupik gentleman storilau s' ish-veh teruk, heh eit'jae wuh favour t' wuh zhit. "willingly, osu, " leralmin-tor monsieur defarge, heh quietly ash-tor k' ish-veh tor wuh svep. Ish-veh conference vesh' maut pen, tonk'peh maut klopau. Siyah na' wuh wuh'rak zhit, monsieur defarge palikau heh became deeply whio'naks. Ish-veh had ri palesh-tor wuh minute, lu au nodded heh went si'. Wuh gentleman yi beckoned tor wuh nu'ri t'sai, heh au, nuh', went si'. Madame defarge knitted k' nimble ozh heh br'xan bezhun-zehl, heh gla-tor nothing. Mr. Jarvis lorry heh din-tor manette, emerging s' wuh wine-mahr-kel thus, hau monsieur defarge svi' wuh svep-sharu tor if au had khartau ish-veh sha' apc'koik aishan fa'. Ish-veh tu'ash s' wuh stinking pi' nesh-kur courtyard, heh vesh' wuh paik tsuri entrance tor wuh lo'uk tuh t' kelek, inhabited k' wuh lo'uk su'etek t' sutra. Svi' wuh gloomy tile-elyutau svin tor wuh gloomy tile-elyutau staircase, monsieur defarge keh'sei ne' fi' veh mal-nef tor wuh kan t' ish-veh hinek trensu, heh shitau ish-veh el'ru tor ish-veh bru-lar. Ish-veh vesh' wuh gentle torai, tonk'peh mokov kogavik ovsoh; wuh maut remarkable mesuvulaya had sarlah abru' ish-veh svi' wuh zamu seconds. Au had rai rom-humour svi' ish-veh limuk, il sovek openness t' pulva losrak, tonk'peh had shetau wuh tsat, reshnek, tehvar-bosh sasu. "ish-veh nam-tor maut pid; ish-veh nam-tor wuh pi' rihagik. Weh-rom tor palikau slowly." thus, monsieur defarge, svi' wuh harr-krus spes, tor mr. Lorry, u' au began ascending wuh kaiden. "nam-tor au sa'awek?" wuh latter zhal-tor. "sa'awek! Oekon gol'nev ish-veh, vi dang nam-tor k' ish-veh!" leralmin-tor wuh vath, svi' wuh ka neik spes. "nam-tor au kwon-hau-ov sa'awek, yi?" "ha." "t' ish-veh sha' aitlun?" "t' ish-veh sha' bolayek. U' au vesh', lu i wuh'rak gla-tor ish-veh po' au afer-tor me heh halishau tor fai-tor kuv i would nem-tor ish-veh, heh, na' t'nash-veh peril nam-tor discreet--u' au vesh' yi, ni au nam-tor i'." "au nam-tor greatly rubai?" "rubai!" wuh keeper t' wuh wine-mahr-kel pehkau tor kwul wuh temok k' ish-veh el'ru, heh mutter wuh tremendous curse. Rai kharik kilko-srashiv kupi ma vesh' ulef ni nekwitau-yehat. Mr. Lorry's tam'a grew heavier heh heavier, u' au heh ish-veh dahkuh besu she-tor higher heh higher. Such wuh staircase, k' its accessories, svi' wuh older heh weht crowded krus t' paris, would nam-tor rasahkos hiyet i'; tonk'peh, na' ik wak, ish-veh vesh' vile indeed tor unaccustomed heh unhardened kash-ral. Kanok pi' habitation k'svi wuh lo'uk flalik ha-kel t' veh pid kelek--ik nam-tor tor leralmin, wuh tvi-shal il tvi-shal k'svi kanok svep ik tu'ash fi' wuh paik staircase--losrak its sha' tuh t' klee'fah fi' its sha' landing, isha flinging vath klee'fah s' its sha' krani. Wuh uncontrollable heh hopeless shivak t' ek'nehau ni engendered, would ma flau wuh sov, kauk kuv poverty heh deprivation had ri putush-tor ish-veh k' ish-veh intangible impurities; wuh dahkuh rasahkos shu-pal puterish-tor tor ish-veh siyah insupportable. K'fai such wuh igen-tukh, k' wuh menal gu'gelik shaft t' kitek heh gisam, wuh yut ti. Yielding tor ish-veh sha' ertaya t' kashek, heh tor ish-veh nu'ri besu's agitation, if became greater kanok instant, mr. Jarvis lorry dah'wak pehkau tor shom. Tik t' aifa stoppages vesh' tor na' wuh doleful grating, k' if sovek languishing rom airs ik vesh' losrak uncorrupted, seemed tor stron, heh ek' spoilt heh sickly muhs seemed tor ukrau svi'. K'fai wuh zhar-tor mofek, zahv-tor, rather do glimpses, vesh' kum-tor t' wuh jumbled neighbourhood; heh nothing k'svi eik'es, nearer il weh-neik do wuh dan-pid-sfek t' wuh dahkuh lo'uk kispek t' notre-dame, had sovek ugaya fi' ish-veh t' muhl-bosh ha'kiv il wholesome aspirations. Na' kim-shah, wuh fik t' wuh staircase vesh' nazh-tor, heh au pehkau na' wuh wuh wak. Tra' vesh' wi wuh upper staircase, t' wuh steeper inclination heh t' contracted retuka, tor nam-tor she-tor, fa' wuh kamu-tvi-shal var vesh' pulau. Wuh keeper t' wuh wine-mahr-kel, kwon-hau-ov going wuh pi' svi' storilaya, heh kwon-hau-ov going fi' wuh vla if mr. Lorry nem-tor, u' hi au dreaded tor nam-tor ya'akash sovek deshker k' wuh nu'ri t'sai, da-tor himself pa' la', heh, carefully olaya svi' wuh abru'lik t' wuh tor-pal au lesh abru' ish-veh tipan, nem-tor si' wuh tal-muv. "wuh svep nam-tor klacha yi, t'nash-veh t'hy'la?" leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, ak'wikmun. "ay. Ha, " vesh' wuh grim kilko t' monsieur defarge. "du nah-tor ish-veh bolayatik tor potau wuh unfortunate gentleman ni retired?" "i nah-tor ish-veh bolayatik tor da-tor wuh tal-muv." monsieur defarge zhal-tor ish-veh closer svi' ish-veh kaluk, heh kwal-tor heavily. "po?" "po! Fai'ei au has ha-tor ni wu, klacha abru, ik au would nam-tor koltha--rave--bezhun-masu himself tor krus--tev-tor--sarlah tor i fai-tor ri ra klau--kuv ish-veh svep vesh' losrak tu'ash." "nam-tor ish-veh tor-yehat!" sporiben mr. Lorry. "nam-tor ish-veh tor-yehat!" ashiv-tor defarge, bitterly. "ha. Heh wuh vaksurik panu etek ha-tor svi', lu ish-veh nam-tor tor-yehat, heh lu wehk vath such vel nam-tor tor-yehat, heh ri goh tor-yehat, tonk'peh ovsoh--ovsoh, gla-tor du!--ne' ik igen tra', kanok gad. Wu ha-tor wuh e'shua. Kal-tor etek hal-tor fi'." nash dialogue had vesh' meskarau svi' ni maut neik wuh zhal, ik ri wuh zhit t' ish-veh had pulau wuh nu'ri t'sai's kaluk. Tonk'peh, k' nash wak she trembled ne' such karik zherka, heh ish-veh limuk sagluvau such glu anxiety, heh, abru' ek', such dread heh vash, ik mr. Lorry olau ish-veh incumbent fi' ish-veh tor stariben wuh zhit il dahkuh t' reassurance. "courage, tal-kam din-tor! Courage! Business! Wuh rasahkos dungi nam-tor abru' svi' wuh moment; ish-veh nam-tor tonk'peh be' dvun-tor wuh tvi-shal-svep, heh wuh rasahkos nam-tor abru'. Yi, ek' wuh rom du katau tor ish-veh, ek' wuh vas, ek' wuh happiness du katau tor ish-veh, palikau. Kal-tor etwel rom t'hy'la la', gol-tor du fi' ik vla. Ik's muhl, t'hy'la defarge. Sarlah, i'. Business, business!" au went abru slowly heh softly. Wuh staircase vesh' pen, heh au vesh' ak na' wuh fik. Tra', u' ish-veh had wuh abrupt da-tor svi' ish-veh, sarlah au ek' na' wuh'wak svi' glan t' rehkuh sasu, t'vi patam vesh' keh'sei ne' ikap-tor teretuhr na' wuh vla t' wuh svep, heh vi vesh' intently looking vi' wuh tvi-shal tor if wuh svep belonged, k'fai ein chinks il razh svi' wuh temok. Fi' khaf-spol footsteps ikap-tor na' el'ru, aifa rehkuh da-tor, heh she-tor, heh gluvau themselves tor nam-tor wuh rehkuh t' veh ahm vi had vesh' drinking svi' wuh wine-mahr-kel. "i forgot au svi' wuh ak'wikmun t' ish-veh yaret, " danau monsieur defarge. "trasha etek, rom sa-kan; etek ma business la'." wuh rehkuh glided k', heh went silently ne'. Tra' appearing tor nam-tor rai vath svep fi' ik lan-tol, heh wuh keeper t' wuh wine-mahr-kel going zehik tor nash-veh lu au vesh' losrak sa'awek, mr. Lorry ya'akash ish-veh svi' wuh zhal, k' wuh pi' reshan: "tor du tor wuh gluvaya t' monsieur manette?" "i gluvaya ish-veh, svi' wuh yut du ma gla-tor, tor wuh pudvel-tor zamu." "nam-tor ik muhl?" "i nah-tor ish-veh nam-tor muhl." "vi nam-tor wuh zamu? Uf tor du dvel-tor au?" "i dvel-tor au u' yeht sasu, t' t'nash-veh ahm--jacques nam-tor t'nash-veh ahm--tor ik wuh glan nam-tor kesik tor tor rom. Hiyet; du nam-tor eingelsu; ik nam-tor wuh'ashiv vel. Stay tra', kuv du sanoi, wuh pi' moment." k' wuh admonitory gesture tor potau au pla', au stooped, heh glazhau svi' k'fai wuh treshaya svi' wuh temok. Ak raising ish-veh patam va'ashiv, au kwul-tor dah'wak il thrice fi-tor wuh svep--evidently k' rai vath vel do tor tor wuh ralash tra'. K' wuh ka intention, au drew wuh tal-muv mes' ish-veh, rehkuh il kehkuh wak, fa' au shitau ish-veh clumsily vi' wuh klachek, heh da-tor ish-veh u' heavily u' au kupi. Wuh svep slowly tu'ash inward ne' ish-veh el'ru, heh au glazhau vi' wuh tvi-shal heh leralmin-tor vel. Wuh faint spes kilko-tor vel. Pi' weht do wuh single zhit-shaya kupi ma vesh' spoken fi' either vla. Au glazhau pla' abru' ish-veh tipan, heh beckoned au tor svi-tor. Mr. Lorry prah ish-veh kar securely pauk wuh ko-fu's san, heh meskarau ish-veh; na' au olau ik she vesh' sinking. "wuh-wuh-wuh-business, business!" au urged, k' wuh masu'es ik vesh' ri t' business shining fi' ish-veh nak. "sarlah svi', sarlah svi'!" "i am kwes t' ish-veh, " she kilko-tor, shuddering. "t' ish-veh? Ra?" "i tvai t' ish-veh. T' t'nash-veh sa-mekh." rendered svi' wuh manner desperate, k' ish-veh fupa s' heh k' wuh beckoning t' ish-veh spayek, au drew abru' ish-veh talu wuh kar ik hutau fi-tor ish-veh tipan, abertau ish-veh wuh pi', heh hurried ish-veh vi' wuh tvi-shal. Au hayal-tor ish-veh ne' aishan k'svi wuh svep, heh meskarau ish-veh, clinging tor ish-veh. Defarge drew si' wuh tal-muv, a'ing wuh svep, klacha ish-veh fi' wuh svi'udish, nem-tor si' wuh tal-muv va'ashiv, heh meskarau ish-veh svi' ish-veh el'ru. Ek' nash au did, methodically, heh k' u' ral heh harsh wuh accompaniment t' ralash u' au kupi tor. T'forti, au lates-tor mes' wuh tvi-shal k' wuh thon-tor tread tor wilat wuh krani vesh'. Au pehkau tra', heh limuk-tor pauk. Wuh kamu-tvi-shal, torvau tor nam-tor wuh depository na' yon-lapan heh wuh spo', vesh' neik-ha'khlup heh gu'gelik: na', wuh krani t' dormer shid, vesh' svi' yeht'es wuh svep svi' wuh kamu, k' wuh pi' aberayek abru' ish-veh na' wuh abertau abru t' mahr-kel s' wuh yut: unglazed, heh ikapik abru wuh svitan svi' dahkuh krus, spo' sovek vath svep t' french torvaya. Tor sanan-tor wuh samu, veh ulef t' nash svep vesh' sahris a'ing, heh wuh vath vesh' tu'ash tonk'peh wuh maut pi' yut.
