Such wuh scanty portion t' ta'hal vesh' nafai-tor k'fai aifa tvai, ik ish-veh vesh' rihagik, fi' wuh'rak coming svi', tor gla-tor sovek-vel; heh wu es'merka sa'awek kupi ma slowly shidau svi' sovek veh, wuh kup'es tor tor sovek ar'kadan requiring nicety svi' such obscurity. Wi, ar'kadan t' ik ves vesh' hasu ovsoh svi' wuh kamu-tvi-shal; na', k' ish-veh pla' na' wuh svep, heh ish-veh limuk na' wuh krani wilat wuh keeper t' wuh wine-mahr-kel lam-tor looking na' ish-veh, wuh wan-kur-haired sasu hayal-tor fi' wuh neik wu-ku-san, stooping fa'rak heh maut toranik, tor ash'el. Chapter vi. Wuh shoemaker "rom gad!" leralmin-tor monsieur defarge, looking ne' na' wuh wan-kur patam ik keh'sei neik abru' wuh shoemaking. Ish-veh vesh' ashenau na' wuh moment, heh wuh maut faint spes kesau tor wuh salutation, u' kuv ish-veh vesh' na' wuh ir: "rom gad!" "du nam-tor fam dvun lerash na' ar'kadan, gla-tor nash-veh?" po' wuh wu silence, wuh patam vesh' abertau na' wuh'ashiv moment, heh wuh spes kilko-tor, "ha--i am working." nash wak, wuh shif t' haggard bezhun had glazhau na' wuh questioner, fa' wuh limuk had eku-tor va'ashiv. Wuh faintness t' wuh spes vesh' pitiable heh dreadful. Ish-veh vesh' ri wuh faintness t' tukhik kobat'es, hi confinement heh lerash panavau rai vet had ish-veh krus svi' ish-veh. Its deplorable peculiarity vesh', ik ish-veh vesh' wuh faintness t' awek'es heh disuse. Ish-veh vesh' spo' wuh kim-shah kobat vava t' wuh ralash tor wu heh wu ago. Ni entirely had ish-veh pakik wuh ha'kiv heh kusilaya t' wuh komihn spes, ik ish-veh dau wuh kash-ral spo' wuh wuh'wak vaksurik kur spoh-tor maf vi' wuh ri donku-tor kobat kuraya. Ni sunken heh nelau ish-veh vesh', ik ish-veh vesh' spo' wuh spes underground. Ni expressive ish-veh vesh', t' wuh hopeless heh pakik creature, ik wuh famished traveller, wearied si' k' lonely wandering svi' wuh shi'kwai, would ma vokau ha-kel heh t'hylara svi' such wuh molu fa' lying ne' tor tev-tor. Ein minutes t' ralash-fam ar'kadan had be' dvun-tor: heh wuh haggard bezhun had glazhau abru va'ashiv: ri k' sovek eku'ko il curiosity, tonk'peh k' wuh pasik mechanical pakashogaya, beforehand, ik wuh gla-tor wilat wuh goh visitor au vesh' aware t' had lam-tor, vesh' ri wi herbosh. "i aitlun, " leralmin-tor defarge, vi had ri snem-tor ish-veh gaze s' wuh shoemaker, "tor kal-tor svi' wuh pi' weht ta'hal la'. Du mokuhlek lesh wuh pi' weht?" wuh shoemaker pehkau ish-veh ar'kadan; glazhau k' wuh vacant sov t' listening, na' wuh lan-tol fi' veh vla t' ish-veh; yi similarly, na' wuh lan-tol fi' wuh vath vla t' ish-veh; yi, abru'le na' wuh saralashek. "ra did du leralmin?" "du mokuhlek lesh wuh pi' weht ta'hal?" "i bolau lesh ish-veh, kuv du kal-tor ish-veh svi'." (laying wuh palest duv t' wuh hishel fi-tor wuh dahr zhit.) wuh tu'ash ulef-svep vesh' tu'ash wuh pi' further, heh shar-tor na' ik vulu na' wuh wak. Wuh sax'ksei ha'zehl t' ta'hal tevan-tor vi' wuh kamu-tvi-shal, heh gluvau wuh workman k' wuh unfinished ash'el fi-tor ish-veh lap, pausing svi' ish-veh zup. Ish-veh zamu tsuri raul heh vuhnauk moguhsh t' duf vesh' na' ish-veh ash'ya heh fi' ish-veh wu-ku-san. Au had wuh wan-kur hisahk, raggedly tresahk, tonk'peh ri maut wu, wuh hollow limuk, heh exceedingly ugelik bezhun. Wuh hollowness heh thinness t' ish-veh limuk would ma aisha au tor glazhau suk, ne' ish-veh wi gu'gelik bezhun-zehl heh ish-veh confused wan-kur isachya, hi au had vesh' really vathru; tonk'peh, au vesh' naturally suk, heh glazhau unnaturally ni. Ish-veh kin-kur a'cit t' sav'el ti tu'ash na' wuh drahk, heh gluvau ish-veh ak'shem tor nam-tor withered heh worn. Au, heh ish-veh hinek canvas pelal, heh ish-veh thal stockings, heh ek' ish-veh ri donku-tor tatters t' sai-vel, had, svi' wuh wu seclusion s' kharik ta'hal heh sov, spoh-tor ne' tor such wuh pasik uniformity t' parchment-kin-kur, ik ish-veh would ma vesh' lerash tor leralmin if vesh' if. Au had shitau abru wuh el'ru svi' ish-veh bezhun heh wuh ta'hal, heh wuh maut hinek t' ish-veh seemed fnaglaik. Ni au hayal-tor, k' wuh steadfastly vacant gaze, pausing svi' ish-veh ar'kadan. Au worla glazhau na' wuh khlop fa' ish-veh, rik' wuh'rak looking ne' fi' nash vla t' himself, yi fi' ik, u' kuv au had pakik wuh es'merka t' associating shi k' ralash; au worla stariben, rik' wuh'rak wandering svi' nash manner, heh forgetting tor stariben. "nam-tor du going tor shaht ik shif t' ash'el tor-gad?" ya'akash defarge, motioning tor mr. Lorry tor sarlah fa'rak. "ra did du leralmin?" "tor du tvai tor shaht ik shif t' ash'el tor-gad?" "i mokuhlek't leralmin ik i tvai tor. I suppose ni. I ri tor fai-tor." tonk'peh, wuh deshker reminded ish-veh t' ish-veh ar'kadan, heh au keh'sei abru' ish-veh va'ashiv. Mr. Lorry sarlah silently fa'rak, leaving wuh ko-fu k' wuh svep. Lu au had lam-tor, na' wuh minute il dahkuh, k' wuh vla t' defarge, wuh shoemaker glazhau abru. Au gluvau rai ak'wikmun na' seeing wuh'ashiv khlop, tonk'peh wuh unsteady ozh t' veh t' ish-veh el'ru fam-kelek-tor tor ish-veh bru-lar u' au glazhau na' ish-veh (ish-veh bru-lar heh ish-veh felu vesh' t' wuh ka spoh ras-tukh-kur), heh yi wuh el'ru eku-tor tor ish-veh ar'kadan, heh au wuh'wak weht keh'sei abru' wuh ash'el. Wuh glazhau heh wuh torai had occupied tonk'peh wuh instant. "du ma wuh visitor, gla-tor du, " leralmin-tor monsieur defarge. "ra did du leralmin?" "la' nam-tor wuh visitor." wuh shoemaker glazhau abru u' fa', tonk'peh rik' removing wuh el'ru s' ish-veh ar'kadan. "sarlah!" leralmin-tor defarge. "la' nam-tor monsieur, vi fai-tor wuh muhl-tor ash'el lu gla-tor ish-veh veh. Gluvaya ish-veh ik ash'el du nam-tor working na'. Nem-tor ish-veh, monsieur." mr. Lorry nem-tor ish-veh svi' ish-veh el'ru. "var-tor monsieur ra ves t' ash'el ish-veh nam-tor, heh wuh maker's ahm." tra' vesh' wuh longer svizh do tsuri, fa' wuh shoemaker kilko-tor: "i yen-tor ra ish-veh vesh' du ya'akash me. Ra did du leralmin?" "i leralmin-tor, couldn't du kethelvau wuh ves t' ash'el, na' monsieur's ro'fori?" "ish-veh nam-tor wuh t'sai's ash'el. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh nu'ri t'sai's walking-ash'el. Ish-veh nam-tor svi' wuh la' nuk. I worla gla-tor wuh nuk. I ma had wuh nel-dath svi' t'nash-veh el'ru." au glanced na' wuh ash'el k' ein pi' be' dvun-tor esta t' pride. "heh wuh maker's ahm?" leralmin-tor defarge. I' ik au had rai ar'kadan tor meskaraya, au laid wuh ozh-lesek t' wuh gas'rak el'ru svi' wuh hollow t' wuh losrak, heh yi wuh ozh-lesek t' wuh losrak el'ru svi' wuh hollow t' wuh gas'rak, heh yi be' dvun-tor wuh el'ru mes' ish-veh bearded chin, heh ni fi' svi' regular rubai, rik' wuh moment's intermission. Wuh task t' recalling ish-veh s' wuh vagrancy vi' if au kwon-hau-ov sank lu au had spoken, vesh' spo' recalling ein maut kobat person s' wuh swoon, il endeavouring, svi' wuh rok t' ein disclosure, tor stay wuh tam'a t' wuh sahris-dying sasu. "did du ya'akash me na' t'nash-veh ahm?" "assuredly i did." "teh heh kaukuh, desh'rak kispek." "nam-tor ik ek'?" "teh heh kaukuh, desh'rak kispek." k' wuh weary ralash ik vesh' ri wuh spes-tevan, il wuh groan, au keh'sei tor ar'kadan va'ashiv, abi' wuh silence vesh' va'ashiv pushau. "du nam-tor ri wuh shoemaker k' trade?" leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, looking steadfastly na' ish-veh. Ish-veh haggard bezhun da-tor tor defarge u' kuv au would ma transferred wuh deshker tor ish-veh: tonk'peh u' rai gol'nev sarlah s' ik yonuk, au da-tor pla' fi' wuh questioner lu au had sought wuh solektra. "i am ri wuh shoemaker k' trade? Rai, i vesh' ri wuh shoemaker k' trade. I-i oren-tor ish-veh la'. I saven-tor myself. I ya'akash trasha tor--" au lapsed maf, kauk na' minutes, ringing eifa thon-tor rubai fi' ish-veh el'ru wuh bosh wak. Ish-veh bezhun sarlah slowly pla', na' kim-shah, tor wuh limuk s' if au had czar-tor; lu au shom-tor fi' ish-veh, au palikau, heh resumed, svi' wuh manner t' wuh sleeper ik moment kum'i, reverting tor wuh subject t' kim-shah mu-yor. "i ya'akash trasha tor saven-tor myself, heh i prah ish-veh k' mau rihag'es po' wuh wu du', heh i ma tor ash'el ek'wak opi'." u' au meskarau si' ish-veh el'ru na' wuh ash'el ik had vesh' taken s' ish-veh, mr. Lorry leralmin-tor, fam dvun looking steadfastly svi' ish-veh limuk: "monsieur manette, tor du vokau nothing t' me?" wuh ash'el eku-tor tor wuh solektra, heh au hayal-tor looking fixedly na' wuh questioner. "monsieur manette"; mr. Lorry laid ish-veh el'ru fi-tor defarge's kar; "tor du vokau nothing t' nash sasu? Glazhau na' ish-veh. Glazhau na' me. Nam-tor tra' rai hinek banker, rai hinek business, rai hinek dvinsu, rai hinek wak, rising svi' ish-veh kashek, monsieur manette?" u' wuh captive t' wehk tevun hayal-tor looking fixedly, k' da-tor, na' mr. Lorry heh na' defarge, ein wu obliterated ulidar t' wuh actively intent kash-tor'es svi' wuh svitan t' wuh fa-patam, gradually punekwitau themselves k'fai wuh nesh-kur mist ik had tevan-tor fi' ish-veh. Au vesh' overclouded va'ashiv, au vesh' fainter, au vesh' hal-tor; tonk'peh au had vesh' tra'. Heh ni exactly vesh' wuh sagluvaya ashiv-tor fi' wuh rom nu'ri limuk t' ish-veh vi had crept bi' wuh temok tor wuh sfek wilat she kupi gla-tor ish-veh, heh wilat she i' lam-tor looking na' ish-veh, k' el'ru if palikauk had vesh' goh ashenau svi' koltha utan'es, kuv ri kauk tor potau ish-veh ska' heh ikap-tor si' wuh glan t' ish-veh, tonk'peh if vesh' i' extending na' ish-veh, trembling k' eagerness tor ti wuh spectral limuk fi-tor ish-veh lamekh nu'ri thasek, heh ashaya ish-veh pla' tor ha'kiv heh rok--ni exactly vesh' wuh sagluvaya ashiv-tor (hi svi' stronger characters) fi' ish-veh rom nu'ri limuk, ik ish-veh glazhau u' hi ish-veh had be' dvun-tor spo' wuh dvun-tor ta'hal, s' ish-veh tor ish-veh. Mu'khlup'es had tevan-tor fi' ish-veh svi' its shi. Au glazhau na' wuh dahkuh, lehkuh heh lehkuh attentively, heh ish-veh bezhun svi' gloomy abstraction sought wuh solektra heh glazhau pa' ish-veh svi' wuh hinek yut. T'forti, k' wuh glu wu spes-tevan, au nem-tor wuh ash'el abru, heh resumed ish-veh ar'kadan. "ma du naglanshau ish-veh, monsieur?" ya'akash defarge svi' wuh zhal. "ha; na' wuh moment. Palikauk i nahp ish-veh ved hopeless, tonk'peh i ma unquestionably gla-tor, na' wuh single moment, wuh limuk ik i wuh'wak fai-tor ni muhl. Hush! Kal-tor etek bes-tor further pla'. Hush!" she had dvun-tor s' wuh temok t' wuh kamu-tvi-shal, maut be' tor wuh wu-ku-san fi' if au hayal-tor. Tra' vesh' vel awful svi' ish-veh unconsciousness t' wuh khlop ik kupi ma shitau si' its el'ru heh estuhl ish-veh u' au stooped abru' ish-veh zup. Ri wuh zhit vesh' spoken, ri wuh ralash vesh' tor. She lam-tor, spo' wuh tam'a, be' ish-veh, heh au keh'sei abru' ish-veh ar'kadan. Ish-veh pavesh-tor, na' wu-vath, ik au had occasion tor rubah wuh instrument svi' ish-veh el'ru, na' ish-veh shoemaker's lipau. Ish-veh ti fi' ik vla t' ish-veh if vesh' ri wuh vla fi' if she lam-tor. Au had taken ish-veh abru, heh vesh' stooping tor ar'kadan va'ashiv, lu ish-veh bezhun kum-tor wuh skirt t' ish-veh sai-vel. Au ashenau au, heh gla-tor ish-veh limuk. Wuh dahkuh spectators palikau fa'rak, tonk'peh she stayed au k' wuh dvunel t' ish-veh el'ru. She had rai pthak t' ish-veh striking na' ish-veh k' wuh lipau, hi au had. Au nantau na' ish-veh k' wuh pthak-bosh glazhau, heh po' wuh du' ish-veh bru-lar began tor shid ein zhit, hi rai ralash proceeded s' au. K' degrees, svi' wuh svizh-tor t' ish-veh sahris heh zup-tor eshan, au vesh' puzhu-tor tor leralmin: "ra nam-tor nash?" k' wuh bezhun-masu streaming ne' ish-veh limuk, she shitau ish-veh dahkuh el'ru tor ish-veh bru-lar, heh shok-tor au tor ish-veh; yi clasped au fi' ish-veh thasek, u' kuv she laid ish-veh ruined patam tra'. "du nam-tor ri wuh gaoler's ko-fu?" she spes-tevan "rai." "vi nam-tor du?" ri wi trusting wuh molu t' ish-veh spes, she hayal-tor ne' fi' wuh wu-ku-san be' ish-veh. Au recoiled, tonk'peh she laid ish-veh el'ru fi-tor ish-veh kar. Wuh flekh thrill kwul-tor ish-veh lu she did ni, heh visibly be' dvun-tor abru' ish-veh nentu; au laid wuh lipau ne' softly, u' au hayal-tor staring na' ish-veh. Ish-veh pi-maat-kur isachya, if she sai-vel-tor svi' wu tcha-tor, had vesh' hurriedly kwitau aside, heh tevan-tor ne' abru' ish-veh talu. Advancing ish-veh el'ru k' pi' heh pi', au nem-tor ish-veh abru heh glazhau na' ish-veh. Svi' wuh midst t' wuh torai au went astray, heh, k' wuh'ashiv glu spes-tevan, tevan-tor tor ar'kadan na' ish-veh shoemaking. Tonk'peh ri na' wu. Releasing ish-veh kar, she laid ish-veh el'ru fi-tor ish-veh tipan. Po' looking doubtfully na' ish-veh, dahkuh il rehkuh wak, u' kuv tor nam-tor sure ik ish-veh vesh' really tra', au laid ne' ish-veh ar'kadan, shitau ish-veh el'ru tor ish-veh talu, heh nem-tor ska' wuh blackened string k' wuh moguhsh t' hesha a'cit attached tor ish-veh. Au tu'ash nash, carefully, fi' ish-veh mal-nef, heh ish-veh tuhlau wuh maut pi' nosahp t' isachya: ri weht do veh il dahkuh wu pi-maat-kur isachya, if au had, svi' ein hinek gad, skek ska' fi-tor ish-veh ozh. Au nem-tor ish-veh isachya vi' ish-veh el'ru va'ashiv, heh glazhau closely na' ish-veh. "ish-veh nam-tor wuh ka. Uf mokuhlek ish-veh nam-tor! Lu vesh' ish-veh! Uf vesh' ish-veh!" u' wuh concentrated sagluvaya fun-tor tor ish-veh fa-patam, au seemed tor shetau d'wonil ik ish-veh vesh' svi' ish-veh nuh'. Au da-tor ish-veh bosh tor wuh ta'hal, heh glazhau na' ish-veh. "she had laid ish-veh patam fi-tor t'nash-veh tipan, ik mu-yor lu i vesh' summoned si'--she had wuh pthak t' t'nash-veh going, hi i had rim--heh lu i vesh' katau tor wuh desh'rak kispek au afer-tor aifa fi-tor t'nash-veh sleeve. 'du dungi trasha me au? Au mokuhlek worla gol'nev me tor stron svi' wuh ak'shem, hi au lau svi' wuh tam'a.' eifa vesh' wuh zhit i leralmin-tor. I vokau au maut muhl." au shidau nash starun k' ish-veh bru-lar wehk wak fa' au kupi utter ish-veh. Tonk'peh lu au did talal spoken zhit na' ish-veh, sarlah au tor ish-veh coherently, hi slowly. "uf vesh' nash?--vesh' ish-veh du?" wuh'wak weht, wuh dahkuh spectators palikau, u' au da-tor fi-tor ish-veh k' wuh frightful suddenness. Tonk'peh she hayal-tor perfectly fam dvun svi' ish-veh ruskaraya, heh goh leralmin-tor, svi' wuh neik spes, "i entreat du, rom gentlemen, ri tor sarlah be' etek, ri tor stariben, ri tor dvun!" "hark!" au sporiben. "t'vi spes vesh' ik?" ish-veh el'ru sadalau ish-veh u' au uttered nash maf, heh went abru tor ish-veh wan-kur isachya, if au tore svi' wuh frenzy. Ish-veh tev-tor si', u' kanok-vei tonk'peh ish-veh shoemaking did tev-tor s' ish-veh, heh au refolded ish-veh pi' packet heh ar'kada tor shar ish-veh svi' ish-veh thasek; tonk'peh au fam dvun glazhau na' ish-veh, heh gloomily hutau ish-veh patam. "rai, rai, rai; du nam-tor nuh' nu'ri, nuh' svai-tu-ashya. Ish-veh mokuhlek't nam-tor. Gla-tor ra wuh prisoner nam-tor. Aifa nam-tor ri wuh el'ru she fai-tor, nash nam-tor ri wuh limuk she fai-tor, nash nam-tor ri wuh spes she ek'wak puzhu-tor. Rai, rai. She vesh'--heh au vesh'--fa' wuh vohris tevun t' wuh desh'rak kispek--ya'shakhuv ago. Ra nam-tor ish-veh ahm, t'nash-veh gentle ha'su?" hailing ish-veh softened molu heh manner, ish-veh ko-fu tevan-tor fi-tor ish-veh mal-nef fa' ish-veh, k' ish-veh appealing el'ru fi-tor ish-veh thasek. "o, osu, na' wuh'ashiv wak du dungau fai-tor t'nash-veh ahm, heh vi t'nash-veh ko-mekh vesh', heh vi t'nash-veh sa-mekh, heh uf i worla fai-tor ish-veh lerash, lerash vesht-var. Tonk'peh i fam yehat var-tor du na' nash wak, heh i fam yehat var-tor du la'. Ek' ik i lau var-tor du, la' heh i', nam-tor, ik i pray tor du tor esta me heh tor kudau me. Shok me, shok me! O t'nash-veh tal-kam, t'nash-veh tal-kam!" ish-veh samu wan-kur patam mingled k' ish-veh radiant isachya, if warmed heh lighted ish-veh u' hi ish-veh vesh' wuh ta'hal t' el'es shining fi' ish-veh. "kuv du zhu-tor svi' t'nash-veh spes--i ri tor fai-tor ik ish-veh nam-tor ni, tonk'peh i rok ish-veh nam-tor--kuv du zhu-tor svi' t'nash-veh spes sovek resemblance tor wuh spes ik wuh'wak vesh' slor ralash-tanaf svi' ish-veh kaluk, tusa na' ish-veh, tusa na' ish-veh! Kuv du esta, svi' touching t'nash-veh isachya, sovek-vel ik recalls wuh k'diwa patam ik ti fi' ish-veh thasek lu du vesh' nu'ri heh elik, tusa na' ish-veh, tusa na' ish-veh! Kuv, lu i hint tor du t' wuh ha-kel ik nam-tor fa' etek, wilat i dungi nam-tor yeht tor du k' ek' t'nash-veh gu-vam heh k' ek' t'nash-veh faithful dvin, i katau pla' wuh remembrance t' wuh ha-kel wu desolate, du' ish-veh ri donku-tor khaf-spol pined maf, tusa na' ish-veh, tusa na' ish-veh!" she meskarau ish-veh closer pauk wuh talu, heh rocked ish-veh fi' ish-veh thasek spo' wuh kan. "kuv, lu i var-tor du, dearest tal-kam, ik ish-veh agony nam-tor abru', heh ik i ma sarlah la' tor nem-tor du s' ish-veh, heh ik etek hal-tor tor england tor nam-tor na' sochya heh na' shom, i aishan du tor nah-tor t' ish-veh useful ha'kiv laid thinoi, heh t' etwel salatik france ni wicked tor du, tusa na' ish-veh, tusa na' ish-veh! Heh kuv, lu i dungau var-tor du t' t'nash-veh ahm, heh t' t'nash-veh sa-mekh vi nam-tor living, heh t' t'nash-veh ko-mekh vi nam-tor tevik, du oren-tor ik i ma tor kneel tor t'nash-veh pudor-tor sa-mekh, heh implore ish-veh pardon na' having worla na' ish-veh sake striven ek' gad heh lain kum'i heh wept ek' mu-yor, fai'ei wuh ashaya t' t'nash-veh ri donku-tor ko-mekh ip-sut ish-veh torture s' me, tusa na' ish-veh, tusa na' ish-veh! Tusa na' ish-veh, yi, heh na' me! Rom gentlemen, itaren oekon! I olau ish-veh sacred bezhun-masu fi-tor t'nash-veh limuk, heh ish-veh sobs kwul tehnat t'nash-veh khaf-spol. O, gla-tor! Itaren oekon na' etek, itaren oekon!" au had ne'hal-tor svi' ish-veh kar, heh ish-veh limuk eku-tor fi' ish-veh thasek: wuh glan ni touching, wi ni terrible svi' wuh tremendous riyeht heh suffering if had hal-tor fa' ish-veh, ik wuh dahkuh beholders wein-tor ish-veh limuk. Lu wuh hizhuk t' wuh kamu-tvi-shal had vesh' wu undisturbed, heh ish-veh heaving thasek heh shaken shid had wu yielded tor wuh hayal ik bolau zahal-tor ek' sahriv--emblem tor humanity, t' wuh shom heh silence vi' if wuh sahriv puvutau ha'kiv bolau hush na' kim-shah--sarlah au fa'rak tor ashenau wuh sa-mekh heh ko-fu s' wuh solektra. Au had gradually eku-tor tor wuh lan-tol, heh ti tra' svi' wuh lethargy, worn si'. She had nestled ne' k' ish-veh, ik ish-veh patam lau ti fi-tor ish-veh kar; heh ish-veh isachya tevan-tor abru' ish-veh curtained ish-veh s' wuh ta'hal. "kuv, rik' disturbing ish-veh, " she leralmin-tor, raising ish-veh el'ru tor mr. Lorry u' au stooped abru' au, po' ashiv-tor blowings t' ish-veh han, "ek' kupi nam-tor arranged na' etwel leaving paris na' wuh'wak, ni ik, s' wuh maut svep, au kupi nam-tor taken maf--" "tonk'peh, panah-tor. Nam-tor au nunau na' wuh halovaya?" ya'akash mr. Lorry. "weht nunau na' ik, i nah-tor, do tor hafau svi' nash kahr, ni dreadful tor ish-veh." "ish-veh nam-tor yeht, " leralmin-tor defarge, vi vesh' kneeling tor glazhau fi' heh zhu-tor. "weht do ik; monsieur manette nam-tor, na' ek' utvau, buhfik s' france. Leralmin, dungau i hire wuh carriage heh lehk-jarel?" "ik's business, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, resuming fi' wuh shortest beglanau ish-veh methodical manners; "heh kuv business nam-tor tor nam-tor ovsoh, i had weh-rom tor ish-veh." "yi nam-tor ni ves, " urged din-tor manette, "u' tor trasha etek la'. Gla-tor du uf tertitau au has shetau, heh du fam yehat nam-tor kwes tor trasha ish-veh k' me i'. Po dang du nam-tor? Kuv du dungi klachek wuh svep tor shar etek s' svi-shaya, i ri tor vet ik du dungi talal ish-veh, lu sarlah du pla', u' hizhuk u' du trasha ish-veh. Svi' sovek nuf, i dungi nem-tor tun t' ish-veh abi' du fun, heh yi etek dungi snem-tor ish-veh zehik." fi' mr. Lorry heh defarge vesh' rather disinclined tor nash rivak, heh svi' favour t' veh t' au remaining. Tonk'peh, u' tra' vesh' ri goh carriage heh jarel tor nam-tor gla-tor tor, tonk'peh travelling dun; heh u' wak hish-tor, na' wuh gad vesh' bestan tor wuh shaht, sarlah ish-veh na' kim-shah tor ish-veh hastily dividing wuh business ik vesh' bolayatik tor nam-tor ovsoh, heh hurrying maf tor tor ish-veh. Yi, u' wuh mu'khlup'es a'ing svi', wuh ko-fu laid ish-veh patam ne' fi' wuh lerash solektra ikap-tor na' wuh sa-mekh's vla, heh glantau ish-veh. Wuh mu'khlup'es deepened heh deepened, heh au fi' ti hizhuk, abi' wuh ta'hal gleamed k'fai wuh chinks svi' wuh temok. Mr. Lorry heh monsieur defarge had tor ek' pok na' wuh halovaya, heh had katau k' au, isha travelling tor-sai heh wrappers, kap heh kahm, wine, heh fal mon. Monsieur defarge shitau nash provender, heh wuh ha'gelek au lesh, fi' wuh shoemaker's wu-ku-san (tra' vesh' nothing else svi' wuh kamu-tvi-shal tonk'peh wuh pallet sar-tak), heh au heh mr. Lorry kastorilau wuh captive, heh gol-tor ish-veh tor ish-veh ash'ya. Rai komihn kash-tor'es kupi ma telv-tor wuh mysteries t' ish-veh kashek, svi' wuh pahth-tor blank wonder t' ish-veh limuk. Whether au fai-tor ra had pavesh-tor, whether au recollected ra au had leralmin-tor tor ish-veh, whether au fai-tor ik au vesh' elik, vesh' deshkau if rai sagacity kupi ma kilau. Au ar'kada speaking tor ish-veh; tonk'peh, au vesh' ni confused, heh ni maut vohris tor kilko-srashiv, ik au nem-tor kolthak na' ish-veh bewilderment, heh sep-wafikh na' wuh wak tor tamper k' ish-veh rai weht. Au had wuh kwai, pakik manner t' occasionally clasping ish-veh patam svi' ish-veh el'ru, ik had ri vesh' gla-tor svi' ish-veh fa'; wi, au had ein sanosh svi' wuh mere ralash t' ish-veh ko-fu's spes, heh invariably da-tor tor ish-veh lu she stariben. Svi' wuh nepik yut t' veh wu accustomed tor obey ne' coercion, au ate heh drank ra au mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tor yokul heh mon, heh shitau fi' wuh tor-sai heh vath wrappings, ik au mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh sai-vel-tor. Au readily kesau tor ish-veh ko-fu's bestan ish-veh kar k'fai ish-veh, heh nem-tor--heh potau--ish-veh el'ru svi' fi' ish-veh sha'. Au began tor tev-tor; monsieur defarge going wuh'rak k' wuh ha'gelek, mr. Lorry ikapik wuh pi' procession. Au had ri traversed wehk ash-tor t' wuh wu nen staircase lu au pehkau, heh nantau na' wuh kamu heh pauk na' wuh temok. "du vokau wuh shi, t'nash-veh sa-mekh? Du vokau coming abru la'?" "ra did du leralmin?" tonk'peh, fa' she kupi ashiv-tor wuh deshker, au murmured wuh kilko-srashiv u' kuv she had ashiv-tor ish-veh. "vokau? Rai, i ri tor vokau. Ish-veh vesh' ni maut wu ago." ik au had rai recollection whatever t' ish-veh having vesh' katau s' ish-veh prison tor ik kelek, vesh' apparent tor au. Au puzhu-tor ish-veh mutter, "teh heh kaukuh, desh'rak kispek; " heh lu au glazhau pa' ish-veh, ish-veh evidently vesh' na' wuh karik klomak-temok if had wu encompassed ish-veh. Fi' ish-veh reaching wuh courtyard au instinctively rubitau ish-veh tread, u' hasu svi' gishat t' wuh drawbridge; heh lu tra' vesh' rai drawbridge, heh gla-tor ish-veh wuh carriage waiting svi' wuh tu'ash yut, au eku-tor ish-veh ko-fu's el'ru heh clasped ish-veh patam va'ashiv. Rai patreitan vesh' pa' wuh svep; rai sutra vesh' discernible na' sovek t' wuh wehk krani; ri kauk wuh pavesh passerby vesh' svi' wuh yut. Wuh unnatural silence heh desertion reigned tra'. Goh veh soul vesh' tor nam-tor gla-tor, heh ik vesh' madame defarge--vi gal-tor tehnat wuh svep-lehk, knitting, heh gla-tor nothing. Wuh prisoner had prah vi' wuh coach, heh ish-veh ko-fu had zahal-tor ish-veh, lu mr. Lorry's ash'ya vesh' pehkau fi' wuh ash k' ish-veh asking, miserably, na' ish-veh shoemaking raul heh wuh unfinished ash'el. Madame defarge iyi puvutau tor ish-veh sa-telsu ik she would prah au, heh went, knitting, s' wuh lamplight, k'fai wuh courtyard. She sahris katau au ne' heh handed au svi'; --heh iyi afterwards gal-tor tehnat wuh svep-lehk, knitting, heh gla-tor nothing. Defarge prah fi-tor wuh natuhn, heh mazhiv-kur-tor wuh zhit "tor wuh foshek!" wuh postilion treshau ish-veh wonil-zehl, heh au clattered maf ne' wuh kobat abru'-swinging ha'gelek. Ne' wuh abru'-swinging ha'gelek--swinging ek'wak brighter svi' wuh weh-rom yut, heh ek'wak ha'khlup-neyek svi' wuh weh-rasahkos--heh k' lighted mahr-kel, sa-ka-ashausu patreitan, illuminated mon-kelek, heh theatre-svep, tor veh t' wuh kahr temep. Ask'ersu k' makh-yonet, na' wuh klashausu-kelek tra'. "ish-veh dun, travellers!" "gla-tor la' yi, monsieur wuh officer, " leralmin-tor defarge, getting ne', heh taking ish-veh gravely k'wuhli, "aifa nam-tor wuh dun t' monsieur svi'udish, k' wuh wan-kur patam. Au vesh' consigned tor me, k' ish-veh, na' wuh--" au eku-tor ish-veh spes, tra' vesh' wuh nuv among wuh askital makh-yonet, heh veh t' au hasu handed vi' wuh coach k' wuh kar svi' uniform, wuh bezhun tersau k' wuh kar glazhau, ri wuh kanok gad il wuh kanok mu-yor glazhau, na' monsieur k' wuh wan-kur patam. "ish-veh nam-tor muhl. Fa'rak!" s' wuh uniform. "adieu!" s' defarge. Heh ni, ne' wuh pen pi'laptra t' feebler heh feebler abru'-swinging ha'gelek, si' ne' wuh lo'uk pi'laptra t' yel. Ne'rak ik kesek t' unmoved heh ek'wakik ha'ge; ein, ni remote s' nash pi' terra ik wuh oren-tor var-tor etek ish-veh nam-tor vet-bosh whether ish-veh ha'zehl ma kauk wi discovered ish-veh, u' wuh sfek svi' ret wilat sovek-vel nam-tor dashau il ovsoh: wuh duv t' wuh mu-yor vesh' sax'ksei heh nesh-kur. Ek' k'fai wuh samu heh restless tvi-wak, abi' gad-keshtan, au wuh'wak weht zhal-tor svi' wuh kaluk t' mr. Jarvis lorry--sitting mesyutik wuh visolektau sasu vi had vesh' hil-tor si', heh wondering ra subtle tepul vesh' na' ek'wak pakik tor ish-veh, heh ra vesh' capable t' restoration--wuh hinek inquiry: "i rok du tun tor nam-tor recalled tor ha'kiv?" heh wuh hinek kilko-srashiv: "i mokuhlek't leralmin." wuh shaht t' wuh wuh'rak dunap. Dunap wuh dahr--wuh pi-maat-kur og-elakh chapter i. Kaukuh tevun later tellson's kutra k' temple mofek vesh' wuh hinek-fashioned shi, kauk svi' wuh tevun leh-teh stehkuh hundred heh oh-leh. Ish-veh vesh' maut pi', maut gu'gelik, maut watosh, maut incommodious. Ish-veh vesh' wuh hinek-fashioned shi, moreover, svi' wuh moral attribute ik wuh tersu svi' wuh kelek vesh' yaut t' its smallness, yaut t' its mu'khlup'es, yaut t' its ugliness, yaut t' its incommodiousness. Au vesh' kauk boastful t' its eminence svi' eifa particulars, heh vesh' pohshau k' wuh sagluvau conviction ik, kuv ish-veh vesh' lehkuh objectionable, ish-veh would nam-tor lehkuh respectable. Nash vesh' rai ritorupik dva, tonk'peh wuh torupik wun if au kahai na' weht convenient shitau t' business. Tellson's (au leralmin-tor) aitlu rai kar-nef-tvi-shal, tellson's aitlu rai ta'hal, tellson's aitlu rai embellishment. Noakes heh co.'s lau, il snooks sa-kai' lau; tonk'peh tellson's, itaren sha-ka-ri--! Sovek veh t' aifa tersu would ma disinherited ish-veh sa-fu fi' wuh deshker t' rebuilding tellson's. Svi' nash respect wuh kelek vesh' mau fi' wuh par k' wuh shasol; if did maut k'ashiv disinherit its sa-fu na' suggesting improvements svi' tor-gav heh customs ik had wu vesh' highly objectionable, tonk'peh vesh' goh wuh weht respectable. Thus ish-veh had sarlah tor be' dvun, ik tellson's vesh' wuh triumphant perfection t' inconvenience. Po' bursting tu'ash wuh svep t' idiotic obstinacy k' wuh kobat rattle svi' its drahk, du tevan-tor vi' tellson's ne' dahkuh ash-tor, heh sarlah tor ish-veh kash-ral svi' wuh miserable pi' mahr-kel, k' dahkuh pi' tumek, wilat wuh oldest t' sasu tor ish-veh cheque hutau u' kuv wuh salan rustled ish-veh, du' au linisau wuh signature k' wuh dingiest t' krani, if vesh' kwon-hau-ov ne' wuh mashulayek-wu'sibav t' vral s' halitra-yut, heh if vesh' tor wuh dingier k' ish-veh sha' shek-tukh mofek proper, heh wuh ras duv t' temple mofek. Kuv ish-veh business necessitated ish-veh seeing "wuh kelek, " du vesh' shitau vi' wuh koshtri t' condemned meskaraya na' wuh pla', wilat du meditated fi' wuh misspent ha'kiv, abi' wuh kelek sarlah k' its el'ru svi' its abru'lik, heh du kupi hardly blink na' ish-veh svi' wuh dismal twilight. Ish-veh donku sasarlah t', il went vi', wormy hinek wooden zish-nef, pi'gal t' if flew abru ish-veh han heh ne' ish-veh drahk lu au vesh' tu'ash heh ikap-tor. Ish-veh kutra-pitoh had wuh musty vil, u' kuv au vesh' sahris decomposing vi' a'cit va'ashiv. Ish-veh math vesh' stowed maf among wuh neighbouring cesspools, heh ek'rasah communications corrupted its rom polish svi' wuh gad il dahkuh. Ish-veh deeds prah vi' extemporised karik-tvi-shal tor t' af'tum heh sculleries, heh fretted ek' wuh thelik s' ish-veh parchments vi' wuh banking-kelek sov. Ish-veh lighter natuhn t' skan dun went abru-kaiden vi' wuh barmecide tvi-shal, ik kwon-hau-ov had wuh lo'uk dining-pasu svi' ish-veh heh worla had wuh aru-yem, heh wilat, kauk svi' wuh tevun leh-teh stehkuh hundred heh oh-leh, wuh wuh'rak nuhm written tor du k' ish-veh hinek ashaya, il k' ish-veh pi' kanu, vesh' tonk'peh newly sadalau s' wuh horror t' hasu ogled k'fai wuh krani, k' wuh patam ko'nar fi' temple mofek k' wuh insensate brutality heh keimen'es worthy t' abyssinia il ashantee. Tonk'peh indeed, na' ik wak, putting tor tevakh vesh' wuh recipe mau svi' vogue k' ek' trades heh ha'yigal, heh ri least t' ek' k' tellson's. Tevakh nam-tor malat's remedy na' ek' vel, heh po ri legislation's? Accordingly, wuh forger vesh' tostau; wuh utterer t' wuh rasahkos pitoh vesh' tostau; wuh unlawful opener t' wuh nuhm vesh' tostau; wuh purloiner t' keh-leh shillings heh sixpence vesh' tostau; wuh holder t' wuh jarel na' tellson's svep, vi tor ska' k' ish-veh, vesh' shitau tor tevakh; wuh coiner t' wuh rasahkos shilling vesh' tostau; wuh sounders t' rehkuh-fourths t' wuh pitoh svi' wuh bosh gamut t' tr'y'kak, vesh' shitau tor tevakh. Ri ik ish-veh did wuh least rom svi' wuh yut t' prevention--ish-veh lau siyah ma vesh' don remarking ik wuh kla-min vesh' exactly wuh reverse--tonk'peh, ish-veh pa'shu ska' (u' tor nash panu) wuh trouble t' tik particular nuf, heh losrak nothing else tersau k' ish-veh tor nam-tor glazhau po'. Thus, tellson's, svi' its gad, spo' greater shitau t' business, its contemporaries, had taken ni wehk ha-tor, ik, kuv wuh patam laid neik fa' ish-veh had vesh' ranged fi' temple mofek instead t' hasu privately sashitau t', au would probably ma sanan-tor ra pi' ta'hal wuh solektra lan-tol had, svi' wuh rather significant manner. Runelau svi' ek' ves t' neik-ha'khlup cupboards heh hutches na' tellson's, wuh oldest t' sasu lesh fi' wuh business gravely. Lu au nem-tor wuh nu'ri sasu vi' tellson's london kelek, au ip-sut ish-veh ein-wilat till au vesh' hinek. Au potau ish-veh svi' wuh gu'gelik shi, spo' wuh thuhk, abi' au had wuh bosh tellson zahv heh pla-kur-mould fi-tor ish-veh. Yi goh vesh' au permitted tor nam-tor gla-tor, spectacularly poring abru' suk dunap, heh casting ish-veh breeches heh gaiters vi' wuh paik rasath t' wuh establishment. S'udish tellson's--worla k' sovek tvai svi' ish-veh, vita puvutau svi'--vesh' wuh shaik-job-sasu, wuh occasional porter heh skladasu, vi dvin-tor u' wuh ha-tor glat t' wuh kelek. Au vesh' worla tadek-adir du' business wadan, vita fi-tor wuh skrol, heh yi au vesh' represented k' ish-veh sa-fu: wuh grisly urchin t' leh-dah, vi vesh' ish-veh sagluvau glakuv. Sutra ken-tor ik tellson's, svi' wuh stately yut, wivelau wuh shaik-job-sasu. Wuh kelek had kwon-hau-ov wivelau ein person svi' ik tsoh, heh wak heh mashen had marau nash person tor wuh lehk. Ish-veh surname vesh' cruncher, heh fi' wuh youthful occasion t' ish-veh renouncing k' proxy wuh ar'kada t' mu'khlup'es, svi' wuh easterly parish church t' hounsditch, au had poprah wuh hau appellation t' jerry. Wuh scene vesh' mr. Cruncher's awek lodging svi' hanging-shek-alley, whitefriars: wuh wak, ulef-vesht stehkuh t' wuh wak-vel fi' wuh salanayik march asal, anno domini leh- steh hundred heh oh-leh. (mr. Cruncher himself kwon-hau-ov stariben t' wuh tevun t' etwel s'haile u' anna dominoes: sauyaing ne' wuh impression ik wuh christian nuhs dated s' wuh fereik-vel t' wuh popular zhagra, k' wuh t'sai vi had bestowed ish-veh ahm fi-tor ish-veh.) mr. Cruncher's ha-shal vesh' ri svi' wuh savoury neighbourhood, heh vesh' tonk'peh dahkuh svi' su'etek, kauk kuv wuh tsorayek k' wuh single pane t' makh svi' ish-veh lau nam-tor tum-tor u' veh. Tonk'peh au vesh' maut decently potau. Lehkuh-mal u' ish-veh vesh', fi' wuh salanayik march asal, wuh tvi-shal svi' if au ti abed vesh' already scrubbed throughout; heh svi' wuh cups heh ne-mathra arranged na' asal-yem, heh wuh lumbering deal pasu, wuh maut sok'i wan-kur sai vesh' sak-tor. Mr. Cruncher reposed ne' wuh patchwork counterpane, spo' wuh harlequin na' ha-kel. Palikauk, au yuk-tor heavily, tonk'peh, k' degrees, began tor padukau heh tral svi' sar-tak, abi' au she-tor abru' wuh skonn, k' ish-veh spiky isachya looking u' kuv ish-veh bolau bezhun-masu wuh thalv tor ribbons. Na' if juncture, au sporiben, svi' wuh spes t' dire exasperation: "bust me, kuv she ain't na' ish-veh agin!" wuh kosu t' orderly heh industrious appearance she-tor s' ish-veh mal-nef svi' wuh teruk, k' sufficient haste heh trepidation tor gluvaya ik she vesh' wuh person referred tor. "ra!" leralmin-tor mr. Cruncher, looking s' sar-tak na' wuh kluf. "du're na' ish-veh agin, nam-tor du?" po' hailing wuh morn k' nash dahr salutation, au threw wuh kluf na' wuh kosu u' wuh wuh. Ish-veh vesh' wuh maut muddy kluf, heh lau ragtau wuh shaik circumstance tersau k' mr. Cruncher's ka'kelik iskan, ik, whereas au k'ashiv sarlah ha-kel po' banking wadan k' sok'i kluf, au k'ashiv prah abru thurai asal tor talal wuh ka kluf wein-tor k' krizhiv. "ra, " leralmin-tor mr. Cruncher, varying ish-veh apostrophe po' missing ish-veh ulidar--"ra nam-tor du abru tor, aggerawayter?" "i vesh' goh taran t'nash-veh prayers." "taran ish-veh prayers! Du're wuh nice kosu! Ra tor du tvai k' tevan-tor yourself ne' heh praying agin me?" "i vesh' ri praying tehnat du; i vesh' praying na' du." "du weren't. Heh kuv du vesh', i skil-tor't nam-tor nem-tor wuh liberty k'. La'! Ish-veh ko-mekh's wuh nice kosu, nu'ri jerry, going wuh praying agin ish-veh sa-mekh's smusma'es. Du've prah wuh dutiful ko-mekh, du ma, t'nash-veh sa-fu. Du've prah wuh religious ko-mekh, du ma, t'nash-veh sa-kan: going heh tevan-tor herself ne', heh praying ik wuh kap-heh-butter lau nam-tor snatched si' t' wuh ru'lut t' ish-veh goh kan." trensu cruncher (vi vesh' svi' ish-veh sav'el) nem-tor nash maut has-bosh, heh, turning tor ish-veh ko-mekh, strongly deprecated sovek praying maf t' ish-veh personal dohn. "heh ra tor du suppose, du conceited kotik, " leralmin-tor mr. Cruncher, k' unconscious inconsistency, "ik wuh don t' ish-veh prayers lau nam-tor? Ahm wuh price ik du shitau ish-veh prayers na'!" "au goh sarlah s' wuh khaf-spol, jerry. Au nam-tor don rai weht do ik." "don rai weht do ik, " ashiv-tor mr. Cruncher. "au ain't don mau, yi. Whether il rai, i skil-tor't nam-tor prayed agin, i var-tor du. I mokuhlek't afford ish-veh. I'm ri wuh going tor nam-tor tor unlucky k' ish-veh sneaking. Kuv du bolau hal-tor tevan-tor yourself ne', tevan-tor svi' favour t' ish-veh sa-telsu heh kan, heh ri svi' opposition tor 'em. Kuv i had had sovek tonk'peh wuh unnat'ral ko-telsu, heh nash ri donku-tor sa-kan had had sovek tonk'peh wuh unnat'ral ko-mekh, i lau ma tor ein donku kim-shah wehk gad instead t' hasu tumek-prayed heh countermined heh religiously circumwented vi' wuh rasahkos t' kunli. B-u-u-ust me!" leralmin-tor mr. Cruncher, vi ek' nash wak had vesh' putting fi' ish-veh sai-vel, "kuv i ain't, ra k' piety heh veh salur vel heh wuh'ashiv, vesh' choused nash kim-shah wehk gad vi' u' rasahkos kunli u' ek'wak wuh ri donku-tor e'shua t' wuh trau tradesman ragel-tor k'! Nu'ri jerry, sai-vel yourself, t'nash-veh sa-kan, heh du' i sok'i t'nash-veh kluf potau wuh bezhun fi-tor ish-veh ko-mekh i' heh yi, heh kuv gla-tor du sovek glat t' weht tevan-tor, mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh vutau. Na', i var-tor du, " la' au addressed ish-veh ko-telsu wuh'wak weht, "i skil-tor't nam-tor hal-tor agin, svi' nash manner. I am u' rickety u' wuh hackney-coach, i'm u' sleepy u' laudanum, t'nash-veh zehl nam-tor ish-veh-tor tor ik degree ik i shouldn't fai-tor, kuv ish-veh wasn't na' wuh kusut svi' 'em, if vesh' me heh if somebody else, wi i'm rim wuh weh-rom na' ish-veh svi' abru'lik; heh ish-veh's t'nash-veh suspicion ik du've vesh' na' ish-veh s' asal tor mu-yor tor prevent me s' hasu wuh weh-rom na' ish-veh svi' abru'lik, heh i skil-tor't shitau abru k' ish-veh, aggerawayter, heh ra tor du leralmin i'!" growling, svi' haya, such zhit-bal u' "ah! Ha! Du're religious, nuh'. Du wouldn't shitau yourself svi' opposition tor wuh eku'ko t' ish-veh sa-telsu heh kan, would du? Ri du!" heh throwing ska' vath sarcastic kil-tor s' wuh whirling grindstone t' ish-veh indignation, mr. Cruncher betook himself tor ish-veh kluf-cleaning heh ish-veh paik preparation na' business. Svi' wuh meantime, ish-veh sa-fu, t'vi patam vesh' garnished k' tenderer spikes, heh t'vi nu'ri bezhun lam-tor beyik veh wuh'ashiv, u' ish-veh sa-mekh's did, potau wuh required glantau fi-tor ish-veh ko-mekh. Au greatly ertau ik ri donku-tor kosu na' tvi-wak, k' darting s' ish-veh sleeping tsorayek, wilat au tor ish-veh toilet, k' wuh nelau maf t' "du nam-tor going tor tevan-tor, ko-mekh. --halloa, sa-mekh!" heh, po' raising nash glenonik vikayek, darting svi' va'ashiv k' wuh undutiful wa'limatau. Mr. Cruncher's temper vesh' mokov improved lu sarlah ish-veh tor ish-veh asal-yem. Au resented mrs. Cruncher's taran takov k' particular animosity. "i', aggerawayter! Ra nam-tor du abru tor? Na' ish-veh va'ashiv?" ish-veh ko-telsu danau ik she had goh "ya'akash wuh kudaya." "ri tor tor ish-veh!" leralmin-tor mr. Crunches looking pa', u' kuv au rather gishu tor gla-tor wuh loaf sasaudau ne' wuh efficacy t' ish-veh ko-telsu's petitions. "i ain't wuh going tor nam-tor blest s' kelek heh ha-kel. I skil-tor't ma t'nash-veh wittles blest ska' t'nash-veh pasu. Potau fam dvun!" exceedingly yon-kur-eyed heh grim, u' kuv au had vesh' abru ek' mu-yor na' wuh party if had taken sovek-vel tonk'peh wuh convivial da-tor, jerry cruncher worried ish-veh asal-yem rather do ate ish-veh, growling abru' ish-veh spo' sovek kehkuh-footed inmate t' wuh menagerie. Na' naukuh o'wak-vel au smoothed ish-veh ruffled pulva, heh, presenting u' respectable heh business-spo' wuh sin u' au kupi overlay ish-veh malatik shal k', issued forth tor wuh occupation t' wuh gad. Ish-veh kupi scarcely nam-tor puvutau wuh trade, svi' spite t' ish-veh favourite kethelvaya t' himself u' "wuh trau tradesman." ish-veh fek consisted t' wuh wooden stool, tor s' wuh pushau-backed ku-san tresahk ne', if stool, nu'ri jerry, walking na' ish-veh sa-mekh's vla, lesh kanok asal tor ne'rak wuh banking-kelek krani ik vesh' nearest temple mofek: wilat, k' wuh haya t' wuh wuh'rak handful t' terp ik kupi nam-tor gleaned s' sovek be' dvun-tor hali tor potau wuh samu heh masupik s' wuh shaik-job-sasu's ash'ya, ish-veh shidau wuh encampment na' wuh gad. Fi' nash lehk t' ish-veh, mr. Cruncher vesh' u' muhl fainu tor halitra-yut heh wuh temple, u' wuh mofek itself, --heh vesh' siyah u' svi'-looking. Encamped na' wuh yonuk fa' naukuh, svi' rom wak tor esta ish-veh rehkuh-cornered taik tor wuh oldest t' sasu u' au be' dvun-tor svi' tor tellson's, jerry nem-tor abru ish-veh wurzel fi' nash salanayik march asal, k' nu'ri jerry standing k' ish-veh, lu ri engaged svi' tor forays k'fai wuh mofek, tor inflict bodily heh mental dash t' wuh zat kethelvaya fi' be' dvun-tor sa-kan vi vesh' pi' hiyet na' ish-veh amiable lof. Sa-mekh heh sa-fu, extremely spo' tik vath, looking silently fi' na' wuh asal traffic svi' halitra-yut, k' ish-veh dahkuh patam u' be' tor veh wuh'ashiv u' wuh dahkuh bezhun t' tik vesh', spitau wuh considerable resemblance tor wuh shif t' monkeys. Wuh resemblance vesh' ri lessened k' wuh ur'kif circumstance, ik wuh vinik jerry zeshau heh spat si' terp, du' wuh twinkling bezhun t' wuh youthful jerry vesh' u' restlessly tun-tor t' ish-veh u' t' kanok-vei else svi' halitra-yut. Wuh patam t' veh t' wuh regular indoor skladasu attached tor tellson's establishment vesh' shitau k'fai wuh svep, heh wuh zhit vesh' putan-tor: "porter aitlu!" "hooray, sa-mekh! La''s wuh lehkuh-mal job tor palikau k'!" having thus putan-tor ish-veh parent oekon threshan, nu'ri jerry hayal-tor himself fi' wuh stool, svi-tor fi' ish-veh reversionary eku'ko svi' wuh terp ish-veh sa-mekh had vesh' chewing, heh cogitated. "al-yut zhar-tor! Ish-veh ozh nam-tor al-yut zhar-tor!" muttered nu'ri jerry. "wilat tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh prah ek' ik shek-tukh zhar s'? Au ri tor prah rai shek-tukh zhar la'!" chapter ii. Wuh glan "du fai-tor wuh hinek bailey muhl, rai vet?" leralmin-tor veh t' wuh oldest t' clerks tor jerry wuh skladasu. "ye-es, osu, " fun-tor jerry, svi' vel t' wuh dogged manner. "i tor fai-tor wuh bailey." "aishan ni. Heh du fai-tor mr. Lorry." "i fai-tor mr. Lorry, osu, mau weh-rom do i fai-tor wuh bailey. Mau weh-rom, " leralmin-tor jerry, ri rikes wuh reluctant toglantausu na' wuh establishment svi' deshker, "do i, u' wuh trau tradesman, istaya tor fai-tor wuh bailey." "maut muhl. Talal wuh svep wilat wuh toglantausu hal-tor svi', heh gluvaya wuh svep-keeper nash pitoh na' mr. Lorry. Au dungi yi kal-tor du svi'." "vi' wuh kelek, osu?" "vi' wuh kelek." mr. Cruncher's bezhun seemed tor prah wuh pi' closer tor veh wuh'ashiv, heh tor interchange wuh inquiry, "ra tor du nah-tor t' nash?" "am i tor bek-tor svi' wuh kelek, osu?" au ya'akash, u' wuh result t' ik conference. "i am going tor var-tor du. Wuh svep-keeper dungi be' dvun wuh pitoh tor mr. Lorry, heh tor du tor sovek gesture ik dungi skamau mr. Lorry's attention, heh gluvaya ish-veh wilat du lamok. Yi ra du ma tor tor, nam-tor, tor hafau tra' abi' au aitlu du." "nam-tor ik ek', osu?" "ik's ek'. Au istau ki' wuh skladasu na' el'ru. Nash nam-tor tor var-tor ish-veh du nam-tor tra'." u' wuh t'kahr clerk deliberately hesha heh superscribed wuh pitoh, mr. Cruncher, po' surveying ish-veh svi' silence abi' sarlah ish-veh tor wuh blotting-dun skaf, remarked: "i suppose au'll nam-tor trying forgeries nash asal?" "kam'nat!" "ik's quartering, " leralmin-tor jerry. "barbarous!" "ish-veh nam-tor wuh tor-gav, " remarked wuh t'kahr clerk, turning ish-veh ak'wikmun spectacles fi-tor ish-veh. "ish-veh nam-tor wuh tor-gav." "ish-veh's lerash svi' wuh tor-gav tor spile wuh sasu, i nah-tor. Ish-veh's lerash hiyet tor stau ish-veh, tonk'peh ish-veh's wery lerash tor spile ish-veh, osu." "mokov, " retained wuh t'kahr clerk. "stariben muhl t' wuh tor-gav. Nem-tor tun t' ish-veh tuf heh spes, t'nash-veh rom t'hy'la, heh trasha wuh tor-gav tor nem-tor tun t' itself. I mazhiv-kur-tor du ik na'shikh." "ish-veh's wuh damp, osu, ra settles fi' t'nash-veh tuf heh spes, " leralmin-tor jerry. "i trasha du tor judge ra wuh damp yut t' earning wuh living t'nash-veh nam-tor." "muhl, muhl, " leralmin-tor wuh hinek clerk; "etek ek' ma etwel vuhnauk yut t' gaining wuh livelihood. Ein t' etek ma damp yut, heh ein t' etek ma pseth yut. La' nam-tor wuh nuhm. Hal-tor bi'." jerry nem-tor wuh nuhm, heh, remarking tor himself k' lehkuh internal deference do au tor wuh outward gluvaya t', "du nam-tor wuh galat hinek veh, nuh', " tor ish-veh kes-wun, informed ish-veh sa-fu, svi' be' dvun-tor, t' ish-veh destination, heh went ish-veh yut. Au geldau na' tyburn, svi' eifa gad, ni wuh yut s'udish newgate had ri prah veh infamous notoriety ik has opi' attached tor ish-veh. Tonk'peh, wuh gaol vesh' wuh vile shi, svi' if danik ves t' debauchery heh villainy vesh' practised, heh wilat dire has vesh' bred, ik sarlah vi' kelek k' wuh prisoners, heh sometimes rushed zehik s' wuh kif na' t'nash-veh s'haile chief yeht-gav himself, heh seshau ish-veh ska' wuh wu-ku-san. Ish-veh had weht do wuh'wak pavesh-tor, ik wuh judge svi' wuh nesh-kur taik pronounced ish-veh sha' doom u' certainly u' wuh prisoner's, heh kauk tev-tor fa' ish-veh. Na' wuh shom, wuh hinek bailey vesh' khinik u' wuh ves t' tevalik ha-shal-ker, s' if spoh travellers eku si' continually, svi' hal heh coaches, fi' wuh khrashik tvur vi' wuh vath panu: traversing ein dahkuh miles heh wuh ulef t' tsuri yut heh fau-yut, heh shaming zamu rom citizens, kuv sovek. Ni powerful nam-tor nam-tor-tor, heh ni desirable tor nam-tor rom nam-tor-tor svi' wuh palikaya. Ish-veh vesh' khinik, nuh', na' wuh pillory, wuh kau-bosh hinek trahokna, ik inflicted wuh taflaya t' if kling kupi fa-glan-tor wuh sadvun; isha, na' wuh whipping-lehk, wuh'ashiv tal-kam hinek trahokna, maut humanising heh softening tor behold svi' torai; isha, na' extensive transactions svi' khaf-donku, wuh'ashiv karf t' ancestral kau, systematically leading tor wuh danik frightful mercenary tr'y'kak ik kupi nam-tor committed ne' sha-ka-ri. Altogether, wuh hinek bailey, na' ik kinuf, vesh' wuh dvel illustration t' wuh precept, ik "whatever nam-tor nam-tor gas'rak; " wuh aphorism ik would nam-tor u' kim-shah u' ish-veh nam-tor kas'el, did ish-veh ri vinan-tor wuh troublesome consequence, ik nothing ik ek'wak vesh', vesh' riyeht. Tor ish-veh yut k'fai wuh tainted patreitan, pusaganau abru heh ne' nash hideous scene t' torai, k' wuh renkup'es t' wuh sasu accustomed tor tor ish-veh yut quietly, wuh skladasu afer-tor si' wuh svep au sought, heh handed svi' ish-veh nuhm k'fai wuh pash svi' ish-veh. Na', sutra yi vlitau tor gla-tor wuh mavau na' wuh hinek bailey, aishan u' au vlitau tor gla-tor wuh mavau svi' bedlam--goh wuh former entertainment vesh' mau wuh dearer. Therefore, ek' wuh hinek bailey svep vesh' muhl klashau--kaula, indeed, wuh shilaik svep k' if wuh criminals prah tra', heh eifa vesh' kwon-hau-ov losrak eik tu'ash. Po' ein vohtaya heh demur, wuh svep grudgingly da-tor fi' its tu'adayek wuh maut pi' yut, heh kal-tor mr. Jerry cruncher tor lerakhovau himself vi' kelek. "ra's fi'?" au ya'akash, svi' wuh zhal, t' wuh sasu au afer-tor himself thurai tor. "nothing wi." "ra's coming fi'?" "wuh kam'nat nuf." "wuh quartering veh, eh?" "ah!" fun-tor wuh sasu, k' wuh relish; "au'll nam-tor drawn fi' wuh hurdle tor nam-tor ulef geldau, heh yi au'll nam-tor taken ne' heh shihvek-tor fa' ish-veh sha' limuk, heh yi ish-veh svi'udish dungi nam-tor taken si' heh yontau du' au glazhau fi', heh yi ish-veh patam dungi nam-tor chopped ska', heh au'll nam-tor tresahk vi' ha-shal. Ik's wuh zhit-bal." "kuv au's afer-tor guilty, du tvai tor leralmin?" jerry hau, k' yut t' proviso. "oh! Au'll talal ish-veh guilty, " leralmin-tor wuh vath. "ri tor du nam-tor kwes t' ik." mr. Cruncher's attention vesh' la' matau tor wuh svep-keeper, ik au gla-tor tor ish-veh yut tor mr. Lorry, k' wuh pitoh svi' ish-veh el'ru. Mr. Lorry hayal-tor na' wuh pasu, among wuh gentlemen svi' wigs: ri irak s' wuh wigged gentleman, wuh prisoner's counsel, vi had wuh lo'uk uzh'a'lek t' dun fa' ish-veh: heh nearly mesyutik wuh'ashiv wigged gentleman k' ish-veh el'ru svi' ish-veh abru'lik, t'vi bosh attention, lu mr. Cruncher glazhau na' ish-veh yi il afterwards, seemed tor nam-tor concentrated fi' wuh abru-tol t' wuh kelek. Po' ein gruff coughing heh rubbing t' ish-veh chin heh signing k' ish-veh el'ru, jerry skamau wuh beglanau t' mr. Lorry, vi had lam-tor abru tor glazhau na' ish-veh, heh vi quietly nodded heh hayal-tor ne' va'ashiv. "ra's au prah tor tor k' wuh nuf?" ya'akash wuh sasu au had spoken k'. "blest kuv i fai-tor, " leralmin-tor jerry. "ra ma du prah tor tor k' ish-veh, yi, kuv wuh person lau inquire?" "blest kuv i fai-tor ik either, " leralmin-tor jerry. Wuh entrance t' wuh judge, heh wuh consequent lo'uk stir heh settling ne' svi' wuh kelek, pehkau wuh dialogue. Presently, wuh kif became wuh central sfek t' eku'ko. Dahkuh gaolers, vi had vesh' standing tra', went si', heh wuh prisoner vesh' katau svi', heh shitau tor wuh mofek. Kanok-veh la', kaula wuh veh wigged gentleman vi glazhau na' wuh abru-tol, nantau na' ish-veh. Ek' wuh komihn esh svi' wuh shi, padukau na' ish-veh, spo' wuh masutra, il wuh salan, il wuh yon. Nayik limuk ish-veh-tor pauk pillars heh teruk, tor prah wuh glan t' ish-veh; spectators svi' pla' fel-tor lam-tor abru, ri tor din-tor wuh isachya t' ish-veh; sutra fi' wuh lan-tol t' wuh kelek, laid ish-veh el'ru fi' wuh tipan t' wuh sutra fa' au, tor gol'nev themselves, na' anybody's kodona, tor wuh zan-tor t' ish-veh--lam-tor wuh-tiptoe, prah fi-tor ledges, lam-tor fi-tor nam-tor' nothing, tor gla-tor kanok inch t' ish-veh. Conspicuous among aifa latter, spo' wuh animated zeshau t' wuh spiked temok t' newgate, jerry lam-tor: aiming na' wuh prisoner wuh beery esh t' wuh whet au had taken u' sarlah ish-veh bi', heh discharging ish-veh tor mingle k' wuh pral t' vath naliveh, heh gin, heh theris-masu, heh mon, heh ra ri, ik yumau na' ish-veh, heh already shau fi-tor wuh lo'uk krani za' ish-veh svi' wuh impure mist heh sov-masu. Wuh vel t' ek' nash staring heh blaring, vesh' wuh nu'ri sasu t' pa' kaukuh-heh-dah-leh, muhl-grown heh muhl-looking, k' wuh sunburnt nak heh wuh gu'gelik bezhun. Ish-veh nosh vesh' ik t' wuh nu'ri gentleman. Au vesh' plainly sai-vel-tor svi' nesh-kur, il maut ras-kur, heh ish-veh isachya, if vesh' wu heh gu'gelik, vesh' hoknau svi' wuh ribbon na' wuh pla' t' ish-veh talu; weht tor nam-tor si' t' ish-veh yut do na' fanet. U' wuh zherka t' wuh kashek dungi sagluvau itself k'fai sovek covering t' wuh ak'shem, ni wuh paleness if ish-veh situation engendered sarlah k'fai wuh khav-kur fi-tor ish-veh nak, showing wuh soul tor nam-tor stronger do wuh yel. Au vesh' vathru ved shal-ma, ovalau tor wuh judge, heh lam-tor hizhuk. Wuh wihfelau t' eku'ko k' if nash sasu vesh' nantau heh breathed na', vesh' ri wuh wihfelau ik ashenau humanity. Had au lam-tor svi' peril t' wuh lehkuh horrible zhit-bal--had tra' vesh' wuh pavesh t' sovek veh t' its savage details hasu spared--k' aishan ni mau would au ma pakik svi' ish-veh sem. Wuh shid ik vesh' tor nam-tor doomed tor nam-tor ni shamefully mangled, vesh' wuh glan; wuh immortal creature ik vesh' tor nam-tor ni butchered heh torn asunder, yielded wuh kashan. Whatever gloss wuh vuhnauk spectators shitau fi-tor wuh eku'ko, fupa s' ish-veh several arts heh tepul t' shal-tehs, wuh eku'ko vesh', na' wuh gir t' ish-veh, ogreish. Silence svi' wuh kelek! Charles darnay had za-gad pleaded ri guilty tor wuh indictment denouncing ish-veh (k' vaik jingle heh jangle) na' ik au vesh' wuh riyeht traitor tor etwel serene, illustrious, marom, heh ni forth, prince, etwel s'haile wuh sa-te'kru, k' utvau t' ish-veh having, fi' taulsu occasions, heh k' taulsu tvai heh yut, gol-tor lewis, wuh french sa-te'kru, svi' ish-veh t'naehm tehnat etwel leralmin-tor serene, illustrious, marom, heh ni forth; ik vesh' tor leralmin, k' coming heh going, svi' wuh dominions t' etwel leralmin-tor serene, illustrious, marom, heh ni forth, heh eifa t' wuh leralmin-tor french lewis, heh wickedly, falsely, traitorously, heh vathru ek'rasah-adverbiously, revealing tor wuh leralmin-tor french lewis ra nekwitau etwel leralmin-tor serene, illustrious, marom, heh ni forth, had svi' preparation tor satau tor canada heh desh'rak america. Nash mau, jerry, k' ish-veh patam becoming weht heh weht spiky u' wuh tor-gav zhil bristled ish-veh, tor si' k' masuk' satisfaction, heh ni lasha circuitously na' wuh understanding ik wuh aforesaid, heh abru' heh abru' va'ashiv aforesaid, charles darnay, lam-tor tra' fa' ish-veh fi-tor ish-veh trial; ik wuh jury vesh' swearing svi'; heh ik mr. Attorney-paik vesh' tor pok tor stariben. Wuh accused, vi vesh' (heh vi fai-tor au vesh') hasu mentally geldau, beheaded, heh quartered, k' kanok-veh tra', neither flinched s' wuh situation, il assumed sovek theatrical sov svi' ish-veh. Au vesh' hizhuk heh whio'naks; glantau wuh sharu proceedings k' wuh shi'vukhut eku'ko; heh lam-tor k' ish-veh el'ru resting fi' wuh slab t' lapan fa' ish-veh, ni composedly, ik au had ri sa'dvun-tor wuh mor t' wuh bar-got k' if ish-veh vesh' strewn. Wuh kelek vesh' ek' bestrewn k' bar-got heh sprinkled k' sfith-masu, u' wuh precaution tehnat gaol sov heh gaol tau. Abru' wuh prisoner's patam tra' vesh' wuh haulat, tor lehm wuh ta'hal ne' fi-tor ish-veh. Patreitan t' wuh wicked heh wuh wretched had vesh' haul-tor svi' ish-veh, heh had be' dvun-tor s' its skonn heh nash terra's teretuhr. Haunted svi' wuh danik ghastly manner ik abominable shi would ma vesh', kuv wuh makh kupi ek'wak ma rendered pla' its haulan, u' wuh masutra nam-tor veh gad tor mazhiv-kur-tor abru its tevik. Ein be' dvun-tor nahp t' wuh infamy heh disgrace na' if ish-veh had vesh' reserved, lau ma kwul-tor wuh prisoner's kashek. Nam-tor ik u' ish-veh lau, wuh rubah svi' ish-veh shul tor ish-veh d'wonil t' wuh mofek t' ta'hal mes' ish-veh limuk, au glazhau abru; heh lu gla-tor ish-veh wuh makh ish-veh limuk kluhvau, heh ish-veh gas'rak el'ru kwitau wuh bar-got maf. Ish-veh pavesh-tor, ik wuh torai da-tor ish-veh limuk tor ik vla t' wuh kelek if vesh' fi' ish-veh losrak. Pa' fi' wuh volik k' ish-veh bezhun, tra' hayal-tor, svi' ik teruk t' wuh judge's wu-ku-san, dahkuh persons fi-tor ik ish-veh glazhau iyi shom-tor; ni iyi, heh ni mau tor wuh rubai t' ish-veh pulva, ik ek' wuh bezhun ik vesh' da-tor fi-tor ish-veh, da-tor tor au. Wuh spectators gla-tor svi' wuh dahkuh khlop, wuh nu'ri t'sai t' pi' weht do dah-leh, heh wuh gentleman vi vesh' evidently ish-veh sa-mekh; wuh sasu t' wuh maut remarkable appearance svi' respect t' wuh ek'esik whiteness t' ish-veh isachya, heh wuh ac'ruth indescribable flan'es t' limuk: ri t' wuh torupik ves, tonk'peh pondering heh shal-communing. Lu nash sagluvaya vesh' fi-tor ish-veh, au glazhau u' kuv au vesh' hinek; tonk'peh lu ish-veh vesh' stirred heh pushau abru--u' ish-veh vesh' i', svi' wuh moment, fi' ish-veh speaking tor ish-veh ko-fu--au became wuh handsome sasu, ri vesht wuh nenat t' ha'kiv. Ish-veh ko-fu had veh t' ish-veh el'ru drawn k'fai ish-veh kar, u' she hayal-tor k' ish-veh, heh wuh vath hish-tor fi-tor ish-veh. She had drawn beyik ish-veh, svi' ish-veh dread t' wuh scene, heh svi' ish-veh pity na' wuh prisoner. Ish-veh fa-patam had vesh' strikingly expressive t' wuh engrossing vash heh utan'es ik gla-tor nothing tonk'peh wuh peril t' wuh accused. Nash had vesh' ni maut noticeable, ni maut powerfully heh naturally shown, ik starers vi had had rai pity na' ish-veh vesh' estuhl k' ish-veh; heh wuh zhal went pa', "vi nam-tor au?" jerry, wuh skladasu, vi had tor ish-veh sha' glantaya, svi' ish-veh sha' manner, heh vi had vesh' sucking wuh zhar ska' ish-veh ozh svi' ish-veh vi-seshaya, sakadau ish-veh talu tor zhu-tor vi au vesh'. Wuh patreitan pa' ish-veh had hish-tor heh be' dvun-tor wuh inquiry fi' tor wuh nearest attendant, heh s' ish-veh ish-veh had vesh' weht slowly hish-tor heh be' dvun-tor pla'; na' kim-shah ish-veh prah tor jerry: "toglantausu." "na' if vla?" "tehnat." "tehnat ra vla?" "wuh prisoner's." wuh judge, t'vi bezhun had hal-tor svi' wuh paik kharat, recalled au, gal-tor pla' svi' ish-veh ku-san, heh glazhau steadily na' wuh sasu t'vi ha'kiv vesh' svi' ish-veh el'ru, u' mr. Attorney-paik she-tor tor padan wuh man-elakh, grazhau wuh la'ash, heh mah-vel wuh felu vi' wuh scaffold. Chapter iii. Wuh disappointment mr. Attorney-paik had tor inform wuh jury, ik wuh prisoner fa' au, hi nu'ri svi' tevun, vesh' hinek svi' wuh treasonable practices if claimed wuh forfeit t' ish-veh ha'kiv. Ik nash correspondence k' wuh tsuri nemut vesh' ri wuh correspondence t' tor-gad, il t' za-gad, il kauk t' kim-shah tevun, il t' wuh tevun fa'. Ik, ish-veh vesh' ac'ruth wuh prisoner had, na' longer do ik, vesh' svi' wuh es'merka t' be' dvun-tor heh repassing svi' france heh england, fi' tsat business t' if au kupi mazhiv-kur-tor rai trau khrosahp. Ik, kuv ish-veh vesh' svi' wuh malat t' traitorous yut tor smusma (if kunling ish-veh worla vesh'), wuh yeht wickedness heh guilt t' ish-veh business lau ma hafau undiscovered. Ik providence, however, had shitau ish-veh vi' wuh khaf-spol t' wuh person vi vesh' mesakh pthak heh mesakh reproach, tor ferret si' wuh malat t' wuh prisoner's schemes, heh, kwul-tor k' horror, tor disclose au tor ish-veh majesty's chief secretary t' fupa s' heh danik dorli privy shikh-orna. Ik, nash patriot would nam-tor torvau fa' au. Ik, ish-veh shul heh attitude vesh', fi' wuh bosh, sublime. Ik, au had vesh' wuh prisoner's t'hy'la, tonk'peh, na' wuh'wak svi' wuh auspicious heh wuh ek'rasah wadan detecting ish-veh infamy, had resolved tor immolate wuh traitor au kupi rai longer tishau svi' ish-veh bosom, fi' wuh sacred altar t' ish-veh shasol. Ik, kuv sukhlop vesh' decreed svi' britain, u' svi' t'kahr greece heh rome, tor tsuri benefactors, nash shining citizen would assuredly ma had veh. Ik, u' au vesh' ri ni decreed, au probably would ri ma veh. Ik, virtue, u' had vesh' glantau k' wuh poets (svi' wehk tvur if au muhl fai-tor wuh jury would ma, zhit na' zhit, na' wuh um t' ish-veh lahv; whereat wuh jury's countenances gluvaya wuh guilty hokni'es ik au fai-tor nothing pa' wuh tvur), vesh' svi' wuh manner contagious; weht wa' wuh ugelik virtue fainu u' patriotism, il ashaya t' shasol. Ik, wuh lofty li-fal t' nash immaculate heh unimpeachable toglantausu na' wuh tarkiv, tor dzhinau tor ik however unworthily vesh' wuh dor, had sviribau itself tor wuh prisoner's dvinsu, heh had engendered svi' ish-veh wuh vai determination tor linisau ish-veh trensu's pasu-zish-nef heh abru'lik, heh secrete ish-veh dun. Ik, au (mr. Attorney-paik) vesh' dator tor zhu-tor ein disparagement attempted t' nash admirable dvinsu; tonk'peh ik, svi' wuh paik yut, au preferred ish-veh tor ish-veh (mr. Attorney-paik's) sa-kai heh ko-kai, heh pudor-tor ish-veh weht do ish-veh (mr. Attorney-paik's) sa-mekh heh ko-mekh. Ik, au puvutau k' guhl'es fi' wuh jury tor sarlah heh tor likewise. Ik, wuh evidence t' aifa dahkuh toglantausu, coupled k' wuh kisev t' ish-veh discovering ik would nam-tor torvau, would gluvaya wuh prisoner ki' vesh' furnished k' feim-tor t' ish-veh majesty's nekwitau, heh t' ish-veh disposition heh preparation, fi' k' masutra heh solektra, heh would trasha rai vet ik au had habitually zhelesh such ro'fori tor wuh hostile tepul. Ik, aifa feim-tor kupi ri nam-tor skan-tor tor nam-tor svi' wuh prisoner's handwriting; tonk'peh ik ish-veh vesh' ek' wuh ka; ik, indeed, ish-veh vesh' rather wuh weh-rom na' wuh prosecution, u' showing wuh prisoner tor nam-tor artful svi' ish-veh precautions. Ik, wuh skan would hal-tor pla' kaukuh tevun, heh would gluvaya wuh prisoner already engaged svi' aifa pernicious skrol, k'svi wuh zamu wehk gad fa' wuh kinuf t' wuh maut wuh'rak torai fought svi' wuh british vus heh wuh americans. Ik, na' aifa utvau, wuh jury, hasu wuh fonn jury (u' au fai-tor au vesh'), heh hasu wuh responsible jury (u' au fai-tor au vesh'), bolau positively talal wuh prisoner guilty, heh tor wuh shaht t' ish-veh, whether au tishau ish-veh il ri. Ik, au worla kupi ti ish-veh patam fi-tor ish-veh trak; ik, au worla kupi wivelau wuh idea t' ish-veh ko-telsu laying ish-veh patam fi-tor ish-veh trak; ik, au worla kupi palesh-tor wuh notion t' ish-veh kanu laying ish-veh patam fi-tor ish-veh trak; svi' pen, ik tra' worla weht kupi nam-tor, na' au il ish-veh, sovek laying t' patam fi-tor trak na' ek', vita wuh prisoner's patam vesh' taken ska'. Ik patam mr. Attorney-paik concluded k' demanding t' au, svi' wuh ahm t' kanok-vei au kupi nah-tor t' k' wuh pauk da-tor svi' ish-veh, heh fi' wuh odva t' ish-veh solemn asseveration ik au already panah-tor wuh prisoner u' rom u' tevik heh hal-tor. Lu wuh attorney-paik ceased, wuh buzz arose svi' wuh kelek u' kuv wuh wan t' lo'uk pla-kur-hash-tor vesh' swarming pa' wuh prisoner, svi' anticipation t' ra au vesh' ak tor shetau. Lu toned ne' va'ashiv, wuh unimpeachable patriot saudau svi' wuh toglantausu-natuhn. Mr. Solicitor-paik yi, zahalik ish-veh leader's ras-tukh, linisau wuh patriot: john barsad, gentleman, k' ahm. Wuh var t' ish-veh pure soul vesh' exactly ra mr. Attorney-paik had kethelvau ish-veh tor nam-tor--sos'eh, kuv ish-veh had wuh lafot, wuh pi' nuh' exactly. Having sadalau ish-veh thol bosom t' its burden, au would ma modestly saseshau himself, tonk'peh ik wuh wigged gentleman k' wuh dun fa' ish-veh, sitting ri irak s' mr. Lorry, eit'jae tor ya'akash ish-veh wuh zamu deshkau. Wuh wigged gentleman sitting mesyutik, fam dvun looking na' wuh abru-tol t' wuh kelek. Had au ek'wak vesh' wuh zamasu himself? Rai, au scorned wuh nen insinuation. Ra did au ha-tor fi-tor? Ish-veh veltra. Wilat vesh' ish-veh veltra? Au didn't precisely vokau wilat ish-veh vesh'. Ra vesh' ish-veh? Rai business t' anybody's. Had au inherited ish-veh? Ha, au had. S' ik? Irak relation. Maut irak? Rather. Ek'wak vesh' svi' prison? Certainly ri. Worla svi' wuh debtors' prison? Didn't gla-tor ra ik had tor tor k' ish-veh. Worla svi' wuh debtors' prison?--sarlah, wuh'wak va'ashiv. Worla? Ha. Uf wehk wak? Dahkuh il rehkuh wak. Ri kaukuh il shehkuh? Sos'eh. T' ra ha'yigal? Gentleman. Ek'wak vesh' kicked? Lau ma vesh'. Frequently? Rai. Ek'wak kicked downstairs? Decidedly ri; wuh'wak poprah wuh kick fi' wuh fik t' wuh staircase, heh tevan-tor downstairs t' ish-veh sha' accord. Kicked fi' ik occasion na' cheating na' dice? Vel tor ik daya vesh' leralmin-tor k' wuh intoxicated liar vi committed wuh assault, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' ri yeht. Swear ish-veh vesh' ri yeht? Positively. Ek'wak ha-tor k' cheating na' mavau? Worla. Ek'wak ha-tor k' mavau? Ri weht do vath gentlemen tor. Ek'wak yahv-tor donku t' wuh prisoner? Ha. Ek'wak vlitau ish-veh? Rai. Vesh' ri nash intimacy k' wuh prisoner, svi' reality wuh maut slight veh, punekwitau fi-tor wuh prisoner svi' coaches, ha-shal, heh packets? Rai. Sure gla-tor ish-veh wuh prisoner k' aifa feim-tor? Ac'ruth. Fai-tor rai weht pa' wuh feim-tor? Rai. Had ri procured au himself, na' instance? Rai. Gish tor prah sovek-vel k' nash evidence? Rai. Ri svi' regular government vlitau heh employment, tor ti pash-tor? Oh tal-kam rai. Il tor tor sovek-vel? Oh tal-kam rai. Swear ik? Abru' heh abru' va'ashiv. Rai dvubolek tonk'peh dvubolek t' sheer patriotism? Rim whatever. Wuh virtuous dvinsu, roger cly, swore ish-veh yut k'fai wuh nuf na' wuh lo'uk tav. Au had taken dvin k' wuh prisoner, svi' rom odva heh simplicity, kehkuh tevun ago. Au had ya'akash wuh prisoner, aboard wuh calais packet, kuv au aitlu wuh handy katravahsu, heh wuh prisoner had engaged ish-veh. Au had ri ya'akash wuh prisoner tor nem-tor wuh handy katravahsu u' wuh bae'cok t' charity--worla nahp t' such wuh vel. Au began ki' suspicions t' wuh prisoner, heh tor potau wuh bezhun fi-tor ish-veh, ak afterwards. Svi' arranging ish-veh sai-vel, du' travelling, au had gla-tor kahwa feim-tor tor aifa svi' wuh prisoner's abru'lik, abru' heh abru' va'ashiv. Au had taken aifa feim-tor s' wuh zish-nef t' wuh prisoner's kitau-skaf. Au had ri shitau au tra' wuh'rak. Au had gla-tor wuh prisoner gluvaya aifa ka feim-tor tor french gentlemen na' calais, heh kahwa feim-tor tor french gentlemen, fi' na' calais heh boulogne. Au ashau ish-veh shasol, heh couldn't lesh ish-veh, heh had putan-tor ro'fori. Au had worla vesh' suspected t' stealing wuh haul-tukh theris-masu-sunil; au had vesh' maligned respecting wuh mustard-sunil, tonk'peh ish-veh da-tor si' tor nam-tor goh wuh slau-tor veh. Au had fainu wuh kim-shah toglantausu stehkuh il ohkuh tevun; ik vesh' goh wuh coincidence. Au didn't vutau ish-veh wuh wa' curious coincidence; danik coincidences vesh' curious. Neither did au vutau ish-veh wuh curious coincidence ik yeht patriotism vesh' ish-veh goh dvubolek nuh'. Au vesh' wuh yeht briton, heh rok-tor tra' vesh' wehk spo' ish-veh. Wuh igen-va vesh' stormy, heh wuh tvur wu heh rough, heh i ti fi' wuh ku-san, siyah s' gef tor gef." "din-tor manette!" wuh nu'ri t'sai, tor ik ek' bezhun had vesh' da-tor fa', heh vesh' i' da-tor va'ashiv, lam-tor abru wilat she had hayal-tor. Ish-veh sa-mekh she-tor k' ish-veh, heh potau ish-veh el'ru drawn k'fai ish-veh kar. "din-tor manette, glazhau fi-tor wuh prisoner." tor nam-tor nagau k' such pity, heh such earnest youth heh vaksur, vesh' irak weht trying tor wuh accused do tor nam-tor nagau k' ek' wuh patreitan. Standing, u' ish-veh vesh', k'wuhli k' ish-veh fi' wuh rihk t' ish-veh shi'vukhut, ri ek' wuh staring curiosity ik glazhau fi', kupi, na' wuh moment, tor'tsu ish-veh tor hafau ved fam dvun. T'nash-veh sa-mekh vesh' ni netakidau ik i vesh' kwes tor nem-tor ish-veh s' wuh sov, heh i had tor wuh sar-tak na' ish-veh fi' wuh lan-tol be' wuh thif'etek ash-tor, heh i hayal-tor fi' wuh lan-tol na' ish-veh vla tor nem-tor tun t' ish-veh. Sanoi tor hal-tor fi'." "au var-tor me ik au vesh' travelling fi' business t' wuh delicate heh rihagik malat, if lau prah sutra vi' trouble, heh ik au vesh' therefore travelling ne' wuh assumed ahm. "au ar'kada tor danau tor me uf ik quarrel had arisen, heh au leralmin-tor ik, ni irak u' au kupi judge, ish-veh vesh' wuh riyeht heh duhik veh fi' england's krus. Au hau, svi' wuh jesting yut, ik sos'eh george washington lau nazh-kap siyah u' lo'uk wuh ahm svi' vesht-var u' george wuh wuh. Tonk'peh tra' vesh' rai klau svi' ish-veh yut t' taran nash: ish-veh vesh' leralmin-tor laughingly, heh tor beguile wuh wak." sovek strongly pu'ulidau sagluvaya t' limuk fi' wuh krus t' wuh chief fundauik-ithop svi' wuh scene t' lo'uk eku'ko tor ik wehk bezhun nam-tor khartau, dungi nam-tor unconsciously va'amau k' wuh spectators. Ish-veh fa-patam vesh' painfully anxious heh intent u' she mazhiv-kur-tor nash evidence, heh, svi' wuh svizh-tor lu she pehkau na' wuh judge tor kitau ish-veh ne', glantau its daya fi-tor wuh counsel na' heh tehnat. Among wuh lookers-fi' tra' vesh' wuh ka sagluvaya svi' ek' ha-shal t' wuh kelek; insomuch, ik wuh lo'uk majority t' wuh fa-patam tra', lau ma vesh' haulat reflecting wuh toglantausu, lu wuh judge glazhau abru s' ish-veh pitoh tor glare na' ik tremendous heresy pa' george washington. Mr. Attorney-paik i' signified tor t'nash-veh s'haile, ik au deemed ish-veh bolayatik, u' wuh tukh t' precaution heh shid, tor vutau wuh nu'ri t'sai's sa-mekh, hassu manette. Vi vesh' puvutau accordingly. "hassu manette, glazhau fi-tor wuh prisoner. Ma du ek'wak gla-tor ish-veh fa'?" "wuh'wak. Lu au puvutau na' t'nash-veh lodgings svi' london. Ein rehkuh tevun, il rehkuh tevun heh wuh ulef ago." "mokuhlek du shasutan-tor ish-veh u' ish-veh katravahsu-passenger fi' dohn wuh packet, il stariben tor ish-veh conversation k' ish-veh ko-fu?" "osu, i mokuhlek tor neither." "nam-tor tra' sovek particular heh special utvau na' ish-veh hasu unable tor tor either?" au kilko-tor, svi' wuh neik spes, "tra' nam-tor." "has ish-veh vesh' ish-veh misfortune tor undergo wuh wu imprisonment, rik' trial, il kauk accusation, svi' ish-veh salatik shasol, hassu manette?" au kilko-tor, svi' wuh molu ik went tor kanok khaf-spol, "wuh wu imprisonment." "vesh' du newly sadalau fi' wuh occasion svi' deshker?" "au var-tor me ni." "ma du rai remembrance t' wuh occasion?" "rim. T'nash-veh kashek nam-tor wuh blank, s' ein wak--i fam yehat kauk leralmin ra wak--lu i employed myself, svi' t'nash-veh captivity, svi' tor ash'el, tor wuh wak lu i afer-tor myself living svi' london k' t'nash-veh tal-kam ko-fu la'. She had shetau familiar tor me, lu wuh gracious oekon restored t'nash-veh sutra; tonk'peh, i am ved unable kauk tor leralmin uf she had shetau familiar. I ma rai remembrance t' wuh torek." mr. Attorney-paik hayal-tor ne', heh wuh sa-mekh heh ko-fu hayal-tor ne' teretuhr. Wuh singular circumstance yi arose svi' wuh nuf. Wuh vel svi' el'ru hasu tor gluvaya ik wuh prisoner went ne', k' ein katravahsu-besayek untracked, svi' wuh dover sakat fi' ik gad mu-yor svi' november kaukuh tevun ago, heh prah s' wuh sakat svi' wuh mu-yor, u' wuh glan-fam, na' wuh shi wilat au did ri hafau, tonk'peh s' if au travelled pla' ein dozen miles il weht, tor wuh shi'ask'ersu heh dockyard, heh tra' tershau ro'fori; wuh toglantausu vesh' puvutau tor shasutan-tor ish-veh u' having vesh' na' wuh precise wak required, svi' wuh mon-tvi-shal t' wuh hotel svi' ik shi'ask'ersu-heh-dockyard kahr, waiting na' wuh'ashiv person. Wuh prisoner's counsel vesh' tuhs-examining nash toglantausu k' rai result, kaula ik au had worla gla-tor wuh prisoner fi' sovek vath occasion, lu wuh wigged gentleman vi had ek' nash wak vesh' looking na' wuh abru-tol t' wuh kelek, kitau wuh zhit il dahkuh fi' wuh pi' krus t' dun, screwed ish-veh abru, heh tossed ish-veh tor ish-veh. Sharu nash krus t' dun svi' wuh thurai svizh, wuh counsel glazhau k' lo'uk attention heh curiosity na' wuh prisoner. "du leralmin va'ashiv du nam-tor ved sure ik ish-veh vesh' wuh prisoner?" wuh toglantausu vesh' ved sure. "did du ek'wak gla-tor anybody maut spo' wuh prisoner?" ri ni spo' (wuh toglantausu leralmin-tor) u' ik au kupi nam-tor mistaken. "glazhau muhl fi-tor ik gentleman, t'nash-veh oren-tor t'hy'la tra', " pointing tor ish-veh vi had tossed wuh dun abru', "heh yi glazhau muhl fi-tor wuh prisoner. Uf leralmin du? Nam-tor au maut spo' tik vath?" allowing na' t'nash-veh oren-tor t'hy'la's appearance hasu careless heh slovenly kuv ri debauched, au vesh' sufficiently spo' tik vath tor ak'wikmun, ri goh wuh toglantausu, tonk'peh kanok-veh la', lu au vesh' thus katau vi' comparison. T'nash-veh s'haile hasu prayed tor nufai t'nash-veh oren-tor t'hy'la ti aside ish-veh wig, heh giving rai maut gracious consent, wuh likeness became mau weht remarkable. T'nash-veh s'haile inquired t' mr. Stryver (wuh prisoner's counsel), whether au vesh' nam-tor' ar'kadan mr. Carton (ahm t' t'nash-veh oren-tor t'hy'la) na' kam'nat? Tonk'peh, mr. Stryver kilko-tor tor t'nash-veh s'haile, rai; tonk'peh au would ya'akash wuh toglantausu tor var-tor ish-veh whether ra pavesh-tor wuh'wak, lau pavesh-tor dah'wak; whether au would ma vesh' ni confident kuv au had gla-tor nash illustration t' ish-veh rashness sooner, whether au would nam-tor ni confident, having gla-tor ish-veh; heh weht. Wuh upshot t' if, vesh', tor smash nash toglantausu spo' wuh crockery hali, heh shiver ish-veh krus t' wuh nuf tor nam-tor-fam lumber. Mr. Cruncher had k' nash wak taken ved wuh khi-gad-yem t' zhar ska' ish-veh ozh svi' ish-veh zahalik t' wuh evidence. Au had i' tor attend du' mr. Stryver fitted wuh prisoner's nuf fi' wuh jury, spo' wuh lerakhovau saikhut t' sai-vel; showing au uf wuh patriot, barsad, vesh' wuh hired zamasu heh traitor, wuh unblushing trafficker svi' khaf, heh veh t' wuh greatest scoundrels fi-tor terra opi' accursed judas--if au certainly did glazhau rather spo'. Uf wuh virtuous dvinsu, cly, vesh' ish-veh t'hy'la heh tersu, heh vesh' worthy tor nam-tor; uf wuh tun-tor bezhun t' eifa forgers heh riyeht swearers had shom-tor fi' wuh prisoner u' wuh shi-kar-tor, fai'ei ein skan tek'ik svi' france, au hasu t' french saseshaya, did require ish-veh tor eifa tvur mes' wuh mashyut--hi ra eifa tek'ik vesh', wuh consideration na' vath vi vesh' be' heh tal-kam tor ish-veh, forbade ish-veh, kauk na' ish-veh ha'kiv, tor disclose. Uf wuh evidence ik had vesh' warped heh wrested s' wuh nu'ri t'sai, t'vi thonaya svi' giving ish-veh au had toglantau, sarlah tor nothing, involving wuh mere pi' innocent gallantries heh politenesses kesik tor be' dvun svi' sovek nu'ri gentleman heh nu'ri t'sai ni lehm-tor teretuhr; --k' wuh kaulauf t' ik dzhinaya tor george washington, if vesh' altogether nuh' madonik heh impossible tor nam-tor fudau svi' sovek vath ta'hal do u' wuh monstrous kha'wal. Uf ish-veh would nam-tor wuh kobat'es svi' wuh government tor shaya ne' svi' nash attempt tor practise na' popularity fi' wuh lowest national antipathies heh ptha, heh therefore mr. Attorney-paik had tor wuh danik t' ish-veh; uf, nevertheless, ish-veh shom-tor fi-tor nothing, korsau ik vile heh infamous character t' evidence nuh' k'ashiv disfiguring such nuf, heh t' if wuh fupa s' trials t' nash shasol vesh' bosh. Tonk'peh, tra' t'nash-veh s'haile interposed (k' u' shi'vukhut wuh limuk u' kuv ish-veh had ri vesh' yeht), taran ik au kupi ri hayal-tor fi-tor ik wu-ku-san heh dash eifa allusions. Mr. Stryver yi puvutau ish-veh zamu toglantausu, heh mr. Cruncher had nam-tor' attend du' mr. Attorney-paik da-tor wuh bosh saikhut t' sai-vel mr. Stryver had fitted fi' wuh jury, svi'udish si'; showing uf barsad heh cly vesh' kauk wuh hundred wak weh-rom do au had nahp au, heh wuh prisoner wuh hundred wak weh-rasahkos. Lastly, sarlah t'nash-veh s'haile himself, turning wuh saikhut t' sai-vel, i' svi'udish si', i' s'udish svi', tonk'peh fi' wuh bosh decidedly trimming heh shaping au vi' shi'vukhut-sai-vel na' wuh prisoner. Heh i', wuh jury da-tor tor panah-tor, heh wuh lo'uk hash-tor bishau va'ashiv. Mr. Carton, vi had ni wu hayal-tor looking na' wuh abru-tol t' wuh kelek, rubai neither ish-veh shi il ish-veh attitude, kauk svi' nash tepor'es. Du' ish-veh oren-tor t'hy'la, mr. Stryver, massing ish-veh dun fa' ish-veh, zhal-tor k' eifa vi hayal-tor be', heh s' wak tor wak glanced anxiously na' wuh jury; du' ek' wuh spectators dvun-tor weht il lehkuh, heh grouped themselves anew; du' kauk t'nash-veh s'haile himself arose s' ish-veh ku-san, heh slowly sahr-tor abru heh ne' ish-veh skaf, ri unattended k' wuh suspicion svi' wuh kashkau t' wuh audience ik ish-veh fupa s' vesh' taulik; nash-veh sasu hayal-tor leaning pla', k' ish-veh torn gown ulef ska' ish-veh, ish-veh untidy wig shitau fi' aishan u' ish-veh had pavesh-tor tor ta'hal fi' ish-veh patam po' its removal, ish-veh el'ru svi' ish-veh abru'lik, heh ish-veh bezhun fi' wuh abru-tol u' au had vesh' ek' gad. Vel wa' reckless svi' ish-veh demeanour, ri goh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh disreputable glazhau, tonk'peh ni nelau wuh karik resemblance au undoubtedly spitau tor wuh prisoner (if ish-veh momentary earnestness, lu au vesh' tcok'at teretuhr, had strengthened), ik wehk t' wuh lookers-fi', taking pitoh t' ish-veh i', leralmin-tor tor veh wuh'ashiv au would hardly ma nahp wuh dahkuh vesh' ni kahkwa. Mr. Cruncher tor wuh glantaya tor ish-veh thurai behsu, heh hau, "i'd meskaraya ulef wuh guinea ik au ri tor prah rai tor-gav-ar'kadan tor tor. Ri tor glazhau spo' wuh wihfelau t' veh tor prah sovek, tor au?" wi, nash mr. Carton nem-tor svi' weht t' wuh details t' wuh scene do au saudau tor nem-tor svi'; na' i', lu din-tor manette's patam eku-tor fi-tor ish-veh sa-mekh's thasek, au vesh' wuh wuh'rak tor gla-tor ish-veh, heh tor leralmin audibly: "officer! Glazhau tor ik nu'ri t'sai. Gol'nev wuh gentleman tor nem-tor ish-veh si'. Ri tor gla-tor du she dungi tevan!" tra' vesh' mau commiseration na' ish-veh u' she vesh' snem-tor, heh mau sympathy k' ish-veh sa-mekh. Ish-veh had evidently vesh' wuh lo'uk flakosh tor ish-veh, ki' wuh gad t' ish-veh imprisonment recalled. Au had shown karik internal agitation lu au vesh' deshkau, heh ik pondering il brooding glazhau if tor ish-veh hinek, had vesh' fi-tor ish-veh, spo' wuh ras wan, ek'wak opi'. U' au be' dvun-tor si', wuh jury, vi had da-tor pla' heh svizh-tor wuh moment, stariben, k'fai ish-veh zup-fulagsu. Au vesh' ri sep-wafikh, heh istau tor retire. T'nash-veh s'haile (sos'eh k' george washington fi' ish-veh kashek) gluvau ein ak'wikmun ik au vesh' ri sep-wafikh, tonk'peh signified ish-veh sanosh ik au dang retire ne' glantau heh ward, heh retired himself. Wuh trial had palesh-tor ek' gad, heh wuh ha'gelek svi' wuh kelek vesh' i' hasu lighted. Ish-veh began tor nam-tor rumoured ik wuh jury would nam-tor si' wuh wu du'. Wuh spectators eku-tor ska' tor prah refreshment, heh wuh prisoner withdrew tor wuh pla' t' wuh kif, heh hayal-tor ne'. Mr. Lorry, vi had hal-tor si' lu wuh nu'ri t'sai heh ish-veh sa-mekh went si', i' reappeared, heh beckoned tor jerry: vi, svi' wuh slackened eku'ko, kupi easily prah be' ish-veh. "jerry, kuv du istaya tor nem-tor vel tor yokul, du mokuhlek. Tonk'peh, potau svi' wuh yut. Du dungi nam-tor sure tor zhu-tor lu wuh jury sarlah svi'. Ri tor nam-tor wuh moment za' au, na' i aitlun du tor nem-tor wuh verdict pla' tor wuh kutra. Du nam-tor wuh quickest skladasu i fai-tor, heh dungi prah tor temple mofek wu fa' i mokuhlek." jerry had aishan hiyet fa-patam tor ozh-lesek, heh au knuckled ish-veh svi' acknowledgment t' nash sviribaya heh wuh shilling. Mr. Carton sarlah abru na' wuh moment, heh estuhl mr. Lorry fi' wuh kar. "uf nam-tor wuh nu'ri t'sai?" "she nam-tor greatly flakosh; tonk'peh ish-veh sa-mekh nam-tor comforting ish-veh, heh she olau wuh weh-rom na' hasu s' kelek." "i'll var-tor wuh prisoner ni. Ish-veh skil-tor't tor na' wuh respectable kutra gentleman spo' du, tor nam-tor gla-tor speaking tor ish-veh publicly, du fai-tor." mr. Lorry reddened u' kuv au vesh' d'wonil t' having debated wuh sfek svi' ish-veh kashek, heh mr. Carton tor ish-veh yut tor wuh si' wuh mofek. Wuh yut s' kelek ti svi' ik kharat, heh jerry zahal-tor ish-veh, ek' bezhun, kaluk, heh spikes. "mr. Darnay!" wuh prisoner sarlah fa'rak directly. "du dungi naturally nam-tor anxious tor zhu-tor t' wuh toglantausu, din-tor manette. She dungi tor maut muhl. Du ma gla-tor wuh rasahkos t' ish-veh agitation." "i am deeply sorry ki' vesh' wuh aishan t' ish-veh. Kupi du var-tor ish-veh ni na' me, k' t'nash-veh fervent acknowledgments?" "ha, i kupi. I dungi, kuv du ya'akash ish-veh." mr. Carton's manner vesh' ni careless u' tor nam-tor siyah insolent. Au lam-tor, ulef da-tor s' wuh prisoner, lounging k' ish-veh kar-nef tehnat wuh mofek. "i tor ya'akash ish-veh. Nar-tor t'nash-veh cordial itaren." "ra, " leralmin-tor carton, fam dvun goh ulef da-tor na' ish-veh, "tor du gish, mr. Darnay?" "wuh rasahkos." "ish-veh's wuh wisest vel tor gish, heh wuh likeliest. Tonk'peh i nah-tor ish-veh withdrawing nam-tor svi' ish-veh favour." loitering fi' wuh yut s' kelek ri hasu kal-tor, jerry puzhu-tor rai weht: tonk'peh losrak au--ni spo' tik vath svi' feature, ni rikes tik vath svi' manner--standing vla k' vla, fi' haul-tor svi' wuh makh abru' au. Wuh wadan heh wuh ulef limped heavily maf svi' wuh pi'tak-heh-rascal crowded tvur ne', kauk hi gol-tor ska' k' mutton pies heh ale. Wuh hoarse skladasu, uncomfortably hayal-tor fi' wuh shid po' taking ik refection, had eku-tor vi' wuh doze, lu wuh ral murmur heh wuh rapid mashen t' sutra setting abru wuh kaiden ik pufulag-tor tor wuh kelek, lesh ish-veh bi' k' au. "jerry! Jerry!" mr. Lorry vesh' already calling na' wuh svep lu au prah tra'. "la', osu! Ish-veh's wuh puk tor zaprah va'ashiv. La' i am, osu!" mr. Lorry handed ish-veh wuh dun k'fai wuh throng. "sahris! Ma du prah ish-veh?" "ha, osu." hastily written fi' wuh dun vesh' wuh zhit "acquitted." "kuv du had satau wuh skladan, 'recalled tor ha'kiv, ' va'ashiv, " muttered jerry, u' au da-tor, "i dang ma fainu ra du tvai, nash wak." au had rai opportunity t' taran, il ni mau u' thinking, sovek-kitok, abi' au vesh' pa'shik t' wuh hinek bailey; na', wuh patreitan sarlah pouring si' k' wuh vehemence ik nearly nem-tor ish-veh ska' ish-veh mal, heh wuh ral buzz swept vi' wuh yut u' kuv wuh hertak-tor pla-kur-hash-tor vesh' dispersing svi' psthan t' vath tevikeh. Chapter iv. Congratulatory s' wuh dimly-lighted tvur t' wuh kelek, wuh kim-shah ne'ti-tukh t' wuh komihn shur ik had vesh' boiling tra' ek' gad, vesh' straining ska', lu hassu manette, lucie manette, ish-veh ko-fu, mr. Lorry, wuh solicitor na' wuh defence, heh its counsel, mr. Stryver, lam-tor hoknau pauk mr. Charles darnay--aishan sadalau--congratulating ish-veh fi' ish-veh stron s' tevakh. Ish-veh would ma vesh' rihagik k' wuh irak brighter ta'hal, tor naglanshau svi' hassu manette, intellectual t' limuk heh abruvenik t' kuvish, wuh shoemaker t' wuh kamu-tvi-shal svi' paris. Wi, kling kupi ma glazhau na' ish-veh dah'wak, rik' looking va'ashiv: kauk hi wuh opportunity t' glantaya had ri sadvun-tor tor wuh mournful cadence t' ish-veh neik shi'vukhut spes, heh tor wuh abstraction ik overclouded ish-veh fitfully, rik' sovek apparent utvau.
