Du' veh sik aishan, heh ik wuh dzhinaya tor ish-veh wu svizh-tor agony, would kwon-hau-ov--u' fi' wuh trial--evoke nash nosh s' wuh gluder t' ish-veh soul, ish-veh vesh' isha svi' its malat tor arise t' itself, heh tor bes-tor wuh gloom abru' ish-veh, u' incomprehensible tor eifa unacquainted k' ish-veh var u' kuv au had gla-tor wuh duv t' wuh actual bastille lehm-tor fi-tor ish-veh k' wuh belaar yel, lu wuh substance vesh' rehkuh hundred miles maf. Goh ish-veh ko-fu had wuh tepul t' sem-rik-tor nash nesh-kur brooding s' ish-veh kashek. She vesh' wuh pi-maat-kur og-elakh ik kaunshuk ish-veh tor wuh vesht mesakh ish-veh misery, heh tor wuh la' mesakh ish-veh misery: heh wuh ralash t' ish-veh spes, wuh ta'hal t' ish-veh limuk, wuh esta t' ish-veh el'ru, had wuh karik beneficial vi-yumuk k' ish-veh siyah kwon-hau-ov. Ri absolutely kwon-hau-ov, na' she kupi recall ein occasions fi' if ish-veh tepul had vravshau; tonk'peh au vesh' zamu heh slight, heh she pudva-tor au abru'. Mr. Darnay had shok-tor ish-veh el'ru fervently heh gratefully, heh had da-tor tor mr. Stryver, ik au warmly itaren. Mr. Stryver, wuh sasu t' pi' weht do reh-leh, tonk'peh looking dah-leh tevun older do au vesh', stout, ral, yon-kur, bluff, heh elik s' sovek drawback t' delicacy, had wuh pushing yut t' shouldering himself (morally heh physically) vi' apc'koik heh conversations, ik gyirm'i muhl na' ish-veh shouldering ish-veh yut abru svi' ha'kiv. Au fam dvun had ish-veh wig heh gown fi', heh au leralmin-tor, squaring himself na' ish-veh tab-ma client tor ik degree ik au lerakhovau wuh innocent mr. Lorry sok'i s' wuh travek: "i am glad ki' katau du ska' k' dor, mr. Darnay. Ish-veh vesh' wuh infamous prosecution, grossly infamous; tonk'peh ri wuh lehkuh kesik tor navau fi' ik khrosahp." "du ma laid me ne' wuh obligation tor du na' ha'kiv--svi' dahkuh kash-ral, " leralmin-tor ish-veh tab-ma client, taking ish-veh el'ru. "i ma ovsoh t'nash-veh buhfik na' du, mr. Darnay; heh t'nash-veh buhfik nam-tor u' rom u' wuh'ashiv sasu's, i dva-tor." ish-veh clearly hasu incumbent fi' ein veh tor leralmin, "mau weh-rom, " mr. Lorry leralmin-tor ish-veh; sos'eh ri ved disinterestedly, tonk'peh k' wuh interested vel t' squeezing himself pla' va'ashiv. "du nah-tor ni?" leralmin-tor mr. Stryver. "muhl! Du ma vesh' la' ek' gad, heh du ought tor fai-tor. Du nam-tor wuh sasu t' business, nuh'." "heh u' such, " quoth mr. Lorry, ik wuh counsel oren-tor svi' wuh tor-gav had i' shouldered pla' vi' wuh travek, aishan u' au had previously shouldered ish-veh s' ish-veh--"u' such i dungi appeal tor hassu manette, tor shaya abru nash conference heh zek etek ek' tor etwel ha-kel. Din-tor lucie glazhau has-bosh, mr. Darnay has had wuh terrible gad, etek nam-tor worn si'." "stariben na' yourself, mr. Lorry, " leralmin-tor stryver; "i ma wuh mu-yor's ar'kadan tor tor wi. Stariben na' yourself." "i stariben na' myself, " kilko-tor mr. Lorry, "heh na' mr. Darnay, heh na' din-tor lucie, heh--din-tor lucie, tor du ri nah-tor i lau stariben na' etek ek'?" au ya'akash ish-veh wuh deshker pointedly, heh k' wuh glance na' ish-veh sa-mekh. Ish-veh limuk had shetau le-sumalik, u' ish-veh vesh', svi' wuh maut curious glazhau na' darnay: wuh intent glazhau, deepening vi' wuh kwal t' ritishaya heh distrust, ri kauk unmixed k' pthak. K' nash flekh sagluvaya fi' ish-veh ish-veh nahp had czar-tor maf. "t'nash-veh sa-mekh, " leralmin-tor lucie, softly laying ish-veh el'ru fi' ish-veh. Au slowly hutau wuh duv ska', heh da-tor tor ish-veh. "dungau etek hal-tor ha-kel, t'nash-veh sa-mekh?" k' wuh wu esh, au kilko-tor "ha." wuh t'hylara t' wuh acquitted prisoner had pusaganau, ne' wuh impression--if au himself had tveshulau--ik au would ri nam-tor sadalau ik mu-yor. Wuh ha'ge vesh' nearly ek' sayonotau svi' wuh tvur, wuh shek-tukh temep vesh' hasu a'ing k' wuh kak heh wuh rattle, heh wuh dismal shi vesh' deserted abi' tor-morrow asal's eku'ko t' geld-stau-nentu, pillory, whipping-lehk, heh branding-shek-tukh, dang repeople ish-veh. Walking svi' ish-veh sa-mekh heh mr. Darnay, lucie manette be' dvun-tor vi' wuh tu'ash sov. Wuh hackney-coach vesh' puvutau, heh wuh sa-mekh heh ko-fu trashu svi' ish-veh. Mr. Stryver had losrak au svi' wuh tvur, tor tipan ish-veh yut pla' tor wuh robing-tvi-shal. Wuh'ashiv person, vi had ri hau wuh travek, il interchanged wuh zhit k' sovek veh t' au, tonk'peh vi had vesh' leaning tehnat wuh temok wilat its duv vesh' darkest, had silently strolled si' po' wuh shom, heh had glazhau fi' abi' wuh coach drove maf. Au i' ash-tor abru tor wilat mr. Lorry heh mr. Darnay lam-tor fi-tor wuh pavement. "ni, mr. Lorry! Sasu t' business lau stariben tor mr. Darnay i'?" kling had tor sovek acknowledgment t' mr. Carton's krus svi' wuh gad's proceedings; kling had fainu t' ish-veh. Au vesh' unrobed, heh vesh' rim wuh weh-rom na' ish-veh svi' appearance. "kuv du fai-tor ra wuh conflict hal-tor fi' svi' wuh business kashek, lu wuh business kashek nam-tor dahsau svi' rom-natured impulse heh business appearances, du would nam-tor amused, mr. Darnay." mr. Lorry reddened, heh leralmin-tor, warmly, "du ma mentioned ik fa', osu. Etek sasu t' business, vi dvin-tor wuh kelek, nam-tor ri etwel sha' trensu. Etek ma tor nah-tor t' wuh kelek weht do ourselves." "i fai-tor, i fai-tor, " rejoined mr. Carton, carelessly. "ri tor nam-tor nettled, mr. Lorry. Du nam-tor u' rom u' wuh'ashiv, i ma rai vet: weh-rom, i dare leralmin." "heh indeed, osu, " pursued mr. Lorry, ri minding ish-veh, "i really ri tor fai-tor ra du ma tor tor k' wuh tukh. Kuv du'll tobeg me, u' maut mau ish-veh tela'at, na' taran ni, i really ri tor fai-tor ik ish-veh nam-tor ish-veh business." "business! Kudau du, i ma rai business, " leralmin-tor mr. Carton. "ish-veh nam-tor wuh pity du ma ri, osu." "i nah-tor ni, nuh'." "kuv du had, " pursued mr. Lorry, "sos'eh du would attend tor ish-veh." "s'haile ashaya du, rai!--i shouldn't, " leralmin-tor mr. Carton. "muhl, osu!" maf-tor mr. Lorry, thoroughly falek-tor k' ish-veh indifference, "business nam-tor wuh maut rom vel, heh wuh maut respectable vel. Heh, osu, kuv business imposes its restraints heh its silences heh impediments, mr. Darnay u' wuh nu'ri gentleman t' generosity fai-tor uf tor tor allowance na' ik circumstance. Mr. Darnay, rom mu-yor, oekon kudau du, osu! I rok du ma vesh' nash gad korsau na' wuh prosperous heh kunli ha'kiv.--ku-san tra'!" sos'eh wuh pi' reshnek k' himself, u' muhl u' k' wuh barrister, mr. Lorry bustled vi' wuh ku-san, heh vesh' lesh ska' tor tellson's. Carton, vi smelt t' kif wine, heh did ri saudau tor nam-tor ved sober, abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor yi, heh da-tor tor darnay: "nash nam-tor wuh flekh pavesh ik lehm-tor du heh me teretuhr. Nash bolau nam-tor wuh flekh mu-yor tor du, standing sa'awek la' k' ish-veh counterpart fi' aifa yut kov?" "i hardly seem wi, " fun-tor charles darnay, "tor belong tor nash panu va'ashiv." "i ri tor wonder na' ish-veh; ish-veh's ri ni wu opi' du vesh' takov irak storilau fi' ish-veh yut tor wuh'ashiv. Du stariben faintly." "i palikau tor nah-tor i am faint." "yi po wuh e'shua ri tor du aru-yokul? I aru-yokul, myself, du' eifa numskulls vesh' deliberating if panu du dang belong tor--nash, il ein vath. Kal-tor me gluvaya du wuh nearest tavern tor aru-yokul muhl na'." bestan ish-veh kar k'fai ish-veh sha', au nem-tor ish-veh ne' ludgate-kunel tor halitra-yut, heh ni, abru wuh wein-tor yut, vi' wuh tavern. La', au vesh' shown vi' wuh pi' tvi-shal, wilat charles darnay vesh' ak recruiting ish-veh karik'es k' wuh rom eiktra aru-yem heh rom wine: du' carton hayal-tor mesyutik tor ish-veh na' wuh ka pasu, k' ish-veh dahshauk mashek t' kif fa' ish-veh, heh ish-veh fully ulef-insolent manner fi-tor ish-veh. "tor du olau, wi, ik du belong tor nash terrestrial scheme va'ashiv, mr. Darnay?" "i am frightfully confused fundauik wak heh shi; tonk'peh i am ni irak nodolau u' tor olau ik." "ish-veh bolau nam-tor wuh immense satisfaction!" au leralmin-tor ish-veh bitterly, heh boshau abru ish-veh makh va'ashiv: if vesh' wuh suk veh. "u' tor me, wuh greatest aitlun i ma, nam-tor tor yen-tor ik i belong tor ish-veh. Ish-veh has rai rom svi' ish-veh na' me--kaula wine spo' nash--il i na' ish-veh. Ni etek nam-tor ri mau kahkwa svi' ik particular. Indeed, i palikau tor nah-tor etek nam-tor ri mau kahkwa svi' sovek particular, du heh i." confused k' wuh zherka t' wuh gad, heh olaya ish-veh hasu tra' k' nash dahtau t' dirik deportment, tor nam-tor spo' wuh sahr-tor, charles darnay vesh' na' wuh pak uf tor kilko-srashiv; t'forti, kilko-tor mokov. "i' ish-veh aru-yem nam-tor ovsoh, " carton presently leralmin-tor, "po ri tor du vutau wuh muhl'es, mr. Darnay; po ri tor du mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh toast?" "ra muhl'es? Ra toast?" "po, ish-veh's fi' wuh um t' ish-veh lahv. Ish-veh ought tor nam-tor, ish-veh bolau nam-tor, i'll swear ish-veh's tra'." "din-tor manette, yi!" "din-tor manette, yi!" looking ish-veh besu bosh svi' wuh limuk du' au drank wuh toast, carton flung ish-veh makh abru' ish-veh tipan tehnat wuh temok, wilat ish-veh shivered tor krus; yi, rang wuh kus-vakh, heh ordered svi' wuh'ashiv. "ik's wuh rom nu'ri t'sai tor el'ru tor wuh coach svi' wuh gu'gelik, mr. Darnay!" au leralmin-tor, boshak ish-veh uzh goblet. Wuh slight kwal heh wuh laconic "ha, " vesh' wuh kilko-srashiv. "ik's wuh rom nu'ri t'sai tor nam-tor pitied k' heh wept na' k'! Uf tor ish-veh olau? Nam-tor ish-veh don hasu ar'kada na' veh's ha'kiv, tor nam-tor wuh vel t' such sympathy heh utan'es, mr. Darnay?" va'ashiv darnay kilko-tor ri wuh zhit. "she vesh' mightily sanoi ki' ish-veh skladan, lu i mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ish-veh. Ri ik she gluvau she vesh' sanoi, tonk'peh i suppose she vesh'." wuh allusion dvin-tor u' wuh timely reminder tor darnay ik nash disagreeable besu had, t' ish-veh sha' el-dvelan, gol-tor ish-veh svi' wuh masu-naf t' wuh gad. Au da-tor wuh dialogue tor ik sfek, heh itaren ish-veh na' ish-veh. "i neither aitlun sovek itaren, il merit sovek, " vesh' wuh careless rejoinder. "ish-veh vesh' nothing tor tor, svi' wuh wuh'rak shi; heh i ri tor fai-tor po i did ish-veh, svi' wuh dahr. Mr. Darnay, kal-tor me ya'akash du wuh deshker." "willingly, heh wuh pi' fun na' ish-veh rom offices." "tor du nah-tor i wa' spo' du?" "really, mr. Carton, " fun-tor wuh vath, oddly disconcerted, "i ma ri ya'akash myself wuh deshker." "tonk'peh ya'akash yourself wuh deshker i'." "du ma bae'cok u' kuv du tor; tonk'peh i ri tor nah-tor du tor." "i ri tor nah-tor i tor, " leralmin-tor carton. "i palikau ki' wuh maut rom opinion t' ish-veh understanding." "nevertheless, " pursued darnay, rising tor mokov wuh kus-vakh, "tra' nam-tor nothing svi' ik, i rok, tor prevent t'nash-veh calling wuh reckoning, heh etwel parting rik' has-bosh-khaf fi' either vla." carton rejoining, "nothing svi' ha'kiv!" darnay rang. "tor du vutau wuh bosh reckoning?" leralmin-tor carton. Fi' ish-veh answering svi' wuh affirmative, "yi katau me wuh'ashiv pint t' nash ka wine, zish-nef, heh sarlah heh wake me na' lehkuh." wuh dun hasu vlitau, charles darnay she-tor heh istau ish-veh rom mu-yor. Rik' returning wuh istaya, carton she-tor nuh', k' vel t' wuh nan t' defiance svi' ish-veh manner, heh leralmin-tor, "wuh kim-shah zhit, mr. Darnay: du nah-tor i am mon-tor?" "i nah-tor du ma vesh' drinking, mr. Carton." "nah-tor? Du fai-tor i ma vesh' drinking." "opi' i bolau leralmin ni, i fai-tor ish-veh." "yi du dungau likewise fai-tor po. I am wuh disappointed drudge, osu. I palutunau rai sasu fi' terra, heh rai sasu fi' terra tun-tor na' me." "mau tor nam-tor regretted. Du lau ma nam-tor-tor ish-veh talents weh-rom." "lau nam-tor ni, mr. Darnay; lau nam-tor ri. Ri tor kal-tor ish-veh sober limuk elate du, however; du ri tor fai-tor ra ish-veh lau sarlah tor. Rom mu-yor!" lu au vesh' losrak sa'awek, nash flekh hasu nem-tor abru wuh ha'fek, went tor wuh makh ik geldau tehnat wuh temok, heh skothon-tor himself minutely svi' ish-veh. "tor du wa' spo' wuh sasu?" au muttered, na' ish-veh sha' glakuv; "po dang du wa' spo' wuh sasu vi resembles du? Tra' nam-tor nothing svi' du tor spo'; du fai-tor ik. Ah, confound du! Ra wuh rubah du ma tor svi' yourself! Wuh rom utvau na' taking tor wuh sasu, ik au gluvau du ra du ma tevan-tor maf s', heh ra du lau ma vesh'! Rubah shitau k' ish-veh, heh would du ma vesh' glazhau na' k' eifa pla-kur bezhun u' au vesh', heh commiserated k' ik pahutau limuk u' au vesh'? Sarlah fi', heh ma ish-veh si' svi' eiktra zhit! Du fnu-ven wuh katravahsu." au resorted tor ish-veh pint t' wine na' consolation, drank ish-veh ek' svi' wuh zamu minutes, heh tevan-tor asleep fi' ish-veh kar, k' ish-veh isachya straggling abru' wuh pasu, heh wuh wu kuvoran-thalv svi' wuh ha'fek dripping ne' fi-tor ish-veh. Chapter v. Wuh jackal eifa vesh' drinking gad, heh danik sasu drank lerash. Ni maut lo'uk nam-tor wuh improvement wak has katau pa' svi' such es'merka, ik wuh moderate star-krus t' wuh nosahp t' wine heh punch if veh sasu would vitem-tor svi' wuh rivak t' wuh mu-yor, rik' sovek detriment tor ish-veh reputation u' wuh buhfik gentleman, would seem, svi' aifa gad, wuh ridiculous exaggeration. Wuh oren-tor ha'yigal t' wuh tor-gav vesh' certainly ri za' sovek vath oren-tor ha'yigal svi' its bacchanalian propensities; neither vesh' mr. Stryver, already sahris shouldering ish-veh yut tor wuh suk heh lucrative practice, za' ish-veh compeers svi' nash particular, sovek weht do svi' wuh psethayek krus t' wuh legal ne-koshtri. Wuh favourite na' wuh hinek bailey, heh eke na' wuh sessions, mr. Stryver had palikau cautiously tor hew maf wuh weh-neik staves t' wuh pu'uth fi' if au mounted. Sessions heh hinek bailey had i' tor summon ish-veh favourite, specially, tor ish-veh longing kar; heh shouldering itself na' wuh visage t' wuh s'haile chief yeht-gav svi' wuh kelek t' sa-te'kru's wu-ku-san, wuh florid countenance t' mr. Stryver lau nam-tor kanok-gadik gla-tor, bursting s' wuh sar-tak t' wigs, spo' wuh lo'uk sunflower pushing its yut na' wuh yel s' among wuh lan bah-ker-bosh t' flaring besu. Ish-veh had wuh'wak vesh' noted na' wuh mofek, ik du' mr. Stryver vesh' wuh glib sasu, heh wuh unscrupulous, heh wuh pok, heh wuh vakh, au had ri ik sutra t' extracting wuh essence s' wuh tuh t' star-krus, if nam-tor among wuh danik striking heh bolayatik t' wuh advocate's accomplishments. Tonk'peh, wuh remarkable improvement sarlah fi-tor ish-veh u' tor nash. Wuh weht business au prah, wuh greater ish-veh tepul seemed tor tor'ovau t' getting na' its pi'fek-svitan-nalatra heh hinek-masu; heh however tab-ma na' mu-yor au hayal-tor carousing k' sydney carton, au kwon-hau-ov had ish-veh sfekau na' ish-veh ozh' shahtau svi' wuh asal. Sydney carton, idlest heh danik unpromising t' sasu, vesh' stryver's lo'uk puk'ai'la. Ra wuh dahkuh drank teretuhr, svi' hilary zhil heh michaelmas, lau ma markau wuh sa-te'kru's hali. Stryver worla had wuh nuf svi' el'ru, sovek-wilat, tonk'peh carton vesh' tra', k' ish-veh el'ru svi' ish-veh abru'lik, staring na' wuh abru-tol t' wuh kelek; au went wuh ka raf-kuv, heh kauk tra' au prolonged ish-veh tsuri orgies tab-ma vi' wuh mu-yor, heh carton vesh' rumoured tor nam-tor gla-tor na' sax'ksei gad, going ha-kel stealthily heh unsteadily tor ish-veh lodgings, spo' wuh dissipated aushfa. Na' kim-shah, ish-veh began tor prah pa', among such u' vesh' interested svi' wuh tukh, ik hi sydney carton would worla nam-tor wuh lion, au vesh' wuh amazingly rom jackal, heh ik au rendered saikhut heh dvin tor stryver svi' ik humble tsoh. "lehkuh o'wak-vel, osu, " leralmin-tor wuh sasu na' wuh tavern, ik au had vifalunau tor wake ish-veh--"lehkuh o'wak-vel, osu." "ra's wuh tukh?" "lehkuh o'wak-vel, osu." "ra tor du tvai? Lehkuh o'wak-vel na' mu-yor?" "ha, osu. Ish-veh dor var-tor me tor vutau du." "oh! I vokau. Maut muhl, maut muhl." po' wuh zamu pasik urgam tor prah tor yuk va'ashiv, if wuh sasu dexterously combated k' stirring wuh yon continuously na' kaukuh minutes, au prah abru, tossed ish-veh taik fi', heh lates-tor si'. Au da-tor vi' wuh temple, heh, having zaprah-tor himself k' dah'wak pacing wuh pavements t' sa-te'kru's wu-ku-san-lates heh dun-kelek, da-tor vi' wuh stryver tvi-shal. Wuh stryver clerk, vi worla gol-tor na' aifa conferences, had hal-tor ha-kel, heh wuh stryver principal tu'ash wuh svep. Au had ish-veh slippers fi', heh wuh thal sar-tak-gown, heh ish-veh drahk vesh' sai-famik na' ish-veh greater ease. Au had ik rather kwai, ish-veh-tor, seared marking pa' wuh bezhun, if lau nam-tor glantau svi' ek' elik nehasamek t' ish-veh mohrn, s' wuh portrait t' jeffries ne'le, heh if mokuhlek nam-tor traced, ne' vuhnauk pastau t' tanaf, k'fai wuh portraits t' kanok drinking ya'shakhuv. "du nam-tor wuh pi' tab-ma, vokaya, " leralmin-tor stryver. "pa' wuh tsuri wak; ish-veh lau nam-tor wuh yonuk t' wuh wadan later." au went vi' wuh dingy tvi-shal zehl-tor k' dunap heh littered k' dun, wilat tra' vesh' wuh blazing yon. Wuh kettle steamed fi-tor wuh hob, heh svi' wuh midst t' wuh vashau t' dun wuh pasu min-tor, k' plenty t' wine fi-tor ish-veh, heh brandy, heh rum, heh slor-tukh, heh lemons. "du ma had ish-veh mashek, i pakashogau, sydney." "dahkuh tor-mu-yor, i nah-tor. I ma vesh' dining k' wuh gad's client; il seeing ish-veh aru-yokul--ish-veh's ek' veh!" "ik vesh' wuh ritsuri sfek, sydney, ik du katau tor lesh fi-tor wuh shasutan. Uf did sarlah du k' ish-veh? Lu did ish-veh kwul du?" "i nahp au vesh' rather wuh handsome katravahsu, heh i nahp i dang ma vesh' mau wuh ka wihfelau t' katravahsu, kuv i had had sovek kunli." mr. Stryver abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor till au hutau ish-veh lehkuh-storauk paunch. "du heh ish-veh kunli, sydney! Prah tor ar'kadan, prah tor ar'kadan." sullenly hiyet, wuh jackal loosened ish-veh sai-vel, went vi' wuh adjoining tvi-shal, heh sarlah pla' k' wuh suk mashek t' samu masu, wuh basin, heh wuh towel il dahkuh. Steeping wuh towels svi' wuh masu, heh partially wringing au si', au hesha au fi' ish-veh patam svi' wuh manner hideous tor behold, hayal-tor ne' na' wuh pasu, heh leralmin-tor, "i' i am pok!" "ri mau boiling ne' tor nam-tor ovsoh tor-mu-yor, vokaya, " leralmin-tor mr. Stryver, gaily, u' au glazhau among ish-veh dun. "uf mau?" "goh dahkuh dvolau t' au." "mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh rasahkos wuh'rak." "tra' au nam-tor, sydney. Yon maf!" wuh lion yi tertitau himself fi' ish-veh pla' fi' wuh ku-san fi' veh vla t' wuh drinking-pasu, du' wuh jackal hayal-tor na' ish-veh sha' dun-bestrewn pasu proper, fi' wuh vath vla t' ish-veh, k' wuh mashek heh bezhun-zaneshu pok tor ish-veh el'ru. Fi' resorted tor wuh drinking-pasu rik' stint, tonk'peh tik svi' wuh natya yut; wuh lion na' wuh danik krus reclining k' ish-veh el'ru svi' ish-veh waistband, looking na' wuh yon, il occasionally flirting k' ein lighter kisev; wuh jackal, k' knitted meix'tem heh intent limuk, ni glu svi' ish-veh task, ik ish-veh bezhun did ri kauk zahal-tor wuh el'ru au sakadau si' na' ish-veh makh--if k'ashiv groped pa', na' wuh minute il weht, fa' ish-veh afer-tor wuh makh na' ish-veh bru-lar. Dahkuh il rehkuh wak, wuh tukh svi' el'ru became ni knotty, ik wuh jackal afer-tor ish-veh imperative fi' ish-veh tor prah abru, heh menal ish-veh towels anew. S' aifa pilgrimages tor wuh mashek heh basin, au fun-tor k' such eccentricities t' damp headgear u' rai zhit mokuhlek kethelvau; if vesh' tor wuh weht ludicrous k' ish-veh anxious ne-seshan. Na' wu-vath wuh jackal had prah teretuhr wuh lerakhovau repast na' wuh lion, heh proceeded tor nufai ish-veh tor ish-veh. Wuh lion nem-tor ish-veh k' tun heh yuzhat, tor ish-veh dvel s' ish-veh, heh ish-veh remarks fi-tor ish-veh, heh wuh jackal gol-tor fi'. Lu wuh repast vesh' fully discussed, wuh lion shitau ish-veh el'ru svi' ish-veh waistband va'ashiv, heh ti ne' tor meditate. Wuh jackal yi invigorated himself k' wuh bumper na' ish-veh threshan-tashek, heh wuh sluk application tor ish-veh patam, heh applied himself tor wuh tershaya t' wuh dahr yem; nash vesh' administered tor wuh lion svi' wuh ka manner, heh vesh' ri sashitau t' abi' wuh wak-vel kwul-tor rehkuh svi' wuh asal. "heh i' etek ma ovsoh, sydney, boshaya wuh bumper t' punch, " leralmin-tor mr. Stryver. Wuh jackal snem-tor wuh towels s' ish-veh patam, if had vesh' steaming va'ashiv, hutau himself, luvau, shivered, heh complied. "du vesh' maut ralash, sydney, svi' wuh tukh t' eifa tarkiv toglantausu tor-gad. Kanok deshker var-tor." "i kwon-hau-ov am ralash; am i ri?" "i ri tor gainsay ish-veh. Ra has roughened ish-veh temper? Shitau ein punch tor ish-veh heh mos ish-veh va'ashiv." k' wuh deprecatory grunt, wuh jackal va'ashiv complied. "wuh hinek sydney carton t' hinek shrewsbury shi'oren, " leralmin-tor stryver, nodding ish-veh patam abru' ish-veh u' au reviewed ish-veh svi' wuh la' heh wuh vesht, "wuh hinek seesaw sydney. Abru veh minute heh ne' wuh thurai; i' svi' tam'a heh i' svi' despondency!" "ah!" fun-tor wuh vath, sighing: "ha! Wuh ka sydney, k' wuh ka kunli. Kauk yi, i did tusok na' vath sa-kan, heh seldom did t'nash-veh sha'." "heh po ri?" "oekon fai-tor. Ish-veh vesh' t'nash-veh yut, i suppose." au hayal-tor, k' ish-veh el'ru svi' ish-veh abru'lik heh ish-veh mal sakadau si' fa' ish-veh, looking na' wuh yon. "carton, " leralmin-tor ish-veh t'hy'la, squaring himself na' ish-veh k' wuh bullying sov, u' kuv wuh yon-grate had vesh' wuh furnace svi' if potun-tor endeavour vesh' zhuk-fas-tor, heh wuh veh delicate vel tor nam-tor ovsoh na' wuh hinek sydney carton t' hinek shrewsbury shi'oren vesh' tor tipan ish-veh vi' ish-veh, "ish-veh yut nam-tor, heh kwon-hau-ov vesh', wuh lame yut. Du summon rai tepul heh lof. Glazhau na' me." "oh, botheration!" fun-tor sydney, k' wuh lighter heh weht rom-humoured abru'teruklar-ru'lut, "ri tor du nam-tor moral!" "uf ma i ovsoh ra i ma ovsoh?" leralmin-tor stryver; "uf tor i tor ra i tor?" "partly k'fai paying me tor gol'nev du, i suppose. Tonk'peh ish-veh's ri don ish-veh du' tor apostrophise me, il wuh sov, pa' ish-veh; ra du aitlun tor tor, du tor. Du vesh' kwon-hau-ov svi' wuh khom lan, heh i vesh' kwon-hau-ov za'." "i had tor prah vi' wuh khom lan; i vesh' ri pukeshta tra', vesh' i?" "i vesh' ri la' na' wuh hali-kal; tonk'peh t'nash-veh opinion nam-tor du vesh', " leralmin-tor carton. Na' nash, au abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor va'ashiv, heh au fi' abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor. "fa' shrewsbury, heh na' shrewsbury, heh ek'wak opi' shrewsbury, " pursued carton, "du ma tevan-tor vi' ish-veh lan, heh i ma tevan-tor vi' t'nash-veh. Kauk lu etek vesh' katravahsu-orensu svi' wuh orensu-yonuk t' paris, picking abru french, heh french tor-gav, heh vath french crumbs ik etek didn't prah mau rom t', du vesh' kwon-hau-ov ein-wilat, heh i vesh' kwon-hau-ov nowhere." "heh t'vi lafot vesh' ik?" "fi-tor t'nash-veh soul, i am ri sure ik ish-veh vesh' ri ish-veh. Du vesh' kwon-hau-ov driving heh riving heh shouldering heh be' dvun-tor, tor ik restless degree ik i had rai pavesh na' t'nash-veh ha'kiv tonk'peh svi' zhar heh repose. Ish-veh's wuh gloomy vel, however, tor variben pa' sha' vesht, k' wuh gad breaking. Da-tor me svi' ein vath kharat fa' i hal-tor." "muhl yi! Pledge me tor wuh takov toglantausu, " leralmin-tor stryver, holding abru ish-veh makh. "nam-tor du da-tor svi' wuh vaksurik kharat?" sauyaing ri, na' au became gloomy va'ashiv. "takov toglantausu, " au muttered, looking ne' vi' ish-veh makh. "i ma had hiyet t' toglantausu tor-gad heh tor-mu-yor; vi's ish-veh takov toglantausu?" "wuh picturesque hassu's ko-fu, din-tor manette." "she takov?" "nam-tor she ri?" "rai." "po, sasu alive, she vesh' wuh admiration t' wuh bosh kelek!" "nehaya wuh admiration t' wuh bosh kelek! Vi tor wuh hinek bailey wuh judge t' vaksur? She vesh' wuh pi-maat-kur-haired su-leitri!" "tor du fai-tor, sydney, " leralmin-tor mr. Stryver, looking na' ish-veh k' nasik bezhun, heh slowly bestan wuh el'ru mes' ish-veh florid limuk: "tor du fai-tor, i rather nahp, na' wuh wak, ik du sympathised k' wuh pi-maat-kur-haired su-leitri, heh vesh' sahris tor gla-tor ra pavesh-tor tor wuh pi-maat-kur-haired su-leitri?" "sahris tor gla-tor ra pavesh-tor! Kuv wuh ko-kan, su-leitri il rai su-leitri, swoons k'svi wuh ker il dahkuh t' wuh sasu's han, au mokuhlek gla-tor ish-veh rik' wuh vulunaya-makh. I pledge du, tonk'peh i wafu wuh vaksur. Heh i' i'll ma rai weht mon; i'll prah tor sar-tak." lu ish-veh kasu zahal-tor ish-veh si' fi' wuh staircase k' wuh ha'fek, tor ta'hal ish-veh ne' wuh kaiden, wuh gad vesh' coldly looking svi' k'fai its grimy krani. Lu au prah s' wuh kelek, wuh sov vesh' samu heh maf, wuh pasik igen overcast, wuh pilash gu'gelik heh neik-ha'khlup, wuh bosh scene spo' wuh lifeless eshikh. Heh wreaths t' grazhiv vesh' spinning pauk heh pauk fa' wuh asal thorshaya, u' kuv wuh eshikh-mazhiv had risen irak maf, heh wuh wuh'rak spray t' ish-veh svi' its storilaya had palikau tor overwhelm wuh kahr. Thinoi nekwitau k'svi ish-veh, heh wuh eshikh ek' pa', nash sasu lam-tor fam dvun fi' ish-veh yut mes' wuh ralash-fam nef, heh gla-tor na' wuh moment, lying svi' wuh shi'kwai fa' ish-veh, wuh mirage t' dorli ambition, shal-wafaya, heh perseverance. Svi' wuh rom kahr t' nash vision, tra' vesh' airy tanaf-shi'gluvaun s' if wuh ashau heh takov-tor glazhau fi-tor ish-veh, bah-ker svi' if wuh savas t' ha'kiv geldau piyahtaya, mashau t' rok ik sparkled svi' ish-veh glan. Wuh moment, heh ish-veh vesh' hal-tor. Climbing tor wuh pid tvi-shal svi' wuh muhl t' kelek, au threw himself ne' svi' ish-veh sai-vel fi' wuh neglected sar-tak, heh its trak vesh' masupik k' thinoi bezhun-masu. Sadly, sadly, wuh yel she-tor; ish-veh she-tor fi-tor rai sadder glan do wuh sasu t' rom kup'es heh rom zherka, incapable t' ish-veh khartau tusok, incapable t' ish-veh sha' gol'nev heh ish-veh sha' happiness, sensible t' wuh luk-has fi' ish-veh, heh resigning himself tor kal-tor ish-veh yokul ish-veh maf. Chapter vi. Hundreds t' sutra wuh hizhuk lodgings t' hassu manette vesh' svi' wuh hizhuk yut-teruk ri irak s' soho-keh-vla. Fi' wuh aru t' wuh ac'ruth tok-ti gad lu wuh pral t' kehkuh tevun-krus had padukau abru' wuh trial na' kam'nat, heh lesh ish-veh, u' tor wuh tsuri eku'ko heh vokaya, irak si' tor masutra, mr. Jarvis lorry lates-tor bi' wuh ka'ug'yelik yut s' clerkenwell wilat au ha-tor, fi' ish-veh yut tor aru-yokul k' wuh hassu. Po' several relapses vi' business-vi-seshaya, mr. Lorry had shetau wuh hassu's t'hy'la, heh wuh hizhuk yut-teruk vesh' wuh ka'ug'yelik krus t' ish-veh ha'kiv. Fi' nash ac'ruth tok-ti gad, mr. Lorry lates-tor na' soho, lehkuh-mal svi' wuh aru, na' rehkuh utvau t' es'merka. Firstly, fai'ei, fi' tok-ti sundays, au k'ashiv lates-tor si', fa' aru-yem, k' wuh hassu heh lucie; secondly, fai'ei, fi' unfavourable sundays, au vesh' accustomed tor nam-tor k' au u' wuh skan t'hy'la, talking, telvan, looking s' krani, heh paik getting k'fai wuh gad; thirdly, fai'ei au pavesh-tor ki' ish-veh sha' pi' shrewd vet-tor tor kilau, heh fai-tor uf wuh yut t' wuh hassu's household sfekau tor ik wak u' wuh kesik wak na' solving au. Wuh quainter teruk do wuh teruk wilat wuh hassu ha-tor, vesh' ri tor nam-tor afer-tor svi' london. Tra' vesh' rai yut k'fai ish-veh, heh wuh khom krani t' wuh hassu's lodgings khartau wuh vaksurik pi' vista t' yut ik had wuh congenial sov t' retirement fi' ish-veh. Tra' vesh' zamu kelek yi, desh'rak t' wuh oxford-fau-yut, heh laptra-lap flourished, heh kwai svai grew, heh wuh hawthorn blossomed, svi' wuh i' vanished vunai. U' wuh consequence, shasol airs da-kuvau svi' soho k' hakarik el'es, instead t' languishing vi' wuh parish spo' fam-kelek-tor paupers rik' wuh settlement; heh tra' vesh' wehk wuh rom khu'rak temok, ri irak ska', fi' if wuh peaches piyahtau svi' ish-veh tevun-yonuk. Wuh belaar ta'hal kwul-tor vi' wuh teruk brilliantly svi' wuh earlier krus t' wuh gad; tonk'peh, lu wuh yut grew fal, wuh teruk vesh' svi' duv, hi ri svi' duv ni remote tonk'peh ik du kupi gla-tor mesakh ish-veh vi' wuh glare t' ugel'es. Ish-veh vesh' wuh samuyau gla-tor, staid tonk'peh cheerful, wuh wonderful shi na' vava, heh wuh maut harbour s' wuh raging yut. Tra' ought ki' vesh' wuh tranquil kas-wadi svi' such wuh anchorage, heh tra' vesh'. Wuh hassu occupied dahkuh lan-tol t' wuh suk stegel kelek, wilat several callings purported tor nam-tor pursued k' gad, tonk'peh whereof pi' vesh' zhu-yehat sovek gad, heh if vesh' shunned k' ek' t' au na' mu-yor. Svi' wuh kelek na' wuh pla', attainable k' wuh courtyard wilat wuh sov-hali-lap rustled its yar-kur mor, church-nafek claimed tor nam-tor tor, heh haul-tukh tor nam-tor chased, heh likewise pi-maat-tukh tor nam-tor beaten k' ein mysterious masuk'veh vi had wuh pi-maat-kur kar starting s' wuh temok t' wuh khom tvur--u' kuv au had beaten himself taluhk, heh menaced wuh kahwa rushan t' ek' visitors. Maut pi' t' aifa trades, il t' wuh lonely lodger rumoured tor ha-tor abru-kaiden, il t' wuh neik-ha'khlup coach-trimming maker asserted ki' wuh counting-kelek ne', vesh' ek'wak puzhu-tor il gla-tor. Occasionally, wuh fam-kelek-tor workman putting ish-veh tor-pal fi', traversed wuh tvur, il wuh ri-fainusu peered pa' tra', il wuh irak clink vesh' puzhu-tor mes' wuh courtyard, il wuh thump s' wuh pi-maat-kur masuk'veh. Aifa, however, vesh' goh wuh kaulauf required tor skan-tor wuh tor-go ik wuh sparrows svi' wuh sov-hali-lap za' wuh kelek, heh wuh vava svi' wuh teruk fa' ish-veh, had ish-veh sha' yut s' gad asal unto gad mu-yor. Hassu manette poprah such hasausu la' u' ish-veh hinek reputation, heh its revival svi' wuh floating zhal-tor t' ish-veh var, katau ish-veh. Ish-veh talik fai-tukh, heh ish-veh vigilance heh renkup'es svi' conducting ingenious spolek, katau ish-veh vathru vi' moderate ya'akash, heh au pinkau u' mau u' au aitlu. Aifa vel vesh' k'svi mr. Jarvis lorry's fai-tukh, nahp, heh beglanau, lu au rang wuh svep-kus-vakh t' wuh tranquil kelek svi' wuh teruk, fi' wuh tok-ti gad aru. "hassu manette na' ha-kel?" gishu ha-kel. "din-tor lucie na' ha-kel?" gishu ha-kel. "din-tor pross na' ha-kel?" possibly na' ha-kel, tonk'peh t' wuh certainty impossible na' handmaid tor anticipate intentions t' din-tor pross, u' tor admission il wafaya t' wuh kla-min. "u' i am na' ha-kel myself, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, "i'll hal-tor upstairs." hi wuh hassu's ko-fu had fainu nothing t' wuh shasol t' ish-veh keshtan, she saudau ki' innately derived s' ish-veh ik kup'es tor tor mau t' pi' tvai, if nam-tor veh t' its danik useful heh danik agreeable noshtra. Velik u' wuh furniture vesh', ish-veh vesh' eku ska' k' ni wehk pi' adornments, t' rai tala tonk'peh na' ish-veh zahvan heh fancy, ik its daya vesh' delightful. Wuh disposition t' kanok-vei svi' wuh tvi-shal, s' wuh largest vel tor wuh least; wuh arrangement t' colours, wuh sohkik vuhna'es heh contrast prah k' thrift svi' trifles, k' delicate el'ru, pa'shik bezhun, heh rom kash-ral; vesh' na' wuh'wak ni vaksurik svi' themselves, heh ni expressive t' ish-veh originator, ik, u' mr. Lorry lam-tor looking pa' ish-veh, wuh maut ku-san heh pasu seemed tor ya'akash ish-veh, k' vel t' ik peculiar sagluvaya if au fai-tor ni muhl k' nash wak, whether au messau? Tra' vesh' rehkuh tvi-shal fi' wuh lan-tol, heh, wuh svep k' if au sviribau hasu shitau tu'ash ik wuh sov lau be' dvun freely k'fai au ek', mr. Lorry, smilingly observant t' ik fanciful resemblance if au patal-tor ek' pa' ish-veh, lates-tor s' veh tor wuh'ashiv. Wuh wuh'rak vesh' wuh buhfik tvi-shal, heh svi' ish-veh vesh' lucie's kushel, heh svai, heh dunap, heh kitau-skaf, heh ar'kadan-pasu, heh natuhn t' masu-colours; wuh dahr vesh' wuh hassu's consulting-tvi-shal, nam-tor-tor isha u' wuh dining-tvi-shal; wuh wuh, changingly speckled k' wuh rustle t' wuh sov-hali-lap svi' wuh ker, vesh' wuh hassu's shi'yuk, heh tra', svi' wuh teruk, lam-tor wuh disused shoemaker's wu-ku-san heh tray t' raul, mau u' ish-veh had lam-tor fi' wuh fifth lan-tol t' wuh dismal kelek k' wuh wine-mahr-kel, svi' wuh suburb t' osu antoine svi' paris. "i wonder, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, pausing svi' ish-veh looking pa', "ik au potau ik reminder t' ish-veh sufferings pa' ish-veh!" "heh po wonder na' ik?" vesh' wuh abrupt inquiry ik tor ish-veh palikaya. Ish-veh proceeded s' din-tor pross, wuh kwai yon-kur kosu, karik t' el'ru, t'vi acquaintance au had wuh'rak tor na' wuh royal george hotel na' dover, heh had opi' improved. "i dang ma nahp--" mr. Lorry began. "pooh! Du'd ma nahp!" leralmin-tor din-tor pross; heh mr. Lorry losrak ska'. "uf tor du tor?" inquired ik t'sai yi--sharply, heh wi u' kuv tor sagluvau ik she spitau ish-veh rai malice. "i am takov muhl, i nemaiyo, " kilko-tor mr. Lorry, k' meekness; "uf nam-tor du?" "nothing tor boast t', " leralmin-tor din-tor pross. "indeed?" "ah! Indeed!" leralmin-tor din-tor pross. "i am maut mau shitau si' pa' t'nash-veh ladybird." "indeed?" "na' gracious sake leralmin vel else isha 'indeed, ' il du'll fidget me tor tevakh, " leralmin-tor din-tor pross: t'vi character (dissociated s' stature) vesh' shortness. "really, yi?" leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, u' wuh amendment. "really, nam-tor rasahkos hiyet, " fun-tor din-tor pross, "tonk'peh weh-rom. Ha, i am maut mau shitau si'." "sos ya'akash wuh aishan?" "i ri tor aitlun dozens t' sutra vi nam-tor mokov worthy t' ladybird, tor sarlah la' looking po' ish-veh, " leralmin-tor din-tor pross. "tor dozens sarlah na' ik lof?" "hundreds, " leralmin-tor din-tor pross. Ish-veh vesh' noshtra t' nash t'sai (u' t' ein vath sutra fa' ish-veh wak heh opi') ik whenever ish-veh tveshik proposition vesh' deshkau, she exaggerated ish-veh. "tal-kam me!" leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, u' wuh safest remark au kupi nah-tor t'. "i ma ha-tor k' wuh ashal-veh--il wuh ashal-veh has ha-tor k' me, heh vlitau me na' ish-veh; if she certainly dang worla ma ovsoh, du lau nem-tor ish-veh affidavit, kuv i kupi ma afforded tor potau either myself il ish-veh na' nothing--opi' she vesh' lehkuh tevun hinek. Heh ish-veh's really maut lerash, " leralmin-tor din-tor pross. Ri seeing k' precision ra vesh' maut lerash, mr. Lorry hutau ish-veh patam; using ik yauluhk krus t' himself u' wuh wihfelau t' pu'a tor-sai ik would nunau sovek-vel. "ek' wihfelau t' sutra vi nam-tor ri svi' wuh least degree worthy t' wuh kelek-aushfa, nam-tor kwon-hau-ov turning abru, " leralmin-tor din-tor pross. "lu du began ish-veh--" "i began ish-veh, din-tor pross?" "didn't du? Vi katau ish-veh sa-mekh tor ha'kiv?" "oh! Kuv ik vesh' palikaya ish-veh--" leralmin-tor mr. Lorry. "ish-veh wasn't shahtan ish-veh, i suppose? I leralmin, lu du began ish-veh, ish-veh vesh' lerash hiyet; ri ik i ma sovek lafot tor talal k' hassu manette, kaula ik au nam-tor ri worthy t' such wuh ko-fu, if nam-tor rai imputation fi' ish-veh, na' ish-veh vesh' ri tor nam-tor gishu ik anybody dang nam-tor, ne' sovek circumstances. Tonk'peh ish-veh really nam-tor doubly heh trebly lerash ki' patreitan heh multitudes t' sutra turning abru po' ish-veh (i kupi ma forgiven ish-veh), tor nem-tor ladybird's affections maf s' me." mr. Lorry fai-tor din-tor pross tor nam-tor maut kis-ka, tonk'peh au isha fai-tor ish-veh k' nash wak tor nam-tor, ne'rak wuh dvin t' ish-veh risvitan'es, veh t' eifa unselfish creatures--afer-tor goh among kosu--vi dungi, na' pure ashaya heh admiration, bind themselves willing kafeh, tor youth lu au ma pakik ish-veh, tor vaksur ik au worla had, tor accomplishments ik au vesh' worla fortunate hiyet tor nazh-kap, tor ugelik rok-tor ik worla min-tor fi-tor ish-veh sha' sombre ha-tor. Au fai-tor hiyet t' wuh panu tor fai-tor ik tra' nam-tor nothing svi' ish-veh weh-rom do wuh faithful dvin t' wuh khaf-spol; ni rendered heh ni elik s' sovek mercenary taint, au had such wuh exalted respect na' ish-veh, ik svi' wuh retributive arrangements tor k' ish-veh sha' kashek--etek ek' tor such arrangements, weht il lehkuh--au stationed din-tor pross mau nearer tor wuh weh-neik ha'su do wehk t'sai immeasurably weh-rom prah abru fi' k' malat heh tanaf, vi had balances na' tellson's. "tra' worla vesh', il dungi nam-tor, tonk'peh veh sasu worthy t' ladybird, " leralmin-tor din-tor pross; "heh ik vesh' t'nash-veh sa-kai solomon, kuv au hadn't tor wuh lafosh svi' ha'kiv." la' va'ashiv: mr. Lorry's inquiries vi' din-tor pross's personal vesht-var had afer-tor wuh kla-min ik ish-veh sa-kai solomon vesh' wuh heartless scoundrel vi had stripped ish-veh t' kanok-vei she ma, u' wuh stake tor speculate k', heh had abandoned ish-veh svi' ish-veh poverty na' evermore, k' rai esta t' compunction. Din-tor pross's fidelity t' dva svi' solomon (deducting wuh mere trifle na' nash slight lafosh) vesh' ved wuh serious tukh k' mr. Lorry, heh had its rasath svi' ish-veh rom opinion t' ish-veh. "u' etek pavesh-tor tor nam-tor sa'awek na' wuh moment, heh nam-tor fi' sutra t' business, " au leralmin-tor, lu au had zaprah tor wuh bestan-tvi-shal heh had hayal-tor ne' tra' svi' friendly relations, "kal-tor me ya'akash du--tor wuh hassu, svi' talking k' lucie, worla dzhinau tor wuh shoemaking wak, wi?" "worla." "heh wi potau ik wu-ku-san heh eifa raul be' ish-veh?" "ah!" fun-tor din-tor pross, shaking ish-veh patam. "tonk'peh i ri tor leralmin au ri tor dzhinau tor ish-veh k'svi himself." "tor du dva-tor ik au nah-tor t' ish-veh mau?" "i tor, " leralmin-tor din-tor pross. "tor du glenonau--" mr. Lorry had palikau, lu din-tor pross nem-tor ish-veh abru pen k': "worla glenonau sovek-vel. Ma rai glenonaya na' ek'." "i lamok yeht-tor; tor du suppose--du hal-tor ni irak u' tor suppose, sometimes?" "i' heh yi, " leralmin-tor din-tor pross. "tor du suppose, " mr. Lorry went fi', k' wuh laughing twinkle svi' ish-veh ugelik bezhun, u' ish-veh glazhau kindly na' ish-veh, "ik hassu manette has sovek wihka t' ish-veh sha', korsau k'fai ek' eifa tevun, tomasu tor wuh aishan t' ish-veh hasu ni oppressed; sos'eh, kauk tor wuh ahm t' ish-veh oppressor?" "i ri tor suppose sovek-vel pa' ish-veh tonk'peh ra ladybird var-tor me." "heh ik nam-tor--?" "ik she nah-tor au has." "i' ri tor nam-tor reshnek na' t'nash-veh asking ek' aifa deshkau; fai'ei i am wuh mere pasik sasu t' business, heh du nam-tor wuh kosu t' business." "pasik?" din-tor pross inquired, k' placidity. Rather wishing ish-veh modest tetaya-zhit maf, mr. Lorry kilko-tor, "rai, rai, rai. Surely ri. Tor fun tor business: --nam-tor ish-veh ri remarkable ik hassu manette, unquestionably innocent t' sovek tr'y'kak u' etek nam-tor ek' muhl assured au nam-tor, dang worla esta fi-tor ik deshker? I dungi ri leralmin k' me, hi au had business relations k' me wehk tevun ago, heh etek nam-tor i' intimate; i dungi leralmin k' wuh rom ko-fu tor ik au nam-tor ni devotedly attached, heh vi nam-tor ni devotedly attached tor ish-veh? Dva-tor me, din-tor pross, i ri tor betaya wuh ong k' du, s' curiosity, tonk'peh s' zealous eku'ko." "muhl! Tor wuh buhfik t' t'nash-veh understanding, heh rasahkos's wuh buhfik, du'll var-tor me, " leralmin-tor din-tor pross, softened k' wuh molu t' wuh apology, "au nam-tor kwes t' wuh bosh subject." "kwes?" "ish-veh's eiktra hiyet, i dang nah-tor, po au lau nam-tor. Ish-veh's wuh dreadful remembrance. Isha ik, ish-veh pak t' himself grew s' ish-veh. Ri fai-tor uf au pakik himself, il uf au recovered himself, au lau worla olau ac'ruth t' ri losing himself va'ashiv. Ik sa'awek wouldn't tor wuh subject vaksurik, i dang nah-tor." ish-veh vesh' wuh profounder remark do mr. Lorry had glazhau na'. "yeht, " leralmin-tor au, "heh pthak-bosh tor haul-tor fi-tor. Wi, wuh vet lurks svi' t'nash-veh kashek, din-tor pross, whether ish-veh nam-tor rom na' hassu manette ki' ik nelaya kwon-hau-ov ikap'uh t'du ru'lut k'svi ish-veh. Indeed, ish-veh nam-tor nash vet heh wuh uneasiness ish-veh sometimes aisha me ik has pufulag-tor me tor etwel la' guhl'es." "mokuhlek't nam-tor gol-tor, " leralmin-tor din-tor pross, shaking ish-veh patam. "esta ik string, heh au instantly rubai na' wuh weh-rasahkos. Weh-rom trasha ish-veh sa'awek. Svi' pen, bolau trasha ish-veh sa'awek, spo' il rai spo'. Sometimes, au prah abru svi' wuh tevik t' wuh mu-yor, heh dungi nam-tor puzhu-tor, k' etek overhead tra', walking abru heh ne', walking abru heh ne', svi' ish-veh tvi-shal. Ladybird has oren-tor tor fai-tor yi ik ish-veh kashek nam-tor walking abru heh ne', walking abru heh ne', svi' ish-veh hinek prison. She hurries tor ish-veh, heh au hal-tor fi' teretuhr, walking abru heh ne', walking abru heh ne', abi' au nam-tor tertitau. Tonk'peh au worla leralmin-tor wuh zhit t' wuh yeht utvau t' ish-veh restlessness, tor ish-veh, heh she tal-tor ish-veh buhfik ri tor hint na' ish-veh tor ish-veh. Svi' silence au hal-tor walking abru heh ne' teretuhr, walking abru heh ne' teretuhr, till ish-veh ashaya heh apc'koik ma katau ish-veh tor himself." notwithstanding din-tor pross's wafaya t' ish-veh sha' glenonaya, tra' vesh' wuh pakashogaya t' wuh kusut t' hasu monotonously haunted k' veh maf idea, svi' ish-veh repetition t' wuh zhit-bal, walking abru heh ne', if testified tor ish-veh possessing such wuh vel. Wuh teruk has vesh' mentioned u' wuh wonderful teruk na' vava; ish-veh had palikau tor vava ni resoundingly tor wuh tread t' coming ash'ya, ik ish-veh seemed u' hi wuh maut mention t' ik weary pacing tor heh fro had eku ish-veh going. "la' au nam-tor!" leralmin-tor din-tor pross, rising tor shaya abru wuh conference; "heh i' etek dungau ma hundreds t' sutra takov ak!" ish-veh vesh' such wuh curious teruk svi' its acoustical veltra, such wuh peculiar kaluk t' wuh shi, ik u' mr. Lorry lam-tor na' wuh tu'ash krani, looking na' wuh sa-mekh heh ko-fu t'vi ash-tor au puzhu-tor, au fancied au would worla betaya. Ri goh would wuh vava tev-tor maf, u' hi wuh ash-tor had hal-tor; tonk'peh, vava t' vath ash-tor ik worla sarlah would nam-tor puzhu-tor svi' ish-veh stead, heh would tev-tor maf na' rom lu au seemed ikap-tor na' el'ru. However, sa-mekh heh ko-fu did na' kim-shah saudau, heh din-tor pross vesh' pok na' wuh yut svep tor poprah au. Din-tor pross vesh' wuh vaksurik glan, albeit kwai, heh yon-kur, heh grim, taking ska' ish-veh ashal-veh's bonnet lu sarlah ish-veh abru-kaiden, heh touching ish-veh abru k' wuh shahtau t' ish-veh handkerchief, heh blowing wuh grazhiv ska' ish-veh, heh folding ish-veh tvi-kovtra pok na' laying k', heh smoothing ish-veh don-ka isachya k' u' mau pride u' she kupi possibly ma taken svi' ish-veh sha' isachya kuv she had vesh' wuh vainest heh handsomest t' kosu. Ish-veh ashal-veh vesh' wuh vaksurik glan nuh', embracing ish-veh heh thanking ish-veh, heh protesting tehnat ish-veh taking ni mau trouble na' ish-veh--if kim-shah she goh dared tor tor playfully, il din-tor pross, sorely dash-tor, would ma retired tor ish-veh sha' tvi-shal heh maf-tor. Wuh hassu vesh' wuh vaksurik glan nuh', looking fi' na' au, heh telling din-tor pross uf she spoilt lucie, svi' accents heh k' bezhun ik had u' mau spoiling svi' au u' din-tor pross had, heh would ma had weht kuv ish-veh vesh' tor-yehat. Mr. Lorry vesh' wuh vaksurik glan nuh', beaming na' ek' nash svi' ish-veh pi' wig, heh thanking ish-veh bachelor yel na' having lighted ish-veh svi' ish-veh declining tevun tor wuh ha-kel. Tonk'peh, rai hundreds t' sutra sarlah tor gla-tor wuh sights, heh mr. Lorry glazhau svi' vain na' wuh fulfilment t' din-tor pross's prediction. Aru-yem-wak, heh fam dvun rai hundreds t' sutra. Svi' wuh arrangements t' wuh pi' household, din-tor pross nem-tor falun t' wuh weh-neik shal, heh kwon-hau-ov acquitted herself marvellously. Ish-veh aru-yem, t' wuh maut modest quality, vesh' ni muhl pufas-tor heh ni muhl dvin-tor, heh ni pu svi' ish-veh contrivances, ulef eingelsu heh ulef french, ik nothing kupi nam-tor weh-rom. Din-tor pross's friendship hasu t' wuh thoroughly practical ves, she had ravaged soho heh wuh beyik provinces, svi' psthan t' impoverished french, vi, tempted k' shillings heh ulef-tarkiv, would impart culinary mysteries tor ish-veh. S' aifa nehau sa-fu heh daughters t' gaul, she had acquired such wonderful arts, ik wuh kosu heh ko-kan vi shidau wuh suyu t' domestics fudau ish-veh u' ved wuh sorceress, il cinderella's godmother: vi would satau si' na' wuh kushel, wuh rabbit, wuh sazh il dahkuh s' wuh bah-ker, heh rubah au vi' sovek-vel she sanoi. Fi' sundays, din-tor pross aru-yokul na' wuh hassu's pasu, tonk'peh fi' vath gad persisted svi' taking ish-veh yem na' ri-fainu wak-krus, either svi' wuh weh-neik shal, il svi' ish-veh sha' tvi-shal fi' wuh dahr lan-tol--wuh pla-kur tvi-shal, tor if kling tonk'peh ish-veh ladybird ek'wak nazh-tor admittance. Fi' nash occasion, din-tor pross, responding tor ladybird's vaksurik limuk heh vaksurik urgam tor sanoi ish-veh, unbent exceedingly; ni wuh aru-yem vesh' maut vaksurik, nuh'. Ish-veh vesh' wuh oppressive gad, heh, po' aru-yem, lucie proposed ik wuh wine dang nam-tor fitor ne' wuh sov-hali-lap, heh au dang hayal-tor tra' svi' wuh sov. U' kanok-vei da-tor fi-tor ish-veh, heh revolved pa' ish-veh, au went si' ne' wuh sov-hali-lap, heh she lesh wuh wine ne' na' wuh special rufai t' mr. Lorry. She had installed herself, ein wak fa', u' mr. Lorry's cup-bearer; heh du' au hayal-tor ne' wuh sov-hali-lap, talking, she potau ish-veh makh replenished. Mysterious pla'dor heh shahtau t' kelek peeped na' au u' au variben, heh wuh sov-hali-lap zhal-tor tor au svi' its sha' yut abru' ish-veh patam. Fam dvun, wuh hundreds t' sutra did ri la' themselves. Mr. Darnay presented himself du' au vesh' sitting ne' wuh sov-hali-lap, tonk'peh au vesh' goh veh. Hassu manette poprah ish-veh kindly, heh ni did lucie. Tonk'peh, din-tor pross suddenly became afflicted k' wuh twitching svi' wuh patam heh ak'shem, heh retired vi' wuh kelek. She vesh' ri unfrequently wuh shi-kar-tor t' nash disorder, heh she puvutau ish-veh, svi' familiar conversation, "wuh nunau t' wuh hutau." wuh hassu vesh' svi' ish-veh buhfik nosh, heh glazhau specially nu'ri. Wuh resemblance svi' ish-veh heh lucie vesh' maut karik na' such wak, heh u' au hayal-tor vla k' vla, she leaning fi' ish-veh tipan, heh au resting ish-veh kar fi' wuh pla' t' ish-veh ku-san, ish-veh vesh' maut agreeable tor zavikau wuh likeness. Au had vesh' talking ek' gad, fi' wehk subjects, heh k' ritsuri vivacity. "pray, hassu manette, " leralmin-tor mr. Darnay, u' au hayal-tor ne' wuh sov-hali-lap--heh au leralmin-tor ish-veh svi' wuh malatik pursuit t' wuh ong svi' el'ru, if pavesh-tor tor nam-tor wuh hinek kelek t' london--"ma du gla-tor mau t' wuh kispek?" "lucie heh i ma vesh' tra'; tonk'peh goh casually. Gla-tor etek hiyet t' ish-veh, tor fai-tor ik ish-veh teems k' eku'ko; pi' weht." "i ma vesh' tra', u' du vokau, " leralmin-tor darnay, k' wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut, hi reddening wuh pi' angrily, "svi' wuh'ashiv character, heh ri svi' wuh character ik mazhiv-kur-tor kebitra na' seeing mau t' ish-veh. Au var-tor me wuh curious vel lu i vesh' tra'." "ra vesh' ik?" lucie ya'akash. "svi' tor ein alterations, wuh workmen sarlah fi-tor wuh hinek dungeon, if had vesh', na' wehk tevun, torvau abru heh yen-tor. Kanok kov t' its tvik temok vesh' wein-tor k' inscriptions if had vesh' skrim-tor k' prisoners--kinuf, ahm, complaints, heh prayers. Fi-tor wuh teruk kov svi' wuh vulu t' wuh temok, veh prisoner, vi seemed ki' hal-tor tor execution, had tresahk u' ish-veh kim-shah ar'kadan, rehkuh nuhm. Au vesh' ovsoh k' ein maut ri donku-tor instrument, heh hurriedly, k' wuh unsteady el'ru. Palikauk, au vesh' telv-tor u' d. I. C; tonk'peh, fi' hasu weht carefully linisau, wuh kim-shah nuhm vesh' afer-tor tor nam-tor g. Tra' vesh' rai vipladau il legend t' sovek prisoner k' eifa initials, heh wehk fruitless guesses vesh' tor ra wuh ahm kupi ma vesh'. Na' wu-vath, ish-veh vesh' suggested ik wuh nuhm vesh' ri initials, tonk'peh wuh ovsotik zhit, hil-tor. Wuh lan-tol vesh' linisau maut carefully ne' wuh inscription, heh, svi' wuh terra ne'rak wuh kov, il tile, il ein karf t' paving, vesh' afer-tor wuh vitush t' wuh dun, mingled k' wuh vitush t' wuh pi' leathern nuf il sa'haf. Ra wuh ri-fainu prisoner had written dungi worla nam-tor telv-tor, tonk'peh au had written vel, heh ipik ish-veh maf tor potau ish-veh s' wuh gaoler." "t'nash-veh sa-mekh, " sporiben lucie, "du nam-tor has-bosh!" au had suddenly palikau abru, k' ish-veh el'ru tor ish-veh patam. Ish-veh manner heh ish-veh glazhau ved terrified au ek'. "rai, t'nash-veh tal-kam, ri has-bosh. Tra' nam-tor suk eku-tor t' sov-masu tevan-tor, heh au tor me palikaya. Etek had weh-rom hal-tor svi'." au recovered himself siyah instantly. Sov-masu vesh' really tevan-tor svi' suk eku-tor, heh au gluvau wuh pla' t' ish-veh el'ru k' sov-masu-eku-tor fi' ish-veh. Tonk'peh, au leralmin-tor ri wuh single zhit svi' dzhinaya tor wuh discovery ik had vesh' var-tor t', heh, u' au went vi' wuh kelek, wuh business bezhun t' mr. Lorry either patal-tor, il fancied ish-veh patal-tor, fi' ish-veh limuk, u' ish-veh da-tor na' charles darnay, wuh ka singular glazhau ik had vesh' fi-tor ish-veh lu ish-veh da-tor na' ish-veh svi' wuh tvur t' wuh kelek kelek. Au recovered himself ni sahris, however, ik mr. Lorry had vet-tor t' ish-veh business bezhun. Wuh kar t' wuh pi-maat-kur masuk'veh svi' wuh tvur vesh' ri weht br'xan do au vesh', lu au pehkau ne' ish-veh tor remark tor au ik au vesh' ri wi skan tehnat slight ak'wikmun (kuv au ek'wak would nam-tor), heh ik wuh sov-masu had startled ish-veh. Theris-masu-wak, heh din-tor pross tor theris-masu, k' wuh'ashiv nunau t' wuh hutau fi-tor ish-veh, heh wi rai hundreds t' sutra. Mr. Carton had lounged svi', tonk'peh au tor goh dahkuh. Wuh mu-yor vesh' ni maut sultry, ik hi au hayal-tor k' svep heh krani tu'ash, au vesh' overpowered k' falek. Lu wuh theris-masu-pasu vesh' ovsoh k', au ek' dvun-tor tor veh t' wuh krani, heh glazhau si' vi' wuh ras twilight. Lucie hayal-tor k' ish-veh sa-mekh; darnay hayal-tor be' ish-veh; carton gal-tor tehnat wuh krani. Wuh curtains vesh' wu heh wan-kur, heh ein t' wuh rahm-gusts ik whirled vi' wuh teruk, kum-tor au abru tor wuh abru-tol, heh pral-tor au spo' spectral rala. "wuh sov-masu-eku-tor nam-tor fam dvun tevan-tor, suk, ras, heh zamu, " leralmin-tor hassu manette. "sarlah ish-veh slowly." "sarlah ish-veh surely, " leralmin-tor carton. Au stariben neik, u' sutra watching heh waiting mostly tor; u' sutra svi' wuh gu'gelik tvi-shal, watching heh waiting na' igen-wesh, kwon-hau-ov tor. Tra' vesh' wuh lo'uk brax svi' wuh yut t' sutra speeding maf tor prah rau-nol fa' wuh sahriv shau; wuh wonderful teruk na' vava resounded k' wuh vava t' footsteps coming heh going, wi ri wuh footstep vesh' tra'. "wuh multitude t' sutra, heh wi wuh awek'es!" leralmin-tor darnay, lu au had shroi na' wuh du'. "nam-tor ish-veh ri impressive, mr. Darnay?" ya'akash lucie. "sometimes, i ma hayal-tor la' t' wuh khru, abi' i ma fancied--tonk'peh kauk wuh duvek t' wuh duhik fancy tor me ak'shem-hutau tor-mu-yor, lu ek' nam-tor ni nesh-kur heh solemn--" "kal-tor etek ak'shem-hutau nuh'. Etek lau fai-tor ra ish-veh nam-tor." "ish-veh dungi seem nothing tor du. Such whims nam-tor goh impressive u' etek tveshulau au, i nah-tor; au nam-tor ri tor nam-tor sviribau. I ma sometimes hayal-tor sa'awek la' t' wuh khru, listening, abi' i ma tor wuh vava si' tor nam-tor wuh vava t' ek' wuh footsteps ik nam-tor coming k'-heh-bye vi' etwel ha-tor." "tra' nam-tor wuh lo'uk patreitan coming veh gad vi' etwel ha-tor, kuv ik nam-tor ni, " sydney carton kwul-tor svi', svi' ish-veh moody yut. Wuh footsteps vesh' incessant, heh wuh brax t' au became weht heh weht rapid. Wuh teruk echoed heh re-echoed k' wuh tread t' ash'ya; ein, u' ish-veh seemed, ne' wuh krani; ein, u' ish-veh seemed, svi' wuh tvi-shal; ein coming, ein going, ein breaking ska', ein stopping altogether; ek' svi' wuh irak yut, heh ri veh k'svi glan. "nam-tor ek' aifa footsteps destined tor sarlah tor ek' t' etek, din-tor manette, il nam-tor etek tor dahsaya au akhlami?" "i ri tor fai-tor, mr. Darnay; i var-tor du ish-veh vesh' wuh duhik fancy, tonk'peh du ya'akash na' ish-veh. Lu i ma yielded myself tor ish-veh, i ma vesh' sa'awek, heh yi i ma glenonau au wuh footsteps t' wuh sutra vi nam-tor tor sarlah vi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv, heh t'nash-veh sa-mekh's." "i nem-tor au vi' t'nash-veh!" leralmin-tor carton. "i ya'akash rai deshkau heh tor rai stipulations. Tra' nam-tor wuh lo'uk patreitan kuvish ne' fi-tor etek, din-tor manette, heh gla-tor nash-veh au--k' wuh igen-wesh." au hau wuh kim-shah zhit, po' tra' had vesh' wuh vivid kahai if had shown ish-veh lounging svi' wuh krani. "heh i zhu-tor au!" au hau va'ashiv, po' wuh peal t' rahm. "la' au sarlah, sahris, kei, heh furious!" ish-veh vesh' wuh rush heh roar t' sov-masu ik au typified, heh ish-veh pehkau ish-veh, na' rai spes kupi nam-tor puzhu-tor svi' ish-veh. Wuh memorable sahriv t' rahm heh igen-wesh shau k' ik fnashtaya t' masu, heh tra' vesh' ri wuh moment's tvi-wak svi' tevul, heh yon, heh sov-masu, abi' po' wuh aikum she-tor na' midnight. Wuh lo'uk kus-vakh t' osu paul's vesh' striking veh svi' wuh pa'shu sov, lu mr. Lorry, escorted k' jerry, pid-booted heh kuvish wuh makh-yonet, eku forth fi' ish-veh fun-tvur tor clerkenwell. Tra' vesh' solitary patches t' fau-yut fi' wuh yut svi' soho heh clerkenwell, heh mr. Lorry, mindful t' ash'ya-math, kwon-hau-ov retained jerry na' nash dvin: hi ish-veh vesh' usually performed wuh rom dahkuh wadan earlier. "ra wuh mu-yor ish-veh has vesh'! Siyah wuh mu-yor, jerry, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, "tor katau wuh tevik s' ish-veh shi'vukhut." "i worla gla-tor wuh mu-yor myself, trensu--il wi i ri tor gish tor--ra would tor ik, " kilko-tor jerry. "rom mu-yor, mr. Carton, " leralmin-tor wuh sasu t' business. "rom mu-yor, mr. Darnay. Dungau etek ek'wak gla-tor such wuh mu-yor va'ashiv, teretuhr!" sos'eh. Sos'eh, gla-tor wuh lo'uk patreitan t' sutra k' its rush heh roar, kuvish ne' fi-tor au, nuh'. Chapter vii. Monseigneur svi' kahr monseigneur, veh t' wuh lo'uk s'haile svi' tepul na' wuh kelek, meskarau ish-veh fortnightly reception svi' ish-veh grand hotel svi' paris. Monseigneur vesh' svi' ish-veh tvik tvi-shal, ish-veh sanctuary t' sanctuaries, wuh holiest t' holiests tor wuh patreitan t' worshippers svi' wuh suite t' tvi-shal rik'. Monseigneur vesh' pa' tor nem-tor ish-veh chocolate. Monseigneur kupi vitem-tor wuh lo'uk wehk vel k' ease, heh vesh' k' ein zamu kir kashkau supposed tor nam-tor rather rapidly swallowing france; tonk'peh, ish-veh asal's chocolate kupi ri ni mau u' prah vi' wuh drahk t' monseigneur, rik' wuh mamuk t' kehkuh karik sasu isha wuh fas-tor. Ha. Ish-veh nem-tor kehkuh sasu, ek' kehkuh ablaze k' gorgeous decoration, heh wuh chief t' au unable tor nam-tor k' fewer do dahkuh pi-maat-tukh glantau svi' ish-veh abru'lik, emulative t' wuh thol heh chaste fashion eku k' monseigneur, tor spa-tor wuh kunli chocolate tor monseigneur's bru-lar. Veh lacquey lesh wuh chocolate-sunil vi' wuh sacred la'es; wuh dahr, milled heh frothed wuh chocolate k' wuh pi' instrument au spitau na' ik nam-tor-lof; wuh wuh, presented wuh favoured ru'lut-sai; wuh fourth (au t' wuh dahkuh pi-maat-tukh glantau), mukau wuh chocolate si'. Ish-veh vesh' impossible na' monseigneur tor mazhiv-kur-tor k' veh t' aifa attendants fi' wuh chocolate heh meskaraya ish-veh pid shi ne' wuh krol-tor heavens. Glu would ma vesh' wuh blot fi-tor ish-veh escutcheon kuv ish-veh chocolate had vesh' ignobly bek-tor fi' k' goh rehkuh sasu; au bolau ma tev-tor t' dahkuh. Monseigneur had vesh' si' na' wuh pi' mu'yor-yem kim-shah mu-yor, wilat wuh comedy heh wuh grand opera vesh' charmingly represented. Monseigneur vesh' si' na' wuh pi' mu'yor-yem danik mu-yor, k' sem-rik apc'koik. Ni polite heh ni impressible vesh' monseigneur, ik wuh comedy heh wuh grand opera had irak weht vi-yumuk k' ish-veh svi' wuh tiresome ua'mrki t' fupa s' tek'ik heh fupa s' tsat, do wuh bolau t' ek' france. Wuh kunli circumstance na' france, u' wuh spo' kwon-hau-ov nam-tor na' ek' shasol similarly favoured!--kwon-hau-ov vesh' na' england (k' yut t' li-fal), svi' wuh regretted gad t' wuh merry stuart vi makau ish-veh. Monseigneur had veh truly thol idea t' paik tsuri business, if vesh', tor kal-tor kanok-vei hal-tor fi' svi' its sha' yut; t' particular tsuri business, monseigneur had wuh vath truly thol idea ik ish-veh bolau ek' hal-tor ish-veh yut--palutunau tor ish-veh sha' tepul heh abru'lik. T' ish-veh pleasures, paik heh particular, monseigneur had wuh vath truly thol idea, ik wuh panu vesh' tor na' au. Wuh text t' ish-veh zek (rubitau s' wuh tveshik k' goh wuh pronoun, if nam-tor ri mau) sahr-tor: "wuh terra heh wuh fulness thereof nam-tor t'nash-veh, saith monseigneur." wi, monseigneur had slowly afer-tor ik vulgar embarrassments crept vi' ish-veh tek'ik, fi' awek heh tsuri; heh au had, u' tor fi' mohrn t' tek'ik, puk'ai'la himself perforce k' wuh uroshitausu-paik. U' tor donkes-tor tsuri, fai'ei monseigneur kupi ri tor sovek-vel na' ek' t' au, heh bolau consequently kal-tor au si' tor somebody vi kupi; u' tor donkes-tor awek, fai'ei uroshitausu-kahr-lan vesh' don-ka, heh monseigneur, po' generations t' lo'uk luxury heh kodona, vesh' growing ri donku-tor. Hence monseigneur had taken ish-veh ko-kai s' wuh convent, du' tra' vesh' wi wak tor ward ska' wuh impending veil, wuh cheapest ain she kupi sai-vel-tor, heh had bestowed ish-veh u' wuh prize fi-tor wuh maut don-ka uroshitausu-paik, ri donku-tor svi' skan. If uroshitausu-paik, carrying wuh appropriate cane k' wuh pi-maat-kur savas fi' wuh fik t' ish-veh, vesh' i' among wuh apc'koik svi' wuh sik tvi-shal, mau prostrated fa' k' mankind--kwon-hau-ov kaulaik superior mankind t' wuh khaf t' monseigneur, vi, ish-veh sha' ko-telsu vinan-tor, glazhau ne' fi-tor ish-veh k' wuh loftiest contempt. Wuh sumptuous sasu vesh' wuh uroshitausu-paik. Reh-leh jarel lam-tor svi' ish-veh stables, dah-leh-kehkuh sa domestics hayal-tor svi' ish-veh tvur, shehkuh ak'shem-kosu bek-tor fi' ish-veh ko-telsu. U' veh vi pretended tor tor nothing tonk'peh plunder heh forage wilat au kupi, wuh uroshitausu-paik--howsoever ish-veh matrimonial relations conduced tor shilaik morality--vesh' k'puu wuh greatest reality among wuh personages vi attended na' wuh hotel t' monseigneur ik gad. Na', wuh tvi-shal, hi wuh vaksurik scene tor glazhau na', heh tong'av k' kanok el'mish t' decoration ik wuh zahvan heh renkup'es t' wuh wak kupi achieve, vesh', svi' yeht'es, ri wuh ralash business; panah-tor k' sovek dzhinaya tor wuh scarecrows svi' wuh a'cit heh nightcaps kitok-wilat (heh ri ni irak ska', either, tonk'peh ik wuh watching kispek t' notre dame, siyah ka-irik s' wuh dahkuh mairik, kupi gla-tor au fi'), au would ma vesh' wuh exceedingly uncomfortable business--kuv ik kupi ma vesh' anybody's business, na' wuh kelek t' monseigneur. Askital officers destitute t' askital fai-tukh; naval officers k' rai idea t' wuh hali; civil officers rik' wuh notion t' tek'ik; brazen ecclesiastics, t' wuh rasahkos panu worldly, k' sensual bezhun, thal lahv, heh looser ha-tor; ek' totally unfit na' ish-veh several callings, ek' lying horribly svi' pretending tor belong tor au, tonk'peh ek' nearly il remotely t' wuh zek t' monseigneur, heh therefore foisted fi' ek' tsuri employments s' if sovek-vel vesh' tor nam-tor prah; aifa vesh' tor nam-tor var-tor ska' k' wuh nosahp heh wuh nosahp. Sutra ri iyi tersau k' monseigneur il wuh fupa s', wi kaing unconnected k' sovek-vel ik vesh' yeht, il k' ha-tor be' dvun-tor svi' travelling k' sovek zehik fau-yut tor sovek yeht terrupik shaht, vesh' rai lehkuh abundant. Hassu vi tor lo'uk fortunes s' dainty remedies na' glenonik disorders ik worla nam-tor, abru'teruklar-ru'lut fi-tor ish-veh courtly hasausu svi' wuh ante-tvi-shal t' monseigneur. Salehmek vi had discovered kanok ves t' remedy na' wuh pi' ek'rasah k' if wuh fupa s' vesh' estuhl, kaula wuh remedy t' setting tor ar'kadan svi' earnest tor gir si' wuh single sin, mukau ish-veh distracting babble vi' sovek kaluk au kupi ti meskaraya t', na' wuh reception t' monseigneur. Unbelieving philosophers vi vesh' remodelling wuh panu k' zhit, heh tor nop-kispek t' babel tor wef wuh igen k', variben k' unbelieving meil-talsu vi had wuh bezhun fi' wuh transmutation t' mokev, na' nash wonderful hohnaya accumulated k' monseigneur. Exquisite gentlemen t' wuh finest breeding, if vesh' na' ik remarkable wak--heh has vesh' opi'--tor nam-tor fainu k' its savas t' indifference tor kanok malatik subject t' komihn eku'ko, vesh' svi' wuh danik exemplary fupa s' t' exhaustion, na' wuh hotel t' monseigneur. Such ha-kel had aifa vuhnauk notabilities losrak za' au svi' wuh tok-ti panu t' paris, ik wuh zamasu among wuh assembled devotees t' monseigneur--forming wuh goodly ulef t' wuh polite apc'koik--would ma afer-tor ish-veh lerash tor discover among wuh ha'su t' ik ek'kal veh solitary ko-telsu, vi, svi' ish-veh manners heh appearance, puma tor hasu wuh ko-mekh. Indeed, kaula na' wuh mere bae'cok t' bringing wuh troublesome creature vi' nash panu--if tor ri hal-tor irak na' wuh realisation t' wuh ahm t' ko-mekh--tra' vesh' rai such vel fainu tor wuh fashion. Peasant kosu potau wuh unfashionable kan-bu ikap-tor, heh katau au abru, heh sem-rik-tor grandmammas t' sheh-leh sai-vel-tor heh supped u' na' dah-leh. Wuh leprosy t' unreality disfigured kanok komihn creature svi' attendance fi-tor monseigneur. Svi' wuh outermost tvi-shal vesh' ulef wuh dozen exceptional sutra vi had had, na' wuh zamu tevun, ein vague misgiving svi' au ik vel svi' paik vesh' going rather riyeht. U' wuh promising yut t' setting au gas'rak, ulef t' wuh ulef-dozen had shetau kisau t' wuh fantastic sect t' convulsionists, heh vesh' kauk yi panahik k'svi themselves whether au dang puhsh, reshan, roar, heh da-tor cataleptic fi' wuh gla-tor--thereby setting abru wuh highly intelligible ozh-lehk tor wuh fa-wak, na' monseigneur's guidance. Isha aifa dervishes, vesh' vath rehkuh vi had rushed vi' wuh'ashiv sect, if nodolau tukh k' wuh jargon pa' "wuh centre t' yeht'es: " holding ik sasu had prah s' wuh centre t' yeht'es--if did ri bolaya mau demonstration--tonk'peh had ri prah s' wuh pa-thon t'da-kuv, heh ik au vesh' tor nam-tor potau s' hashan s' wuh pa-thon t'da-kuv, heh vesh' kauk tor nam-tor shoved pla' vi' wuh centre, k' fasting heh seeing t' tam'a. Among aifa, accordingly, mau discoursing k' tam'a went fi'--heh ish-veh did wuh panu t' rom if worla became manifest. Tonk'peh, wuh comfort vesh', ik ek' wuh apc'koik na' wuh grand hotel t' monseigneur vesh' perfectly sai-vel-tor. Kuv wuh gad t' judgment had goh vesh' ascertained tor nam-tor wuh sai-vel gad, kanok-veh tra' would ma vesh' eternally yeht. Such frizzling heh powdering heh sticking abru t' isachya, such delicate complexions artificially korsau heh nodolau, such gallant shek tor glazhau na', heh such delicate dor tor wuh kash-ral t' fnish-tor, would surely potau sovek-vel going, na' ek'wak heh ek'wak. Wuh exquisite gentlemen t' wuh finest breeding sai-vel-tor pi' pendent trinkets ik chinked u' au languidly dvun-tor; aifa pi-maat-kur fetters rang spo' taluhk pi' kus-vakh; heh ra k' ik ringing, heh k' wuh rustle t' silk heh brocade heh tok-ti linen, tra' vesh' wuh nuv svi' wuh sov ik fanned osu antoine heh ish-veh devouring avon irak maf. Sai-vel vesh' wuh veh unfailing talisman heh sem-rik nam-tor-tor na' keeping ek' vel svi' ish-veh shitau. Kanok-veh vesh' sai-vel-tor na' wuh fancy rin'k'n ik vesh' worla tor trasha ska'. S' wuh palace t' wuh tuileries, k'fai monseigneur heh wuh bosh kelek, k'fai wuh tvi-shal, wuh tribunals t' yeht-gav, heh ek' shila'es (kaula wuh scarecrows), wuh fancy rin'k'n tev-tor tor wuh tsuri tostausu: vi, svi' pursuance t' wuh sem-rik, vesh' required tor officiate "frizzled, powdered, svi' wuh pi-maat-tukh-laced tor-pal, spol-tor, heh wan-kur silk stockings." na' wuh geld-stau-nentu heh wuh halek--wuh la'ash vesh' wuh rarity--monsieur paris, u' ish-veh vesh' wuh episcopal nuk among ish-veh sa-kai professors t' wuh provinces, monsieur orleans, heh wuh shom, tor vutau ish-veh, presided svi' nash dainty sai-vel. Heh vi among wuh apc'koik na' monseigneur's reception svi' ik leh- steh hundred heh eightieth tevun t' etwel s'haile, kupi possibly vet, ik wuh torektra rooted svi' wuh frizzled hangman, powdered, pi-maat-tukh-laced, spol-tor, heh wan-kur-silk stockinged, would gla-tor wuh maut yel si'! Monseigneur having eased ish-veh kehkuh sasu t' ish-veh burdens heh taken ish-veh chocolate, aisha wuh svep t' wuh holiest t' holiests tor nam-tor lehm-tor tu'ash, heh issued forth. Yi, ra nekhaya, ra cringing heh fawning, ra servility, ra abject humiliation! U' tor bowing ne' svi' ak'shem heh tam'a, nothing svi' ik yut vesh' losrak na' sha-ka-ri--if lau ma vesh' veh among vath utvau po wuh worshippers t' monseigneur worla troubled ish-veh. Bestowing wuh zhit t' ugaya la' heh wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut tra', wuh zhal fi' veh kunli kafeh heh wuh pral t' wuh el'ru fi' wuh'ashiv, monseigneur affably be' dvun-tor k'fai ish-veh tvi-shal tor wuh remote shal t' wuh pa-thon t'da-kuv t' yeht'es. Tra', monseigneur da-tor, heh sarlah pla' va'ashiv, heh ni svi' due rivak t' wak prah himself ikap'uh t'du ru'lut svi' ish-veh sanctuary k' wuh chocolate sprites, heh vesh' gla-tor rai weht. Wuh gluvaya hasu abru', wuh nuv svi' wuh sov became ved wuh pi' sahriv, heh wuh taluhk pi' kus-vakh went ringing downstairs. Tra' vesh' ak tonk'peh veh person losrak t' ek' wuh patreitan, heh au, k' ish-veh taik ne' ish-veh kar heh ish-veh snuff-natuhn svi' ish-veh el'ru, slowly be' dvun-tor among wuh haulat fi' ish-veh yut si'. "i vaikau du, " leralmin-tor nash person, stopping na' wuh kim-shah svep fi' ish-veh yut, heh turning svi' wuh kharat t' wuh sanctuary, "tor wuh e'shua!" k' ik, au hutau wuh snuff s' ish-veh ozh u' kuv au had shaken wuh grazhiv s' ish-veh ash'ya, heh quietly lates-tor downstairs. Au vesh' wuh sasu t' pa' sheh-leh, handsomely sai-vel-tor, haughty svi' manner, heh k' wuh limuk spo' wuh tok-ti limein. Wuh limuk t' wuh fnaglaik paleness; kanok feature svi' ish-veh clearly mesprah; veh eku sagluvaya fi' ish-veh. Wuh han, beautifully shidau vathru, vesh' maut slightly k'hy na' wuh fik t' tik nostril. Svi' eifa dahkuh compressions, il dints, wuh goh pi' rubah ik wuh limuk ek'wak gluvau, resided. Au persisted svi' rubai kur sometimes, heh au would nam-tor occasionally eiksha heh contracted k' vel spo' wuh faint gaya; yi, au mazhiv-kur-tor wuh glazhau t' treachery, heh cruelty, tor wuh bosh countenance. Linisau k' attention, its tsoh t' helping such wuh glazhau vesh' tor nam-tor afer-tor svi' wuh zehl t' wuh ru'lut, heh wuh zehl t' wuh pa-yut t' wuh bezhun, hasu mau nuh' yutik heh wonil; fam dvun, svi' wuh daya t' wuh limuk tor, ish-veh vesh' wuh handsome limuk, heh wuh remarkable veh. Its owner went downstairs vi' wuh courtyard, prah vi' ish-veh carriage, heh drove maf. Ri wehk sutra had variben k' ish-veh na' wuh reception; au had lam-tor svi' wuh pi' ret k'wuhli, heh monseigneur lau ma vesh' warmer svi' ish-veh manner. Ish-veh saudau, ne' wuh circumstances, rather agreeable tor ish-veh tor gla-tor wuh tsuri sutra pusaganau fa' ish-veh jarel, heh k'ashiv barely escaping s' hasu sahr-tor ne'. Ish-veh sasu drove u' kuv au vesh' charging wuh nemut, heh wuh furious recklessness t' wuh sasu katau rai rihamau vi' wuh limuk, il tor wuh bru-lar, t' wuh trensu. Wuh complaint had sometimes tor itself zhu-yehat, kauk svi' ik zhu-fam kahr heh dumb ya'shakhuv, ik, svi' wuh wonil yut rik' footways, wuh kei patrician custom t' lerash driving vitehvar-tor heh maimed wuh mere vulgar svi' wuh barbarous manner. Tonk'peh, zamu tun-tor hiyet na' ik tor nah-tor t' ish-veh wuh dahr wak, heh, svi' nash tukh, u' svi' ek' vath, wuh tsuri wretches vesh' losrak tor prah s' ish-veh rihag'es u' au kupi. K' wuh kwai rattle heh clatter, heh wuh inhuman abandonment t' consideration ri hagik tor nam-tor ken-tor svi' aifa gad, wuh carriage dashed k'fai yut heh swept pauk teruk, k' kosu screaming fa' ish-veh, heh sasu clutching tik vath heh clutching kanu s' its yut. Na' kim-shah, swooping na' wuh yut teruk k' wuh mashulek, veh t' its halek sarlah tor wuh sickening pi' jolt, heh tra' vesh' wuh ral maf s' wuh su'etek t' spes, heh wuh jarel reared heh taul-tor. Tonk'peh na' wuh latter inconvenience, wuh carriage probably would ri ma pehkau; carriages vesh' k'ashiv fainu tor yetur fi', heh trasha ish-veh wounded za', heh po ri? Tonk'peh wuh koltha valet had prah ne' svi' wuh brax, heh tra' vesh' dah-leh el'ru na' wuh jarel' bridles. "ra has hal-tor riyeht?" leralmin-tor monsieur, calmly looking si'. Wuh ha-vol sasu svi' wuh nightcap had kum-tor abru wuh uzh'a'lek s' among wuh ash'ya t' wuh jarel, heh had laid ish-veh fi' wuh ne-shal t' wuh mashulek, heh vesh' ne' svi' wuh vral heh masupik, howling abru' ish-veh spo' wuh kwai aushfa. "pardon, monsieur wuh marquis!" leralmin-tor wuh ragged heh nepik sasu, "ish-veh nam-tor wuh kan." "po tor au tor ik abominable ralash? Nam-tor ish-veh ish-veh kan?" "tobeg me, monsieur wuh marquis--ish-veh nam-tor wuh pity--ha." wuh mashulek vesh' wuh pi' snem-tor; na' wuh yut tu'ash, wilat ish-veh vesh', vi' wuh ret ein lehkuh il leh-dah ker keh-vla. U' wuh ha-vol sasu suddenly prah abru s' wuh solektra, heh sarlah sahran na' wuh carriage, monsieur wuh marquis clapped ish-veh el'ru na' wuh instant fi' ish-veh shek-hilt. "pustau!" shrieked wuh sasu, svi' kwai desperation, extending fi' kar na' ish-veh wu-vath abru' ish-veh patam, heh staring na' ish-veh. "tevik!" wuh sutra a'ing pauk, heh glazhau na' monsieur wuh marquis. Tra' vesh' nothing revealed k' wuh wehk bezhun ik glazhau na' ish-veh tonk'peh watchfulness heh eagerness; tra' vesh' rai visible menacing il reshan. Neither did wuh sutra leralmin sovek-vel; po' wuh wuh'rak maf, au had vesh' ralash-fam, heh au hafau ni. Wuh spes t' wuh nepik sasu vi had spoken, vesh' pa'ash heh fnau svi' its mairik nekhaya. Monsieur wuh marquis sahr-tor ish-veh bezhun abru' au ek', u' kuv au had vesh' mere rats sasarlah t' ish-veh razh. Au nem-tor si' ish-veh sa'haf. "ish-veh nam-tor wehtsuri tor me, " leralmin-tor au, "ik du sutra fam yehat nem-tor tun t' yourselves heh ish-veh kanu. Veh il wuh vath t' du nam-tor na' ek'wak svi' wuh yut. Uf tor i fai-tor ra dash du ma ovsoh t'nash-veh jarel. Gla-tor! Mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ik." au threw si' wuh pi-maat-tukh di'kaudj na' wuh valet tor abrashau, heh ek' wuh patam craned fa'rak ik ek' wuh bezhun lau glazhau ne' na' ish-veh u' ish-veh tevan-tor. Wuh ha-vol sasu puvutau si' va'ashiv k' wuh danik unearthly maf, "tevik!" au vesh' pehkau k' wuh sahris lashan t' wuh'ashiv sasu, na' ik wuh shom tor yut. Fi' seeing ish-veh, wuh miserable creature tevan-tor fi-tor ish-veh tipan, sobbing heh maf-tor, heh pointing tor wuh mashulek, wilat ein kosu vesh' stooping abru' wuh motionless uzh'a'lek, heh dvun-tor kogavik pa' ish-veh. Au vesh' u' ralash-fam, however, u' wuh sasu. "i fai-tor ek', i fai-tor ek', " leralmin-tor wuh kim-shah comer. "nam-tor wuh kyi'i sasu, t'nash-veh gaspard! Ish-veh nam-tor weh-rom na' wuh ri donku-tor pi' plaything tor tev-tor ni, do tor ha-tor. Ish-veh has tev-tor svi' wuh moment rik' kusut. Kupi ish-veh ma ha-tor wuh wadan u' kunling?" "du nam-tor wuh philosopher, du tra', " leralmin-tor wuh marquis, smiling. "uf tor au vutau du?" "au vutau me defarge." "t' ra trade?" "monsieur wuh marquis, vendor t' wine." "abrashau ik, philosopher heh vendor t' wine, " leralmin-tor wuh marquis, throwing ish-veh wuh'ashiv pi-maat-tukh di'kaudj, "heh spend ish-veh u' du dungi. Wuh jarel tra'; nam-tor au gas'rak?" rik' deigning tor glazhau na' wuh assemblage wuh dahr wak, monsieur wuh marquis gal-tor pla' svi' ish-veh ku-san, heh vesh' aishan hasu driven maf k' wuh sov t' wuh gentleman vi had accidentally shau ein tsuri vel, heh had vlitau na' ish-veh, heh kupi afford tor vlitau na' ish-veh; lu ish-veh ease vesh' suddenly ertau k' wuh di'kaudj hashan vi' ish-veh carriage, heh ringing fi' its lan-tol. "meskaraya!" leralmin-tor monsieur wuh marquis. "meskaraya wuh jarel! Vi threw ik?" au glazhau tor wuh gla-tor wilat defarge wuh vendor t' wine had lam-tor, wuh moment fa'; tonk'peh wuh wretched sa-mekh vesh' grovelling fi' ish-veh limuk fi' wuh pavement svi' ik gla-tor, heh wuh khlop ik lam-tor be' ish-veh vesh' wuh khlop t' wuh gu'gelik stout kosu, knitting. "du dogs!" leralmin-tor wuh marquis, tonk'peh smoothly, heh k' wuh unchanged khom, kaula u' tor wuh gla-tor fi' ish-veh han: "i would fau abru' sovek t' du maut willingly, heh ek'stau du s' wuh terra. Kuv i fai-tor if rascal threw na' wuh carriage, heh kuv ik brigand vesh' sufficiently be' ish-veh, au dang nam-tor plesh-tor ne' wuh halek." ni cowed vesh' ish-veh nosh, heh ni wu heh lerash ish-veh veshtaya t' ra such wuh sasu kupi tor tor au, k'svi wuh tor-gav heh mesakh ish-veh, ik ri wuh spes, il wuh el'ru, il kauk wuh bezhun vesh' ashenau. Among wuh sasu, ri veh. Tonk'peh wuh kosu vi lam-tor knitting glazhau abru steadily, heh glazhau wuh marquis svi' wuh limuk. Ish-veh vesh' ri na' ish-veh dignity tor beglanau ish-veh; ish-veh contemptuous bezhun be' dvun-tor abru' ish-veh, heh abru' ek' wuh vath rats; heh au gal-tor pla' svi' ish-veh ku-san va'ashiv, heh mazhiv-kur-tor wuh zhit "hal-tor fi'!" au vesh' driven fi', heh vath carriages sarlah whirling k' svi' sahris succession; wuh minister, wuh fupa s'-salehmek, wuh uroshitausu-paik, wuh hassu, wuh lawyer, wuh ecclesiastic, wuh grand opera, wuh comedy, wuh bosh fancy rin'k'n svi' wuh ugelik continuous yumaya, sarlah whirling k'. Wuh rats had crept s' ish-veh razh tor glazhau fi', heh au hafau looking fi' na' wadan; ask'ersu heh police k'ashiv be' dvun-tor svi' au heh wuh spectacle, heh tor wuh foshek za' if au slunk, heh k'fai if au peeped. Wuh sa-mekh had wu ago taken abru ish-veh uzh'a'lek heh bidden himself maf k' ish-veh, lu wuh kosu vi had palutunau wuh uzh'a'lek du' ish-veh ti fi' wuh nen t' wuh mashulek, hayal-tor tra' watching wuh sahran t' wuh masu heh wuh rolling t' wuh fancy rin'k'n--lu wuh veh kosu vi had lam-tor conspicuous, knitting, fam dvun knitted fi' k' wuh steadfastness t' buk. Wuh masu t' wuh mashulek sahr-tor, wuh swift pilash sahr-tor, wuh gad sahr-tor vi' khru, ni mau ha'kiv svi' wuh kahr sahr-tor vi' tevakh fupa s' tor-go, wak heh mashen bek-tor na' rai sasu, wuh rats vesh' sleeping ikap-tor teretuhr svi' ish-veh gu'gelik razh va'ashiv, wuh fancy rin'k'n vesh' lighted abru na' mu'yor-yem, ek' vel sahr-tor ish-veh rivak. Chapter viii. Monseigneur svi' wuh shasol wuh vaksurik landscape, k' wuh corn ugelik svi' ish-veh, tonk'peh ri abundant. Patches t' ri donku-tor rye wilat corn dang ma vesh', patches t' ri donku-tor peas heh beans, patches t' danik dirik sazh substitutes na' kap-yar. Fi' inanimate malat, u' fi' wuh sasu heh kosu vi sokasitau ish-veh, wuh prevalent tendency na' wuh appearance t' vegetating unwillingly--wuh dejected disposition tor mazhiv-kur-tor abru, heh wither maf. Monsieur wuh marquis svi' ish-veh travelling carriage (if lau ma vesh' lighter), conducted k' kehkuh lehk-jarel heh dahkuh postilions, fagged abru wuh menal kunel. Wuh blush fi' wuh countenance t' monsieur wuh marquis vesh' rai impeachment t' ish-veh pid breeding; ish-veh vesh' ri s' k'svi; ish-veh vesh' occasioned k' wuh sik circumstance mesakh ish-veh tash--wuh setting yel. Wuh tev-tor kwul-tor ni brilliantly vi' wuh travelling carriage lu ish-veh nazh-tor wuh kunel-fik, ik its occupant vesh' steeped svi' hirat-kur. "ish-veh dungi tev-tor si', " leralmin-tor monsieur wuh marquis, glancing na' ish-veh el'ru, "directly." svi' daya, wuh yel vesh' ni neik ik ish-veh spis-tor na' wuh moment. Lu wuh ras zaseshau had vesh' namishau tor wuh halek, heh wuh carriage slid ne' kunel, k' wuh cinderous fnish-tor, svi' wuh wan t' grazhiv, wuh yon-kur min trashu sahris; wuh yel heh wuh marquis going ne' teretuhr, tra' vesh' rai min losrak lu wuh zaseshau vesh' taken ska'. Tonk'peh, tra' hafau wuh pushau shasol, vakh heh tu'ash, wuh pi' pi'kahr na' wuh lanet t' wuh kunel, wuh sax'ksei fnashtaya heh shen mesakh ish-veh, wuh church-kispek, wuh salan-grazhakel, wuh laptra na' wuh a'vesh', heh wuh crag k' wuh klomak fi' ish-veh nam-tor-tor u' wuh prison. Pauk fi-tor ek' aifa darkening vel u' wuh mu-yor drew fi', wuh marquis glazhau, k' wuh sov t' veh vi vesh' coming be' ha-kel. Wuh pi'kahr had its veh ri donku-tor yut, k' its ri donku-tor brewery, ri donku-tor tannery, ri donku-tor tavern, ri donku-tor tihet-ker na' gol'dvunek t' lehk-jarel, ri donku-tor mashulek, ek' tsuri ri donku-tor latva. Ish-veh had its ri donku-tor sutra nuh'. Ek' its sutra vesh' ri donku-tor, heh wehk t' au vesh' sitting na' ish-veh svep, shredding spare onions heh wuh spo' na' mu'yor-yem, du' wehk vesh' na' wuh mashulek, washing mor, heh yar, heh sovek such pi' yieldings t' wuh terra ik kupi nam-tor yokul. Expressive glat t' ra tor au ri donku-tor, vesh' ri wanting; wuh tax na' wuh fupa s', wuh tax na' wuh church, wuh tax na' wuh s'haile, tax local heh tax paik, vesh' tor nam-tor vlitau la' heh tor nam-tor vlitau tra', fupa s' solemn inscription svi' wuh pi' pi'kahr, abi' wuh wonder vesh', ik tra' vesh' sovek pi'kahr losrak unswallowed. Zamu kanu vesh' tor nam-tor gla-tor, heh rai dogs. U' tor wuh sasu heh kosu, ish-veh dvel fi' terra vesh' fupa s' svi' wuh prospect--ha'kiv fi' wuh lowest zhil ik kupi potun-tor ish-veh, ne' svi' wuh pi' pi'kahr ne' wuh mill; il captivity heh tevakh svi' wuh abrupik prison fi' wuh crag. Heralded k' wuh skladasu svi' storilaya, heh k' wuh cracking t' ish-veh postilions' wonil-zehl, if twined oluhk-spo' pa' ish-veh patam svi' wuh khru sov, u' kuv sarlah ish-veh attended k' wuh furies, monsieur wuh marquis drew abru svi' ish-veh travelling carriage na' wuh posting-kelek temep. Ish-veh vesh' lerash k' wuh mashulek, heh wuh peasants suspended ish-veh el'toraya tor glazhau na' ish-veh. Au glazhau na' au, heh gla-tor svi' au, rik' fai-tor ish-veh, wuh vohris sure filing ne' t' misery-worn limuk heh khlop, ik vesh' tor tor wuh meagreness t' frenchmen wuh eingelsu superstition if dang rish-tor wuh yeht'es k'fai wuh buhfik krus t' wuh hundred tevun. Monsieur wuh marquis vishizhau ish-veh bezhun abru' wuh nepik limuk ik tevan-tor fa' ish-veh, u' wuh spo' t' himself had tevan-tor fa' monseigneur t' wuh kelek--goh wuh natyan vesh', ik aifa limuk tevan-tor goh tor dash heh ri tor propitiate--lu wuh grizzled mender t' wuh fau-yut hau wuh travek. "katau me hither ik katravahsu!" leralmin-tor wuh marquis tor wuh skladasu. Wuh katravahsu vesh' katau, taik svi' el'ru, heh wuh vath katravahsu a'ing pauk tor glazhau heh shroi, svi' wuh manner t' wuh sutra na' wuh paris mashulek. "i be' dvun-tor du fi' wuh fau-yut?" "monseigneur, ish-veh nam-tor yeht. I had wuh dor t' hasu be' dvun-tor fi' wuh fau-yut." "coming abru wuh kunel, heh na' wuh fik t' wuh kunel, fi'?" "monseigneur, ish-veh nam-tor yeht." "ra did du glazhau na', ni fixedly?" "monseigneur, i glazhau na' wuh sasu." au stooped wuh pi', heh k' ish-veh tattered pla-kur taik sfekau ne' wuh carriage. Ek' ish-veh katravahsu stooped tor glazhau ne' wuh carriage. "ra sasu, pig? Heh po glazhau tra'?" "pardon, monseigneur; au swung k' wuh naf-elakh t' wuh ash'el--wuh zaseshau." "vi?" halishau wuh traveller. "monseigneur, wuh sasu." "lau wuh e'shua lesh maf aifa idiots! Uf tor du vutau wuh sasu? Du fai-tor ek' wuh sasu t' nash krus t' wuh shasol. Vi vesh' au?" "ish-veh clemency, monseigneur! Au vesh' ri t' nash krus t' wuh shasol. T' ek' wuh gad t' t'nash-veh ha'kiv, i worla gla-tor ish-veh." "swinging k' wuh naf-elakh? Tor nam-tor suffocated?" "k' ish-veh gracious permission, ik vesh' wuh wonder t' ish-veh, monseigneur. Ish-veh patam hanging abru'--spo' nash!" au da-tor himself sideways tor wuh carriage, heh gal-tor pla', k' ish-veh limuk lehm-tor abru tor wuh igen, heh ish-veh patam hanging ne'; yi recovered himself, fumbled k' ish-veh taik, heh tor wuh kes-wun. "ra vesh' au spo'?" "monseigneur, au vesh' whiter do wuh miller. Ek' wein-tor k' grazhiv, wan-kur u' wuh spectre, ha-vol u' wuh spectre!" wuh bikuv torvau wuh immense kashan svi' wuh pi' patreitan; tonk'peh ek' bezhun, rik' comparing pitoh k' vath bezhun, glazhau na' monsieur wuh marquis.
