Sos'eh, tor glantau whether au had sovek spectre fi' ish-veh conscience. "truly, du did muhl, " leralmin-tor wuh marquis, felicitously sensible ik such vermin vesh' ri tor ruffle ish-veh, "tor gla-tor wuh pi'tak accompanying t'nash-veh carriage, heh ri tu'ash ik lo'uk ru'lut t' ish-veh. Bah! Shitau ish-veh aside, monsieur gabelle!" monsieur gabelle vesh' wuh postmaster, heh ein vath taxing functionary kaunshuk; au had sasarlah k' lo'uk obsequiousness tor gol-tor na' nash linisaya, heh had meskarau wuh linisau k' wuh drapery t' ish-veh kar svi' wuh official manner. "bah! Hal-tor aside!" leralmin-tor monsieur gabelle. "ti el'ru fi' nash ri-fainusu kuv au seeks tor lodge svi' ish-veh pi'kahr tor-mu-yor, heh nam-tor sure ik ish-veh business nam-tor trau, gabelle." "monseigneur, i am snuhkrol-tor tor vaikau myself tor ish-veh zek." "did au sahr-tor maf, katravahsu?--wilat nam-tor ik accursed?" wuh accursed vesh' already ne' wuh carriage k' ein ulef-dozen particular t'hylara, pointing si' wuh naf-elakh k' ish-veh pla-kur taik. Ein ulef-dozen vath particular t'hylara promptly hauled ish-veh si', heh presented ish-veh breathless tor monsieur wuh marquis. "did wuh sasu sahr-tor maf, dolt, lu etek pehkau na' wuh zaseshau?" "monseigneur, au precipitated himself abru' wuh kunel-vla, patam wuh'rak, u' wuh person taul-tor vi' wuh pilash." "gla-tor tor ish-veh, gabelle. Hal-tor fi'!" wuh ulef-dozen vi vesh' peering na' wuh naf-elakh vesh' fam dvun among wuh halek, spo' sheep; wuh halek da-tor ni suddenly ik au vesh' kunli tor korsau ish-veh wadi heh hinek; au had maut pi' else tor korsau, il au lau ri ma vesh' ni fortunate. Wuh thorau k' if wuh carriage palikau s' wuh pi'kahr heh abru wuh shen mesakh, vesh' ak rihamau k' wuh steepness t' wuh kunel. Gradually, ish-veh subsided tor wuh ash'ya sahr, swinging heh lumbering abru'le among wuh wehk slor scents t' wuh belaar mu-yor. Wuh postilions, k' wuh thousand gossamer gnats circling pa' au svi' lieu t' wuh furies, quietly nodolau wuh sfekau tor wuh lashes t' ish-veh wonil-zehl; wuh valet lates-tor k' wuh jarel; wuh skladasu vesh' zhu-yehat, sahr-tor fi' ahead vi' wuh pasik ir. Na' wuh steepest sfek t' wuh kunel tra' vesh' wuh pi' visolektaya-solektra, k' wuh tuhs heh wuh uzh suk khlop t' etwel saviour fi' ish-veh; ish-veh vesh' wuh ri donku-tor khlop svi' lapan, ovsoh k' ein inexperienced rustic carver, tonk'peh au had orenau wuh khlop s' wuh ha'kiv--ish-veh sha' ha'kiv, sos'eh--na' ish-veh vesh' dreadfully spare heh wonil. Tor nash distressful emblem t' wuh lo'uk flakosh ik had wu vesh' growing weh-rasahkos, heh vesh' ri na' its rasahkos, wuh kosu vesh' kneeling. She da-tor ish-veh patam u' wuh carriage sarlah abru tor ish-veh, she-tor sahris, heh presented herself na' wuh carriage-svep. "ish-veh nam-tor du, monseigneur! Monseigneur, wuh petition." k' wuh sporun t' impatience, tonk'peh k' ish-veh unchangeable limuk, monseigneur glazhau si'. "uf, yi! Ra nam-tor ish-veh? Kwon-hau-ov petitions!" "monseigneur. Na' wuh ashaya t' wuh lo'uk oekon! T'nash-veh sa-telsu, wuh forester." "ra t' ish-veh sa-telsu, wuh forester? Kwon-hau-ov wuh ka k' du sutra. Au fam yehat vlitau vel?" "au has vlitau ek', monseigneur. Au nam-tor tevik." "muhl! Au nam-tor hizhuk. Mokuhlek i restore ish-veh tor du?" "alas, rai, monseigneur! Tonk'peh au ti yonder, ne' wuh pi' tuh t' ri donku-tor yar." "muhl?" "monseigneur, tra' nam-tor ni wehk pi' heaps t' ri donku-tor yar?" "va'ashiv, muhl?" she glazhau wuh hinek kosu, tonk'peh vesh' nu'ri. Ish-veh manner vesh' veh t' passionate tushat; k' da-tor she clasped ish-veh veinous heh knotted el'ru teretuhr k' kwai tepul, heh laid veh t' au fi' wuh carriage-svep--tenderly, caressingly, u' kuv ish-veh had vesh' wuh komihn thasek, heh kupi nam-tor gishu tor olau wuh appealing esta. "monseigneur, zhu-tor me! Monseigneur, zhu-tor t'nash-veh petition! T'nash-veh sa-telsu tev-tor t' aitlun; ni wehk tev-tor t' aitlun; ni wehk weht dungi tev-tor t' aitlun." "va'ashiv, muhl? Mokuhlek i yem-tor au?" "monseigneur, wuh rom oekon fai-tor; tonk'peh i ri tor ya'akash ish-veh. T'nash-veh petition nam-tor, ik wuh morsel t' kov il lapan, k' t'nash-veh sa-telsu's ahm, lau nam-tor shitau abru' ish-veh tor gluvaya wilat au ti. Vathru, wuh shi dungi nam-tor sahris yen-tor, ish-veh dungi worla nam-tor afer-tor lu i am tevik t' wuh ka malady, i dungau nam-tor laid ne' ein vath tuh t' ri donku-tor yar. Monseigneur, au nam-tor ni wehk, au increase ni sahris, tra' nam-tor ni mau aitlun. Monseigneur! Monseigneur!" wuh valet had shitau ish-veh maf s' wuh svep, wuh carriage had pushau vi' wuh brax sahr-tor, wuh postilions had quickened wuh sahr, she vesh' losrak irak za', heh monseigneur, va'ashiv escorted k' wuh furies, vesh' rapidly diminishing wuh league il dahkuh t' ir ik hafau svi' ish-veh heh ish-veh chateau. Wuh slor scents t' wuh belaar mu-yor she-tor ek' pa' ish-veh, heh she-tor, u' wuh sov-masu tevan-tor, impartially, fi' wuh grazhiv, ragged, heh toil-worn travek na' wuh mashulek ri irak maf; tor ik wuh mender t' fau-yut, k' wuh mamuk t' wuh pla-kur taik rik' if au vesh' nothing, fam dvun sukau fi-tor ish-veh sasu spo' wuh spectre, u' wu u' au kupi lesh ish-veh. K' degrees, u' au kupi lesh rai weht, au eku-tor ska' veh k' veh, heh ha'ge twinkled svi' pi' casements; if ha'ge, u' wuh casements mu'glau, heh weht yel sasarlah, seemed ki' pohshaya abru vi' wuh igen instead t' having vesh' sayonotau. Wuh duv t' wuh suk pid-roofed kelek, heh t' wehk abru'-hanging lap, vesh' fi-tor monsieur wuh marquis k' ik wak; heh wuh duv vesh' di'kizh-tor na' wuh ta'hal t' wuh yonag, u' ish-veh carriage pehkau, heh wuh lo'uk svep t' ish-veh chateau vesh' tu'ash tor ish-veh. "monsieur charles, ik i gish; nam-tor au lasha s' england?" "monseigneur, ri wi." chapter ix. Wuh gorgon's patam ish-veh vesh' wuh ras shivak t' kelek, ik chateau t' monsieur wuh marquis, k' wuh suk kov courtyard fa' ish-veh, heh dahkuh kov fnashtau t' staircase latva svi' wuh kov nef fa' wuh principal svep. Wuh stony business altogether, k' ras kov balustrades, heh kov urns, heh kov svai, heh kov limuk t' sasu, heh kov patam t' lions, svi' ek' kharat. U' kuv wuh gorgon's patam had skothon-tor ish-veh, lu ish-veh vesh' shahtau, dahkuh centuries ago. Abru wuh sax'ksei hash t' gan ash-tor, monsieur wuh marquis, yonag preceded, went s' ish-veh carriage, sufficiently disturbing wuh mu'khlup'es tor elicit ral remonstrance s' wuh owl svi' wuh kamu t' wuh lo'uk tuh t' tihet kelek maf among wuh lap. Ek' else vesh' ni hizhuk, ik wuh yonag lesh abru wuh ash-tor, heh wuh vath yonag meskarau na' wuh lo'uk svep, yontau u' kuv au vesh' svi' wuh ikap-tor tvi-shal t' fupa s', instead t' hasu svi' wuh tu'ash mu-yor-sov. Vath ralash do wuh owl's spes tra' vesh' rim, korsau wuh tevan-tor t' wuh mashulek vi' its kov basin; na', ish-veh vesh' veh t' eifa gu'gelik mu-yor ik meskaraya ish-veh esh k' wuh wadan teretuhr, heh yi heave wuh wu neik spes-tevan, heh meskaraya ish-veh esh va'ashiv. Wuh lo'uk svep clanged za' ish-veh, heh monsieur wuh marquis tuhsau wuh tvur grim k' ac'ruth hinek boar-tilek, shek, heh lipau t' wuh a'vesh'; grimmer k' ac'ruth ras riding-fek heh riding-wonil-zehl, t' if wehk wuh peasant, hal-tor tor ish-veh benefactor tevakh, had olau wuh rasath lu ish-veh s'haile vesh' reshnek. Avoiding wuh larger tvi-shal, if vesh' gu'gelik heh tor sahris na' wuh mu-yor, monsieur wuh marquis, k' ish-veh yonag-bearer going fi' fa', went abru wuh staircase tor wuh svep svi' wuh tvur. Nash lehm-tor tu'ash, nafai-tor ish-veh tor ish-veh sha' awek ha-shal t' rehkuh tvi-shal: ish-veh sar-tak-tvi-shal heh dahkuh vath. Pid vaulted tvi-shal k' samuyau uncarpeted lan-tol, lo'uk dogs fi-tor wuh hearths na' wuh yontau t' lapan svi' karil wak, heh ek' luxuries befitting wuh fupa s' t' wuh marquis svi' wuh luxurious ya'shakhuv heh shasol. Wuh fashion t' wuh kim-shah louis tonk'peh veh, t' wuh zehl ik vesh' worla tor shaya--wuh fourteenth louis--vesh' conspicuous svi' ish-veh don-ka furniture; tonk'peh, ish-veh vesh' diversified k' wehk vel ik vesh' illustrations t' hinek thalv svi' wuh vesht-var t' france. Wuh mu'yor-yem-pasu vesh' laid na' dahkuh, svi' wuh wuh t' wuh tvi-shal; wuh pauk tvi-shal, svi' veh t' wuh chateau's kehkuh sayonotayek-topped kispek. Wuh pi' lofty tvi-shal, k' its krani eik tu'ash, heh wuh wooden jalousie-blinds a'ing, ni ik wuh gu'gelik mu-yor goh gluvau svi' slight yutik zehl t' nesh-kur, alternating k' ish-veh sax'ksei zehl t' kov kur. "t'nash-veh sa-bath, " leralmin-tor wuh marquis, glancing na' wuh mu'yor-yem preparation; "au leralmin-tor au vesh' ri lasha." il vesh' au; tonk'peh, au had vesh' gishu k' monseigneur. "ah! Ish-veh nam-tor ri yesik au dungi lasha tor-mu-yor; nevertheless, trasha wuh pasu u' ish-veh nam-tor. I dungau nam-tor pok svi' wuh yonuk t' wuh wadan." svi' wuh yonuk t' wuh wadan monseigneur vesh' pok, heh hayal-tor ne' sa'awek tor ish-veh sumptuous heh dvel mu'yor-yem. Ish-veh ku-san vesh' mesyutik tor wuh krani, heh au had taken ish-veh shur, heh vesh' raising ish-veh makh t' bordeaux tor ish-veh bru-lar, lu au shitau ish-veh ne'. "ra nam-tor ik?" au calmly ya'akash, looking k' attention na' wuh yutik zehl t' nesh-kur heh kov kur. "monseigneur? Ik?" "s'udish wuh blinds. Tu'ash wuh blinds." ish-veh vesh' ovsoh. "muhl?" "monseigneur, ish-veh nam-tor nothing. Wuh lap heh wuh mu-yor nam-tor ek' ik nam-tor la'." wuh dvinsu vi stariben, had lehm-tor wuh blinds eik, had glazhau si' vi' wuh vacant mu'khlup'es, heh lam-tor k' ik blank za' ish-veh, looking pauk na' instructions. "rom, " leralmin-tor wuh imperturbable trensu. "ikap-tor au va'ashiv." ik vesh' ovsoh nuh', heh wuh marquis went fi' k' ish-veh mu'yor-yem. Au vesh' ulef yut k'fai ish-veh, lu au va'ashiv pehkau k' ish-veh makh svi' ish-veh el'ru, khaf-spol wuh ralash t' halek. Sarlah ish-veh fi' brax, heh sarlah abru tor wuh khom t' wuh chateau. "ya'akash vi nam-tor lasha." ish-veh vesh' wuh sa-bath t' monseigneur. Au had vesh' ein zamu leagues za' monseigneur, lehkuh-mal svi' wuh aru. Au had nelau wuh ir rapidly, tonk'peh ri ni rapidly u' tor sarlah abru k' monseigneur fi' wuh fau-yut. Au had puzhu-tor t' monseigneur, na' wuh posting-kelek, u' hasu fa' ish-veh. Au vesh' tor nam-tor var-tor (leralmin-tor monseigneur) ik mu'yor-yem awaited ish-veh yi heh tra', heh ik au vesh' prayed tor sarlah tor ish-veh. Svi' wuh pi' du' sarlah ish-veh. Au had vesh' fainu svi' england u' charles darnay. Monseigneur poprah ish-veh svi' wuh courtly manner, tonk'peh au did ri hutau el'ru. "du losrak paris za-gad, osu?" au leralmin-tor tor monseigneur, u' au nem-tor ish-veh ku-san na' pasu. "za-gad. Heh du?" "sarlah nash-veh kharik." "s' london?" "ha." "du ma vesh' wuh akarshif coming, " leralmin-tor wuh marquis, k' wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut. "fi' wuh contrary; sarlah nash-veh kharik." "pardon me! I tvai, ri wuh akarshif fi' wuh halovaya; wuh akarshif intending wuh halovaya." "i ma vesh' detained k'"--wuh sa-bath pehkau wuh moment svi' ish-veh kilko-srashiv--"vuhnauk business." "rik' vet, " leralmin-tor wuh polished sa-kuk. Ni wu u' wuh dvinsu vesh' la', rai vath zhit be' dvun-tor svi' au. Lu mon had vesh' dvin-tor heh au vesh' sa'awek teretuhr, wuh sa-bath, looking na' wuh sa-kuk heh latva wuh bezhun t' wuh limuk ik vesh' spo' wuh tok-ti limein, tu'ash wuh conversation. "ki'sarlah nash-veh pla', osu, u' du anticipate, pursuing wuh vel ik nem-tor me maf. Ish-veh lesh me vi' lo'uk heh ri-gishu peril; tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor wuh sacred vel, heh kuv ish-veh had lesh me tor tevakh i rok ish-veh would ma potun-tor me." "ri tor tevakh, " leralmin-tor wuh sa-kuk; "ish-veh nam-tor ri bolayatik tor leralmin, tor tevakh." "i vet, osu, " fun-tor wuh sa-bath, "whether, kuv ish-veh had lesh me tor wuh utmost rihk t' tevakh, du would ma tun-tor tor pehkaya me tra'." wuh deepened ulidar svi' wuh han, heh wuh lengthening t' wuh tok-ti zehik zehl svi' wuh pi-maat'rer limuk, glazhau ominous u' tor ik; wuh sa-kuk tor wuh graceful gesture t' protest, if vesh' ni clearly wuh slight shid t' rom breeding ik ish-veh vesh' ri reassuring. "indeed, osu, " pursued wuh sa-bath, "na' sovek-vel i fai-tor, du lau ma expressly ar'kada tor mazhiv-kur-tor wuh weht suspicious appearance tor wuh suspicious circumstances ik vikuvau me." "rai, rai, rai, " leralmin-tor wuh sa-kuk, pleasantly. "tonk'peh, however ik lau nam-tor, " resumed wuh sa-bath, glancing na' ish-veh k' glu distrust, "i fai-tor ik ish-veh duta'es would pehkaya me k' sovek tvai, heh would fai-tor rai scruple u' tor tvai." "t'nash-veh t'hy'la, i var-tor du ni, " leralmin-tor wuh sa-kuk, k' wuh tok-ti gaya svi' wuh dahkuh ulidar. "tor me wuh favour tor recall ik i var-tor du ni, wu ago." "i recall ish-veh." "nemaiyo, " leralmin-tor wuh marquis--maut sweetly indeed. Ish-veh molu svizh-tor svi' wuh sov, siyah spo' wuh molu t' wuh musical instrument. "svi' daya, osu, " pursued wuh sa-bath, "i dva-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor na' wuh'wak ish-veh rasahkos fortune, heh t'nash-veh rom fortune, ik has potau me s' wuh prison svi' france la'." "i ri tor ved ken-tor, " fun-tor wuh sa-kuk, mon-tor ish-veh mon. "dare i ya'akash du tor danau?" "i dva-tor ik kuv du vesh' ri svi' disgrace k' wuh kelek, heh had ri vesh' overshadowed k' ik wan na' tevun vesht, wuh nuhm de cachet would ma satau me tor ein klomak indefinitely." "ish-veh nam-tor tor-yehat, " leralmin-tor wuh sa-kuk, k' lo'uk calmness. "na' wuh dor t' wuh skan, i kupi kauk resolve tor incommode du tor ik sadvun. Pray tobeg me!" "i pakashogau ik, kunling na' me, wuh reception t' wuh gad fa' za-gad vesh', u' tsuri, wuh samu veh, " glantau wuh sa-bath. "i would ri leralmin kunling, t'nash-veh t'hy'la, " fun-tor wuh sa-kuk, k' refined politeness; "i would ri nam-tor sure t' ik. Wuh rom opportunity na' consideration, vikuvau k' wuh advantages t' awek'es, lau vi-yumuk ish-veh buk tor irak greater advantage do du vi-yumuk ish-veh na' yourself. Tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor nam-tor-fam tor discuss wuh deshker. I am, u' du leralmin, na' wuh disadvantage. Aifa pi' instruments t' yehtan, aifa gentle mamuk tor wuh tepul heh dor t' skan, aifa slight favours ik lau ni incommode du, nam-tor goh tor nam-tor prah i' k' eku'ko heh importunity. Au nam-tor sought k' ni wehk, heh au nam-tor vahl (comparatively) tor ni zamu! Ish-veh nam-tor-tor ri tor nam-tor ni, tonk'peh france svi' ek' such vel nam-tor rubai na' wuh weh-rasahkos. Etwel ri remote orfik-kel meskarau wuh gas'rak t' ha'kiv heh tevakh abru' wuh surrounding vulgar. S' nash tvi-shal, wehk such dogs ma vesh' taken si' tor nam-tor geldau; svi' wuh thurai tvi-shal (t'nash-veh shi'yuk), veh katravahsu, tor etwel fai-tukh, vesh' poniarded fi' wuh gla-tor na' professing ein insolent delicacy respecting ish-veh ko-fu--ish-veh ko-fu? Etek ma pakik wehk privileges; wuh uzh ven-dol-leralmin has shetau wuh nuk; heh wuh assertion t' etwel wurzel, svi' aifa gad, lau (i ri tor hal-tor ni irak u' tor leralmin would, tonk'peh lau) aishan etek yeht inconvenience. Ek' maut rasahkos, maut rasahkos!" wuh marquis nem-tor wuh gentle pi' k'hy t' snuff, heh hutau ish-veh patam; u' elegantly despondent u' au kupi becomingly nam-tor t' wuh shasol fam dvun containing himself, ik lo'uk tvai t' regeneration. "etek ma ni asserted etwel wurzel, fi' svi' wuh hinek wak heh svi' wuh iyik wak isha, " leralmin-tor wuh sa-bath, gloomily, "ik i dva-tor etwel ahm tor nam-tor weht detested do sovek ahm svi' france." "kal-tor etek rok ni, " leralmin-tor wuh sa-kuk. "detestation t' wuh pid nam-tor wuh shatipik homage t' wuh neik." "tra' nam-tor ri, " pursued wuh sa-bath, svi' ish-veh former molu, "wuh limuk i mokuhlek glazhau na', svi' ek' nash shasol pauk pa' etek, if glazhau na' me k' sovek deference fi' ish-veh tonk'peh wuh gu'gelik deference t' pthak heh slavery." "wuh compliment, " leralmin-tor wuh marquis, "tor wuh grandeur t' wuh skan, merited k' wuh manner svi' if wuh skan has potun-tor its grandeur. Hah!" heh au nem-tor wuh'ashiv gentle pi' k'hy t' snuff, heh lightly tuhsau ish-veh mal. Tonk'peh, lu ish-veh sa-bath, leaning wuh kar-nef fi' wuh pasu, wein-tor ish-veh bezhun thoughtfully heh dejectedly k' ish-veh el'ru, wuh tok-ti limein glazhau na' ish-veh sideways k' wuh stronger concentration t' keenness, closeness, heh ritishaya, do vesh' comportable k' its wearer's assumption t' indifference. "repression nam-tor wuh goh lasting ven-dol-leralmin. Wuh gu'gelik deference t' pthak heh slavery, t'nash-veh t'hy'la, " glantau wuh marquis, "dungi potau wuh dogs obedient tor wuh wonil-zehl, u' wu u' nash kamu, " looking abru tor ish-veh, "ikap-tor si' wuh igen." ik lau ri nam-tor ni wu u' wuh marquis supposed. Kuv wuh bikuv t' wuh chateau u' ish-veh vesh' tor nam-tor wuh maut zamu tevun hence, heh t' kau-leh spo' ish-veh u' au nuh' vesh' tor nam-tor wuh maut zamu tevun hence, kupi ma vesh' shown tor ish-veh ik mu-yor, au lau ma vesh' na' wuh pak tor claim ish-veh sha' s' wuh ghastly, yon-yonol-tor, plunder-vashau sov-mashau. U' na' wuh kamu au vaunted, au lau ma afer-tor ik shutting si' wuh igen svi' wuh uzh yut--tor wit, na' ek'wak, s' wuh bezhun t' wuh ak'shem vi' if its ras-tukh vesh' pohshau, s' wuh subok t' wuh hundred thousand muskets. "meanwhile, " leralmin-tor wuh marquis, "i dungi korsau wuh dor heh repose t' wuh skan, kuv du dungi ri. Tonk'peh du bolau nam-tor zung-tor. Dungau etek terminate etwel conference na' wuh mu-yor?" "wuh moment weht." "wuh wadan, kuv du sanoi." "osu, " leralmin-tor wuh sa-bath, "etek ma ovsoh riyeht, heh nam-tor reaping wuh savas t' riyeht." "etek ma ovsoh riyeht?" ashiv-tor wuh marquis, k' wuh inquiring abru'teruklar-ru'lut, heh delicately pointing, wuh'rak tor ish-veh sa-bath, yi tor himself. "etwel skan; etwel dorli skan, t'vi dor nam-tor t' ni mau khrosahp tor fi' t' etek, svi' such natya yut. Kauk svi' t'nash-veh sa-mekh's wak, etek did wuh panu t' riyeht, injuring kanok komihn creature vi sarlah svi' etek heh etwel sanosh, whatever ish-veh vesh'. Po bolaya i stariben t' t'nash-veh sa-mekh's wak, lu ish-veh nam-tor kaing ish-veh? Mokuhlek i dahshauk t'nash-veh sa-mekh's t'dahsu-sa-kai, joint inheritor, heh thurai successor, s' himself?" "tevakh has ovsoh ik!" leralmin-tor wuh marquis. "heh has losrak me, " kilko-tor wuh sa-bath, "bound tor wuh torektra ik nam-tor frightful tor me, responsible na' ish-veh, tonk'peh powerless svi' ish-veh; seeking tor fitor wuh kim-shah ya'akash t' t'nash-veh tal-kam ko-mekh's bru-lar, heh obey wuh kim-shah glazhau t' t'nash-veh tal-kam ko-mekh's bezhun, if implored me ki' mercy heh tor redress; heh tortured k' seeking assistance heh tepul svi' vain." "seeking au s' me, t'nash-veh sa-bath, " leralmin-tor wuh marquis, touching ish-veh fi' wuh thasek k' ish-veh kehr-oth--au vesh' i' standing k' wuh hearth--"du dungi na' ek'wak seek au svi' vain, nam-tor assured." kanok tok-ti zehik zehl svi' wuh pa'shik whiteness t' ish-veh limuk, vesh' cruelly, craftily, heh closely lerakhovau, du' au lam-tor looking quietly na' ish-veh sa-bath, k' ish-veh snuff-natuhn svi' ish-veh el'ru. Wuh'wak va'ashiv au estuhl ish-veh fi' wuh thasek, u' hi ish-veh ozh vesh' wuh tok-ti sfek t' wuh pi' shek, k' if, svi' delicate finesse, au sahr-tor ish-veh k'fai wuh ak'shem, heh leralmin-tor, "t'nash-veh t'hy'la, i dungi tev-tor, perpetuating wuh torektra ne' if i ma ha-tor." lu au had leralmin-tor ish-veh, au nem-tor wuh culminating k'hy t' snuff, heh shitau ish-veh natuhn svi' ish-veh abru'lik. "weh-rom tor nam-tor wuh rational creature, " au hau yi, po' ringing wuh pi' kus-vakh fi' wuh pasu, "heh nar-tor ish-veh malatik buk. Tonk'peh du nam-tor pakik, monsieur charles, gla-tor nash-veh." "nash veltra heh france nam-tor pakik tor me, " leralmin-tor wuh sa-bath, sadly; "i renounce au." "nam-tor au fi' ish-veh tor renounce? France lau nam-tor, tonk'peh nam-tor wuh veltra? Ish-veh nam-tor scarcely don mentioning; tonk'peh, nam-tor ish-veh wi?" "i had rai intention, svi' wuh zhit i nam-tor-tor, tor claim ish-veh wi. Kuv ish-veh be' dvun-tor tor me s' du, tor-morrow--" "if i ma wuh vanity tor rok nam-tor ri yesik." "--il dah-leh tevun hence--" "du tor me nuh' mau dor, " leralmin-tor wuh marquis; "fam dvun, i prefer ik supposition." "--i would abandon ish-veh, heh ha-tor vathru heh kitok-wilat. Ish-veh nam-tor pi' tor relinquish. Ra nam-tor ish-veh tonk'peh wuh shi'kwai t' misery heh ruin!" "hah!" leralmin-tor wuh marquis, glancing pauk wuh luxurious tvi-shal. "tor wuh bezhun ish-veh nam-tor rom hiyet, la'; tonk'peh gla-tor svi' its ket'es, ne' wuh igen, heh k' wuh gad-ha'khlup, ish-veh nam-tor wuh crumbling kispek t' thinoi, mismanagement, extortion, sa'akh, mortgage, oppression, avon, nakedness, heh suffering." "hah!" leralmin-tor wuh marquis va'ashiv, svi' wuh muhl-satisfied manner. "kuv ish-veh ek'wak shetau t'nash-veh, ish-veh dungau nam-tor shitau vi' ein el'ru weh-rom qualified tor elik ish-veh slowly (kuv such wuh vel nam-tor tor-yehat) s' wuh rasath ik zaseshau ish-veh ne', ni ik wuh miserable sutra vi fam yehat trasha ish-veh heh vi ma vesh' wu wrung tor wuh kim-shah sfek t' palesh, lau, svi' wuh'ashiv generation, dash lehkuh; tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor ri na' me. Tra' nam-tor wuh curse fi' ish-veh, heh fi' ek' nash solektra." "heh du?" leralmin-tor wuh sa-kuk. "forgive t'nash-veh curiosity; tor du, ne' ish-veh uzh ven-dol-leralmin, graciously intend tor ha-tor?" "i bolau tor, tor ha-tor, ra vath t' t'nash-veh countrymen, kauk k' thol'es na' ish-veh pla'dor, lau ma tor tor ein gad--ar'kadan." "svi' england, na' li-fal?" "ha. Wuh skan dor, osu, nam-tor safe s' me svi' nash shasol. Wuh skan ahm mokuhlek dash s' me svi' rai vath, na' i lesh ish-veh svi' rai vath." wuh ringing t' wuh kus-vakh had aisha wuh adjoining sar-tak-tvi-shal tor nam-tor lighted. Ish-veh i' min-tor brightly, k'fai wuh svep t' sviribaya. Wuh marquis glazhau ik yut, heh shroi na' wuh retreating ash t' ish-veh valet. "england nam-tor maut attractive tor du, seeing uf indifferently du ma smusma tra', " au glantau yi, turning ish-veh hayal limuk tor ish-veh sa-bath k' wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut. "i ma already leralmin-tor, ik na' t'nash-veh prospering tra', i am sensible i lau nam-tor indebted tor du, osu. Na' wuh shom, ish-veh nam-tor t'nash-veh rau-nol." "au leralmin, eifa boastful eingelsu, ik ish-veh nam-tor wuh rau-nol t' wehk. Du fai-tor wuh compatriot vi has afer-tor wuh rau-nol tra'? Wuh hassu?" "ha." "k' wuh ko-fu?" "ha." "ha, " leralmin-tor wuh marquis. "du nam-tor zung-tor. Rom mu-yor!" u' au keh'sei ish-veh patam svi' ish-veh danik courtly manner, tra' vesh' wuh secrecy svi' ish-veh smiling limuk, heh au zhelesh wuh sov t' mystery tor eifa zhit, if kwul-tor wuh bezhun heh kaluk t' ish-veh sa-bath forcibly. Na' wuh ka wak, wuh wonil zehik zehl t' wuh setting t' wuh bezhun, heh wuh wonil zehik bru-lar, heh wuh markings svi' wuh han, curved k' wuh sarcasm ik glazhau handsomely diabolic. "ha, " ashiv-tor wuh marquis. "wuh hassu k' wuh ko-fu. Ha. Ni palikau wuh uzh ven-dol-leralmin! Du nam-tor zung-tor. Rom mu-yor!" ish-veh would ma vesh' t' u' mau avail tor interrogate sovek kov limuk s'udish wuh chateau u' tor interrogate ik limuk t' ish-veh. Wuh sa-bath glazhau na' ish-veh, svi' vain, svi' be' dvun-tor fi' tor wuh svep. "rom mu-yor!" leralmin-tor wuh sa-kuk. "i glazhau tor wuh sanosh t' seeing du va'ashiv svi' wuh asal. Rom repose! Ta'hal monsieur t'nash-veh sa-bath tor ish-veh tvi-shal tra'!--heh yontau monsieur t'nash-veh sa-bath svi' ish-veh sar-tak, kuv du dungi, " au hau tor himself, fa' au rang ish-veh pi' kus-vakh va'ashiv, heh summoned ish-veh valet tor ish-veh sha' shi'yuk. Wuh valet sarlah heh hal-tor, monsieur wuh marquis lates-tor tor heh fro svi' ish-veh thal tvi-shal-pelal, tor dator himself kogavik na' yuk, ik fal fam dvun mu-yor. Rustling pa' wuh tvi-shal, ish-veh softly-slippered ash'ya tor rai ralash fi' wuh lan-tol, au dvun-tor spo' wuh refined tiger: --glazhau spo' ein enchanted marquis t' wuh impenitently wicked wihfelau, svi' var, t'vi periodical rubah vi' tiger shid vesh' either aishan going ska', il aishan coming fi'. Au dvun-tor s' shaht tor shaht t' ish-veh voluptuous shi'yuk, looking va'ashiv na' wuh moguhsh t' wuh gad's halovaya ik sarlah unbidden vi' ish-veh kashek; wuh vohris toil abru wuh kunel na' tev-tor, wuh setting yel, wuh tevan, wuh mill, wuh prison fi' wuh crag, wuh pi' pi'kahr svi' wuh hollow, wuh peasants na' wuh mashulek, heh wuh mender t' fau-yut k' ish-veh pla-kur taik pointing si' wuh naf-elakh ne' wuh carriage. Ik mashulek suggested wuh paris mashulek, wuh pi' uzh'a'lek lying fi' wuh ash, wuh kosu bending abru' ish-veh, heh wuh ha-vol sasu k' ish-veh kar abru, maf-tor, "tevik!" "i am samuyau i', " leralmin-tor monsieur wuh marquis, "heh lau hal-tor tor sar-tak." ni, leaving goh veh ta'hal yontau fi' wuh suk hearth, au kal-tor ish-veh wonil gauze curtains tevan pa' ish-veh, heh puzhu-tor wuh mu-yor shaya its silence k' wuh wu spes-tevan u' au tertitau himself tor yuk. Wuh kov limuk fi' wuh sik temok nantau blindly na' wuh nesh-kur mu-yor na' rehkuh ras wadan; na' rehkuh ras wadan, wuh jarel svi' wuh stables rattled na' ish-veh racks, wuh dogs barked, heh wuh owl tor wuh ralash k' maut pi' resemblance svi' ish-veh tor wuh ralash conventionally assigned tor wuh owl k' sasu-poets. Tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor wuh obstinate custom t' such creatures hardly ek'wak tor leralmin ra nam-tor eku ne' na' au. Na' rehkuh ras wadan, wuh kov limuk t' wuh chateau, lion heh komihn, nantau blindly na' wuh mu-yor. Tevik mu'khlup'es ti fi' ek' wuh landscape, tevik mu'khlup'es hau its sha' hush tor wuh hushing grazhiv fi' ek' wuh fau-yut. Wuh visolektaya-shi had prah tor wuh be' dvun ik its pi' heaps t' ri donku-tor yar vesh' undistinguishable s' veh wuh'ashiv; wuh khlop fi' wuh tuhs lau ma sarlah ne', na' sovek-vel ik kupi nam-tor gla-tor t' ish-veh. Svi' wuh pi'kahr, taxers heh taxed vesh' sahris asleep. Dreaming, sos'eh, t' banquets, u' wuh starved usually tor, heh t' ease heh shom, u' wuh driven kafeh heh wuh yoked ox lau, its galat inhabitants yuk-tor soundly, heh vesh' puyem-tot heh el-tor. Wuh mashulek svi' wuh pi'kahr yumau unseen heh unheard, heh wuh mashulek na' wuh chateau eku-tor unseen heh unheard--fi' melting maf, spo' wuh minutes ik vesh' tevan-tor s' wuh sikar t' wak--k'fai rehkuh gu'gelik wadan. Yi, wuh zhai-kur masu t' fi' began tor nam-tor ghostly svi' wuh ta'hal, heh wuh bezhun t' wuh kov limuk t' wuh chateau vesh' tu'ash. Lighter heh lighter, abi' na' kim-shah wuh yel estuhl wuh fik t' wuh fam dvun lap, heh mukau its radiance abru' wuh kunel. Svi' wuh min, wuh masu t' wuh chateau mashulek seemed tor da-tor tor khaf, heh wuh kov limuk crimsoned. Wuh carol t' wuh kushel vesh' ral heh pid, heh, fi' wuh igen-va-beaten sku t' wuh lo'uk krani t' wuh sar-tak-tvi-shal t' monsieur wuh marquis, veh pi' kushel sang its sweetest song k' ek' its lau. Na' nash, wuh nearest kov limuk seemed tor nantaya putaurau, heh, k' tu'ash ru'lut heh eku-tor ne'-ahs, glazhau teshan-stricken. I', wuh yel vesh' bosh abru, heh dvun began svi' wuh pi'kahr. Casement krani tu'ash, amp svep vesh' unbarred, heh sutra sarlah forth shivering--chilled, u' wi, k' wuh uzh slor sov. Yi began wuh rarely lightened toil t' wuh gad among wuh pi'kahr population. Ein, tor wuh mashulek; ein, tor wuh vunai; sasu heh kosu la', tor hil-tor heh delve; sasu heh kosu tra', tor gla-tor tor wuh ri donku-tor ha-tor fek, heh ras-tukh wuh bony aushfa si', tor such pasture u' kupi nam-tor afer-tor k' wuh roadside. Svi' wuh church heh na' wuh tuhs, wuh kneeling khlop il dahkuh; attendant fi' wuh latter prayers, wuh pufulag-tor aushfa, trying na' wuh asal-yem among wuh vedik na' its ash'ya. Wuh chateau awoke later, u' became its quality, tonk'peh awoke gradually heh surely. Wuh'rak, wuh lonely boar-tilek heh lipau t' wuh a'vesh' had vesh' reddened u' t' hinek; yi, had gleamed trenchant svi' wuh asal sunshine; i', svep heh krani vesh' lehm-tor tu'ash, jarel svi' ish-veh stables glazhau pauk abru' ish-veh tipan na' wuh ta'hal heh freshness pouring svi' na' svep-sharu, mor sparkled heh rustled na' shek-tukh-grated krani, dogs seshau lerash na' ish-veh naf-elakh, heh reared impatient tor nam-tor loosed. Ek' aifa trivial incidents belonged tor wuh routine t' ha'kiv, heh wuh fun t' asal. Surely, ri ni wuh ringing t' wuh lo'uk kus-vakh t' wuh chateau, il wuh sahran abru heh ne' wuh kaiden; il wuh hurried khlop fi' wuh nef; il wuh booting heh tramping la' heh tra' heh kanok-wilat, il wuh sahris saddling t' jarel heh riding maf? Ra salan zhelesh nash brax tor wuh grizzled mender t' fau-yut, already na' ar'kadan fi' wuh kunel-fik mesakh wuh pi'kahr, k' ish-veh gad's aru-yem (ri mau tor lesh) lying svi' wuh uzh'a'lek ik ish-veh vesh' don rai kushel's du' tor peck na', fi' wuh tuh t' kov? Had wuh kushel, carrying ein kap-yar t' ish-veh tor wuh ir, eku-tor veh abru' ish-veh u' au sow pavesh nei? Whether il rai, wuh mender t' fau-yut sahr-tor, fi' wuh sultry asal, u' kuv na' ish-veh ha'kiv, ne' wuh kunel, mal-nef-pid svi' grazhiv, heh worla pehkau till au prah tor wuh mashulek. Ek' wuh sutra t' wuh pi'kahr vesh' na' wuh mashulek, standing pa' svi' ish-veh depressed manner, heh zhalan neik, tonk'peh showing rai vath zherka do grim curiosity heh ak'wikmun. Wuh pufulag-tor aushfa, hastily katau svi' heh elsak-tor tor sovek-vel ik would meskaraya au, vesh' looking stupidly fi', il lying ne' chewing wuh cud t' nothing wa' repaying ish-veh trouble, if au had abrashau svi' ish-veh svi-shau saunter. Ein t' wuh sutra t' wuh chateau, heh ein t' eifa t' wuh posting-kelek, heh ek' wuh taxing ek'te'kru, vesh' armed weht il lehkuh, heh vesh' crowded fi' wuh vath vla t' wuh pi' yut svi' wuh purposeless yut, ik vesh' highly fraught k' nothing. Already, wuh mender t' fau-yut had penetrated vi' wuh midst t' wuh travek t' kau-leh particular t'hylara, heh vesh' smiting himself svi' wuh thasek k' ish-veh pla-kur taik. Ra did ek' nash portend, heh ra portended wuh swift abertau-abru t' monsieur gabelle za' wuh dvinsu fi' horseback, heh wuh conveying maf t' wuh leralmin-tor gabelle (dahtau-laden hi wuh jarel vesh'), na' wuh ausahr, spo' wuh uzh version t' wuh german ballad t' leonora? Ish-veh portended ik tra' vesh' veh kov limuk nuh' wehk, abru na' wuh chateau. Wuh gorgon had skothon-tor wuh kelek va'ashiv svi' wuh mu-yor, heh had hau wuh veh kov limuk wanting; wuh kov limuk na' if ish-veh had bek-tor k'fai pa' dah-teh tevun. Ish-veh ti pla' fi' wuh trak t' monsieur wuh marquis. Ish-veh vesh' spo' wuh tok-ti limein, suddenly startled, tor reshnek, heh kovtulik. Driven ha-kel vi' wuh khaf-spol t' wuh kov khlop attached tor ish-veh, vesh' wuh lipau. Pauk its hilt vesh' wuh frill t' dun, fi' if vesh' scrawled: "yetur ish-veh sahris tor ish-veh braq. Nash, s' jacques." chapter x. Dahkuh ugau weht tevun-krus, tor wuh su'etek t' leh-dah, had sarlah heh hal-tor, heh mr. Charles darnay vesh' afer-tor svi' england u' wuh higher savensu t' wuh french gen-lis vi vesh' conversant k' french kitau-tanaf. Svi' nash ya'shakhuv, au would ma vesh' wuh professor; svi' ik ya'shakhuv, au vesh' wuh tutor. Au telv-tor k' nu'ri sasu vi kupi talal sovek el-wak heh eku'ko na' wuh orenau t' wuh living lahv spoken ek' abru' wuh panu, heh au sokasitau wuh zahvan na' its mahr-kel t' fai-tukh heh fancy. Au kupi kitau t' au, isha, svi' ralash eingelsu, heh render au vi' ralash eingelsu. Such trensu vesh' ri na' ik wak easily afer-tor; princes ik had vesh', heh sa-te'kru ik vesh' tor nam-tor, vesh' ri wi t' wuh savensu mohrn, heh rai ruined thol'es had eku-tor s' tellson's ledgers, tor da-tor fas-tor heh carpenters. U' wuh tutor, t'vi bai'elkhrul-akteiben tor wuh orensu's yut unusually vaksurik heh profitable, heh u' wuh sohkik translator vi katau vel tor ish-veh ar'kadan isha mere zhit-dunap fai-tukh, nu'ri mr. Darnay ak became fainu heh kastorau. Au vesh' muhl acquainted, weht-abru', k' wuh circumstances t' ish-veh shasol, heh eifa vesh' t' ek'wak-growing eku'ko. Ni, k' lo'uk perseverance heh untiring industry, au smusma. Svi' london, au had gishu neither tor lates fi' pavements t' pi-maat-tukh, il tor ti fi' sar-tak t' roses; kuv au had had sovek such exalted gishat, au would ri ma smusma. Au had gishu zup, heh au afer-tor ish-veh, heh did ish-veh heh tor wuh buhfik t' ish-veh. Svi' nash, ish-veh smusma'es consisted. Wuh ac'ruth portion t' ish-veh wak vesh' be' dvun-tor na' cambridge, wilat au telv-tor k' undergraduates u' wuh wihfelau t' wivelau smuggler vi drove wuh contraband trade svi' european gen-lis, instead t' conveying greek heh latin k'fai wuh custom-kelek. Wuh shom t' ish-veh wak au be' dvun-tor svi' london. I', s' wuh gad lu ish-veh vesh' kwon-hau-ov belaar svi' eden, tor aifa gad lu ish-veh nam-tor mostly karil svi' tevan-tor latitudes, wuh panu t' wuh sasu has invariably hal-tor veh yut--charles darnay's yut--wuh yut t' wuh ashaya t' wuh kosu. Au had ashau lucie manette s' wuh wadan t' ish-veh tehvar. Au had worla puzhu-tor wuh ralash ni slor heh tal-kam u' wuh ralash t' ish-veh compassionate spes; au had worla gla-tor wuh limuk ni tenderly vaksurik, u' ish-veh lu ish-veh vesh' nagau k' ish-veh sha' fi' wuh rihk t' wuh shi'vukhut ik had vesh' hil-tor na' ish-veh. Tonk'peh, au had ri wi spoken tor ish-veh fi' wuh subject; wuh assassination na' wuh deserted chateau irak maf mesakh wuh heaving masu heh wuh wu, wu, grazhiv fau-yut--wuh huhtik kov chateau if had itself shetau wuh mere mist t' wuh sahr-tor--had vesh' ovsoh wuh tevun, heh au had worla wi, k' ni mau u' wuh single spoken zhit, disclosed tor ish-veh wuh fupa s' t' ish-veh khaf-spol. Ik au had ish-veh utvau na' nash, au fai-tor bosh muhl. Ish-veh vesh' va'ashiv wuh belaar gad lu, lately lasha svi' london s' ish-veh college occupation, au da-tor vi' wuh hizhuk teruk svi' soho, keh'sei fi' seeking wuh opportunity t' sharu ish-veh kashek tor hassu manette. Ish-veh vesh' wuh ikap-tor t' wuh belaar gad, heh au fai-tor lucie tor nam-tor si' k' din-tor pross. Au afer-tor wuh hassu telvan svi' ish-veh kar-ku-san na' wuh krani. Wuh tepul if had na' wuh'wak nenikau ish-veh ne' ish-veh hinek sufferings heh aggravated ish-veh sharpness, had vesh' gradually restored tor ish-veh. Au vesh' i' wuh maut energetic sasu indeed, k' lo'uk firmness t' lof, karik'es t' resolution, heh vigour t' torai. Svi' ish-veh recovered tepul au vesh' sometimes wuh pi' fitful heh sudden, u' au had palikauk vesh' svi' wuh tusok t' ish-veh vath recovered sutra; tonk'peh, nash had worla vesh' frequently observable, heh had grown weht heh weht ritsuri. Au orenau mau, yuk-tor pi', potun-tor wuh lo'uk deal t' zung k' ease, heh vesh' equably cheerful. Tor ish-veh, i' svi-tor charles darnay, na' glan t' ik au laid aside ish-veh dunap heh meskarau si' ish-veh el'ru. "charles darnay! I rejoice tor gla-tor du. Etek ma vesh' counting fi' ish-veh fun aifa rehkuh il kehkuh gad vesht. Mr. Stryver heh sydney carton vesh' fi' la' za-gad, heh fi' tor du si' tor nam-tor weht do due." "i am obliged tor au na' ish-veh eku'ko svi' wuh tukh, " au kilko-tor, wuh pi' coldly u' tor au, hi maut warmly u' tor wuh hassu. "din-tor manette--" "nam-tor muhl, " leralmin-tor wuh hassu, u' au pehkau pen, "heh ish-veh fun dungi delight etek ek'. She has hal-tor si' fi' ein household tukh, tonk'peh dungi ak nam-tor ha-kel." "hassu manette, i fai-tor she vesh' s' ha-kel. I nem-tor wuh opportunity t' ish-veh hasu s' ha-kel, tor eit'jae tor stariben tor du." tra' vesh' wuh blank silence. "ha?" leralmin-tor wuh hassu, k' evident constraint. "katau ish-veh ku-san la', heh stariben fi'." au complied u' tor wuh ku-san, tonk'peh saudau tor talal wuh speaking fi' lehkuh hagik. "i ma had wuh happiness, hassu manette, t' hasu ni intimate la', " ni au na' wu-vath began, "na' ein tevun heh wuh ulef, ik i rok wuh ong fi' if i am pa' tor esta lau ri--" au vesh' stayed k' wuh hassu's putting si' ish-veh el'ru tor pehkaya ish-veh. Lu au had potau ish-veh ni wuh pi' du', au leralmin-tor, bestan ish-veh pla': "nam-tor lucie wuh ong?" "she nam-tor." "ish-veh nam-tor lerash na' me tor stariben t' ish-veh na' sovek wak. Ish-veh nam-tor maut lerash na' me tor zhu-tor ish-veh spoken t' svi' ik molu t' ish-veh, charles darnay." "ish-veh nam-tor wuh molu t' fervent admiration, yeht homage, heh glu ashaya, hassu manette!" au leralmin-tor deferentially. Tra' vesh' wuh'ashiv blank silence fa' ish-veh sa-mekh rejoined: "i dva-tor ish-veh. I tor du yeht-gav; i dva-tor ish-veh." ish-veh constraint vesh' ni manifest, heh ish-veh vesh' ni manifest, nuh', ik ish-veh tveshulau svi' wuh unwillingness tor betaya wuh subject, ik charles darnay hesitated. "dungau i hal-tor fi', osu?" wuh'ashiv blank. "ha, hal-tor fi'." "du anticipate ra i would leralmin, hi du fam yehat fai-tor uf earnestly i leralmin ish-veh, uf earnestly i olau ish-veh, rik' fai-tor t'nash-veh tsat khaf-spol, heh wuh rok-tor heh ptha heh anxieties k' if ish-veh has wu vesh' laden. Tal-kam hassu manette, i ashaya ish-veh ko-fu fondly, dearly, disinterestedly, devotedly. Kuv ek'wak tra' vesh' ashaya svi' wuh panu, i ashaya ish-veh. Du ma ashau yourself; kal-tor ish-veh hinek ashaya stariben na' me!" wuh hassu hayal-tor k' ish-veh limuk da-tor maf, heh ish-veh bezhun keh'sei fi' wuh solektra. Na' wuh kim-shah zhit, au sakadau si' ish-veh el'ru va'ashiv, hurriedly, heh maf-tor: "ri ik, osu! Kal-tor ik nam-tor! I adjure du, ri tor recall ik!" ish-veh maf vesh' ni spo' wuh maf t' actual kusut, ik ish-veh rang svi' charles darnay's kaluk wu po' au had ceased. Au motioned k' wuh el'ru au had sadvun-tor, heh ish-veh seemed tor nam-tor wuh appeal tor darnay tor svizh. Wuh latter ni poprah ish-veh, heh hafau ralash-fam. "i ya'akash ish-veh pardon, " leralmin-tor wuh hassu, svi' wuh nessau molu, po' ein moments. "i ri tor vet ish-veh loving lucie; du lau nam-tor satisfied t' ish-veh." au da-tor na' ish-veh svi' ish-veh ku-san, tonk'peh did ri glazhau na' ish-veh, il ashenau ish-veh bezhun. Ish-veh chin eku-tor fi-tor ish-veh el'ru, heh ish-veh wan-kur isachya overshadowed ish-veh limuk: "ma du spoken tor lucie?" "rai." "il written?" "worla." "ish-veh would nam-tor ungenerous tor dau ri tor fai-tor ik ish-veh shal-wafaya nam-tor tor nam-tor referred tor ish-veh consideration na' ish-veh sa-mekh. Ish-veh sa-mekh itaren du." au nufau ish-veh el'ru; tonk'peh ish-veh bezhun did ri hal-tor k' ish-veh. "i fai-tor, " leralmin-tor darnay, respectfully, "uf mokuhlek i vravshau tor fai-tor, hassu manette, i vi ma gla-tor du teretuhr s' gad tor gad, ik svi' du heh din-tor manette tra' nam-tor wuh affection ni ritsuri, ni touching, ni t' wuh circumstances svi' if ish-veh has vesh' nurtured, ik ish-veh mokuhlek ma zamu vlavla, kauk svi' wuh tenderness svi' wuh sa-mekh heh kan. I fai-tor, hassu manette--uf mokuhlek i vravshau tor fai-tor--ik, mingled k' wuh affection heh gu-vam t' wuh ko-fu vi has shetau wuh kosu, tra' nam-tor, svi' ish-veh khaf-spol, na' du, ek' wuh ashaya heh reliance t' infancy itself. I fai-tor ik, u' svi' ish-veh kan-wak she had rai parent, ni she nam-tor i' vaikau tor du k' ek' wuh constancy heh fervour t' ish-veh la' tevun heh character, kaunshuk tor wuh trustfulness heh attachment t' wuh lehkuh-mal gad svi' if du vesh' pakik tor ish-veh. I fai-tor perfectly muhl ik kuv du had vesh' restored tor ish-veh s' wuh panu mesakh nash ha'kiv, du kupi hardly nam-tor invested, svi' ish-veh glan, k' wuh weht sacred character do ik svi' if du nam-tor kwon-hau-ov k' ish-veh. I fai-tor ik lu she nam-tor clinging tor du, wuh el'ru t' kan-bu, ko-kan, heh kosu, ek' svi' veh, nam-tor pauk ish-veh talu. I fai-tor ik svi' loving du gla-tor ish-veh heh ashau ish-veh ko-mekh na' ish-veh sha' ya'shakhuv, gla-tor heh ashau du na' t'nash-veh ya'shakhuv, ashau ish-veh ko-mekh pushau-hearted, ashau du k'fai ish-veh dreadful trial heh svi' ish-veh blessed restoration. I ma fainu nash, mu-yor heh gad, opi' i ma fainu du svi' ish-veh ha-kel." ish-veh sa-mekh hayal-tor ralash-fam, k' ish-veh limuk keh'sei ne'. Ish-veh eshan vesh' wuh pi' quickened; tonk'peh au repressed ek' vath glat t' agitation. "tal-kam hassu manette, kwon-hau-ov fai-tor nash, kwon-hau-ov seeing ish-veh heh du k' nash hallowed ta'hal pa' du, i ma forborne, heh forborne, u' wu u' ish-veh vesh' svi' wuh malat t' sasu tor tor ish-veh. I ma olau, heh tor kauk i' olau, ik tor katau t'nash-veh ashaya--kauk t'nash-veh--svi' du, nam-tor tor esta ish-veh vesht-var k' vel ri ved ni rom u' itself. Tonk'peh i ashaya ish-veh. Sha-ka-ri nam-tor t'nash-veh toglantausu ik i ashaya ish-veh!" "i dva-tor ish-veh, " kilko-tor ish-veh sa-mekh, mournfully. "i ma nahp ni fa' i'. I dva-tor ish-veh." "tonk'peh, ri tor dva-tor, " leralmin-tor darnay, fi-tor t'vi kaluk wuh mournful spes kwul-tor k' wuh reproachful ralash, "ik kuv t'nash-veh fortune vesh' ni vishizhau u' ik, hasu veh gad ni kunli u' tor tor ish-veh t'nash-veh ko-telsu, i bolau na' sovek wak shitau sovek dahshaya svi' ish-veh heh du, i kupi il would esh-tor wuh zhit t' ra i i' leralmin. Isha ik i dang fai-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor hopeless, i dang fai-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor wuh baseness. Kuv i had sovek such possibility, kauk na' wuh remote ir t' tevun, harboured svi' t'nash-veh nahp, heh ipik svi' t'nash-veh khaf-spol--kuv ish-veh ek'wak had vesh' tra'--kuv ish-veh ek'wak kupi nam-tor tra'--i kupi ri i' esta nash pudor-tor el'ru." au laid ish-veh sha' fi-tor ish-veh u' au stariben. "rai, tal-kam hassu manette. Spo' du, wuh toripik sashasolaya s' france; spo' du, driven s' ish-veh k' its distractions, oppressions, heh miseries; spo' du, striving tor ha-tor maf s' ish-veh k' t'nash-veh sha' pideshan, heh trusting svi' wuh happier fa-wak; i glazhau goh tor thresh-tor ish-veh fortunes, thresh-tor ish-veh ha'kiv heh ha-kel, heh hasu faithful tor du tor wuh tevakh. Ri tor dahsaya k' lucie ish-veh privilege u' ish-veh kan, besu, heh t'hy'la; tonk'peh tor sarlah svi' mamuk t' ish-veh, heh bind ish-veh closer tor du, kuv such wuh vel mokuhlek nam-tor." ish-veh esta fam dvun svizh-tor fi' ish-veh sa-mekh's el'ru. Answering wuh esta na' wuh moment, tonk'peh ri coldly, ish-veh sa-mekh shom-tor ish-veh el'ru fi-tor wuh kar t' ish-veh ku-san, heh glazhau abru na' wuh wuh'rak wak opi' wuh palikaya t' wuh conference. Wuh struggle vesh' evidently svi' ish-veh limuk; wuh struggle k' ik occasional glazhau if had wuh tendency svi' ish-veh tor gu'gelik vet heh dread. "du stariben ni feelingly heh ni manfully, charles darnay, ik i itaren du k' ek' t'nash-veh khaf-spol, heh dungi tu'ash ek' t'nash-veh khaf-spol--il nearly ni. Ma du sovek utvau tor dva-tor ik lucie ashau du?" "rim. U' wi, rim." "nam-tor ish-veh wuh iyi vel t' nash guhl'es, ik du lau na' wuh'wak ascertain ik, k' t'nash-veh fai-tukh?" "ri kauk ni. I lau ri ma wuh hopefulness tor tor ish-veh na' wehk gad; i lau (mistaken il ri mistaken) ma ik hopefulness tor-morrow." "tor du seek sovek guidance s' me?" "i ya'akash rim, osu. Tonk'peh i ma nahp ish-veh tor-yehat ik du lau ma ish-veh svi' ish-veh tepul, kuv du dang deem ish-veh gas'rak, tor mazhiv-kur-tor me ein." "tor du seek sovek ugaya s' me?" "i tor seek ik." "ra nam-tor ish-veh?" "i muhl ken-tor ik, rik' du, i kupi ma rai rok. I muhl ken-tor ik, kauk kuv din-tor manette meskarau me i' svi' ish-veh innocent khaf-spol--ri tor nah-tor i ma wuh presumption tor ngiq'e ni mau--i kupi retain rai shi svi' ish-veh tehnat ish-veh ashaya na' ish-veh sa-mekh." "kuv ik nam-tor ni, tor gla-tor du ra, fi' wuh vath el'ru, nam-tor involved svi' ish-veh?" "i ken-tor kaing muhl, ik wuh zhit s' ish-veh sa-mekh svi' sovek suitor's favour, would spunsau herself heh ek' wuh panu. Na' if utvau, hassu manette, " leralmin-tor darnay, modestly tonk'peh firmly, "i would ri ya'akash ik zhit, tor korsau t'nash-veh ha'kiv." "i am sure t' ish-veh. Charles darnay, mysteries arise s' ikap-tor ashaya, u' muhl u' s' eik dahsaya; svi' wuh former nuf, au nam-tor subtle heh delicate, heh rihagik tor penetrate. T'nash-veh ko-fu lucie nam-tor, svi' nash-veh respect, such wuh mystery tor me; i mokuhlek tor rai guess na' wuh fupa s' t' ish-veh khaf-spol." "sos ya'akash, osu, kuv du nah-tor she nam-tor--" u' au hesitated, ish-veh sa-mekh tanilau wuh shom. "nam-tor sought k' sovek vath suitor?" "ish-veh nam-tor ra i tvai tor leralmin." ish-veh sa-mekh panah-tor wuh pi' fa' au kilko-tor: "du ma gla-tor mr. Carton la', yourself. Mr. Stryver nam-tor la' nuh', occasionally. Kuv ish-veh nam-tor na' ek', ish-veh mokuhlek goh nam-tor k' veh t' aifa." "il fi', " leralmin-tor darnay. "i had ri nahp t' fi'; i dang ri nah-tor either, kesik. Du aitlun wuh ugaya s' me. Var-tor me ra ish-veh nam-tor." "ish-veh nam-tor, ik kuv din-tor manette dang katau tor du na' sovek wak, fi' ish-veh sha' krus, such wuh guhl'es u' i ma ventured tor ti fa' du, du dungi lesh testimony tor ra i ma leralmin-tor, heh tor ish-veh dva svi' ish-veh. I rok du lau nam-tor kup tor nah-tor ni muhl t' me, u' tor urge rai vi-yumuk tehnat me. I leralmin nothing weht t' t'nash-veh stake svi' nash; nash nam-tor ra i ya'akash. Wuh nosh fi' if i ya'akash ish-veh, heh if du ma wuh undoubted gas'rak tor require, i dungi glantau iyi." "i mazhiv-kur-tor wuh ugaya, " leralmin-tor wuh hassu, "rik' sovek nosh. I dva-tor ish-veh vel tor nam-tor, purely heh truthfully, u' du ma fupa s' ish-veh. I dva-tor ish-veh intention nam-tor tor perpetuate, heh ri tor kobatau, wuh ties svi' me heh t'nash-veh vath heh irak dearer shal. Kuv she dang ek'wak var-tor me ik du nam-tor bolayatik tor ish-veh buhfik happiness, i dungi mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tor du. Kuv tra' vesh'--charles darnay, kuv tra' vesh'--" wuh nu'ri sasu had taken ish-veh el'ru gratefully; ish-veh el'ru vesh' hau u' wuh hassu stariben: "--sovek fancies, sovek utvau, sovek apprehensions, sovek-vel whatsoever, uzh il hinek, tehnat wuh sasu she really ashau--wuh kharik responsibility thereof ri lying fi' ish-veh patam--au dang ek' nam-tor obliterated na' ish-veh sake. She nam-tor kanok-vei tor me; weht tor me do suffering, weht tor me do riyeht, weht tor me--muhl! Nash nam-tor idle variben." ni flekh vesh' wuh yut svi' if au spoh-tor vi' silence, heh ni flekh ish-veh teslau glazhau lu au had ceased tor stariben, ik darnay olau ish-veh sha' el'ru da-tor samu svi' wuh el'ru ik slowly sadalau heh eku-tor ish-veh. "du leralmin-tor vel tor me, " leralmin-tor hassu manette, breaking vi' wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut. "ra vesh' ish-veh du leralmin-tor tor me?" au vesh' na' wuh pak uf tor kilko-srashiv, abi' au vokau having spoken t' wuh nosh. Vas-tor u' ish-veh kashek reverted tor ik, au kilko-tor: "ish-veh guhl'es svi' me ought tor nam-tor fun-tor k' bosh guhl'es fi' t'nash-veh krus. T'nash-veh la' ahm, hi tonk'peh slightly rubai s' t'nash-veh ko-mekh's, nam-tor ri, u' du dungi vokau, t'nash-veh sha'. I istaya tor var-tor du ra ik nam-tor, heh po i am svi' england." "pehkaya!" leralmin-tor wuh hassu t' beauvais. "i istaya ish-veh, ik i lau wuh weh-rom nazh ish-veh guhl'es, heh ma rai tsat s' du." "pehkaya!" na' wuh instant, wuh hassu kauk had ish-veh dahkuh el'ru na' ish-veh kaluk; na' wuh'ashiv instant, kauk had ish-veh dahkuh el'ru laid fi' darnay's bru-lar. "var-tor me lu i ya'akash du, ri i'. Kuv ish-veh saikhut dang smusma, kuv lucie dang ashaya du, du dungau var-tor me fi' ish-veh kal'i'farr asal. Tor du ugaya?" "willingly. "mazhiv-kur-tor me ish-veh el'ru. She dungi nam-tor ha-kel directly, heh ish-veh nam-tor weh-rom she dang ri gla-tor etek teretuhr tor-mu-yor. Hal-tor! Oekon kudau du!" ish-veh vesh' gu'gelik lu charles darnay losrak ish-veh, heh ish-veh vesh' wuh wadan later heh darker lu lucie sarlah ha-kel; she hurried vi' wuh tvi-shal sa'awek--na' din-tor pross had hal-tor zehik abru-kaiden--heh vesh' ak'wikmun tor talal ish-veh telvan-ku-san herbosh. "t'nash-veh sa-mekh!" she puvutau tor ish-veh. "sa-mekh tal-kam!" nothing vesh' leralmin-tor svi' kilko-srashiv, tonk'peh she puzhu-tor wuh neik hammering ralash svi' ish-veh shi'yuk. Be' dvun-tor lightly mes' wuh intermediate tvi-shal, she glazhau svi' na' ish-veh svep heh sarlah sahran pla' koltha, maf-tor tor herself, k' ish-veh khaf ek' chilled, "ra dungau i tor! Ra dungau i tor!" ish-veh uncertainty palesh-tor tonk'peh wuh moment; she hurried pla', heh tapped na' ish-veh svep, heh softly puvutau tor ish-veh. Wuh ralash ceased na' wuh ralash t' ish-veh spes, heh au presently sasarlah tor ish-veh, heh au lates-tor abru heh ne' teretuhr na' wuh akarshif. Sarlah ish-veh ne' s' ish-veh sar-tak, tor glazhau na' ish-veh svi' ish-veh yuk ik mu-yor. Au yuk-tor heavily, heh ish-veh tray t' shoemaking raul, heh ish-veh hinek unfinished ar'kadan, vesh' ek' u' tsuri. Chapter xi. Wuh besu bikuv "sydney, " leralmin-tor mr. Stryver, fi' ik shal-ka mu-yor, il asal, tor ish-veh jackal; "rish wuh'ashiv yerak t' punch; i ma vel tor leralmin tor du." sydney had vesh' working dahtau mashen ik mu-yor, heh wuh mu-yor fa', heh wuh mu-yor fa' ik, heh wuh rom wehk mu-yor svi' succession, tor wuh grand clearance among mr. Stryver's dun fa' wuh setting svi' t' wuh wu vacation. Wuh clearance vesh' effected na' kim-shah; wuh stryver arrears vesh' handsomely zaprah abru; kanok-vei vesh' prah rid t' abi' november dang sarlah k' its fogs atmospheric, heh fogs legal, heh katau grist tor wuh mill va'ashiv. Sydney vesh' rim wuh livelier heh rim wuh soberer na' ni mau application. Ish-veh had taken wuh deal t' hayaik masupik-towelling tor seshaya ish-veh k'fai wuh mu-yor; wuh correspondingly hayaik nosahp t' wine had preceded wuh towelling; heh au vesh' svi' wuh maut zakar-tor nosh, u' au i' seshau ish-veh turban ska' heh threw ish-veh vi' wuh basin svi' if au had steeped ish-veh na' tvi-wak na' wuh kim-shah shehkuh wadan. "nam-tor du mixing ik vath yerak t' punch?" leralmin-tor stryver wuh portly, k' ish-veh el'ru svi' ish-veh waistband, glancing pauk s' wuh ku-san wilat au ti fi' ish-veh pla'. "i am." "i', glazhau la'! I am going tor var-tor du vel ik dungi rather ak'wikmun du, heh ik sos'eh dungi tor du nah-tor me ri ved u' shrewd u' du usually tor nah-tor me. I intend tor marry." "tor du?" "ha. Heh ri na' donku. Ra tor du leralmin i'?" "i ri tor olau sashitau tor leralmin mau. Vi nam-tor she?" "guess." "tor i fai-tor ish-veh?" "guess." "i am ri going tor guess, na' kaukuh o'wak-vel svi' wuh asal, k' t'nash-veh shi'nahp frying heh sputtering svi' t'nash-veh patam. Kuv du aitlun me tor guess, du bolau ya'akash me tor aru-yem." "muhl yi, i'll var-tor du, " leralmin-tor stryver, coming slowly vi' wuh sitting posture. "sydney, i rather despair t' tor myself intelligible tor du, fai'ei du nam-tor such wuh insensible dog." "heh du, " fun-tor sydney, toranik concocting wuh punch, "nam-tor such wuh kash-zakar heh poetical tam'a--" "sarlah!" rejoined stryver, laughing boastfully, "hi i ri tor prefer sovek claim tor hasu wuh soul t' romance (na' i rok i fai-tor weh-rom), fam dvun i am wuh tenderer wihfelau t' katravahsu do du." "du nam-tor wuh luckier, kuv du tvai ik." "i ri tor tvai ik. I tvai i am wuh sasu t' weht--weht--" "leralmin gallantry, du' du nam-tor pa' ish-veh, " suggested carton. "muhl! I'll leralmin gallantry. T'nash-veh meaning nam-tor ik i am wuh sasu, " leralmin-tor stryver, inflating himself na' ish-veh t'hy'la u' au tor wuh punch, "vi tun-tor weht tor nam-tor agreeable, vi nem-tor weht kusut-tor tor nam-tor agreeable, vi fai-tor weh-rom uf tor nam-tor agreeable, svi' wuh kosu's shila'es, do du tor." "hal-tor fi', " leralmin-tor sydney carton. "rai; tonk'peh fa' i hal-tor fi', " leralmin-tor stryver, shaking ish-veh patam svi' ish-veh bullying yut, "i'll ma nash si' k' du. Du've vesh' na' hassu manette's kelek u' mau u' i ma, il weht do i ma. Po, i ma vesh' kafusik t' ish-veh moroseness tra'! Ish-veh manners ma vesh' t' ik ralash-fam heh kir heh hangdog ves, ik, fi-tor t'nash-veh ha'kiv heh soul, i ma vesh' kafusik t' du, sydney!" "ish-veh dang nam-tor maut beneficial tor wuh sasu svi' ish-veh practice na' wuh mofek, tor nam-tor kafusik t' sovek-vel, " fun-tor sydney; "du ought tor nam-tor mau obliged tor me." "du dungau ri prah ska' svi' ik yut, " rejoined stryver, shouldering wuh rejoinder na' ish-veh; "rai, sydney, ish-veh's t'nash-veh gu-vam tor var-tor du--heh i var-tor du tor ish-veh limuk tor tor du rom--ik du nam-tor wuh devilish has-bosh-conditioned katravahsu svi' ik wihfelau t' shila'es. Du nam-tor wuh disagreeable katravahsu." sydney drank wuh bumper t' wuh punch au had tor, heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor. "glazhau na' me!" leralmin-tor stryver, squaring himself; "i ma lehkuh bolaya tor tor myself agreeable do du ma, hasu weht independent svi' circumstances. Po tor i tor ish-veh?" "du ri tor prah fi' k' ish-veh khrosahp t' ish-veh matrimonial intentions, " kilko-tor carton, k' wuh careless sov; "i istaya du would potau tor ik. U' tor me--dungi du worla ken-tor ik i am incorrigible?" au ya'akash wuh deshker k' ein appearance t' scorn. Stryver, preparing ish-veh k' ostentatious friendliness na' wuh disclosure au vesh' pa' tor tor, "fai'ei i fai-tor du ri tor tvai ulef du leralmin; heh kuv du tvai ish-veh ek', ish-veh would nam-tor t' rai importance. "du tor mention t' wuh nu'ri t'sai u' wuh pi-maat-kur-haired su-leitri. Wuh nu'ri t'sai nam-tor din-tor manette. Du aitlun ik kash-ral altogether; therefore i am rai weht annoyed lu i nah-tor t' wuh sagluvaya, do i dang nam-tor annoyed k' wuh sasu's opinion t' wuh bikuv t' t'nash-veh, vi had rai bezhun na' bikuv: il t' wuh krus t' ralash-tanaf t' t'nash-veh, vi had rai kaluk na' ralash-tanaf." sydney carton drank wuh punch na' wuh lo'uk tav; drank ish-veh k' bumpers, looking na' ish-veh t'hy'la. "i' du fai-tor ek' pa' ish-veh, syd, " leralmin-tor mr. Stryver. "i ri tor tun pa' fortune: she nam-tor wuh sem-rik-tor creature, heh i ma tor abru t'nash-veh kashek tor sanoi myself: fi' wuh bosh, i nah-tor i mokuhlek afford tor sanoi myself. She dungi ma svi' me wuh sasu already takov muhl ska', heh wuh rapidly rising sasu, heh wuh sasu t' ein distinction: ish-veh nam-tor wuh krus t' rom fortune na' ish-veh, tonk'peh she nam-tor worthy t' rom fortune. Nam-tor du astonished?" carton, fam dvun drinking wuh punch, rejoined, "po dang i nam-tor astonished?" "du messau?" carton, fam dvun drinking wuh punch, rejoined, "po dang i ri messau?" "muhl!" leralmin-tor ish-veh t'hy'la stryver, "du nem-tor ish-veh weht easily do i fancied du would, heh nam-tor lehkuh mercenary fi' t'nash-veh behalf do i nahp du would nam-tor; hi, tor nam-tor sure, du fai-tor muhl hiyet k' nash wak ik ish-veh t'kahr chum nam-tor wuh sasu t' wuh takov karik dungi. Ha, sydney, i ma had hiyet t' nash style t' ha'kiv, k' rai vath u' wuh rubah s' ish-veh; i olau ik ish-veh nam-tor wuh vaksurik vel na' wuh sasu ki' wuh ha-kel lu au olau vul-tor tor hal-tor tor ish-veh (lu au doesn't, au mokuhlek stay maf), heh i olau ik din-tor manette dungi var-tor muhl svi' sovek wurzel, heh dungi kwon-hau-ov tor me lit. Ni i ma tor abru t'nash-veh kashek. Heh i', sydney, hinek sa-kan, i aitlun tor leralmin wuh zhit tor du pa' ish-veh prospects. Du nam-tor svi' wuh rasahkos yut, du fai-tor; du really nam-tor svi' wuh rasahkos yut. "i', kal-tor me recommend du, " pursued stryver, "tor glazhau ish-veh svi' wuh limuk. I ma glazhau ish-veh svi' wuh limuk, svi' t'nash-veh natya yut; glazhau ish-veh svi' wuh limuk, du, svi' ish-veh natya yut. Marry. Tanilau somebody tor nem-tor tun t' du. Worla kashek ish-veh having rai tizh'es t' kosu's shila'es, il understanding t' ish-veh, il ish-veh na' ish-veh. Talal si' somebody. Talal si' ein respectable kosu k' wuh pi' veltra--somebody svi' wuh landlady yut, il lodging-letting yut--heh marry ish-veh, tehnat wuh sov-masuyanik gad. Ik's wuh ves t' vel na' du. I' nah-tor t' ish-veh, sydney." "i'll nah-tor t' ish-veh, " leralmin-tor sydney. Chapter xii. Wuh katravahsu t' delicacy mr. Stryver having tor abru ish-veh kashek tor ik magnanimous bestowal t' rom fortune fi' wuh hassu's ko-fu, resolved tor tor ish-veh happiness fainu tor ish-veh fa' au losrak kahr na' wuh wu vacation. Po' ein mental debating t' wuh sfek, sarlah ish-veh tor wuh conclusion ik ish-veh would nam-tor u' muhl tor prah ek' wuh preliminaries ovsoh k', heh au kupi yi arrange na' ish-veh el-wak whether au dang mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ish-veh el'ru wuh wehk gad il dahkuh fa' michaelmas zhil, il svi' wuh pi' christmas vacation svi' ish-veh heh hilary. U' tor wuh karik'es t' ish-veh nuf, au had ri wuh vet pa' ish-veh, tonk'peh clearly gla-tor ish-veh yut tor wuh verdict. Gyirm'i k' wuh jury fi' substantial worldly solektra--wuh goh solektra ek'wak don taking vi' khrosahp--ish-veh vesh' wuh eiktra nuf, heh had ri wuh kobat gla-tor svi' ish-veh. Au puvutau himself na' wuh plaintiff, tra' vesh' rai getting abru' ish-veh evidence, wuh counsel na' wuh defendant threw abru ish-veh brief, heh wuh jury did ri kauk da-tor tor panah-tor. Po' trying ish-veh, stryver, c. J, vesh' satisfied ik rai plainer nuf kupi nam-tor. Accordingly, mr. Stryver inaugurated wuh wu vacation k' wuh hotorik mnah tor nem-tor din-tor manette tor vauxhall bah-ker; ik failing, tor ranelagh; ik unaccountably failing nuh', ish-veh behoved ish-veh tor la' himself svi' soho, heh tra' afsakau ish-veh thol kashek. Na' soho, therefore, mr. Stryver shouldered ish-veh yut s' wuh temple, du' wuh svai t' wuh wu vacation's infancy vesh' fam dvun fi-tor ish-veh. Anybody vi had gla-tor ish-veh projecting himself vi' soho du' au vesh' wi fi' osu dunstan's vla t' temple mofek, bursting svi' ish-veh bosh-blown yut bi' wuh pavement, tor wuh jostlement t' ek' weaker sutra, lau ma gla-tor uf safe heh karik au vesh'. Ish-veh yut taking ish-veh vesht tellson's, heh au fi' banking na' tellson's heh fai-tor mr. Lorry u' wuh intimate t'hy'la t' wuh manettes, ish-veh svi-tor mr. "halloa!" leralmin-tor mr. Stryver. "uf tor du tor? I rok du nam-tor muhl!" ish-veh vesh' stryver's grand peculiarity ik au kwon-hau-ov seemed nuh' suk' na' sovek shi, il ret. Rom asal." yi mr. Eifa venerable heh kobat persons vesh' kwon-hau-ov gla-tor k' wuh tsuri svi' wuh bae'cok t' bowing, heh vesh' popularly pudva-tor, lu au had ovalau wuh klepovausu si', fam dvun tor potau fi' bowing svi' wuh herbosh office abi' au ovalau wuh'ashiv klepovausu svi'. I fai-tor nash bolau kwon-hau-ov nam-tor wuh sival subject k' wuh skan; kal-tor etek leralmin rai weht pa' ish-veh." "i ri tor ken-tor du, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry. "i dare leralmin ri, " rejoined stryver, nodding ish-veh patam svi' wuh smoothing heh kim-shah yut; "rai tukh, rai tukh." "tonk'peh ish-veh tor tukh, " mr. Lorry urged. "rai ish-veh doesn't; i assure du ish-veh doesn't. Having supposed ik tra' vesh' kash-ral wilat tra' nam-tor rai kash-ral, heh wuh laudable ambition wilat tra' nam-tor ri wuh laudable ambition, i am muhl s' t'nash-veh lafosh, heh rai klau nam-tor ovsoh. Nu'ri kosu ma committed kahwa follies k'ashiv fa', heh ma repented au svi' poverty heh obscurity k'ashiv fa'. Svi' wuh unselfish pulva, ni'droi'ik nar-tor ik wuh vel nam-tor eku-tor, fai'ei ish-veh would ma vesh' wuh rasahkos vel na' me svi' wuh worldly sfek t' zan-tor; svi' wuh selfish pulva, i am glad ik wuh vel has eku-tor, fai'ei ish-veh would ma vesh' wuh rasahkos vel na' me svi' wuh worldly sfek t' zan-tor--ish-veh nam-tor hardly bolayatik tor leralmin i kupi ma nazh-tor nothing k' ish-veh. Tra' nam-tor rai klau na' ek' ovsoh. I ma ri proposed tor wuh nu'ri t'sai, heh, svi' ourselves, i am k' rai tvai ac'ruth, fi' haulan, ik i ek'wak dang ma committed myself tor ik sadvun. Mr. Lorry, du fam yehat tash wuh mincing vanities heh giddinesses t' herbosh-headed ko-kan; du bolau ri gish tor tor ish-veh, il du dungi kwon-hau-ov nam-tor disappointed. I', pray leralmin rai weht pa' ish-veh. I var-tor du, i regret ish-veh fi' khrosahp t' vath, tonk'peh i am satisfied fi' t'nash-veh sha' khrosahp. Heh i am really maut mau obliged tor du na' allowing me tor ralash du, heh na' giving me ish-veh na'shikh; du fai-tor wuh nu'ri t'sai weh-rom do i tor; du vesh' gas'rak, ish-veh worla would ma ovsoh." mr. Lorry vesh' ni taken aback, ik au glazhau ved stupidly na' mr. Stryver shouldering ish-veh na' wuh svep, k' wuh appearance t' showering generosity, forbearance, heh goodwill, fi' ish-veh erring patam. "tor wuh buhfik t' ish-veh, t'nash-veh tal-kam osu, " leralmin-tor stryver; "leralmin rai weht pa' ish-veh; nemaiyo va'ashiv na' allowing me tor ralash du; rom mu-yor!" mr. Lorry vesh' si' svi' wuh mu-yor, fa' au fai-tor wilat au vesh'. Mr. Stryver vesh' lying pla' fi' ish-veh ku-san, winking na' ish-veh abru-tol. Chapter xiii. Wuh katravahsu t' rai delicacy kuv sydney carton ek'wak min-tor sovek-wilat, au certainly worla min-tor svi' wuh kelek t' hassu manette. Au had vesh' tra' k'ashiv, du' wuh bosh tevun, heh had kwon-hau-ov vesh' wuh ka moody heh morose lounger tra'. Lu au tun-tor tor variben, au variben muhl; tonk'peh, wuh wan t' caring na' nothing, if overshadowed ish-veh k' such wuh fatal mu'khlup'es, vesh' maut rarely tilau k' wuh ta'hal k'svi ish-veh. Heh wi au did tun vel na' wuh yut ik environed ik kelek, heh na' wuh senseless kov ik tor ish-veh pavements. Wehk wuh mu-yor au vaguely heh unhappily czar-tor tra', lu wine had katau rai transitory gladness tor ish-veh; wehk wuh dreary gad-keshtan revealed ish-veh solitary khlop svizh-tor tra', heh fam dvun svizh-tor tra' lu wuh wuh'rak ha-zehl t' wuh yel katau vi' karik vas, snem-tor beauties t' te'koshif svi' spires t' churches heh lofty kelek, u' sos'eh wuh hizhuk wak katau ein kash-ral t' weh-rom vel, else yen-tor heh unattainable, vi' ish-veh kashek. T' tab-ma, wuh neglected sar-tak svi' wuh temple kelek had fainu ish-veh weht scantily do ek'wak; heh k'ashiv lu au had lehm-tor himself fi-tor ish-veh rai longer do wuh zamu minutes, au had prah abru va'ashiv, heh haunted ik neighbourhood. Fi' wuh gad svi' august, lu mr. Stryver (po' notifying tor ish-veh jackal ik "au had nahp weh-rom t' ik marrying tukh") had lesh ish-veh delicacy vi' devonshire, heh lu wuh glan heh scent t' svai svi' wuh kahr yut had ein waifs t' goodness svi' au na' wuh rasahkos, t' muhl'es na' wuh sickliest, heh t' youth na' wuh oldest, sydney's ash'ya fam dvun sahr-tor eifa kov. S' hasu irresolute heh purposeless, ish-veh ash'ya became animated k' wuh intention, heh, svi' wuh working s' ik intention, au nem-tor ish-veh tor wuh hassu's svep. Au vesh' shown abru-kaiden, heh afer-tor lucie na' ish-veh ar'kadan, sa'awek. She had worla vesh' ved na' ish-veh ease k' ish-veh, heh poprah ish-veh k' ein pi' embarrassment u' au hayal-tor himself be' ish-veh pasu. Tonk'peh, looking abru na' ish-veh limuk svi' wuh interchange t' wuh wuh'rak zamu tsuri-shitau, she glantau wuh rubah svi' ish-veh. "i pthak du nam-tor ri muhl, mr. Carton!" "rai. Tonk'peh wuh ha'kiv i ras-tukh, din-tor manette, nam-tor ri conducive tor muhl'es. Ra nam-tor tor nam-tor gishu t', il k', such profligates?" "nam-tor ish-veh ri--forgive me; i ma palikau wuh deshker fi' t'nash-veh bru-lar--wuh pity tor ha-tor rai weh-rom ha'kiv?" "oekon fai-tor ish-veh nam-tor wuh mesh!" "yi po ri rubah ish-veh?" looking kogavik na' ish-veh va'ashiv, she vesh' ak'wikmun heh saddened tor gla-tor ik tra' vesh' bezhun-masu svi' ish-veh bezhun. Tra' vesh' bezhun-masu svi' ish-veh spes nuh', u' au kilko-tor: "ish-veh nam-tor nuh' tab-ma na' ik. I dungau worla nam-tor weh-rom do i am. I dungau ne'hal-tor weh-neik, heh nam-tor weh-rasahkos." au gal-tor wuh kar-nef fi' ish-veh pasu, heh wein-tor ish-veh bezhun k' ish-veh el'ru. Wuh pasu trembled svi' wuh silence ik zahal-tor. She had worla gla-tor ish-veh softened, heh vesh' mau flakosh. Au fai-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor ni, rik' looking na' ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor: "pray forgive me, din-tor manette. I shaya ne' fa' wuh fai-tukh t' ra i aitlun tor leralmin tor du. Dungi du zhu-tor me?" "kuv ish-veh dungi tor du sovek rom, mr. Carton, kuv ish-veh would tor du happier, ish-veh would tor me maut glad!" "oekon kudau du na' ish-veh slor utan'es!" au unshaded ish-veh limuk po' wuh pi' du', heh stariben steadily. "ri tor nam-tor kwes tor zhu-tor me. Ri tor shrink s' sovek-vel i leralmin. I am spo' veh vi tev-tor nu'ri. Ek' t'nash-veh ha'kiv lau ma vesh'." "rai, mr. Carton. I am sure ik wuh buhfik krus t' ish-veh lau fam dvun nam-tor; i am sure ik du lau nam-tor mau, mau worthier t' yourself." "leralmin t' du, din-tor manette, heh hi i fai-tor weh-rom--hi svi' wuh mystery t' t'nash-veh sha' wretched khaf-spol i fai-tor weh-rom--i dungau worla yen-tor ish-veh!" she vesh' spoh heh trembling. Sarlah ish-veh tor ish-veh vas k' wuh teslau despair t' himself if tor wuh interview rikes sovek vath ik kupi ma vesh' holden. "kuv ish-veh had vesh' tor-yehat, din-tor manette, ik du kupi ma fun-tor wuh ashaya t' wuh sasu gla-tor du fa' yourself--flung maf, thinoi, drunken, ri donku-tor creature t' misuse u' du fai-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor--au would ma vesh' d'wonil nash gad heh wadan, svi' spite t' ish-veh happiness, ik au would katau du tor misery, katau du tor sorrow heh repentance, luk-has du, disgrace du, seshaya du ne' k' ish-veh. I fai-tor maut muhl ik du mokuhlek ma rai tenderness na' me; i ya'akash na' rim; i am kauk itar-bosh ik ish-veh fam yehat nam-tor." "rik' ish-veh, mokuhlek i ri korsau du, mr. Carton? Mokuhlek i ri recall du--forgive me va'ashiv!--tor wuh weh-rom rivak? Mokuhlek i svi' rai yut repay ish-veh guhl'es? I fai-tor nash nam-tor wuh guhl'es, " she modestly leralmin-tor, po' wuh pi' vaunah, heh svi' earnest bezhun-masu, "i fai-tor du would leralmin nash tor kling else. Mokuhlek i da-tor ish-veh tor rai rom khrosahp na' yourself, mr. Carton?" au hutau ish-veh patam. "tor rim. Rai, din-tor manette, tor rim. Kuv du dungi zhu-tor me k'fai wuh maut pi' weht, ek' du mokuhlek ek'wak tor na' me nam-tor ovsoh. I istaya du tor fai-tor ik du ma vesh' wuh kim-shah sahr-tor t' t'nash-veh soul. Svi' t'nash-veh degradation i ma ri vesh' ni degraded tonk'peh ik wuh glan t' du k' ish-veh sa-mekh, heh t' nash ha-kel tor such wuh ha-kel k' du, has stirred hinek duv ik i nahp had tev-tor s' me. Opi' i fai-tor du, i ma vesh' troubled k' wuh remorse ik i nahp would worla reproach me va'ashiv, heh ma puzhu-tor zhal-tor s' hinek spes impelling me abru'le, ik i nahp vesh' ralash-fam na' ek'wak. I ma had unformed ideas t' striving afresh, palikaya anew, shaking ska' sloth heh sensuality, heh fighting si' wuh abandoned puk. Wuh sahr-tor, ek' wuh sahr-tor, ik shahtau svi' nothing, heh mor wuh sleeper wilat au ti ne', tonk'peh i istaya du tor fai-tor ik du vi'le-esh-tor ish-veh." "dungi nothing t' ish-veh hafau? O mr. Carton, nah-tor va'ashiv! Ar'kadan va'ashiv!" "rai, din-tor manette; ek' k'fai ish-veh, i ma fainu myself tor nam-tor ved undeserving. Heh wi i ma had wuh kobat'es, heh ma fam dvun wuh kobat'es, tor istaya du tor fai-tor k' ra wuh sudden tren'es du kindled me, tuh t' vitush ik i am, vi' yon--wuh yon, however, inseparable svi' its malat s' myself, quickening nothing, ha'gelan nothing, doing rai dvin, idly yontau maf." "opi' ish-veh nam-tor t'nash-veh misfortune, mr. Carton, ki' tor du weht unhappy do du vesh' fa' du fai-tor me--" "ri tor leralmin ik, din-tor manette, na' du would ma reclaimed me, kuv sovek-vel kupi. Du dungi ri nam-tor wuh aishan t' t'nash-veh becoming weh-rasahkos." "opi' wuh fupa s' t' ish-veh kashek ik du kethelvau, nam-tor, na' ek' pavek, attributable tor ein vi-yumuk t' t'nash-veh--nash nam-tor ra i tvai, kuv i mokuhlek tor ish-veh eiktra--mokuhlek i nam-tor-tor rai vi-yumuk tor dvin-tor du? Ma i rai tepul na' rom, k' du, na' ek'?" "wuh utmost rom ik i am capable t' i', din-tor manette, ki'sarlah nash-veh la' tor realise. Kal-tor me lesh k'fai wuh shom t' t'nash-veh misdirected ha'kiv, wuh remembrance ik i tu'ash t'nash-veh khaf-spol tor du, kim-shah t' ek' wuh panu; heh ik tra' vesh' vel losrak svi' me na' nash wak if du kupi deplore heh pity." "if i entreated du tor dva-tor, va'ashiv heh va'ashiv, danik fervently, k' ek' t'nash-veh khaf-spol, vesh' capable t' weh-rom vel, mr. Carton!" "entreat me tor dva-tor ish-veh rai weht, din-tor manette. I ma skan-tor myself, heh i fai-tor weh-rom. I flakosh du; i bes-tor sahris tor wuh shaht. Dungi du kal-tor me dva-tor, lu i recall nash gad, ik wuh kim-shah guhl'es t' t'nash-veh ha'kiv vesh' reposed svi' ish-veh pure heh innocent thasek, heh ik ish-veh ti tra' sa'awek, heh dungi nam-tor thresh-tor k' kling?" "kuv ik dungi nam-tor wuh consolation tor du, ha." "ri kauk k' wuh dearest veh ek'wak tor nam-tor fainu tor du?" "mr. Carton, " she kilko-tor, po' wuh pahutau svizh, "wuh tsat nam-tor ish-veh, ri t'nash-veh; heh i ugaya tor respect ish-veh." "nemaiyo. Heh va'ashiv, oekon kudau du." au shitau ish-veh el'ru tor ish-veh bru-lar, heh dvun-tor na' wuh svep. "nam-tor ne' rai apprehension, din-tor manette, t' t'nash-veh ek'wak resuming nash conversation k' ni mau u' wuh be' dvun-tor zhit. I dungi worla dzhinau tor ish-veh va'ashiv. Kuv i vesh' tevik, ik kupi ri nam-tor surer do ish-veh nam-tor henceforth. Svi' wuh wadan t' t'nash-veh tevakh, i dungau meskaraya sacred wuh veh rom remembrance--heh dungau itaren heh kudau du na' ish-veh--ik t'nash-veh kim-shah avowal t' myself vesh' tor tor du, heh ik t'nash-veh ahm, heh lafot, heh miseries vesh' kogavik lesh svi' ish-veh khaf-spol. Lau ish-veh vathru nam-tor ta'hal heh kunli!" au vesh' ni rikes ra au had ek'wak shown himself tor nam-tor, heh ish-veh vesh' ni maf tor nah-tor uf mau au had lehm-tor maf, heh uf mau au kanok gad potau ne' heh perverted, ik lucie manette wept mournfully na' ish-veh u' au lam-tor looking pla' na' ish-veh. "nam-tor comforted!" au leralmin-tor, "i am ri don such olaya, din-tor manette. Wuh wadan il dahkuh hence, heh wuh neik besu heh neik es'merka ik i scorn tonk'peh yield tor, dungi render me lehkuh don such bezhun-masu u' eifa, do sovek wretch vi creeps bi' wuh yut. Nam-tor comforted! Tonk'peh, k'svi myself, i dungau kwon-hau-ov nam-tor, na' du, ra i am i', hi outwardly i dungau nam-tor ra du ma heretofore gla-tor me. Wuh kim-shah supplication tonk'peh veh i tor tor du, nam-tor, ik du dungi dva-tor nash t' me." "i dungi, mr. Carton." "t'nash-veh kim-shah supplication t' ek', nam-tor nash; heh k' ish-veh, i dungi vas-tor du t' wuh visitor k' ik i muhl fai-tor du ma nothing svi' unison, heh svi' ik heh du tra' nam-tor wuh impassable ret. Ish-veh nam-tor nam-tor-fam tor leralmin ish-veh, i fai-tor, tonk'peh ish-veh she-tor s' t'nash-veh soul. Na' du, heh na' sovek tal-kam tor du, i would tor sovek-vel. Kuv t'nash-veh career vesh' t' ik weh-rom ves ik tra' vesh' sovek opportunity il tsoh t' sacrifice svi' ish-veh, i would nartaya sovek sacrifice na' du heh na' eifa tal-kam tor du. Ar'kadan tor meskaraya me svi' ish-veh kashek, na' ein hizhuk wak, u' ardent heh sincere svi' nash-veh vel. Wuh wak dungi sarlah, wuh wak dungi ri nam-tor wu svi' coming, lu uzh ties dungi nam-tor shidau pa' du--ties ik dungi bind du wi weht tenderly heh strongly tor wuh ha-kel du ni tong'av--wuh dearest ties ik dungi ek'wak takov heh gladden du. O din-tor manette, lu wuh pi' bikuv t' wuh kunli sa-mekh's limuk glazhau abru svi' ish-veh, lu gla-tor du ish-veh sha' ugelik vaksur springing abru anew na' ish-veh ash'ya, nah-tor i' heh yi ik tra' nam-tor wuh sasu vi would mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ha'kiv, tor potau wuh ha'kiv du ashaya be' du!" au leralmin-tor, "rom-halan!" leralmin-tor wuh kim-shah "oekon kudau du!" heh losrak ish-veh. Chapter xiv. Wuh trau tradesman tor wuh bezhun t' mr. Jeremiah cruncher, sitting fi' ish-veh stool svi' halitra-yut k' ish-veh grisly urchin be' ish-veh, wuh vast su'etek heh vuhna'es t' vel svi' dvun vesh' kanok gad presented. Vi kupi hayal-tor fi-tor sovek-vel svi' halitra-yut du' wuh toranik wadan t' wuh gad, heh ri nam-tor dazed heh deafened k' dahkuh immense processions, veh ek'wak tending na'tev'rak k' wuh yel, wuh vath ek'wak tending na'she'rak s' wuh yel, fi' ek'wak tending tor wuh eiktra mesakh wuh eik'es t' yon-kur heh gahv-kur wilat wuh yel hal-tor ne'! K' ish-veh terp svi' ish-veh ru'lut, mr. Cruncher hayal-tor watching wuh dahkuh pilash, spo' wuh heathen rustic vi has na' several centuries vesh' fi' gu-vam watching veh pilash--saving ik jerry had rai gishat t' ish-veh ek'wak sahran pseth. Il would ish-veh ma vesh' wuh gishat t' wuh hopeful ves, opi' wuh pi' krus t' ish-veh income vesh' derived s' wuh pilotage t' timid kosu (mostly t' wuh bosh es'merka heh vesht wuh svitan zhil t' ha'kiv) s' tellson's vla t' wuh mashen tor wuh mesyutik gef. Brief u' such besu'es vesh' svi' kanok dahshauk instance, mr. Cruncher worla vravshau tor shetau ni interested svi' wuh t'sai u' tor sagluvau wuh karik aitlun tor ma wuh dor t' drinking ish-veh maut rom muhl'es. Heh ish-veh vesh' s' wuh mazhiv-kur bestowed fi-tor ish-veh na' wuh execution t' nash benevolent lof, ik au recruited ish-veh donkes-tor, u' aishan i' glantau. Wak vesh', lu wuh poet hayal-tor fi-tor wuh stool svi' wuh tsuri shi, heh mused svi' wuh glan t' sasu. Mr. Cruncher, sitting fi' wuh stool svi' wuh tsuri shi, tonk'peh ri hasu wuh poet, mused u' pi' u' tor-yehat, heh glazhau pa' ish-veh. Ish-veh tevan-tor si' ik au vesh' thus engaged svi' wuh tevun-yonuk lu patreitan vesh' zamu, heh belated kosu zamu, heh lu ish-veh tek'ik svi' paik vesh' ni unprosperous u' tor awaken wuh karik suspicion svi' ish-veh thasek ik mrs. Cruncher bolau ma vesh' "tevan-tor" svi' ein sfekau manner, lu wuh ritsuri concourse pouring ne' halitra-yut na'tev'rak, skamau ish-veh attention. Looking ik yut, mr. Cruncher tor si' ik ein ves t' mem-lu til-kum vesh' coming bi', heh ik tra' vesh' popular objection tor nash mem-lu til-kum, if engendered uproar. "nu'ri jerry, " leralmin-tor mr. Cruncher, turning tor ish-veh offspring, "ish-veh's wuh buryin'." "hooroar, sa-mekh!" maf-tor nu'ri jerry. Wuh nu'ri gentleman uttered nash exultant ralash k' mysterious significance. Wuh tela'at gentleman nem-tor wuh maf ni has-bosh, ik au glantau ish-veh opportunity, heh smote wuh nu'ri gentleman fi' wuh kaluk. "ra d'ye tvai? Ra nam-tor du hooroaring na'? Ra tor du aitlun tor conwey tor ish-veh sha' sa-mekh, du nu'ri tres? Nash sa-kan nam-tor wuh getting nuh' wehk na' me!" leralmin-tor mr. Cruncher, surveying ish-veh. "ish-veh heh ish-veh hooroars! Ri tor kal-tor me zhu-tor rai weht t' du, il du dungau olau ein weht t' me. D'ye zhu-tor?" "i vikau't doing rai klau, " nu'ri jerry protested, rubbing ish-veh nak. "eku ish-veh yi, " leralmin-tor mr. Cruncher; "i skil-tor't ma rim t' ish-veh rai klau. Prah wuh fik t' ik tra' ku-san, heh glazhau na' wuh patreitan." ish-veh sa-fu obeyed, heh wuh patreitan betau; au vesh' bawling heh hissing pauk wuh dingy hearse heh dingy mourning coach, svi' if mourning coach tra' vesh' goh veh mourner, sai-vel-tor svi' wuh dingy trappings ik vesh' panah-tor bolayatik tor wuh dignity t' wuh shul. Wuh shul saudau k' rai tvai tor sanoi ish-veh, however, k' wuh increasing rabble surrounding wuh coach, deriding ish-veh, tor grimaces na' ish-veh, heh incessantly groaning heh calling si': "yah! Zamasu! Tst! Yaha! Zamasu!" k' wehk compliments nuh' numerous heh nekwitau-yehat tor ashiv-tor. Mem-lu til-kum had na' ek' wak wuh remarkable skamaya na' mr. Cruncher; au kwon-hau-ov pricked abru ish-veh kash-ral, heh became teporilau, lu wuh mem-lu til-kum be' dvun-tor tellson's. Naturally, therefore, wuh mem-lu til-kum k' nash uncommon attendance teporilau ish-veh greatly, heh au ya'akash t' wuh wuh'rak sasu vi sahr-tor tehnat ish-veh: "ra nam-tor ish-veh, sa-kai? Ra's ish-veh pa'?" "i ri tor fai-tor, " leralmin-tor wuh sasu. "zamasu! Yaha! Tst! Zamasu!" au ya'akash wuh'ashiv sasu. "vi nam-tor ish-veh?" "i ri tor fai-tor, " fun-tor wuh sasu, clapping ish-veh el'ru tor ish-veh ru'lut nevertheless, heh vociferating svi' wuh surprising falek heh k' wuh greatest ardour, "zamasu! Yaha! Tst, tst! Spi--ies!" na' wu-vath, wuh person weh-rom informed fi' wuh merits t' wuh nuf, tumbled tehnat ish-veh, heh s' nash person au oren-tor ik wuh mem-lu til-kum vesh' wuh mem-lu til-kum t' veh roger cly. "vesh' au wuh zamasu?" ya'akash mr. Cruncher. "hinek bailey zamasu, " fun-tor ish-veh informant. "yaha! Tst! Yah! Hinek bailey spi--i--ies!" "po, tor nam-tor sure!" sporiben jerry, recalling wuh trial na' if au had gol-tor. "i've gla-tor ish-veh. Tevik, nam-tor au?" "tevik u' mutton, " fun-tor wuh vath, "heh mokuhlek't nam-tor nuh' tevik. Ma 'em si', tra'! Zamasu! Seshaya 'em si', tra'! Zamasu!" wuh idea vesh' ni acceptable svi' wuh prevalent k'torr sovek idea, ik wuh patreitan kum-tor ish-veh abru k' eagerness, heh loudly repeating wuh suggestion ki' 'em si', heh tor seshaya 'em si', patreitau wuh dahkuh hali ni closely ik sarlah au tor wuh pehkaya. Fi' wuh patreitan's sharu wuh coach svep, wuh veh mourner scuffled si' k' himself heh vesh' svi' ish-veh el'ru na' wuh moment; tonk'peh au vesh' ni alert, heh tor such rom nam-tor-tor t' ish-veh wak, ik svi' wuh'ashiv moment au vesh' scouring maf abru wuh bye-yut, po' fosha ish-veh tor-sai, taik, wu hatband, wan-kur abru'lik-handkerchief, heh vath symbolical bezhun-masu. Aifa, wuh sutra tore tor krus heh scattered irak heh eik k' lo'uk tizh'es, du' wuh tradesmen hurriedly ikap'uh t'du ru'lut ish-veh mahr-kel; na' wuh patreitan svi' eifa wak pehkau na' nothing, heh vesh' wuh stislak mau dreaded. Au had already prah wuh wu-vath t' sharu wuh hearse tor nem-tor wuh tevikeh-natuhn si', lu ein brighter genius proposed instead, its hasu escorted tor its destination amidst paik rejoicing. Practical suggestions hasu mau bolau, nash suggestion, nuh', vesh' poprah k' acclamation, heh wuh coach vesh' iyi boshau k' ohkuh svi'udish heh wuh dozen si', du' u' wehk sutra prah fi' wuh kamu t' wuh hearse u' kupi k' sovek tusok t' ingenuity terpau fi-tor ish-veh. Among wuh wuh'rak t' aifa volunteers vesh' jerry cruncher himself, vi modestly ip-sut ish-veh spiky patam s' wuh glantaya t' tellson's, svi' wuh further teruk t' wuh mourning coach. Wuh officiating undertakers tor ein protest tehnat aifa rubai svi' wuh hali-kal; tonk'peh, wuh pilash hasu alarmingly be', heh several spes remarking fi' wuh efficacy t' samu immersion svi' bringing refractory kisau t' wuh ha'yigal tor utvau, wuh protest vesh' faint heh brief. Wuh remodelled procession palikau, k' wuh vuzh-mev-fnashtaya driving wuh hearse--na'shikhau k' wuh regular yetursu, vi vesh' perched be' ish-veh, ne' ikap-tor inspection, na' wuh lof--heh k' wuh pieman, isha attended k' ish-veh tsorayek minister, driving wuh mourning coach. Wuh lesh-leader, wuh popular yut character t' wuh wak, vesh' impressed u' wuh hayaik fanet, fa' wuh cavalcade had hal-tor irak ne' wuh strand; heh ish-veh lesh, vi vesh' nesh-kur heh maut mangy, mazhiv-kur-tor ved wuh undertaking sov tor ik krus t' wuh procession svi' if au lates-tor. Thus, k' naliveh-drinking, mev-smoking, song-roaring, heh vaik caricaturing t' woe, wuh disorderly procession went its yut, recruiting na' kanok ash, heh ek' wuh mahr-kel shutting abru fa' ish-veh. Its destination vesh' wuh hinek church t' osu pancras, irak ska' svi' wuh vunai. Ish-veh prah tra' svi' rivak t' wak; insisted fi' pouring vi' wuh visolektaya-solektra; t'forti, accomplished wuh interment t' wuh tevik roger cly svi' its sha' yut, heh highly tor its sha' satisfaction. Wuh tevik sasu sashitau t', heh wuh patreitan hasu ne' wuh bolayek t' providing ein vath entertainment na' itself, wuh'ashiv brighter genius (il sos'eh wuh ka) conceived wuh humour t' impeaching casual passers-k', u' hinek bailey zamasu, heh wreaking vengeance fi' au. A'vesh' vesh' putan-tor tor ein nosahp t' inoffensive persons vi had worla vesh' be' wuh hinek bailey svi' ish-veh ha-tor, svi' wuh realisation t' nash fancy, heh au vesh' roughly hustled heh maltreated. Wuh transition tor wuh torvukh t' krani-breaking, heh thence tor wuh plundering t' tsuri-kelek, vesh' hagik heh malatik. Na' kim-shah, po' several wadan, lu sundry belaar-kelek had vesh' seshau ne', heh ein shal-railings had vesh' torn abru, tor kar wuh weht belligerent tam'a, wuh rumour prah pa' ik wuh klashau vesh' coming.
