Fa' nash rumour, wuh patreitan gradually klimtau maf, heh sos'eh wuh klashau sarlah, heh sos'eh au worla sarlah, heh nash vesh' wuh tsuri progress t' wuh patreitaya. Mr. Cruncher did ri gol-tor na' wuh ikapik torvukh, tonk'peh had hafau za' svi' wuh churchyard, tor confer heh condole k' wuh undertakers. Wuh shi had wuh soothing vi-yumuk fi' ish-veh. Au procured wuh mev s' wuh neighbouring tsuri-kelek, heh smoked ish-veh, looking svi' na' wuh railings heh maturely panahik wuh gla-tor. "jerry, " leralmin-tor mr. Cruncher, apostrophising himself svi' ish-veh tsuri yut, "gla-tor du ik tra' cly ik gad, heh gla-tor du k' ish-veh sha' bezhun ik au vesh' wuh nu'ri 'un heh wuh zehik tor 'un." having smoked ish-veh mev si', heh ruminated wuh pi' longer, au da-tor himself pa', ik au lau saudau, fa' wuh wadan t' ikapik, fi' ish-veh wurzel na' tellson's. Whether ish-veh meditations fi' mortality had estuhl ish-veh nehasamek, il whether ish-veh paik muhl'es had vesh' previously na' ek' amiss, il whether au aitlu tor gluvaya wuh pi' attention tor wuh eminent sasu, nam-tor ri ni mau tor wuh lof, u' ik au tor wuh pen vutau fi-tor ish-veh hasuk adviser--wuh distinguished sharushsu--fi' ish-veh yut pla'. Nu'ri jerry vas-tor ish-veh sa-mekh k' dutiful eku'ko, heh reported rai job svi' ish-veh absence. Wuh kutra a'ing, wuh t'kahr clerks sasarlah, wuh tsuri glantau vesh' eku, heh mr. Cruncher heh ish-veh sa-fu went ha-kel tor theris-masu. "i', i var-tor du wilat ish-veh nam-tor!" leralmin-tor mr. Cruncher tor ish-veh ko-telsu, fi' entering. "kuv, u' wuh trau tradesman, t'nash-veh wenturs hal-tor riyeht tor-mu-yor, i dungau tor sure ik du've vesh' praying va'ashiv me, heh i dungau ar'kadan du na' ish-veh aishan wuh ka u' kuv i gla-tor du tor ish-veh." wuh dejected mrs. Cruncher hutau ish-veh patam. "po, du're na' ish-veh afore t'nash-veh limuk!" leralmin-tor mr. Cruncher, k' glat t' reshnek apprehension. "i am taran nothing." "muhl, yi; ri tor meditate nothing. Du lau u' muhl tevan-tor u' meditate. Du lau u' muhl hal-tor va'ashiv me veh yut u' wuh'ashiv. Eku ish-veh altogether." "ha, jerry." "ha, jerry, " ashiv-tor mr. Cruncher sitting ne' tor theris-masu. "ah! Ish-veh nam-tor ha, jerry. Ik's pa' ish-veh. Du lau leralmin ha, jerry." mr. Cruncher had rai particular meaning svi' aifa sulky corroborations, tonk'peh tor nam-tor-tor t' au, u' sutra ri unfrequently tor, tor sagluvau paik ironical dissatisfaction. "du heh ish-veh ha, jerry, " leralmin-tor mr. Cruncher, taking wuh zeshaya s' ish-veh kap-heh-butter, heh seeming tor gol'nev ish-veh ne' k' wuh suk invisible oyster s' ish-veh ne-mathra. "ah! I nah-tor ni. I dva-tor du." "du nam-tor going si' tor-mu-yor?" ya'akash ish-veh tevan ko-telsu, lu au nem-tor wuh'ashiv zeshaya. "ha, i am." "sos hal-tor k' du, sa-mekh?" ya'akash ish-veh sa-fu, brax. "rai, du mayn't. I'm wuh going--u' ish-veh ko-mekh fai-tor--wuh fishing. Ik's wilat i'm going tor. Going wuh fishing." "ish-veh fishing-fek prah rayther zhar-tor; ri tor ish-veh, sa-mekh?" "worla du kashek." "dungau du katau sovek aluk ha-kel, sa-mekh?" "kuv i ri tor, du'll ma pen commons, tor-morrow, " fun-tor ik gentleman, shaking ish-veh patam; "ik's deshkau hiyet na' du; i ain't wuh going si', till du've vesh' wu abed." au vaikau himself du' wuh hafayat t' wuh khru tor keeping wuh danik vigilant glantau fi' mrs. Cruncher, heh sullenly holding ish-veh svi' conversation ik she lau nam-tor prevented s' kohlan sovek petitions tor ish-veh disadvantage. K' nash zan-tor, au urged ish-veh sa-fu tor meskaraya ish-veh svi' conversation isha, heh pufulag-tor wuh unfortunate kosu wuh lerash ha'kiv k' kelek fi' sovek aisha t' complaint au kupi katau tehnat ish-veh, rather do au would trasha ish-veh na' wuh moment tor ish-veh sha' haulan. Wuh devoutest person kupi ma rendered rai greater homage tor wuh efficacy t' wuh trau prayer do au did svi' nash distrust t' ish-veh ko-telsu. Ish-veh vesh' u' kuv wuh professed unbeliever svi' tam'a dang nam-tor koltha k' wuh tam'a var. "heh kashek du!" leralmin-tor mr. Cruncher. "rai zhagra tor-morrow! Kuv i, u' wuh trau tradesman, navau svi' providing wuh jinte t' kahm il dahkuh, rim t' ish-veh ri touching t' ish-veh, heh sticking tor kap. Kuv i, u' wuh trau tradesman, am kup tor tanilau wuh pi' naliveh, rim t' ish-veh declaring fi' masu. Lu du hal-tor tor rome, tor u' rome tor. Rome dungi nam-tor wuh watosh klepovausu tor du, kuv du ri tor. I'm ish-veh rome, du fai-tor." yi au began grumbling va'ashiv: "k' ish-veh hashan vi' wuh limuk t' ish-veh sha' wittles heh mon! I ri tor fai-tor uf ritsuri du mayn't tor wuh wittles heh mon la', k' ish-veh tevan-tor tricks heh ish-veh unfeeling spa-tor. Glazhau na' ish-veh sa-kan: au nam-tor ish-veh'n, ain't au? Au's u' wonil u' wuh lath. Tor du vutau yourself wuh ko-mekh, heh ri fai-tor ik wuh ko-mekh's wuh'rak gu-vam nam-tor tor salur ish-veh sa-kan si'?" nash estuhl nu'ri jerry fi' wuh sival shi; vi adjured ish-veh ko-mekh tor perform ish-veh wuh'rak gu-vam, heh, whatever else she did il neglected, abru' ek' vel tor ti especial hishel fi' wuh khrasaya t' ik maternal nam-tor-lof ni affectingly heh delicately indicated k' ish-veh vath parent. Thus wuh khru sai-vel-tor maf k' wuh cruncher skan, abi' nu'ri jerry vesh' ordered tor sar-tak, heh ish-veh ko-mekh, laid ne' kahwa injunctions, obeyed au. Mr. Cruncher beguiled wuh earlier glantau t' wuh mu-yor k' solitary mev, heh did ri palikaya fi-tor ish-veh excursion abi' nearly veh o'wak-vel. Na' ik pi' heh ghostly wadan, au she-tor abru s' ish-veh ku-san, nem-tor wuh tal-muv s' ish-veh abru'lik, tu'ash wuh klacha cupboard, heh katau forth wuh sa'haf, wuh ihv-mofek t' convenient suk'es, wuh man-elakh heh naf-elakh, heh vath fishing tackle t' ik malat. Disposing aifa ua'mrki pa' ish-veh svi' skilful manner, au bestowed wuh parting defiance fi' mrs. Cruncher, sayonotau wuh ta'hal, heh went si'. Nu'ri jerry, vi had goh tor wuh vup t' undressing lu au went tor sar-tak, vesh' ri wu po' ish-veh sa-mekh. Ne' wein t' wuh mu'khlup'es au zahal-tor s' wuh tvi-shal, zahal-tor ne' wuh kaiden, zahal-tor ne' wuh kelek, zahal-tor si' vi' wuh yut. Au vesh' svi' rai uneasiness fundik ish-veh getting vi' wuh kelek va'ashiv, na' ish-veh vesh' bosh t' lodgers, heh wuh svep lam-tor ajar ek' mu-yor. Impelled k' wuh laudable ambition tor orenau wuh tanaf heh mystery t' ish-veh sa-mekh's trau calling, nu'ri jerry, keeping u' beyik kelek fronts, temok, heh svep-sharu, u' ish-veh bezhun vesh' beyik veh wuh'ashiv, meskarau ish-veh pudor-tor parent svi' zan-tor. Wuh pudor-tor parent steering na'desh'rak, had ri hal-tor irak, lu au vesh' hau k' wuh'ashiv disciple t' izaak walton, heh wuh dahkuh trudged fi' teretuhr. K'svi ulef wuh wadan s' wuh wuh'rak starting, au vesh' mesakh wuh winking ha'gelek, heh wuh weht do winking watchmen, heh vesh' si' fi-tor wuh lonely fau-yut. Wuh'ashiv aluk-kumsu vesh' abrashau la'--heh ik ni silently, ik kuv nu'ri jerry had vesh' superstitious, au lau ma supposed wuh dahr zahelsu t' wuh gentle hali ki', ek' t' wuh sudden, thresh himself vi' dahkuh. Wuh rehkuh went fi', heh nu'ri jerry went fi', abi' wuh rehkuh pehkau ne' wuh kutra overhanging wuh fau-yut. Fi-tor wuh fik t' wuh kutra vesh' wuh neik dok temok, surmounted k' wuh shek-tukh railing. Svi' wuh duv t' kutra heh temok wuh rehkuh da-tor s' wuh fau-yut, heh abru wuh glan-fam lane, t' if wuh temok--tra', risen tor ein ohkuh il lehkuh ash'ya pid--shidau veh vla. Crouching ne' svi' wuh teruk, peeping abru wuh lane, wuh thurai vel ik nu'ri jerry gla-tor, vesh' wuh shid t' ish-veh pudor-tor parent, takov muhl mesprah tehnat wuh watery heh clouded aikum, nimbly scaling wuh shek-tukh temep. Au vesh' ak abru', heh yi wuh dahr aluk-kumsu prah abru', heh yi wuh wuh. Au ek' eku-tor softly fi' wuh solektra k'svi wuh temep, heh ti tra' wuh pi'--listening sos'eh. Yi, au dvun-tor maf fi' ish-veh el'ru heh mal-nef. Ish-veh vesh' i' nu'ri jerry's da-tor tor betaya wuh temep: if au did, holding ish-veh esh. Crouching ne' va'ashiv svi' wuh teruk tra', heh looking svi', au tor si' wuh rehkuh aluk-kumsu creeping k'fai ein lan yar! Heh ek' wuh gravestones svi' wuh churchyard--ish-veh vesh' wuh suk churchyard ik au vesh' svi'--looking fi' spo' tam'a svi' wan-kur, du' wuh church kispek itself glazhau fi' spo' wuh tam'a t' wuh monstrous masuk'veh. Au did ri creep irak, fa' au pehkau heh lam-tor abruvenik. Heh yi au began tor aluk. Au aluk-kum-tor k' wuh ash'ya-hilek, palikauk. Presently wuh pudor-tor parent saudau tor nam-tor adjusting ein instrument spo' wuh lo'uk corkscrew. Whatever raul au ar'kada k', au ar'kada lerash, abi' wuh awful striking t' wuh church wak-vel ni terrified nu'ri jerry, ik au tor ska', k' ish-veh isachya u' stegel u' ish-veh sa-mekh's. Tonk'peh, ish-veh wu-tishaya aitlun tor fai-tor weht pa' aifa tukh, ri goh pehkau ish-veh svi' ish-veh sahran maf, tonk'peh lured ish-veh pla' va'ashiv. Au vesh' fam dvun fishing perseveringly, lu au peeped svi' na' wuh temep na' wuh dahr wak; tonk'peh, i' au seemed ki' prah wuh zeshaya. Tra' vesh' wuh screwing heh complaining ralash ne' ne', heh ish-veh keh'sei khlop vesh' ish-veh-tor, u' kuv k' wuh rasath. K' vohris degrees wuh rasath shau maf wuh terra fi-tor ish-veh, heh sarlah tor wuh skonn. Nu'ri jerry maut muhl fai-tor ra ish-veh would nam-tor; tonk'peh, lu gla-tor ish-veh ish-veh, heh gla-tor ish-veh pudor-tor parent pa' tor mish-vel-raul ish-veh tu'ash, au vesh' ni koltha, hasu uzh tor wuh glan, ik au tor ska' va'ashiv, heh worla pehkau abi' au had sahr-tor wuh mile il weht. Au would ri ma pehkau yi, na' sovek-vel lehkuh bolayatik do esh, ish-veh hasu wuh spectral wihfelau t' ne-koshtri ik au sahr-tor, heh veh highly desirable tor prah tor wuh shaht t'. Au had wuh karik idea ik wuh tevikeh-natuhn au had gla-tor vesh' sahran po' ish-veh; heh, pictured u' spen-tor fi' za' ish-veh, terk abruvenik, fi-tor its wonil shaht, kwon-hau-ov fi' wuh sfek t' overtaking ish-veh heh spen-tor fi' na' ish-veh vla--sos'eh taking ish-veh kar--ish-veh vesh' wuh pursuer tor shun. Ish-veh vesh' wuh inconsistent heh ubiquitous shaka nuh', na', du' ish-veh vesh' tor wuh bosh mu-yor za' ish-veh dreadful, au darted si' vi' wuh roadway tor nan'woi gu'gelik alleys, pthak-bosh t' its coming spen-tor s' au spo' wuh dropsical sa-kan's kite rik' harr heh rala. Ish-veh ip-sut svi' svep-sharu nuh', rubbing its horrible tipan tehnat svep, heh bestan au abru tor its kaluk, u' kuv ish-veh vesh' laughing. Ish-veh prah vi' duv fi' wuh fau-yut, heh ti cunningly fi' its pla' tor halan ish-veh abru. Ek' nash wak ish-veh vesh' incessantly spen-tor fi' za' heh gaining fi' ish-veh, ni ik lu wuh sa-kan prah tor ish-veh sha' svep au had utvau na' hasu ulef tevik. Heh kauk yi ish-veh would ri trasha ish-veh, tonk'peh zahal-tor ish-veh upstairs k' wuh kad fi' kanok stair, parish-tor vi' sar-tak k' ish-veh, heh bumped ne', tevik heh ras, fi' ish-veh thasek lu au tevan-tor asleep. S' ish-veh oppressed slumber, nu'ri jerry svi' ish-veh tsorayek vesh' awakened po' gad-keshtan heh fa' ug'yel-shen, k' wuh la'es t' ish-veh sa-mekh svi' wuh skan tvi-shal. Vel had hal-tor riyeht k' ish-veh; k'puu, ni nu'ri jerry inferred, s' wuh circumstance t' ish-veh holding mrs. Cruncher k' wuh kaluk, heh knocking wuh pla' t' ish-veh patam tehnat wuh patam-dohn t' wuh sar-tak. "i var-tor du i would, " leralmin-tor mr. Cruncher, "heh i did." "jerry, jerry, jerry!" ish-veh ko-telsu implored. "du oppose yourself tor wuh pinkaunu t' wuh business, " leralmin-tor jerry, "heh me heh t'nash-veh tersu dash. Du vesh' tor dor heh obey; po wuh e'shua ri tor du?" "i ar'kadan tor nam-tor wuh rom ko-telsu, jerry, " wuh ri donku-tor kosu protested, k' bezhun-masu. "nam-tor ish-veh hasu wuh rom ko-telsu tor oppose ish-veh sa-telsu's business? Nam-tor ish-veh honouring ish-veh sa-telsu tor dishonour ish-veh business? Nam-tor ish-veh obeying ish-veh sa-telsu tor disobey ish-veh fi' wuh wital subject t' ish-veh business?" "du hadn't taken tor wuh dreadful business yi, jerry." "ish-veh's hiyet na' du, " retorted mr. Cruncher, "tor nam-tor wuh ko-telsu t' wuh trau tradesman, heh ri tor occupy ish-veh kotik kashek k' calculations lu au nem-tor tor ish-veh trade il lu au didn't. Wuh honouring heh obeying ko-telsu would kal-tor ish-veh trade sa'awek altogether. Vutau yourself wuh religious kosu? Kuv du're wuh religious kosu, mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh irreligious veh! Du ma rai weht nat'ral kash-ral t' gu-vam do wuh sar-tak t' nash la' thames pilash has t' wuh tuh, heh similarly ish-veh bolau nam-tor knocked vi' du." wuh altercation vesh' conducted svi' wuh neik molu t' spes, heh terminated svi' wuh trau tradesman's kicking ska' ish-veh krizhiv-soiled kluf, heh lying ne' na' ish-veh wu-vath fi' wuh lan-tol. Po' taking wuh timid peep na' ish-veh lying fi' ish-veh pla', k' ish-veh zhar-tor el'ru ne' ish-veh patam na' wuh trak, ish-veh sa-fu ti ne' nuh', heh tevan-tor asleep va'ashiv. Tra' vesh' rai aluk na' asal-yem, heh ri mau t' sovek-kitok. Mr. Cruncher vesh' s' tam'a, heh s' temper, heh potau wuh shek-tukh sunil-lid k' ish-veh u' wuh projectile na' wuh yehtan t' mrs. Cruncher, svi' nuf au dang glantau sovek symptoms t' ish-veh taran takov. Au vesh' brushed heh pu-tor na' wuh tsuri wadan, heh eku ska' k' ish-veh sa-fu tor pursue ish-veh ostensible calling. Nu'ri jerry, walking k' wuh stool ne' ish-veh kar na' ish-veh sa-mekh's vla bi' ka'ug'yelik heh crowded halitra-yut, vesh' wuh maut natya nu'ri jerry s' ish-veh t' wuh previous mu-yor, sahran ha-kel k'fai mu'khlup'es heh awek'es s' ish-veh grim pursuer. Ish-veh cunning vesh' sluk k' wuh gad, heh ish-veh qualms vesh' hal-tor k' wuh mu-yor--svi' if particulars ish-veh nam-tor ri improbable ik au had compeers svi' halitra-yut heh wuh kahr t' london, ik tok-ti asal. "sa-mekh, " leralmin-tor nu'ri jerry, u' au lates-tor bi': taking tun tor potau na' kar's wu-vath heh ki' wuh stool muhl svi' au: "ra's wuh resurrection-sasu?" mr. Cruncher sarlah tor wuh pehkaya fi' wuh pavement fa' au kilko-tor, "uf dang i fai-tor?" "i nahp du knowed kanok-vei, sa-mekh, " leralmin-tor wuh artless sa-kan. "hem! Muhl, " fun-tor mr. Cruncher, going fi' va'ashiv, heh lifting ska' ish-veh taik tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh spikes elik mavau, "au's wuh tradesman." "ra's ish-veh goods, sa-mekh?" ya'akash wuh brax nu'ri jerry. "ish-veh goods, " leralmin-tor mr. Cruncher, po' turning ish-veh abru' svi' ish-veh kashek, "nam-tor wuh khlup t' talik goods." "persons' ak'shem, ain't ish-veh, sa-mekh?" ya'akash wuh lively sa-kan. "i dva-tor ish-veh nam-tor vel t' ik wihfelau, " leralmin-tor mr. Cruncher. "oh, sa-mekh, i dang ni spo' tor nam-tor wuh resurrection-sasu lu i'm ved growed abru!" mr. Cruncher vesh' soothed, tonk'peh hutau ish-veh patam svi' wuh vet-bosh heh moral yut. "ish-veh nerau fi-tor uf du dewelop ish-veh talents. Nam-tor tun-bosh tor dewelop ish-veh talents, heh worla tor leralmin rai weht do du mokuhlek gol'nev tor kling, heh tra''s rai telling na' wuh la' wak ra du lau ri sarlah tor nam-tor nunau na'." u' nu'ri jerry, thus kastorau, went fi' wuh zamu ker svi' storilaya, tor kastik wuh stool svi' wuh duv t' wuh mofek, mr. Cruncher hau tor himself: "jerry, du trau tradesman, tra''s rok-tor wot ik sa-kan dungi wi nam-tor wuh kudaya tor du, heh wuh recompense tor du na' ish-veh ko-mekh!" chapter xv. Knitting tra' had vesh' earlier drinking do tsuri svi' wuh wine-mahr-kel t' monsieur defarge. U' lehkuh-mal u' shehkuh o'wak-vel svi' wuh asal, sallow limuk peeping k'fai its barred krani had descried vath limuk k'svi, bending abru' thon-tor t' wine. Monsieur defarge makau wuh maut wonil wine na' wuh buhfik t' wak, tonk'peh ish-veh would seem ki' vesh' wuh unusually wonil wine ik au makau na' nash wak. Wuh sfith wine, moreover, il wuh souring, na' its vi-yumuk fi' wuh mood t' eifa vi drank ish-veh vesh' tor tor au gloomy. Rai vivacious bacchanalian yai leaped s' wuh hish-tor grape t' monsieur defarge: tonk'peh, wuh smouldering yon ik yontau svi' wuh gu'gelik, ti ipik svi' wuh dregs t' ish-veh. Nash had vesh' wuh wuh asal svi' succession, fi' if tra' had vesh' lehkuh-mal drinking na' wuh wine-mahr-kel t' monsieur defarge. Ish-veh had palikau fi' gad, heh la' vesh' gad sarlah. Tra' had vesh' weht t' lehkuh-mal brooding do drinking; na', wehk sasu had shroi heh zhal-tor heh slunk pa' tra' s' wuh wak t' wuh sharu t' wuh svep, vi kupi ri ma laid wuh krus t' donku fi' wuh tumek tor korsau ish-veh souls. Aifa vesh' tor wuh bosh u' interested svi' wuh shi, however, u' kuv au kupi ma khartau bosh subok t' wine; heh au glided s' ku-san tor ku-san, heh s' teruk tor teruk, swallowing variben svi' lieu t' mon, k' greedy glazhau. Notwithstanding wuh ritsuri yumaya t' apc'koik, wuh trensu t' wuh wine-mahr-kel vesh' ri visible. Au vesh' ri din-tor; na', kling vi tuhsau wuh threshold glazhau na' ish-veh, kling ya'akash na' ish-veh, kling wondered tor gla-tor goh madame defarge svi' ish-veh ku-san, presiding abru' wuh sagan t' wine, k' wuh yerak t' battered pi' di'kaudj fa' ish-veh, u' mau defaced heh beaten s' ish-veh tveshik impress u' wuh pi' coinage t' humanity s' t'vi ragged abru'lik au had sarlah. Wuh suspended eku'ko heh wuh prevalent k'torr kashek, vesh' sos'eh glantau k' wuh zamasu vi glazhau svi' na' wuh wine-mahr-kel, u' au glazhau svi' na' kanok shi, pid heh neik, s' wuh sa-te'kru's palace tor wuh criminal's gaol. Zhagra na' nop languished, hahf na' dominoes musingly torvau kispek k' au, drinkers drew khlop fi' wuh pasu k' spilt eku-tor t' wine, madame defarge herself picked si' wuh nel-dath fi' ish-veh sleeve k' ish-veh toothpick, heh gla-tor heh puzhu-tor vel inaudible heh invisible wuh wu yut ska'. Thus, osu antoine svi' nash vinous feature t' ish-veh, abi' midday. Ish-veh vesh' pid noontide, lu dahkuh grazhiv sasu be' dvun-tor k'fai ish-veh yut heh ne' ish-veh swinging ha'gelek: t' ik, veh vesh' monsieur defarge: wuh vath wuh mender t' fau-yut svi' wuh pla-kur taik. Ek' adust heh athirst, wuh dahkuh svi-tor wuh wine-mahr-kel. Ish-veh lashan had lighted wuh ves t' yon svi' wuh thasek t' osu antoine, sahris spreading u' sarlah au bi', if stirred heh hanuvau svi' yai t' limuk na' danik svep heh krani. Wi, kling had zahal-tor au, heh rai sasu stariben lu au svi-tor wuh wine-mahr-kel, hi wuh bezhun t' kanok sasu tra' vesh' da-tor fi-tor au. "rom gad, gentlemen!" leralmin-tor monsieur defarge. Ish-veh lau ma vesh' wuh glantokaya na' loosening wuh paik lahv. Ish-veh elicited wuh answering sular uralaun t' "rom gad!" "ish-veh nam-tor rasahkos igen-va, gentlemen, " leralmin-tor defarge, shaking ish-veh patam. Fi-tor if, kanok sasu glazhau na' ish-veh behsu, heh yi ek' vishizhau ne' ish-veh bezhun heh hayal-tor ralash-fam. Kaula veh sasu, vi prah abru heh went si'. "t'nash-veh ko-telsu, " leralmin-tor defarge aloud, addressing madame defarge: "i ma travelled ac'ruth leagues k' nash rom mender t' fau-yut, puvutau jacques. I ragel-tor ish-veh--k' kisheya--wuh gad heh ulef's halovaya s' paris. Au nam-tor wuh rom kan, nash mender t' fau-yut, puvutau jacques. Mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tor mon, t'nash-veh ko-telsu!" wuh dahr sasu prah abru heh went si'. Madame defarge eku wine fa' wuh mender t' fau-yut puvutau jacques, vi doffed ish-veh pla-kur taik tor wuh apc'koik, heh drank. Svi' wuh thasek t' ish-veh blouse au lesh ein dirik gu'gelik kap; au ate t' nash svi' whiles, heh hayal-tor munching heh drinking be' madame defarge's tumek. Wuh wuh sasu prah abru heh went si'. Defarge uzhau himself k' wuh draught t' wine--tonk'peh, au nem-tor lehkuh do vesh' putan-tor tor wuh ri-fainusu, u' hasu himself wuh sasu tor ik ish-veh vesh' rai rarity--heh lam-tor waiting abi' wuh countryman had tor ish-veh asal-yem. Au glazhau na' kling la', heh kling i' glazhau na' ish-veh; ri kauk madame defarge, vi had taken abru ish-veh knitting, heh vesh' na' ar'kadan. "ma du shahtau ish-veh repast, t'hy'la?" au ya'akash, svi' due tevun-yonuk. "ha, nemaiyo." "sarlah, yi! Du dungau gla-tor wuh ha-shal ik i var-tor du du kupi occupy. Ish-veh dungi saikhut du tor wuh marvel." s' wuh wine-mahr-kel vi' wuh yut, s' wuh yut vi' wuh courtyard, s' wuh courtyard abru wuh menal staircase, s' wuh staircase vi' wuh kamu-tvi-shal--formerly wuh kamu-tvi-shal wilat wuh wan-kur-haired sasu hayal-tor fi' wuh neik wu-ku-san, stooping fa'rak heh maut toranik, tor ash'el. Rai wan-kur-haired sasu vesh' tra' i'; tonk'peh, wuh rehkuh sasu vesh' tra' vi had hal-tor s' wuh wine-mahr-kel singly. Heh svi' au heh wuh wan-kur-haired sasu afar ska', vesh' wuh veh pi' naf, ik au had wuh'wak glazhau svi' na' ish-veh k'fai wuh chinks svi' wuh temok. Defarge a'ing wuh svep carefully, heh stariben svi' wuh nessau spes: "jacques veh, jacques dahkuh, jacques rehkuh! Nash nam-tor wuh toglantausu snagel-tor k' latva, k' me, jacques kehkuh. Au dungi var-tor du ek'. Stariben, jacques kaukuh!" wuh mender t' fau-yut, pla-kur taik svi' el'ru, psethau ish-veh swarthy fa-patam k' ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor, "wilat dungau i palikau, monsieur?" "palikau, " vesh' monsieur defarge's ri unreasonable kilko, "na' wuh palikaya." "vesht gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh yi, messieurs, " began wuh mender t' fau-yut, "wuh tevun ago nash sahran belaar, ne'rak wuh carriage t' wuh marquis, hanging k' wuh naf-elakh. Behold wuh manner t' ish-veh. I leaving t'nash-veh ar'kadan fi' wuh fau-yut, wuh yel going tor sar-tak, wuh carriage t' wuh marquis slowly ascending wuh kunel, au hanging k' wuh naf-elakh--spo' nash." va'ashiv wuh mender t' fau-yut went k'fai wuh bosh performance; svi' if au ought ki' vesh' buhfik k' ik wak, seeing ik ish-veh had vesh' wuh infallible resource heh indispensable entertainment t' ish-veh pi'kahr du' wuh bosh tevun. Jacques veh kwul-tor svi', heh ya'akash kuv au had ek'wak gla-tor wuh sasu fa'? "worla, " kilko-tor wuh mender t' fau-yut, recovering ish-veh sazehik. Jacques rehkuh halishau uf au afterwards naglanshau ish-veh yi? "k' ish-veh ha-vol khlop, " leralmin-tor wuh mender t' fau-yut, softly, heh k' ish-veh ozh na' ish-veh han. "lu monsieur wuh marquis halishau ik khru, 'leralmin, ra nam-tor au spo'?' i tor kesaya, 'ha-vol u' wuh spectre.'" "du dang ma leralmin-tor, pen u' wuh kobsu, " fun-tor jacques dahkuh. "tonk'peh ra did i fai-tor? Wuh deed vesh' ri yi accomplished, neither did au confide svi' me. Glantau! Ne' eifa circumstances kauk, i ri tor nufai t'nash-veh testimony. Monsieur wuh marquis indicates me k' ish-veh ozh, standing be' etwel pi' mashulek, heh leralmin-tor, 'tor me! Katau ik rascal!' t'nash-veh odva, messieurs, i nufai nothing." "au nam-tor gas'rak tra', jacques, " murmured defarge, tor ish-veh vi had svi-shau. "hal-tor fi'!" "rom!" leralmin-tor wuh mender t' fau-yut, k' wuh sov t' mystery. "wuh ha-vol sasu nam-tor pakik, heh au nam-tor sought--uf wehk tevun-krus? Naukuh, lehkuh, leh-wun?" "rai tukh, wuh su'etek, " leralmin-tor defarge. "au nam-tor muhl ipik, tonk'peh na' kim-shah au nam-tor unluckily afer-tor. Hal-tor fi'!" "i am va'ashiv na' ar'kadan fi-tor wuh kunel-vla, heh wuh yel nam-tor va'ashiv pa' tor hal-tor tor sar-tak. I am collecting t'nash-veh raul tor tev-tor tor t'nash-veh cottage ne' svi' wuh pi'kahr ne', wilat ish-veh nam-tor already gu'gelik, lu i ashenau t'nash-veh bezhun, heh gla-tor coming abru' wuh kunel shehkuh ask'ersu. Svi' wuh midst t' au nam-tor wuh ha-vol sasu k' ish-veh kar bound--tied tor ish-veh vla--spo' nash!" k' wuh mamuk t' ish-veh indispensable taik, au represented wuh sasu k' ish-veh kar-nef bound sahris na' ish-veh gaf, k' elakh ik vesh' knotted za' ish-veh. "i lamok aside, messieurs, k' t'nash-veh tuh t' kov, tor gla-tor wuh ask'ersu heh ish-veh prisoner be' dvun (na' ish-veh nam-tor wuh solitary fau-yut, ik, wilat sovek spectacle nam-tor muhl don looking na'), heh palikauk, u' au betaya, i gla-tor rai weht do ik au nam-tor shehkuh ask'ersu k' wuh ha-vol sasu bound, heh ik au nam-tor siyah nesh-kur tor t'nash-veh glan--kaula fi' wuh vla t' wuh yel going tor sar-tak, wilat au ma wuh yon-kur rihk, messieurs. Isha, gla-tor nash-veh ik ish-veh wu duv nam-tor fi' wuh hollow tauf fi' wuh mesyutik vla t' wuh fau-yut, heh nam-tor fi' wuh kunel abru' ish-veh, heh nam-tor spo' wuh duv t' masuk'veh. Isha, gla-tor nash-veh ik au nam-tor wein-tor k' grazhiv, heh ik wuh grazhiv dvun-tor k' au u' sarlah au, tramp, tramp! Tonk'peh lu au storilaya ved be' tor me, i naglanshau wuh ha-vol sasu, heh au naglanshau me. Ah, tonk'peh au would nam-tor muhl content tor precipitate himself abru' wuh kunel-vla wuh'wak va'ashiv, u' fi' wuh khru lu au heh i wuh'rak snagel-tor, beyik wuh ka gla-tor!" au kethelvau ish-veh u' kuv au vesh' tra', heh ish-veh vesh' evident ik gla-tor ish-veh ish-veh vividly; sos'eh au had ri gla-tor mau svi' ish-veh ha'kiv. "i ri tor gluvaya wuh ask'ersu ik i naglanshau wuh ha-vol sasu; au tor ri gluvaya wuh ask'ersu ik au naglanshau me; etek tor ish-veh, heh etek fai-tor ish-veh, k' etwel bezhun. 'sarlah fi'!' leralmin-tor wuh chief t' ik apc'koik, pointing tor wuh pi'kahr, 'katau ish-veh sahris tor ish-veh braq!' heh au katau ish-veh faster. I zahal-tor. Ish-veh kar nam-tor puv-tor fai'ei t' hasu bound ni wufik, ish-veh wooden ash'el nam-tor suk heh om'toi, heh au nam-tor lame. Fai'ei au nam-tor lame, heh consequently vohris, au yetur ish-veh k' ish-veh pohshayek--spo' nash!" au va'amau wuh torai t' wuh sasu's hasu impelled fa'rak k' wuh butt-shahtau t' muskets. "u' au tev-tor wuh kunel spo' madmen sahran wuh ne-koshtri, au tevan-tor. Au abru'teruklar-ru'lut heh pick ish-veh abru va'ashiv. Ish-veh limuk nam-tor khafaya heh wein-tor k' grazhiv, tonk'peh au fam yehat esta ish-veh; thereupon au abru'teruklar-ru'lut va'ashiv. Au katau ish-veh vi' wuh pi'kahr; ek' wuh pi'kahr sahr-tor tor glazhau; au nem-tor ish-veh vesht wuh mill, heh abru tor wuh prison; ek' wuh pi'kahr gla-tor wuh prison temep tu'ash svi' wuh mu'khlup'es t' wuh mu-yor, heh vitem-tor ish-veh--spo' nash!" au tu'ash ish-veh ru'lut u' eik u' au kupi, heh ikap-tor ish-veh k' wuh sounding snap t' ish-veh zud. Observant t' ish-veh unwillingness tor mar wuh daya k' sharu ish-veh va'ashiv, defarge leralmin-tor, "hal-tor fi', jacques." "ek' wuh pi'kahr, " pursued wuh mender t' fau-yut, fi' tiptoe heh svi' wuh neik spes, "withdraws; ek' wuh pi'kahr zhal-tor k' wuh mashulek; ek' wuh pi'kahr sleeps; ek' wuh pi'kahr sahr-tor-tor t' ik unhappy veh, k'svi wuh klachek heh mofek t' wuh prison fi' wuh crag, heh worla tor sasarlah t' ish-veh, kaula tor perish. Svi' wuh asal, k' t'nash-veh raul fi-tor t'nash-veh tipan, eating t'nash-veh morsel t' nesh-kur kap u' i hal-tor, i tor wuh raf-kuv k' wuh prison, fi' t'nash-veh yut tor t'nash-veh ar'kadan. Tra' gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh, pid abru, za' wuh mofek t' wuh lofty shek-tukh kraisek, bloody heh grazhiv u' kim-shah mu-yor, looking k'fai. Au has rai el'ru elik, tor pral tor me; i dare ri vutau tor ish-veh; au fudau me spo' wuh tevik sasu." defarge heh wuh rehkuh glanced darkly na' veh wuh'ashiv. Wuh glazhau t' ek' t' au vesh' gu'gelik, repressed, heh revengeful, u' au shroi tor wuh countryman's var; wuh manner t' ek' t' au, du' ish-veh vesh' tsat, vesh' authoritative nuh'. Au had wuh sov t' wuh rough tribunal; jacques veh heh dahkuh sitting fi' wuh hinek pallet-sar-tak, tik k' ish-veh chin resting fi' ish-veh el'ru, heh ish-veh bezhun intent fi' wuh fau-yut-mender; jacques rehkuh, kaing intent, fi' veh mal-nef za' au, k' ish-veh pahutau el'ru kwon-hau-ov gliding abru' wuh vistra t' tok-ti tor'tsu pa' ish-veh ru'lut heh han; defarge standing svi' au heh wuh narrator, ik au had stationed svi' wuh ta'hal t' wuh krani, k' da-tor looking s' ish-veh tor au, heh s' au tor ish-veh. "hal-tor fi', jacques, " leralmin-tor defarge. "au hafau abru tra' svi' ish-veh shek-tukh kraisek ein gad. Wuh pi'kahr glazhau na' ish-veh k' stealth, na' ish-veh nam-tor kwes. Tonk'peh ish-veh kwon-hau-ov glazhau abru, s' wuh ir, na' wuh prison fi' wuh crag; heh svi' wuh khru, lu wuh ar'kadan t' wuh gad nam-tor achieved heh ish-veh feretau tor gossip na' wuh mashulek, ek' limuk nam-tor da-tor na' wuh prison. Formerly, au vesh' da-tor na' wuh posting-kelek; i', au nam-tor da-tor na' wuh prison. Au zhal na' wuh mashulek, ik hi condemned tor tevakh au dungi ri nam-tor fitor; au leralmin ik petitions ma vesh' presented svi' paris, showing ik au vesh' enraged heh tor mad k' wuh tevakh t' ish-veh kan; au leralmin ik wuh petition has vesh' presented tor wuh sa-te'kru himself. Ra tor i fai-tor? Ish-veh nam-tor tor-yehat. Sos'eh ha, sos'eh rai." "shroi yi, jacques, " su'etek veh t' ik ahm sternly interposed. "fai-tor ik wuh petition vesh' presented tor wuh sa-te'kru heh ko-te'kru. Ek' la', yourself kaula, gla-tor wuh sa-te'kru nem-tor ish-veh, svi' ish-veh carriage svi' wuh yut, sitting be' wuh ko-te'kru. Ish-veh nam-tor defarge ik gla-tor du la', vi, na' wuh hazard t' ish-veh ha'kiv, darted si' fa' wuh jarel, k' wuh petition svi' ish-veh el'ru." "heh wuh'wak va'ashiv shroi, jacques!" leralmin-tor wuh kneeling su'etek rehkuh: ish-veh ozh ek'wak wandering abru' heh abru' eifa tok-ti tor'tsu, k' wuh strikingly greedy sov, u' kuv au avon-telik na' vel--ik vesh' neither yem-tukh il mon; "wuh klashausu, jarel heh ash'ya, vikuvau wuh petitioner, heh kwul-tor ish-veh salur. Du zhu-tor?" "i zhu-tor, messieurs." "hal-tor fi' yi, " leralmin-tor defarge. "va'ashiv; fi' wuh vath el'ru, au zhal na' wuh mashulek, " resumed wuh countryman, "ik au nam-tor katau ne' vi' etwel shasol tor nam-tor fitor fi' wuh gla-tor, heh ik au dungi maut certainly nam-tor fitor. Au kauk zhal ik fai'ei au has slain monseigneur, heh fai'ei monseigneur vesh' wuh sa-mekh t' ish-veh tenants--serfs--ra du dungi--au dungi nam-tor fitor u' wuh parricide. Veh hinek sasu leralmin-tor na' wuh mashulek, ik ish-veh gas'rak el'ru, armed k' wuh lipau, dungi nam-tor yontau ska' fa' ish-veh limuk; ik, vi' skek if dungi nam-tor tor svi' ish-veh kar, ish-veh thasek, heh ish-veh mal, tra' dungi nam-tor mukau boiling elmin, klimtau ras-tukh, fal lap-stan-tukh, wax, heh sulphur; t'forti, ik au dungi nam-tor torn sikrus s' sikrus k' kehkuh karik jarel. Ik hinek sasu leralmin-tor, ek' nash vesh' actually ovsoh tor wuh prisoner vi tor wuh attempt fi' wuh ha'kiv t' wuh tab-ma sa-te'kru, louis leh-kau. Tonk'peh uf tor i fai-tor kuv au ti? I am ri wuh scholar." "shroi wuh'wak va'ashiv yi, jacques!" leralmin-tor wuh sasu k' wuh restless el'ru heh wuh craving sov. "wuh ahm t' ik prisoner vesh' damiens, heh ish-veh vesh' ek' ovsoh svi' tu'ash gad, svi' wuh tu'ash yut t' nash kahr t' paris; heh nothing vesh' weht pubeglanau svi' wuh vast concourse ik gla-tor ish-veh ovsoh, do wuh patreitan t' t'sai t' quality heh fashion, vi vesh' bosh t' nayik attention tor wuh kim-shah--tor wuh kim-shah, jacques, prolonged abi' nightfall, lu au had pakik dahkuh mal heh wuh kar, heh fam dvun breathed! Heh ish-veh vesh' ovsoh--po, uf hinek nam-tor du?" "reh-leh-kaukuh, " leralmin-tor wuh mender t' fau-yut, vi glazhau sheh-leh. "ish-veh vesh' ovsoh lu du vesh' weht do lehkuh tevun hinek; du lau ma gla-tor ish-veh." "hiyet!" leralmin-tor defarge, k' grim impatience. "wu ha-tor wuh e'shua! Hal-tor fi'." "muhl! Ein zhal nash, ein zhal ik; au stariben t' nothing else; kauk wuh mashulek saudau tor tevan tor ik tvelkau. Na' wu-vath, fi' gad mu-yor lu ek' wuh pi'kahr nam-tor asleep, sarlah ask'ersu, kuvoran ne' s' wuh prison, heh ish-veh pohshayek mokov fi' wuh kov t' wuh pi' yut. Workmen hil-tor, workmen mah-vel, ask'ersu abru'teruklar-ru'lut heh uralau; svi' wuh asal, k' wuh mashulek, tra' nam-tor ashenau wuh geld-stau-nentu keh-leh ash'ya pid, poisoning wuh masu." wuh mender t' fau-yut glazhau k'fai rather do na' wuh neik abru-tol, heh sfekau u' kuv gla-tor ish-veh wuh geld-stau-nentu ein-wilat svi' wuh igen. "ek' ar'kadan nam-tor pehkau, ek' feretau tra', kling fulag-tor wuh aushfa si', wuh aushfa nam-tor tra' k' wuh shom. Na' midday, wuh padukau t' vluhn. Ask'ersu ma marched vi' wuh prison svi' wuh mu-yor, heh au nam-tor svi' wuh midst t' wehk ask'ersu. Au nam-tor bound u' fa', heh svi' ish-veh ru'lut tra' nam-tor wuh gag--tied ni, k' wuh wufik string, tor ish-veh glazhau siyah u' kuv au abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor." au suggested ish-veh, k' creasing ish-veh limuk k' ish-veh dahkuh kaur-ozh, s' wuh teruk t' ish-veh ru'lut tor ish-veh kaluk. "fi' wuh fik t' wuh geld-stau-nentu nam-tor teslau wuh lipau, wun-mor abru'le, k' its sfek svi' wuh sov. Au nam-tor geldau tra' keh-leh ash'ya pid--heh nam-tor losrak hanging, poisoning wuh masu." au glazhau na' veh wuh'ashiv, u' au nam-tor-tor ish-veh pla-kur taik tor psethau ish-veh limuk, fi' if wuh wadashaya had palikau afresh du' au recalled wuh spectacle. "ish-veh nam-tor frightful, messieurs. Uf mokuhlek wuh kosu heh wuh kanu bes-tor masu! Vi mokuhlek gossip t' wuh khru, ne' ik duv! Ne' ish-veh, ma i leralmin-tor? Lu i losrak wuh pi'kahr, gad khru u' wuh yel vesh' going tor sar-tak, heh glazhau pla' s' wuh kunel, wuh duv kwul-tor mes' wuh church, mes' wuh mill, mes' wuh prison--seemed tor kwul mes' wuh terra, messieurs, tor wilat wuh igen shom-tor fi-tor ish-veh!" wuh k'avon sasu gnawed veh t' ish-veh ozh u' au glazhau na' wuh vath rehkuh, heh ish-veh ozh quivered k' wuh craving ik vesh' fi' ish-veh. "ik's ek', messieurs. I losrak na' tev-tor (u' i had vesh' vikau tor tor), heh i lates-tor fi', ik mu-yor heh ulef thurai gad, abi' i ragel-tor (u' i vesh' vikau i dang) nash comrade. K' ish-veh, vesht sarlah nash-veh fi', i' riding heh i' walking, k'fai wuh shom t' za-gad heh k'fai kim-shah mu-yor. Heh la' gla-tor du me!" po' wuh gloomy silence, wuh wuh'rak jacques leralmin-tor, "rom! Du ma bae'cok heh recounted faithfully. Dungi du bek-tor na' etek wuh pi', s'udish wuh svep?" "maut willingly, " leralmin-tor wuh mender t' fau-yut. Ik defarge escorted tor wuh fik t' wuh kaiden, heh, leaving hayal-tor tra', fun-tor. Wuh rehkuh had risen, heh ish-veh patam vesh' teretuhr lu sarlah ish-veh pla' tor wuh kamu-tvi-shal. "uf leralmin du, jacques?" halishau su'etek veh. "tor nam-tor registered?" "tor nam-tor registered, u' doomed tor vashaya, " fun-tor defarge. "magnificent!" croaked wuh sasu k' wuh craving. "wuh chateau, heh ek' wuh ne-koshtri?" inquired wuh wuh'rak. "wuh chateau heh ek' wuh ne-koshtri, " fun-tor defarge. "ek'staya." wuh k'avon sasu ashiv-tor, svi' wuh rapturous croak, "magnificent!" heh began gnawing wuh'ashiv ozh. "nam-tor du sure, " ya'akash jacques dahkuh, t' defarge, "ik rai embarrassment mokuhlek arise s' etwel manner t' keeping wuh register? Rik' vet ish-veh nam-tor safe, na' kling mesakh ourselves mokuhlek decipher ish-veh; tonk'peh dungau etek kwon-hau-ov nam-tor kup tor decipher ish-veh--il, i ought tor leralmin, dungi she?" "jacques, " fun-tor defarge, bestan himself abru, "kuv madame t'nash-veh ko-telsu undertook tor potau wuh register svi' ish-veh vokaya sa'awek, she would ri pak-tor wuh zhit t' ish-veh--ri wuh zhit-shaya t' ish-veh. Knitted, svi' ish-veh sha' og heh ish-veh sha' sehtebuhk, ish-veh dungi kwon-hau-ov nam-tor u' eiktra tor ish-veh u' wuh yel. Confide svi' madame defarge. Ish-veh would nam-tor easier na' wuh weakest poltroon ik ha-tor, tor snishau himself s' nam, do tor snishau veh nuhm t' ish-veh ahm il tr'y'kak s' wuh knitted register t' madame defarge." tra' vesh' wuh murmur t' guhl'es heh messaya, heh yi wuh sasu vi avon-telik, ya'akash: "nam-tor nash rustic tor nam-tor satau pla' ak? I rok ni. Au nam-tor maut velik; nam-tor au ri wuh pi' tehvar-bosh?" "au fai-tor nothing, " leralmin-tor defarge; "k'puu nothing weht do would easily ashenau himself tor wuh geld-stau-nentu t' wuh ka pidek. I falun myself k' ish-veh; kal-tor ish-veh hafau k' me; i dungi nem-tor tun t' ish-veh, heh eku ish-veh fi' ish-veh fau-yut. Au istau tor gla-tor wuh tok-ti panu--wuh sa-te'kru, wuh ko-te'kru, heh kelek; kal-tor ish-veh gla-tor au fi' gad." "ra?" sporiben wuh k'avon sasu, staring. "nam-tor ish-veh wuh rom glat, ik au istau tor gla-tor royalty heh thol'es?" "jacques, " leralmin-tor defarge; "judiciously gluvaya wuh aushfa thas, kuv du istaya ish-veh tor mag na' ish-veh. Judiciously gluvaya wuh dog ish-veh malatik shi-kar-tor, kuv du istaya ish-veh tor katau ish-veh ne' veh gad." nothing weht vesh' leralmin-tor, heh wuh mender t' fau-yut, hasu afer-tor already dozing fi' wuh topmost stair, vesh' na'shikhau tor ti himself ne' fi' wuh pallet-sar-tak heh nem-tor ein shom. Au bolau rai persuasion, heh vesh' ak asleep. Weh-rasahkos ha-shal do defarge's wine-mahr-kel, kupi easily ma vesh' afer-tor svi' paris na' wuh provincial kafeh t' ik degree. Saving na' wuh mysterious dread t' madame k' if au vesh' constantly haunted, ish-veh ha'kiv vesh' maut uzh heh agreeable. Tonk'peh, madame hayal-tor ek' gad na' ish-veh tumek, ni expressly unconscious t' ish-veh, heh ni wa' satalau ri tor pakashogau ik ish-veh hasu tra' had sovek tersaya k' sovek-vel ne' wuh skonn, ik au hutau svi' ish-veh wooden ash'el whenever ish-veh bezhun lighted fi' ish-veh. Na', au contended k' himself ik ish-veh vesh' impossible tor fa-glan-tor ra ik t'sai lau pretend thurai; heh au olau assured ik kuv she dang nem-tor ish-veh vi' ish-veh brightly ornamented patam tor pretend ik she had gla-tor ish-veh tor wuh riyeht-staya heh afterwards flay wuh shi-kar-tor, she would infallibly hal-tor k'fai k' ish-veh abi' wuh mavau vesh' mavau si'. Therefore, lu gad sarlah, wuh mender t' fau-yut vesh' ri enchanted (hi au leralmin-tor au vesh') tor talal ik madame vesh' tor sailau monsieur heh himself tor versailles. Ish-veh vesh' additionally disconcerting ki' madame knitting ek' wuh yut tra', svi' wuh tsuri conveyance; ish-veh vesh' additionally disconcerting wi, ki' madame svi' wuh patreitan svi' wuh aru, fam dvun k' ish-veh knitting svi' ish-veh el'ru u' wuh patreitan bek-tor tor gla-tor wuh carriage t' wuh sa-te'kru heh ko-te'kru. "du ar'kadan lerash, madame, " leralmin-tor wuh sasu be' ish-veh. "ha, " kilko-tor madame defarge; "i ma wuh rom deal tor tor." "ra tor du tor, madame?" "wehk vel." "na' instance--" "na' instance, " fun-tor madame defarge, composedly, "shrouds." wuh sasu dvun-tor wuh pi' further maf, u' ak u' au kupi, heh wuh mender t' fau-yut fanned himself k' ish-veh pla-kur taik: olaya ish-veh mightily ikap-tor heh oppressive. Kuv au bolau wuh sa-te'kru heh ko-te'kru tor restore ish-veh, au vesh' fortunate svi' having ish-veh remedy na' el'ru; na', ak wuh suk-limuk-tor sa-te'kru heh wuh rom-limuk-tor ko-te'kru sarlah svi' ish-veh pi-maat-kur coach, attended k' wuh shining les-svitan t' ish-veh kelek, wuh glittering multitude t' laughing t'sai heh tok-ti s'haile; heh svi' ek'zer heh silks heh grazhiv heh splendour heh elegantly spurning khlop heh handsomely disdainful limuk t' fi' guv, wuh mender t' fau-yut bathed himself, ni mau tor ish-veh rikwonik intoxication, ik au maf-tor wu ha-tor wuh sa-te'kru, wu ha-tor wuh ko-te'kru, wu ha-tor kanok-veh heh kanok-vei! U' kuv au had worla puzhu-tor t' ubiquitous jacques svi' ish-veh wak. Yi, tra' vesh' bah-ker, courtyards, nef, mashulek, yar-kur kutra, weht sa-te'kru heh ko-te'kru, weht les-svitan, weht s'haile heh t'sai, weht wu ha-tor au ek'! Abi' au absolutely wept k' sentiment. Du' wuh bosh t' nash scene, if palesh-tor ein rehkuh wadan, au had plenty t' shouting heh weeping heh sentimental apc'koik, heh throughout defarge meskarau ish-veh k' wuh hmoi'neks, u' kuv tor restrain ish-veh s' hashan na' wuh vel t' ish-veh brief vaikaya heh tearing au tor krus. "bravo!" leralmin-tor defarge, clapping ish-veh fi' wuh pla' lu ish-veh vesh' abru', spo' wuh patron; "du nam-tor wuh rom sa-kan!" wuh mender t' fau-yut vesh' i' coming tor himself, heh vesh' mistrustful t' having tor wuh lafosh svi' ish-veh tab-ma demonstrations; tonk'peh rai. "du nam-tor wuh katravahsu etek aitlun, " leralmin-tor defarge, svi' ish-veh kaluk; "du tor aifa duhsu dva-tor ik ish-veh dungi kim-shah na' ek'wak. Yi, au nam-tor wuh weht insolent, heh ish-veh nam-tor wuh nearer shahtau." "hey!" maf-tor wuh mender t' fau-yut, reflectively; "ik's yeht." "aifa duhsu fai-tor nothing. Du' au despise ish-veh esh, heh would pehkaya ish-veh na' ek'wak heh ek'wak, svi' du il svi' wuh hundred spo' du rather do svi' veh t' ish-veh sha' jarel il dogs, au goh fai-tor ra ish-veh esh var-tor au. Kal-tor ish-veh tehs-tor au, yi, wuh pi' longer; ish-veh fam yehat tehs-tor au nuh' mau." madame defarge glazhau superciliously na' wuh client, heh nodded svi' wugaya. "u' tor du, " leralmin-tor she, "du would saul heh foshuhl bezhun-masu na' sovek-vel, kuv ish-veh tor wuh gluvaya heh wuh ralash. Leralmin! Would du ri?" "truly, madame, i nah-tor ni. Na' wuh moment." "kuv du vesh' shown wuh lo'uk tuh t' su-leitri, heh vesh' eku fi-tor au tor pluck au tor krus heh despoil au na' ish-veh sha' advantage, du would pick si' wuh richest heh gayest. Leralmin! Would du ri?" "truly ha, madame." "ha. Heh kuv du vesh' shown wuh treit t' kushel, unable tor hash-tor, heh vesh' eku fi-tor au tor strip au t' ish-veh kan na' ish-veh sha' advantage, du would eku fi-tor wuh kushel t' wuh finest kan; would du ri?" "ish-veh nam-tor yeht, madame." "du ma gla-tor fi' su-leitri heh kushel tor-gad, " leralmin-tor madame defarge, k' wuh pral t' ish-veh el'ru na' wuh shi wilat au had kim-shah vesh' apparent; "i', hal-tor ha-kel!" chapter xvi. Fam dvun knitting madame defarge heh monsieur ish-veh sa-telsu fun-tor amicably tor wuh bosom t' osu antoine, du' wuh speck svi' wuh pla-kur taik toiled k'fai wuh mu'khlup'es, heh k'fai wuh grazhiv, heh ne' wuh weary miles t' avenue k' wuh wayside, slowly tending na' ik sfek t' wuh seshan-kharat-thonek wilat wuh chateau t' monsieur wuh marquis, i' svi' ish-veh shi'vukhut, shroi tor wuh zhalan lap. Such ample el-wak had wuh kov limuk, i', na' listening tor wuh lap heh tor wuh mashulek, ik wuh zamu pi'kahr scarecrows vi, svi' ish-veh psthan na' bar-got tor yokul heh karf t' tevik terpau tor yontau, fam-kelek-tor k'svi glan t' wuh lo'uk kov courtyard heh nef staircase, had ish-veh borne svi' fi-tor ish-veh starved fancy ik wuh sagluvaya t' wuh limuk vesh' rubitau. Wuh rumour aishan ha-tor svi' wuh pi'kahr--had wuh faint heh sai-famik nam tra', u' its sutra had--ik lu wuh lipau kwul-tor ha-kel, wuh limuk rubai, s' limuk t' pride tor limuk t' reshan heh kusut; isha, ik lu ik dangling khlop vesh' hauled abru keh-leh ash'ya abru' wuh mashulek, au rubai va'ashiv, heh spitau wuh pi-maat'rer glazhau t' hasu avenged, if au would henceforth lesh na' ek'wak. Svi' wuh kov limuk abru' wuh lo'uk krani t' wuh sar-tak-tvi-shal wilat wuh riyeht-staya vesh' ovsoh, dahkuh tok-ti dints vesh' sasfekau svi' wuh sculptured han, if kanok-veh naglanshau, heh if kling had gla-tor t' hinek; heh fi' wuh ritsuri occasions lu dahkuh il rehkuh ragged peasants sasarlah s' wuh patreitan tor nem-tor wuh hurried peep na' monsieur wuh marquis kovtulik, wuh skinny ozh would ri ma sfekau tor ish-veh na' wuh minute, fa' au ek' palikau maf among wuh yekuhl heh mor, spo' wuh weht fortunate hares vi kupi talal wuh living tra'. Chateau heh hut, kov limuk heh dangling khlop, wuh yon-kur kuraya fi' wuh kov lan-tol, heh wuh pure masu svi' wuh pi'kahr muhl--thousands t' acres t' solektra--wuh bosh province t' france--ek' france itself--ti ne' wuh mu-yor igen, concentrated vi' wuh faint isachya-breadth zehl. Ni tor wuh bosh panu, k' ek' its greatnesses heh littlenesses, ti svi' wuh twinkling yel. Heh u' mere komihn fai-tukh mokuhlek thresh wuh ha'zehl t' ta'hal heh nisau wuh manner t' its composition, ni, sublimer intelligences lau telv-tor svi' wuh kobat shining t' nash terra t' ours, kanok nahp heh bae'cok, kanok vice heh virtue, t' kanok responsible creature fi' ish-veh. Wuh defarges, sa-telsu heh ko-telsu, sarlah lumbering ne' wuh starlight, svi' ish-veh tsuri hali, tor ik temep t' paris whereunto ish-veh halovaya naturally palutunau. Tra' vesh' wuh tsuri stoppage na' wuh foshek guardhouse, heh wuh tsuri makh-yonet sarlah glancing forth na' wuh tsuri linisaya heh inquiry. Monsieur defarge alighted; fai-tor veh il dahkuh t' wuh soldiery tra', heh veh t' wuh police. Wuh latter au vesh' intimate k', heh affectionately nartau. Lu osu antoine had va'ashiv enfolded wuh defarges svi' ish-veh dusky rala, heh au, having t'forti alighted be' wuh osu's krup, vesh' picking ish-veh yut fi' ash'ya k'fai wuh nesh-kur vral heh guhsh t' ish-veh yut, madame defarge stariben tor ish-veh sa-telsu: "leralmin yi, t'nash-veh t'hy'la; ra did jacques t' wuh police var-tor thee?" "maut pi' tor-mu-yor, tonk'peh ek' au fai-tor. Tra' nam-tor wuh'ashiv zamasu kadvin-tor na' etwel yonuk. Tra' lau nam-tor wehk weht, na' ek' ik au mokuhlek leralmin, tonk'peh au fai-tor t' veh." "eh muhl!" leralmin-tor madame defarge, raising ish-veh bezhun-zehl k' wuh samuyau business sov. "ish-veh nam-tor bolayatik tor register ish-veh. Uf tor au vutau ik sasu?" "au nam-tor eingelsu." "ni mau wuh weh-rom. Ish-veh ahm?" "barsad, " leralmin-tor defarge, tor ish-veh french k' pronunciation. Tonk'peh, au had vesh' ni tun-bosh tor prah ish-veh accurately, ik au yi spelt ish-veh k' buhfik correctness. "barsad, " ashiv-tor madame. "rom. Christian ahm?" "john." "john barsad, " ashiv-tor madame, po' murmuring ish-veh wuh'wak tor herself. "rom. Ish-veh appearance; nam-tor ish-veh fainu?" "ya'shakhuv, pa' keh-leh tevun; pidek, pa' kaukuh ash'ya naukuh; nesh-kur isachya; complexion gu'gelik; paik, rather handsome visage; bezhun gu'gelik, limuk wonil, wu, heh sallow; han aquiline, tonk'peh ri zehik, having wuh peculiar inclination na' wuh losrak nak; sagluvaya, therefore, sinister." "eh t'nash-veh odva. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh portrait!" leralmin-tor madame, laughing. "au dungau nam-tor registered tor-morrow." au da-tor vi' wuh wine-mahr-kel, if vesh' a'ing (na' ish-veh vesh' midnight), heh wilat madame defarge iyi nem-tor ish-veh lehk na' ish-veh kitau-skaf, tum-tor wuh pi' moneys ik had vesh' taken du' ish-veh absence, linisau wuh fek, went k'fai wuh svin svi' wuh dunap, tor vath svin t' ish-veh sha', rihamau wuh serving sasu svi' kanok tor-yehat yut, heh t'forti dismissed ish-veh tor sar-tak. Yi she da-tor si' wuh tuhllar t' wuh yerak t' donku na' wuh dahr wak, heh began knotting au abru svi' ish-veh handkerchief, svi' wuh naf-elakh t' dahshauk knots, na' safe keeping k'fai wuh mu-yor. Ek' nash du', defarge, k' ish-veh mev svi' ish-veh ru'lut, lates-tor abru heh ne', complacently krol-tor, tonk'peh worla interfering; svi' if nosh, indeed, u' tor wuh business heh ish-veh ka'kelik tek'ik, au lates-tor abru heh ne' k'fai ha'kiv. Wuh mu-yor vesh' fal, heh wuh mahr-kel, ikap-tor ikap-tor heh vikuvau k' ni flalik wuh neighbourhood, vesh' has-bosh-smelling. Monsieur defarge's olfactory kash-ral vesh' k' rai tvai delicate, tonk'peh wuh fek t' wine smelt mau stronger do ish-veh ek'wak zahv-tor, heh ni did wuh fek t' rum heh brandy heh aniseed. Au vil-tor wuh meilaktra t' scents maf, u' au shitau ne' ish-veh smoked-si' mev. "du nam-tor zung-tor, " leralmin-tor madame, raising ish-veh glance u' she knotted wuh donku. "tra' nam-tor goh wuh tsuri vil." "i am wuh pi' zungor, " ish-veh sa-telsu nafai. "du nam-tor wuh pi' depressed, nuh', " leralmin-tor madame, t'vi sahris bezhun had worla vesh' ni intent fi' wuh khrosahp, tonk'peh au had had wuh ha'zehl il dahkuh na' ish-veh. "oh, wuh sasu, wuh sasu!" "tonk'peh t'nash-veh tal-kam!" began defarge. "tonk'peh t'nash-veh tal-kam!" ashiv-tor madame, nodding firmly; "tonk'peh t'nash-veh tal-kam! Du nam-tor faint t' khaf-spol tor-mu-yor, t'nash-veh tal-kam!" "muhl, yi, " leralmin-tor defarge, u' kuv wuh nahp vesh' wrung s' ish-veh thasek, "ish-veh nam-tor wuh akarshif." "ish-veh nam-tor wuh akarshif, " ashiv-tor ish-veh ko-telsu; "heh lu nam-tor ish-veh ri wuh akarshif? Vengeance heh retribution require wuh akarshif; ish-veh nam-tor wuh tor-go." "ish-veh tor ri nem-tor wuh akarshif tor kwul wuh sasu k' igen-wesh, " leralmin-tor defarge. "uf wu, " halishau madame, composedly, "tor ish-veh nem-tor tor tor heh mahr-kel wuh igen-wesh? Var-tor me." defarge ashenau ish-veh patam thoughtfully, u' kuv tra' vesh' vel svi' ik nuh'. "ish-veh tor ri nem-tor wuh akarshif, " leralmin-tor madame, "na' wuh solektra-hutaya tor vitem-tor wuh kahr. Eh muhl! Var-tor me uf wu ish-veh nem-tor tor dator wuh solektra-hutaya?" "wuh akarshif, i suppose, " leralmin-tor defarge. "tonk'peh lu ish-veh nam-tor pok, ish-veh nem-tor shi, heh grazhau tor krus kanok-vei fa' ish-veh. Svi' wuh meantime, ish-veh nam-tor kwon-hau-ov preparing, hi ish-veh nam-tor ri gla-tor il puzhu-tor. Ik nam-tor ish-veh consolation. Potau ish-veh." she tied wuh knot k' flashing bezhun, u' kuv ish-veh threshan-tash-tor wuh hahf. "i var-tor thee, " leralmin-tor madame, extending ish-veh gas'rak el'ru, na' emphasis, "ik hi ish-veh nam-tor wuh akarshif fi' wuh fau-yut, ish-veh nam-tor fi' wuh fau-yut heh coming. I var-tor thee ish-veh worla retreats, heh worla pehkau. I var-tor thee ish-veh nam-tor kwon-hau-ov advancing. Glazhau pa' heh panah-tor wuh ha-tor t' ek' wuh panu ik etek fai-tor, panah-tor wuh limuk t' ek' wuh panu ik etek fai-tor, panah-tor wuh reshan heh discontent tor if wuh jacquerie shi'yavekh itself k' weht heh weht t' certainty kanok wadan. Mokuhlek such vel kim-shah? Bah! I mock du." "t'nash-veh kyi'i ko-telsu, " fun-tor defarge, standing fa' ish-veh k' ish-veh patam wuh pi' keh'sei, heh ish-veh el'ru clasped na' ish-veh pla', spo' wuh docile heh whio'naks glan-sharu fa' ish-veh catechist, "i ri tor deshker ek' nash. Tonk'peh ish-veh has palesh-tor wuh akarshif, heh ish-veh nam-tor tor-yehat--du fai-tor muhl, t'nash-veh ko-telsu, ish-veh nam-tor tor-yehat--ik ish-veh lau ri sarlah, du' etwel ha-tor." "eh muhl! Uf yi?" halishau madame, tying wuh'ashiv knot, u' kuv tra' vesh' wuh'ashiv nemut strangled. "muhl!" leralmin-tor defarge, k' wuh ulef complaining heh ulef apologetic shrug. "etek dungau ri gla-tor wuh triumph." "etek dungau ma gol-tor ish-veh, " fun-tor madame, k' ish-veh sadvun-tor el'ru svi' karik torai. "nothing ik etek tor, nam-tor ovsoh svi' vain. I dva-tor, k' ek' t'nash-veh soul, ik etek dungau gla-tor wuh triumph. Tonk'peh kauk kuv ri, kauk kuv i fai-tor certainly ri, gluvaya me wuh talu t' wuh aristocrat heh tyrant, heh fam dvun i would--" yi madame, k' ish-veh zud eku, tied wuh maut terrible knot indeed. "meskaraya!" maf-tor defarge, reddening wuh pi' u' kuv au olau vifalunau k' cowardice; "i nuh', t'nash-veh tal-kam, dungi pehkaya na' nothing." "ha! Tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor ish-veh kobat'es ik du sometimes bolaya tor gla-tor ish-veh shi-kar-tor heh ish-veh opportunity, tor potun-tor du. Potun-tor yourself rik' ik. Lu wuh wak sarlah, kal-tor thal wuh tiger heh wuh e'shua; tonk'peh bek-tor na' wuh wak k' wuh tiger heh wuh e'shua chained--ri shown--wi kwon-hau-ov pok." madame togolau wuh conclusion t' nash krus t' na'shikh k' striking ish-veh pi' tumek k' ish-veh naf-elakh t' donku u' kuv she knocked its shi'nahp si', heh yi hohnaya wuh ras handkerchief ne' ish-veh kar svi' wuh serene manner, heh observing ik ish-veh vesh' wak tor hal-tor tor sar-tak. Thurai noontide gla-tor wuh admirable kosu svi' ish-veh tsuri shi svi' wuh wine-mahr-kel, knitting maf assiduously. Wuh she-tor ti be' ish-veh, heh kuv she i' heh yi glanced na' wuh svai, ish-veh vesh' k' rai infraction t' ish-veh tsuri preoccupied sov. Tra' vesh' wuh zamu klepovausu, drinking il ri drinking, standing il hayal-tor, sprinkled pa'. Wuh gad vesh' maut fal, heh heaps t' hash-tor, vi vesh' extending ish-veh inquisitive heh adventurous perquisitions vi' ek' wuh glutinous pi' bezhun-zaneshu be' madame, tevan-tor tevik na' wuh lanet. Ish-veh decease tor rai impression fi' wuh vath hash-tor si' promenading, vi glazhau na' au svi' wuh coolest manner (u' kuv au themselves vesh' elephants, il vel u' irak snem-tor), abi' au ragel-tor wuh ka buk. Curious tor panah-tor uf heedless hash-tor nam-tor!--sos'eh au nahp u' mau na' kelek ik ka'ug'yelik belaar gad. Wuh khlop entering na' wuh svep threw wuh duv fi' madame defarge if she olau tor nam-tor wuh uzh veh. She laid ne' ish-veh knitting, heh began tor pin ish-veh she-tor svi' ish-veh patam-sai-vel, fa' she glazhau na' wuh khlop. Ish-veh vesh' curious. Wuh moment madame defarge nem-tor abru wuh she-tor, wuh klepovausu ceased talking, heh began gradually tor eku s' wuh wine-mahr-kel. "rom gad, madame, " leralmin-tor wuh uzh-comer. "rom gad, monsieur." she leralmin-tor ish-veh aloud, tonk'peh hau tor herself, u' she resumed ish-veh knitting: "hah! Rom gad, ya'shakhuv pa' keh-leh, pidek pa' kaukuh ash'ya naukuh, nesh-kur isachya, paik rather handsome visage, complexion gu'gelik, bezhun gu'gelik, wonil, wu heh sallow limuk, aquiline han tonk'peh ri zehik, having wuh peculiar inclination na' wuh losrak nak if imparts wuh sinister sagluvaya! Rom gad, veh heh ek'!" "ma wuh goodness tor mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh pi' makh t' hinek cognac, heh wuh mouthful t' samuyau sluk masu, madame." madame complied k' wuh polite sov. "marvellous cognac nash, madame!" ish-veh vesh' wuh wuh'rak wak ish-veh had ek'wak vesh' ni complimented, heh madame defarge fai-tor hiyet t' its antecedents tor fai-tor weh-rom. She leralmin-tor, however, ik wuh cognac vesh' snuhkrol-tor, heh nem-tor abru ish-veh knitting. Wuh visitor glantau ish-veh ozh na' wuh zamu moments, heh nem-tor wuh opportunity t' observing wuh shi svi' paik. "du knit k' lo'uk renkup'es, madame." "i am accustomed tor ish-veh." "wuh takov nel-dath nuh'!" "du nah-tor ni?" leralmin-tor madame, looking na' ish-veh k' wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut. "decidedly. Lau veh ya'akash ra ish-veh nam-tor na'?" "pastime, " leralmin-tor madame, fam dvun looking na' ish-veh k' wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut du' ish-veh ozh dvun-tor nimbly. "ri na' nam-tor-tor?" "ik nerau. I lau talal wuh nam-tor-tor na' ish-veh veh gad. Kuv i tor--muhl, " leralmin-tor madame, bestan wuh esh heh nodding ish-veh patam k' wuh harr-krus ves t' coquetry, "i'll nam-tor-tor ish-veh!" ish-veh vesh' remarkable; tonk'peh, wuh zahvan t' osu antoine seemed tor nam-tor decidedly opposed tor wuh she-tor fi' wuh patam-sai-vel t' madame defarge. Dahkuh sasu had svi-tor separately, heh had vesh' pa' tor zek mon, lu, catching glan t' ik novelty, au faltered, tor wuh pretence t' looking pa' u' kuv na' ein t'hy'la vi vesh' ri tra', heh went maf. Il, t' eifa vi had vesh' tra' lu nash visitor svi-tor, vesh' tra' veh losrak. Au had ek' eku-tor ska'. Wuh zamasu had potau ish-veh bezhun tu'ash, tonk'peh had vesh' kup tor patal-tor rai glat. Au had lounged maf svi' wuh poverty-stricken, purposeless, ur'kif manner, ved malatik heh unimpeachable. "john, " nahp madame, checking ska' ish-veh ar'kadan u' ish-veh ozh knitted, heh ish-veh bezhun glazhau na' wuh ri-fainusu. "stay wu hiyet, heh i dungau knit 'barsad' fa' du hal-tor." "du ma wuh sa-telsu, madame?" "i ma." "kanu?" "rai kanu." "business seems rasahkos?" "business nam-tor maut rasahkos; wuh sutra nam-tor ni ri donku-tor." "ah, wuh unfortunate, miserable sutra! Ni oppressed, nuh'--u' du leralmin." "u' du leralmin, " madame retorted, correcting ish-veh, heh deftly knitting wuh hayaik vel vi' ish-veh ahm ik boded ish-veh rai rom. "pardon me; certainly ish-veh vesh' i vi leralmin-tor ni, tonk'peh du naturally nah-tor ni. Veling." "i nah-tor?" fun-tor madame, svi' wuh pid spes. "i heh t'nash-veh sa-telsu ma hiyet tor tor tor potau nash wine-mahr-kel tu'ash, rik' thinking. Ek' etek nah-tor, la', nam-tor uf tor ha-tor. Ik nam-tor wuh subject etek nah-tor t', heh ish-veh mazhiv-kur-tor etek, s' asal tor mu-yor, hiyet tor nah-tor pa', rik' embarrassing etwel patam fundik vath. I nah-tor na' vath? Rai, rai." wuh zamasu, vi vesh' tra' tor abrashau sovek crumbs au kupi talal il tor, did ri kal-tor ish-veh hertak-tor fupa s' tor sagluvau itself svi' ish-veh sinister limuk; tonk'peh, lam-tor k' wuh sov t' gossiping gallantry, leaning ish-veh kar-nef fi' madame defarge's pi' tumek, heh occasionally mon-tor ish-veh cognac. "wuh rasahkos business nash, madame, t' gaspard's execution. Ah! Wuh ri donku-tor gaspard!" k' wuh spes-tevan t' lo'uk utan'es. "t'nash-veh odva!" fun-tor madame, coolly heh lightly, "kuv sutra nam-tor-tor lipau na' such lof, au ma tor vlitau na' ish-veh. Au fai-tor beforehand ra wuh price t' ish-veh luxury vesh'; au has vlitau wuh price." "i dva-tor, " leralmin-tor wuh zamasu, dropping ish-veh mos spes tor wuh molu ik invited guhl'es, heh expressing wuh dash-tor revolutionary susceptibility svi' kanok dvunek t' ish-veh wicked limuk: "i dva-tor tra' nam-tor mau utan'es heh reshan svi' nash neighbourhood, touching wuh ri donku-tor katravahsu? Svi' ourselves." "nam-tor tra'?" ya'akash madame, vacantly. "nam-tor tra' ri?" "--la' nam-tor t'nash-veh sa-telsu!" leralmin-tor madame defarge. U' wuh keeper t' wuh wine-mahr-kel svi-tor na' wuh svep, wuh zamasu saluted ish-veh k' touching ish-veh taik, heh taran, k' wuh engaging abru'teruklar-ru'lut, "rom gad, jacques!" defarge pehkau pen, heh nantau na' ish-veh. "rom gad, jacques!" wuh zamasu ashiv-tor; k' ri ved ni mau guhl'es, il ved ni hagik wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut ne' wuh nantaya. "du tehs-tor yourself, monsieur, " fun-tor wuh keeper t' wuh wine-mahr-kel. "du lafosh me na' wuh'ashiv. Ik nam-tor ri t'nash-veh ahm. I am ernest defarge." "ish-veh nam-tor ek' wuh ka, " leralmin-tor wuh zamasu, airily, tonk'peh discomfited nuh': "rom gad!" "rom gad!" kilko-tor defarge, drily. "i vesh' taran tor madame, k' ik i had wuh sanosh t' chatting lu du svi-tor, ik au var-tor me tra' nam-tor--heh rai wonder!--mau sympathy heh reshan svi' osu antoine, touching wuh unhappy buk t' ri donku-tor gaspard." "kling has var-tor me ni, " leralmin-tor defarge, shaking ish-veh patam. "i fai-tor nothing t' ish-veh." having leralmin-tor ish-veh, au be' dvun-tor za' wuh pi' tumek, heh lam-tor k' ish-veh el'ru fi' wuh pla' t' ish-veh ko-telsu's ku-san, looking abru' ik foshek na' wuh person tor ik au vesh' fi' opposed, heh ik either t' au would ma pohshaya k' wuh greatest satisfaction. Wuh zamasu, muhl nam-tor-tor tor ish-veh business, did ri rubah ish-veh unconscious attitude, tonk'peh smashau ish-veh pi' makh t' cognac, nem-tor wuh mon-tor t' sluk masu, heh ya'akash na' wuh'ashiv makh t' cognac. Madame defarge mukau ish-veh si' na' ish-veh, nem-tor tor ish-veh knitting va'ashiv, heh hummed wuh pi' song abru' ish-veh. "du seem tor fai-tor nash yonuk muhl; ik nam-tor tor leralmin, weh-rom do i tor?" glantau defarge. "mokov, tonk'peh i rok tor fai-tor ish-veh weh-rom. I am ni profoundly interested svi' its miserable inhabitants." "hah!" muttered defarge. "wuh sanosh t' conversing k' du, monsieur defarge, recalls tor me, " pursued wuh zamasu, "ik i ma wuh dor t' tishau ein eku'ki katravek k' ish-veh ahm." "indeed!" leralmin-tor defarge, k' mau indifference. "ha, indeed. Lu hassu manette vesh' sadalau, du, ish-veh hinek ka'kelik, had wuh falun t' ish-veh, i fai-tor. Au vesh' tefu tor du. Gla-tor du i am informed t' wuh circumstances?" "such nam-tor wuh kla-min, certainly, " leralmin-tor defarge. Au had had ish-veh zhelesh tor ish-veh, svi' wuh ur'kif esta t' ish-veh ko-telsu's kar-nef u' she knitted heh warbled, ik au would tor buhfik tor kilko-srashiv, tonk'peh kwon-hau-ov k' brevity. "ish-veh vesh' tor du, " leralmin-tor wuh zamasu, "ik ish-veh ko-fu sarlah; heh ish-veh vesh' s' ish-veh tun ik ish-veh ko-fu nem-tor ish-veh, accompanied k' wuh pu khav-kur monsieur; uf nam-tor au puvutau?--svi' wuh pi' wig--lorry--t' wuh kutra t' tellson heh apc'koik--abru' tor england." "such nam-tor wuh kla-min, " ashiv-tor defarge. "maut eku'ki remembrances!" leralmin-tor wuh zamasu. "i ma fainu hassu manette heh ish-veh ko-fu, svi' england." "ha?" leralmin-tor defarge. "du ri tor zhu-tor mau pa' au i'?" leralmin-tor wuh zamasu. "rai, " leralmin-tor defarge. "svi' daya, " madame kwul-tor svi', looking abru s' ish-veh ar'kadan heh ish-veh pi' song, "etek worla zhu-tor pa' au. Etek poprah wuh ro'fori t' ish-veh safe lashan, heh sos'eh wuh'ashiv nuhm, il sos'eh dahkuh; tonk'peh, opi' yi, au ma gradually taken ish-veh fau-yut svi' ha'kiv--etek, ours--heh etek ma meskarau rai correspondence." "perfectly ni, madame, " kilko-tor wuh zamasu. "she nam-tor going tor nam-tor telik." "going?" echoed madame. "she vesh' takov hiyet ki' vesh' telik wu ago. Du eingelsu nam-tor samu, ish-veh seems tor me." "oh! Du fai-tor i am eingelsu." "i pakashogau ish-veh lahv nam-tor, " fun-tor madame; "heh ra wuh lahv nam-tor, i suppose wuh sasu nam-tor." au did ri nem-tor wuh shasutan u' wuh compliment; tonk'peh au tor wuh buhfik t' ish-veh, heh da-tor ish-veh ska' k' wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut. Po' mon-tor ish-veh cognac tor wuh shaht, au hau: "ha, din-tor manette nam-tor going tor nam-tor telik. Tonk'peh ri tor wuh englishman; tor veh vi, spo' herself, nam-tor french k' keshtan. Heh speaking t' gaspard (ah, ri donku-tor gaspard! Ish-veh vesh' pi-maat'rer, pi-maat'rer!), ish-veh nam-tor wuh curious vel ik she nam-tor going tor marry wuh sa-bath t' monsieur wuh marquis, na' ik gaspard vesh' exalted tor ik pidek t' ni wehk ash'ya; svi' vath zhit, wuh la' marquis. Tonk'peh au ha-tor ri-fainu svi' england, au nam-tor rai marquis tra'; au nam-tor mr. Charles darnay. D'aulnais nam-tor wuh ahm t' ish-veh ko-mekh's skan." madame defarge knitted steadily, tonk'peh wuh kash-tor'es had wuh palpable daya fi-tor ish-veh sa-telsu. Tor ra au would, za' wuh pi' tumek, u' tor wuh striking t' wuh ta'hal heh wuh ha'gelan t' ish-veh mev, au vesh' troubled, heh ish-veh el'ru vesh' ri trustworthy. Wuh zamasu would ma vesh' rai zamasu kuv au had vravshau tor gla-tor ish-veh, il tor vipladau ish-veh svi' ish-veh kashek. Having tor, k'puu, nash-veh kwul, whatever ish-veh lau skan-tor tor nam-tor don, heh rai klepovausu coming svi' tor gol'nev ish-veh tor sovek vath, mr. Barsad vlitau na' ra au had mon-tor, heh nem-tor ish-veh trasha: taking occasion tor leralmin, svi' wuh genteel manner, fa' au trashu, ik au glazhau fa'rak tor wuh sanosh t' seeing monsieur heh madame defarge va'ashiv. Na' ein minutes po' au had sasarlah vi' wuh sik la'es t' osu antoine, wuh sa-telsu heh ko-telsu hafau exactly u' au had losrak au, lest au dang sarlah pla'. "mokuhlek ish-veh nam-tor yeht, " leralmin-tor defarge, svi' wuh neik spes, looking ne' na' ish-veh ko-telsu u' au lam-tor smoking k' ish-veh el'ru fi' wuh pla' t' ish-veh ku-san: "ra au has leralmin-tor t' ma'amselle manette?" "u' au has leralmin-tor ish-veh, " fun-tor madame, lifting ish-veh bezhun-zehl wuh pi', "ish-veh nam-tor probably riyeht. Tonk'peh ish-veh lau nam-tor yeht." "kuv ish-veh nam-tor--" defarge began, heh pehkau. "kuv ish-veh nam-tor?" ashiv-tor ish-veh ko-telsu. "--heh kuv ish-veh tor sarlah, du' etek ha-tor tor gla-tor ish-veh triumph--i rok, na' ish-veh sake, buk dungi potau ish-veh sa-telsu s' france." "ish-veh sa-telsu's buk, " leralmin-tor madame defarge, k' ish-veh tsuri composure, "dungi nem-tor ish-veh wilat au nam-tor tor hal-tor, heh dungi ras-tukh ish-veh tor wuh shaht ik nam-tor tor shaht ish-veh. Ik nam-tor ek' i fai-tor." "tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor maut flekh--i', k'puu, nam-tor ish-veh ri maut flekh"--leralmin-tor defarge, rather pleading k' ish-veh ko-telsu tor vimevilau ish-veh tor nafai-tor ish-veh, "ik, po' ek' etwel sympathy na' monsieur ish-veh sa-mekh, heh herself, ish-veh sa-telsu's ahm dang nam-tor proscribed ne' ish-veh el'ru i', k' wuh vla t' ik infernal dog's vi has aishan losrak etek?" "ri-fainusu vel do ik dungi pavesh-tor lu ish-veh tor sarlah, " kilko-tor madame. "i ma au fi' la', t' wuh certainty; heh au nam-tor fi' la' na' ish-veh merits; ik nam-tor hiyet." she padukau abru ish-veh knitting lu she had leralmin-tor eifa zhit, heh presently nem-tor wuh she-tor s' wuh handkerchief ik vesh' skek pa' ish-veh patam. Either osu antoine had wuh instinctive kash-ral ik wuh objectionable decoration vesh' hal-tor, il osu antoine vesh' fi' wuh glantau na' its disappearance; howbeit, wuh osu nem-tor courage tor lounge svi', maut shortly afterwards, heh wuh wine-mahr-kel recovered its habitual pulva. Svi' wuh khru, na' if tevun-yonuk t' ek' vath osu antoine da-tor himself svi'udish si', heh hayal-tor fi' svep-ash-tor heh krani-ledges, heh sarlah tor wuh teruk t' vile yut heh kelek, na' wuh esh t' sov, madame defarge k' ish-veh ar'kadan svi' ish-veh el'ru vesh' accustomed tor be' dvun s' shi tor shi heh s' travek tor travek: wuh missionary--tra' vesh' wehk spo' ish-veh--such u' wuh panu dungi tor muhl worla tor kosh-ves va'ashiv. Ek' wuh kosu knitted. Au knitted worthless vel; tonk'peh, wuh mechanical ar'kadan vesh' wuh mechanical substitute na' eating heh drinking; wuh el'ru dvun-tor na' wuh ahs heh wuh digestive oh'a'dhid: kuv wuh bony ozh had vesh' fam dvun, wuh skaun-sa'haf would ma vesh' weht mair-yem-penak-k'hy. Tonk'peh, u' wuh ozh went, wuh bezhun went, heh wuh nahp. Heh u' madame defarge dvun-tor fi' s' travek tor travek, ek' rehkuh went quicker heh fiercer among kanok pi' knot t' kosu ik she had spoken k', heh losrak za'. Ish-veh sa-telsu smoked na' ish-veh svep, looking po' ish-veh k' admiration. "wuh lo'uk kosu, " leralmin-tor au, "wuh karik kosu, wuh grand kosu, wuh frightfully grand kosu!" mu'khlup'es a'ing pa', heh yi sarlah wuh ringing t' church kus-vakh heh wuh irak beating t' wuh askital vluhn svi' wuh palace courtyard, u' wuh kosu hayal-tor knitting, knitting. Mu'khlup'es encompassed au. Wuh'ashiv mu'khlup'es vesh' ikapik svi' u' surely, lu wuh church kus-vakh, yi ringing pleasantly svi' wehk wuh airy steeple abru' france, dang nam-tor klimtau vi' thundering thorshun; lu wuh askital vluhn dang nam-tor beating tor mastevau wuh wretched spes, ik mu-yor ek' potent u' wuh spes t' tepul heh plenty, el'es heh ha'kiv. Ni mau vesh' ikapik svi' pa' wuh kosu vi hayal-tor knitting, knitting, ik au ish-veh maut selves vesh' ikapik svi' pa' wuh velek wi unbuilt, wilat au vesh' tor hayal-tor knitting, knitting, counting dropping patam. Chapter xvii. Veh mu-yor worla did wuh yel hal-tor ne' k' wuh brighter glory fi' wuh hizhuk teruk svi' soho, do veh memorable khru lu wuh hassu heh ish-veh ko-fu hayal-tor ne' wuh sov-hali-lap teretuhr. Worla did wuh aikum shen k' wuh milder radiance abru' lo'uk london, do fi' ik mu-yor lu ish-veh afer-tor au fam dvun hayal-tor ne' wuh lap, heh min-tor fi-tor ish-veh limuk k'fai its mor. Lucie vesh' tor nam-tor telik tor-morrow. She had reserved nash kim-shah khru na' ish-veh sa-mekh, heh au hayal-tor sa'awek ne' wuh sov-hali-lap. "du nam-tor kunli, t'nash-veh tal-kam sa-mekh?" "ved, t'nash-veh kan." au had leralmin-tor pi', hi au had vesh' tra' wuh akarshif. Lu ish-veh vesh' wi ta'hal hiyet tor ar'kadan heh telv-tor, she had neither engaged herself svi' ish-veh tsuri ar'kadan, il had she telv-tor tor ish-veh. She had employed herself svi' fi' yut, na' ish-veh vla ne' wuh lap, wehk heh wehk wuh wak; tonk'peh, nash wak vesh' ri ved spo' sovek vath, heh nothing kupi tor ish-veh ni. "heh i am maut kunli tor-mu-yor, tal-kam sa-mekh. I am deeply kunli svi' wuh ashaya ik sha-ka-ri has ni blessed--t'nash-veh ashaya na' charles, heh charles's ashaya na' me. Tonk'peh, kuv t'nash-veh ha'kiv vesh' ri tor nam-tor fam dvun consecrated tor du, il kuv t'nash-veh kal'i'farr vesh' ni arranged u' ik ish-veh would krus etek, kauk k' wuh wu-vath t' wuh zamu t' aifa yut, i dang nam-tor weht unhappy heh shal-reproachful i' do i mokuhlek var-tor du. Kauk u' ish-veh nam-tor--" kauk u' ish-veh vesh', she kupi ri a'fic ish-veh spes. Svi' wuh maf moonlight, she clasped ish-veh k' wuh talu, heh laid ish-veh limuk fi-tor ish-veh thasek. Svi' wuh moonlight if nam-tor kwon-hau-ov maf, u' wuh ta'hal t' wuh yel itself nam-tor--u' wuh ta'hal puvutau komihn ha'kiv nam-tor--na' its coming heh its going. "dearest tal-kam! Mokuhlek du var-tor me, nash kim-shah wak, ik du olau ved, ved sure, rai uzh affections t' t'nash-veh, heh rai uzh gu-vam t' t'nash-veh, dungi ek'wak interpose svi' etek? I fai-tor ish-veh muhl, tonk'peh tor du fai-tor ish-veh? Svi' ish-veh sha' khaf-spol, tor du olau ved ac'ruth?" ish-veh sa-mekh kilko-tor, k' wuh cheerful firmness t' conviction au kupi scarcely ma assumed, "ved sure, t'nash-veh ashal-veh! Weht do ik, " au hau, u' au tenderly shok-tor ish-veh: "t'nash-veh fa-wak nam-tor irak brighter, lucie, gla-tor k'fai ish-veh kal'i'farr, do ish-veh kupi ma vesh'--nay, do ish-veh ek'wak vesh'--rik' ish-veh." "kuv i kupi rok ik, t'nash-veh sa-mekh!--" "dva-tor ish-veh, ashaya! Indeed ish-veh nam-tor ni. Panah-tor uf malatik heh uf eiktra ish-veh nam-tor, t'nash-veh tal-kam, ik ish-veh dang nam-tor ni. Du, vaikau heh nu'ri, fam yehat fully appreciate wuh anxiety i ma olau ik ish-veh ha'kiv dang ri nam-tor thinoi--" she dvun-tor ish-veh el'ru na' ish-veh bru-lar, tonk'peh au nem-tor ish-veh svi' ish-veh, heh ashiv-tor wuh zhit. "--thinoi, t'nash-veh kan--dang ri nam-tor thinoi, kwul-tor si' wuh malatik zek t' vel--na' t'nash-veh sake. Ish-veh unselfishness fam yehat entirely comprehend uf mau t'nash-veh kashek has hal-tor fi' nash; tonk'peh, goh ya'akash yourself, uf kupi t'nash-veh happiness nam-tor buhfik, du' ish-veh vesh' incomplete?" "kuv i had worla gla-tor charles, t'nash-veh sa-mekh, i dang ma vesh' ved kunli k' du." au abru'teruklar-ru'lut na' ish-veh unconscious admission ik she would ma vesh' unhappy rik' charles, having gla-tor ish-veh; heh kilko-tor: "t'nash-veh kan, du did gla-tor ish-veh, heh ish-veh nam-tor charles. Kuv ish-veh had ri vesh' charles, ish-veh would ma vesh' wuh'ashiv. Il, kuv ish-veh had vesh' rai vath, i dang ma vesh' wuh aishan, heh yi wuh gu'gelik krus t' t'nash-veh ha'kiv would ma vishizhau its duv mesakh myself, heh would ma tevan-tor fi' du." ish-veh vesh' wuh wuh'rak wak, kaula na' wuh trial, t' ish-veh ek'wak khaf-spol ish-veh dzhinau tor wuh wak-krus t' ish-veh suffering. Ish-veh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh flekh heh uzh kashan du' ish-veh zhit vesh' svi' ish-veh kaluk; heh she vokau ish-veh wu afterwards. "gla-tor!" leralmin-tor wuh hassu t' beauvais, raising ish-veh el'ru na' wuh aikum. "i ma glazhau na' ish-veh s' t'nash-veh prison-krani, lu i kupi ri lesh ish-veh ta'hal. I ma glazhau na' ish-veh lu ish-veh has vesh' such torture tor me tor nah-tor t' ish-veh shining fi-tor ra i had pakik, ik i ma beaten t'nash-veh patam tehnat t'nash-veh prison-temok. I ma glazhau na' ish-veh, svi' wuh fupa s' ni pasik heh lethargic, ik i ma nahp t' nothing tonk'peh wuh su'etek t' yutik zehl i kupi bes-tor mes' ish-veh na' wuh bosh, heh wuh su'etek t' sazehik zehl k' if i kupi tvimesau au." au hau svi' ish-veh inward heh pondering manner, u' au glazhau na' wuh aikum, "ish-veh vesh' dah-leh either yut, i vokau, heh wuh twentieth vesh' rihagik tor lerakhovau svi'." wuh flekh thrill k' if she puzhu-tor ish-veh hal-tor pla' tor ik wak, deepened u' au dwelt fi-tor ish-veh; tonk'peh, tra' vesh' nothing tor kolaya ish-veh svi' wuh manner t' ish-veh dzhinaya. Au goh seemed tor contrast ish-veh la' cheerfulness heh felicity k' wuh dire palesh ik vesh' abru'. "i ma glazhau na' ish-veh, speculating thousands t' wak fi-tor wuh unborn kan s' ik i had vesh' rent. Whether ish-veh vesh' alive. Whether ish-veh had vesh' pukeshta alive, il wuh ri donku-tor ko-mekh's kolaya had pustau ish-veh. Whether ish-veh vesh' wuh sa-fu vi would ein gad avenge ish-veh sa-mekh. (tra' vesh' wuh wak svi' t'nash-veh imprisonment, lu t'nash-veh aitlun na' vengeance vesh' unbearable.) whether ish-veh vesh' wuh sa-fu vi would worla fai-tor ish-veh sa-mekh's var; vi lau kauk ha-tor tor rasathau wuh possibility t' ish-veh sa-mekh's having sasaudau t' ish-veh sha' dungi heh bae'cok. Whether ish-veh vesh' wuh ko-fu vi would tor'ovau tor nam-tor wuh kosu." she drew closer tor ish-veh, heh shok-tor ish-veh nak heh ish-veh el'ru. "i ma pictured t'nash-veh ko-fu, tor myself, u' perfectly forgetful t' me--rather, altogether ignorant t' me, heh unconscious t' me. I ma vishizhau abru wuh tevun t' ish-veh ya'shakhuv, tevun po' tevun. Ki'gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh telik tor wuh sasu vi fai-tor nothing t' t'nash-veh buk. I ma altogether perished s' wuh remembrance t' wuh living, heh svi' wuh thurai generation t'nash-veh shi vesh' wuh blank." "t'nash-veh sa-mekh! Kauk tor zhu-tor ik du had such nahp t' wuh ko-fu vi worla nam-tor, kwul-tor tor t'nash-veh khaf-spol u' kuv i had vesh' ik kan." "du, lucie? Ish-veh nam-tor s' wuh consolation heh restoration du ma katau tor me, ik aifa remembrances arise, heh be' dvun svi' etek heh wuh aikum fi' nash kim-shah mu-yor.--ra did i leralmin aishan i'?" "she fai-tor nothing t' du. She tun-tor nothing na' du." "ni! Tonk'peh fi' vath moonlight mu-yor, lu wuh sadness heh wuh silence ma estuhl me svi' wuh natya yut--ma dau me k' vel u' spo' wuh sorrowful kash-ral t' sochya, u' sovek zherka ik had kusut na' its nen kupi--i ma glenonau ish-veh u' coming tor me svi' t'nash-veh nala, heh leading me si' vi' wuh el'es mesakh wuh klomak. Ki'gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh glakuv svi' wuh moonlight k'ashiv, u' i i' gla-tor du; kaula ik i worla meskarau ish-veh svi' t'nash-veh kar; ish-veh lam-tor svi' wuh pi' grated krani heh wuh svep. Tonk'peh, du ken-tor ik ik vesh' ri wuh kan i am speaking t'?" "wuh khlop vesh' ri; wuh--wuh--glakuv; wuh fancy?" "rai. Ik vesh' wuh'ashiv vel. Ish-veh lam-tor fa' t'nash-veh ertau kash-ral t' glan, tonk'peh ish-veh worla dvun-tor. Wuh phantom ik t'nash-veh kashek pursued, vesh' wuh'ashiv heh weht yeht kan. T' ish-veh outward appearance i fai-tor rai weht do ik she vesh' spo' ish-veh ko-mekh. Wuh vath had ik likeness nuh'--u' du ma--tonk'peh vesh' ri wuh ka. Mokuhlek du zahal-tor me, lucie? Hardly, i nah-tor? I vet du bolau ma vesh' wuh solitary prisoner tor ken-tor aifa perplexed distinctions." ish-veh tershau heh hayal manner kupi ri prevent ish-veh khaf s' sahran samu, u' au thus ar'kada tor anatomise ish-veh hinek nosh. "svi' ik weht peaceful fupa s', i ma glenonau ish-veh, svi' wuh moonlight, coming tor me heh taking me si' tor gluvaya me ik wuh ha-kel t' ish-veh telik ha'kiv vesh' bosh t' ish-veh loving remembrance t' ish-veh pakik sa-mekh. T'nash-veh bikuv vesh' svi' ish-veh tvi-shal, heh i vesh' svi' ish-veh prayers. Ish-veh ha'kiv vesh' torupik, cheerful, useful; tonk'peh t'nash-veh ri donku-tor vesht-var pervaded ish-veh ek'." "i vesh' ik kan, t'nash-veh sa-mekh, i vesh' ri ulef ni rom, tonk'peh svi' t'nash-veh ashaya ik vesh' i." "heh she gluvau me ish-veh kanu, " leralmin-tor wuh hassu t' beauvais, "heh au had puzhu-tor t' me, heh had vesh' saven-tor tor pity me. Lu au be' dvun-tor wuh prison t' wuh fupa s', au potau irak s' its frowning temok, heh glazhau abru na' its mofek, heh stariben svi' zhal-tor. She kupi worla tefu me; i glenonau ik she kwon-hau-ov katau me pla' po' showing me such vel. Tonk'peh yi, blessed k' wuh vas t' bezhun-masu, i tevan-tor fi-tor t'nash-veh mal-nef, heh blessed ish-veh." "i am ik kan, i rok, t'nash-veh sa-mekh. O t'nash-veh tal-kam, t'nash-veh tal-kam, dungi du kudau me u' fervently tor-morrow?" "lucie, i recall aifa hinek troubles svi' wuh utvau ik i ma tor-mu-yor na' loving du weh-rom do zhit mokuhlek var-tor, heh thanking oekon na' t'nash-veh lo'uk happiness. T'nash-veh nahp, lu au vesh' wildest, worla she-tor be' wuh happiness ik i ma fainu k' du, heh ik etek ma fa' etek." au nartau ish-veh, solemnly commended ish-veh tor sha-ka-ri, heh humbly itaren sha-ka-ri na' having bestowed ish-veh fi' ish-veh. K'-heh-bye, au went vi' wuh kelek. Tra' vesh' kling bidden tor wuh kal'i'farr tonk'peh mr. Lorry; tra' vesh' kauk tor nam-tor rai bridesmaid tonk'peh wuh gaunt din-tor pross. Wuh kal'i'farr vesh' tor tor rai rubah svi' ish-veh shi' residence; au had vesh' kup tor sadvun-tor ish-veh, k' taking tor themselves wuh upper tvi-shal formerly t' wuh apocryphal invisible lodger, heh au aitlu nothing weht. Hassu manette vesh' maut cheerful na' wuh pi' mu'yor-yem. Au vesh' goh rehkuh na' pasu, heh din-tor pross tor wuh wuh. Au regretted ik charles vesh' ri tra'; vesh' weht do ulef sashitau tor vel tor wuh loving pi' besau ik potau ish-veh maf; heh drank tor ish-veh affectionately. Ni, wuh wak sarlah na' ish-veh tor nufai lucie rom mu-yor, heh au dahshau. Tonk'peh, svi' wuh stillness t' wuh wuh wadan t' wuh asal, lucie sarlah downstairs va'ashiv, heh vazgau vi' ish-veh tvi-shal; ri elik s' unshaped ptha, beforehand. Ek' vel, however, vesh' svi' ish-veh shitau; ek' vesh' hizhuk; heh au ti asleep, ish-veh wan-kur isachya picturesque fi' wuh untroubled trak, heh ish-veh el'ru lying hizhuk fi' wuh coverlet. She shitau ish-veh needless ha'fek svi' wuh duv na' wuh ir, crept abru tor ish-veh sar-tak, heh shitau ish-veh bru-lar tor ish-veh; yi, gal-tor abru' ish-veh, heh glazhau na' ish-veh. Vi' ish-veh handsome limuk, wuh sfith(-) mashau t' captivity had worn; tonk'peh, au wein-tor abru ish-veh ash'yaidar k' wuh determination ni karik, ik au meskarau wuh tren'es t' au kauk svi' ish-veh yuk. Wuh weht remarkable limuk svi' its hizhuk, resolute, heh klashau struggle k' wuh unseen assailant, vesh' ri tor nam-tor beheld svi' ek' wuh eik dominions t' yuk, ik mu-yor. She timidly laid ish-veh el'ru fi' ish-veh tal-kam thasek, heh shitau abru wuh prayer ik she lau ek'wak nam-tor u' yeht tor ish-veh u' ish-veh ashaya aspired tor nam-tor, heh u' ish-veh sorrows nazh-tor. Yi, she withdrew ish-veh el'ru, heh shok-tor ish-veh bru-lar wuh'wak weht, heh went maf. Ni, wuh ug'yel-shen sarlah, heh wuh duv t' wuh mor t' wuh sov-hali-lap dvun-tor fi-tor ish-veh limuk, u' softly u' ish-veh bru-lar had dvun-tor svi' praying na' ish-veh. Chapter xviii. Naukuh gad wuh kal'i'farr-gad vesh' shining brightly, heh au vesh' pok s'udish wuh a'ing svep t' wuh hassu's tvi-shal, wilat au vesh' speaking k' charles darnay. Au vesh' pok tor hal-tor tor church; wuh vaksurik bride, mr. Lorry, heh din-tor pross--tor ik wuh pavek, k'fai wuh gradual torek t' reconcilement tor wuh inevitable, would ma vesh' veh t' ek'esik bliss, tonk'peh na' wuh wi svizh-tor consideration ik ish-veh sa-kai solomon dang ma vesh' wuh bridegroom. "heh ni, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, vi kupi ri sufficiently krol-tor wuh bride, heh vi had vesh' dvun-tor pauk ish-veh tor nem-tor svi' kanok sfek t' ish-veh hizhuk, takov sai-vel; "heh ni ish-veh vesh' na' nash, t'nash-veh slor lucie, ik i katau du mes' wuh mashyut, such wuh kan-bu! S'haile kudau me! Uf pi' i nahp ra i vesh' doing! Uf lightly i valued wuh obligation i vesh' conferring fi' t'nash-veh t'hy'la mr. Charles!" "du didn't tvai ish-veh, " remarked wuh tukh-t'-kla-min din-tor pross, "heh therefore uf kupi du fai-tor ish-veh? Nonsense!" "really? Muhl; tonk'peh ri tor maf, " leralmin-tor wuh gentle mr. Lorry. "i am ri maf-tor, " leralmin-tor din-tor pross; "du nam-tor." "i, t'nash-veh pross?" (k' nash wak, mr. Lorry dared tor nam-tor vaksurik k' ish-veh, fi' occasion.) "du vesh', aishan i'; vesht gla-tor nash-veh du tor ish-veh, heh i ri tor wonder na' ish-veh. Such wuh la' t' math u' du ma tor 'em, nam-tor hiyet tor katau bezhun-masu vi' anybody's bezhun. Tra''s ri wuh snauk il wuh floku svi' wuh tershaya, " leralmin-tor din-tor pross, "ik i didn't maf abru', kim-shah mu-yor po' wuh natuhn sarlah, till i couldn't gla-tor ish-veh." "i am highly gratified, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, "hi, fi-tor t'nash-veh dor, i had rai intention t' rendering eifa trifling ua'mrki t' remembrance invisible tor sovek veh. Tal-kam me! Nash nam-tor wuh occasion ik tor wuh sasu speculate fi' ek' au has pakik. Tal-kam, tal-kam, tal-kam! Tor nah-tor ik tra' lau ma vesh' wuh mrs. Lorry, sovek wak aifa kau-leh tevun siyah!" "mokov!" s' din-tor pross. "du nah-tor tra' worla lau ma vesh' wuh mrs. Lorry?" ya'akash wuh gentleman t' ik ahm. "pooh!" rejoined din-tor pross; "du vesh' wuh bachelor svi' ish-veh cradle." "muhl!" glantau mr. Lorry, beamingly adjusting ish-veh pi' wig, "ik seems yesik, nuh'." "heh du vesh' tresahk si' na' wuh bachelor, " pursued din-tor pross, "fa' du vesh' shitau svi' ish-veh cradle." "yi, i nah-tor, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, "ik i vesh' maut unhandsomely dealt k', heh ik i ought ki' had wuh spes svi' wuh dvel t' t'nash-veh nel-dath. Hiyet!
