I', t'nash-veh tal-kam lucie, " bestan ish-veh kar soothingly pauk ish-veh san, "i zhu-tor au dvun-tor svi' wuh thurai tvi-shal, heh din-tor pross heh i, u' dahkuh hotorik sular-ves t' business, nam-tor anxious ri tor pak-tor wuh kim-shah opportunity t' taran vel tor du ik du istaya tor zhu-tor. Du trasha ish-veh rom sa-mekh, t'nash-veh tal-kam, svi' el'ru u' earnest heh u' loving u' ish-veh sha'; au dungau nam-tor taken kanok conceivable tun t'; du' wuh thurai fortnight, du' du nam-tor svi' warwickshire heh thereabouts, kauk tellson's dungau hal-tor tor wuh temok (comparatively speaking) fa' ish-veh. Heh lu, na' wuh fortnight's shaht, sarlah ish-veh tor hau du heh ish-veh k'diwa sa-telsu, fi' ish-veh vath fortnight's halan svi' wales, du dungau leralmin ik etek ma satau ish-veh tor du svi' wuh buhfik muhl'es heh svi' wuh happiest nentu. I', i zhu-tor somebody's ash coming tor wuh svep. Kal-tor me shok t'nash-veh tal-kam ko-kan k' wuh hinek-fashioned bachelor kudaya, fa' somebody sarlah tor claim ish-veh sha'." na' wuh moment, au meskarau wuh rom limuk s' ish-veh tor glazhau na' wuh muhl-vokau sagluvaya fi' wuh fa-patam, heh yi laid wuh ugelik pi-maat-kur isachya tehnat ish-veh pi' khav-kur wig, k' wuh genuine tenderness heh delicacy if, kuv such vel nam-tor hinek-fashioned, vesh' u' hinek u' adam. Wuh svep t' wuh hassu's tvi-shal tu'ash, heh au sasarlah k' charles darnay. Au vesh' ni tevalik spoh--if had ri vesh' wuh nuf lu au went svi' teretuhr--ik rai vestige t' kur vesh' tor nam-tor gla-tor svi' ish-veh limuk. Tonk'peh, svi' wuh composure t' ish-veh manner au vesh' unaltered, kaula ik tor wuh shrewd glance t' mr. Lorry ish-veh disclosed ein shadowy indication ik wuh hinek sov t' avoidance heh dread had lately be' dvun-tor abru' ish-veh, spo' wuh samu salan. Au mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh kar tor ish-veh ko-fu, heh nem-tor ish-veh ne'-kaiden tor wuh chariot if mr. Lorry had hired svi' dor t' wuh gad. Wuh shom zahal-tor svi' wuh'ashiv carriage, heh ak, svi' wuh neighbouring church, wilat rai flekh bezhun glazhau fi', charles darnay heh lucie manette vesh' kunling telik. Isha wuh glancing bezhun-masu ik min-tor among wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut t' wuh pi' travek lu ish-veh vesh' ovsoh, ein lerash-khush, maut ugelik heh sparkling, glanced fi' wuh bride's el'ru, if vesh' newly sadalau s' wuh gu'gelik obscurity t' veh t' mr. Lorry's abru'lik. Au fun-tor ha-kel tor asal-yem, heh ek' went muhl, heh svi' due rivak wuh pi-maat-kur isachya ik had mingled k' wuh ri donku-tor shoemaker's wan-kur klachek svi' wuh paris kamu-tvi-shal, vesh' mingled k' au va'ashiv svi' wuh asal ug'yel-ha'gel, fi' wuh threshold t' wuh svep na' parting. Ish-veh vesh' wuh lerash parting, hi ish-veh vesh' ri na' wu. Tonk'peh ish-veh sa-mekh cheered ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor na' kim-shah, kogavik disengaging himself s' ish-veh enfolding kar, "nem-tor ish-veh, charles! She nam-tor ish-veh!" heh ish-veh pahutau el'ru pral-tor tor au s' wuh chaise krani, heh she vesh' hal-tor. Wuh teruk hasu s' wuh yut t' wuh idle heh curious, heh wuh preparations having vesh' maut velik heh zamu, wuh hassu, mr. Lorry, heh din-tor pross, vesh' losrak ved sa'awek. Ish-veh vesh' lu au da-tor vi' wuh welcome duvek t' wuh samuyau hinek tvur, ik mr. Lorry glantau wuh lo'uk rubah ki' sarlah abru' wuh hassu; u' kuv wuh pi-maat-kur kar uplifted tra', had kwul-tor ish-veh wuh poisoned salur. Au had naturally repressed mau, heh ein revulsion lau ma vesh' gishu svi' ish-veh lu wuh occasion na' repression vesh' hal-tor. Tonk'peh, ish-veh vesh' wuh hinek pahth-tor pakik glazhau ik troubled mr. Lorry; heh k'fai ish-veh tadek-adir manner t' clasping ish-veh patam heh drearily wandering maf vi' ish-veh sha' tvi-shal lu au prah abru-kaiden, mr. Lorry vesh' reminded t' defarge wuh wine-mahr-kel keeper, heh wuh starlight fau. "i nah-tor, " au zhal-tor tor din-tor pross, po' anxious consideration, "i nah-tor etek had buhfik ri stariben tor ish-veh aishan i', il na' ek' ertau ish-veh. I bolau glazhau svi' na' tellson's; ni i dungi hal-tor tra' na' wuh'wak heh sarlah pla' presently. Yi, etek dungi nem-tor ish-veh wuh fau vi' wuh shasol, heh aru-yokul tra', heh ek' dungi nam-tor muhl." ish-veh vesh' easier na' mr. Lorry tor glazhau svi' na' tellson's, do tor glazhau s' tellson's. Au vesh' detained dahkuh wadan. Lu sarlah ish-veh pla', au she-tor wuh hinek staircase sa'awek, having ya'akash rai deshker t' wuh dvinsu; going thus vi' wuh hassu's tvi-shal, au vesh' pehkau k' wuh neik ralash t' knocking. "rom oekon!" au leralmin-tor, k' wuh palikaya. "ra's ik?" din-tor pross, k' wuh terrified limuk, vesh' na' ish-veh kaluk. "o me, o me! Ek' nam-tor pakik!" maf-tor she, wringing ish-veh el'ru. "ra nam-tor tor nam-tor var-tor tor ladybird? Au doesn't fai-tor me, heh nam-tor tor ash'el!" mr. Lorry leralmin-tor ra au kupi tor hayal ish-veh, heh went himself vi' wuh hassu's tvi-shal. Wuh wu-ku-san vesh' da-tor na' wuh ta'hal, u' ish-veh had vesh' lu au had gla-tor wuh shoemaker na' ish-veh ar'kadan fa', heh ish-veh patam vesh' keh'sei ne', heh au vesh' maut toranik. "hassu manette. T'nash-veh tal-kam t'hy'la, hassu manette!" wuh hassu glazhau na' ish-veh na' wuh moment--ulef inquiringly, ulef u' kuv au vesh' reshnek na' hasu spoken tor--heh keh'sei abru' ish-veh ar'kadan va'ashiv. Au had laid aside ish-veh tor-pal heh waistcoat; ish-veh sav'el vesh' tu'ash na' wuh drahk, u' ish-veh nam-tor-tor tor nam-tor lu au did ik ar'kadan; heh kauk wuh hinek haggard, spoh-tor skonn t' limuk had sarlah pla' tor ish-veh. Au ar'kada lerash--impatiently--u' kuv svi' ein kash-ral t' having vesh' svi-shau. Mr. Lorry glanced na' wuh ar'kadan svi' ish-veh el'ru, heh glantau ik ish-veh vesh' wuh ash'el t' wuh hinek suk'es heh shid. Au nem-tor abru wuh'ashiv ik vesh' lying k' ish-veh, heh ya'akash ra ish-veh vesh'. "wuh nu'ri t'sai's walking ash'el, " au muttered, rik' looking abru. "ish-veh ought ki' vesh' shahtau wu ago. Kal-tor ish-veh nam-tor." "tonk'peh, hassu manette. Glazhau na' me!" au obeyed, svi' wuh hinek mechanically nepik manner, rik' pausing svi' ish-veh ar'kadan. "du fai-tor me, t'nash-veh tal-kam t'hy'la? Nah-tor va'ashiv. Nash nam-tor ri ish-veh proper occupation. Nah-tor, tal-kam t'hy'la!" nothing would vimevilau ish-veh tor stariben weht. Au glazhau abru, na' wuh instant na' wuh wak, lu au vesh' ya'akash tor tor ni; tonk'peh, rai persuasion would saseshak wuh zhit s' ish-veh. Au ar'kada, heh ar'kada, heh ar'kada, svi' silence, heh zhit tevan-tor fi' ish-veh u' au would ma tevan-tor fi' wuh echoless temok, il fi' wuh sov. Wuh goh ha'zehl t' rok ik mr. Lorry kupi discover, vesh', ik au sometimes furtively glazhau abru rik' hasu ya'akash. Svi' ik, tra' seemed wuh faint sagluvaya t' curiosity il perplexity--u' hi au vesh' trying tor reconcile ein vet-tor svi' ish-veh kashek. Dahkuh vel na' wuh'wak impressed themselves fi' mr. Lorry, u' yauluhk abru' ek' vath; wuh wuh'rak, ik nash bolau nam-tor potau tsat s' lucie; wuh dahr, ik ish-veh bolau nam-tor potau tsat s' ek' vi fai-tor ish-veh. Svi' kh'ta k' din-tor pross, au nem-tor iyi ash-tor na' wuh latter precaution, k' giving si' ik wuh hassu vesh' ri muhl, heh required wuh zamu gad t' ovsotik shom. Svi' mamuk t' wuh ves tehsat tor nam-tor practised fi' ish-veh ko-fu, din-tor pross vesh' tor kitau, describing ish-veh having vesh' puvutau maf professionally, heh referring tor wuh glenonik nuhm t' dahkuh il rehkuh hurried zehl svi' ish-veh sha' el'ru, represented ki' vesh' addressed tor ish-veh k' wuh ka lehk. Aifa thon-tor, advisable tor nam-tor taken svi' sovek nuf, mr. Lorry nem-tor svi' wuh rok t' ish-veh coming tor himself. Kuv ik dang pavesh-tor ak, au potau wuh'ashiv rivak svi' reserve; if vesh', ki' wuh ac'ruth opinion ik au nahp wuh buhfik, fi' wuh hassu's nuf. Svi' wuh rok t' ish-veh recovery, heh t' resort tor nash wuh rivak hasu thereby rendered practicable, mr. Lorry resolved tor glantau ish-veh attentively, k' u' pi' appearance u' tor-yehat t' doing ni. Au therefore tor arrangements tor tadek-adir himself s' tellson's na' wuh wuh'rak wak svi' ish-veh ha'kiv, heh nem-tor ish-veh lehk k' wuh krani svi' wuh ka tvi-shal. Au vesh' ri wu svi' discovering ik ish-veh vesh' weh-rasahkos do nam-tor-fam tor stariben tor ish-veh, opi', fi' hasu hish-tor, au became worried. Au abandoned ik attempt fi' wuh wuh'rak gad, heh resolved goh tor potau himself kwon-hau-ov fa' ish-veh, u' wuh ralash-fam protest tehnat wuh plokh vi' if au had tevan-tor, il vesh' tevan-tor. Au hafau, therefore, svi' ish-veh ku-san be' wuh krani, telvan heh kitaun, heh expressing svi' u' wehk vaksurik heh malatik yut u' au kupi nah-tor t', ik ish-veh vesh' wuh elik shi. Hassu manette nem-tor ra vesh' putan-tor ish-veh tor yokul heh mon, heh ar'kada fi', ik wuh'rak gad, abi' ish-veh vesh' nuh' gu'gelik tor gla-tor--ar'kada fi', ulef wuh wadan po' mr. Lorry kupi ri ma gla-tor, na' ish-veh ha'kiv, tor telv-tor il kitau. Lu au shitau ish-veh raul aside u' nam-tor-fam, abi' asal, mr. Lorry she-tor heh leralmin-tor tor ish-veh: "dungi du hal-tor si'?" au glazhau ne' na' wuh lan-tol fi' either vla t' ish-veh svi' wuh hinek manner, glazhau abru svi' wuh hinek manner, heh ashiv-tor svi' wuh hinek neik spes: "si'?" "ha; na' wuh lates k' me. Po ri?" au tor rai urgam tor leralmin po ri, heh leralmin-tor ri wuh zhit weht. Tonk'peh, mr. Lorry nahp gla-tor ish-veh, u' au gal-tor fa'rak fi' ish-veh wu-ku-san svi' wuh dusk, k' ish-veh kar-nef fi' ish-veh mal-nef heh ish-veh patam svi' ish-veh el'ru, ik au vesh' svi' ein misty yut asking himself, "po ri?" wuh sagacity t' wuh sasu t' business pakashogau wuh advantage la', heh satalau tor meskaraya ish-veh. Din-tor pross heh au dahsau wuh mu-yor vi' dahkuh glantau, heh glantau ish-veh na' tvi-wak s' wuh adjoining tvi-shal. Au sahr-tor abru heh ne' na' wuh wu wak fa' au ti ne'; tonk'peh, lu au did t'forti ti himself ne', au tevan-tor asleep. Svi' wuh asal, au vesh' abru betimes, heh went zehik tor ish-veh wu-ku-san heh tor ar'kadan. Fi' nash dahr gad, mr. Lorry saluted ish-veh cheerfully k' ish-veh ahm, heh stariben tor ish-veh fi' ong ik had vesh' t' tab-ma familiar tor au. Au fun-tor rai kilko, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' evident ik au puzhu-tor ra vesh' leralmin-tor, heh ik au nahp pa' ish-veh, however confusedly. Nash kastorau mr. Lorry ki' din-tor pross svi' k' ish-veh ar'kadan, several wak du' wuh gad; na' eifa wak, au quietly stariben t' lucie, heh t' ish-veh sa-mekh yi la', precisely svi' wuh tsuri manner, heh u' kuv tra' vesh' nothing amiss. Nash vesh' ovsoh rik' sovek demonstrative accompaniment, ri wu hiyet, il k'ashiv hiyet tor smertau ish-veh; heh ish-veh lightened mr. Lorry's friendly khaf-spol tor dva-tor ik au glazhau abru oftener, heh ik au saudau tor nam-tor stirred k' ein pakashogaya t' inconsistencies surrounding ish-veh. Lu ish-veh tevan-tor gu'gelik va'ashiv, mr. Lorry ya'akash ish-veh u' fa': "tal-kam hassu, dungi du hal-tor si'?" u' fa', au ashiv-tor, "si'?" "ha; na' wuh lates k' me. Po ri?" nash wak, mr. Lorry vup-tor tor hal-tor si' lu au kupi saseshak rai kilko-srashiv s' ish-veh, heh, po' remaining tadek-adir na' wuh wadan, fun-tor. Svi' wuh meanwhile, wuh hassu had snem-tor tor wuh ku-san svi' wuh krani, heh had hayal-tor tra' looking ne' na' wuh sov-hali-lap; tonk'peh, fi' mr. Lorry's fun, au trel-tor maf tor ish-veh wu-ku-san. Wuh wak went maut slowly fi', heh mr. Lorry's rok mu'glau, heh ish-veh khaf-spol grew heavier va'ashiv, heh grew wi heavier heh heavier kanok gad. Wuh wuh gad sarlah heh went, wuh fourth, wuh fifth. Kaukuh gad, shehkuh gad, stehkuh gad, ohkuh gad, naukuh gad. K' wuh rok ek'wak darkening, heh k' wuh khaf-spol kwon-hau-ov growing heavier heh heavier, mr. Lorry be' dvun-tor k'fai nash anxious wak. Wuh tsat vesh' muhl potau, heh lucie vesh' unconscious heh kunli; tonk'peh au kupi ri vravshau tor glantau ik wuh shoemaker, t'vi el'ru had vesh' wuh pi' si' palikauk, vesh' growing dreadfully skilful, heh ik au had worla vesh' ni intent fi' ish-veh ar'kadan, heh ik ish-veh el'ru had worla vesh' ni nimble heh hiyasu, u' svi' wuh dusk t' wuh ninth khru. Chapter xix. Wuh opinion worn si' k' anxious watching, mr. Lorry tevan-tor asleep na' ish-veh lehk. Fi' wuh tenth asal t' ish-veh suspense, au vesh' startled k' wuh shining t' wuh yel vi' wuh tvi-shal wilat wuh ras slumber had overtaken ish-veh lu ish-veh vesh' gu'gelik mu-yor. Au tetau ish-veh bezhun heh kastorilau himself; tonk'peh au vet-tor, lu au had ovsoh ni, whether au vesh' ri fam dvun asleep. Na', going tor wuh svep t' wuh hassu's tvi-shal heh looking svi', au pakashogau ik wuh shoemaker's wu-ku-san heh raul vesh' shitau aside va'ashiv, heh ik wuh hassu himself hayal-tor telvan na' wuh krani. Au vesh' svi' ish-veh tsuri asal sai-vel, heh ish-veh limuk (if mr. Lorry kupi distinctly gla-tor), hi fam dvun maut spoh, vesh' calmly studious heh whio'naks. Kauk lu au had satisfied himself ik au vesh' kum'i, mr. Lorry olau giddily uncertain na' ein zamu moments whether wuh tab-ma shoemaking lau ri nam-tor wuh ertau sahr-tor t' ish-veh sha'; na', did ri ish-veh bezhun gluvaya ish-veh ish-veh t'hy'la fa' ish-veh svi' ish-veh accustomed sai-vel heh pulva, heh employed u' tsuri; heh vesh' tra' sovek glat k'svi ish-veh eik'es, ik wuh rubah t' if au had ni karik wuh impression had actually pavesh-tor? Ish-veh vesh' tonk'peh wuh inquiry t' ish-veh wuh'rak confusion heh astonishment, wuh kilko-srashiv hasu obvious. Kuv wuh impression vesh' ri torvau k' wuh yeht corresponding heh sufficient aishan, uf sarlah au, jarvis lorry, tra'? Uf sarlah au ki' tevan-tor asleep, svi' ish-veh sai-vel, fi' wuh ku-san svi' hassu manette's consulting-tvi-shal, heh tor nam-tor debating aifa sfekau s'udish wuh hassu's shi'yuk svep svi' wuh lehkuh-mal asal? K'svi wuh zamu minutes, din-tor pross lam-tor zhalan na' ish-veh vla. Kuv au had had sovek pi'gal t' vet losrak, ish-veh variben would t' bolayek ma resolved ish-veh; tonk'peh au vesh' k' ik wak pa'shik-headed, heh had rim. Au na'shikhau ik au dang kal-tor wuh wak hal-tor k' abi' wuh regular asal-yem-wadan, heh dang yi ragel-tor wuh hassu u' kuv nothing ritsuri had paresh-tor. Kuv au saudau tor nam-tor svi' ish-veh customary fupa s' t' kashek, mr. Lorry would yi cautiously proceed tor seek kharat heh guidance s' wuh opinion au had vesh', svi' ish-veh anxiety, ni anxious tor prah. Din-tor pross, submitting herself tor ish-veh judgment, wuh scheme vesh' ar'kada si' k' tun. Having mau-yan t' wak na' ish-veh tsuri methodical toilette, mr. Lorry presented himself na' wuh asal-yem-wadan svi' ish-veh tsuri wan-kur linen, heh k' ish-veh tsuri pu mal. Wuh hassu vesh' summoned svi' wuh tsuri yut, heh sarlah tor asal-yem. Ni irak u' ish-veh vesh' tor-yehat tor comprehend ish-veh rik' overstepping eifa delicate heh gradual betau if mr. Lorry olau tor nam-tor wuh goh safe storilaya, au palikauk supposed ik ish-veh ko-fu's kal'i'farr had taken shi za-gad. Wuh incidental allusion, purposely lehm-tor si', tor wuh gad t' wuh wehk gad, heh wuh gad t' wuh tevun-krus, eku ish-veh thinking heh counting, heh evidently tor ish-veh uneasy. Svi' ek' vath respects, however, au vesh' ni composedly himself, ik mr. Lorry satalau ki' wuh mamuk au sought. Heh ik mamuk vesh' ish-veh sha'. Therefore, lu wuh asal-yem vesh' ovsoh heh pa'shu maf, heh au heh wuh hassu vesh' losrak teretuhr, mr. Lorry leralmin-tor, feelingly: "t'nash-veh tal-kam manette, i am anxious ki' ish-veh opinion, svi' guhl'es, fi' wuh maut curious nuf svi' if i am deeply interested; ik nam-tor tor leralmin, ish-veh nam-tor maut curious tor me; sos'eh, tor ish-veh weh-rom ro'fori ish-veh lau nam-tor lehkuh ni." glancing na' ish-veh el'ru, if vesh' discoloured k' ish-veh tab-ma ar'kadan, wuh hassu glazhau troubled, heh shroi attentively. Au had already glanced na' ish-veh el'ru weht do wuh'wak. "hassu manette, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, touching ish-veh affectionately fi' wuh kar, "wuh nuf nam-tor wuh nuf t' wuh wa' tal-kam t'hy'la t' t'nash-veh. Pray mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh kashek tor ish-veh, heh na'shikhau me muhl na' ish-veh sake--heh abru' ek', na' ish-veh ko-fu's--ish-veh ko-fu's, t'nash-veh tal-kam manette." "kuv i ken-tor, " leralmin-tor wuh hassu, svi' wuh nessau molu, "ein mental kolaya--?" "ha!" "nam-tor explicit, " leralmin-tor wuh hassu. "spare rai detail." mr. Lorry gla-tor ik au ken-tor veh wuh'ashiv, heh proceeded. "t'nash-veh tal-kam manette, ish-veh nam-tor wuh nuf t' wuh hinek heh wuh prolonged kolaya, t' lo'uk acuteness heh severity tor wuh affections, wuh feelings, wuh--wuh--u' du sagluvau ish-veh--wuh kashek. Wuh kashek. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh nuf t' wuh kolaya ne' if wuh sufferer vesh' borne ne', veh fam yehat leralmin na' uf wu, fai'ei i dva-tor au fam yehat ka'pra wuh wak himself, heh tra' nam-tor rai vath tvai t' getting na' ish-veh. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh nuf t' wuh kolaya s' if wuh sufferer recovered, k' wuh torek ik au fam yehat zavikau himself--u' i wuh'wak puzhu-tor ish-veh publicly relate svi' wuh striking manner. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh nuf t' wuh kolaya s' if au has recovered, ni completely, u' tor nam-tor wuh highly kash-tok sasu, capable t' ikap-tor application t' kashek, heh lo'uk pideshan t' ak'shem, heh t' constantly tor sluk haya tor ish-veh fek t' fai-tukh, if vesh' already maut suk. Tonk'peh, unfortunately, tra' has vesh', " au svizh-tor heh nem-tor wuh glu esh--"wuh slight relapse." wuh hassu, svi' wuh neik spes, ya'akash, "t' uf wu duration?" "naukuh gad heh mu-yor." "uf did ish-veh gluvaya itself? I infer, " glancing na' ish-veh el'ru va'ashiv, "svi' wuh resumption t' ein hinek pursuit tersau k' wuh kolaya?" "ik nam-tor wuh kla-min." "i', did du ek'wak gla-tor ish-veh, " ya'akash wuh hassu, distinctly heh collectedly, hi svi' wuh ka neik spes, "engaged svi' ik pursuit originally?" "wuh'wak." "heh lu wuh relapse tevan-tor fi' ish-veh, vesh' au svi' danik respects--il svi' ek' respects--u' au vesh' yi?" "i nah-tor svi' ek' respects." "du stariben t' ish-veh ko-fu. Tor ish-veh ko-fu fai-tor t' wuh relapse?" "rai. Ish-veh has vesh' potau s' ish-veh, heh i rok dungi kwon-hau-ov nam-tor potau s' ish-veh. Ish-veh nam-tor fainu goh tor myself, heh tor veh vath vi lau nam-tor trusted." wuh hassu ruskarau ish-veh el'ru, heh murmured, "ik vesh' maut ves. Ik vesh' maut thoughtful!" mr. Lorry ruskarau ish-veh el'ru svi' fun, heh neither t' wuh dahkuh stariben na' wuh pi' du'. "i', t'nash-veh tal-kam manette, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, na' wu-vath, svi' ish-veh danik considerate heh danik affectionate yut, "i am wuh mere sasu t' business, heh unfit tor cope k' such intricate heh rihagik tukh. I ri tor ma wuh ves t' ro'fori bolayatik; i ri tor ma wuh ves t' kash-tor'es; i aitlun guiding. Tra' nam-tor rai sasu svi' nash panu fi' ik i kupi ni rely na' gas'rak guidance, u' fi' du. Var-tor me, uf tor nash relapse sarlah pa'? Nam-tor tra' tehvar t' wuh'ashiv? Kupi wuh repetition t' ish-veh nam-tor prevented? Uf dang wuh repetition t' ish-veh nam-tor skasau? Uf tor ish-veh sarlah pa' na' ek'? Ra mokuhlek i tor na' t'nash-veh t'hy'la? Rai sasu ek'wak mokuhlek ma vesh' weht desirous svi' ish-veh khaf-spol tor dvin-tor wuh t'hy'la, do i am tor dvin-tor t'nash-veh, kuv i fai-tor uf. "tonk'peh i ri tor fai-tor uf tor tveshulau, svi' such wuh nuf. Kuv ish-veh sagacity, fai-tukh, heh veshtaya, kupi shitau me fi' wuh gas'rak yut, i lau nam-tor kup tor tor ni mau; unenlightened heh undirected, i mokuhlek tor ni pi'. Pray discuss ish-veh k' me; pray enable me tor gla-tor ish-veh wuh pi' weht clearly, heh saven-tor me uf tor nam-tor wuh pi' weht useful." hassu manette hayal-tor kohlan po' aifa earnest zhit vesh' spoken, heh mr. Lorry did ri hish-tor ish-veh. "i nah-tor ish-veh yesik, " leralmin-tor wuh hassu, breaking silence k' wuh urgam, "ik wuh relapse du ma kethelvau, t'nash-veh tal-kam t'hy'la, vesh' ri ved unforeseen k' its subject." "vesh' ish-veh dreaded k' ish-veh?" mr. Lorry ventured tor ya'akash. "maut mau." au leralmin-tor ish-veh k' wuh shatipik ak'shem-hutau. "du ma rai idea uf such wuh apprehension rasathau fi' wuh sufferer's kashek, heh uf rihagik--uf siyah impossible--ish-veh nam-tor, na' ish-veh tor nekwitaya himself tor utter wuh zhit fi-tor wuh ong ik oppresses ish-veh." "would au, " ya'akash mr. Lorry, "nam-tor sensibly vas-tor kuv au kupi fakovau fi-tor himself tor impart ik tsat brooding tor sovek veh, lu ish-veh nam-tor fi' ish-veh?" "i nah-tor ni. Tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor, u' i ma var-tor du, nam-tor' impossible. I kauk dva-tor ish-veh--svi' ein nuf--tor nam-tor ved impossible." "i', " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, kogavik laying ish-veh el'ru fi' wuh hassu's kar va'ashiv, po' wuh pen silence fi' fi' vla, "tor ra would du dzhinau nash nashiv-tor?" "i dva-tor, " fun-tor hassu manette, "ik tra' had vesh' wuh karik heh wehtsuri revival t' wuh ranau t' nahp heh remembrance ik vesh' wuh wuh'rak aishan t' wuh malady. Ein intense katravek t' wuh danik distressing malat vesh' vividly recalled, i nah-tor. Ish-veh nam-tor yesik ik tra' had wu vesh' wuh dread lurking svi' ish-veh kashek, ik eifa katravek would nam-tor recalled--leralmin, ne' ac'ruth circumstances--leralmin, fi' wuh particular occasion. Au ar'kada tor dator himself svi' vain; sos'eh wuh urgam tor dator himself tor ish-veh lehkuh kup tor lesh ish-veh." "would au vokau ra nem-tor shi svi' wuh relapse?" ya'akash mr. Lorry, k' malatik vaunah. Wuh hassu glazhau desolately pauk wuh tvi-shal, hutau ish-veh patam, heh kilko-tor, svi' wuh neik spes, "mokov." "i', u' tor wuh fa-wak, " hinted mr. Lorry. "u' tor wuh fa-wak, " leralmin-tor wuh hassu, recovering firmness, "i dang ma lo'uk rok. U' ish-veh sanoi sha-ka-ri svi' its mercy tor restore ish-veh ni ak, i dang ma lo'uk rok. Au, yielding ne' wuh ne'hish t' wuh i'sait vel, wu dreaded heh wu vaguely fa-glan-tor heh contended tehnat, heh recovering po' wuh wan had thorau heh be' dvun-tor, i dang rok ik wuh rasahkos vesh' abru'." "muhl, muhl! Ik's rom comfort. I am itar-bosh!" leralmin-tor mr. Lorry. "i am itar-bosh!" ashiv-tor wuh hassu, bending ish-veh patam k' reverence. "tra' nam-tor dahkuh vath sfekau, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, "fi' if i am anxious tor nam-tor instructed. I lau hal-tor fi'?" "du fam yehat tor ish-veh t'hy'la wuh weh-rom dvin." wuh hassu mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ish-veh el'ru. "tor wuh wuh'rak, yi. Au nam-tor t' wuh studious es'merka, heh unusually energetic; au applies himself k' lo'uk ardour tor wuh prai t' professional fai-tukh, tor wuh conducting t' spolek, tor wehk vel. I', tor au tor nuh' mau?" "i nah-tor ri. Ish-veh lau nam-tor wuh character t' ish-veh kashek, tor nam-tor kwon-hau-ov svi' singular bolaya t' occupation. Ik lau nam-tor, svi' krus, malatik tor ish-veh; svi' krus, wuh result t' affliction. Wuh lehkuh ish-veh vesh' occupied k' muhl-bosh vel, wuh weht ish-veh would nam-tor svi' tehvar t' turning svi' wuh unhealthy kharat. Au lau ma glantau himself, heh tor wuh discovery." "du nam-tor sure ik au nam-tor ri ne' nuh' lo'uk wuh ish-veh?" "i nah-tor i am ved sure t' ish-veh." "t'nash-veh tal-kam manette, kuv au vesh' overworked i'--" "t'nash-veh tal-kam lorry, i vet kuv ik kupi easily nam-tor. Tra' has vesh' wuh khrashik hishel svi' veh kharat, heh ish-veh bolau wuh counterweight." "tobeg me, u' wuh persistent sasu t' business. Assuming na' wuh moment, ik au vesh' overworked; ish-veh would gluvaya itself svi' ein renewal t' nash disorder?" "i ri tor nah-tor ni. I ri tor nah-tor, " leralmin-tor hassu manette k' wuh firmness t' shal-conviction, "ik sovek-vel tonk'peh wuh veh ranau t' katravek would uzhau ish-veh. I nah-tor ik, henceforth, nothing tonk'peh ein wehtsuri jarring t' ik chord kupi uzhau ish-veh. Po' ra has pavesh-tor, heh po' ish-veh recovery, i talal ish-veh rihagik tor glenonau sovek such khrashik sounding t' ik string va'ashiv. I sahrafel, heh i siyah dva-tor, ik wuh circumstances kesik tor uzhau ish-veh nam-tor saguhsh-tor." au stariben k' wuh diffidence t' wuh sasu vi fai-tor uf slight wuh vel would overset wuh delicate organisation t' wuh kashek, heh wi k' wuh guhl'es t' wuh sasu vi had slowly skil-tor ish-veh assurance s' personal palesh heh flakosh. Ish-veh vesh' ri na' ish-veh t'hy'la tor abate ik guhl'es. Au professed himself weht vas-tor heh kastorau do au really vesh', heh betau ish-veh dahr heh kim-shah sfek. Au olau ish-veh tor nam-tor wuh danik rihagik t' ek'; tonk'peh, remembering ish-veh hinek gad asal conversation k' din-tor pross, heh remembering ra au had gla-tor svi' wuh kim-shah naukuh gad, au fai-tor ik au bolau limuk ish-veh. "wuh occupation resumed ne' wuh vi-yumuk t' nash be' dvun-tor affliction ni kunling recovered s', " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, clearing ish-veh drahk, "etek dungi vutau--shek-zhuksu's ar'kadan, shek-zhuksu's ar'kadan. Etek dungi leralmin, tor shitau wuh nuf heh na' wuh sake t' illustration, ik au had vesh' nam-tor-tor, svi' ish-veh rasahkos wak, tor ar'kadan na' wuh pi' zhuk-fasek. Etek dungi leralmin ik au vesh' unexpectedly afer-tor na' ish-veh zhuk-fasek va'ashiv. Nam-tor ish-veh ri wuh pity ik au dang potau ish-veh k' ish-veh?" wuh hassu duvek-tor ish-veh fa-patam k' ish-veh el'ru, heh kuhsh-tor ish-veh ash'ya nervously fi' wuh solektra. "au has kwon-hau-ov potau ish-veh k' ish-veh, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, k' wuh anxious glazhau na' ish-veh t'hy'la. "i', would ish-veh ri nam-tor weh-rom ik au dang kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor?" fam dvun, wuh hassu, k' duvek-tor fa-patam, kuhsh-tor ish-veh ash'ya nervously fi' wuh solektra. "du ri tor talal ish-veh hagik tor na'shikhau me?" leralmin-tor mr. Lorry. "i ved ken-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor wuh nice deshker. Heh wi i nah-tor--" heh tra' au hutau ish-veh patam, heh pehkau. "gla-tor du, " leralmin-tor hassu manette, turning tor ish-veh po' wuh uneasy svizh, "ish-veh nam-tor maut lerash tor danau, consistently, wuh innermost workings t' nash ri donku-tor sasu's kashek. Au wuh'wak yearned ni frightfully na' ik occupation, heh ish-veh vesh' ni welcome lu sarlah ish-veh; rai vet ish-veh vas-tor ish-veh kusut ni mau, k' substituting wuh perplexity t' wuh ozh na' wuh perplexity t' wuh shi'nahp, heh k' substituting, u' au became weht practised, wuh ingenuity t' wuh el'ru, na' wuh ingenuity t' wuh mental torture; ik au has worla vesh' kup tor lesh wuh nahp t' putting ish-veh ved s' ish-veh pulau. Kauk i', lu i dva-tor au nam-tor weht hopeful t' himself do au has ek'wak vesh', heh kauk stariben t' himself k' wuh ves t' guhl'es, wuh idea ik au lau bolaya ik hinek employment, heh ri talal ish-veh, mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh sudden kash-ral t' vash, spo' ik if veh lau fancy kwul-tor tor wuh khaf-spol t' wuh pakik kan." au glazhau spo' ish-veh illustration, u' au ashenau ish-veh bezhun tor mr. Lorry's limuk. "tonk'peh lau ri--kashek! I ya'akash na' ro'fori, u' wuh plodding sasu t' business vi goh deals k' such tukh vel u' guineas, shillings, heh kutra-pitoh--lau ri wuh retention t' wuh vel involve wuh retention t' wuh idea? Kuv wuh vel vesh' hal-tor, t'nash-veh tal-kam manette, lau ri wuh pthak hal-tor k' ish-veh? Svi' pen, nam-tor ish-veh ri wuh concession tor wuh misgiving, tor potau wuh zhuk-fasek?" tra' vesh' wuh'ashiv silence. "gla-tor du, nuh', " leralmin-tor wuh hassu, tremulously, "ish-veh nam-tor such wuh hinek besu." "i would ri potau ish-veh, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, shaking ish-veh patam; na' au nazh-tor svi' firmness u' gla-tor ish-veh wuh hassu disquieted. "i would recommend ish-veh tor sacrifice ish-veh. I goh aitlun ish-veh ek'te'kru. I am sure ish-veh tor rai rom. Sarlah! Mazhiv-kur-tor me ish-veh ek'te'kru, spo' wuh tal-kam rom sasu. Na' ish-veh ko-fu's sake, t'nash-veh tal-kam manette!" maut flekh tor gla-tor ra wuh struggle tra' vesh' k'svi ish-veh! "svi' ish-veh ahm, yi, kal-tor ish-veh nam-tor ovsoh; i sanction ish-veh. Tonk'peh, i would ri nem-tor ish-veh maf du' au vesh' la'. Kal-tor ish-veh nam-tor snem-tor lu au nam-tor ri tra'; kal-tor ish-veh din-tor ish-veh hinek besu po' wuh absence." mr. Lorry readily engaged na' ik, heh wuh conference vesh' shahtau. Au be' dvun-tor wuh gad svi' wuh shasol, heh wuh hassu vesh' ved restored. Fi' wuh rehkuh zahalik gad au hafau perfectly muhl, heh fi' wuh fourteenth gad au went maf tor hau lucie heh ish-veh sa-telsu. Wuh precaution ik had vesh' taken tor khrosahp na' ish-veh silence, mr. Lorry had previously danau tor ish-veh, heh au had written tor lucie svi' accordance k' ish-veh, heh she had rai suspicions. Fi' wuh mu-yor t' wuh gad fi' if au losrak wuh kelek, mr. Lorry went vi' ish-veh tvi-shal k' wuh chopper, gla-tor, chisel, heh mah-vel, attended k' din-tor pross carrying wuh ta'hal. Tra', k' a'ing svep, heh svi' wuh mysterious heh guilty manner, mr. Lorry hacked wuh shoemaker's wu-ku-san tor krus, du' din-tor pross meskarau wuh ha'fek u' kuv she vesh' assisting na' wuh riyeht-staya--na' if, indeed, svi' ish-veh grimness, she vesh' rai unsuitable khlop. Wuh yontau t' wuh ak'shem (previously netakidau tor krus convenient na' wuh lof) vesh' palikau rik' vohtaya svi' wuh af'tum yon; heh wuh raul, ash'el, heh duf, vesh' visolektau svi' wuh bah-ker. Ni wicked tor vashaya heh secrecy saudau tor trau kashkau, ik mr. Lorry heh din-tor pross, du' engaged svi' wuh kadvin t' ish-veh deed heh svi' wuh removal t' its zavikau, siyah olau, heh siyah glazhau, spo' accomplices svi' wuh horrible tr'y'kak. Chapter xx. Wuh plea lu wuh newly-telik shif sarlah ha-kel, wuh wuh'rak person vi saudau, tor nufai ish-veh congratulations, vesh' sydney carton. Au had ri vesh' na' ha-kel wehk wadan, lu au presented himself. Au vesh' ri improved svi' es'merka, il svi' glazhau, il svi' manner; tonk'peh tra' vesh' wuh ac'ruth rugged sov t' fidelity pa' ish-veh, if vesh' uzh tor wuh glantaya t' charles darnay. Au glantau ish-veh opportunity t' taking darnay aside vi' wuh krani, heh t' speaking tor ish-veh lu kling overheard. "mr. Darnay, " leralmin-tor carton, "i istaya etek lau nam-tor t'hylara." "etek nam-tor already t'hylara, i rok." "du nam-tor rom hiyet tor leralmin ni, u' wuh fashion t' starun; tonk'peh, i ri tor tvai sovek fashion t' starun. Indeed, lu i leralmin i istaya etek lau nam-tor t'hylara, i scarcely tvai ved ik, either." charles darnay--u' vesh' malatik--ya'akash ish-veh, svi' ek' rom-humour heh rom-fellowship, ra au did tvai? "fi-tor t'nash-veh ha'kiv, " leralmin-tor carton, smiling, "i talal ik easier tor comprehend svi' t'nash-veh sha' kashek, do tor zhelesh tor ish-veh. However, kal-tor me ar'kadan. Du vokau wuh ac'ruth khinik occasion lu i vesh' weht mon-tor do--do tsuri?" "i vokau wuh ac'ruth khinik occasion lu du punekwitau me tor confess ik du had vesh' drinking." "i vokau ish-veh nuh'. Wuh curse t' eifa occasions nam-tor ras fi-tor me, na' i kwon-hau-ov vokau au. I rok ish-veh lau nam-tor taken vi' khrosahp veh gad, lu ek' gad nam-tor na' wuh shaht na' me! Ri tor nam-tor alarmed; i am ri going tor preach." "i am mokov alarmed. Earnestness svi' du, nam-tor sovek-vel tonk'peh alarming tor me." "ah!" leralmin-tor carton, k' wuh careless pral t' ish-veh el'ru, u' kuv au pral-tor ik maf. "fi' wuh drunken occasion svi' deshker (veh t' wuh suk su'etek, u' du fai-tor), i vesh' insufferable pa' liking du, heh ri liking du. I istaya du would yen-tor ish-veh." "i forgot ish-veh wu ago." "fashion t' starun va'ashiv! Tonk'peh, mr. Darnay, oblivion nam-tor ri ni hagik tor me, u' du represent ish-veh tor nam-tor tor du. I ma k' rai tvai yen-tor ish-veh, heh wuh ta'hal kilko-srashiv tor ri gol'nev me tor yen-tor ish-veh." "kuv ish-veh vesh' wuh ta'hal kilko-srashiv, " fun-tor darnay, "i eit'jae ish-veh thrap-fam'es nufau na' ish-veh. I had rai vath vel do tor da-tor wuh slight vel, if, tor t'nash-veh ak'wikmun, seems tor trouble du nuh' mau, aside. I afsakau tor du, fi' wuh odva t' wuh gentleman, ik i ma wu dismissed ish-veh s' t'nash-veh kashek. Rom sha-ka-ri, ra vesh' tra' tor dismiss! Ma i had nothing weht yauluhk tor vokau, svi' wuh lo'uk dvin du rendered me ik gad?" "u' tor wuh lo'uk dvin, " leralmin-tor carton, "i am bound tor avow tor du, lu du stariben t' ish-veh svi' ik yut, ik ish-veh vesh' mere professional claptrap, i ri tor fai-tor ik i tun-tor ra became t' du, lu i rendered ish-veh.--kashek! I leralmin lu i rendered ish-veh; i am speaking t' wuh vesht." "du tor ta'hal t' wuh obligation, " fun-tor darnay, "tonk'peh i dungi ri quarrel k' ish-veh ta'hal kilko-srashiv." "genuine yeht'es, mr. Darnay, sahrafel me! I ma hal-tor si' t'nash-veh lof; i vesh' speaking pa' etwel hasu t'hylara. I', du fai-tor me; du fai-tor i am incapable t' ek' wuh higher heh weh-rom hash t' sasu. Kuv du vet ish-veh, ya'akash stryver, heh au'll var-tor du ni." "i prefer tor shid t'nash-veh sha' opinion, rik' wuh mamuk t' ish-veh." "muhl! Na' sovek tav du fai-tor me u' wuh dissolute dog, vi has worla ovsoh sovek rom, heh worla dungi." "i ri tor fai-tor ik du 'worla dungi.'" "tonk'peh i tor, heh du bolau nem-tor t'nash-veh zhit na' ish-veh. Muhl! Kuv du kupi palesh-tor ki' such wuh worthless katravahsu, heh wuh katravahsu t' such indifferent reputation, coming heh going na' shaik wak, i dang ya'akash ik i lau nam-tor permitted tor sarlah heh hal-tor u' wuh privileged person la'; ik i lau nam-tor fudau u' wuh nam-tor-fam (heh i would hau, kuv ish-veh vesh' ri na' wuh resemblance i patal-tor svi' du heh me, wuh unornamental) krus t' furniture, wivelau na' its hinek dvin, heh taken rai beglanau t'. I vet kuv i dang abuse wuh permission. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh hundred tor veh kuv i dang avail myself t' ish-veh kehkuh wak svi' wuh tevun. Ish-veh would satisfy me, i dare leralmin, tor fai-tor ik i had ish-veh." "dungi du ar'kadan?" "ik nam-tor wuh'ashiv yut t' taran ik i am shitau fi' wuh footing i ma indicated. I nemaiyo, darnay. I lau nam-tor-tor ik el'es k' ish-veh ahm?" "i nah-tor ni, carton, k' nash wak." au hutau el'ru fi-tor ish-veh, heh sydney da-tor maf. K'svi wuh minute afterwards, au vesh', tor ek' outward appearance, u' unsubstantial u' ek'wak. Lu au vesh' hal-tor, heh svi' wuh rivak t' wuh khru be' dvun-tor k' din-tor pross, wuh hassu, heh mr. Lorry, charles darnay tor ein mention t' nash conversation svi' paik zhil, heh stariben t' sydney carton u' wuh wat t' carelessness heh recklessness. Au stariben t' ish-veh, svi' pen, ri bitterly il meaning tor lesh lerash fi-tor ish-veh, tonk'peh u' anybody lau vi gla-tor ish-veh u' au gluvau himself. Au had rai idea ik nash kupi dwell svi' wuh nahp t' ish-veh rom nu'ri ko-telsu; tonk'peh, lu au afterwards hau ish-veh svi' ish-veh sha' tvi-shal, au afer-tor ish-veh waiting na' ish-veh k' wuh hinek takov lifting t' wuh fa-patam strongly pu'ulidau. "etek nam-tor thoughtful tor-mu-yor!" leralmin-tor darnay, bestan ish-veh kar pa' ish-veh. "ha, dearest charles, " k' ish-veh el'ru fi' ish-veh thasek, heh wuh inquiring heh whio'naks sagluvaya teslau fi-tor ish-veh; "etek nam-tor rather thoughtful tor-mu-yor, na' etek ma vel fi' etwel kashek tor-mu-yor." "ra nam-tor ish-veh, t'nash-veh lucie?" "dungi du ugaya ri tor hish-tor veh deshker fi' me, kuv i eit'jae du ri tor ya'akash ish-veh?" "dungi i ugaya? Ra dungi i ri ugaya tor t'nash-veh ashaya?" ra, indeed, k' ish-veh el'ru putting aside wuh pi-maat-kur isachya s' wuh nak, heh ish-veh vath el'ru tehnat wuh khaf-spol ik kuhsh-tor na' ish-veh! "i nah-tor, charles, ri donku-tor mr. Carton nazh-tor weht consideration heh respect do du sagluvau na' ish-veh tor-mu-yor." "indeed, t'nash-veh sha'? Po ni?" "ik nam-tor ra du nam-tor ri tor ya'akash me. Tonk'peh i nah-tor--i fai-tor--au tor." "kuv du fai-tor ish-veh, ish-veh nam-tor hiyet. Ra would du ma me tor, t'nash-veh ha'kiv?" "i would ya'akash du, dearest, tor nam-tor maut generous k' ish-veh kwon-hau-ov, heh maut lenient fi' ish-veh lafot lu au nam-tor ri k'. I would ya'akash du tor dva-tor ik au has wuh khaf-spol au maut, maut seldom reveals, heh ik tra' nam-tor glu skek svi' ish-veh. T'nash-veh tal-kam, ki'gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh khafaya." "ish-veh nam-tor wuh kusut-tor haulan tor me, " leralmin-tor charles darnay, ved astounded, "ik i dang ma ovsoh ish-veh sovek riyeht. I worla nahp nash t' ish-veh." "t'nash-veh sa-telsu, ish-veh nam-tor ni. I pthak au nam-tor ri tor nam-tor reclaimed; tra' nam-tor scarcely wuh rok ik sovek-vel svi' ish-veh character il fortunes nam-tor reparable i'. Tonk'peh, i am sure ik au nam-tor capable t' rom vel, gentle vel, kauk magnanimous vel." she glazhau ni vaksurik svi' wuh purity t' ish-veh odva svi' nash pakik sasu, ik ish-veh sa-telsu kupi ma glazhau na' ish-veh u' she vesh' na' wadan. "heh, o t'nash-veh dearest ashaya!" she urged, clinging nearer tor ish-veh, laying ish-veh patam fi-tor ish-veh thasek, heh raising ish-veh bezhun tor ish-veh, "vokau uf karik etek nam-tor svi' etwel happiness, heh uf kobat au nam-tor svi' ish-veh misery!" wuh supplication estuhl ish-veh ha-kel. "i dungi kwon-hau-ov vokau ish-veh, tal-kam khaf-spol! I dungi vokau ish-veh u' wu u' i ha-tor." au keh'sei abru' wuh pi-maat-kur patam, heh shitau wuh rosy bru-lar tor ish-veh, heh hesha ish-veh svi' ish-veh kar. Kuv veh forlorn wanderer yi pacing wuh gu'gelik yut, kupi ma puzhu-tor ish-veh innocent disclosure, heh kupi ma gla-tor wuh eku-tor t' pity shok-tor maf k' ish-veh sa-telsu s' wuh mos pla-kur bezhun ni loving t' ik sa-telsu, au lau ma maf-tor tor wuh mu-yor--heh wuh zhit would ri ma parted s' ish-veh bru-lar na' wuh wuh'rak wak-- "oekon kudau ish-veh na' ish-veh slor utan'es!" chapter xxi. Echoing footsteps wuh wonderful teruk na' vava, ish-veh has vesh' remarked, ik teruk wilat wuh hassu ha-tor. Ek'wak busily kuvoran wuh pi-maat-kur og-elakh if bound ish-veh sa-telsu, heh ish-veh sa-mekh, heh herself, heh ish-veh hinek directress heh besu, svi' wuh ha'kiv t' hizhuk bliss, lucie hayal-tor svi' wuh fam dvun kelek svi' wuh tranquilly resounding teruk, listening tor wuh echoing footsteps t' tevun. Palikauk, tra' vesh' wak, hi she vesh' wuh perfectly kunli nu'ri ko-telsu, lu ish-veh ar'kadan would slowly tevan s' ish-veh el'ru, heh ish-veh bezhun would nam-tor ha'khlup-ne-tor. Na', tra' vesh' vel coming svi' wuh vava, vel ta'hal, afar ska', heh scarcely zhu-yehat wi, ik stirred ish-veh khaf-spol nuh' mau. Fluttering rok-tor heh vet-tor--rok-tor, t' wuh ashaya u' wi ri-fainu tor ish-veh: vet-tor, t' ish-veh remaining fi-tor terra, tor tizh-tor ik uzh delight--dahsau ish-veh thasek. Among wuh vava yi, tra' would arise wuh ralash t' footsteps na' ish-veh sha' lehkuh-mal shi'vukhut; heh nahp t' wuh sa-telsu vi would nam-tor losrak ni desolate, heh vi would la'tusa na' ish-veh ni mau, puv-tor tor ish-veh bezhun, heh shau spo' pral. Ik wak be' dvun-tor, heh ish-veh pi' lucie ti fi' ish-veh bosom. Yi, among wuh advancing vava, tra' vesh' wuh tread t' ish-veh tiny ash'ya heh wuh ralash t' ish-veh prattling zhit. Kal-tor greater vava resound u' au would, wuh nu'ri ko-mekh na' wuh cradle vla kupi kwon-hau-ov zhu-tor eifa coming. Sarlah au, heh wuh shady kelek vesh' ka'ug'yelik k' wuh kan's abru'teruklar-ru'lut, heh wuh ekonik t'hy'la t' kanu, tor ik svi' ish-veh trouble she had confided ish-veh, seemed tor nem-tor ish-veh kan svi' ish-veh kar, u' au nem-tor wuh kan t' hinek, heh tor ish-veh wuh sacred mak tor ish-veh. Ek'wak busily kuvoran wuh pi-maat-kur og-elakh ik bound au ek' teretuhr, pris-tor wuh dvin t' ish-veh kunli vi-yumuk k'fai wuh nalatra t' ek' ish-veh ha-tor, heh tor ish-veh predominate nowhere, lucie puzhu-tor svi' wuh vava t' tevun rim tonk'peh friendly heh soothing sounds. Ish-veh sa-telsu's ash vesh' karik heh prosperous ekhlami; ish-veh sa-mekh's pesik heh kaik. Lo, din-tor pross, svi' harness t' string, awakening wuh vava, u' wuh unruly vifalunek, wonil-zehl-yeht-tor, snorting heh pawing wuh terra ne' wuh sov-hali-lap svi' wuh bah-ker! Kauk lu tra' vesh' sounds t' sorrow among wuh shom, au vesh' ri harsh il pi-maat'rer. Kauk lu pi-maat-kur isachya, spo' ish-veh sha', ti svi' wuh pau fi' wuh trak pauk wuh worn limuk t' wuh pi' sa-kan, heh au leralmin-tor, k' wuh radiant abru'teruklar-ru'lut, "tal-kam papa heh mamma, i am maut sorry tor trasha du fi', heh tor trasha t'nash-veh takov ko-kai; tonk'peh i am puvutau, heh i bolau hal-tor!" eifa vesh' ri bezhun-masu ek' t' agony ik wetted ish-veh nu'ri ko-mekh's nak, u' wuh tam'a trashu s' ish-veh nartaya ik had vesh' entrusted tor ish-veh. Dash au heh zadau au ri. Gla-tor au t'nash-veh sa-mekh's limuk. O sa-mekh, blessed zhit! Thus, wuh rustling t' wuh ha'su's rala prah herish-tor k' wuh vath vava, heh au vesh' ri wholly t' terra, tonk'peh had svi' au ik esh t' sha-ka-ri. Spes-tevan t' wuh salan ik blew abru' wuh pi' bah-ker-braq vesh' mingled k' au isha, heh fi' vesh' zhu-yehat tor lucie, svi' wuh hushed murmur--spo' wuh eshan t' wuh belaar masutra asleep fi-tor wuh mazhivik gef--u' wuh pi' lucie, comically studious na' wuh task t' wuh asal, il sai-vel-tor wuh su-leitri na' ish-veh ko-mekh's footstool, chattered svi' wuh lahv t' wuh dahkuh kahr ik vesh' herish-tor svi' ish-veh ha'kiv. Wuh vava rarely kilko-tor tor wuh actual tread t' sydney carton. Ein ulef-dozen wak wuh tevun, na' danik, au claimed ish-veh privilege t' coming svi' uninvited, heh would hayal-tor ekhlami k'fai wuh khru, u' au had wuh'wak ovsoh k'ashiv. Au worla sarlah tra' falek-tor k' wine. Heh veh vath vel fundauik ish-veh vesh' zhal-tor svi' wuh vava, if has vesh' zhal-tor k' ek' yeht vava na' ya'shakhuv heh ya'shakhuv. Rai sasu ek'wak really ashau wuh kosu, pakik ish-veh, heh fai-tor ish-veh k' wuh blameless hi wuh unchanged kashek, lu she vesh' wuh ko-telsu heh wuh ko-mekh, tonk'peh ish-veh kanu had wuh flekh sympathy k' ish-veh--wuh instinctive delicacy t' pity na' ish-veh. Ra tok-ti ipik sensibilities nam-tor estuhl svi' such wuh nuf, rai vava var-tor; tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor ni, heh ish-veh vesh' ni la'. Carton vesh' wuh wuh'rak ri-fainusu tor ik pi' lucie meskarau si' ish-veh chubby kar, heh au potau ish-veh shi k' ish-veh u' she grew. Wuh pi' sa-kan had spoken t' ish-veh, siyah na' wuh kim-shah. "ri donku-tor carton! Shok ish-veh na' me!" mr. Stryver shouldered ish-veh yut k'fai wuh tor-gav, spo' ein lo'uk mishu forcing itself k'fai turbid masu, heh zaseshau ish-veh useful t'hy'la svi' ish-veh wake, spo' wuh masu-hali towed astern. U' wuh masu-hali ni favoured nam-tor usually svi' wuh rough plight, heh mostly ne' masu, ni, sydney had wuh flash-tor ha'kiv t' ish-veh. Tonk'peh, hagik heh karik custom, unhappily ni mau easier heh stronger svi' ish-veh do sovek stimulating kash-ral t' eshikh il disgrace, tor ish-veh wuh ha'kiv au vesh' tor ras-tukh; heh au rai weht nahp t' emerging s' ish-veh fupa s' t' lion's jackal, do sovek yeht jackal lau nam-tor supposed tor nah-tor t' rising tor nam-tor wuh lion. Stryver vesh' don-ka; had telik wuh florid kir'an k' veltra heh rehkuh sa-kan, vi had nothing wa' shining pa' au tonk'peh wuh zehik isachya t' ish-veh dumpling patam. Aifa rehkuh nu'ri gentlemen, mr. Stryver, exuding patronage t' wuh danik offensive quality s' kanok wadi-sharu, had lates-tor fa' ish-veh spo' rehkuh sheep tor wuh hizhuk teruk svi' soho, heh had nufau u' glan-sharu tor lucie's sa-telsu: delicately taran "halloa! La' nam-tor rehkuh vihk t' kap-heh-thuhk na' ish-veh matrimonial picnic, darnay!" wuh polite rejection t' wuh rehkuh vihk t' kap-heh-thuhk had ved bloated mr. Stryver k' indignation, if au afterwards da-tor tor khrosahp svi' wuh training t' wuh nu'ri gentlemen, k' directing au tor beware t' wuh pride t' beggars, spo' ik tutor-katravahsu. Au vesh' isha svi' wuh es'merka t' declaiming tor mrs. Stryver, abru' ish-veh bosh-bodied wine, fi' wuh arts mrs. Darnay had wuh'wak shitau svi' practice tor "kum" ish-veh, heh fi' wuh lerash-khush-tresahk-lerash-khush arts svi' himself, madam, if had rendered ish-veh "ri tor nam-tor kum-tor." ein t' ish-veh sa-te'kru's wu-ku-san familiars, vi vesh' occasionally parties tor wuh bosh-bodied wine heh wuh ti, tobeg-tor ish-veh na' wuh latter k' taran ik au had var-tor ish-veh ni k'ashiv, ik au pudva-tor ish-veh himself--if nam-tor surely such wuh incorrigible aggravation t' wuh originally rasahkos offence, u' tor justify sovek such offender's hasu lesh ska' tor ein suitably retired gla-tor, heh tra' geldau s' wuh yut. Aifa vesh' among wuh vava tor if lucie, sometimes pensive, sometimes amused heh laughing, shroi svi' wuh echoing teruk, abi' ish-veh pi' ko-fu vesh' shehkuh tevun hinek. Uf be' tor ish-veh khaf-spol wuh vava t' ish-veh kan's tread sarlah, heh eifa t' ish-veh sha' tal-kam sa-mekh's, kwon-hau-ov torupik heh shal-ma, heh eifa t' ish-veh tal-kam sa-telsu's, bolaya ri nam-tor var-tor. Il, uf wuh lightest vava t' ish-veh kaunshuk ha-kel, khartau k' herself k' such wuh kau-bosh heh sohkik thrift ik ish-veh vesh' weht abundant do sovek thinoi, vesh' ralash-tanaf tor ish-veh. Il, uf tra' vesh' vava ek' pa' ish-veh, slor svi' ish-veh kaluk, t' wuh wehk wak ish-veh sa-mekh had var-tor ish-veh ik au afer-tor ish-veh weht vaikau tor ish-veh telik (kuv ik kupi nam-tor) do single, heh t' wuh wehk wak ish-veh sa-telsu had leralmin-tor tor ish-veh ik rai tun-tor heh gu-vam seemed tor dahsaya ish-veh ashaya na' ish-veh il ish-veh gol'nev tor ish-veh, heh ya'akash ish-veh "ra nam-tor wuh magic tsat, t'nash-veh ashal-veh, t' ish-veh hasu kanok-vei tor ek' t' etek, u' kuv tra' vesh' goh veh t' etek, wi worla seeming tor nam-tor hurried, il tor ma nuh' mau tor tor?" tonk'peh, tra' vesh' vath vava, kwi', ik rumbled menacingly svi' wuh teruk ek' k'fai nash ret t' wak. Heh ish-veh vesh' i', pa' pi' lucie's sixth gad t'keshtan, ik au began ki' wuh awful ralash, u' t' wuh lo'uk sahriv svi' france k' wuh dreadful masutra rising. Fi' wuh mu-yor svi' mid-july, leh-teh stehkuh hundred heh oh-leh-naukuh, mr. Lorry sarlah svi' tab-ma, s' tellson's, heh hayal-tor himself ne' k' lucie heh ish-veh sa-telsu svi' wuh gu'gelik krani. Ish-veh vesh' wuh fal, kwai mu-yor, heh au vesh' ek' rehkuh reminded t' wuh hinek gad mu-yor lu au had glazhau na' wuh igen-wesh s' wuh ka shi. "i began tor nah-tor, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, pushing ish-veh khav-kur wig pla', "ik i dang ma tor be' dvun wuh mu-yor na' tellson's. Etek ma vesh' ni bosh t' business ek' gad, ik etek ma ri fainu ra tor tor wuh'rak, il if yut tor da-tor. Tra' nam-tor such wuh uneasiness svi' paris, ik etek ma actually wuh sahr-tor t' guhl'es fi-tor etek! Etwel klepovausu abru' tra', seem ri kup tor confide ish-veh veltra tor etek sahris hiyet. Tra' nam-tor positively wuh mania among ein t' au na' sending ish-veh tor england." "ik has wuh rasahkos glazhau, " leralmin-tor darnay-- "wuh rasahkos glazhau, du leralmin, t'nash-veh tal-kam darnay? Ha, tonk'peh etek ri tor fai-tor ra utvau tra' nam-tor svi' ish-veh. Sutra nam-tor ni unreasonable! Ein t' etek na' tellson's nam-tor getting hinek, heh etek really mokuhlek't nam-tor troubled s' wuh ordinary rivak rik' due occasion." "fam dvun, " leralmin-tor darnay, "du fai-tor uf gloomy heh threatening wuh igen nam-tor." "i fai-tor ik, tor nam-tor sure, " assented mr. Lorry, trying tor persuade himself ik ish-veh slor temper vesh' soured, heh ik au grumbled, "tonk'peh i am satalau tor nam-tor peevish po' t'nash-veh wu gad's botheration. Wilat nam-tor manette?" "la' au nam-tor, " leralmin-tor wuh hassu, entering wuh gu'gelik tvi-shal na' wuh moment. "i am ved glad du nam-tor na' ha-kel; na' aifa hurries heh forebodings k' if i ma vesh' vikuvau ek' gad wu, ma tor me nervous rik' utvau. Du nam-tor ri going si', i rok?" "rai; i am going tor mavau nesh-kur heh yon-kur k' du, kuv du spo', " leralmin-tor wuh hassu. "i ri tor nah-tor i tor spo', kuv i lau stariben t'nash-veh kashek. I am ri nunau tor nam-tor pitted tehnat du tor-mu-yor. Nam-tor wuh teaboard fam dvun tra', lucie? I mokuhlek't gla-tor." "veling, ish-veh has vesh' potau na' du." "itaren ye, t'nash-veh tal-kam. Wuh taluhk kan nam-tor safe svi' sar-tak?" "heh sleeping soundly." "ik's gas'rak; ek' safe heh muhl! I ri tor fai-tor po sovek-vel dang nam-tor vathru do safe heh muhl la', itaren oekon; tonk'peh i ma vesh' ni shitau si' ek' gad, heh i am ri u' nu'ri u' i vesh'! T'nash-veh theris-masu, t'nash-veh tal-kam! Itaren ye. I', sarlah heh nem-tor ish-veh shi svi' wuh da-kuv, heh kal-tor etek hayal-tor hizhuk, heh zhu-tor wuh vava pa' if du ma ish-veh wihka." "ri wuh wihka; ish-veh vesh' wuh fancy." "wuh fancy, yi, t'nash-veh kau-bosh kelek-aushfa, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, patting ish-veh el'ru. "au nam-tor maut numerous heh maut ral, hi, nam-tor au ri? Goh zhu-tor au!" headlong, mad, heh tehvar-bosh footsteps tor nekwitaya ish-veh yut vi' anybody's ha'kiv, footsteps ri easily tor sok'i va'ashiv kuv wuh'wak kurau yon-kur, wuh footsteps raging svi' osu antoine afar ska', u' wuh pi' da-kuv hayal-tor svi' wuh gu'gelik london krani. Osu antoine had vesh', ik asal, wuh vast dusky shivak t' scarecrows heaving tor heh fro, k' vakavik gleams t' ta'hal abru' wuh billowy patam, wilat pishek wun-mor heh pohshayek-tilek min-tor svi' wuh yel. Wuh tremendous roar arose s' wuh drahk t' osu antoine, heh wuh laptra t' sai-fam kar struggled svi' wuh sov spo' shrivelled khlup t' lap svi' wuh karil salan: ek' wuh ozh convulsively clutching na' kanok wun il semblance t' wuh wun ik vesh' lehm-tor abru s' wuh gluder ne', rai tukh uf irak ska'. Vi mazhiv-kur-tor au si', whence au kim-shah sarlah, wilat au began, k'fai ra agency au crookedly quivered heh hutau, nosahp na' wuh wak, abru' wuh patam t' wuh patreitan, spo' wuh ves t' igen-wesh, rai bezhun svi' wuh throng kupi ma var-tor; tonk'peh, muskets vesh' hasu sagan-tor--ni vesh' cartridges, grazhiv, heh rin'k'n, mofek t' shek-tukh heh lapan, lipau, la'ash, pikes, kanok wun ik saglakolau ingenuity kupi discover il devise. Sutra vi kupi ti meskaraya t' nothing else, eku themselves k' khafaya el'ru tor nekwitaya kov heh dok s' ish-veh shitau svi' temok. Kanok khaf-spol-gaya heh khaf-spol svi' osu antoine vesh' fi' pid-tau ish-veh heh na' pid-tau falek. Kanok living creature tra' meskarau ha'kiv u' t' rai khrosahp, heh vesh' demented k' wuh passionate readiness tor sacrifice ish-veh. U' wuh whirlpool t' boiling mashau has wuh centre sfek, ni, ek' nash raging circled pauk defarge's wine-mahr-kel, heh kanok komihn eku svi' wuh caldron had wuh tendency tor nam-tor sucked na' wuh tchef wilat defarge himself, already begrimed k' gunpowder heh wadashaya, issued zek, issued kar, kwit nash sasu pla', zaseshau nash sasu fa'rak, disarmed veh tor kar wuh'ashiv, zup-tor heh strove svi' wuh thickest t' wuh uproar. "potau be' tor me, jacques rehkuh, " maf-tor defarge; "heh tor du, jacques veh heh dahkuh, dahshauk heh shitau yourselves na' wuh patam t' u' wehk t' aifa patriots u' du mokuhlek. Wilat nam-tor t'nash-veh ko-telsu?" "eh, muhl! La' gla-tor du me!" leralmin-tor madame, tertitau u' ek'wak, tonk'peh ri knitting tor-gad. Madame's resolute gas'rak el'ru vesh' occupied k' wuh la'ash, svi' shi' wuh tsuri softer implements, heh svi' ish-veh girdle vesh' wuh el'ru-pohshayek heh wuh pi-maat'rer lipau. "wilat tor du hal-tor, t'nash-veh ko-telsu?" "i hal-tor, " leralmin-tor madame, "k' du na' la'. Du dungau gla-tor me na' wuh patam t' kosu, k'-heh-bye." "sarlah, yi!" maf-tor defarge, svi' wuh resounding spes. "patriots heh t'hylara, etek nam-tor pok! Wuh bastille!" k' wuh roar ik sounded u' kuv ek' wuh esh svi' france had vesh' kushizhau vi' wuh detested zhit, wuh living masutra she-tor, pral fi' pral, gluder fi' gluder, heh overflowed wuh kahr tor ik sfek. Vikayek-kus-vakh ringing, vluhn beating, wuh masutra raging heh thundering fi' its uzh shahov, wuh nashiv-tor began. Glu ruk-tor, dahtau drawbridge, masuk' kov temok, ohkuh lo'uk kispek, thorshun, muskets, yon heh vuzh. K'fai wuh yon heh k'fai wuh vuzh--svi' wuh yon heh svi' wuh vuzh, na' wuh masutra vishizhau ish-veh abru tehnat wuh thorshun, heh fi' wuh instant au became wuh cannonier--defarge t' wuh wine-mahr-kel ar'kada spo' wuh manful ask'ersu, dahkuh kei wadan. Glu razh, single drawbridge, masuk' kov temok, ohkuh lo'uk kispek, thorshun, muskets, yon heh vuzh. Veh drawbridge ne'! "ar'kadan, comrades ek', ar'kadan! Ar'kadan, jacques veh, jacques dahkuh, jacques leh-teh, jacques dah-leh-teh, jacques kaukuh-heh-dah-leh thousand; svi' wuh ahm t' ek' wuh ha'su il wuh e'shua--if du prefer--ar'kadan!" thus defarge t' wuh wine-mahr-kel, fam dvun na' ish-veh pohshayek, if had wu grown fal. "tor me, kosu!" maf-tor madame ish-veh ko-telsu. "ra! Etek mokuhlek stau u' muhl u' wuh sasu lu wuh shi nam-tor taken!" heh tor ish-veh, k' wuh shrill thirsty maf, vus-tor kosu variously armed, tonk'peh ek' armed kahkwa svi' avon heh revenge. Thorshun, muskets, yon heh vuzh; tonk'peh, fam dvun wuh glu razh, wuh single drawbridge, wuh masuk' kov temok, heh wuh ohkuh lo'uk kispek. Slight displacements t' wuh raging masutra, tor k' wuh tevan-tor wounded. Flashing wun, blazing torches, smoking waggonloads t' masupik terp, lerash ar'kadan na' neighbouring barricades svi' ek' kharat, shrieks, volleys, execrations, bravery rik' stint, ork smash heh rattle, heh wuh furious sounding t' wuh living masutra; tonk'peh, fam dvun wuh glu razh, heh wuh single drawbridge, heh wuh masuk' kov temok, heh wuh ohkuh lo'uk kispek, heh fam dvun defarge t' wuh wine-mahr-kel na' ish-veh pohshayek, grown doubly fal k' wuh dvin t' kehkuh kei wadan. Wuh wan-kur haifan s' k'svi wuh klomak, heh wuh parley--nash dimly perceptible k'fai wuh raging sahriv, nothing zhu-yehat svi' ish-veh--suddenly wuh masutra she-tor immeasurably wider heh higher, heh swept defarge t' wuh wine-mahr-kel abru' wuh ne-tor drawbridge, vesht wuh masuk' kov sik temok, svi' among wuh ohkuh lo'uk kispek surrendered! Ni resistless vesh' wuh nekwitaya t' wuh masutra kuvish ish-veh fi', ik kauk tor bes-tor ish-veh esh il da-tor ish-veh patam vesh' u' impracticable u' kuv au had vesh' struggling svi' wuh surf na' wuh khu'rak masutra, abi' au vesh' landed svi' wuh sik courtyard t' wuh bastille. Tra', tehnat wuh vulu t' wuh temok, au tor wuh struggle tor glazhau pa' ish-veh. Jacques rehkuh vesh' nearly na' ish-veh vla; madame defarge, fam dvun heading ein t' ish-veh kosu, vesh' visible svi' wuh tvik ir, heh ish-veh lipau vesh' svi' ish-veh el'ru. Kanok-wilat vesh' tumult, exultation, deafening heh maniacal bewilderment, astounding ralash, wi furious dumb-gluvaya. "wuh prisoners!" "wuh vipladau!" "wuh tsat nala!" "wuh instruments t' torture!" "wuh prisoners!" t' ek' aifa maf-tor, heh lehkuh thousand incoherences, "wuh prisoners!" vesh' wuh maf danik taken abru k' wuh masutra ik rushed svi', u' kuv tra' vesh' wuh ek'wak'es t' sutra, u' muhl u' t' wak heh ret. Lu wuh dan-faik billows padukau vesht, kuvish wuh prison officers k' au, heh threatening au ek' k' instant tevakh kuv sovek tsat sha-ti hafau undisclosed, defarge laid ish-veh karik el'ru fi' wuh thasek t' veh t' aifa sasu--wuh sasu k' wuh zhai-kur patam, vi had wuh lighted torch svi' ish-veh el'ru--dahshau ish-veh s' wuh shom, heh prah ish-veh svi' himself heh wuh temok. "gluvaya me wuh desh'rak kispek!" leralmin-tor defarge. "sahris!" "i dungi faithfully, " kilko-tor wuh sasu, "kuv du dungi sarlah k' me. Tonk'peh tra' nam-tor kling tra'." "ra nam-tor wuh meaning t' teh heh kaukuh, desh'rak kispek?" ya'akash defarge. "sahris!" "wuh meaning, monsieur?" "tor ish-veh tvai wuh captive, il wuh shi' captivity? Il tor du tvai ik i dungau kwul du tevik?" "stau ish-veh!" croaked jacques rehkuh, vi had sarlah ikap-tor abru. "monsieur, ish-veh nam-tor wuh nala." "gluvaya ish-veh me!" "be' dvun nash yut, yi." jacques rehkuh, k' ish-veh tsuri craving fi' ish-veh, heh evidently disappointed k' wuh dialogue taking wuh da-tor ik did ri seem tor ugaya bloodshed, meskarau k' defarge's kar u' au meskarau k' wuh turnkey's. Ish-veh rehkuh patam had vesh' ikap-tor teretuhr du' nash brief discourse, heh ish-veh had vesh' u' mau u' au kupi tor tor zhu-tor veh wuh'ashiv, kauk yi: ni tremendous vesh' wuh ralash t' wuh living masutra, svi' its irruption vi' wuh klomak, heh its inundation t' wuh kelek heh tvur heh staircases. Ek' pa' s'udish, nuh', ish-veh kuhsh-tor wuh temok k' wuh glu, hoarse roar, s' if, occasionally, ein ulik saul-tor t' tumult shau heh leaped vi' wuh sov spo' spray. K'fai gloomy vaults wilat wuh ta'hal t' gad had worla min-tor, vesht hideous svep t' gu'gelik dens heh kraisek, ne' cavernous hash t' ash-tor, heh va'ashiv abru menal rugged ascents t' kov heh dok, weht spo' pseth waterfalls do staircases, defarge, wuh turnkey, heh jacques rehkuh, punaf-tor el'ru heh kar, went k' ek' wuh threshan au kupi tor. La' heh tra', wa' palikauk, wuh inundation palikau fi' au heh swept k'; tonk'peh lu au had ovsoh descending, heh vesh' kuvoran heh climbing abru wuh kispek, au vesh' sa'awek. Hemmed svi' la' k' wuh masuk' thickness t' temok heh kesek, wuh sahriv k'svi wuh klomak heh rik' vesh' goh zhu-yehat tor au svi' wuh pasik, nessau yut, u' kuv wuh ralash s' if au had sarlah had siyah vashau ish-veh kash-ral t' khaf-spol. Wuh turnkey pehkau na' wuh neik svep, shitau wuh tal-muv svi' wuh clashing klachek, swung wuh svep slowly tu'ash, heh leralmin-tor, u' au ek' keh'sei ish-veh patam heh be' dvun-tor svi': "teh heh kaukuh, desh'rak kispek!" tra' vesh' wuh pi', heavily-grated, unglazed krani pid svi' wuh temok, k' wuh kov gluvayek fa' ish-veh, ni ik wuh igen kupi nam-tor goh gla-tor k' stooping neik heh looking abru. Tra' vesh' wuh pi' vuzh-mev, heavily barred mes', wuh zamu ash'ya k'svi. Tra' vesh' wuh tuh t' hinek kidik lapan-vitush fi' wuh hearth. Tra' vesh' wuh stool, heh pasu, heh wuh terp sar-tak. Tra' vesh' wuh kehkuh blackened temok, heh wuh zhar-tor shek-tukh mokov svi' veh t' au. "be' dvun ik torch slowly bi' aifa temok, ik i lau gla-tor au, " leralmin-tor defarge tor wuh turnkey. Wuh sasu obeyed, heh defarge zahal-tor wuh ta'hal closely k' ish-veh bezhun. "pehkaya!--glazhau la', jacques!" "wuh. M!" croaked jacques rehkuh, u' au telv-tor greedily. "alexandre manette, " leralmin-tor defarge svi' ish-veh kaluk, zahalik wuh nuhm k' ish-veh swart kehr-oth, deeply engrained k' gunpowder. "heh la' au kitau 'wuh ri donku-tor hassu.' heh ish-veh vesh' au, rik' vet, vi scratched wuh gad-besan fi' nash kov. Ra nam-tor ik svi' ish-veh el'ru? Wuh ihv-mofek? Mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh me!" au had fam dvun wuh linstock t' ish-veh pohshayek svi' ish-veh sha' el'ru. Au tor wuh sudden di'kizh t' wuh dahkuh instruments, heh turning fi' wuh worm-yokul stool heh pasu, kuhsh-tor au tor krus svi' wuh zamu salur. "meskaraya wuh ta'hal higher!" au leralmin-tor, wrathfully, tor wuh turnkey. "glazhau among eifa karf k' tun, jacques. Heh gla-tor! La' nam-tor t'nash-veh lipau, " throwing ish-veh tor ish-veh; "tres tu'ash ik sar-tak, heh psthan wuh terp. Meskaraya wuh ta'hal higher, du!" k' wuh menacing glazhau na' wuh turnkey au ukrau fi-tor wuh hearth, heh, peering abru wuh vuzh-mev, kwul-tor heh prised na' its vla k' wuh ihv-mofek, heh ar'kada na' wuh shek-tukh grating mes' ish-veh. Svi' wuh zamu minutes, ein mortar heh grazhiv sarlah dropping ne', if au averted ish-veh limuk tor nan'woi; heh svi' ish-veh, heh svi' wuh hinek lapan-vitush, heh svi' wuh treshaya svi' wuh vuzh-mev vi' if ish-veh wun had trel-tor il wrought itself, au groped k' wuh cautious esta. "nothing svi' wuh lapan, heh nothing svi' wuh terp, jacques?" "nothing." "kal-tor etek tershau au teretuhr, svi' wuh svitan t' wuh nala. Ni! Ta'hal au, du!" wuh turnkey pohshau wuh pi' tuh, if blazed pid heh fal. Stooping va'ashiv tor sasarlah na' wuh neik-arched svep, au losrak ish-veh yontau, heh retraced ish-veh yut tor wuh courtyard; seeming tor recover ish-veh kash-ral t' khaf-spol u' sarlah au ne', abi' au vesh' svi' wuh raging abrash wuh'wak weht. Au afer-tor ish-veh surging heh tossing, svi' psthan t' defarge himself. Osu antoine vesh' clamorous ki' its wine-mahr-kel keeper dan-faik svi' wuh klashausu fi-tor wuh governor vi had fosh-tor wuh bastille heh pohshaya wuh sutra. Vathru, wuh governor would ri nam-tor marched tor wuh hotel de ville na' judgment. Vathru, wuh governor would stron, heh wuh sutra's khaf (suddenly t' ein tala, po' wehk tevun t' worthlessness) nam-tor unavenged. Svi' wuh howling stukhtra t' shaukaush heh contention ik seemed tor encompass nash grim hinek officer conspicuous svi' ish-veh zhai-kur tor-pal heh yon-kur decoration, tra' vesh' tonk'peh veh ved br'xan khlop, heh ik vesh' wuh kosu's. "gla-tor, tra' nam-tor t'nash-veh sa-telsu!" she maf-tor, pointing ish-veh si'. "gla-tor defarge!" she lam-tor immovable beyik wuh grim hinek officer, heh hafau immovable beyik ish-veh; hafau immovable beyik ish-veh k'fai wuh yut, u' defarge heh wuh shom spitau ish-veh bi'; hafau immovable beyik ish-veh lu au vesh' prah be' ish-veh destination, heh began tor nam-tor kwul-tor na' s' za'; hafau immovable beyik ish-veh lu wuh wu-hohnaya sov-masu t' stabs heh salur tevan-tor ras; vesh' ni beyik ish-veh lu au eku-tor tevik ne' ish-veh, ik, suddenly animated, she shitau ish-veh ash'ya fi-tor ish-veh talu, heh k' ish-veh pi-maat'rer lipau--wu pok--hewed ska' ish-veh patam. Wuh wadan vesh' sarlah, lu osu antoine vesh' tor fitor ish-veh horrible idea t' abertau abru sasu na' ha'gelek tor gluvaya ra au kupi nam-tor heh tor. Osu antoine's khaf vesh' abru, heh wuh khaf t' tyranny heh abrukhaya k' wuh shek-tukh el'ru vesh' ne'--ne' fi' wuh ash-tor t' wuh hotel de ville wilat wuh governor's ak'shem ti--ne' fi' wuh lad t' wuh ash'el t' madame defarge wilat she had trodden fi' wuh ak'shem tor br'xan ish-veh na' mutilation. "weh-neik wuh ha'gelek yonder!" maf-tor osu antoine, po' glaring pauk na' wuh uzh tvai t' tevakh; "la' nam-tor veh t' ish-veh ask'ersu tor nam-tor losrak fi' klashausu!" wuh swinging sentinel vesh' posted, heh wuh masutra rushed fi'. Wuh masutra t' nesh-kur heh threatening mashau, heh t' vashauk upheaving t' pral tehnat pral, t'vi gluder vesh' wi unfathomed heh t'vi nekwitau vesh' wi ri-fainu. Wuh remorseless masutra t' turbulently swaying shid, spes t' vengeance, heh limuk hardened svi' wuh furnaces t' suffering abi' wuh esta t' pity kupi tor rai ulidar fi' au. Tonk'peh, svi' wuh masutra t' limuk wilat kanok kei heh furious sagluvaya vesh' svi' vivid ha'kiv, tra' vesh' dahkuh travek t' limuk--tik stehkuh svi' su'etek--ni fixedly contrasting k' wuh shom, ik worla did masutra padukau if spitau weht memorable vashau k' ish-veh. Stehkuh limuk t' prisoners, suddenly sadalau k' wuh sahriv ik had thorau ish-veh braq, vesh' lesh pid overhead: ek' pahth-tor, ek' pakik, ek' wondering heh putaurau, u' kuv wuh kim-shah gad vesh' sarlah, heh eifa vi rejoiced pa' au vesh' pakik tam'a. Vath stehkuh limuk tra' vesh', lesh higher, stehkuh tevik limuk, t'vi tevan-tor bezhun-wein heh ulef-gla-tor bezhun awaited wuh kim-shah gad. Impassive limuk, wi k' wuh suspended--ri wuh abolished--sagluvaya fi' au; limuk, rather, svi' wuh pthak-bosh svizh, u' having wi tor ashenau wuh eku-tor lids t' wuh bezhun, heh lesh toglantausu k' wuh bloodless bru-lar, "thou didst ish-veh!" stehkuh prisoners sadalau, stehkuh gory patam fi' pikes, wuh tal-muv t' wuh accursed klomak t' wuh ohkuh karik kispek, ein discovered nuhm heh vath memorials t' prisoners t' hinek wak, wu tevik t' pushau khaf-spol, --such, heh such--spo', wuh loudly echoing footsteps t' osu antoine escort k'fai wuh paris yut svi' mid-july, leh-teh stehkuh hundred heh oh-leh-naukuh. I', sha-ka-ri defeat wuh fancy t' lucie darnay, heh potau aifa ash'ya irak s' ish-veh ha'kiv! Na', au nam-tor headlong, mad, heh tehvar-bosh; heh svi' wuh tevun ni wu po' wuh breaking t' wuh cask na' defarge's wine-mahr-kel svep, au nam-tor ri easily purified lu wuh'wak kurau yon-kur. Chapter xxii. Wuh masutra fam dvun she-tor haggard osu antoine had had goh veh exultant wehk gad, svi' if tor soften ish-veh modicum t' lerash heh sfith(-) kap tor such sadvun u' au kupi, k' wuh relish t' fraternal nartau heh congratulations, lu madame defarge hayal-tor na' ish-veh tumek, u' tsuri, presiding abru' wuh klepovausu. Madame defarge sai-vel-tor rai she-tor svi' ish-veh patam, na' wuh lo'uk brotherhood t' zamasu had shetau, kauk svi' veh pen wehk gad, extremely chary t' trusting themselves tor wuh osu's mercies. Wuh ha'gelek mes' ish-veh yut had wuh portentously elastic swing k' au. Madame defarge, k' ish-veh kar hesha, hayal-tor svi' wuh asal ta'hal heh falek, contemplating wuh wine-mahr-kel heh wuh yut. Svi' fi', tra' vesh' several knots t' loungers, squalid heh miserable, tonk'peh i' k' wuh manifest kash-ral t' tepul enthroned fi' ish-veh flakosh. Wuh raggedest nightcap, awry fi' wuh wretchedest patam, had nash pi'tak-tor significance svi' ish-veh: "i fai-tor uf lerash ish-veh has grown na' me, wuh wearer t' nash, tor nenikaya ha'kiv svi' myself; tonk'peh tor du fai-tor uf hagik ish-veh has grown na' me, wuh wearer t' nash, tor vashau ha'kiv svi' du?" kanok galat sai-famik kar, ik had vesh' rik' ar'kadan fa', had nash ar'kadan kwon-hau-ov pok na' ish-veh i', ik ish-veh kupi kwul. Wuh ozh t' wuh knitting kosu vesh' vicious, k' wuh veshtaya ik au kupi bezhun-masu. Tra' vesh' wuh rubah svi' wuh appearance t' osu antoine; wuh glakuv had vesh' hammering vi' nash na' hundreds t' tevun, heh wuh kim-shah finishing salur had var-tor mightily fi' wuh sagluvaya. Madame defarge hayal-tor observing ish-veh, k' such nelau messaya u' vesh' tor nam-tor aitlu svi' wuh leader t' wuh osu antoine kosu. Veh t' ish-veh sisterhood knitted be' ish-veh. Wuh pen, rather plump ko-telsu t' wuh starved grocer, heh wuh ko-mekh t' dahkuh kanu withal, nash ot-lan had already pinkau wuh complimentary ahm t' wuh vengeance. "hark!" leralmin-tor wuh vengeance. "shroi, yi! Vi sarlah?" u' kuv wuh ranau t' grazhiv laid s' wuh outermost bound t' osu antoine yonuk tor wuh wine-mahr-kel svep, had vesh' suddenly pohshau, wuh sahris-spreading murmur sarlah rushing bi'. "ish-veh nam-tor defarge, " leralmin-tor madame. "silence, patriots!" defarge sarlah svi' breathless, seshau ska' wuh yon-kur taik au sai-vel-tor, heh glazhau pa' ish-veh! "shroi, kanok-wilat!" leralmin-tor madame va'ashiv. "shroi tor ish-veh!" defarge lam-tor, panting, tehnat wuh za-mesu t' nayik bezhun heh tu'ash ru'lut, shidau s'udish wuh svep; ek' eifa k'svi wuh wine-mahr-kel had sprung tor ish-veh ash'ya. "leralmin yi, t'nash-veh sa-telsu. Ra nam-tor ish-veh?" "ro'fori s' wuh vath panu!" "uf, yi?" maf-tor madame, contemptuously. "wuh vath panu?" "tor kanok-veh la' recall hinek foulon, vi var-tor wuh famished sutra ik au lau yokul yar, heh vi tev-tor, heh went tor bogozh?" "kanok-veh!" s' ek' drahk. "wuh ro'fori nam-tor t' ish-veh. Au nam-tor akhlami!" "akhlami!" s' wuh universal drahk va'ashiv. "heh tevik?" "ri tevik! Au ptha etek ni mau--heh k' utvau--ik au aisha himself tor nam-tor represented u' tevik, heh had wuh grand mock-mem-lu til-kum. Tonk'peh au ma afer-tor ish-veh alive, hiding svi' wuh shasol, heh ma katau ish-veh svi'. I ma gla-tor ish-veh tonk'peh i', fi' ish-veh yut tor wuh hotel de ville, wuh prisoner. I ma leralmin-tor ik au had utvau tor pthak etek. Leralmin ek'! Had au utvau?" wretched hinek sinner t' weht do threescore tevun heh lehkuh, kuv au had worla fainu ish-veh wi, au would ma fainu ish-veh svi' ish-veh khaf-spol t' khaf-spol kuv au kupi ma puzhu-tor wuh answering maf. Wuh moment t' profound silence zahal-tor. Defarge heh ish-veh ko-telsu glazhau steadfastly na' veh wuh'ashiv. Wuh vengeance stooped, heh wuh kak t' wuh vluhn vesh' puzhu-tor u' she dvun-tor ish-veh na' ish-veh ash'ya za' wuh tumek. "patriots!" leralmin-tor defarge, svi' wuh satalau spes, "nam-tor etek pok?" instantly madame defarge's lipau vesh' svi' ish-veh girdle; wuh vluhn vesh' beating svi' wuh yut, u' kuv ish-veh heh wuh drummer had flown teretuhr k' magic; heh wuh vengeance, uttering terrific shrieks, heh flinging ish-veh kar pa' ish-veh patam spo' ek' wuh keh-leh furies na' wuh'wak, vesh' tearing s' kelek tor kelek, kastorilau wuh kosu. Wuh sasu vesh' terrible, svi' wuh bloody-minded reshan k' if au glazhau s' krani, kum-tor abru ra kar au had, heh sarlah pouring ne' vi' wuh yut; tonk'peh, wuh kosu vesh' wuh glan tor chill wuh boldest. S' such household occupations u' ish-veh sai-famik poverty yielded, s' ish-veh kanu, s' ish-veh aged heh ish-veh has-bosh crouching fi' wuh sai-famik solektra famished heh sai-fam, au sahr-tor si' k' streaming isachya, urging veh wuh'ashiv, heh themselves, tor ni-resh k' wuh wildest maf-tor heh torai. Villain foulon taken, t'nash-veh ko-kai! Hinek foulon taken, t'nash-veh ko-mekh! Miscreant foulon taken, t'nash-veh ko-fu! Yi, wuh nosahp t' vath sahr-tor vi' wuh midst t' aifa, beating ish-veh thasek, tearing ish-veh isachya, heh screaming, foulon alive! Foulon vi var-tor wuh starving sutra au lau yokul yar! Foulon vi var-tor t'nash-veh hinek sa-mekh ik au lau yokul yar, lu i had rai kap tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh! Foulon vi var-tor t'nash-veh kan-bu ish-veh lau suck yar, lu aifa thasek vesh' pseth k' aitlun! O ko-mekh t' oekon, nash foulon! O sha-ka-ri etwel suffering! Zhu-tor me, t'nash-veh tevik kan-bu heh t'nash-veh withered sa-mekh: i swear fi' t'nash-veh mal-nef, fi' aifa kov, tor avenge du fi' foulon! Sa-telsu, heh sa-kai, heh nu'ri sasu, mazhiv-kur-tor etek wuh khaf t' foulon, mazhiv-kur-tor etek wuh patam t' foulon, mazhiv-kur-tor etek wuh khaf-spol t' foulon, mazhiv-kur-tor etek wuh ak'shem heh soul t' foulon, tresahk-tor foulon tor krus, heh hil-tor ish-veh vi' wuh solektra, ik yar lau tor'ovau s' ish-veh! K' aifa maf-tor, su'etek t' wuh kosu, lashed vi' glan-fam frenzy, whirled pa', striking heh tearing na' ish-veh sha' t'hylara abi' au eku-tor vi' wuh passionate swoon, heh vesh' goh korsau k' wuh sasu t' au s' hasu sahr-tor ne' ash'ya. Nevertheless, ri wuh moment vesh' pakik; ri wuh moment! Nash foulon vesh' na' wuh hotel de ville, heh lau nam-tor loosed. Worla, kuv osu antoine fai-tor ish-veh sha' sufferings, viltah, heh wrongs! Armed sasu heh kosu patreitau si' t' wuh yonuk ni sahris, heh drew kauk aifa kim-shah dregs po' au k' such wuh nekwitaya t' suction, ik k'svi wuh yonuk t' wuh wadan tra' vesh' ri wuh komihn creature svi' osu antoine's bosom tonk'peh wuh zamu hinek crones heh wuh wailing kanu. Rai. Au vesh' ek' k' ik wak choking wuh tvur t' linisaya wilat nash hinek sasu, watosh heh wicked, vesh', heh overflowing vi' wuh beyik tu'ash ret heh yut. Wuh defarges, sa-telsu heh ko-telsu, wuh vengeance, heh jacques rehkuh, vesh' svi' wuh wuh'rak hish-tor, heh na' rai lo'uk ir s' ish-veh svi' wuh tvur. "gla-tor!" maf-tor madame, pointing k' ish-veh lipau. "gla-tor wuh hinek villain bound k' man-elakh. Ik vesh' muhl ovsoh tor tie wuh bunch t' yar fi-tor ish-veh pla'. Ha, ha! Ik vesh' muhl ovsoh. Kal-tor ish-veh yokul ish-veh i'!" madame shitau ish-veh lipau ne' ish-veh kar, heh clapped ish-veh el'ru u' na' wuh mavau. Wuh sutra iyi za' madame defarge, explaining wuh aishan t' ish-veh satisfaction tor eifa za' au, heh eifa va'ashiv explaining tor vath, heh eifa tor vath, wuh neighbouring yut resounded k' wuh clapping t' el'ru. Similarly, du' dahkuh il rehkuh wadan t' drawl, heh wuh winnowing t' wehk bushels t' zhit, madame defarge's vakavik sagluvaya t' impatience vesh' taken abru, k' marvellous quickness, na' wuh ir: wuh weht readily, fai'ei ac'ruth sasu vi had k' ein wonderful tusok t' agility sasu-tor abru wuh sik te'koshif tor glazhau svi' s' wuh krani, fai-tor madame defarge muhl, heh bae'cok u' wuh telegraph svi' ish-veh heh wuh patreitan s'udish wuh kelek. Na' wu-vath wuh yel she-tor ni pid ik ish-veh kwul-tor wuh kindly ha'zehl u' t' rok il protection, directly ne' fi-tor wuh hinek prisoner's patam. Wuh favour vesh' nuh' mau tor lesh; svi' wuh instant wuh foshek t' grazhiv heh chaff ik had lam-tor surprisingly wu, went tor wuh salan, heh osu antoine had prah ish-veh! Ish-veh vesh' fainu directly, tor wuh furthest confines t' wuh patreitan. Defarge had tonk'peh sprung abru' wuh railing heh wuh pasu, heh hesha wuh miserable wretch svi' wuh tevalik nartaya--madame defarge had tonk'peh zahal-tor heh da-tor ish-veh el'ru svi' veh t' wuh man-elakh k' if au vesh' tied--wuh vengeance heh jacques rehkuh vesh' ri wi abru k' au, heh wuh sasu na' wuh krani had ri wi swooped vi' wuh tvur, spo' kushel t' shi-kar-tor s' ish-veh pid perches--lu wuh maf seemed tor hal-tor abru, ek' abru' wuh kahr, "katau ish-veh si'! Katau ish-veh tor wuh ha'gelek!" ne', heh abru, heh patam dan-faik fi' wuh ash-tor t' wuh kelek; i', fi' ish-veh mal-nef; i', fi' ish-veh ash'ya; i', fi' ish-veh pla'; zaseshau, heh kwul-tor na', heh stifled k' wuh bunches t' yar heh terp ik vesh' kwit vi' ish-veh limuk k' hundreds t' el'ru; torn, bruised, panting, khafaya, wi kwon-hau-ov entreating heh beseeching na' mercy; i' bosh t' vehement agony t' torai, k' wuh pi' pa'shik ret pa' ish-veh u' wuh sutra drew veh wuh'ashiv pla' ik au lau gla-tor; i', wuh lap-fek t' tevik lapan drawn k'fai wuh laptra t' mal; au vesh' hauled tor wuh nearest yut teruk wilat veh t' wuh fatal ha'gelek swung, heh tra' madame defarge kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor--u' wuh aushfa lau ma ovsoh tor wuh aushfa--heh silently heh composedly glazhau na' ish-veh du' au tor pok, heh du' au besought ish-veh: wuh kosu passionately screeching na' ish-veh ek' wuh wak, heh wuh sasu sternly calling si' ki' ish-veh pustau k' yar svi' ish-veh ru'lut. Wuh'wak, au went aloft, heh wuh man-elakh shau, heh au kum-tor ish-veh shrieking; dah'wak, au went aloft, heh wuh man-elakh shau, heh au kum-tor ish-veh shrieking; yi, wuh man-elakh vesh' merciful, heh meskarau ish-veh, heh ish-veh patam vesh' ak fi-tor wuh pike, k' yar hiyet svi' wuh ru'lut na' ek' osu antoine tor tam na' wuh glan t'. Il vesh' nash wuh shaht t' wuh gad's rasahkos ar'kadan, na' osu antoine ni saul-tor heh tam-tor ish-veh reshnek khaf abru, ik ish-veh kan-tor va'ashiv, fi' khaf-spol lu wuh gad a'ing svi' ik wuh sa-fu-svi'-tor-gav t' wuh despatched, wuh'ashiv t' wuh sutra's nemut heh insulters, vesh' coming vi' paris ne' wuh klashausu kaukuh hundred karik, svi' cavalry sa'awek. Osu antoine kitau ish-veh tr'y'kak fi' flaring thalv t' dun, seized ish-veh--would ma torn ish-veh s' wuh thasek t' wuh ya'akash'er tor lesh foulon apc'koik--eku ish-veh patam heh khaf-spol fi' pikes, heh lesh wuh rehkuh spoils t' wuh gad, svi' wolf-procession k'fai wuh yut. Ri fa' gu'gelik mu-yor did wuh sasu heh kosu sarlah pla' tor wuh kanu, wailing heh breadless. Yi, wuh miserable leipausu' mahr-kel vesh' beset k' wu deik-tor t' au, patiently waiting tor mahr-tor rasahkos kap; heh du' au bek-tor k' skaun-sa'haf faint heh herbosh, au beguiled wuh wak k' embracing veh wuh'ashiv fi' wuh triumphs t' wuh gad, heh achieving au va'ashiv svi' gossip. Gradually, aifa strings t' ragged sutra pen-tor heh shrau maf; heh yi ri donku-tor ha'ge began tor min-tor svi' pid krani, heh slender yon vesh' tor svi' wuh yut, na' if behsu pufas-tor svi' tsuri, afterwards supping na' ish-veh svep. Scanty heh insufficient mu'yor-yem eifa, heh innocent t' kahm, u' t' danik vath mun tor wretched kap. Wi, komihn fellowship infused ein tem-mazhiv-kur'es vi' wuh flinty viands, heh kwul-tor ein kil-tor t' cheerfulness s' au. Sa-mekh heh ko-mekh vi had had ish-veh bosh thresh svi' wuh rasahkos t' wuh gad, mavau kogavik k' ish-veh meagre kanu; heh lovers, k' such wuh panu pa' au heh fa' au, ashau heh rok-tor. Ish-veh vesh' siyah asal, lu defarge's wine-mahr-kel parted k' its kim-shah knot t' klepovausu, heh monsieur defarge leralmin-tor tor madame ish-veh ko-telsu, svi' husky molu, du' fastening wuh svep: "na' kim-shah ish-veh nam-tor sarlah, t'nash-veh tal-kam!" "eh muhl!" fun-tor madame. "siyah." osu antoine yuk-tor, wuh defarges yuk-tor: kauk wuh vengeance yuk-tor k' ish-veh starved grocer, heh wuh vluhn vesh' na' shom. Wuh vluhn's vesh' wuh goh spes svi' osu antoine ik khaf heh brax had ri rubai. Wuh vengeance, u' custodian t' wuh vluhn, kupi ma wakened ish-veh abru heh had wuh ka starun s' ish-veh u' fa' wuh bastille tevan-tor, il hinek foulon vesh' seized; ri ni k' wuh hoarse molu t' wuh sasu heh kosu svi' osu antoine's bosom. Chapter xxiii. Yon she-tor tra' vesh' wuh rubah fi' wuh pi'kahr wilat wuh mashulek tevan-tor, heh wilat wuh mender t' fau-yut went forth kanok-gadik tor mah-vel s' wuh kov fi' wuh yut such morsels t' kap u' lau dvin-tor na' patches tor meskaraya ish-veh ri donku-tor ignorant soul heh ish-veh ri donku-tor netakidau ak'shem teretuhr. Wuh prison fi' wuh crag vesh' ri ni abrupik u' t' yore; tra' vesh' ask'ersu tor klashausu ish-veh, tonk'peh ri wehk; tra' vesh' officers tor klashausu wuh ask'ersu, tonk'peh ri veh t' au fai-tor ra ish-veh sasu would tor--mesakh nash: ik ish-veh would probably ri nam-tor ra au vesh' ordered. Irak heh eik ti wuh ruined shasol, yielding nothing tonk'peh desolation. Kanok yar-kur mor, kanok wun-mor t' yar heh wun-mor t' kap-yar, vesh' u' shrivelled heh ri donku-tor u' wuh miserable sutra. Kanok-vei vesh' ovalau ne', dejected, oppressed, heh pushau. Habitations, foshek, ha'kelikau animals, sasu, kosu, kanu, heh wuh solek ik spitau au--ek' worn si'. Monseigneur (k'ashiv wuh danik worthy wuhsu gentleman) vesh' wuh national kudaya, mazhiv-kur-tor wuh chivalrous molu tor vel, vesh' wuh polite li-fal t' luxurious heh shining ha'kiv, heh wuh lo'uk deal weht tor kaik lof; nevertheless, monseigneur u' wuh mohrn had, somehow il vath, katau vel tor nash. Flekh ik fereikan, designed expressly na' monseigneur, dang nam-tor ni ak wrung pseth heh lerakhovau si'! Tra' bolau nam-tor vel pen-sighted svi' wuh ek'wakik arrangements, surely! Thus ish-veh vesh', however; heh wuh kim-shah eku t' khaf having vesh' saseshau s' wuh flints, heh wuh kim-shah wufkau t' wuh rack having vesh' da-tor ni k'ashiv ik its purchase snaipau, heh ish-veh i' da-tor heh da-tor k' nothing tor zeshaya, monseigneur began tor sahr-tor maf s' wuh stivan ni neik heh unaccountable. Tonk'peh, nash vesh' ri wuh rubah fi' wuh pi'kahr, heh fi' wehk wuh pi'kahr spo' ish-veh. Na' nosahp t' tevun hal-tor k', monseigneur had lerakhovau ish-veh heh wrung ish-veh, heh had seldom takov-tor ish-veh k' ish-veh la'es kaula na' wuh pleasures t' wuh a'vesh'--i', afer-tor svi' hunting wuh sutra; i', afer-tor svi' hunting wuh beasts, na' t'vi preservation monseigneur tor edifying ret t' barbarous heh barren shi'kwai. Rai. Wuh rubah consisted svi' wuh appearance t' flekh limuk t' neik caste, rather do svi' wuh disappearance t' wuh pid caste, chiselled, heh vathru beautified heh beautifying features t' monseigneur. Na', svi' aifa wak, u' wuh mender t' fau-yut ar'kada, solitary, svi' wuh grazhiv, ri k'ashiv troubling himself tor haul-tor ik grazhiv au vesh' heh tor grazhiv au bolau fun, hasu na' wuh danik krus nuh' mau occupied svi' thinking uf pi' au had na' mu'yor-yem heh uf mau weht au would yokul kuv au had ish-veh--svi' aifa wak, u' au ashenau ish-veh bezhun s' ish-veh lonely zup, heh zan-tor wuh prospect, au would gla-tor ein rough khlop approaching fi' ash'ya, wuh spo' t' if vesh' wuh'wak wuh rarity svi' eifa krus, tonk'peh vesh' i' wuh vakavik la'es. U' ish-veh storilau, wuh mender t' fau-yut would discern rik' ak'wikmun, ik ish-veh vesh' wuh shaggy-haired sasu, t' siyah barbarian pulva, ha-vol, svi' wooden ash'el ik vesh' om'toi kauk tor wuh bezhun t' wuh mender t' fau-yut, grim, rough, swart, steeped svi' wuh vral heh grazhiv t' wehk yut, dank k' wuh marshy masu'es t' wehk neik solektra, sprinkled k' wuh thorns heh mor heh yekuhl t' wehk byways k'fai lapan. Such wuh sasu sarlah fi-tor ish-veh, spo' wuh tam'a, na' aru svi' wuh july igen-va, u' au hayal-tor fi' ish-veh tuh t' kov ne' wuh kutra, taking such rau-nol u' au kupi prah s' wuh mashulayek t' masu-kov. Wuh sasu glazhau na' ish-veh, glazhau na' wuh pi'kahr svi' wuh hollow, na' wuh mill, heh na' wuh prison fi' wuh crag. Lu au had shasutan-tor aifa vel svi' ra benighted kashek au had, au leralmin-tor, svi' wuh dialect ik vesh' aishan intelligible: "uf hal-tor ish-veh, jacques?" "ek' muhl, jacques." "esta yi!" au hau el'ru, heh wuh sasu hayal-tor ne' fi' wuh tuh t' kov. "rai aru-yem?" "nothing tonk'peh mu'yor-yem i', " leralmin-tor wuh mender t' fau-yut, k' wuh k'avon limuk. "ish-veh nam-tor wuh fashion, " growled wuh sasu.
