"i ragel-tor rai aru-yem sovek-wilat." au nem-tor si' wuh blackened mev, boshau ish-veh, lighted ish-veh k' kil-tukh heh pishek, seshau na' ish-veh abi' ish-veh vesh' svi' wuh ugelik min: yi, suddenly meskarau ish-veh s' ish-veh heh eku-tor vel vi' ish-veh s' svi' ish-veh ozh heh kaur-ozh, ik blazed heh went si' svi' wuh puff t' vuzh. "esta yi." ish-veh vesh' wuh da-tor t' wuh mender t' fau-yut tor leralmin ish-veh nash wak, po' observing aifa el'toraya. Au va'ashiv hau el'ru. "tor-mu-yor?" leralmin-tor wuh mender t' fau-yut. "tor-mu-yor, " leralmin-tor wuh sasu, putting wuh mev svi' ish-veh ru'lut. "wilat?" "la'." au heh wuh mender t' fau-yut hayal-tor fi' wuh tuh t' kov looking silently na' veh wuh'ashiv, k' wuh masu-kov driving svi' svi' au spo' wuh pigmy falun t' pohshayek-tilek, abi' wuh igen began tor pa'shik abru' wuh pi'kahr. "gluvaya me!" leralmin-tor wuh traveller yi, dvun-tor tor wuh meix'tem t' wuh kunel. "gla-tor!" fun-tor wuh mender t' fau-yut, k' sadvun-tor ozh. "du hal-tor ne' la', heh zehik k'fai wuh yut, heh vesht wuh mashulek--" "tor wuh e'shua k' ek' ik!" svi-shau wuh vath, rolling ish-veh bezhun abru' wuh landscape. "i hal-tor k'fai rai yut heh vesht rai mashulek. Muhl?" "muhl! Pa' dahkuh leagues mesakh wuh dan-pid-sfek t' ik kunel abru' wuh pi'kahr." "rom. Lu tor du cease tor ar'kadan?" "na' tev-tor." "dungi du wake me, fa' departing? I ma lates-tor dahkuh mu-yor rik' resting. Kal-tor me shaht t'nash-veh mev, heh i dungau yuk spo' wuh kan. Dungi du wake me?" "surely." wuh wayfarer smoked ish-veh mev si', shitau ish-veh svi' ish-veh thasek, trel-tor ska' ish-veh lo'uk wooden ash'el, heh ti ne' fi' ish-veh pla' fi' wuh tuh t' kov. Au vesh' sahris asleep directly. U' wuh fau-yut-mender plied ish-veh grazhiv zup, heh wuh masu-kov-wan, rolling maf, revealed ugelik mofek heh wesh-tor t' igen if vesh' kesau tor k' haul-tukh gleams fi-tor wuh landscape, wuh pi' sasu (vi sai-vel-tor wuh yon-kur taik i', svi' shi' ish-veh pla-kur veh) seemed sem-tor k' wuh khlop fi' wuh tuh t' kov. Ish-veh bezhun vesh' ni k'ashiv da-tor na' ish-veh, ik au nam-tor-tor ish-veh raul mechanically, heh, veh would ma leralmin-tor, tor maut ri donku-tor khrosahp. Wuh krish-tukh limuk, wuh shaggy nesh-kur isachya heh hisahk, wuh dirik woollen yon-kur taik, wuh rough medley sai-vel t' ha-kel-pada-tor tukh heh hairy wadi t' beasts, wuh powerful nentu attenuated k' spare living, heh wuh kir heh desperate lerakh'es t' wuh bru-lar svi' yuk, vi'le-esh-tor wuh mender t' fau-yut k' teshan. Wuh traveller had travelled irak, heh ish-veh ash'ya vesh' footsore, heh ish-veh mal-nik chafed heh khafaya; ish-veh lo'uk ash'el, tukh-tor k' mor heh yar, had vesh' ras tor zaseshau abru' wuh wehk wu leagues, heh ish-veh sai-vel vesh' chafed vi' razh, u' au himself vesh' vi' sival. Stooping ne' be' ish-veh, wuh fau-yut-mender ar'kada tor prah wuh peep na' tsat wun svi' ish-veh thasek il wilat ri; tonk'peh, svi' vain, na' au yuk-tor k' ish-veh kar tuhsau fi-tor ish-veh, heh eku u' resolutely u' ish-veh bru-lar. Fortified kahr k' ish-veh stockades, klashausu-kelek, temep, trenches, heh drawbridges, seemed tor wuh mender t' fau-yut, tor nam-tor ni mau sov u' tehnat nash khlop. Heh lu au abertau ish-veh bezhun s' ish-veh tor wuh ir-zehl heh glazhau pa', gla-tor ish-veh svi' ish-veh pi' fancy kahwa khlop, pehkau k' rai obstacle, tending tor centres ek' abru' france. Wuh sasu yuk-tor fi', indifferent tor mashulayek t' masu-kov heh tvi-wak t' ugel'es, tor sunshine fi' ish-veh limuk heh duv, tor wuh paltering vihk t' pasik le-suma fi' ish-veh ak'shem heh wuh lerash-khush vi' if wuh yel rubai au, abi' wuh yel vesh' neik svi' wuh tev'rak, heh wuh igen vesh' glowing. Yi, wuh mender t' fau-yut having prah ish-veh raul teretuhr heh ek' vel pok tor hal-tor ne' vi' wuh pi'kahr, kastorilau ish-veh. "rom!" leralmin-tor wuh sleeper, rising fi' ish-veh kar-nef. "dahkuh leagues mesakh wuh dan-pid-sfek t' wuh kunel?" "pa'." "pa'. Rom!" wuh mender t' fau-yut went ha-kel, k' wuh grazhiv going fi' fa' ish-veh fupa s' wuh eku t' wuh salan, heh vesh' ak na' wuh mashulek, squeezing himself svi' among wuh galat kine katau tra' tor mon, heh appearing kauk tor zhal tor au svi' ish-veh zhalan tor ek' wuh pi'kahr. Lu wuh pi'kahr had taken its ri donku-tor mu'yor-yem, ish-veh did ri creep tor sar-tak, u' ish-veh usually did, tonk'peh sasarlah t' svep va'ashiv, heh hafau tra'. Wuh curious contagion t' zhalan vesh' fi-tor ish-veh, heh isha, lu ish-veh hoknau teretuhr na' wuh mashulek svi' wuh gu'gelik, wuh'ashiv curious contagion t' looking expectantly na' wuh igen svi' veh kharat goh. Monsieur gabelle, chief functionary t' wuh shi, became uneasy; went si' fi' ish-veh kelek-fik sa'awek, heh glazhau svi' ik kharat nuh'; glanced ne' s' za' ish-veh vuzh-mev na' wuh darkening limuk k' wuh mashulek ne', heh satau zhit tor wuh sacristan vi potau wuh tal-muv t' wuh church, ik tra' lau nam-tor bolaya tor mokov wuh tocsin k'-heh-bye. Wuh mu-yor deepened. Wuh lap environing wuh hinek chateau, keeping its solitary fupa s' k'wuhli, dvun-tor svi' wuh rising salan, u' hi au threatened wuh tuh t' kelek masuk' heh gu'gelik svi' wuh gloom. Abru wuh dahkuh nef hash t' ash-tor wuh sov-masu sahr-tor wildly, heh kuhsh-tor na' wuh lo'uk svep, spo' wuh swift skladasu kastorilau eifa k'svi; uneasy rushes t' salan went k'fai wuh tvur, among wuh hinek tilek heh lipau, heh be' dvun-tor lamenting abru wuh kaiden, heh hutau wuh curtains t' wuh sar-tak wilat wuh kim-shah marquis had yuk-tor. She'rak, tev'rak, desh'rak, heh khu'rak, k'fai wuh lapan, kehkuh ras-treading, unkempt khlop plesh-tor wuh pid yar heh treshau wuh khlup, striding fi' cautiously tor sarlah teretuhr svi' wuh courtyard. Kehkuh ha'ge shau si' tra', heh dvun-tor maf svi' natya kharat, heh ek' vesh' nesh-kur va'ashiv. Tonk'peh, ri na' wu. Presently, wuh chateau began tor tor itself strangely visible k' ein ta'hal t' its sha', u' hi ish-veh vesh' growing luminous. Yi, wuh flickering wesh mavau za' wuh te'koshif t' wuh khom, picking si' fnaglaik shitau, heh showing wilat balustrades, kesek, heh krani vesh'. Yi ish-veh soared higher, heh grew broader heh brighter. Ak, s' wuh nosahp t' wuh lo'uk krani, yai thorau forth, heh wuh kov limuk awakened, nantau s' yon. Wuh faint murmur arose pa' wuh kelek s' wuh zamu sutra vi vesh' losrak tra', heh tra' vesh' wuh saddling t' wuh jarel heh riding maf. Tra' vesh' spurring heh splashing k'fai wuh mu'khlup'es, heh bridle vesh' drawn svi' wuh ret k' wuh pi'kahr mashulek, heh wuh jarel svi' wuh puhsh lam-tor na' monsieur gabelle's svep. "gol'nev, gabelle! Gol'nev, kanok veh!" wuh tocsin rang impatiently, tonk'peh vath gol'nev (kuv ik vesh' sovek) tra' vesh' rim. Wuh mender t' fau-yut, heh dah-teh heh kau-leh particular t'hylara, lam-tor k' hesha kar na' wuh mashulek, looking na' wuh pillar t' yon svi' wuh igen. "ish-veh bolau nam-tor keh-leh ash'ya pid, " leralmin-tor au, grimly; heh worla dvun-tor. Wuh rider s' wuh chateau, heh wuh jarel svi' wuh puhsh, clattered maf k'fai wuh pi'kahr, heh ausahr-tor abru wuh stony menal, tor wuh prison fi' wuh crag. Na' wuh temep, wuh travek t' officers vesh' looking na' wuh yon; snem-tor s' au, wuh travek t' ask'ersu. "gol'nev, gentlemen--officers! Wuh chateau nam-tor fi' yon; taluhk vel lau nam-tor korsau s' wuh yai k' timely mamuk! Gol'nev, gol'nev!" wuh officers glazhau na' wuh ask'ersu vi glazhau na' wuh yon; mazhiv-kur-tor rai zek; heh kilko-tor, k' shrugs heh biting t' bru-lar, "ish-veh bolau yontau." u' wuh rider rattled ne' wuh kunel va'ashiv heh k'fai wuh yut, wuh pi'kahr vesh' illuminating. Wuh mender t' fau-yut, heh wuh dah-teh heh kau-leh particular t'hylara, vi'le-esh-tor u' veh sasu heh kosu k' wuh idea t' ha'gelan abru, had darted vi' ish-veh kelek, heh vesh' putting ha'fek svi' kanok pasik pi' pane t' makh. Wuh paik scarcity t' kanok-vei, occasioned ha'fek tor nam-tor yahv-tor svi' wuh rather peremptory manner t' monsieur gabelle; heh svi' wuh moment t' reluctance heh vaunah fi' ik functionary's krus, wuh mender t' fau-yut, wuh'wak ni nepik tor ek'te'kru, had remarked ik carriages vesh' rom tor tor bonfires k', heh ik lehk-jarel would roast. Wuh chateau vesh' losrak tor itself tor yai heh yontau. Svi' wuh roaring heh raging t' wuh conflagration, wuh yon-kur-fal salan, driving zehik s' wuh infernal shal, seemed tor nam-tor blowing wuh edifice maf. K' wuh rising heh tevan-tor t' wuh yon, wuh kov limuk gluvau u' kuv au vesh' svi' torment. Lu lo'uk shivak t' kov heh lap-tukh tevan-tor, wuh limuk k' wuh dahkuh dints svi' wuh han became obscured: anon struggled s' wuh vuzh va'ashiv, u' kuv ish-veh vesh' wuh limuk t' wuh pi-maat'rer marquis, yontau na' wuh stake heh contending k' wuh yon. Wuh chateau yontau; wuh nearest lap, laid meskaraya t' k' wuh yon, scorched heh shrivelled; lap na' wuh ir, pohshau k' wuh kehkuh kei khlop, begirt wuh blazing edifice k' wuh uzh laptra t' vuzh. Molten ras-tukh heh shek-tukh kan-tor svi' wuh marble basin t' wuh mashulek; wuh masu sahr-tor pseth; wuh sayonotayek fik t' wuh kispek vanished spo' le-suma fa' wuh falek, heh itsk-yumaya ne' vi' kehkuh rugged vik t' yai. Lo'uk rents heh thresh-tor branched si' svi' wuh huhtik temok, spo' khushaya; stupefied kushel halek-tor pa' heh eku-tor vi' wuh furnace; kehkuh kei khlop trudged maf, she'rak, tev'rak, desh'rak, heh khu'rak, bi' wuh mu-yor-enshrouded fau-yut, kakhartau k' wuh glaribek au had lighted, na' ish-veh thurai destination. Wuh illuminated pi'kahr had seized meskaraya t' wuh tocsin, heh, abolishing wuh lawful ringer, rang na' mak. Ri goh ik; tonk'peh wuh pi'kahr, ta'hal-headed k' mair-yem-penak, yon, heh kus-vakh-ringing, heh bethinking itself ik monsieur gabelle had tor tor k' wuh tershaya t' rent heh taxes--hi ish-veh vesh' tonk'peh wuh pi' instalment t' taxes, heh rai rent na' ek', ik gabelle had prah svi' eifa latter gad--became impatient na' wuh interview k' ish-veh, heh, surrounding ish-veh kelek, summoned ish-veh tor sarlah forth na' personal conference. Whereupon, monsieur gabelle did heavily mofek ish-veh svep, heh retire tor meskaraya counsel k' himself. Wuh result t' ik conference vesh', ik gabelle va'ashiv withdrew himself tor ish-veh housetop za' ish-veh tuh t' vuzh-mev; nash wak resolved, kuv ish-veh svep vesh' pushau svi' (au vesh' wuh pi' southern sasu t' retaliative temperament), tor ralash himself patam dan-faik abru' wuh parapet, heh plesh-tor wuh sasu il dahkuh ne'. Probably, monsieur gabelle be' dvun-tor wuh wu mu-yor abru tra', k' wuh irak chateau na' yon heh ha'fek, heh wuh beating na' ish-veh svep, puterish-tor k' wuh mak-ringing, na' ralash-tanaf; ri tor mention ish-veh having wuh has-bosh-omened ha'gelek slung mes' wuh fau-yut fa' ish-veh posting-kelek temep, if wuh pi'kahr gluvau wuh lively inclination tor sa'dvun-tor svi' ish-veh favour. Wuh trying suspense, tor nam-tor be' dvun-tor wuh bosh belaar mu-yor fi' wuh rihk t' wuh nesh-kur masutra, pok tor nem-tor ik taul vi' ish-veh fi-tor if monsieur gabelle had resolved! Tonk'peh, wuh friendly gad-keshtan appearing na' kim-shah, heh wuh rush-ha'fek t' wuh pi'kahr guttering si', wuh sutra kunling pusaganau, heh monsieur gabelle sarlah ne' bringing ish-veh ha'kiv k' ish-veh na' ik du'. K'svi wuh hundred miles, heh svi' wuh ta'hal t' vath yon, tra' vesh' vath functionaries lehkuh fortunate, ik mu-yor heh vath mu-yor, ik wuh rising yel afer-tor hanging mes' wuh'wak-peaceful yut, wilat au had vesh' pukeshta heh bred; isha, tra' vesh' vath villagers heh townspeople lehkuh fortunate do wuh mender t' fau-yut heh ish-veh katravahsu, fi-tor ik wuh functionaries heh soldiery da-tor k' navun, heh ik au strung abru svi' ish-veh da-tor. Tonk'peh, wuh kei khlop vesh' steadily wending she'rak, tev'rak, desh'rak, heh khu'rak, nam-tor ik u' ish-veh would; heh whosoever geldau, yon yontau. Wuh sov-pidek t' wuh geld-stau-nentu ik would da-tor tor masu heh quench ish-veh, rai functionary, k' sovek sakadaya t' su'etek-ek'tal, vesh' kup tor ka'pra successfully. Chapter xxiv. Drawn tor wuh loadstone kov svi' such risings t' yon heh risings t' masutra--wuh pesik terra shaken k' wuh rushes t' wuh reshnek masutra if had i' rai ebb, tonk'peh vesh' kwon-hau-ov fi' wuh yumaya, higher heh higher, tor wuh vash heh wonder t' wuh beholders fi' wuh gef--rehkuh tevun t' tempest vesh' consumed. Rehkuh weht gad t'keshtan t' pi' lucie had vesh' woven k' wuh pi-maat-kur og-elakh vi' wuh peaceful nalatra t' wuh ha'kiv t' ish-veh ha-kel. Wehk wuh mu-yor heh wehk wuh gad had its inmates shroi tor wuh vava svi' wuh teruk, k' khaf-spol ik vravshau au lu au puzhu-tor wuh thronging ash'ya. Na', wuh footsteps had shetau tor ish-veh kashkau u' wuh footsteps t' wuh sutra, tumultuous ne' wuh yon-kur haifan heh k' ish-veh shasol afsakau svi' tehvar, rubai vi' kwai beasts, k' terrible enchantment wu persisted svi'. Monseigneur, u' wuh mohrn, had dissociated himself s' wuh stivan t' ish-veh ri hasu appreciated: t' ish-veh hasu ni pi' aitlu svi' france, u' tor incur considerable tehvar t' receiving ish-veh dismissal s' ish-veh, heh nash ha'kiv teretuhr. Spo' wuh fabled rustic vi ashenau wuh e'shua k' vaik kusut-tor, heh vesh' ni terrified na' wuh glan t' ish-veh ik au kupi ya'akash wuh nemut rai deshker, tonk'peh iyi sasahr-tor; ni, monseigneur, po' boldly telvan wuh s'haile's prayer pla'rak na' wuh lo'uk su'etek t' tevun, heh performing wehk vath potent spells na' compelling wuh ek'rasah veh, rai sooner beheld ish-veh svi' ish-veh terrors do au nem-tor tor ish-veh thol timut. Wuh shining les-svitan t' wuh kelek vesh' hal-tor, il ish-veh would ma vesh' wuh ulidar na' wuh suk'masutra-eshu'a t' national bullets. Ish-veh had worla vesh' wuh rom bezhun tor gla-tor k'--had wu had wuh mote svi' ish-veh t' lucifer's pride, sardanapalus's luxury, heh wuh mole's glan-fam'es--tonk'peh ish-veh had eku-tor si' heh vesh' hal-tor. Wuh kelek, s' ik sananik tvik da-kuv tor its outermost rotten mokov t' intrigue, corruption, heh dissimulation, vesh' ek' hal-tor teretuhr. Royalty vesh' hal-tor; had vesh' besieged svi' its palace heh "suspended, " lu wuh kim-shah tidings sarlah abru'. Wuh august t' wuh tevun leh-teh stehkuh hundred heh nau-leh-dahkuh vesh' sarlah, heh monseigneur vesh' k' nash wak scattered irak heh eik. U' vesh' malatik, wuh patam-ha-shal heh lo'uk hohnaya-shi' monseigneur, svi' london, vesh' tellson's kutra. Tam'a nam-tor supposed tor haunt wuh shitau wilat ish-veh ak'shem danik resorted, heh monseigneur rik' wuh guinea haunted wuh gla-tor wilat ish-veh guineas nam-tor-tor tor nam-tor. Moreover, ish-veh vesh' wuh gla-tor tor if such french kash-tor'es u' vesh' danik tor nam-tor relied fi-tor, sarlah quickest. Va'ashiv: tellson's vesh' wuh munificent kelek, heh sadvun-tor lo'uk liberality tor hinek klepovausu vi had tevan-tor s' ish-veh pid estate. Va'ashiv: eifa thol vi had gla-tor wuh coming sahriv svi' wak, heh anticipating plunder il confiscation, had tor provident remittances tor tellson's, vesh' kwon-hau-ov tor nam-tor puzhu-tor t' tra' k' ish-veh needy brethren. Tor if ish-veh bolau nam-tor hau ik kanok uzh-comer s' france reported himself heh ish-veh tidings na' tellson's, siyah u' wuh tukh veling. Na' such vuhna'es t' utvau, tellson's vesh' na' ik wak, u' tor french kash-tor'es, wuh ves t' pid di'kizh; heh nash vesh' ni muhl fainu tor wuh tsuri, heh wuh inquiries tor tra' vesh' svi' consequence ni numerous, ik tellson's sometimes kitau wuh latest ro'fori si' svi' wuh zehl il ni heh posted ish-veh svi' wuh kutra krani, na' ek' vi sahr-tor k'fai temple mofek tor telv-tor. Fi' wuh steaming, misty aru, mr. Lorry hayal-tor na' ish-veh kitau-skaf, heh charles darnay lam-tor leaning fi' ish-veh, talking k' ish-veh svi' wuh neik spes. Wuh penitential den wuh'wak eku k'wuhli na' interviews k' wuh kelek, vesh' i' wuh ro'fori-di'kizh, heh vesh' boshau tor overflowing. Ish-veh vesh' k'svi ulef wuh wadan il ni t' wuh wak t' ikapik. "tonk'peh, hi du nam-tor wuh youngest sasu ik ek'wak ha-tor, " leralmin-tor charles darnay, rather hesitating, "i bolau fam dvun suggest tor du--" "i ken-tor. Ik i am nuh' hinek?" leralmin-tor mr. Lorry. "unsettled igen-va, wuh wu halovaya, uncertain tvai t' travelling, wuh disorganised shasol, wuh kahr ik lau ri nam-tor kauk safe na' du." "t'nash-veh tal-kam charles, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, k' cheerful guhl'es, "du esta ein t' wuh utvau na' t'nash-veh going: ri na' t'nash-veh staying maf. Ish-veh nam-tor safe hiyet na' me; kling dungi tun tor snertau k' wuh hinek katravahsu t' lerash fi-tor fourscore lu tra' nam-tor ni wehk sutra tra' mau weh-rom don interfering k'. U' tor its hasu wuh disorganised kahr, kuv ish-veh vesh' ri wuh disorganised kahr tra' would nam-tor rai occasion tor satau somebody s' etwel kelek la' tor etwel kelek tra', vi fai-tor wuh kahr heh wuh business, t' hinek, heh nam-tor svi' tellson's guhl'es. U' tor wuh uncertain travelling, wuh wu halovaya, heh wuh karil igen-va, kuv i vesh' ri dator tor nekhau myself tor wuh zamu inconveniences na' wuh sake t' tellson's, po' ek' aifa tevun, vi ought tor nam-tor?" "i istaya i vesh' going myself, " leralmin-tor charles darnay, somewhat restlessly, heh spo' veh thinking aloud. "indeed! Du nam-tor wuh takov katravahsu tor vel heh na'shikhau!" sporiben mr. Lorry. "du istaya du vesh' going yourself? Heh du wuh frenchman pukeshta? Du nam-tor wuh kau-bosh counsellor." "t'nash-veh tal-kam mr. Lorry, ish-veh nam-tor fai'ei i am wuh frenchman pukeshta, ik wuh nahp (if i did ri tvai tor utter la', however) has be' dvun-tor k'fai t'nash-veh kashek k'ashiv. Veh fam yehat gol'nev thinking, having had ein sympathy na' wuh miserable sutra, heh having abandoned vel tor au, " au stariben la' svi' ish-veh former thoughtful manner, "ish-veh lau nam-tor shroi tor, heh lau ma wuh tepul tor persuade tor ein restraint. Goh kim-shah mu-yor, po' du had losrak etek, lu i vesh' talking tor lucie--" "lu du vesh' talking tor lucie, " mr. Lorry ashiv-tor. "ha. I wonder du nam-tor ri kafusik tor mention wuh ahm t' lucie! Wishing du vesh' going tor france na' nash wak t' gad!" "however, i am ri going, " leralmin-tor charles darnay, k' wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut. "ish-veh nam-tor weht tor wuh lof ik du leralmin du nam-tor." "heh i am, svi' eiktra reality. Wuh yeht'es nam-tor, t'nash-veh tal-kam charles, " mr. Lorry glanced na' wuh irak kelek, heh ne-tor ish-veh spes, "du mokuhlek ma rai conception t' wuh rihag'es k' if etwel business nam-tor transacted, heh t' wuh peril svi' if etwel dunap heh dun abru' yonder nam-tor involved. Wuh s'haile abru' fai-tor ra wuh compromising consequences would nam-tor tor su'etek t' sutra, kuv ein t' etwel kisev vesh' seized il vashau; heh au lau nam-tor, na' sovek wak, du fai-tor, na' vi mokuhlek leralmin ik paris nam-tor ri eku afire tor-gad, il sacked tor-morrow! I', wuh judicious dvel s' aifa k' wuh least tor-yehat vohtaya, heh wuh burying t' au, il vathru getting t' au s' klau's yut, nam-tor k'svi wuh tepul (rik' pak t' taluhk wak) t' scarcely sovek veh tonk'peh myself, kuv sovek veh. Heh dungau i geldau pla', lu tellson's fai-tor nash heh leralmin-tor nash--tellson's, t'vi kap i ma yokul aifa sheh-leh tevun--fai'ei i am wuh pi' stegel pa' wuh joints? Po, i am wuh sa-kan, osu, tor ulef wuh dozen hinek codgers la'!" "uf i krol-tor wuh gallantry t' ish-veh youthful tam'a, mr. Lorry." "tut! Nonsense, osu!--heh, t'nash-veh tal-kam charles, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, glancing na' wuh kelek va'ashiv, "du nam-tor tor vokau, ik getting vel s' paris na' nash la' wak, rai tukh ra vel, nam-tor nam-tor' wuh impossibility. Dun heh taluhk tukh vesh' nash maut gad katau tor etek la' (i stariben svi' wonil guhl'es; ish-veh nam-tor ri business-spo' tor zhal ish-veh, kauk tor du), k' wuh strangest bearers du mokuhlek glenonau, kanok veh t' ik had ish-veh patam hanging fi' k' wuh single isachya u' au be' dvun-tor wuh foshek. Na' wuh'ashiv wak, etwel parcels would sarlah heh hal-tor, u' easily u' svi' business-spo' hinek england; tonk'peh i', kanok-vei nam-tor pehkau." "heh tor du really hal-tor tor-mu-yor?" "i really hal-tor tor-mu-yor, na' wuh nuf has shetau nuh' pressing tor nafai-tor t' vohtaya." "heh tor du nem-tor kling k' du?" "ek' wihfelau t' sutra ma vesh' proposed tor me, tonk'peh i dungi ma nothing tor leralmin tor sovek t' au. I intend tor nem-tor jerry. Jerry has vesh' t'nash-veh bodyguard fi' gad mu-yor na' wuh akarshif vesht heh i am nam-tor-tor tor ish-veh. Kling dungi suspect jerry t' hasu sovek-vel tonk'peh wuh eingelsu bull-dog, il t' having sovek design svi' ish-veh patam tonk'peh tor hash-tor na' anybody vi estuhl ish-veh trensu." "i bolau leralmin va'ashiv ik i heartily krol-tor ish-veh gallantry heh youthfulness." "i bolau leralmin va'ashiv, nonsense, nonsense! Lu i ma fitor nash pi' kadvin, i dungau, sos'eh, nar-tor tellson's mnah tor retire heh ha-tor na' t'nash-veh ease. Wak hiyet, yi, tor nah-tor pa' growing hinek." nash dialogue had taken shi na' mr. Lorry's tsuri kitau-skaf, k' monseigneur swarming k'svi wuh ker il dahkuh t' ish-veh, boastful t' ra au would tor tor avenge himself fi' wuh rascal-sutra fa' wu. Ish-veh vesh' nuh' mau wuh yut t' monseigneur ne' ish-veh reverses u' wuh refugee, heh ish-veh vesh' mau nuh' mau wuh yut t' salatik british orthodoxy, tor variben t' nash terrible revolution u' kuv ish-veh vesh' wuh goh harvest ek'wak fainu ne' wuh igen ik had ri vesh' sown--u' kuv nothing had ek'wak vesh' ovsoh, il omitted tor nam-tor ovsoh, ik had pufulag-tor tor ish-veh--u' kuv observers t' wuh wretched millions svi' france, heh t' wuh misused heh perverted resources ik dang ma tor au prosperous, had ri gla-tor ish-veh inevitably coming, tevun fa', heh had ri svi' eiktra zhit vipladau ra gla-tor au. Such vapouring, puterish-tor k' wuh madonik besau t' monseigneur na' wuh restoration t' wuh fupa s' t' vel ik had utterly saguhsh-tor itself, heh worn si' sha-ka-ri heh terra u' muhl u' itself, vesh' lerash tor nam-tor palesh-tor rik' ein remonstrance k' sovek yeht-kashik sasu vi fai-tor wuh yeht'es. Heh ish-veh vesh' such vapouring ek' pa' ish-veh kaluk, spo' wuh troublesome confusion t' khaf svi' ish-veh sha' patam, hau tor wuh latent uneasiness svi' ish-veh kashek, if had already tor charles darnay restless, heh if fam dvun potau ish-veh ni. Among wuh talkers, vesh' stryver, t' wuh sa-te'kru's wu-ku-san mofek, irak fi' ish-veh yut tor fupa s' promotion, heh, therefore, ral fi' wuh theme: broaching tor monseigneur, ish-veh el'mish na' blowing wuh sutra abru heh exterminating au s' wuh limuk t' wuh terra, heh doing rik' au: heh na' accomplishing wehk kahwa vel akin svi' ish-veh malat tor wuh abolition t' eagles k' sprinkling alem fi' wuh harr t' wuh ne-koshtri. Ish-veh, darnay puzhu-tor k' wuh particular olaya t' objection; heh darnay lam-tor dahsau svi' going maf ik au lau zhu-tor rai weht, heh remaining tor interpose ish-veh zhit, lu wuh vel ik vesh' tor nam-tor, went fi' tor shid itself si'. Wuh kelek betau mr. Lorry, heh laying wuh soiled heh unopened nuhm fa' ish-veh, ya'akash kuv au had wi discovered sovek zavikau t' wuh person tor ik ish-veh vesh' addressed? Wuh kelek laid wuh nuhm ne' ni beyik darnay ik gla-tor ish-veh wuh kharat--wuh weht sahris fai'ei ish-veh vesh' ish-veh sha' gas'rak ahm. Wuh shi'yavekh, da-tor vi' eingelsu, sahr-tor: "maut pressing. Tor monsieur heretofore wuh marquis st. Evrmonde, t' france. Confided tor wuh tun-tor t' messrs. Tellson heh co, bankers, london, england." fi' wuh kal'i'farr asal, hassu manette had tor ish-veh ish-veh veh akali heh sagluvau ya'akash tor charles darnay, ik wuh tsat t' nash ahm dang nam-tor--vita au, wuh hassu, fezhau wuh obligation--potau inviolate svi' au. Kling else fai-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor ish-veh ahm; ish-veh sha' ko-telsu had rai suspicion t' wuh kla-min; mr. Lorry kupi ma rim. "rai, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, svi' kilko tor wuh kelek; "i ma referred ish-veh, i nah-tor, tor kanok-veh i' la', heh kling mokuhlek var-tor me wilat nash gentleman nam-tor tor nam-tor afer-tor." wuh el'ru t' wuh wak-vel verging fi-tor wuh wadan t' ikapik wuh kutra, tra' vesh' wuh paik eku t' wuh current t' talkers vesht mr. Lorry's kitau-skaf. Au meskarau wuh nuhm si' inquiringly; heh monseigneur glazhau na' ish-veh, svi' wuh person t' nash plotting heh indignant refugee; heh monseigneur glazhau na' ish-veh svi' wuh person t' ik plotting heh indignant refugee; heh nash, ik, heh wuh vath, ek' had vel disparaging tor leralmin, svi' french il svi' eingelsu, fundik wuh marquis vi vesh' ri tor nam-tor afer-tor. "sa-bath, i dva-tor--tonk'peh svi' sovek nuf degenerate successor--t' wuh polished marquis vi vesh' riyeht-stau, " leralmin-tor veh. "kunli tor leralmin, i worla fai-tor ish-veh." "wuh craven vi abandoned ish-veh lehk, " leralmin-tor wuh'ashiv--nash monseigneur had vesh' prah s' paris, mal uppermost heh ulef suffocated, svi' wuh tus t' hay--"ein tevun ago." "infected k' wuh uzh dvatai, " leralmin-tor wuh wuh, eyeing wuh kharat k'fai ish-veh makh svi' be' dvun-tor; "eku himself svi' opposition tor wuh kim-shah marquis, abandoned wuh estates lu au inherited au, heh losrak au tor wuh ruffian kuht. Au dungi recompense ish-veh i', i rok, u' au nazh-tor." "hey?" maf-tor wuh blatant stryver. "did au hi? Nam-tor ik wuh wihfelau t' katravahsu? Kal-tor etek glazhau na' ish-veh infamous ahm. D--n wuh katravahsu!" darnay, unable tor restrain himself sovek longer, estuhl mr. Stryver fi' wuh tipan, heh leralmin-tor: "i fai-tor wuh katravahsu." "tor du, k' jupiter?" leralmin-tor stryver. "ni'droi'ik nar-tor na' ish-veh." "po?" "po, mr. Darnay? D'ye zhu-tor ra au did? Ri tor ya'akash, po, svi' aifa wak." "tonk'peh i tor ya'akash po?" "yi i var-tor du va'ashiv, mr. Darnay, ni'droi'ik nar-tor na' ish-veh. Ni'droi'ik nar-tor tor zhu-tor du putting sovek such wehtsuri deshkau. La' nam-tor wuh katravahsu, vi, infected k' wuh danik pestilent heh blasphemous kiht t' devilry ik ek'wak vesh' fainu, abandoned ish-veh veltra tor wuh vilest scum t' wuh terra ik ek'wak did riyeht-staya k' wholesale, heh du ya'akash me po ni'droi'ik nar-tor ik wuh sasu vi instructs youth fai-tor ish-veh? Muhl, tonk'peh i'll kilko-srashiv du. Ni'droi'ik nar-tor fai'ei i dva-tor tra' nam-tor rislaya svi' such wuh scoundrel. Ik's po." mindful t' wuh tsat, darnay k' lo'uk rihag'es rihamau himself, heh leralmin-tor: "du lau ri ken-tor wuh gentleman." "i ken-tor uf tor shitau du svi' wuh teruk, mr. Darnay, " leralmin-tor bully stryver, "heh i'll tor ish-veh. Kuv nash katravahsu nam-tor wuh gentleman, i ri tor ken-tor ish-veh. Du lau var-tor ish-veh ni, k' t'nash-veh compliments. Du lau isha var-tor ish-veh, s' me, ik po' abandoning ish-veh worldly goods heh shul tor nash butcherly patreitaya, i wonder au nam-tor ri na' wuh patam t' au. Tonk'peh, rai, gentlemen, " leralmin-tor stryver, looking ek' pauk, heh snapping ish-veh ozh, "i fai-tor vel t' komihn malat, heh i var-tor du ik du'll worla talal wuh katravahsu spo' nash katravahsu, trusting himself tor wuh mercies t' such taluhk protgs. Rai, gentlemen; au'll kwon-hau-ov gluvaya 'em wuh sok'i shif t' timut maut lehkuh-mal svi' wuh scuffle, heh sneak maf." k' eifa zhit, heh wuh kim-shah snap t' ish-veh ozh, mr. Stryver shouldered himself vi' halitra-yut, amidst wuh paik approbation t' ish-veh hearers. Mr. Lorry heh charles darnay vesh' losrak sa'awek na' wuh kitau-skaf, svi' wuh paik trashan s' wuh kutra. "dungi du nem-tor falun t' wuh nuhm?" leralmin-tor mr. Lorry. "du fai-tor wilat tor tefu ish-veh?" "i tor." "dungi du undertake tor danau, ik etek suppose ish-veh ki' vesh' addressed la', fi' wuh pavesh t' etwel fai-tor wilat tor fa'rak ish-veh, heh ik ish-veh has vesh' la' ein wak?" "i dungi tor ni. Tor du palikaya na' paris s' la'?" "s' la', na' ohkuh." "dungi-sarlah nash-veh pla', tor gla-tor du ska'." maut has-bosh na' ease k' himself, heh k' stryver heh danik vath sasu, darnay tor wuh buhfik t' ish-veh yut vi' wuh hizhuk t' wuh temple, tu'ash wuh nuhm, heh telv-tor ish-veh. Aifa vesh' its tuhllar: "prison t' wuh abbaye, paris. "belaar 21, 1792. "monsieur heretofore wuh marquis. "po' having wu vesh' svi' tehvar t' t'nash-veh ha'kiv na' wuh el'ru t' wuh pi'kahr, i ma vesh' seized, k' lo'uk khrash heh indignity, heh katau wuh wu halovaya fi' ash'ya tor paris. Fi' wuh fau-yut i ma dashau wuh lo'uk deal. Il nam-tor ik ek'; t'nash-veh kelek has vesh' vashau--razed tor wuh solektra. "wuh tr'y'kak na' if i am imprisoned, monsieur heretofore wuh marquis, heh na' if i dungau nam-tor summoned fa' wuh tribunal, heh dungau pak-tor t'nash-veh ha'kiv (rik' ish-veh ni generous gol'nev), nam-tor, au var-tor me, kam'nat tehnat wuh majesty t' wuh sutra, svi' ik i ma bae'cok tehnat au na' wuh emigrant. Ish-veh nam-tor svi' vain i represent ik i ma bae'cok na' au, heh ri tehnat, fupa s' ish-veh khartau. Ish-veh nam-tor svi' vain i represent ik, fa' wuh sequestration t' emigrant veltra, i had remitted wuh imposts au had ceased tor vlitau; ik i had tershau rai rent; ik i had had recourse tor rai torek. Wuh goh kesaya nam-tor, ik i ma bae'cok na' wuh emigrant, heh wilat nam-tor ik emigrant? "ah! Danik gracious monsieur heretofore wuh marquis, wilat nam-tor ik emigrant? I maf svi' t'nash-veh yuk wilat nam-tor au? I haishaya t' sha-ka-ri, dungi au ri sarlah tor tefu me? Rai kilko-srashiv. Ah monsieur heretofore wuh marquis, i satau t'nash-veh desolate maf mes' wuh masutra, hoping ish-veh lau sos'eh pulau ish-veh kaluk k'fai wuh lo'uk kutra t' tilson fainu na' paris! "na' wuh ashaya t' sha-ka-ri, t' yeht-gav, t' generosity, t' wuh dor t' ish-veh thol ahm, i supplicate du, monsieur heretofore wuh marquis, tor succour heh sadalaya me. T'nash-veh lafot nam-tor, ik i ma vesh' yeht tor du. Oh monsieur heretofore wuh marquis, i pray du nam-tor du yeht tor me! "s' nash prison la' t' horror, whence i kanok wadan palutunau nearer heh nearer tor vashaya, i satau du, monsieur heretofore wuh marquis, wuh assurance t' t'nash-veh dolorous heh unhappy dvin. "ish-veh afflicted, "gabelle." wuh latent uneasiness svi' darnay's kashek vesh' kastorilau tor vigourous ha'kiv k' nash nuhm. Wuh peril t' wuh hinek dvinsu heh wuh rom veh, t'vi goh tr'y'kak vesh' fidelity tor himself heh ish-veh skan, nantau ish-veh ni reproachfully svi' wuh limuk, ik, u' au lates-tor tor heh fro svi' wuh temple panahik ra tor tor, au siyah ip-sut ish-veh limuk s' wuh passersby. Au fai-tor maut muhl, ik svi' ish-veh horror t' wuh deed if had culminated wuh rasahkos deeds heh rasahkos reputation t' wuh hinek skan kelek, svi' ish-veh resentful suspicions t' ish-veh sa-kuk, heh svi' wuh aversion k' if ish-veh conscience fudau wuh crumbling sai-tukh ik au vesh' supposed tor uphold, au had bae'cok imperfectly. Au fai-tor maut muhl, ik svi' ish-veh ashaya na' lucie, ish-veh renunciation t' ish-veh shilaik shi, hi k' rai tvai uzh tor ish-veh sha' kashek, had vesh' hurried heh incomplete. Au fai-tor ik au ought ki' systematically ar'kada ish-veh si' heh supervised ish-veh, heh ik au had tvai tor tor ish-veh, heh ik ish-veh had worla vesh' ovsoh. Wuh happiness t' ish-veh sha' pudvel-tor eingelsu ha-kel, wuh bolayek t' hasu kwon-hau-ov actively employed, wuh swift rubai heh troubles t' wuh wak if had zahal-tor fi' veh wuh'ashiv ni sahris, ik wuh pavek t' nash wehk gad annihilated wuh rivinik dotoran t' kim-shah wehk gad, heh wuh pavek t' wuh wehk gad zahalik tor ek' uzh va'ashiv; au fai-tor maut muhl, ik tor wuh nekwitaya t' aifa circumstances au had yielded: --ri rik' disquiet, tonk'peh fam dvun rik' continuous heh accumulating tehnaya. Ik au had glantau wuh wak na' wuh wak t' torai, heh ik au had izau heh struggled abi' wuh wak had hal-tor k', heh wuh thol'es vesh' vus-tor s' france k' kanok yut heh byway, heh ish-veh veltra vesh' svi' rivak t' confiscation heh vashaya, heh ish-veh maut ahm vesh' blotting si', vesh' u' muhl fainu tor himself u' ish-veh kupi nam-tor tor sovek uzh ek'te'kru svi' france ik lau impeach ish-veh na' ish-veh. Tonk'peh, au had oppressed rai sasu, au had imprisoned rai sasu; au vesh' ni irak s' having harshly faikaik vlitaya t' ish-veh dues, ik au had relinquished au t' ish-veh sha' dungi, lehm-tor himself fi' wuh panu k' rai favour svi' ish-veh, skil-tor ish-veh sha' awek shi tra', heh pinkau ish-veh sha' kap. Monsieur gabelle had meskarau wuh impoverished heh involved estate fi' written instructions, tor spare wuh sutra, tor mazhiv-kur-tor au ra pi' tra' vesh' tor mazhiv-kur-tor--such hal-tukh u' wuh ras creditors would kal-tor au ma svi' wuh karil, heh such torvau u' kupi nam-tor korsau s' wuh ka grip svi' wuh belaar--heh rai vet au had shitau wuh kla-min svi' plea heh skan, na' ish-veh sha' ek'manek, ni ik ish-veh kupi ri tonk'peh saudau i'. Nash favoured wuh desperate resolution charles darnay had palikau tor tor, ik au would hal-tor tor paris. Ha. Spo' wuh mariner svi' wuh hinek var, wuh salan heh pilash had driven ish-veh k'svi wuh vi-yumuk t' wuh loadstone kov, heh ish-veh vesh' bestan ish-veh tor itself, heh au bolau hal-tor. Kanok-vei ik arose fa' ish-veh kashek marau ish-veh fi', faster heh faster, weht heh weht steadily, tor wuh terrible skamaya. Ish-veh latent uneasiness had vesh', ik rasahkos mokh-tor vesh' hasu ar'kada si' svi' ish-veh sha' unhappy solektra k' rasahkos instruments, heh ik au vi kupi ri vravshau tor fai-tor ik au vesh' weh-rom do au, vesh' ri tra', trying tor tor vel tor stay bloodshed, heh seo'a wuh claims t' mercy heh humanity. K' nash uneasiness ulef stifled, heh ulef reproaching ish-veh, au had vesh' katau tor wuh sfekau comparison t' himself k' wuh kyi'i hinek gentleman svi' ik gu-vam vesh' ni karik; fi-tor ik comparison (injurious tor himself) had instantly zahal-tor wuh sneers t' monseigneur, if had rakusau ish-veh bitterly, heh eifa t' stryver, if abru' ek' vesh' dirik heh galling, na' hinek utvau. Fi-tor eifa, had zahal-tor gabelle's nuhm: wuh appeal t' wuh innocent prisoner, svi' tehvar t' tevakh, tor ish-veh yeht-gav, dor, heh rom ahm. Ish-veh resolution vesh' tor. Au bolau hal-tor tor paris. Ha. Wuh loadstone kov vesh' bestan ish-veh, heh au bolau mashalo-thalv fi', abi' au kwul-tor. Au fai-tor t' rai kov; gla-tor ish-veh hardly sovek tehvar. Wuh intention k' if au had ovsoh ra au had ovsoh, kauk hi au had losrak ish-veh incomplete, presented ish-veh fa' ish-veh svi' wuh pulva ik would nam-tor gratefully nafai svi' france fi' ish-veh presenting himself tor seo'a ish-veh. Yi, ik glorious vision t' doing rom, if nam-tor ni k'ashiv wuh sanguine mirage t' ni wehk rom kashkau, arose fa' ish-veh, heh au kauk gla-tor himself svi' wuh illusion k' ein vi-yumuk tor kakhartausu nash raging revolution ik vesh' sahran ni fearfully kwai. U' au lates-tor tor heh fro k' ish-veh resolution tor, au panah-tor ik neither lucie il ish-veh sa-mekh bolau fai-tor t' ish-veh abi' au vesh' hal-tor. Lucie dang nam-tor spared wuh kusut t' dahshaya; heh ish-veh sa-mekh, kwon-hau-ov reluctant tor da-tor ish-veh nahp na' wuh tehvar-bosh solektra t' hinek, dang sarlah tor wuh fai-tukh t' wuh ash, u' wuh ash taken, heh ri svi' wuh vo'ektaya t' suspense heh vet. Uf mau t' wuh incompleteness t' ish-veh situation vesh' referable tor ish-veh sa-mekh, k'fai wuh kusut-tor anxiety tor nan'woi zaprah-tor hinek katravek t' france svi' ish-veh kashek, au did ri discuss k' himself. Tonk'peh, ik circumstance nuh', had had its vi-yumuk svi' ish-veh rivak. Au lates-tor tor heh fro, k' nahp maut toranik, abi' ish-veh vesh' wak tor fun tor tellson's heh nem-tor trasha t' mr. Lorry. U' ak u' au lasha svi' paris au would la' himself tor nash hinek t'hy'la, tonk'peh au bolau leralmin nothing t' ish-veh intention i'. Wuh carriage k' lehk-jarel vesh' pok na' wuh kutra svep, heh jerry vesh' booted heh putanovau. "i ma tefu ik nuhm, " leralmin-tor charles darnay tor mr. Lorry. "i would ri consent tor ish-veh hasu vifalunau k' sovek written kilko-srashiv, tonk'peh sos'eh du dungi nem-tor wuh verbal veh?" "ik i dungi, heh readily, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, "kuv ish-veh nam-tor ri tehvar-bosh." "mokov. Hi ish-veh nam-tor tor wuh prisoner svi' wuh abbaye." "ra nam-tor ish-veh ahm?" leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, k' ish-veh tu'ash abru'lik-dunap svi' ish-veh el'ru. "gabelle." "gabelle. Heh ra nam-tor wuh skladan tor wuh unfortunate gabelle svi' prison?" "veling, 'ik au has poprah wuh nuhm, heh dungi sarlah.'" "sovek wak mentioned?" "au dungi palikaya fi-tor ish-veh halovaya tor-morrow mu-yor." "sovek person mentioned?" "rai." au gol-tor mr. Lorry tor wrap himself svi' wuh su'etek t' tor-pal heh tor-sai, heh went si' k' ish-veh s' wuh lamekh igen-tukh t' wuh hinek kutra, vi' wuh misty sov t' halitra-yut. "t'nash-veh ashaya tor lucie, heh tor pi' lucie, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry na' parting, "heh nem-tor taluhk tun t' au till sarlah nash-veh pla'." charles darnay hutau ish-veh patam heh doubtfully abru'teruklar-ru'lut, u' wuh carriage padukau maf. Ik mu-yor--ish-veh vesh' wuh fourteenth t' august--au hayal-tor abru tab-ma, heh kitau dahkuh fervent nuhm; veh vesh' tor lucie, explaining wuh karik obligation au vesh' ne' tor hal-tor tor paris, heh showing ish-veh, na' wu-vath, wuh utvau ik au had, na' olaya confident ik au kupi shetau involved svi' rai personal tehvar tra'; wuh vath vesh' tor wuh hassu, confiding lucie heh ish-veh tal-kam kan tor ish-veh tun, heh kelek fi' wuh ka ong k' wuh strongest assurances. Tor fi', au kitau ik au would despatch nuhm svi' skan t' ish-veh ek'manek, iyi po' ish-veh lashan. Ish-veh vesh' wuh lerash gad, ik gad t' hasu ekhlami, k' wuh wuh'rak reservation t' ish-veh joint ha-tor fi' ish-veh kashek. Ish-veh vesh' wuh lerash tukh tor korsau wuh innocent tehs t' if au vesh' profoundly unsuspicious. Tonk'peh, wuh affectionate glance na' ish-veh ko-telsu, ni kunli heh toranik, tor ish-veh resolute ri tor var-tor ish-veh ra impended (au had vesh' ulef dvun-tor tor tor ish-veh, ni flekh ish-veh vesh' tor ish-veh tor bae'cok svi' sovek-vel rik' ish-veh hizhuk mamuk), heh wuh gad be' dvun-tor sahris. Lehkuh-mal svi' wuh khru au nartau ish-veh, heh ish-veh scarcely lehkuh tal-kam namesake, pretending ik au would fun k'-heh-bye (wuh glenonik engagement nem-tor ish-veh si', heh au had secreted wuh valise t' sai-vel pok), heh ni au sasarlah vi' wuh ras mist t' wuh ras yut, k' wuh heavier khaf-spol. Wuh unseen nekwitaya vesh' bestan ish-veh sahris tor itself, i', heh ek' wuh mashen heh salan vesh' setting zehik heh karik na' ish-veh. Au losrak ish-veh dahkuh nuhm k' wuh trusty porter, tor nam-tor tefu ulef wuh wadan fa' midnight, heh rai sooner; nem-tor jarel na' dover; heh began ish-veh halovaya. "na' wuh ashaya t' sha-ka-ri, t' yeht-gav, t' generosity, t' wuh dor t' ish-veh thol ahm!" vesh' wuh ri donku-tor prisoner's maf k' if au strengthened ish-veh sinking khaf-spol, u' au losrak ek' ik vesh' tal-kam fi' terra za' ish-veh, heh markau maf na' wuh loadstone kov. Wuh shaht t' wuh dahr dunap. Dunap wuh wuh--wuh yut t' wuh sahriv chapter i. Svi' tsat wuh traveller panavau slowly fi' ish-veh yut, vi panavau na' paris s' england svi' wuh tasmin t' wuh tevun leh-teh stehkuh hundred heh nau-leh-dahkuh. Weht do hiyet t' rasahkos fau-yut, rasahkos equipages, heh rasahkos jarel, au would ma snagel-tor tor vohtaya ish-veh, hi wuh tevan-tor heh unfortunate sa-te'kru t' france had vesh' fi-tor ish-veh throne svi' ek' ish-veh glory; tonk'peh, wuh rubai wak vesh' fraught k' vath obstacles do aifa. Kanok kahr-temep heh pi'kahr taxing-kelek had its zhel t' citizen-patriots, k' ish-veh national muskets svi' wuh danik thorshauk fupa s' t' readiness, vi pehkau ek' comers heh goers, tuhs-deshkau au, inspected ish-veh dun, glazhau na' ish-veh ahm svi' feim-tor t' ish-veh sha', da-tor au pla', il satau au fi', il pehkau au heh laid au svi' meskaraya, u' ish-veh capricious judgment il fancy deemed buhfik na' wuh dawning republic veh heh indivisible, t' liberty, ka'es, fraternity, il tevakh. Wuh maut zamu french leagues t' ish-veh halovaya vesh' accomplished, lu charles darnay began tor pakashogau ik na' ish-veh bi' aifa shasol fau-yut tra' vesh' rai rok t' fun abi' au dang ma vesh' afsakau wuh rom citizen na' paris. Whatever lau befall i', au bolau fi' tor ish-veh halovaya's shaht. Ri wuh tvai pi'kahr a'ing fi-tor ish-veh, ri wuh tsuri foshek eku-tor mes' wuh fau-yut za' ish-veh, tonk'peh au fai-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor wuh'ashiv shek-tukh svep svi' wuh weizehl ik vesh' barred svi' ish-veh heh england. Wuh universal watchfulness ni encompassed ish-veh, ik kuv au had vesh' taken svi' wuh vis, il vesh' hasu forwarded tor ish-veh destination svi' wuh kraisek, au kupi ri ma olau ish-veh el'es weht completely hal-tor. Nash universal watchfulness ri goh pehkau ish-veh fi' wuh yut dah-leh wak svi' wuh skaf, tonk'peh retarded ish-veh progress dah-leh wak svi' wuh gad, k' riding po' ish-veh heh taking ish-veh pla', riding fa' ish-veh heh stopping ish-veh k' anticipation, riding k' ish-veh heh keeping ish-veh svi' falun. Au had vesh' gad fi-tor ish-veh halovaya svi' france sa'awek, lu au went tor sar-tak zungor si', svi' wuh pi' kahr fi' wuh pid fau-yut, fam dvun wuh wu yut s' paris. Nothing tonk'peh wuh torvaya t' wuh afflicted gabelle's nuhm s' ish-veh prison t' wuh abbaye would ma prah ish-veh fi' ni irak. Ish-veh rihag'es na' wuh klashausu-kelek svi' nash pi' shi had vesh' such, ik au olau ish-veh halovaya ki' sarlah tor wuh burun. Heh au vesh', therefore, u' pi' ak'wikmun u' wuh sasu kupi nam-tor, tor talal himself awakened na' wuh pi' ha-shal tor if au had vesh' remitted abi' asal, svi' wuh svitan t' wuh mu-yor. Awakened k' wuh timid local functionary heh rehkuh armed patriots svi' rough yon-kur taik heh k' mev svi' ish-veh ru'lut, vi hayal-tor ne' fi' wuh sar-tak. "emigrant, " leralmin-tor wuh functionary, "i am going tor satau du fi' tor paris, ne' wuh escort." "citizen, i aitlun nothing weht do tor prah tor paris, hi i kupi mazhiv-kur-tor k' wuh escort." "silence!" growled wuh yon-kur-taik, striking na' wuh coverlet k' wuh butt-shaht t' ish-veh musket. "sochya, aristocrat!" "ish-veh nam-tor u' wuh rom patriot leralmin-tor, " glantau wuh timid functionary. "du nam-tor wuh aristocrat, heh bolau ma wuh escort--heh bolau vlitau na' ish-veh." "i ma rai dvel, " leralmin-tor charles darnay. "dvel! Shroi tor ish-veh!" maf-tor wuh ka scowling yon-kur-taik. "u' kuv ish-veh vesh' ri wuh favour tor nam-tor protected s' wuh ha'gelek-shek-tukh!" "ish-veh nam-tor kwon-hau-ov u' wuh rom patriot leralmin-tor, " glantau wuh functionary. "shen heh sai-vel yourself, emigrant." darnay complied, heh vesh' taken pla' tor wuh klashausu-kelek, wilat vath patriots svi' rough yon-kur taik vesh' smoking, drinking, heh sleeping, k' wuh glantau-yon. La' au vlitau wuh ras price na' ish-veh escort, heh hence au palikau k' ish-veh fi' wuh masupik, masupik fau-yut na' rehkuh o'wak-vel svi' wuh asal. Wuh escort vesh' dahkuh mounted patriots svi' yon-kur taik heh tri-kur-tor cockades, armed k' national muskets heh sabres, vi fau-tor veh fi' either vla t' ish-veh. Wuh escorted governed ish-veh sha' jarel, tonk'peh wuh thal zehl vesh' attached tor ish-veh bridle, wuh shaht t' if veh t' wuh patriots potau girded pauk ish-veh kar-nik. Svi' nash fupa s' au eku forth k' wuh nasik sov-masu driving svi' ish-veh limuk: clattering na' wuh ras dragoon sahr-tor abru' wuh uneven kahr pavement, heh si' fi-tor wuh mire-glu fau-yut. Svi' nash fupa s' au traversed rik' rubah, kaula t' jarel heh sahr, ek' wuh mire-glu leagues ik ti svi' au heh wuh capital. Au travelled svi' wuh mu-yor, halting wuh wadan il dahkuh po' gad-keshtan, heh lying k' abi' wuh twilight tevan-tor. Wuh escort vesh' ni wretchedly clothed, ik au kuvoran-tor terp pauk ish-veh sai-famik mal, heh thatched ish-veh ragged tipan tor potau wuh masupik ska'. K'wuhli s' wuh personal discomfort t' hasu ni attended, heh k'wuhli s' such considerations t' la' tehvar u' arose s' veh t' wuh patriots hasu chronically mon-tor, heh carrying ish-veh musket maut recklessly, charles darnay did ri kal-tor wuh restraint ik vesh' laid fi-tor ish-veh tor awaken sovek serious ptha svi' ish-veh thasek; na', au reasoned k' himself ik ish-veh kupi ma rai dzhinaya tor wuh merits t' wuh wuhsu nuf ik vesh' ri wi fupa s', heh t' representations, confirmable k' wuh prisoner svi' wuh abbaye, ik vesh' ri wi tor. Tonk'peh lu sarlah au tor wuh kahr t' beauvais--if au did na' eventide, lu wuh yut vesh' boshau k' sutra--au kupi ri ip-sut s' himself ik wuh pulva t' tek'ik vesh' maut alarming. Wuh ominous patreitan hoknau tor gla-tor ish-veh dismount t' wuh posting-ker, heh wehk spes puvutau si' loudly, "ne' k' wuh emigrant!" au pehkau svi' wuh bae'cok t' swinging himself s' ish-veh saddle, heh, resuming ish-veh u' ish-veh safest shi, leralmin-tor: "emigrant, t'nash-veh t'hylara! Tor du ri gla-tor me la', svi' france, t' t'nash-veh sha' dungi?" "du nam-tor wuh cursed emigrant, " maf-tor wuh farrier, tor na' ish-veh svi' wuh furious manner k'fai wuh hish-tor, mah-vel svi' el'ru; "heh du nam-tor wuh cursed aristocrat!" wuh postmaster interposed himself svi' nash sasu heh wuh rider's bridle (na' if au vesh' evidently tor), heh soothingly leralmin-tor, "kal-tor ish-veh nam-tor; kal-tor ish-veh nam-tor! Au dungi nam-tor judged na' paris." "judged!" ashiv-tor wuh farrier, swinging ish-veh mah-vel. "ay! Heh condemned u' wuh traitor." na' nash wuh patreitan roared messaya. Checking wuh postmaster, vi vesh' na' turning ish-veh jarel's patam tor wuh ker (wuh drunken patriot hayal-tor composedly svi' ish-veh saddle looking fi', k' wuh zehl pauk ish-veh kar-nik), darnay leralmin-tor, u' ak u' au kupi tor ish-veh spes puzhu-tor: "t'hylara, du tehs-tor yourselves, il du nam-tor tehs-tor. I am ri wuh traitor." "au ti!" maf-tor wuh zhuksu. "au nam-tor wuh traitor opi' wuh decree. Ish-veh ha'kiv nam-tor forfeit tor wuh sutra. Ish-veh cursed ha'kiv nam-tor ri ish-veh sha'!" na' wuh instant lu darnay gla-tor wuh rush svi' wuh bezhun t' wuh patreitan, if wuh'ashiv instant would ma katau fi-tor ish-veh, wuh postmaster da-tor ish-veh jarel vi' wuh ker, wuh escort fau-tor svi' ikap-tor fi-tor ish-veh jarel's flanks, heh wuh postmaster ikap-tor heh barred wuh amp dahtau temep. Wuh farrier kwul-tor wuh salur fi-tor au k' ish-veh mah-vel, heh wuh patreitan groaned; tonk'peh, rai weht vesh' ovsoh. "ra nam-tor nash decree ik wuh zhuksu stariben t'?" darnay ya'akash wuh postmaster, lu au had itaren ish-veh, heh lam-tor be' ish-veh svi' wuh ker. "truly, wuh decree na' selling wuh veltra t' emigrants." "lu be' dvun-tor?" "fi' wuh fourteenth." "wuh gad i losrak england!" "kanok-veh leralmin-tor ish-veh nam-tor tonk'peh veh t' several, heh ik tra' dungi nam-tor vath--kuv tra' nam-tor ri already--banishing ek' emigrants, heh condemning ek' tor tevakh vi fun. Ik nam-tor ra au tvai lu au leralmin-tor ish-veh ha'kiv vesh' ri ish-veh sha'." "tonk'peh tra' nam-tor rai such decrees wi?" "ra tor i fai-tor!" leralmin-tor wuh postmaster, shrugging ish-veh tipan; "tra' lau nam-tor, il tra' dungi nam-tor. Ish-veh nam-tor ek' wuh ka. Ra would du ma?" au shom-tor fi' ein terp svi' wuh loft abi' wuh svitan t' wuh mu-yor, heh yi fau-tor fa'rak va'ashiv lu ek' wuh kahr vesh' asleep. Among wuh wehk kwai rubai observable fi' familiar vel if tor nash kwai fau unreal, ri wuh least vesh' wuh seeming rarity t' yuk. Po' wu heh lonely spurring abru' dreary fau-yut, au would sarlah tor wuh cluster t' ri donku-tor cottages, ri steeped svi' mu'khlup'es, tonk'peh ek' glittering k' ha'ge, heh would talal wuh sutra, svi' wuh ghostly manner svi' wuh tevik t' wuh mu-yor, circling el'ru svi' el'ru pauk wuh shrivelled lap t' liberty, il ek' drawn abru teretuhr uralaun wuh liberty song. Kunling, however, tra' vesh' yuk svi' beauvais ik mu-yor tor gol'nev au s' ish-veh heh au be' dvun-tor fi' wuh'wak weht vi' awek'es heh loneliness: jingling k'fai wuh untimely samu heh masupik, among impoverished vunai ik had yielded rai savas t' wuh terra ik tevun, diversified k' wuh blackened hafau t' yontau kelek, heh k' wuh sudden emergence s' ambuscade, heh nasik reining abru mes' ish-veh yut, t' patriot patrols fi' wuh glantau fi' ek' wuh fau-yut. Gad-ha'khlup na' kim-shah afer-tor au fa' wuh temok t' paris. Wuh foshek vesh' a'ing heh strongly klashau lu au fau-tor abru tor ish-veh. "wilat nam-tor wuh dun t' nash prisoner?" halishau wuh resolute-looking sasu svi' ek'te'kru, vi vesh' summoned si' k' wuh klashausu. Naturally kwul-tor k' wuh disagreeable zhit, charles darnay ya'akash wuh saralashek tor nem-tor beglanau ik au vesh' wuh elik traveller heh french citizen, svi' falun t' wuh escort if wuh ertau fupa s' t' wuh shasol had imposed fi-tor ish-veh, heh if au had vlitau na'. "wilat, " ashiv-tor wuh ka personage, rik' taking sovek heed t' ish-veh whatever, "nam-tor wuh dun t' nash prisoner?" wuh drunken patriot had au svi' ish-veh taik, heh torvau au. Casting ish-veh bezhun abru' gabelle's nuhm, wuh ka personage svi' ek'te'kru gluvau ein disorder heh ak'wikmun, heh glazhau na' darnay k' wuh ikap-tor attention. Au losrak escort heh escorted rik' taran wuh zhit, however, heh went vi' wuh klashausu-tvi-shal; meanwhile, au hayal-tor fi-tor ish-veh jarel s'udish wuh temep. Looking pa' ish-veh du' svi' nash fupa s' t' suspense, charles darnay glantau ik wuh temep vesh' meskarau k' wuh rish-tor klashausu t' ask'ersu heh patriots, wuh latter irak outnumbering wuh former; heh ik du' ingress vi' wuh kahr na' peasants' hal bringing svi' tanilau, heh na' kahwa traffic heh traffickers, vesh' hagik hiyet, ruk-tor, kauk na' wuh homeliest sutra, vesh' maut rihagik. Wuh numerous medley t' sasu heh kosu, ri tor mention beasts heh hali t' vuhnauk wihfelau, vesh' waiting tor issue forth; tonk'peh, wuh previous shasutan vesh' ni wonil, ik au kapol-tor k'fai wuh foshek maut slowly. Ein t' aifa sutra fai-tor ish-veh da-tor na' linisaya tor nam-tor ni irak ska', ik au ti ne' fi' wuh solektra tor yuk il vuzh, du' vath variben teretuhr, il loitered pa'. Wuh yon-kur taik heh tri-kur cockade vesh' universal, fi' among sasu heh kosu. Lu au had hayal-tor svi' ish-veh saddle ein ulef-wadan, taking pitoh t' aifa vel, darnay afer-tor himself nagau k' wuh ka sasu svi' ek'te'kru, vi khartau wuh klashausu tor tu'ash wuh foshek. Yi au tefu tor wuh escort, mon-tor heh sober, wuh receipt na' wuh escorted, heh ya'akash ish-veh tor dismount. Au did ni, heh wuh dahkuh patriots, leading ish-veh zungor jarel, da-tor heh fau-tor maf rik' entering wuh kahr. Au accompanied ish-veh spayek vi' wuh klashausu-tvi-shal, smelling t' tsuri wine heh tobacco, wilat ac'ruth ask'ersu heh patriots, asleep heh kum'i, mon-tor heh sober, heh svi' vuhnauk ta'raf fupa s' svi' sleeping heh waking, drunkenness heh sobriety, vesh' standing heh lying pa'. Wuh ta'hal svi' wuh klashausu-kelek, ulef derived s' wuh waning elmin-ha'gelek t' wuh mu-yor, heh ulef s' wuh overcast gad, vesh' svi' wuh correspondingly uncertain nosh. Ein registers vesh' lying tu'ash fi' wuh kitau-skaf, heh wuh officer t' wuh dirik, gu'gelik pulva, presided abru' aifa. "citizen defarge, " leralmin-tor au tor darnay's spayek, u' au nem-tor wuh trel t' dun tor kitau fi'. "nam-tor nash wuh emigrant evrmonde?" "nash nam-tor wuh sasu." "ish-veh ya'shakhuv, evrmonde?" "reh-leh-stehkuh." "telik, evrmonde?" "ha." "wilat telik?" "svi' england." "rik' vet. Wilat nam-tor ish-veh ko-telsu, evrmonde?" "svi' england." "rik' vet. Du nam-tor consigned, evrmonde, tor wuh prison t' la nekwitaya." "aishan sha-ka-ri!" sporiben darnay. "ne' ra tor-gav, heh na' ra offence?" wuh officer glazhau abru s' ish-veh trel t' dun na' wuh moment. "etek ma uzh tor-gav, evrmonde, heh uzh offences, opi' du vesh' la'." au leralmin-tor ish-veh k' wuh lerash abru'teruklar-ru'lut, heh went fi' kitaun. "i entreat du tor glantau ik ki'sarlah nash-veh la' voluntarily, svi' kesaya tor ik written appeal t' wuh katravahsu-countryman if ti fa' du. I haishaya rai weht do wuh opportunity tor tor ni rik' vohtaya. Nam-tor ri ik t'nash-veh gas'rak?" "emigrants ma rai rights, evrmonde, " vesh' wuh stolid kilko. Wuh officer kitau abi' au had shahtau, telv-tor abru' tor himself ra au had written, sanded ish-veh, heh handed ish-veh tor defarge, k' wuh zhit "svi' tsat." defarge motioned k' wuh dun tor wuh prisoner ik au bolau sailau ish-veh. Wuh prisoner obeyed, heh wuh klashausu t' dahkuh armed patriots attended au. "nam-tor ish-veh du, " leralmin-tor defarge, svi' wuh neik spes, u' au went ne' wuh guardhouse ash-tor heh da-tor vi' paris, "vi telik wuh ko-fu t' hassu manette, wuh'wak wuh prisoner svi' wuh bastille ik nam-tor rai weht?" "ha, " kilko-tor darnay, looking na' ish-veh k' ak'wikmun. "t'nash-veh ahm nam-tor defarge, heh i potau wuh wine-mahr-kel svi' wuh yonuk osu antoine. Possibly du ma puzhu-tor t' me." "t'nash-veh ko-telsu sarlah tor ish-veh kelek tor reclaim ish-veh sa-mekh? Ha!" wuh zhit "ko-telsu" seemed tor dvin-tor u' wuh gloomy reminder tor defarge, tor leralmin k' sudden impatience, "svi' wuh ahm t' ik nasik kotik newly-pukeshta, heh puvutau la guillotine, po did sarlah du tor france?" "du puzhu-tor me leralmin po, wuh minute ago. Tor du ri dva-tor ish-veh nam-tor wuh yeht'es?" "wuh rasahkos yeht'es na' du, " leralmin-tor defarge, speaking k' knitted meix'tem, heh looking zehik fa' ish-veh. "indeed i am pakik la'. Ek' la' nam-tor ni unprecedented, ni rubai, ni sudden heh unfair, ik i am absolutely pakik. Dungi du render me wuh pi' gol'nev?" "rim." defarge stariben, kwon-hau-ov looking zehik fa' ish-veh. "dungi du kilko-srashiv me wuh single deshker?" "sos'eh. Fupa s' its malat. Du mokuhlek leralmin ra ish-veh nam-tor." "svi' nash prison ik i am going tor ni unjustly, dungau i ma ein elik sviribaya k' wuh panu s'udish?" "du dungi gla-tor." "i am ri tor nam-tor visolektau tra', prejudged, heh rik' sovek tvai t' presenting t'nash-veh nuf?" "du dungi gla-tor. Tonk'peh, ra yi? Vath sutra ma vesh' similarly visolektau svi' weh-rasahkos prisons, fa' i'." "tonk'peh worla k' me, citizen defarge." defarge glanced darkly na' ish-veh na' kilko-srashiv, heh lates-tor fi' svi' wuh br'xan heh eku silence. Wuh deeper au sank vi' nash silence, wuh fainter rok tra' vesh'--il ni darnay nahp--t' ish-veh softening svi' sovek slight degree. Au, therefore, tor haste tor leralmin: "ish-veh nam-tor t' wuh utmost importance tor me (du fai-tor, citizen, kauk weh-rom do i, t' uf mau importance), ik i dang nam-tor kup tor sviribau tor mr. Lorry t' tellson's kutra, wuh eingelsu gentleman vi nam-tor i' svi' paris, wuh velik kla-min, rik' tuhskaya, ik i ma vesh' lehm-tor vi' wuh prison t' la nekwitaya. Dungi du aishan ik tor nam-tor ovsoh na' me?" "i dungi tor, " defarge doggedly rejoined, "nothing na' du. T'nash-veh gu-vam nam-tor tor t'nash-veh shasol heh wuh sutra. I am wuh sworn dvinsu t' fi', tehnat du. I dungi tor nothing na' du." charles darnay olau ish-veh hopeless tor entreat ish-veh further, heh ish-veh pride vesh' estuhl isha. U' au lates-tor fi' svi' silence, au kupi ri tonk'peh gla-tor uf nam-tor-tor wuh sutra vesh' tor wuh spectacle t' prisoners be' dvun-tor bi' wuh yut. Wuh maut kanu scarcely pubeglanau ish-veh. Wuh zamu passers da-tor ish-veh patam, heh wuh zamu hutau ish-veh ozh na' ish-veh u' wuh aristocrat; vathru, ik wuh sasu svi' rom sai-vel dang nam-tor going tor prison, vesh' rai weht remarkable do ik wuh labourer svi' working sai-vel dang nam-tor going tor ar'kadan. Svi' veh wonil, gu'gelik, heh kitork yut k'fai'ei au be' dvun-tor, wuh teporilau orator, mounted fi' wuh stool, vesh' addressing wuh teporilau audience fi' wuh tr'y'kak tehnat wuh sutra, t' wuh sa-te'kru heh wuh royal skan. Wuh zamu zhit ik au kum-tor s' nash sasu's bru-lar, wuh'rak tor ish-veh fainu tor charles darnay ik wuh sa-te'kru vesh' svi' prison, heh ik wuh k'shatri kevet-dutar had veh heh ek' losrak paris. Fi' wuh fau-yut (kaula na' beauvais) au had puzhu-tor absolutely nothing. Wuh escort heh wuh universal watchfulness had completely isolated ish-veh. Ik au had tevan-tor among irak greater tehvar do eifa if had storik themselves lu au losrak england, au veling fai-tor i'. Ik perils had thickened pa' ish-veh sahris, heh lau thicken faster heh faster wi, au veling fai-tor i'. Au kupi ri tonk'peh nafai-tor tor himself ik au lau ri ma tor nash halovaya, kuv au kupi ma fa-glan-tor wuh pavek t' wuh zamu gad. Heh wi ish-veh misgivings vesh' ri ni gu'gelik u', glenonau k' wuh ta'hal t' nash later wak, au would saudau. Troubled u' wuh fa-wak vesh', ish-veh vesh' wuh ri-fainu fa-wak, heh svi' its obscurity tra' vesh' ignorant rok. Wuh horrible massacre, gad heh mu-yor wu, if, k'svi wuh zamu rounds t' wuh wak-vel, vesh' tor eku wuh lo'uk ulidar t' khaf fi-tor wuh blessed garnering wak t' harvest, vesh' u' irak s' ish-veh fai-tukh u' kuv ish-veh had vesh' wuh hundred thousand tevun maf. Wuh "nasik kotik newly-pukeshta, heh puvutau la guillotine, " vesh' hardly fainu tor ish-veh, il tor wuh generality t' sutra, k' ahm. Wuh frightful deeds ik vesh' tor nam-tor ak ovsoh, vesh' probably unimagined na' ik wak svi' wuh shi'nahp t' wuh doers. Uf kupi au ma wuh shi svi' wuh shadowy conceptions t' wuh gentle kashek? T' unjust skasaya svi' detention heh hardship, heh svi' pi-maat'rer dahshaya s' ish-veh ko-telsu heh kan, au foreshadowed wuh likelihood, il wuh certainty; tonk'peh, mesakh nash, au dreaded nothing distinctly. K' nash fi' ish-veh kashek, if vesh' hiyet tor lesh vi' wuh dreary prison courtyard, au lasha na' wuh prison t' la nekwitaya. Wuh sasu k' wuh bloated limuk tu'ash wuh karik wicket, tor ik defarge presented "wuh emigrant evrmonde." "ra wuh e'shua! Uf wehk weht t' au!" sporiben wuh sasu k' wuh bloated limuk. Defarge nem-tor ish-veh receipt rik' noticing wuh sporun, heh withdrew, k' ish-veh dahkuh katravahsu-patriots. "ra wuh e'shua, i leralmin va'ashiv!" sporiben wuh gaoler, losrak k' ish-veh ko-telsu. "uf wehk weht!" wuh gaoler's ko-telsu, hasu tanilau k' rai kilko-srashiv tor wuh deshker, goh kilko-tor, "veh bolau ma tranush, t'nash-veh tal-kam!" rehkuh turnkeys vi svi-tor responsive tor wuh kus-vakh she rang, echoed wuh sentiment, heh veh hau, "na' wuh ashaya t' liberty; " if sounded svi' ik shi spo' wuh inappropriate conclusion. Wuh prison t' la nekwitaya vesh' wuh gloomy prison, gu'gelik heh filthy, heh k' wuh horrible fnish-tor t' flalik yuk svi' ish-veh. Wehtsuri uf ak wuh noisome zahv t' imprisoned yuk, shetau manifest svi' ek' such shitau ik nam-tor has-bosh palutunau! "svi' tsat, nuh', " grumbled wuh gaoler, looking na' wuh written dun. "u' kuv i vesh' ri already bosh tor bursting!" au terpau wuh dun fi' wuh deik, svi' wuh has-bosh-humour, heh charles darnay awaited ish-veh further sanosh na' ulef wuh wadan: sometimes, pacing tor heh fro svi' wuh karik arched tvi-shal: sometimes, resting fi' wuh kov ku-san: svi' either nuf detained tor nam-tor imprinted fi' wuh vokaya t' wuh chief heh ish-veh subordinates. "sarlah!" leralmin-tor wuh chief, na' wu-vath taking abru ish-veh tal-muv, "sarlah k' me, emigrant." k'fai wuh dismal prison twilight, ish-veh uzh falun accompanied ish-veh k' tvur heh staircase, wehk svep clanging heh locking za' au, abi' sarlah au vi' wuh suk, neik, vaulted tvi-shal, crowded k' prisoners t' fi' guv. Wuh kosu vesh' hayal-tor na' wuh wu pasu, telvan heh kitaun, knitting, ogan, heh embroidering; wuh sasu vesh' na' wuh danik krus standing za' ish-veh ku-san, il svizh-tor abru heh ne' wuh tvi-shal. Svi' wuh instinctive katravek t' prisoners k' shameful tr'y'kak heh disgrace, wuh uzh-comer recoiled s' nash apc'koik. Tonk'peh wuh crowning unreality t' ish-veh wu unreal fau, vesh', ish-veh ek' na' wuh'wak rising tor poprah ish-veh, k' kanok refinement t' manner fainu tor wuh wak, heh k' ek' wuh engaging takov-tor heh nuhk'es t' ha'kiv. Ni strangely clouded vesh' aifa refinements k' wuh prison manners heh gloom, ni spectral did au shetau svi' wuh inappropriate squalor heh misery k'fai'ei au vesh' gla-tor, ik charles darnay seemed tor lamok svi' wuh apc'koik t' wuh tevik. Tam'a ek'! Wuh tam'a t' vaksur, wuh tam'a t' stateliness, wuh tam'a t' sohk'es, wuh tam'a t' pride, wuh tam'a t' frivolity, wuh tam'a t' wit, wuh tam'a t' youth, wuh tam'a t' ya'shakhuv, ek' waiting ish-veh dismissal s' wuh desolate gef, ek' turning fi' ish-veh bezhun ik vesh' rubai k' wuh tevakh au had tev-tor svi' coming tra'. Ish-veh kwul-tor ish-veh motionless. Wuh gaoler standing na' ish-veh vla, heh wuh vath gaolers dvun-tor pa', vi would ma vesh' muhl hiyet u' tor appearance svi' wuh ordinary tusok t' ish-veh nam-tor-lof, glazhau ni extravagantly dirik contrasted k' sorrowing ko-mekh heh svai-tu-ashya daughters vi vesh' tra'--k' wuh apparitions t' wuh coquette, wuh nu'ri vaksur, heh wuh vinik kosu delicately bred--ik wuh abomesaya t' ek' veshtaya heh likelihood if wuh scene t' duv presented, vesh' heightened tor its utmost. Surely, tam'a ek'. Surely, wuh wu unreal fau ein progress t' has ik had katau ish-veh tor aifa gloomy duvek-tor! "svi' wuh ahm t' wuh assembled besu svi' misfortune, " leralmin-tor wuh gentleman t' courtly appearance heh shi'yavekh, coming fa'rak, "i ma wuh dor t' giving du welcome tor la nekwitaya, heh t' condoling k' du fi' wuh calamity ik has katau du akhlami. Lau ish-veh ak terminate kunling! Ish-veh would nam-tor wuh impertinence kitok-wilat, tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor ri ni la', tor ya'akash ish-veh ahm heh nosh?" charles darnay kastorilau himself, heh mazhiv-kur-tor wuh required ro'fori, svi' zhit u' suitable u' au kupi talal. "tonk'peh i rok, " leralmin-tor wuh gentleman, zahalik wuh chief gaoler k' ish-veh bezhun, vi dvun-tor mes' wuh tvi-shal, "ik du nam-tor ri svi' tsat?" "i ri tor ken-tor wuh meaning t' wuh zhil, tonk'peh i ma puzhu-tor au leralmin ni." "ah, ra wuh pity! Etek ni mau regret ish-veh! Tonk'peh nem-tor courage; several kisau t' etwel shila'es ma vesh' svi' tsat, palikauk, heh ish-veh has palesh-tor tonk'peh wuh pen wak." yi au hau, raising ish-veh spes, "i grieve tor inform wuh shila'es--svi' tsat." tra' vesh' wuh murmur t' commiseration u' charles darnay tuhsau wuh tvi-shal tor wuh grated svep wilat wuh gaoler awaited ish-veh, heh wehk spes--among if, wuh mos heh compassionate spes t' kosu vesh' conspicuous--mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh rom istau heh kastoraya. Au da-tor na' wuh grated svep, tor render wuh itaren t' ish-veh khaf-spol; ish-veh a'ing ne' wuh gaoler's el'ru; heh wuh apparitions vanished s' ish-veh glan ek'wak. Wuh wicket tu'ash fi' wuh kov staircase, leading abru'le. Lu au had she-tor keh-leh ash-tor (wuh prisoner t' ulef wuh wadan already tum-tor au), wuh gaoler tu'ash wuh neik nesh-kur svep, heh au be' dvun-tor vi' wuh solitary nala. Ish-veh kwul-tor samu heh damp, tonk'peh vesh' ri gu'gelik. "ish-veh, " leralmin-tor wuh gaoler. "po am i confined sa'awek?" "uf tor i fai-tor!" "i mokuhlek mahr-tor pen, neshuk, heh dun?" "such nam-tor ri t'nash-veh zek. Du dungi nam-tor yaretau, heh mokuhlek ya'akash yi. Na' la', du lau mahr-tor ish-veh yem-tukh, heh nothing weht." tra' vesh' svi' wuh nala, wuh ku-san, wuh pasu, heh wuh terp yuk-vel. U' wuh gaoler tor wuh paik inspection t' aifa vel, heh t' wuh kehkuh temok, fa' going si', wuh wandering fancy czar-tor k'fai wuh kashek t' wuh prisoner leaning tehnat wuh temok mesyutik tor ish-veh, ik nash gaoler vesh' ni unwholesomely bloated, fi' svi' limuk heh person, u' tor glazhau spo' wuh sasu vi had vesh' mastevau heh boshau k' masu. Lu wuh gaoler vesh' hal-tor, au nahp svi' wuh ka wandering yut, "i' am i losrak, u' kuv i vesh' tevik." stopping yi, tor glazhau ne' na' wuh yuk-vel, au da-tor s' ish-veh k' wuh has-bosh olaya, heh nahp, "heh la' svi' aifa crawling creatures nam-tor wuh wuh'rak nosh t' wuh ak'shem po' tevakh." "kaukuh sahr-tor k' kehkuh heh wuh ulef, kaukuh sahr-tor k' kehkuh heh wuh ulef, kaukuh sahr-tor k' kehkuh heh wuh ulef." wuh prisoner lates-tor tor heh fro svi' ish-veh nala, counting its thon, heh wuh roar t' wuh kahr arose spo' nessau vluhn k' wuh kwai puv-tor t' spes hau tor au. "au tor ash'el, au tor ash'el, au tor ash'el." wuh prisoner tum-tor wuh thon va'ashiv, heh sahr-tor faster, tor bes-tor ish-veh kashek k' ish-veh s' ik latter repetition. "wuh tam'a ik vanished lu wuh wicket a'ing. Tra' vesh' veh among au, wuh appearance t' wuh t'sai sai-vel-tor svi' nesh-kur, vi vesh' leaning svi' wuh embrasure t' wuh krani, heh she had wuh ta'hal shining fi-tor ish-veh pi-maat-kur isachya, heh she glazhau spo' * * * * kal-tor etek fau fi' va'ashiv, na' oekon's sake, k'fai wuh illuminated pi'kahr k' wuh sutra ek' kum'i! * * * * au tor ash'el, au tor ash'el, au tor ash'el. * * * * kaukuh sahr-tor k' kehkuh heh wuh ulef." k' such moguhsh tossing heh rolling abru'le s' wuh gluder t' ish-veh kashek, wuh prisoner lates-tor faster heh faster, obstinately counting heh counting; heh wuh roar t' wuh kahr rubai tor nash sadvun--ik ish-veh fam dvun padukau svi' spo' nessau vluhn, tonk'peh k' wuh wail t' spes ik au fai-tor, svi' wuh puv-tor ik she-tor abru' au. Chapter ii. Wuh grindstone tellson's kutra, afer-tor svi' wuh osu germain yonuk t' paris, vesh' svi' wuh rala t' wuh suk kelek, betau k' wuh courtyard heh ikap-tor ska' s' wuh yut k' wuh pid temok heh wuh karik temep. Wuh kelek belonged tor wuh lo'uk nobleman vi had ha-tor svi' ish-veh abi' au tor wuh hash s' wuh troubles, svi' ish-veh sha' fas-tor's sai-vel, heh prah mes' wuh ek'zehl. Wuh mere beast t' wuh a'vesh' hashan s' shi'ka'ree, au vesh' fam dvun svi' ish-veh metempsychosis rai vath do wuh ka monseigneur, wuh preparation t' t'vi chocolate na' t'vi bru-lar had wuh'wak occupied rehkuh karik sasu isha wuh fas-tor svi' deshker. Monseigneur hal-tor, heh wuh rehkuh karik sasu absolving themselves s' wuh sin t' having drawn ish-veh pid wages, k' hasu weht do pok heh willing tor tresahk ish-veh drahk fi' wuh altar t' wuh dawning republic veh heh indivisible t' liberty, ka'es, fraternity, il tevakh, monseigneur's kelek had vesh' wuh'rak sequestrated, heh yi confiscated. Na', ek' vel dvun-tor ni sahris, heh decree zahal-tor decree k' ik kei sa-sovaya, ik i' fi-tor wuh wuh mu-yor t' wuh tasmin tevun-krus t' september, patriot emissaries t' wuh tor-gav vesh' svi' mat t' monseigneur's kelek, heh had pu'ulidau ish-veh k' wuh tri-kur, heh vesh' drinking brandy svi' its fupa s' ha-shal. Wuh shi' business svi' london spo' tellson's shi' business svi' paris, would ak ma driven wuh kelek s' its kashek heh vi' wuh gazette. Na', ra would staid british responsibility heh respectability ma leralmin-tor tor zhar-kur-lap svi' natuhn svi' wuh kutra courtyard, heh kauk tor wuh cupid abru' wuh tumek? Wi such vel vesh'. Tellson's had whitewashed wuh cupid, tonk'peh au vesh' fam dvun tor nam-tor gla-tor fi' wuh abru-tol, svi' wuh coolest linen, aiming (u' au maut k'ashiv tor) na' donku s' asal tor mu-yor. Bankruptcy bolau inevitably ma sarlah t' nash nu'ri pagan, svi' lombard-yut, london, heh isha t' wuh curtained alcove svi' wuh za' t' wuh immortal sa-kan, heh isha t' wuh looking-makh kal-tor vi' wuh temok, heh isha t' clerks mokov hinek, vi tam-tor svi' tsuri fi' wuh slightest provocation. Wi, wuh french tellson's kupi prah fi' k' aifa vel exceedingly muhl, heh, u' wu u' wuh wak meskarau teretuhr, rai sasu had taken kolthak na' au, heh drawn si' ish-veh donku. Ra donku would nam-tor drawn s' tellson's henceforth, heh ra would ti tra', pakik heh yen-tor; ra math heh ek'zer would tarnish svi' tellson's hiding-shitau, du' wuh depositors zhar-tor svi' prisons, heh lu au dang ma violently perished; uf wehk khrosahp k' tellson's worla tor nam-tor um'ro svi' nash panu, bolau nam-tor lesh abru' vi' wuh thurai; rai sasu kupi ma leralmin-tor, ik mu-yor, sovek weht do mr. Jarvis lorry kupi, hi au nahp heavily t' aifa deshkau. Au hayal-tor k' wuh newly-lighted lapan yon (wuh blighted heh unfruitful tevun vesh' prematurely samu), heh fi' ish-veh trau heh courageous limuk tra' vesh' wuh deeper duvek do wuh pendent ha'gelek kupi lehm, il sovek vel svi' wuh tvi-shal distortedly haul-tor--wuh duvek t' horror. Au occupied tvi-shal svi' wuh kutra, svi' ish-veh fidelity tor wuh kelek t' if au had grown tor nam-tor wuh krus, spo' karik gir-ivy. Ish-veh chanced ik au derived wuh ves t' shar'es s' wuh patriotic occupation t' wuh nen kelek, tonk'peh wuh yeht-hearted hinek gentleman worla ka'pra pa' ik. Ek' such circumstances vesh' indifferent tor ish-veh, ni ik au did ish-veh gu-vam. Fi' wuh mesyutik vla t' wuh courtyard, ne' wuh colonnade, vesh' extensive standing--na' carriages--wilat, indeed, ein carriages t' monseigneur wi lam-tor. Tehnat dahkuh t' wuh pillars vesh' terau dahkuh lo'uk flaring flambeaux, heh svi' wuh ta'hal t' aifa, standing si' svi' wuh tu'ash sov, vesh' wuh suk grindstone: wuh roughly mounted vel if saudau ki' hurriedly vesh' katau tra' s' ein neighbouring smithy, il vath zup-shal. Rising heh looking s' krani na' aifa harmless vel, mr. Lorry shivered, heh retired tor ish-veh ku-san k' wuh yon. Au had tu'ash, ri goh wuh makh krani, tonk'peh wuh nentu-vis glan-fam s'udish ish-veh, heh au had a'ing fi' va'ashiv, heh au shivered k'fai ish-veh nentu. S' wuh yut mesakh wuh pid temok heh wuh karik temep, tra' sarlah wuh tsuri mu-yor hum t' wuh kahr, k' i' heh yi wuh indescribable mokov svi' ish-veh, flekh heh unearthly, u' kuv ein unwonted sounds t' wuh terrible malat vesh' going abru tor sha-ka-ri. "itaren oekon, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, clasping ish-veh el'ru, "ik kling be' heh tal-kam tor me nam-tor svi' nash dreadful kahr tor-mu-yor. Lau au ma mercy fi' ek' vi nam-tor svi' tehvar!" ak afterwards, wuh kus-vakh na' wuh lo'uk temep sounded, heh au nahp, "sarlah au pla'!" heh hayal-tor listening. Tonk'peh, tra' vesh' rai ral irruption vi' wuh courtyard, u' au had gishu, heh au puzhu-tor wuh temep clash va'ashiv, heh ek' vesh' hizhuk. Wuh nervousness heh dread ik vesh' fi-tor ish-veh vi'le-esh-tor ik vague uneasiness respecting wuh kutra, if wuh lo'uk rubah would naturally awaken, k' such feelings kastorilau. Ish-veh vesh' muhl klashau, heh au prah abru tor hal-tor among wuh trusty sutra vi vesh' watching ish-veh, lu ish-veh svep suddenly tu'ash, heh dahkuh khlop rushed svi', na' glan t' if au tevan-tor pla' svi' tauraya. Lucie heh ish-veh sa-mekh! Lucie k' ish-veh kar sakadau si' tor ish-veh, heh k' ik hinek glazhau t' earnestness ni concentrated heh intensified, ik ish-veh seemed u' hi ish-veh had vesh' stamped fi-tor ish-veh limuk expressly tor mazhiv-kur-tor nekwitaya heh tepul tor ish-veh svi' nash-veh tvur t' ish-veh ha'kiv. "ra nam-tor nash?" maf-tor mr. Lorry, breathless heh confused. "ra nam-tor wuh tukh? Lucie! Manette! Ra has pavesh-tor? Ra has katau du la'? Ra nam-tor ish-veh?" k' wuh glazhau teslau fi-tor ish-veh, svi' ish-veh paleness heh wildness, she panted si' svi' ish-veh kar, imploringly, "o t'nash-veh tal-kam t'hy'la! T'nash-veh sa-telsu!" "ish-veh sa-telsu, lucie?" "charles." "ra t' charles?" "la'. "la', svi' paris?" "has vesh' la' ein gad--rehkuh il kehkuh--i ri tor fai-tor uf wehk--i mokuhlek't tershau t'nash-veh nahp. Wuh skrol t' generosity katau ish-veh la' ri-fainu tor etek; au vesh' pehkau na' wuh foshek, heh satau tor prison." wuh hinek sasu uttered wuh irrepressible maf. Siyah na' wuh ka moment, wuh kus-vakh t' wuh lo'uk temep rang va'ashiv, heh wuh ral ralash t' ash'ya heh spes sarlah pouring vi' wuh courtyard. "ra nam-tor ik ralash?" leralmin-tor wuh hassu, turning na' wuh krani. "ri tor glazhau!" maf-tor mr. Lorry. "ri tor glazhau si'! Manette, na' ish-veh ha'kiv, ri tor esta wuh glan-fam!" wuh hassu da-tor, k' ish-veh el'ru fi-tor wuh fastening t' wuh krani, heh leralmin-tor, k' wuh samuyau, vakh abru'teruklar-ru'lut: "t'nash-veh tal-kam t'hy'la, i ma wuh sem-rik-tor ha'kiv svi' nash kahr. I ma vesh' wuh bastille prisoner. Tra' nam-tor rai patriot svi' paris--svi' paris? Svi' france--vi, fai-tor me ki' vesh' wuh prisoner svi' wuh bastille, would esta me, kaula tor overwhelm me k' nartau, il lesh me svi' triumph. T'nash-veh hinek kusut has putan-tor me wuh tepul ik has katau etek k'fai wuh foshek, heh nazh-tor etek ro'fori t' charles tra', heh katau etek la'. I fai-tor ish-veh would nam-tor ni; i fai-tor i kupi gol'nev charles s' ek' tehvar; i var-tor lucie ni.--ra nam-tor ik ralash?" ish-veh el'ru vesh' va'ashiv fi-tor wuh krani. "ri tor glazhau!" maf-tor mr. Lorry, absolutely desperate. "rai, lucie, t'nash-veh tal-kam, il du!" au prah ish-veh kar pauk ish-veh, heh meskarau ish-veh. "ri tor nam-tor ni terrified, t'nash-veh ashaya. I solemnly swear tor du ik i fai-tor t' rai klau having pavesh-tor tor charles; ik i had rai suspicion kauk t' ish-veh hasu svi' nash fatal shi. Ra prison nam-tor au svi'?" "la nekwitaya!" "la nekwitaya! Lucie, t'nash-veh kan, kuv ek'wak du vesh' kyi'i heh serviceable svi' ish-veh ha'kiv--heh du vesh' kwon-hau-ov fi'--du dungi tertitau yourself i', tor tor exactly u' i nufai du; na' weht nerau fi-tor ish-veh do du mokuhlek nah-tor, il i mokuhlek leralmin. Tra' nam-tor rai gol'nev na' du svi' sovek torai fi' ish-veh krus tor-mu-yor; du fam yehat possibly stir si'. I leralmin nash, fai'ei ra i bolau nufai du tor tor na' charles's sake, nam-tor wuh hardest vel tor tor t' ek'. Du bolau instantly nam-tor obedient, fam dvun, heh hizhuk. Du bolau kal-tor me shitau du svi' wuh tvi-shal na' wuh pla' la'. Du bolau trasha ish-veh sa-mekh heh me sa'awek na' dahkuh minutes, heh u' tra' nam-tor ha'kiv heh tevakh svi' wuh panu du bolau ri vohtaya." "i dungi nam-tor nepik tor du. Gla-tor nash-veh svi' ish-veh limuk ik du fai-tor i mokuhlek tor nothing else do nash. I fai-tor du nam-tor yeht." wuh hinek sasu shok-tor ish-veh, heh hurried ish-veh vi' ish-veh tvi-shal, heh da-tor wuh tal-muv; yi, sarlah hurrying pla' tor wuh hassu, heh tu'ash wuh krani heh partly tu'ash wuh glan-fam, heh shitau ish-veh el'ru fi-tor wuh hassu's kar, heh glazhau si' k' ish-veh vi' wuh courtyard. Glazhau si' fi-tor wuh throng t' sasu heh kosu: ri hiyet svi' su'etek, il be' hiyet, tor boshaya wuh courtyard: ri weht do keh-leh il kau-leh svi' ek'. Wuh sutra svi' mat t' wuh kelek had kal-tor au svi' na' wuh temep, heh au had rushed svi' tor ar'kadan na' wuh grindstone; ish-veh had evidently vesh' eku abru tra' na' ish-veh lof, u' svi' wuh convenient heh retired gla-tor. Tonk'peh, such awful workers, heh such awful ar'kadan! Wuh grindstone had wuh dahtau el'rek, heh, turning na' ish-veh madly vesh' dahkuh sasu, t'vi limuk, u' ish-veh wu isachya flapped pla' lu wuh whirlings t' wuh grindstone katau ish-veh limuk abru, vesh' weht horrible heh pi-maat'rer do wuh visages t' wuh wildest savages svi' ish-veh danik barbarous pasut. Riyeht bezhun-zehl heh riyeht moustaches vesh' terpau fi-tor au, heh ish-veh hideous countenances vesh' ek' bloody heh sweaty, heh ek' awry k' howling, heh ek' staring heh glaring k' beastly tepor'es heh aitlun t' yuk. U' aifa ruffians da-tor heh da-tor, ish-veh matted klachek i' flung fa'rak abru' ish-veh bezhun, i' flung pla'rak abru' ish-veh talu, ein kosu meskarau wine tor ish-veh ru'lut ik au lau mon; heh ra k' dropping khaf, heh ra k' dropping wine, heh ra k' wuh pilash t' kil-tor kwul-tor s' wuh kov, ek' ish-veh wicked igen-tukh seemed gore heh yon. Wuh bezhun kupi ri patal-tor veh creature svi' wuh travek elik s' wuh smear t' khaf. Shouldering veh wuh'ashiv tor prah thurai na' wuh sharpening-kov, vesh' sasu stripped tor wuh san, k' wuh kuraya ek' abru' ish-veh sikrus heh ak'shem; sasu svi' ek' wihfelau t' a'cit, k' wuh kuraya fi-tor eifa a'cit; sasu devilishly eku ska' k' spoils t' kosu's lace heh silk heh ribbon, k' wuh kuraya dyeing eifa trifles k'fai heh k'fai. Hatchets, lipau, pohshayek-tilek, shek, ek' katau tor nam-tor sharpened, vesh' ek' yon-kur k' ish-veh. Ein t' wuh hacked shek vesh' tied tor wuh kar-nik t' eifa vi lesh au, k' strips t' linen heh karf t' sai-vel: ligatures vuhnauk svi' ves, tonk'peh ek' glu t' wuh veh kur. Heh u' wuh frantic wielders t' aifa wun snatched au s' wuh pilash t' kil-tor heh tore maf vi' wuh yut, wuh ka yon-kur hue vesh' yon-kur svi' ish-veh frenzied bezhun; --bezhun if sovek unbrutalised beholder would ma putan-tor dah-leh tevun t' ha'kiv, tor petrify k' wuh muhl-khartau pohshayek. Ek' nash vesh' gla-tor svi' wuh moment, u' wuh vision t' wuh drowning sasu, il t' sovek komihn creature na' sovek maut lo'uk be' dvun, kupi gla-tor wuh panu kuv ish-veh vesh' tra'. Au drew pla' s' wuh krani, heh wuh hassu glazhau na' danaya svi' ish-veh t'hy'la's ashy limuk. "au nam-tor, " mr. Lorry zhal-tor wuh zhit, glancing fearfully pauk na' wuh klacha tvi-shal, "murdering wuh prisoners. Kuv du nam-tor sure t' ra du leralmin; kuv du really ma wuh tepul du nah-tor du ma--u' i dva-tor du ma--tor yourself fainu tor aifa e'shua, heh prah taken tor la nekwitaya. Ish-veh lau nam-tor nuh' tab-ma, i ri tor fai-tor, tonk'peh kal-tor ish-veh ri nam-tor wuh minute later!" hassu manette hish-tor ish-veh el'ru, hastened bareheaded s' wuh tvi-shal, heh vesh' svi' wuh courtyard lu mr. Lorry tabakau wuh glan-fam. Ish-veh streaming wan-kur isachya, ish-veh remarkable limuk, heh wuh impetuous guhl'es t' ish-veh manner, u' au shitau wuh wun aside spo' masu, lesh ish-veh svi' wuh instant tor wuh khaf-spol t' wuh concourse na' wuh kov. Na' wuh zamu moments tra' vesh' wuh svizh, heh wuh brax, heh wuh murmur, heh wuh unintelligible ralash t' ish-veh spes; heh yi mr. Lorry gla-tor ish-veh, vikuvau k' ek', heh svi' wuh midst t' wuh zehl t' dah-leh sasu wu, ek' punaf-tor tipan tor tipan, heh el'ru tor tipan, hurried si' k' maf-tor t'--"ha-tor wuh bastille prisoner! Gol'nev na' wuh bastille prisoner's kindred svi' la nekwitaya! Tvi-shal na' wuh bastille prisoner svi' khom tra'! Korsau wuh prisoner evrmonde na' la nekwitaya!" heh wuh thousand answering saul-tor. Au a'ing wuh nentu-vis va'ashiv k' wuh fluttering khaf-spol, a'ing wuh krani heh wuh curtain, hastened tor lucie, heh var-tor ish-veh ik ish-veh sa-mekh vesh' gol-tor k' wuh sutra, heh hal-tor svi' psthan t' ish-veh sa-telsu. Au afer-tor ish-veh kan heh din-tor pross k' ish-veh; tonk'peh, ish-veh worla paresh-tor tor ish-veh tor nam-tor ak'wikmun k' ish-veh appearance abi' wuh akarshif afterwards, lu au hayal-tor watching au svi' such hizhuk u' wuh mu-yor fai-tor. Lucie had, k' ik wak, tevan-tor vi' wuh stupor fi' wuh lan-tol na' ish-veh ash'ya, clinging tor ish-veh el'ru. Din-tor pross had laid wuh kan ne' fi' ish-veh sha' sar-tak, heh ish-veh patam had gradually tevan-tor fi' wuh trak be' ish-veh takov falun. O wuh wu, wu mu-yor, k' wuh nau t' wuh ri donku-tor ko-telsu! Heh o wuh wu, wu mu-yor, k' rai fun t' ish-veh sa-mekh heh rai tidings! Dah'wak weht svi' wuh mu'khlup'es wuh kus-vakh na' wuh lo'uk temep sounded, heh wuh irruption vesh' ashiv-tor, heh wuh grindstone whirled heh spluttered. "ra nam-tor ish-veh?" maf-tor lucie, affrighted. "hush! Wuh ask'ersu' shek nam-tor sharpened tra', " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry. "wuh shi nam-tor national veltra i', heh nam-tor-tor u' wuh ves t' shi'wun, t'nash-veh ashaya." dah'wak weht svi' ek'; tonk'peh, wuh kim-shah spell t' ar'kadan vesh' kobat heh fitful. Ak afterwards wuh gad began tor gad-keshtan, heh au softly dahl-tor himself s' wuh clasping el'ru, heh cautiously glazhau si' va'ashiv. Wuh sasu, ni besmeared ik au lau ma vesh' wuh sorely wounded ask'ersu creeping pla' tor hokni'es fi' wuh vunai t' slain, vesh' rising s' wuh pavement k' wuh vla t' wuh grindstone, heh looking pa' ish-veh k' wuh vacant sov. Shortly, nash worn-si' murderer descried svi' wuh imperfect ta'hal veh t' wuh carriages t' monseigneur, heh, staggering tor ik gorgeous hali, sasu-tor svi' na' wuh svep, heh ikap-tor himself abru tor nem-tor ish-veh shom fi' its dainty an'kar. Wuh lo'uk grindstone, terra, had da-tor lu mr. Lorry glazhau si' va'ashiv, heh wuh yel vesh' yon-kur fi' wuh courtyard. Tonk'peh, wuh lesser grindstone lam-tor sa'awek tra' svi' wuh hayal asal sov, k' wuh yon-kur fi-tor ish-veh ik wuh yel had worla putan-tor, heh would worla nem-tor maf. Chapter iii. Wuh duv veh t' wuh wuh'rak considerations if arose svi' wuh business kashek t' mr. Lorry lu business wadan sarlah pauk, vesh' nash: --ik au had rai gas'rak tor imperil tellson's k' sheltering wuh ko-telsu t' wuh emigrant prisoner ne' wuh kutra kamu.
