Ish-veh sha' ma-vel, ek'manek, ha'kiv, au would ma hazarded na' lucie heh ish-veh kan, rik' wuh moment's demur; tonk'peh wuh lo'uk sahrafel au meskarau vesh' ri ish-veh sha', heh u' tor ik business falun au vesh' wuh wonil sasu t' business. Palikauk, ish-veh kashek reverted tor defarge, heh au nahp t' finding si' wuh wine-mahr-kel va'ashiv heh taking counsel k' its trensu svi' dzhinaya tor wuh safest kelek-shi svi' wuh saglakolau fupa s' t' wuh kahr. Tonk'peh, wuh ka consideration ik suggested ish-veh, repudiated ish-veh; au ha-tor svi' wuh danik khrashik yonuk, heh doubtless vesh' influential tra', heh glu svi' its tehvar-bosh workings. Aru coming, heh wuh hassu ri returning, heh kanok minute's vohtaya tending tor compromise tellson's, mr. Lorry na'shikhau k' lucie. She leralmin-tor ik ish-veh sa-mekh had spoken t' hiring wuh lodging na' wuh pen zhil, svi' ik yonuk, be' wuh banking-kelek. U' tra' vesh' rai business objection tor nash, heh u' au foresaw ik kauk kuv ish-veh vesh' ek' muhl k' charles, heh au vesh' tor nam-tor sadalau, au kupi ri rok tor trasha wuh kahr, mr. Lorry went si' svi' psthan t' such wuh lodging, heh afer-tor wuh suitable veh, pid abru svi' wuh snem-tor k'-yut wilat wuh a'ing blinds svi' ek' wuh vath krani t' wuh pid melancholy keh-vla t' kelek pu'ulidau deserted ha-kel. Tor nash lodging au na' wuh'wak snem-tor lucie heh ish-veh kan, heh din-tor pross: giving au ra comfort au kupi, heh mau weht do au had himself. Au losrak jerry k' au, u' wuh khlop tor boshaya wuh svep-sharu ik would lesh considerable knocking fi' wuh patam, heh fun-tor tor ish-veh sha' occupations. Wuh ertau heh doleful kashek au katau tor lesh fi-tor au, heh slowly heh heavily wuh gad lagged fi' k' ish-veh. Ish-veh sai-vel-tor itself si', heh sai-vel-tor ish-veh si' k' ish-veh, abi' wuh kutra a'ing. Au vesh' va'ashiv sa'awek svi' ish-veh tvi-shal t' wuh previous mu-yor, panahik ra tor tor thurai, lu au puzhu-tor wuh ash'ya fi-tor wuh stair. Svi' wuh zamu moments, wuh sasu lam-tor svi' ish-veh la'es, vi, k' wuh keenly observant glazhau na' ish-veh, addressed ish-veh k' ish-veh ahm. "ish-veh dvinsu, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry. "tor du fai-tor me?" au vesh' wuh strongly tor sasu k' gu'gelik tcha-tor isachya, s' keh-leh-kaukuh tor kau-leh tevun t' ya'shakhuv. Na' kilko-srashiv au ashiv-tor, rik' sovek rubah t' emphasis, wuh zhit: "tor du fai-tor me?" "ki'gla-tor nash-veh du ein-wilat." "sos'eh na' t'nash-veh wine-mahr-kel?" mau interested heh pahutau, mr. Lorry leralmin-tor: "sarlah du s' hassu manette?" "ha. Sarlah nash-veh s' hassu manette." "heh ra leralmin-tor au? Ra tor au satau me?" defarge mazhiv-kur-tor vi' ish-veh anxious el'ru, wuh tu'ash moguhsh t' dun. Ish-veh spitau wuh zhit svi' wuh hassu's kitaun: "charles nam-tor safe, tonk'peh i fam yehat safely trasha nash shi wi. I ma prah wuh favour ik wuh bearer has wuh pen pitoh s' charles tor ish-veh ko-telsu. Kal-tor wuh bearer gla-tor ish-veh ko-telsu." ish-veh vesh' dated s' la nekwitaya, k'svi wuh wadan. "dungi du sailau me, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, joyfully vas-tor po' telvan nash pitoh aloud, "tor wilat ish-veh ko-telsu resides?" "ha, " fun-tor defarge. Scarcely noticing u' wi, svi' ra wuh curiously reserved heh mechanical yut defarge stariben, mr. Lorry shitau fi' ish-veh taik heh au went ne' vi' wuh courtyard. Tra', au afer-tor dahkuh kosu; veh, knitting. "madame defarge, surely!" leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, vi had losrak ish-veh svi' exactly wuh ka attitude ein leh- steh tevun ago. "ish-veh nam-tor she, " glantau ish-veh sa-telsu. "tor madame hal-tor k' etek?" inquired mr. Lorry, seeing ik she dvun-tor u' au dvun-tor. "ha. Ik she lau nam-tor kup tor naglanshau wuh limuk heh fai-tor wuh persons. Ish-veh nam-tor na' ish-veh ek'manek." palikaya tor nam-tor kwul-tor k' defarge's manner, mr. Lorry glazhau dubiously na' ish-veh, heh pufulag-tor wuh yut. Fi' wuh kosu zahal-tor; wuh dahr kosu hasu wuh vengeance. Au be' dvun-tor k'fai wuh intervening yut u' sahris u' au lau, she-tor wuh staircase t' wuh uzh domicile, vesh' nafai-tor k' jerry, heh afer-tor lucie weeping, sa'awek. She vesh' lehm-tor vi' wuh ifis-hali k' wuh tidings mr. Lorry mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh t' ish-veh sa-telsu, heh clasped wuh el'ru ik tefu ish-veh pitoh--pi' thinking ra ish-veh had vesh' doing be' ish-veh svi' wuh mu-yor, heh lau, tonk'peh na' wuh pavesh, ma ovsoh tor ish-veh. "dearest, --nem-tor courage. I am muhl, heh ish-veh sa-mekh has vi-yumuk pa' me. Du fam yehat kilko-srashiv nash. Shok etwel kan na' me." ik vesh' ek' wuh kitaun. Ish-veh vesh' ni mau, however, tor ish-veh vi poprah ish-veh, ik she da-tor s' defarge tor ish-veh ko-telsu, heh shok-tor veh t' wuh el'ru ik knitted. Ish-veh vesh' wuh passionate, loving, itar-bosh, womanly torai, tonk'peh wuh el'ru tor rai kesaya--eku-tor samu heh ras, heh nem-tor tor its knitting va'ashiv. Tra' vesh' vel svi' its esta ik mazhiv-kur-tor lucie wuh rihamau. She pehkau svi' wuh bae'cok t' putting wuh pitoh svi' ish-veh bosom, heh, k' ish-veh el'ru wi na' ish-veh talu, glazhau terrified na' madame defarge. Madame defarge ragel-tor wuh abertau bezhun-zehl heh fa-patam k' wuh samu, impassive nantaya. "t'nash-veh tal-kam, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, striking svi' tor danau; "tra' nam-tor vakavik risings svi' wuh yut; heh, hi ish-veh nam-tor ri kesik au dungi ek'wak trouble du, madame defarge istau tor gla-tor eifa ik she has wuh tepul tor protect na' such wak, tor wuh shaht ik she lau fai-tor au--ik she lau shasutan-tor au. I dva-tor, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, rather halting svi' ish-veh reassuring zhit, u' wuh stony manner t' ek' wuh rehkuh impressed itself fi-tor ish-veh weht heh weht, "i fupa s' wuh nuf, citizen defarge?" defarge glazhau gloomily na' ish-veh ko-telsu, heh mazhiv-kur-tor rai vath kilko-srashiv do wuh gruff ralash t' acquiescence. "du had weh-rom, lucie, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, doing ek' au kupi tor propitiate, k' molu heh manner, "ma wuh tal-kam kan la', heh etwel rom pross. Etwel rom pross, defarge, nam-tor wuh eingelsu t'sai, heh fai-tor rai french." wuh t'sai svi' deshker, t'vi rooted conviction ik she vesh' weht do wuh match na' sovek k'shatrisu, vesh' ri tor nam-tor shaken k' flakosh heh, tehvar, saudau k' hesha kar, heh glantau svi' eingelsu tor wuh vengeance, ik ish-veh bezhun wuh'rak snagel-tor, "muhl, i am sure, boldface! I rok du nam-tor takov muhl!" she isha bestowed wuh british huhsh fi' madame defarge; tonk'peh, neither t' wuh dahkuh nem-tor mau heed t' ish-veh. "nam-tor ik ish-veh kan?" leralmin-tor madame defarge, stopping svi' ish-veh ar'kadan na' wuh wuh'rak wak, heh pointing ish-veh knitting-og-lum na' pi' lucie u' kuv ish-veh vesh' wuh ozh t' buk. "ha, madame, " kilko-tor mr. Lorry; "nash nam-tor etwel ri donku-tor prisoner's ashal-veh ko-fu, heh goh kan." wuh duv attendant fi' madame defarge heh ish-veh party seemed tor tevan ni threatening heh gu'gelik fi' wuh kan, ik ish-veh ko-mekh instinctively kneeled fi' wuh solektra be' ish-veh, heh meskarau ish-veh tor ish-veh thasek. Wuh duv attendant fi' madame defarge heh ish-veh party seemed yi tor tevan, threatening heh gu'gelik, fi' fi' wuh ko-mekh heh wuh kan. "ish-veh nam-tor hiyet, t'nash-veh sa-telsu, " leralmin-tor madame defarge. "ki'gla-tor nash-veh au. Etek lau hal-tor." tonk'peh, wuh nelau manner had hiyet t' menace svi' ish-veh--ri visible heh presented, tonk'peh indistinct heh withheld--tor vikayek lucie vi' taran, u' she laid ish-veh appealing el'ru fi' madame defarge's sai-vel: "du dungi nam-tor rom tor t'nash-veh ri donku-tor sa-telsu. Du dungi tor ish-veh rai klau. Du dungi gol'nev me tor gla-tor ish-veh kuv du mokuhlek?" "ish-veh sa-telsu nam-tor ri t'nash-veh business la', " fun-tor madame defarge, looking ne' na' ish-veh k' buhfik composure. "ish-veh nam-tor wuh ko-fu t' ish-veh sa-mekh vi nam-tor t'nash-veh business la'." "na' t'nash-veh sake, yi, nam-tor merciful tor t'nash-veh sa-telsu. Na' t'nash-veh kan's sake! She dungi shitau ish-veh el'ru teretuhr heh pray du tor nam-tor merciful. Etek nam-tor weht kwes t' du do t' aifa vath." madame defarge poprah ish-veh u' wuh compliment, heh glazhau na' ish-veh sa-telsu. Defarge, vi had vesh' uneasily biting ish-veh kaur-ozh-felu heh looking na' ish-veh, tershau ish-veh limuk vi' wuh sterner sagluvaya. "ra nam-tor ish-veh ik ish-veh sa-telsu leralmin-tor svi' ik pi' nuhm?" ya'akash madame defarge, k' wuh lowering abru'teruklar-ru'lut. "vi-yumuk; au leralmin-tor vel touching vi-yumuk?" "ik t'nash-veh sa-mekh, " leralmin-tor lucie, hurriedly taking wuh dun s' ish-veh thasek, tonk'peh k' ish-veh alarmed bezhun fi' ish-veh questioner heh ri fi' ish-veh, "has mau vi-yumuk pa' ish-veh." "surely ish-veh dungi sadalaya ish-veh!" leralmin-tor madame defarge. "kal-tor ish-veh tor ni." "u' wuh ko-telsu heh ko-mekh, " maf-tor lucie, danik earnestly, "i implore du tor ma pity fi' me heh ri tor tusok sovek tepul ik du ma, tehnat t'nash-veh innocent sa-telsu, tonk'peh tor nam-tor-tor ish-veh svi' ish-veh behalf. O ko-kai-kosu, nah-tor t' me. U' wuh ko-telsu heh ko-mekh!" madame defarge glazhau, coldly u' ek'wak, na' wuh suppliant, heh leralmin-tor, turning tor ish-veh t'hy'la wuh vengeance: "wuh ko-telsu heh ko-mekh etek ma vesh' nam-tor-tor tor gla-tor, opi' etek vesh' u' pi' u' nash kan, heh mau lehkuh, ma ri vesh' greatly panah-tor? Etek ma fainu ish-veh sa-telsu heh sa-mekh laid svi' prison heh potau s' au, k'ashiv hiyet? Ek' etwel ha-tor, gla-tor etek etwel ko-kai-kosu dash, svi' themselves heh svi' ish-veh kanu, poverty, nakedness, avon, mag, has-mar, misery, oppression heh neglect t' ek' ves?" "gla-tor etek nothing else, " fun-tor wuh vengeance. "etek ma borne nash wuh akarshif, " leralmin-tor madame defarge, turning ish-veh bezhun va'ashiv fi-tor lucie. "judge du! Nam-tor ish-veh kesik ik wuh trouble t' veh ko-telsu heh ko-mekh would nam-tor mau tor etek i'?" she resumed ish-veh knitting heh went si'. Wuh vengeance zahal-tor. Defarge went kim-shah, heh a'ing wuh svep. "courage, t'nash-veh tal-kam lucie, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, u' au ashenau ish-veh. "courage, courage! Ni irak ek' hal-tor muhl k' etek--mau, mau weh-rom do ish-veh has t' tab-ma hal-tor k' wehk ri donku-tor souls. Cheer abru, heh ma wuh itar-bosh khaf-spol." "i am ri thankless, i rok, tonk'peh ik dreadful kosu seems tor lehm wuh duv fi' me heh fi' ek' t'nash-veh rok-tor." "tut, tut!" leralmin-tor mr. Lorry; "ra nam-tor nash despondency svi' wuh kyi'i pi' thasek? Wuh duv indeed! Rai substance svi' ish-veh, lucie." tonk'peh wuh duv t' wuh manner t' aifa defarges vesh' gu'gelik fi-tor himself, na' ek' ik, heh svi' ish-veh tsat kashek ish-veh troubled ish-veh greatly. Chapter iv. Hayal svi' sahriv hassu manette did ri fun abi' wuh asal t' wuh fourth gad t' ish-veh absence. Ni mau t' ra had pavesh-tor svi' ik dreadful wak u' kupi nam-tor potau s' wuh fai-tukh t' lucie vesh' ni muhl ip-sut s' ish-veh, ik ri abi' wu afterwards, lu france heh she vesh' irak k'wuhli, did she fai-tor ik leh-wun hundred defenceless prisoners t' fi' guv heh ek' ya'shakhuv had vesh' pustau k' wuh sutra; ik kehkuh gad heh mu-yor had vesh' mu'glau k' nash deed t' horror; heh ik wuh sov pa' ish-veh had vesh' tainted k' wuh slain. She goh fai-tor ik tra' had vesh' wuh nashiv-tor fi-tor wuh prisons, ik ek' political prisoners had vesh' svi' tehvar, heh ik ein had vesh' zaseshau si' k' wuh patreitan heh riyeht-stau. Tor mr. Lorry, wuh hassu sviribau ne' wuh injunction t' secrecy fi' if au had rai bolaya tor dwell, ik wuh patreitan had taken ish-veh k'fai wuh scene t' carnage tor wuh prison t' la nekwitaya. Ik, svi' wuh prison au had afer-tor wuh shal-kru'minaakh tribunal sitting, fa' if wuh prisoners vesh' katau singly, heh k' if au vesh' rapidly ordered tor nam-tor shitau forth tor nam-tor massacred, il tor nam-tor sadalau, il (svi' wuh zamu nuf) tor nam-tor satau pla' tor ish-veh nala. Ik, presented k' ish-veh spayek tor nash tribunal, au had tor'pra himself k' ahm heh ha'yigal u' having vesh' na' leh-oh tevun wuh tsat heh unaccused prisoner svi' wuh bastille; ik, veh t' wuh ak'shem ni sitting svi' judgment had risen heh shasutan-tor ish-veh, heh ik nash sasu vesh' defarge. Ik, hereupon au had ascertained, k'fai wuh registers fi' wuh pasu, ik ish-veh sa-fu-svi'-tor-gav vesh' among wuh living prisoners, heh had pleaded lerash tor wuh tribunal--t' ik ein kisau vesh' asleep heh ein kum'i, ein kitork k' riyeht-staya heh ein sok'i, ein sober heh ein ri--na' ish-veh ha'kiv heh liberty. Ik, svi' wuh wuh'rak frantic na'shaya lavished fi' himself u' wuh notable sufferer ne' wuh overthrown torektra, ish-veh had vesh' accorded tor ish-veh ki' charles darnay katau fa' wuh lawless kelek, heh linisau. Ik, au seemed fi' wuh sfek t' hasu na' wuh'wak sadalau, lu wuh mashen svi' ish-veh favour ragel-tor k' ein unexplained rihamau (ri intelligible tor wuh hassu), if pufulag-tor tor wuh zamu zhit t' tsat conference. Ik, wuh sasu sitting u' president had yi informed hassu manette ik wuh prisoner bolau hafau svi' custody, tonk'peh dang, na' ish-veh sake, nam-tor meskarau inviolate svi' safe custody. Ik, iyi, fi' wuh glantokaya, wuh prisoner vesh' snem-tor tor wuh interior t' wuh prison va'ashiv; tonk'peh, ik au, wuh hassu, had yi ni strongly pleaded na' permission tor hafau heh assure himself ik ish-veh sa-fu-svi'-tor-gav vesh', k'fai rai malice il mischance, tefu tor wuh concourse t'vi murderous saul-tor s'udish wuh temep had k'ashiv mastevau wuh proceedings, ik au had prah wuh permission, heh had hafau svi' ik tvur t' khaf abi' wuh tehvar vesh' abru'. Wuh sights au had gla-tor tra', k' brief snatches t' yem-tukh heh yuk k' tvi-wak, dungau hafau untold. Wuh mad mak abru' wuh prisoners vi vesh' korsau, had astounded ish-veh scarcely lehkuh tor wuh mad keimen'es tehnat eifa vi vesh' tresahk tor krus. Veh prisoner tra' vesh', au leralmin-tor, vi had vesh' khrasau vi' wuh yut elik, tonk'peh na' ik wuh mistaken savage had kwit wuh pike u' au be' dvun-tor si'. Hasu besought tor hal-tor tor ish-veh heh sai-vel wuh skek, wuh hassu had be' dvun-tor si' na' wuh ka temep, heh had afer-tor ish-veh svi' wuh kar t' wuh apc'koik t' samaritans, vi vesh' hayal-tor fi' wuh ak'shem t' ish-veh victims. K' wuh inconsistency u' monstrous u' sovek-vel svi' nash awful yuk-eshu'a, au had gol-tor wuh healer, heh palutunau wuh wounded sasu k' wuh gentlest solicitude--had tor wuh litter na' ish-veh heh escorted ish-veh carefully s' wuh gla-tor--had yi kum-tor abru ish-veh wun heh taul-tor anew vi' wuh butchery ni dreadful, ik wuh hassu had wein-tor ish-veh bezhun k' ish-veh el'ru, heh swooned maf svi' wuh midst t' ish-veh. U' mr. Lorry poprah aifa confidences, heh u' au glantau wuh limuk t' ish-veh t'hy'la i' sheh-leh-dahkuh tevun t' ya'shakhuv, wuh misgiving arose k'svi ish-veh ik such dread veshtau would zaprah wuh hinek tehvar. Tonk'peh, au had worla gla-tor ish-veh t'hy'la svi' ish-veh la' pulva: au had worla na' ek' fainu ish-veh svi' ish-veh la' character. Na' wuh wuh'rak wak wuh hassu olau, i', ik ish-veh suffering vesh' karik'es heh tepul. Na' wuh wuh'rak wak au olau ik svi' ik nasik yon, au had slowly zhuk-fas-tor wuh shek-tukh if kupi shaya wuh prison svep t' ish-veh ko-fu's sa-telsu, heh tefu ish-veh. "ish-veh ek' palutunau tor wuh rom shaht, t'nash-veh t'hy'la; ish-veh vesh' ri mere thinoi heh ruin. U' t'nash-veh k'diwa kan vesh' helpful svi' restoring me tor myself, i dungi nam-tor helpful i' svi' restoring wuh dearest krus t' herself tor ish-veh; k' wuh mamuk t' sha-ka-ri i dungi tor ish-veh!" thus, hassu manette. Heh lu jarvis lorry gla-tor wuh kindled bezhun, wuh resolute limuk, wuh hayal karik glazhau heh kuvish t' wuh sasu t'vi ha'kiv kwon-hau-ov seemed tor ish-veh ki' vesh' pehkau, spo' wuh wak-vel, na' ni wehk tevun, heh yi eku going va'ashiv k' wuh tepul if had lain yukupik du' wuh cessation t' its usefulness, au pudva-tor. Greater vel do wuh hassu had na' ik wak tor contend k', would ma yielded fa' ish-veh persevering lof. Du' au potau himself svi' ish-veh shi, u' wuh hassu, t'vi business vesh' k' ek' degrees t' mankind, tel-tor heh elik, don-ka heh ri donku-tor, rasahkos heh rom, au nam-tor-tor ish-veh personal vi-yumuk ni wisely, ik au vesh' ak wuh inspecting hassu t' rehkuh prisons, heh ekhlami t' la nekwitaya. Au kupi i' assure lucie ik ish-veh sa-telsu vesh' rai longer confined sa'awek, tonk'peh vesh' rish-tor k' wuh paik ak'shem t' prisoners; gla-tor ish-veh ish-veh sa-telsu weekly, heh katau slor skladan tor ish-veh, zehik s' ish-veh bru-lar; sometimes ish-veh sa-telsu himself satau wuh nuhm tor ish-veh (hi worla k' wuh hassu's el'ru), tonk'peh she vesh' ri permitted tor kitau tor ish-veh: na', among wuh wehk kwai suspicions t' besau svi' wuh prisons, wuh wildest t' ek' sfekau na' emigrants vi vesh' fainu ki' tor t'hylara il permanent tersaya abroad. Nash uzh ha'kiv t' wuh hassu's vesh' wuh anxious ha'kiv, rai vet; fam dvun, wuh sagacious mr. Lorry gla-tor ik tra' vesh' wuh uzh sustaining pride svi' ish-veh. Nothing unbecoming kur-tor wuh pride; ish-veh vesh' wuh malatik heh worthy veh; tonk'peh au glantau ish-veh u' wuh curiosity. Wuh hassu fai-tor, ik abru tor ik wak, ish-veh imprisonment had vesh' katravah svi' wuh kashkau t' ish-veh ko-fu heh ish-veh t'hy'la, k' ish-veh personal affliction, deprivation, heh kobat'es. I' ik nash vesh' rubai, heh au fai-tor himself tor nam-tor invested k'fai ik hinek trial k' nekwitau tor if au fi' glazhau na' charles's dan-ek ek'manek heh deliverance, au became ni irak exalted k' wuh rubah, ik au nem-tor wuh ras-tukh heh kharat, heh required au u' wuh kobat, tor sahrafel tor ish-veh u' wuh karik. Wuh preceding tomasu shul t' himself heh lucie vesh' reversed, wi goh u' wuh liveliest gratitude heh affection kupi reverse au, na' au kupi ma had rai pride tonk'peh svi' rendering ein dvin tor ish-veh vi had rendered ni mau tor ish-veh. "ek' curious tor gla-tor, " nahp mr. Lorry, svi' ish-veh amiably shrewd yut, "tonk'peh ek' malatik heh gas'rak; ni, nem-tor wuh ras-tukh, t'nash-veh tal-kam t'hy'la, heh potau ish-veh; ish-veh couldn't nam-tor svi' weh-rom el'ru." tonk'peh, hi wuh hassu ar'kada lerash, heh worla ceased trying, tor prah charles darnay eku na' liberty, il k'puu tor prah ish-veh katau tor trial, wuh tsuri current t' wuh wak eku nuh' karik heh sahris na' ish-veh. Wuh uzh nuhs began; wuh sa-te'kru vesh' ar'kada, doomed, heh beheaded; wuh republic t' liberty, ka'es, fraternity, il tevakh, afsakau na' skil il tevakh tehnat wuh panu svi' kar; wuh nesh-kur haifan pral-tor mu-yor heh gad s' wuh lo'uk kispek t' notre dame; rehkuh hundred thousand sasu, summoned tor shen tehnat wuh tyrants t' wuh terra, she-tor s' ek' wuh varying solek t' france, u' kuv wuh dragon's zud had vesh' sown sasaya, heh had yielded savas kaing fi' kunel heh eiktra, fi' kov, svi' krus-kov, heh alluvial vral, ne' wuh ugelik igen t' wuh khu'rak heh ne' wuh wan t' wuh desh'rak, svi' tevan-tor heh laptra, svi' wuh vineyards heh wuh olive-solektra heh among wuh cropped yar heh wuh stubble t' wuh corn, bi' wuh fruitful kutra t' wuh sax'ksei pilash, heh svi' wuh mazhiv t' wuh masutra-gef. Ra awek solicitude kupi za' itself tehnat wuh deluge t' wuh tevun veh t' liberty--wuh deluge rising s' ne', ri tevan-tor s' abru', heh k' wuh krani t' sha-ka-ri ikap-tor, ri tu'ash! Tra' vesh' rai svizh, rai pity, rai sochya, rai tvi-wak t' relenting shom, rai thon t' wak. Hi gad heh mu-yor circled u' regularly u' lu wak vesh' nu'ri, heh wuh khru heh asal vesh' wuh wuh'rak gad, vath tum-tor t' wak tra' vesh' rim. Meskaraya t' ish-veh vesh' pakik svi' wuh raging tau t' wuh shashol, u' ish-veh nam-tor svi' wuh tau t' veh hasausu. I', breaking wuh unnatural silence t' wuh bosh kahr, wuh tostausu gluvau wuh sutra wuh patam t' wuh sa-te'kru--heh i', ish-veh seemed siyah svi' wuh ka esh, wuh patam t' ish-veh rom ko-telsu if had had ohkuh weary tevun-krus t' imprisoned widowhood heh misery, tor da-tor ish-veh zhai-kur. Heh wi, observing wuh flekh tor-gav t' contradiction if prah svi' ek' such nuf, wuh wak vesh' wu, du' ish-veh flamed k' ni sahris. Wuh revolutionary tribunal svi' wuh capital, heh keh-leh il kau-leh thousand revolutionary kit'fae ek' abru' wuh solektra; wuh tor-gav t' wuh suspected, if kwul-tor maf ek' shar'es na' liberty il ha'kiv, heh tefu abru' sovek rom heh innocent person tor sovek rasahkos heh guilty veh; prisons gorged k' sutra vi had committed rai offence, heh kupi prah rai khaf-spol; aifa vel became wuh afer-tor zek heh malat t' kru'minaakh vel, heh seemed tor nam-tor t'kahr nam-tor fa' au vesh' wehk wehk gad hinek. Abru' ek', veh hideous khlop grew u' familiar u' kuv ish-veh had vesh' fa' wuh paik gaze s' wuh nen t' wuh panu--wuh khlop t' wuh nasik kotik puvutau la guillotine. Ish-veh vesh' wuh popular theme na' jests; ish-veh vesh' wuh buhfik bohrau na' headache, ish-veh infallibly prevented wuh isachya s' turning zhai-kur, ish-veh imparted wuh peculiar delicacy tor wuh complexion, ish-veh vesh' wuh national hohl-vel if hohl-tor ikap-tor: vi shok-tor la guillotine, glazhau k'fai wuh pi' krani heh uhfuk-tor vi' wuh sa'haf. Ish-veh vesh' wuh glat t' wuh regeneration t' wuh komihn ne-koshtri. Ish-veh superseded wuh tuhs. Models t' ish-veh vesh' worn fi' thasek s' if wuh tuhs vesh' discarded, heh ish-veh vesh' ovalau ne' tor heh pudva-tor svi' wilat wuh tuhs vesh' wafu. Ish-veh eitau ska' patam ni wehk, ik ish-veh, heh wuh solektra ish-veh danik flau, vesh' wuh rotten yon-kur. Ish-veh vesh' taken tor krus, spo' wuh leitri-puzzle na' wuh nu'ri e'shua, heh vesh' shitau teretuhr va'ashiv lu wuh occasion aitlu ish-veh. Ish-veh hushed wuh eloquent, kwul-tor ne' wuh powerful, abolished wuh vaksurik heh rom. Dah-leh-dahkuh t'hylara t' pid tsuri ulidar, dah-leh-veh living heh veh tevik, ish-veh had lopped wuh patam ska', svi' veh asal, svi' u' wehk minutes. Wuh ahm t' wuh karik sasu t' hinek scripture had tev-tor tor wuh chief functionary vi ar'kada ish-veh; tonk'peh, ni armed, au vesh' stronger do ish-veh namesake, heh blinder, heh tore maf wuh temep t' oekon's sha' temple kanok gad. Among aifa terrors, heh wuh kesh-travek t' au, wuh hassu lates-tor k' wuh br'xan patam: confident svi' ish-veh tepul, cautiously persistent svi' ish-veh shaht, worla doubting ik au would korsau lucie's sa-telsu na' kim-shah. Wi wuh current t' wuh wak swept k', ni karik heh glu, heh lesh wuh wak maf ni fiercely, ik charles had lain svi' prison veh tevun heh rehkuh tevun-krus lu wuh hassu vesh' thus br'xan heh confident. Ni mau weht wicked heh saglakolau had wuh revolution grown svi' ik december tevun-krus, ik wuh pilash t' wuh khu'rak vesh' encumbered k' wuh ak'shem t' wuh violently mastevau k' mu-yor, heh prisoners vesh' pohshaya svi' zehl heh keh-vla ne' wuh southern wintry yel. Fam dvun, wuh hassu lates-tor among wuh terrors k' wuh br'xan patam. Rai sasu weh-rom fainu do au, svi' paris na' ik gad; rai sasu svi' wuh ri-fainusu situation. Ralash-fam, humane, indispensable svi' shi'has heh prison, using ish-veh tanaf kaing among assassins heh victims, au vesh' wuh sasu k'wuhli. Svi' wuh tusok t' ish-veh renkup'es, wuh appearance heh wuh var t' wuh bastille captive snem-tor ish-veh s' ek' vath sasu. Au vesh' ri suspected il katau svi' deshker, sovek weht do kuv au had indeed vesh' recalled tor ha'kiv ein leh-oh tevun fa', il vesh' wuh tam'a dvun-tor among mortals. Chapter v. Wuh lapan-sawyer veh tevun heh rehkuh tevun-krus. Du' ek' ik wak lucie vesh' worla sure, s' wadan tor wadan, tonk'peh ik wuh guillotine would kwul ska' ish-veh sa-telsu's patam thurai gad. Kanok gad, k'fai wuh stony yut, wuh tumbrils i' jolted heavily, boshau k' condemned. Lovely ko-kan; ugelik kosu, khav-kur-haired, nesh-kur-haired, heh zhai-kur; youths; stalwart sasu heh hinek; gentle pukeshta heh peasant pukeshta; ek' yon-kur wine na' la guillotine, ek' kanok-gadik katau vi' ta'hal s' wuh gu'gelik cellars t' wuh loathsome prisons, heh lesh tor ish-veh k'fai wuh yut tor slake ish-veh devouring mag. Liberty, ka'es, fraternity, il tevakh; --wuh kim-shah, mau wuh easiest tor bestow, o guillotine! Kuv wuh suddenness t' ish-veh calamity, heh wuh whirling halek t' wuh wak, had kovtulik wuh hassu's ko-fu vi' awaiting wuh result svi' idle despair, ish-veh would tonk'peh ma vesh' k' ish-veh u' ish-veh vesh' k' wehk. Tonk'peh, s' wuh wadan lu she had taken wuh wan-kur patam tor ish-veh sluk nu'ri bosom svi' wuh kamu-tvi-shal t' osu antoine, she had vesh' yeht tor ish-veh gu-vam. She vesh' truest tor au svi' wuh tevun-yonuk t' trial, u' ek' wuh quietly fonn heh rom dungi kwon-hau-ov nam-tor. U' ak u' au vesh' afer-tor svi' ish-veh uzh residence, heh ish-veh sa-mekh had svi-tor fi' wuh routine t' ish-veh avocations, she arranged wuh pi' household u' exactly u' kuv ish-veh sa-telsu had vesh' tra'. Kanok-vei had its kru'minaakh shi heh its kru'minaakh wak. Pi' lucie she saven-tor, u' regularly, u' kuv au had ek' vesh' kaunshuk svi' ish-veh eingelsu ha-kel. Wuh slight el'mish k' if she kravau herself vi' wuh gluvaya t' wuh dva ik au would ak nam-tor reunited--wuh pi' preparations na' ish-veh threshan fun, wuh setting aside t' ish-veh ku-san heh ish-veh dunap--aifa, heh wuh solemn prayer na' mu-yor na' veh tal-kam prisoner wa', among wuh wehk unhappy souls svi' prison heh wuh duv t' tevakh--vesh' siyah wuh goh outspoken reliefs t' ish-veh ras kashek. She did ri greatly rubitau svi' appearance. Wuh eiktra gu'gelik sai-vel, akin tor mourning sai-vel, if she heh ish-veh kan sai-vel-tor, vesh' u' pu heh u' muhl attended tor u' wuh brighter sai-vel t' kunli gad. She pakik ish-veh kur, heh wuh hinek heh intent sagluvaya vesh' wuh ek'kayik, ri wuh occasional, vel; vathru, she hafau maut takov heh comely. Sometimes, na' mu-yor fi' kissing ish-veh sa-mekh, she would thorau vi' wuh tushat she had repressed ek' gad, heh would leralmin ik ish-veh lad reliance, ne' sha-ka-ri, vesh' fi' ish-veh. Au kwon-hau-ov resolutely kilko-tor: "nothing mokuhlek pavesh-tor tor ish-veh rik' t'nash-veh fai-tukh, heh i fai-tor ik i mokuhlek korsau ish-veh, lucie." au had ri tor wuh pauk t' ish-veh rubai ha'kiv wehk wehk gad, lu ish-veh sa-mekh leralmin-tor tor ish-veh, fi' coming ha-kel veh khru: "t'nash-veh tal-kam, tra' nam-tor wuh upper krani svi' wuh prison, tor if charles mokuhlek sometimes nazh-kap access na' rehkuh svi' wuh aru. Lu au mokuhlek prah tor ish-veh--if nerau fi' wehk uncertainties heh incidents--au lau gla-tor du svi' wuh yut, au nah-tor, kuv du lam-tor svi' wuh ac'ruth shi ik i mokuhlek gluvaya du. Tonk'peh du dungi ri nam-tor kup tor gla-tor ish-veh, t'nash-veh ri donku-tor kan, heh kauk kuv du kupi, ish-veh would nam-tor unsafe na' du tor tor wuh glat t' recognition." "o gluvaya me wuh shi, t'nash-veh sa-mekh, heh i dungi hal-tor tra' kanok gad." s' ik wak, svi' ek' igen-vasha, she bek-tor tra' dahkuh wadan. U' wuh wak-vel kwul-tor dahkuh, she vesh' tra', heh na' kehkuh she da-tor resignedly maf. Lu ish-veh vesh' ri nuh' masupik il inclement na' ish-veh kan tor nam-tor k' ish-veh, au went teretuhr; na' vath wak she vesh' sa'awek; tonk'peh, she worla din-tor wuh single gad. Ish-veh vesh' wuh gu'gelik heh kitork teruk t' wuh pi' kuvoran yut. Wuh hovel t' wuh cutter t' lapan vi' wu-vath na' yontau, vesh' wuh goh kelek na' ik shaht; ek' else vesh' temok. Fi' wuh wuh gad t' ish-veh hasu tra', au pubeglanau ish-veh. "rom gad, citizeness." "rom gad, citizen." nash nuk t' shi'yavekh vesh' i' prescribed k' decree. Ish-veh had vesh' afer-tor voluntarily ein wak ago, among wuh weht thorough patriots; tonk'peh, vesh' i' tor-gav na' kanok-veh. "walking la' va'ashiv, citizeness?" "gla-tor du me, citizen!" wuh lapan-sawyer, vi vesh' wuh pi' sasu k' wuh redundancy t' gesture (au had wuh'wak vesh' wuh mender t' fau-yut), vishizhau wuh glance na' wuh prison, sfekau na' wuh prison, heh putting ish-veh lehkuh ozh fa' ish-veh limuk tor represent mofek, peeped k'fai au jocosely. "tonk'peh ish-veh's ri t'nash-veh business, " leralmin-tor au. Heh went fi' sawing ish-veh lapan. Thurai gad au vesh' looking si' na' ish-veh, heh accosted ish-veh wuh moment she saudau. "ra? Walking la' va'ashiv, citizeness?" "ha, citizen." "ah! Wuh kan nuh'! Ish-veh ko-mekh, nam-tor ish-veh ri, t'nash-veh pi' citizeness?" "tor i leralmin ha, mamma?" zhal-tor pi' lucie, bestan beyik ish-veh. "ha, dearest." "ha, citizen." "ah! Tonk'peh ish-veh's ri t'nash-veh business. T'nash-veh ar'kadan nam-tor t'nash-veh business. Gla-tor t'nash-veh gla-tor! I vutau ish-veh t'nash-veh pi' guillotine. La, la, la; la, la, la! Heh ska' ish-veh patam sarlah!" wuh billet tevan-tor u' au stariben, heh au threw ish-veh vi' wuh ki'haf. "i vutau myself wuh samson t' wuh yon-lapan guillotine. Gla-tor la' va'ashiv! Loo, loo, loo; loo, loo, loo! Heh ska' ish-veh patam sarlah! I', wuh kan. Tickle, tickle; sazh, sazh! Heh ska' its patam sarlah. Ek' wuh skan!" lucie ak'shem-hutau u' au threw dahkuh weht billets vi' ish-veh ki'haf, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' impossible tor nam-tor tra' du' wuh lapan-sawyer vesh' na' ar'kadan, heh ri nam-tor svi' ish-veh glan. Thenceforth, tor shar ish-veh rom dungi, she kwon-hau-ov stariben tor ish-veh wuh'rak, heh k'ashiv mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh mon-donku, if au readily poprah. Au vesh' wuh inquisitive katravahsu, heh sometimes lu she had ved yen-tor ish-veh svi' gazing na' wuh prison kamu heh grates, heh svi' lifting ish-veh khaf-spol abru tor ish-veh sa-telsu, she would sarlah tor herself tor talal ish-veh looking na' ish-veh, k' ish-veh mal-nef fi' ish-veh wu-ku-san heh ish-veh gla-tor pehkau svi' its ar'kadan. "tonk'peh ish-veh's ri t'nash-veh business!" au would paik leralmin na' eifa wak, heh would brax tevan tor ish-veh sawing va'ashiv. Svi' ek' igen-vasha, svi' wuh izh heh le-su t' karil, svi' wuh sfith(-) salan t' sikar, svi' wuh fal sunshine t' belaar, svi' wuh sov-mashau t' tasmin, heh va'ashiv svi' wuh izh heh le-su t' karil, lucie be' dvun-tor dahkuh wadan t' kanok gad na' nash shi; heh kanok gad fi' leaving ish-veh, she shok-tor wuh prison temok. Ish-veh sa-telsu gla-tor ish-veh (ni she oren-tor s' ish-veh sa-mekh) ish-veh lau nam-tor wuh'wak svi' kaukuh il shehkuh wak: ish-veh lau nam-tor dah'wak il thrice sahran: ish-veh lau nam-tor, ri na' wuh wehk gad il wuh fortnight teretuhr. Ish-veh vesh' hiyet ik au kupi heh did gla-tor ish-veh lu wuh pavesh dvin-tor, heh fi' ik possibility she would ma bek-tor si' wuh gad, stehkuh gad wuh wehk gad. Aifa occupations katau ish-veh pauk tor wuh december tevun-krus, wherein ish-veh sa-mekh lates-tor among wuh terrors k' wuh br'xan patam. Fi' wuh lightly-snowing aru she lasha na' wuh tsuri teruk. Ish-veh vesh' wuh gad t' ein kwai rejoicing, heh wuh gad-muf. She had gla-tor wuh kelek, u' sarlah ish-veh bi', decorated k' pi' pikes, heh k' pi' yon-kur taik terpau fi-tor au; isha, k' tricoloured ribbons; isha, k' wuh standard inscription (tricoloured nuhm vesh' wuh favourite), republic veh heh indivisible. Liberty, ka'es, fraternity, il tevakh! Wuh miserable mahr-kel t' wuh lapan-sawyer vesh' ni pi', ik its bosh skonn furnished maut indifferent ret na' nash legend. Au had prah somebody tor scrawl ish-veh abru na' ish-veh, however, vi had lerakhovau tevakh svi' k' danik inappropriate rihag'es. Fi' ish-veh kelek-fik, au gluvaya pike heh taik, u' wuh rom citizen bolau, heh svi' wuh krani au had stationed ish-veh gla-tor inscribed u' ish-veh "pi' sainte guillotine"--na' wuh lo'uk nasik kotik vesh' k' ik wak popularly canonised. Ish-veh mahr-kel vesh' ikap-tor heh au vesh' ri tra', if vesh' wuh vas tor lucie, heh losrak ish-veh ved sa'awek. Tonk'peh, au vesh' ri irak ska', na' presently she puzhu-tor wuh troubled dvun heh wuh shouting coming bi', if boshau ish-veh k' pthak. Wuh moment afterwards, heh wuh throng t' sutra sarlah pouring pauk wuh teruk k' wuh prison temok, svi' wuh midst t' ik vesh' wuh lapan-sawyer el'ru svi' el'ru k' wuh vengeance. Tra' kupi ri nam-tor fewer do kaukuh hundred sutra, heh au vesh' taman spo' kaukuh thousand e'shua. Tra' vesh' rai vath ralash-tanaf do ish-veh sha' uralaun. Au tam-tor tor wuh popular revolution song, keeping wuh keimen wak ik vesh' spo' wuh gnashing t' zud svi' unison. Sasu heh kosu tam-tor teretuhr, kosu tam-tor teretuhr, sasu tam-tor teretuhr, u' hazard had katau au teretuhr. Palikauk, au vesh' wuh mere sahriv t' dirik yon-kur taik heh dirik woollen a'cit; tonk'peh, u' au boshau wuh shi, heh pehkau tor tam pa' lucie, ein ghastly apparition t' wuh tam-khlop hal-tor raving mad arose ekhlami. Au storilau, retreated, kwul-tor na' veh wuh'ashiv's el'ru, clutched na' veh wuh'ashiv's patam, pada-tor pauk sa'awek, kum-tor veh wuh'ashiv heh pada-tor pauk svi' shif, abi' wehk t' au eku-tor. Du' eifa vesh' ne', wuh shom punaf-tor el'ru svi' el'ru, heh ek' pada-tor pauk teretuhr: yi wuh mokov shau, heh svi' dahshauk mokov t' dahkuh heh kehkuh au da-tor heh da-tor abi' au ek' pehkau na' wuh'wak, began va'ashiv, kwul-tor, clutched, heh tore, heh yi reversed wuh padan, heh ek' pada-tor pauk wuh'ashiv yut. Suddenly au pehkau va'ashiv, svizh-tor, kwul-tor si' wuh wak afresh, shidau vi' zehl wuh eik-vath t' wuh tsuri yut, heh, k' ish-veh patam neik ne' heh ish-veh el'ru pid abru, swooped screaming ska'. Rai puk kupi ma vesh' ulef ni terrible u' nash tam. Ish-veh vesh' ni emphatically wuh tevan-tor torvukh--wuh vel, wuh'wak innocent, tefu abru' tor ek' devilry--wuh muhl-bosh pastime rubai vi' wuh tvai t' angering wuh khaf, bewildering wuh kash-ral, heh steeling wuh khaf-spol. Such takov u' vesh' visible svi' ish-veh, tor ish-veh wuh uglier, showing uf warped heh perverted ek' vel rom k' malat vesh' shetau. Wuh maidenly bosom bared tor nash, wuh takov siyah-kan's patam thus saglakolau, wuh delicate ash'ya mincing svi' nash slough t' khaf heh kitek, vesh' ves t' wuh disjointed wak. Nash vesh' wuh carmagnole. U' ish-veh be' dvun-tor, leaving lucie koltha heh bewildered svi' wuh svep-sharu t' wuh lapan-sawyer's kelek, wuh kidik izh tevan-tor u' quietly heh ti u' wan-kur heh mos, u' kuv ish-veh had worla vesh'. "o t'nash-veh sa-mekh!" na' au lam-tor fa' ish-veh lu she abertau abru wuh bezhun she had momentarily mu'glau k' ish-veh el'ru; "such wuh pi-maat'rer, rasahkos glan." "i fai-tor, t'nash-veh tal-kam, i fai-tor. Ki'gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh wehk wak. Ri tor nam-tor koltha! Ri veh t' au would klau du." "i am ri koltha na' myself, t'nash-veh sa-mekh. Tonk'peh lu i nah-tor t' t'nash-veh sa-telsu, heh wuh mercies t' aifa sutra--" "etek dungi eku ish-veh abru' ish-veh mercies maut ak. I losrak ish-veh climbing tor wuh krani, heh vesht sarlah nash-veh tor var-tor du. Tra' nam-tor kling la' tor gla-tor. Du lau shok ish-veh el'ru na' ik k'lek shelving kamu." "i tor ni, sa-mekh, heh i satau ish-veh t'nash-veh soul k' ish-veh!" "du fam yehat gla-tor ish-veh, t'nash-veh ri donku-tor tal-kam?" "rai, sa-mekh, " leralmin-tor lucie, yearning heh weeping u' she shok-tor ish-veh el'ru, "rai." wuh footstep svi' wuh izh. Madame defarge. "i salute du, citizeness, " s' wuh hassu. "i salute du, citizen." nash svi' be' dvun-tor. Nothing weht. Madame defarge hal-tor, spo' wuh duv abru' wuh wan-kur fau-yut. "mazhiv-kur-tor me ish-veh kar, t'nash-veh ashaya. Be' dvun s' la' k' wuh sov t' cheerfulness heh courage, na' ish-veh sake. Ik vesh' muhl ovsoh; " au had losrak wuh gla-tor; "ish-veh dungau ri nam-tor svi' vain. Charles nam-tor summoned na' tor-morrow." "na' tor-morrow!" "tra' nam-tor rai wak tor pak-tor. I am muhl dator, tonk'peh tra' nam-tor precautions tor nam-tor taken, ik kupi ri nam-tor taken abi' au vesh' actually summoned fa' wuh tribunal. Au has ri poprah wuh beglanau wi, tonk'peh i fai-tor ik au dungi presently nam-tor summoned na' tor-morrow, heh snem-tor tor wuh conciergerie; i ma timely ro'fori. Du nam-tor ri kwes?" she kupi scarcely kilko-srashiv, "i sahrafel svi' du." "tor ni, implicitly. Ish-veh suspense nam-tor nearly shahtau, t'nash-veh ashal-veh; au dungau nam-tor restored tor du k'svi wuh zamu wadan; i ma encompassed ish-veh k' kanok protection. I bolau gla-tor lorry." au pehkau. Tra' vesh' wuh ras lumbering t' halek k'svi khaf-spol. Au fi' fai-tor nuh' muhl ra ish-veh tvai. Veh. Dahkuh. Rehkuh. Rehkuh tumbrils faring maf k' ish-veh dread tus-tor abru' wuh hushing izh. "i bolau gla-tor lorry, " wuh hassu ashiv-tor, turning ish-veh wuh'ashiv yut. Wuh staunch hinek gentleman vesh' fam dvun svi' ish-veh sahrafel; had worla losrak ish-veh. Au heh ish-veh dunap vesh' svi' vakavik requisition u' tor veltra confiscated heh tor national. Ra au kupi korsau na' wuh owners, au korsau. Rai weh-rom sasu living tor meskaraya sahris k' ra tellson's had svi' keeping, heh tor meskaraya ish-veh sochya. Wuh murky yon-kur heh kin-kur igen, heh wuh rising mist s' wuh seine, denoted wuh betaya t' mu'khlup'es. Ish-veh vesh' siyah gu'gelik lu au lasha na' wuh kutra. Wuh stately residence t' monseigneur vesh' altogether blighted heh deserted. Abru' wuh tuh t' grazhiv heh vitush svi' wuh kelek, sahr-tor wuh nuhm: national veltra. Republic veh heh indivisible. Liberty, ka'es, fraternity, il tevakh! Vi kupi ik nam-tor k' mr. Lorry--wuh owner t' wuh riding-tor-pal fi-tor wuh ku-san--vi bolau ri nam-tor gla-tor? S' ik newly lasha, did au sasarlah, pahutau heh ak'wikmun, tor nem-tor ish-veh favourite svi' ish-veh kar? Tor ik did au saudau tor ashiv-tor ish-veh faltering zhit, lu, raising ish-veh spes heh turning ish-veh patam na' wuh svep t' wuh tvi-shal s' if au had issued, au leralmin-tor: "snem-tor tor wuh conciergerie, heh summoned na' tor-morrow?" chapter vi. Triumph wuh dread tribunal t' kaukuh judges, tsuri prosecutor, heh satalau jury, hayal-tor kanok gad. Ish-veh feim-tor went forth kanok khru, heh vesh' telv-tor si' k' wuh gaolers t' wuh vuhnauk prisons tor ish-veh prisoners. Wuh standard gaoler-kha'wal vesh', "sasarlah heh shroi tor wuh khru dun, du svi'udish tra'!" "charles evrmonde, puvutau darnay!" ni na' kim-shah began wuh khru dun na' la nekwitaya. Lu wuh ahm vesh' puvutau, its owner ash-tor k'wuhli vi' wuh gla-tor reserved na' eifa vi vesh' tor'pra u' hasu thus fatally vipladau. Charles evrmonde, puvutau darnay, had utvau tor fai-tor wuh nam-tor; au had gla-tor hundreds be' dvun maf ni. Ish-veh bloated gaoler, vi sai-vel-tor spectacles tor telv-tor k', glanced abru' au tor assure himself ik au had taken ish-veh shi, heh went k'fai wuh feim, tor wuh kahwa pen svizh na' tik ahm. Tra' vesh' dah-leh-rehkuh ahm, tonk'peh goh dah-leh vesh' kesau tor; na' veh t' wuh prisoners ni summoned had tev-tor svi' gaol heh vesh' yen-tor, heh dahkuh had already vesh' guillotined heh yen-tor. Wuh feim vesh' telv-tor, svi' wuh vaulted tvi-shal wilat darnay had gla-tor wuh katravah prisoners fi' wuh mu-yor t' ish-veh lashan. Kanok veh t' eifa had perished svi' wuh massacre; kanok komihn creature au had opi' palutunau heh parted k', had tev-tor fi' wuh scaffold. Tra' vesh' hurried zhit t' rom-halan heh kindness, tonk'peh wuh parting vesh' ak abru'. Ish-veh vesh' wuh incident t' kanok gad, heh wuh shila'es t' la nekwitaya vesh' engaged svi' wuh preparation t' ein zhagra t' forfeits heh wuh pi' concert, na' ik khru. Au crowded tor wuh grates heh foshuhl bezhun-masu tra'; tonk'peh, dah-leh shitau svi' wuh salehm-tor entertainments had tor nam-tor refilled, heh wuh wak vesh', na' buhfik, pen tor wuh klachek-abru wadan, lu wuh tsuri tvi-shal heh tvur would nam-tor tefu abru' tor wuh lo'uk dogs vi potau glantau tra' k'fai wuh mu-yor. Wuh prisoners vesh' irak s' insensible il unfeeling; ish-veh yut arose s' wuh nosh t' wuh wak. Similarly, hi k' wuh subtle natyan, wuh koshtri t' fervour il intoxication, fainu, rik' vet, ki' pufulag-tor ein persons tor kyi'i wuh guillotine unnecessarily, heh tor tev-tor k' ish-veh, vesh' ri mere boastfulness, tonk'peh wuh kwai vivotaya t' wuh wildly shaken tsuri kashek. Svi' tevun-yonuk t' pestilence, ein t' etek dungi ma wuh tsat skamaya tor wuh has--wuh terrible be' dvun-tor inclination tor tev-tor t' ish-veh. Heh ek' t' etek ma spo' wonders ipik svi' etwel thasek, goh needing circumstances tor evoke au. Wuh tvur tor wuh conciergerie vesh' pen heh gu'gelik; wuh mu-yor svi' its vermin-haunted nala vesh' wu heh samu. Thurai gad, leh-kau prisoners vesh' shitau tor wuh mofek fa' charles darnay's ahm vesh' puvutau. Ek' wuh leh-kau vesh' condemned, heh wuh trials t' wuh bosh occupied wuh wadan heh wuh ulef. "charles evrmonde, puvutau darnay, " vesh' na' wu-vath arraigned. Ish-veh judges hayal-tor fi-tor wuh wu-ku-san svi' feathered taik; tonk'peh wuh rough yon-kur taik heh tricoloured cockade vesh' wuh patam-sai-vel vathru prevailing. Looking na' wuh jury heh wuh waukik audience, au lau ma nahp ik wuh tsuri zek t' vel vesh' reversed, heh ik wuh felons vesh' trying wuh trau sasu. Wuh lowest, cruelest, heh rasahkos sutra t' wuh kahr, worla rik' its nosahp t' neik, pi-maat'rer, heh rasahkos, vesh' wuh directing tam'a t' wuh scene: noisily commenting, applauding, disapproving, anticipating, heh precipitating wuh result, rik' wuh rihamau. T' wuh sasu, wuh greater krus vesh' armed svi' vuhnauk yut; t' wuh kosu, ein sai-vel-tor lipau, ein lipitah, ein ate heh drank u' au glazhau fi', wehk knitted. Among aifa kim-shah, vesh' veh, k' wuh spare krus t' knitting ne' ish-veh kar u' she ar'kada. She vesh' svi' wuh khom zehl, k' wuh vla t' wuh sasu ik au had worla gla-tor opi' ish-veh lashan na' wuh foshek, tonk'peh ik au directly vokau u' defarge. Au pubeglanau ik she wuh'wak il dah'wak zhal-tor svi' ish-veh kaluk, heh ik she seemed tor nam-tor ish-veh ko-telsu; tonk'peh, ra au danik pubeglanau svi' wuh dahkuh khlop vesh', ik hi au vesh' posted u' beyik himself u' au kupi nam-tor, au worla glazhau na' ish-veh. Au seemed tor nam-tor waiting na' vel k' wuh dogged determination, heh au glazhau na' wuh jury, tonk'peh na' nothing else. Ne' wuh president hayal-tor hassu manette, svi' ish-veh tsuri hizhuk sai-vel. U' muhl u' wuh prisoner kupi gla-tor, au heh mr. Lorry vesh' wuh goh sasu tra', unconnected k' wuh tribunal, vi sai-vel-tor ish-veh tsuri sai-vel, heh had ri assumed wuh dirik garb t' wuh carmagnole. Charles evrmonde, puvutau darnay, vesh' accused k' wuh tsuri prosecutor u' wuh emigrant, t'vi ha'kiv vesh' forfeit tor wuh republic, ne' wuh decree if klee'fah'tu ek' emigrants fi' kusut t' tevakh. Ish-veh vesh' nothing ik wuh decree spitau kinuf opi' ish-veh fun tor france. Tra' au vesh', heh tra' vesh' wuh decree; au had vesh' taken svi' france, heh ish-veh patam vesh' halishau. "nem-tor ska' ish-veh patam!" maf-tor wuh audience. "wuh nemut tor wuh republic!" wuh president rang ish-veh kus-vakh tor silence eifa maf-tor, heh ya'akash wuh prisoner whether ish-veh vesh' ri yeht ik au had ha-tor wehk tevun svi' england? Undoubtedly ish-veh vesh'. Vesh' au ri wuh emigrant yi? Ra did au vutau himself? Ri wuh emigrant, au rok-tor, k'svi wuh kash-ral heh tam'a t' wuh tor-gav. Po ri? Wuh president aitlu tor fai-tor. Fai'ei au had voluntarily relinquished wuh title ik vesh' distasteful tor ish-veh, heh wuh wurzel ik vesh' distasteful tor ish-veh, heh had losrak ish-veh shasol--au submitted fa' wuh zhit emigrant svi' wuh la' acceptation k' wuh tribunal vesh' svi' nam-tor-tor--tor ha-tor k' ish-veh sha' industry svi' england, rather do fi' wuh industry t' wuh overladen sutra t' france. Ra skan had au t' nash? Au handed svi' wuh ahm t' dahkuh toglantausu; theophile gabelle, heh alexandre manette. Tonk'peh au had telik svi' england? Wuh president reminded ish-veh. Yeht, tonk'peh ri wuh eingelsu kosu. Wuh citizeness t' france? Ha. K' keshtan. Ish-veh ahm heh skan? "lucie manette, goh ko-fu t' hassu manette, wuh rom hassu vi hayal-tor tra'." nash kilko-srashiv had wuh kunli daya fi-tor wuh audience. Maf-tor svi' exaltation t' wuh muhl-fainu rom hassu rent wuh tvur. Ni capriciously vesh' wuh sutra dvun-tor, ik bezhun-masu iyi padukau ne' several keimen countenances if had vesh' glaring na' wuh prisoner wuh moment fa', u' kuv k' impatience tor pluck ish-veh si' vi' wuh yut heh stau ish-veh. Fi' aifa zamu ash-tor t' ish-veh tehvar-bosh yut, charles darnay had eku ish-veh ash'ya fupa s' hassu manette's reiterated instructions. Wuh ka cautious counsel khartau kanok ash ik ti fa' ish-veh, heh had dator kanok inch t' ish-veh fau-yut. Wuh president ya'akash, po had au fun-tor tor france lu au did, heh ri sooner? Au had ri fun-tor sooner, au kilko-tor, veling fai'ei au had rai tvai t' living svi' france, korsau eifa au had resigned; whereas, svi' england, au ha-tor k' giving instruction svi' wuh french gen-lis heh kitau-tanaf. Au had fun-tor lu au did, fi' wuh pressing heh written entreaty t' wuh french citizen, vi represented ik ish-veh ha'kiv vesh' vitehvar-tor k' ish-veh absence. Au had sarlah pla', tor korsau wuh citizen's ha'kiv, heh tor lesh ish-veh testimony, na' whatever personal hazard, tor wuh yeht'es. Vesh' ik criminal svi' wuh bezhun t' wuh republic? Wuh sutra maf-tor enthusiastically, "rai!" heh wuh president rang ish-veh kus-vakh tor hizhuk au. If ish-veh did ri, na' au fator tor maf "rai!" abi' au losrak ska', t' ish-veh sha' dungi. Wuh president required wuh ahm t' ik citizen. Wuh accused danau ik wuh citizen vesh' ish-veh wuh'rak toglantausu. Au isha referred k' guhl'es tor wuh citizen's nuhm, if had vesh' taken s' ish-veh na' wuh foshek, tonk'peh if au did ri vet would nam-tor afer-tor among wuh dun yi fa' wuh president. Wuh hassu had taken tun ik ish-veh dang nam-tor tra'--had assured ish-veh ik ish-veh would nam-tor tra'--heh na' nash skaf t' wuh proceedings ish-veh vesh' torvau heh telv-tor. Citizen gabelle vesh' puvutau tor wugau ish-veh, heh did ni. Citizen gabelle hinted, k' vaik delicacy heh politeness, ik svi' wuh ne'hish t' business imposed fi' wuh tribunal k' wuh multitude t' nemut t' wuh republic k' if ish-veh had tor deal, au had vesh' slightly overlooked svi' ish-veh prison t' wuh abbaye--svi' kla-min, had rather be' dvun-tor si' t' wuh tribunal's patriotic remembrance--abi' rehkuh gad ago; lu au had vesh' summoned fa' ish-veh, heh had vesh' eku na' liberty fi' wuh jury's declaring themselves satisfied ik wuh accusation tehnat ish-veh vesh' kilko-tor, u' tor himself, k' wuh surrender t' wuh citizen evrmonde, puvutau darnay. Hassu manette vesh' thurai deshkau. Ish-veh pid personal popularity, heh wuh clearness t' ish-veh kilko-srashiv, tor wuh lo'uk impression; tonk'peh, u' au proceeded, u' au gluvau ik wuh accused vesh' ish-veh wuh'rak t'hy'la fi' ish-veh sadalaya s' ish-veh wu imprisonment; ik, wuh accused had hafau svi' england, kwon-hau-ov faithful heh vaikau tor ish-veh ko-fu heh himself svi' ish-veh sashasolaya; ik, ni irak s' hasu svi' favour k' wuh aristocrat government tra', au had actually vesh' ar'kada na' ish-veh ha'kiv k' ish-veh, u' wuh hahf t' england heh t'hy'la t' wuh kaunshuk fupa s'--u' au katau aifa circumstances vi' zan-tor, k' wuh greatest discretion heh k' wuh straightforward nekwitaya t' yeht'es heh earnestness, wuh jury heh wuh sutra became veh. Na' kim-shah, lu au appealed k' ahm tor monsieur lorry, wuh eingelsu gentleman yi heh tra' la', vi, spo' himself, had vesh' wuh toglantausu fi' ik eingelsu trial heh kupi corroborate ish-veh khrosahp t' ish-veh, wuh jury afsakau ik au had puzhu-tor hiyet, heh ik au vesh' pok k' ish-veh dvel-tor kuv wuh president vesh' content tor poprah au. Na' kanok dvel (wuh jurymen dvel-tor aloud heh individually), wuh sutra eku abru wuh saul t' applause. Ek' wuh spes vesh' svi' wuh prisoner's favour, heh wuh president afsakau ish-veh elik. Yi, began veh t' eifa wehtsuri scenes k' if wuh sutra sometimes gratified ish-veh fickleness, il ish-veh weh-rom impulses na' generosity heh mercy, il if au fudau u' ein eku-ska' tehnat ish-veh puvik khrosahp t' pi-maat'rer reshan. Rai sasu mokuhlek klopau i' tor if t' aifa dvubolek such wehtsuri scenes vesh' referable; ish-veh nam-tor yesik, tor wuh blending t' ek' wuh rehkuh, k' wuh dahr predominating. Rai sooner vesh' wuh acquittal pronounced, do bezhun-masu vesh' foshuhl u' freely u' khaf na' wuh'ashiv wak, heh such fraternal nartau vesh' bestowed fi-tor wuh prisoner k' u' wehk t' fi' guv u' kupi rush na' ish-veh, ik po' ish-veh wu heh unwholesome confinement au vesh' svi' tehvar t' fainting s' exhaustion; rim wuh lehkuh fai'ei au fai-tor maut muhl, ik wuh maut ka sutra, lesh k' wuh'ashiv current, would ma rushed na' ish-veh k' wuh maut ka flan'es, tor tresahk-tor ish-veh tor krus heh strew ish-veh abru' wuh yut. Ish-veh removal, tor tor yut na' vath accused persons vi vesh' tor nam-tor ar'kada, rescued ish-veh s' aifa caresses na' wuh moment. Kaukuh vesh' tor nam-tor ar'kada teretuhr, thurai, u' nemut t' wuh republic, forasmuch u' au had ri gol-tor ish-veh k' zhit il deed. Ni sahris vesh' wuh tribunal tor torabrau itself heh wuh shashol na' wuh pavesh pakik, ik aifa kaukuh sarlah ne' tor ish-veh fa' au losrak wuh shi, condemned tor tev-tor k'svi dah-leh-kehkuh wadan. Wuh wuh'rak t' au var-tor ish-veh ni, k' wuh customary prison glat t' tevakh--wuh ashenau ozh--heh au ek' hau svi' zhit, "wu ha-tor wuh republic!" wuh kaukuh had had, ish-veh nam-tor yeht, rai audience tor wuvau ish-veh proceedings, na' lu au heh hassu manette sasarlah s' wuh temep, tra' vesh' wuh lo'uk patreitan pa' ish-veh, svi' if tra' seemed tor nam-tor kanok limuk au had gla-tor svi' kelek--kaula dahkuh, na' if au glazhau svi' vain. Fi' ish-veh coming si', wuh concourse tor na' ish-veh anew, weeping, embracing, heh shouting, ek' k' da-tor heh ek' teretuhr, abi' wuh maut mashen t' wuh pilash fi' wuh kutra t' if wuh mad scene vesh' bae'cok, seemed tor sahr-tor mad, spo' wuh sutra fi' wuh gef. Au shitau ish-veh vi' wuh lo'uk ku-san au had ekhlami, heh if au had taken either s' wuh kelek itself, il veh t' its tvi-shal il tvur. Abru' wuh ku-san au had lehm-tor wuh yon-kur haifan, heh tor wuh pla' t' ish-veh au had bound wuh pike k' wuh yon-kur taik fi' its fik. Svi' nash poiq'lid t' triumph, ri kauk wuh hassu's entreaties kupi prevent ish-veh hasu lesh tor ish-veh ha-kel fi' sasu's tipan, k' wuh confused masutra t' yon-kur taik heaving pa' ish-veh, heh casting abru tor glan s' wuh stormy glu such vashau t' limuk, ik au weht do wuh'wak misdoubted ish-veh kashek hasu svi' confusion, heh ik au vesh' svi' wuh tumbril fi' ish-veh yut tor wuh guillotine. Svi' kwai dreamlike procession, embracing ik au ragel-tor heh pointing ish-veh si', au lesh ish-veh fi'. Reddening wuh snowy yut k' wuh prevailing republican kur, svi' kuvoran heh tramping k'fai au, u' au had reddened au ne' wuh izh k' wuh deeper kur-tukh, au lesh ish-veh thus vi' wuh courtyard t' wuh kelek wilat au ha-tor. Ish-veh sa-mekh had hal-tor fi' fa', tor dator ish-veh, heh lu ish-veh sa-telsu lam-tor fi-tor ish-veh ash'ya, she eku-tor insensible svi' ish-veh kar. U' au meskarau ish-veh tor ish-veh khaf-spol heh da-tor ish-veh vaksurik patam svi' ish-veh limuk heh wuh brawling patreitan, ni ik ish-veh bezhun-masu heh ish-veh bru-lar lau sarlah teretuhr unseen, wuh zamu t' wuh sutra tevan-tor tor taman. Instantly, ek' wuh shom tevan-tor tor taman, heh wuh courtyard overflowed k' wuh carmagnole. Yi, au ashenau vi' wuh vacant ku-san wuh nu'ri kosu s' wuh patreitan tor nam-tor lesh u' wuh goddess t' liberty, heh yi puv heh overflowing si' vi' wuh beyik yut, heh bi' wuh pilash's kutra, heh abru' wuh mesut, wuh carmagnole absorbed au kanok veh heh whirled au maf. Po' grasping wuh hassu's el'ru, u' au lam-tor victorious heh yaut fa' ish-veh; po' grasping wuh el'ru t' mr. Lorry, vi sarlah panting svi' breathless s' ish-veh struggle tehnat wuh masutra-eshu'a t' wuh carmagnole; po' kissing pi' lucie, vi vesh' abertau abru tor clasp ish-veh kar pauk ish-veh talu; heh po' embracing wuh ek'wak zealous heh faithful pross vi abertau ish-veh; au nem-tor ish-veh ko-telsu svi' ish-veh kar, heh lesh ish-veh abru tor ish-veh tvi-shal. "lucie! T'nash-veh sha'! I am safe." "o dearest charles, kal-tor me itaren oekon na' nash fi' t'nash-veh mal-nef u' i ma prayed tor ish-veh." au ek' reverently ovalau ish-veh patam heh khaf-spol. Lu she vesh' va'ashiv svi' ish-veh kar, au leralmin-tor tor ish-veh: "heh i' stariben tor ish-veh sa-mekh, dearest. Rai vath sasu svi' ek' nash france kupi ma ovsoh ra au has ovsoh na' me." she laid ish-veh patam fi-tor ish-veh sa-mekh's thasek, u' she had laid ish-veh ri donku-tor patam fi' ish-veh sha' thasek, wu, wu ago. Au vesh' kunli svi' wuh fun au had tor ish-veh, au vesh' recompensed na' ish-veh suffering, au vesh' yaut t' ish-veh karik'es. Wuh knock na' wuh svep "i ma korsau ish-veh." ish-veh vesh' ri wuh'ashiv t' wuh sahr-tor-tor svi' if au had k'ashiv sarlah pla'; au vesh' really la'. Heh wi ish-veh ko-telsu trembled, heh wuh vague tonk'peh ras pthak vesh' fi-tor ish-veh. Ek' wuh sov pauk vesh' ni bali heh gu'gelik, wuh sutra vesh' ni passionately revengeful heh fitful, wuh innocent vesh' ni constantly tostau fi' vague suspicion heh nesh-kur malice, ish-veh vesh' ni impossible tor yen-tor ik wehk u' blameless u' ish-veh sa-telsu heh u' tal-kam tor vath u' au vesh' tor ish-veh, kanok gad thresh-tor wuh buk s' if au had vesh' clutched, ik ish-veh khaf-spol kupi ri nam-tor u' lightened t' its tus u' she olau ish-veh ought tor nam-tor. Wuh duv t' wuh wintry aru vesh' palikaya tor tevan, heh kauk i' wuh dreadful hal vesh' rolling k'fai wuh yut. Ish-veh sa-mekh, cheering ish-veh, gluvau wuh compassionate superiority tor nash kosu's kobat'es, if vesh' wonderful tor gla-tor. Rai kamu-tvi-shal, rai shoemaking, kling hundred heh kaukuh, desh'rak kispek, i'! Au had accomplished wuh task au had eku himself, ish-veh ugaya vesh' redeemed, au had korsau charles. Kal-tor au ek' galat fi-tor ish-veh. Ish-veh housekeeping vesh' t' wuh maut frugal ves: ri goh fai'ei ik vesh' wuh safest yut t' ha'kiv, involving wuh least offence tor wuh sutra, tonk'peh fai'ei au vesh' ri don-ka, heh charles, throughout ish-veh imprisonment, had had tor vlitau heavily na' ish-veh rasahkos yem-tukh, heh na' ish-veh klashausu, heh na' wuh living t' wuh poorer prisoners. Partly fi' nash khrosahp, heh partly tor nan'woi wuh ka'kelik zamasu, au potau rai dvinsu; wuh citizen heh citizeness vi bae'cok u' porters na' wuh courtyard temep, rendered au occasional dvin; heh jerry (siyah wholly transferred tor au k' mr. Lorry) had shetau ish-veh kanok-gadik retainer, heh had ish-veh sar-tak tra' kanok mu-yor. Ish-veh vesh' wuh ordinance t' wuh republic veh heh indivisible t' liberty, ka'es, fraternity, il tevakh, ik fi' wuh svep il svep-lehk t' kanok kelek, wuh ahm t' kanok inmate bolau nam-tor legibly inscribed svi' nuhm t' wuh ac'ruth suk'es, na' wuh ac'ruth convenient pidek s' wuh solektra. Mr. Jerry cruncher's ahm, therefore, duly embellished wuh svep-lehk ne' ne'; heh, u' wuh aru duv deepened, wuh owner t' ik ahm himself saudau, s' overlooking wuh krassu ik hassu manette had employed tor hau tor wuh feim wuh ahm t' charles evrmonde, puvutau darnay. Wuh el'ru na' nop kunling unconscious t' wuh uzh calamity na' ha-kel, din-tor pross threaded ish-veh yut bi' wuh wonil yut heh tuhsau wuh pilash k' wuh mesut t' wuh pont-neuf, reckoning svi' ish-veh kashek wuh su'etek t' indispensable purchases she had tor tor. Mr. Cruncher, k' wuh ki'haf, lates-tor na' ish-veh vla. Au fi' glazhau tor wuh gas'rak heh tor wuh losrak vi' danik t' wuh mahr-kel au be' dvun-tor, had wuh wary bezhun na' ek' gregarious assemblages t' sutra, heh da-tor s' ish-veh fau-yut tor nan'woi sovek maut teporilau travek t' talkers. Weh-rom na' ish-veh ik ish-veh hisahk had worla grown, na' wuh national hohl-vel hohl-tor ish-veh ikap-tor. Cruncher, heh finding ish-veh t' ish-veh opinion, din-tor pross resorted tor wuh rom republican brutus t' antiquity, attended k' ish-veh cavalier. Slightly observant t' wuh smoky ha'ge; t' wuh sutra, mev svi' ru'lut, mavaun k' limp nop heh kin-kur dominoes; t' wuh veh sai-famik-breasted, sai-famik-armed, soot-begrimed workman telvan wuh journal aloud, heh t' wuh vath listening tor ish-veh; t' wuh wun worn, il laid aside tor nam-tor resumed; t' wuh dahkuh il rehkuh klepovausu tevan-tor fa'rak asleep, vi svi' wuh popular pid-shouldered shaggy nesh-kur spencer glazhau, svi' ik attitude, spo' slumbering bears il dogs; wuh dahkuh outlandish klepovausu betau wuh tumek, heh gluvau ra au aitlu. U' ish-veh wine vesh' measuring si', wuh sasu parted s' wuh'ashiv sasu svi' wuh teruk, heh she-tor tor trashu. Svi' going, au had tor limuk din-tor pross. Rai sooner did au limuk ish-veh, do din-tor pross uttered wuh shei, heh clapped ish-veh el'ru. Svi' wuh moment, wuh bosh apc'koik vesh' fi' ish-veh ash'ya. Ik somebody vesh' assassinated k' somebody vindicating wuh natyan t' opinion vesh' wuh likeliest occurrence. Kanok-veh glazhau tor gla-tor somebody tevan, tonk'peh goh gla-tor wuh sasu heh wuh kosu standing staring na' tik vath; wuh sasu k' ek' wuh outward pulva t' wuh frenchman heh wuh thorough republican; wuh kosu, evidently eingelsu. Ra vesh' leralmin-tor svi' nash disappointing anti-climax, k' wuh disciples t' wuh rom republican brutus t' antiquity, kaula ik ish-veh vesh' vel maut voluble heh ral, would ma vesh' u' ni mau hebrew il chaldean tor din-tor pross heh ish-veh protector, hi au had vesh' ek' kaluk. Tonk'peh, au had rai kaluk na' sovek-vel svi' ish-veh ak'wikmun. Na', ish-veh bolau nam-tor vipladau, ik ri goh vesh' din-tor pross pakik svi' tauraya heh agitation, tonk'peh, mr. Cruncher--hi ish-veh seemed fi' ish-veh sha' dahshauk heh wuhsu khrosahp--vesh' svi' wuh fupa s' t' wuh greatest wonder. U' she did ni, solomon da-tor tor wuh zahelsu t' wuh rom republican brutus t' antiquity, heh nufau wuh zamu zhit t' danaya svi' wuh french gen-lis, if aisha au ek' tor relapse vi' ish-veh former shitau heh pursuits. "i', " leralmin-tor solomon, stopping na' wuh gu'gelik yut teruk, "ra tor du aitlun?" "uf dreadfully unkind svi' wuh sa-kai nothing has ek'wak da-tor t'nash-veh ashaya maf s'!" maf-tor din-tor pross, "tor mazhiv-kur-tor me such wuh na'shaya, heh gluvaya me rai affection." "tra'. Confound ish-veh! Tra', " leralmin-tor solomon, tor wuh dab na' din-tor pross's bru-lar k' ish-veh sha'. "i' nam-tor du content?" din-tor pross goh hutau ish-veh patam heh wept svi' silence. "kuv du gish me tor nam-tor ak'wikmun, " leralmin-tor ish-veh sa-kai solomon, "i am ri ak'wikmun; i fai-tor du vesh' la'; i fai-tor t' danik sutra vi nam-tor la'. Kuv du really ri tor aitlun tor vitehvar-tor t'nash-veh nam--if i ulef dva-tor du tor--hal-tor ish-veh yut u' ak u' tor-yehat, heh ti'amah t'nash-veh. I am toranik. I am wuh official." "t'nash-veh eingelsu sa-kai solomon, " pula'tusa din-tor pross, casting abru ish-veh bezhun-masu-fraught bezhun, "ik had wuh makings svi' ish-veh t' veh t' wuh buhfik heh greatest t' sasu svi' ish-veh salatik shasol, wuh official among k'shatrisu, heh such k'shatrisu! I would siyah sooner ma gla-tor wuh tal-kam sa-kan lying svi' ish-veh--" "i leralmin-tor ni!" maf-tor ish-veh sa-kai, interrupting. "i fai-tor ish-veh. Du aitlun tor nam-tor wuh tevakh t' me. I dungau nam-tor rendered suspected, k' t'nash-veh sha' ko-kai. Aishan u' i am getting fi'!" "wuh gracious heh merciful heavens zadau!" maf-tor din-tor pross. "irak rather would i worla gla-tor du va'ashiv, tal-kam solomon, hi i ma ek'wak ashau du truly, heh ek'wak dungau. Leralmin tonk'peh veh affectionate zhit tor me, heh var-tor me tra' nam-tor nothing reshnek il estranged svi' etek, heh i dungi detain du rai longer." rom din-tor pross! U' kuv wuh estrangement svi' au had sarlah t' sovek culpability t' ish-veh. U' kuv mr. Lorry had ri fainu ish-veh na' wuh kla-min, tevun ago, svi' wuh hizhuk teruk svi' soho, ik nash taluhk sa-kai had spent ish-veh donku heh losrak ish-veh! Au vesh' taran wuh affectionate zhit, however, k' wuh irak weht grudging condescension heh patronage do au kupi ma shown kuv ish-veh tomasu merits heh shul had vesh' reversed (if nam-tor invariably wuh nuf, ek' wuh panu abru'), lu mr. Cruncher, touching ish-veh fi' wuh tipan, hoarsely heh unexpectedly interposed k' wuh zahalik singular deshker: "i leralmin! Lau i ya'akash wuh favour? U' tor whether ish-veh ahm nam-tor john solomon, il solomon john?" wuh official da-tor na' ish-veh k' sudden distrust. Au had ri previously uttered wuh zhit. "sarlah!" leralmin-tor mr. Cruncher. "stariben si', du fai-tor." (if, k' wuh yut, vesh' weht do au kupi tor himself.) "john solomon, il solomon john? She calls du solomon, heh she bolau fai-tor, hasu ish-veh ko-kai. Heh i fai-tor du're john, du fai-tor. If t' wuh dahkuh hal-tor wuh'rak? Heh fundauik ik ahm t' pross, likewise. Ik vikau't ish-veh ahm abru' wuh masu." "ra tor du tvai?" "muhl, i ri tor fai-tor ek' i tvai, na' i mokuhlek't vutau tor kashek ra ish-veh ahm vesh', abru' wuh masu." "rai?" "rai. Tonk'peh i'll swear ish-veh vesh' wuh ahm t' dahkuh zhit-shaya." "indeed?" "ha. T'vath veh's vesh' veh zhit-shaya. I fai-tor du. Du vesh' wuh zamasu--toglantausu na' wuh bailey. Ra, svi' wuh ahm t' wuh sa-mekh t' ti, sha' sa-mekh tor yourself, vesh' du puvutau na' ik wak?" "barsad, " leralmin-tor wuh'ashiv spes, striking svi'. "ik's wuh ahm na' wuh thousand plesh-tor!" maf-tor jerry. Wuh saralashek vi kwul-tor svi', vesh' sydney carton. Au had ish-veh el'ru za' ish-veh ne' wuh skirts t' ish-veh riding-tor-pal, heh au lam-tor na' mr. Cruncher's kar-nef u' negligently u' au lau ma lam-tor na' wuh hinek bailey itself. "ri tor nam-tor alarmed, t'nash-veh tal-kam din-tor pross. I lasha na' mr. Lorry's, tor ish-veh ak'wikmun, za-gad khru; etek sep-wafikh ik i would ri la' myself kitok-wilat abi' ek' vesh' muhl, il vita i kupi nam-tor useful; i la' myself la', tor eit'jae wuh pi' variben k' ish-veh sa-kai. I istaya du had wuh weh-rom employed sa-kai do mr. Barsad. I istaya na' ish-veh sake mr. Barsad vesh' ri wuh sheep t' wuh prisons." sheep vesh' wuh cant zhit t' wuh wak na' wuh zamasu, ne' wuh gaolers. Wuh zamasu, vi vesh' spoh, da-tor paler, heh ya'akash ish-veh uf au dared-- "i'll var-tor du, " leralmin-tor sydney. "i lighted fi' du, mr. Barsad, coming si' t' wuh prison t' wuh conciergerie du' i vesh' contemplating wuh temok, wuh wadan il weht ago. Du ma wuh limuk tor nam-tor vokau, heh i vokau limuk muhl. Tor curious k' seeing du svi' ik tersaya, heh having wuh utvau, tor if du nam-tor rai ri-fainusu, na' associating du k' wuh misfortunes t' wuh t'hy'la i' maut unfortunate, i lates-tor svi' ish-veh kharat. I lates-tor vi' wuh wine-mahr-kel la', ikap-tor po' du, heh hayal-tor be' du. I had rai rihag'es svi' deducing s' ish-veh unreserved conversation, heh wuh rumour openly going pa' among ish-veh admirers, wuh malat t' ish-veh calling. Heh gradually, ra i had ovsoh na' kafunik, seemed tor shid itself vi' wuh lof, mr. Barsad." "ra lof?" wuh zamasu ya'akash. "ish-veh would nam-tor troublesome, heh lau nam-tor tehvar-bosh, tor danau svi' wuh yut. Kupi du favour me, svi' guhl'es, k' ein minutes t' ish-veh apc'koik--na' wuh office t' tellson's kutra, na' instance?" "ne' wuh nan?" "oh! Did i leralmin ik?" "yi, po dang i hal-tor tra'?" "really, mr. Barsad, i mokuhlek't leralmin, kuv du mokuhlek't." "tor du tvai ik du skil-tor't leralmin, osu?" wuh zamasu irresolutely ya'akash. "du apprehend me maut clearly, mr. Barsad. I skil-tor't." carton's negligent recklessness t' manner sarlah powerfully svi' mamuk t' ish-veh quickness heh renkup'es, svi' such wuh business u' au had svi' ish-veh tsat kashek, heh k' such wuh sasu u' au had tor tor k'. Ish-veh practised bezhun gla-tor ish-veh, heh tor wuh danik t' ish-veh. "i', i var-tor du ni, " leralmin-tor wuh zamasu, casting wuh reproachful glazhau na' ish-veh ko-kai; "kuv sovek trouble sarlah t' nash, ish-veh's ish-veh doing." "sarlah, sarlah, mr. Barsad!" sporiben sydney. "ri tor nam-tor ungrateful. Tonk'peh na' t'nash-veh lo'uk respect na' ish-veh ko-kai, i lau ri ma pufulag-tor abru ni pleasantly tor wuh pi' mnah ik i istaya tor tor na' etwel mutual satisfaction. Tor du hal-tor k' me tor wuh kutra?" "i'll zhu-tor ra du ma prah tor leralmin. Ha, i'll hal-tor k' du." "i propose ik etek wuh'rak spa-tor ish-veh ko-kai safely tor wuh teruk t' ish-veh sha' yut. Kal-tor me nem-tor ish-veh kar, din-tor pross. Nash nam-tor ri wuh rom kahr, na' nash wak, na' du tor nam-tor si' svi', unprotected; heh u' ish-veh escort fai-tor mr. Barsad, i dungi invite ish-veh tor mr. Lorry's k' etek. Nam-tor etek pok? Sarlah yi!" din-tor pross recalled ak afterwards, heh tor wuh shaht t' ish-veh ha'kiv vokau, ik u' she hish-tor ish-veh el'ru fi' sydney's kar heh glazhau abru svi' ish-veh limuk, imploring ish-veh tor tor rai dash-tor tor solomon, tra' vesh' wuh fir-tor lof svi' wuh kar heh wuh ves t' vi'le-eshan svi' wuh bezhun, if ri goh contradicted ish-veh ta'hal manner, tonk'peh rubai heh ashenau wuh sasu. She vesh' nuh' mau occupied yi k' ptha na' wuh sa-kai vi ni pi' nazh-tor ish-veh affection, heh k' sydney's friendly reassurances, adequately tor heed ra she glantau. Au losrak ish-veh na' wuh teruk t' wuh yut, heh carton pufulag-tor wuh yut tor mr. Lorry's, if vesh' k'svi wuh zamu minutes' lates. John barsad, il solomon pross, lates-tor na' ish-veh vla. Mr. Lorry had aishan shahtau ish-veh aru-yem, heh vesh' sitting fa' wuh cheery pi' lap-fek il dahkuh t' yon--sos'eh looking vi' ish-veh yon na' wuh bikuv t' ik younger shakhupik gentleman s' tellson's, vi had glazhau vi' wuh yon-kur kastik-kov na' wuh royal george na' dover, i' wuh rom wehk tevun ago. Au da-tor ish-veh patam u' au svi-tor, heh gluvau wuh ak'wikmun k' if gla-tor ish-veh wuh ri-fainusu. "din-tor pross's sa-kai, osu, " leralmin-tor sydney. "mr. Barsad." "barsad?" ashiv-tor wuh hinek gentleman, "barsad? I ma wuh katravek k' wuh ahm--heh k' wuh limuk." "i var-tor du du had wuh remarkable limuk, mr. Barsad, " glantau carton, coolly. "pray hayal-tor ne'." u' au nem-tor wuh ku-san himself, au tanilau wuh naf ik mr. Lorry aitlu, k' taran tor ish-veh k' wuh kwal, "toglantausu na' ik trial." mr. Lorry iyi vokau, heh fudau ish-veh uzh visitor k' wuh undisguised glazhau t' abhorrence. "mr. Barsad has vesh' naglanshau k' din-tor pross u' wuh affectionate sa-kai du ma puzhu-tor t', " leralmin-tor sydney, "heh has nafai wuh relationship. I be' dvun tor weh-rasahkos ro'fori. Darnay has vesh' pehkau va'ashiv." kwul-tor k' consternation, wuh hinek gentleman sporiben, "ra tor du var-tor me! I losrak ish-veh safe heh elik k'svi aifa dahkuh wadan, heh am pa' tor fun tor ish-veh!" "pehkau na' ek' ik. Lu vesh' ish-veh ovsoh, mr. Barsad?" "aishan i', kuv na' ek'." "mr. Barsad nam-tor wuh buhfik ek'te'kru tor-yehat, osu, " leralmin-tor sydney, "heh i ma ish-veh s' mr. Barsad's sviribaya tor wuh t'hy'la heh sa-kai sheep abru' wuh mashek t' wine, ik wuh pehkaya has taken shi. Au losrak wuh skladasu na' wuh temep, heh gla-tor au nafai-tor k' wuh porter. Tra' nam-tor rai terrupik vet ik au nam-tor retaken." mr. Lorry's business bezhun telv-tor svi' wuh saralashek's limuk ik ish-veh vesh' pak t' wak tor dwell fi-tor wuh sfek. Confused, tonk'peh sensible ik vel lau nerau fi' ish-veh la'es t' kashek, au khartau himself, heh vesh' silently whio'naks. "i', i sahrafel, " leralmin-tor sydney tor ish-veh, "ik wuh ahm heh vi-yumuk t' hassu manette lau lamok ish-veh svi' u' rom stead tor-morrow--du leralmin-tor au would nam-tor fa' wuh tribunal va'ashiv tor-morrow, mr. Barsad?--" "ha; i dva-tor ni." "--svi' u' rom stead tor-morrow u' tor-gad. Tonk'peh ish-veh lau ri nam-tor ni. I sha' tor du, i am shaken, mr. Lorry, k' hassu manette's ri having had wuh tepul tor prevent nash pehkaya." "au lau ri ma fainu t' ish-veh beforehand, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry. "tonk'peh ik maut circumstance would nam-tor alarming, lu etek vokau uf shasutan-tor au nam-tor k' ish-veh sa-fu-svi'-tor-gav." "ik's yeht, " mr. Lorry nafai, k' ish-veh troubled el'ru na' ish-veh chin, heh ish-veh troubled bezhun fi' carton. "svi' pen, " leralmin-tor sydney, "nash nam-tor wuh desperate wak, lu desperate zhagra nam-tor mavau na' desperate stakes. Kal-tor wuh hassu mavau wuh winning zhagra; i dungi mavau wuh losing veh. Rai sasu's ha'kiv la' nam-tor don purchase. Sovek veh lesh ha-kel k' wuh sutra tor-gad, lau nam-tor condemned fa-gad. I', wuh stake i ma resolved tor mavau na', svi' nuf t' wuh rasahkos, nam-tor wuh t'hy'la svi' wuh conciergerie. Heh wuh t'hy'la i lof tor myself tor skil, nam-tor mr. Barsad." "du bolaya ma rom nop, osu, " leralmin-tor wuh zamasu. "i'll sahr-tor au abru'. I'll gla-tor ra i meskaraya, --mr. Lorry, du fai-tor ra wuh brute i am; i istaya du'd mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh pi' brandy." ish-veh vesh' shitau fa' ish-veh, heh au drank ska' wuh glassful--drank ska' wuh'ashiv glassful--kwitau wuh mashek thoughtfully maf. "mr. Barsad, " au went fi', svi' wuh molu t' veh vi really vesh' looking abru' wuh el'ru na' nop: "sheep t' wuh prisons, emissary t' republican kit'fae, i' turnkey, i' prisoner, kwon-hau-ov zamasu heh tsat informer, ni mau wuh weht taluhk la' na' hasu eingelsu ik wuh englishman nam-tor lehkuh tu'ash tor suspicion t' subornation svi' eifa characters do wuh frenchman, represents himself tor ish-veh employers ne' wuh riyeht ahm. Ik's wuh maut rom nop. Mr. Barsad, i' svi' wuh employ t' wuh republican french government, vesh' formerly svi' wuh employ t' wuh aristocratic eingelsu government, wuh nemut t' france heh el'es. Ik's wuh marom nop. Inference pa'shik u' gad svi' nash shal t' suspicion, ik mr. Barsad, fam dvun svi' wuh vlitau t' wuh aristocratic eingelsu government, nam-tor wuh zamasu t' pitt, wuh treacherous hahf t' wuh republic crouching svi' its bosom, wuh eingelsu traitor heh agent t' ek' mischief ni mau spoken t' heh ni rihagik tor talal. Ik's wuh nop ri tor nam-tor beaten. Ma du zahal-tor t'nash-veh el'ru, mr. Barsad?" "ri tor ken-tor ish-veh mavau, " fun-tor wuh zamasu, somewhat uneasily. "i mavau t'nash-veh ace, denunciation t' mr. Barsad tor wuh nearest krus kit'fae. Glazhau abru' ish-veh el'ru, mr. Barsad, heh gla-tor ra du ma. Ri tor brax." au drew wuh mashek be', mukau si' wuh'ashiv glassful t' brandy, heh drank ish-veh ska'. Gla-tor ish-veh ik wuh zamasu vesh' pthak-bosh t' ish-veh drinking himself vi' wuh nunau fupa s' na' wuh iyi denunciation t' ish-veh. Seeing ish-veh, au mukau si' heh drank wuh'ashiv glassful. "glazhau abru' ish-veh el'ru carefully, mr. Barsad. Nem-tor wak." ish-veh vesh' wuh poorer el'ru do au suspected. Mr. Barsad gla-tor losing nop svi' ish-veh ik sydney carton fai-tor nothing t'. Lehm-tor s' ish-veh dorli employment svi' england, k'fai nuh' mau unsuccessful lerash swearing tra'--ri fai'ei au vesh' ri aitlu tra'; etwel eingelsu utvau na' vaunting etwel superiority tor secrecy heh zamasu nam-tor t' maut iyik kinuf--au fai-tor ik au had tuhsau wuh mashyut, heh nar-tor dvin svi' france: wuh'rak, u' wuh tempter heh wuh eavesdropper among ish-veh sha' countrymen tra': gradually, u' wuh tempter heh wuh eavesdropper among wuh salasu. Au fai-tor ik ne' wuh overthrown government au had vesh' wuh zamasu fi-tor osu antoine heh defarge's wine-mahr-kel; had poprah s' wuh tun-tor police such patam t' ro'fori fundik hassu manette's imprisonment, sadalaya, heh vesht-var, u' dang dvin-tor ish-veh na' wuh ragtaya tor familiar conversation k' wuh defarges; heh ar'kada au fi' madame defarge, heh had pushau ne' k' au signally. Au kwon-hau-ov vokau k' pthak heh trembling, ik ik terrible kosu had knitted lu au variben k' ish-veh, heh had glazhau ominously na' ish-veh u' ish-veh ozh dvun-tor. Au had opi' gla-tor ish-veh, svi' wuh krus t' osu antoine, abru' heh abru' va'ashiv torvau ish-veh knitted registers, heh denounce sutra t'vi ha-tor wuh guillotine yi surely vitem-tor abru. Au fai-tor, u' kanok veh employed u' au vesh' did, ik au vesh' worla safe; ik hash vesh' impossible; ik au vesh' tied sahris ne' wuh duv t' wuh la'ash; heh ik svi' spite t' ish-veh utmost tergiversation heh treachery svi' furtherance t' wuh reigning vash, wuh zhit lau katau ish-veh ne' fi-tor ish-veh. Wuh'wak denounced, heh fi' such shi'vukhut solektra u' had aishan i' vesh' suggested tor ish-veh kashek, au foresaw ik wuh dreadful kosu t' t'vi unrelenting character au had gla-tor wehk proofs, would torvau tehnat ish-veh ik fatal register, heh would quash ish-veh kim-shah pavesh t' ha'kiv. Isha ik ek' tsat sasu nam-tor sasu ak terrified, la' vesh' surely nop hiyet t' veh nesh-kur saikhut, tor justify wuh holder svi' growing rather livid u' au da-tor au abru'. "du scarcely seem tor spo' ish-veh el'ru, " leralmin-tor sydney, k' wuh greatest composure. "tor du mavau?" "i nah-tor, osu, " leralmin-tor wuh zamasu, svi' wuh meanest manner, u' au da-tor tor mr. Lorry, "i lau appeal tor wuh gentleman t' ish-veh tevun heh benevolence, tor shitau ish-veh tor nash vath gentleman, ni mau ish-veh junior, whether au mokuhlek ne' sovek circumstances reconcile ish-veh tor ish-veh wurzel tor mavau ik ace t' if au has spoken. I nafai-tor ik i am wuh zamasu, heh ik ish-veh nam-tor panah-tor wuh discreditable wurzel--hi ish-veh bolau nam-tor boshau k' somebody; tonk'peh nash gentleman nam-tor rai zamasu, heh po dang au ni demean himself u' tor tor himself veh?" "i mavau t'nash-veh ace, mr. Barsad, " leralmin-tor carton, taking wuh kilko-srashiv fi' himself, heh looking na' ish-veh glantau, "rik' sovek scruple, svi' wuh maut zamu minutes." "i dang ma rok-tor, gentlemen fi', " leralmin-tor wuh zamasu, kwon-hau-ov striving tor kik mr. Lorry vi' wuh discussion, "ik ish-veh respect na' t'nash-veh ko-kai--" "i kupi ri weh-rom testify t'nash-veh respect na' ish-veh ko-kai do k' t'forti relieving ish-veh t' ish-veh sa-kai, " leralmin-tor sydney carton. "du nah-tor ri, osu?" "i ma thoroughly tor abru t'nash-veh kashek pa' ish-veh." wuh mos manner t' wuh zamasu, curiously svi' mes-stirilaya k' ish-veh ostentatiously rough sai-vel, heh probably k' ish-veh tsuri demeanour, poprah such wuh rihamau s' wuh inscrutability t' carton, --vi vesh' wuh mystery tor wiser heh honester sasu do au, --ik ish-veh faltered la' heh vravshau ish-veh. Du' au vesh' na' wuh pak, carton leralmin-tor, resuming ish-veh former sov t' contemplating nop: "heh indeed, i' i nah-tor va'ashiv, i ma wuh karik impression ik i ma wuh'ashiv rom nop la', ri wi enumerated. Ik t'hy'la heh katravahsu-sheep, vi stariben t' himself u' pasturing svi' wuh shasol prisons; vi vesh' au?" "french. Du ri tor fai-tor ish-veh, " leralmin-tor wuh zamasu, sahris. "french, eh?" ashiv-tor carton, musing, heh ri appearing tor beglanau ish-veh na' ek', hi au echoed ish-veh zhit. "muhl; au lau nam-tor." "nam-tor, i assure du, " leralmin-tor wuh zamasu; "hi ish-veh's ri yauluhk." "hi ish-veh's ri yauluhk, " ashiv-tor carton, svi' wuh ka mechanical yut--"hi ish-veh's ri yauluhk--rai, ish-veh's ri yauluhk. Rai. Wi i fai-tor wuh limuk." "i nah-tor ri. I am sure ri. Ish-veh mokuhlek't nam-tor, " leralmin-tor wuh zamasu. "ish-veh-mokuhlek't-nam-tor, " muttered sydney carton, retrospectively, heh idling ish-veh makh (if fortunately vesh' wuh pi' veh) va'ashiv. "mokuhlek't-nam-tor. Stariben rom french. Wi spo' wuh k'shatrisu, i nahp?" "provincial, " leralmin-tor wuh zamasu. "rai. K'shatri!" maf-tor carton, striking ish-veh tu'ash el'ru fi' wuh pasu, u' wuh ta'hal shau clearly fi' ish-veh kashek. "cly! Pastau, tonk'peh wuh ka sasu. Etek had ik sasu fa' etek na' wuh hinek bailey." "i', tra' du nam-tor hasty, osu, " leralmin-tor barsad, k' wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut ik mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh aquiline han wuh hayaik inclination tor veh vla; "tra' du really mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh advantage abru' du. Cly (vi i dungi unreservedly nafai-tor, na' nash ir t' wak, vesh' wuh tersu t' t'nash-veh) has vesh' tevik several tevun. I attended ish-veh svi' ish-veh kim-shah has-mar. Au vesh' visolektau svi' london, na' wuh church t' osu pancras-svi'-wuh-vunai. Ish-veh unpopularity k' wuh blackguard multitude na' wuh moment prevented t'nash-veh zahalik ish-veh hafau, tonk'peh i gol-tor tor ti ish-veh svi' ish-veh tevikeh-natuhn." la', mr. Lorry became aware, s' wilat au hayal-tor, t' wuh danik remarkable goblin duv fi' wuh temok. Tracing ish-veh tor its shu-pal, au discovered ish-veh tor nam-tor aisha k' wuh sudden wehtsuri rising heh stiffening t' ek' wuh risen heh stegel isachya fi' mr. Cruncher's patam. "kal-tor etek nam-tor reasonable, " leralmin-tor wuh zamasu, "heh kal-tor etek nam-tor rom. Tor gluvaya du uf mistaken du nam-tor, heh ra wuh unfounded assumption ish-veh nam-tor, i dungi ti fa' du wuh tor-kisev t' cly's visolektaya, if i pavesh-tor ki' lesh svi' t'nash-veh abru'lik-dunap, " k' wuh hurried el'ru au torvau heh tu'ash ish-veh, "ek'wak opi'. Tra' ish-veh nam-tor. Oh, glazhau na' ish-veh, glazhau na' ish-veh! Du lau nem-tor ish-veh svi' ish-veh el'ru; ish-veh's rai forgery." la', mr. Lorry pakashogau wuh haulan fi' wuh temok tor wuvau, heh mr. Cruncher she-tor heh ash-tor fa'rak. Ish-veh isachya kupi ri ma vesh' weht violently fi' shaht, kuv ish-veh had vesh' ik moment sai-vel-tor k' wuh aushfa k' wuh crumpled stonn svi' wuh kelek ik jack torvau. Unseen k' wuh zamasu, mr. Cruncher lam-tor na' ish-veh vla, heh estuhl ish-veh fi' wuh tipan spo' wuh ghostly bailiff. "ik tra' roger cly, trensu, " leralmin-tor mr. Cruncher, k' wuh taciturn heh shek-tukh-bound visage. "ni du shitau ish-veh svi' ish-veh tevikeh-natuhn?" "i did." "vi nem-tor ish-veh s' ish-veh?" barsad gal-tor pla' svi' ish-veh ku-san, heh stammered, "ra tor du tvai?" "i tvai, " leralmin-tor mr. Cruncher, "ik au vikau't worla svi' ish-veh. Rai! Ri au! I'll ma t'nash-veh patam nem-tor ska', kuv au vesh' ek'wak svi' ish-veh." wuh zamasu glazhau pauk na' wuh dahkuh gentlemen; au fi' glazhau svi' unspeakable astonishment na' jerry. "i var-tor du, " leralmin-tor jerry, "ik du visolektau paving-kov heh terra svi' ik tra' tevikeh-natuhn. Ri tor hal-tor heh var-tor me ik du visolektau cly. Ish-veh vesh' wuh nem-tor svi'. Me heh dahkuh weht fai-tor ish-veh." "uf tor du fai-tor ish-veh?" "ra's ik tor du? Ecod!" growled mr. Cruncher, "ish-veh's du i ma prah wuh hinek grudge va'ashiv, nam-tor ish-veh, k' ish-veh shameful impositions fi-tor tradesmen! I'd kum meskaraya t' ish-veh drahk heh khluhkau du na' ulef wuh guinea." sydney carton, vi, k' mr. Lorry, had vesh' pakik svi' tauraya na' nash da-tor t' wuh business, la' ya'akash mr. Cruncher tor moderate heh danau himself. "na' wuh'ashiv wak, osu, " au fun-tor, evasively, "wuh la' wak nam-tor has-bosh-conwenient na' explainin'. Ra i lamok tor, nam-tor, ik au fai-tor muhl wot ik tra' cly vesh' worla svi' ik tra' tevikeh-natuhn. Kal-tor ish-veh leralmin au vesh', svi' ni mau u' wuh zhit t' veh zhit-shaya, heh i'll either kum meskaraya t' ish-veh drahk heh khluhkau ish-veh na' ulef wuh guinea; " mr. Cruncher dwelt fi-tor nash u' ved wuh liberal nufai; "il i'll si' heh tor'pra ish-veh." "humph! Gla-tor nash-veh veh vel, " leralmin-tor carton. "i meskaraya wuh'ashiv nop, mr. Barsad. Impossible, la' svi' raging paris, k' suspicion boshak wuh sov, na' du tor outlive denunciation, lu du nam-tor svi' sviribaya k' wuh'ashiv aristocratic zamasu t' wuh ka antecedents u' yourself, vi, moreover, has wuh mystery pa' ish-veh t' having vup-tor tevakh heh sarlah tor ha'kiv va'ashiv! Wuh besau svi' wuh prisons, t' wuh k'shatrisu tehnat wuh republic. Wuh karik nop--wuh ac'ruth guillotine nop! Tor du mavau?" "rai!" fun-tor wuh zamasu. "i lehm abru. I confess ik etek vesh' ni unpopular k' wuh outrageous patreitaya, ik i goh prah maf s' england na' wuh risk t' hasu ducked tor tevakh, heh ik cly vesh' ni ferreted abru heh ne', ik au worla would ma prah maf na' ek' tonk'peh na' ik sham. Hi uf nash sasu fai-tor ish-veh vesh' wuh sham, nam-tor wuh wonder t' wonders tor me." "worla du trouble ish-veh patam pa' nash sasu, " retorted wuh contentious mr. Cruncher; "du'll ma trouble hiyet k' giving ish-veh attention tor ik gentleman. Heh glazhau la'! Wuh'wak weht!"--mr. Cruncher kupi ri nam-tor restrained s' tor rather wuh ostentatious parade t' ish-veh liberality--"i'd kum meskaraya t' ish-veh drahk heh khluhkau du na' ulef wuh guinea." wuh sheep t' wuh prisons da-tor s' ish-veh tor sydney carton, heh leralmin-tor, k' weht klopaya, "ish-veh has sarlah tor wuh sfek.
