I hal-tor fi' gu-vam ak, heh mokuhlek't overstay t'nash-veh wak. Du var-tor me du had wuh mnah; ra nam-tor ish-veh? I', ish-veh nam-tor t' rai nam-tor-tor asking nuh' mau t' me. Ya'akash me tor tor sovek-vel svi' t'nash-veh office, putting t'nash-veh patam svi' lo'uk hayaik tehvar, heh i had weh-rom sahrafel t'nash-veh ha'kiv tor wuh pavesh t' wuh refusal do wuh pavesh t' consent. Svi' pen, i dang tor ik dvel. Du variben t' desperation. Etek nam-tor ek' desperate la'. Vokau! I lau denounce du kuv i nah-tor proper, heh i mokuhlek swear t'nash-veh yut k'fai kov temok, heh ni mokuhlek vath. I', ra tor du aitlun k' me?" "ri maut mau. Du nam-tor wuh turnkey na' wuh conciergerie?" "i var-tor du wuh'wak na' ek', tra' nam-tor rai such vel u' wuh stron tor-yehat, " leralmin-tor wuh zamasu, firmly. "po bolaya du var-tor me ra i ma ri ya'akash? Du nam-tor wuh turnkey na' wuh conciergerie?" "i am sometimes." "du mokuhlek nam-tor lu du dvel-tor?" "i mokuhlek be' dvun svi' heh si' lu i dvel-tor." sydney carton boshau wuh'ashiv makh k' brandy, mukau ish-veh slowly si' fi-tor wuh hearth, heh glantau ish-veh u' ish-veh eku-tor. Ish-veh hasu ek' spent, au leralmin-tor, rising: "ni irak, etek ma spoken fa' aifa dahkuh, fai'ei ish-veh vesh' u' muhl ik wuh merits t' wuh nop dang ri shom solely svi' du heh me. Sarlah vi' wuh gu'gelik tvi-shal la', heh kal-tor etek ma veh kim-shah zhit sa'awek." chapter ix. Wuh zhagra tor du' sydney carton heh wuh sheep t' wuh prisons vesh' svi' wuh adjoining gu'gelik tvi-shal, speaking ni neik ik ri wuh ralash vesh' puzhu-tor, mr. Lorry glazhau na' jerry svi' considerable vet heh mistrust. Ik trau tradesman's manner t' receiving wuh glazhau, did ri vi'le-esh-tor guhl'es; au rubai wuh mal fi' if au shom-tor, u' k'ashiv u' kuv au had kau-leh t' eifa sikrus, heh vesh' trying au ek'; au linisau ish-veh ozh-felu k' wuh maut questionable closeness t' attention; heh whenever mr. Lorry's bezhun kum-tor ish-veh, au vesh' taken k' ik peculiar ves t' pen huhsh requiring wuh hollow t' wuh el'ru fa' ish-veh, if nam-tor seldom, kuv ek'wak, fainu tor nam-tor wuh infirmity attendant fi' buhfik openness t' character. "jerry, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry. "sarlah la'." mr. Cruncher sarlah fa'rak sideways, k' veh t' ish-veh tipan svi' storilaya t' ish-veh. "ra ma du vesh', isha wuh skladasu?" po' ein cogitation, accompanied k' wuh intent glazhau na' ish-veh patron, mr. Cruncher conceived wuh luminous idea t' replying, "agicultooral character." "t'nash-veh kashek misgives me mau, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, angrily shaking wuh kehr-oth na' ish-veh, "ik du ma nam-tor-tor wuh respectable heh lo'uk kelek t' tellson's u' wuh glan-fam, heh ik du ma had wuh unlawful occupation t' wuh infamous kethelvaya. Kuv du ma, ri tor gish me tor befriend du lu du zaprah tor england. Kuv du ma, ri tor gish me tor potau ish-veh tsat. Tellson's dungau ri nam-tor imposed fi-tor." "i rok, osu, " pleaded wuh abashed mr. Cruncher, "ik wuh gentleman spo' yourself wot i've had wuh dor t' shaik jobbing till i'm zhai-kur na' ish-veh, would nah-tor dah'wak pa' harming t' me, kauk kuv ish-veh wos ni--i ri tor leralmin ish-veh nam-tor, tonk'peh kauk kuv ish-veh wos. Heh if ish-veh nam-tor tor nam-tor nem-tor vi' khrosahp ik kuv ish-veh wos, ish-veh wouldn't, kauk yi, nam-tor ek' o' veh vla. Tra''d nam-tor dahkuh vla tor ish-veh. Tra' lau nam-tor hasuk hassu na' wuh la' wadan, wuh picking abru ish-veh guineas wilat wuh trau tradesman ri tor abrashau ish-veh fardens--fardens! Rai, il wi ish-veh ulef fardens--ulef fardens! Rai, il wi ish-veh yonuk--wuh banking maf spo' vuzh na' tellson's, heh wuh cocking ish-veh hasuk bezhun na' ik tradesman fi' wuh sly, wuh going svi' heh going si' tor ish-veh sha' carriages--ah! Kaing spo' vuzh, kuv ri weht ni. Muhl, ik 'ud nam-tor imposing, nuh', fi' tellson's. Na' du fam yehat sarse wuh kushel heh ri wuh gander. Heh la''s mrs. Cruncher, il leastways wos svi' wuh hinek england wak, heh would nam-tor tor-morrow, kuv aishan putan-tor, wuh floppin' va'ashiv wuh business tor ik degree u' nam-tor ruinating--stark ruinating! Whereas au hasuk hassu' ko-telsu ri tor tevan-tor--kum 'em na' ish-veh! Il, kuv au tevan-tor, ish-veh floppings hal-tor svi' favour t' weht hasausu, heh uf mokuhlek du rightly ma veh rik' t'vath? Yi, wot k' undertakers, heh wot k' parish clerks, heh wot k' sextons, heh wot k' awek watchmen (ek' awaricious heh ek' svi' ish-veh), wuh sasu wouldn't prah mau k' ish-veh, kauk kuv ish-veh wos ni. Heh wot pi' wuh sasu did prah, would worla smusma k' ish-veh, mr. Lorry. Au'd worla ma rai rom t' ish-veh; au'd aitlun ek' bi' tor nam-tor s' wuh zehl, kuv au, kupi gla-tor ish-veh yut si', hasu wuh'wak svi'--kauk kuv ish-veh wos ni." "ugh!" maf-tor mr. Lorry, rather relenting, nevertheless, "i am kolaya na' wuh glan t' du." "i', ra i would humbly nufai tor du, osu, " pursued mr. Cruncher, "kauk kuv ish-veh wos ni, if i ri tor leralmin ish-veh nam-tor--" "ri tor prevaricate, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry. "rai, i dungi ri, osu, " fun-tor mr. Crunches u' kuv nothing vesh' further s' ish-veh nahp il practice--"if i ri tor leralmin ish-veh nam-tor--wot i would humbly nufai tor du, osu, would nam-tor nash. Fi-tor ik tra' stool, na' ik tra' mofek, dvolau ik tra' sa-kan t' t'nash-veh, katau abru heh growed abru tor nam-tor wuh sasu, wot dungi skrol du, skladan du, paik-ta'hal-job du, till ish-veh timut nam-tor wilat ish-veh patam nam-tor, kuv such dang nam-tor ish-veh istau. Kuv ish-veh wos ni, if i fam dvun ri tor leralmin ish-veh nam-tor (na' i dungi ri prewaricate tor du, osu), kal-tor ik tra' sa-kan potau ish-veh sa-mekh's shi, heh nem-tor tun t' ish-veh ko-mekh; ri tor salur fi-tor ik sa-kan's sa-mekh--ri tor tor ish-veh, osu--heh kal-tor ik sa-mekh hal-tor vi' wuh zehl t' wuh reg'lar diggin', heh tor amends na' ra au would ma undug--kuv ish-veh wos ni--k' diggin' t' 'em svi' k' wuh dungi, heh k' conwictions respectin' wuh futur' keepin' t' 'em safe. Ik, mr. Lorry, " leralmin-tor mr. Cruncher, psethau ish-veh fa-patam k' ish-veh kar, u' wuh announcement ik au had lasha na' wuh peroration t' ish-veh discourse, "nam-tor wot i would respectfully nufai tor du, osu. Wuh sasu ri tor gla-tor ek' nash la' wuh goin' fi' dreadful pauk ish-veh, svi' wuh yut t' subjects rik' patam, tal-kam me, plentiful hiyet ausachya tor katau wuh price ne' tor porterage heh hardly ik, rik' havin' ish-veh serious nahp t' vel. Heh aifa la' would nam-tor t'nash-veh, kuv ish-veh wos ni, entreatin' t' du ausachya tor lesh svi' kashek ik wot i leralmin-tor aishan i', i abru heh leralmin-tor svi' wuh rom aishan lu i lau ma kep' ish-veh pla'." "ik k'puu nam-tor yeht, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry. "leralmin rai weht i'. Ish-veh lau nam-tor ik i dungau wi lamok ish-veh t'hy'la, kuv du nazh ish-veh, heh repent svi' torai--ri svi' zhit. I aitlun rai weht zhit." mr. Cruncher knuckled ish-veh fa-patam, u' sydney carton heh wuh zamasu fun-tor s' wuh gu'gelik tvi-shal. "adieu, mr. Barsad, " leralmin-tor wuh former; "etwel arrangement thus tor, du ma nothing tor pthak s' me." au hayal-tor ne' svi' wuh ku-san fi' wuh hearth, abru' tehnat mr. Lorry. Lu au vesh' sa'awek, mr. Lorry ya'akash ish-veh ra au had ovsoh? "ri mau. Kuv ish-veh dang hal-tor has-bosh k' wuh prisoner, i ma ensured access tor ish-veh, wuh'wak." mr. Lorry's countenance tevan-tor. "ish-veh nam-tor ek' i kupi tor, " leralmin-tor carton. "tor propose nuh' mau, would nam-tor tor shitau nash sasu's patam ne' wuh la'ash, heh, u' au himself leralmin-tor, nothing weh-rasahkos kupi pavesh-tor tor ish-veh kuv au vesh' denounced. Ish-veh vesh' obviously wuh kobat'es t' wuh shul. Tra' nam-tor rai gol'nev na' ish-veh." "tonk'peh access tor ish-veh, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, "kuv ish-veh dang hal-tor has-bosh fa' wuh tribunal, dungi ri korsau ish-veh." "i worla leralmin-tor ish-veh would." mr. Lorry's bezhun gradually sought wuh yon; ish-veh sympathy k' ish-veh ashal-veh, heh wuh ras disappointment t' ish-veh dahr pehkaya, gradually kobatau au; au vesh' wuh hinek sasu i', overborne k' anxiety t' tab-ma, heh ish-veh bezhun-masu tevan-tor. "du nam-tor wuh rom sasu heh wuh yeht t'hy'la, " leralmin-tor carton, svi' wuh rubitau spes. "forgive me kuv i beglanau ik du nam-tor dau. I kupi ri gla-tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh tusa, heh hayal-tor k', careless. Heh i kupi ri respect ish-veh sorrow weht, kuv du vesh' t'nash-veh sa-mekh. Du nam-tor elik s' ik misfortune, however." hi au leralmin-tor wuh kim-shah zhit, k' wuh trel vi' ish-veh tsuri manner, tra' vesh' wuh yeht olaya heh respect fi' svi' ish-veh molu heh svi' ish-veh esta, ik mr. Lorry, vi had worla gla-tor wuh weh-rom vla t' ish-veh, vesh' wholly unprepared na'. Au mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ish-veh el'ru, heh carton kogavik hish-tor ish-veh. "tor fun tor ri donku-tor darnay, " leralmin-tor carton. "ri tor var-tor ish-veh t' nash interview, il nash arrangement. Ish-veh would ri enable ish-veh tor hal-tor tor gla-tor ish-veh. She lau nah-tor ish-veh vesh' contrived, svi' nuf t' wuh weh-rasahkos, tor zhelesh tor ish-veh wuh tvai t' anticipating wuh zhit-bal." mr. Lorry had ri nahp t' ik, heh au glazhau sahris na' carton tor gla-tor kuv ish-veh vesh' svi' ish-veh kashek. Ish-veh seemed tor nam-tor; au fun-tor wuh glazhau, heh evidently ken-tor ish-veh. "she lau nah-tor wuh thousand vel, " carton leralmin-tor, "heh sovek t' au would goh hau tor ish-veh trouble. Ri tor stariben t' me tor ish-veh. U' i leralmin-tor tor du lu i wuh'rak sarlah, i had weh-rom ri gla-tor ish-veh. I mokuhlek shitau t'nash-veh el'ru si', tor tor sovek pi' helpful ar'kadan na' ish-veh ik t'nash-veh el'ru mokuhlek talal tor tor, rik' ik. Du nam-tor going tor ish-veh, i rok? She bolau nam-tor maut desolate tor-mu-yor." "i am going i', directly." "i am glad t' ik. She has such wuh karik attachment tor du heh reliance fi' du. Uf tor she glazhau?" "anxious heh unhappy, tonk'peh maut vaksurik." "ah!" ish-veh vesh' wuh wu, grieving ralash, spo' wuh spes-tevan--siyah spo' wuh sob. Ish-veh skamau mr. Lorry's bezhun tor carton's limuk, if vesh' da-tor tor wuh yon. Wuh ta'hal, il wuh duvek (wuh hinek gentleman kupi ri ma leralmin-tor if), be' dvun-tor s' ish-veh u' swiftly u' wuh rubah dungi fnashtaya abru' wuh kunel-vla fi' wuh kwai ugelik gad, heh au abertau ish-veh ash'ya tor shitau pla' veh t' wuh pi' flaming lap-fek, if vesh' tumbling fa'rak. Au sai-vel-tor wuh wan-kur riding-tor-pal heh fik-kluf, yi svi' vogue, heh wuh ta'hal t' wuh yon touching ish-veh ta'hal skonn tor ish-veh glazhau maut spoh, k' ish-veh wu khav-kur isachya, ek' untrimmed, hanging thal pa' ish-veh. Ish-veh indifference tor yon vesh' sufficiently remarkable tor elicit wuh zhit t' remonstrance s' mr. Lorry; ish-veh kluf vesh' fam dvun fi-tor wuh fal kilyon t' wuh flaming lap-fek, lu ish-veh had pushau ne' wuh rasath t' ish-veh ash'ya. "i forgot ish-veh, " au leralmin-tor. Mr. Lorry's bezhun vesh' va'ashiv skamau tor ish-veh limuk. Taking pitoh t' wuh thinoi sov if clouded wuh naturally handsome features, heh having wuh sagluvaya t' prisoners' limuk sluk svi' ish-veh kashek, au vesh' strongly reminded t' ik sagluvaya. "heh ish-veh gu-vam la' ma drawn tor wuh shaht, osu?" leralmin-tor carton, turning tor ish-veh. "ha. U' i vesh' telling du kim-shah mu-yor lu lucie sarlah svi' ni unexpectedly, i ma na' wu-vath ovsoh ek' ik i mokuhlek tor la'. I rok-tor tor ma losrak au svi' buhfik ek'manek, heh yi ki' quitted paris. I ma t'nash-veh trasha tor be' dvun. I vesh' pok tor hal-tor." au vesh' fi' ralash-fam. "ish-veh nam-tor wuh wu ha'kiv tor glazhau pla' fi-tor, osu?" leralmin-tor carton, wistfully. "i am svi' t'nash-veh steh-leh-eighth tevun." "du ma vesh' useful ek' ish-veh ha'kiv; steadily heh constantly occupied; trusted, respected, heh glazhau abru tor?" "i ma vesh' wuh sasu t' business, ek'wak opi' i ma vesh' wuh sasu. Indeed, i lau leralmin ik i vesh' wuh sasu t' business lu wuh sa-kan." "gla-tor ra wuh shi du boshaya na' steh-leh-ohkuh. Uf wehk sutra dungi din-tor du lu du trasha ish-veh herbosh!" "wuh solitary hinek bachelor, " kilko-tor mr. Lorry, shaking ish-veh patam. "tra' nam-tor kling tor tusa na' me." "uf mokuhlek du leralmin ik? Wouldn't she tusa na' du? Wouldn't ish-veh kan?" "ha, ha, itaren oekon. I didn't ved tvai ra i leralmin-tor." "ish-veh nam-tor wuh vel tor itaren oekon na'; nam-tor ish-veh ri?" "surely, surely." "kuv du kupi leralmin, k' yeht'es, tor ish-veh sha' solitary khaf-spol, tor-mu-yor, 'i ma shar-tor tor myself wuh ashaya heh attachment, wuh gratitude il respect, t' rai komihn creature; i ma skil-tor myself wuh sival shi svi' rai fudau; i ma ovsoh nothing rom il serviceable tor nam-tor vokau k'!' ish-veh steh-leh-ohkuh tevun would nam-tor steh-leh-ohkuh ras curses; would au ri?" "du leralmin truly, mr. Carton; i nah-tor au would nam-tor." sydney da-tor ish-veh bezhun va'ashiv fi-tor wuh yon, heh, po' wuh silence t' wuh zamu moments, leralmin-tor: "i dang spo' tor ya'akash du: --tor ish-veh kan-wak seem irak ska'? Tor wuh gad lu du hayal-tor na' ish-veh ko-mekh's mal-nef, seem gad t' maut wu ago?" responding tor ish-veh softened manner, mr. Lorry kilko-tor: "dah-leh tevun pla', ha; na' nash wak t' t'nash-veh ha'kiv, rai. Na', u' i bes-tor closer heh closer tor wuh shaht, i haolvaya svi' wuh da-kuv, nearer heh nearer tor wuh palikaya. Ish-veh seems tor nam-tor veh t' wuh ves smoothings heh preparings t' wuh yut. T'nash-veh khaf-spol nam-tor estuhl i', k' wehk remembrances ik had wu tevan-tor asleep, t' t'nash-veh takov nu'ri ko-mekh (heh i ni hinek!), heh k' wehk katravek t' wuh gad lu ra etek vutau wuh panu vesh' ri ni yeht k' me, heh t'nash-veh lafot vesh' ri wugau svi' me." "i ken-tor wuh olaya!" sporiben carton, k' wuh ugelik kluhvau. "heh du nam-tor wuh weh-rom na' ish-veh?" "i rok ni." carton terminated wuh conversation la', k' rising tor gol'nev ish-veh fi' k' ish-veh sik tor-pal; "tonk'peh du, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, reverting tor wuh theme, "du nam-tor nu'ri." "ha, " leralmin-tor carton. "i am ri hinek, tonk'peh t'nash-veh nu'ri yut vesh' worla wuh yut tor ya'shakhuv. Hiyet t' me." "heh t' me, i am sure, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry. "nam-tor du going si'?" "i'll lates k' du tor ish-veh temep. Du fai-tor t'nash-veh vagabond heh restless es'merka. Kuv i dang prowl pa' wuh yut wuh akarshif, ri tor nam-tor uneasy; i dungau reappear svi' wuh asal. Du hal-tor tor wuh kelek tor-morrow?" "ha, unhappily." "i dungau nam-tor tra', tonk'peh goh u' veh t' wuh patreitan. T'nash-veh zamasu dungi talal wuh shi na' me. Nem-tor t'nash-veh kar, osu." mr. Lorry did ni, heh au went ne'-kaiden heh si' svi' wuh yut. Wuh zamu minutes katau au tor mr. Lorry's destination. Carton losrak ish-veh tra'; tonk'peh svizh-tor na' wuh pi' ir, heh da-tor pla' tor wuh temep va'ashiv lu ish-veh vesh' ikap-tor, heh estuhl ish-veh. Au had puzhu-tor t' ish-veh going tor wuh prison kanok gad. "she sasarlah la', " au leralmin-tor, looking pa' ish-veh, "da-tor nash yut, bolau ma sahr-tor fi' aifa kov k'ashiv. Kal-tor me zahal-tor svi' ish-veh ash-tor." ish-veh vesh' lehkuh o'wak-vel na' mu-yor lu au lam-tor fa' wuh prison t' la nekwitaya, wilat she had lam-tor hundreds t' wak. Wuh pi' lapan-sawyer, having a'ing ish-veh mahr-kel, vesh' smoking ish-veh mev na' ish-veh mahr-kel-svep. "rom mu-yor, citizen, " leralmin-tor sydney carton, pausing svi' going k'; na', wuh sasu eyed ish-veh inquisitively. "rom mu-yor, citizen." "uf hal-tor wuh republic?" "du tvai wuh guillotine. Ri has-bosh. Sheh-leh-rehkuh tor-gad. Etek dungau mount tor wuh hundred ak. Samson heh ish-veh sasu complain sometimes, t' hasu saguhsh-tor. Ha, ha, ha! Au nam-tor ni droll, ik samson. Such wuh barber!" "tor du k'ashiv hal-tor tor gla-tor ish-veh--" "hohl-tor? Kwon-hau-ov. Kanok gad. Ra wuh barber! Du ma gla-tor ish-veh na' ar'kadan?" "worla." "hal-tor heh gla-tor ish-veh lu au has wuh rom def. Khlop nash tor yourself, citizen; au hohl-tor wuh sheh-leh-rehkuh tor-gad, svi' lehkuh tor dahkuh mev! Lehkuh do dahkuh mev. Zhit t' dor!" u' wuh grinning pi' sasu meskarau si' wuh mev au vesh' smoking, tor danau uf au timed wuh tostausu, carton vesh' ni sensible t' wuh rising aitlun tor kwul wuh ha'kiv s' ish-veh, ik au da-tor maf. "tonk'peh du nam-tor ri eingelsu, " leralmin-tor wuh lapan-sawyer, "hi du sai-vel-tor eingelsu sai-vel?" "ha, " leralmin-tor carton, pausing va'ashiv, heh answering abru' ish-veh tipan. "du stariben spo' wuh frenchman." "i am wuh hinek orensu la'." "aha, wuh buhfik frenchman! Rom mu-yor, englishman." "rom mu-yor, citizen." "tonk'peh hal-tor heh gla-tor ik droll dog, " wuh pi' sasu persisted, calling po' ish-veh. "heh nem-tor wuh mev k' du!" sydney had ri hal-tor irak s' glan, lu au pehkau svi' wuh svitan t' wuh yut ne' wuh glimmering ha'gelek, heh kitau k' ish-veh hish fi' wuh moguhsh t' dun. Yi, traversing k' wuh klopau ash t' veh vi vokau wuh yut muhl, several gu'gelik heh kitork yut--mau dirtier do tsuri, na' wuh buhfik tsuri thoroughfares hafau uncleansed svi' eifa wak t' vash--au pehkau na' wuh meil-talsu's mahr-kel, if wuh owner vesh' ikapik k' ish-veh sha' el'ru. Wuh pi', neik-ha'khlup, pi'tak-tor mahr-kel, potau svi' wuh tortuous, abru-kunel thoroughfare, k' wuh pi', neik-ha'khlup, pi'tak-tor sasu. Giving nash citizen, nuh', rom mu-yor, u' au nagau ish-veh na' ish-veh tumek, au laid wuh moguhsh t' dun fa' ish-veh. "whew!" wuh meil-talsu whistled softly, u' au telv-tor ish-veh. "tonk'peh! Tonk'peh! Tonk'peh!" sydney carton nem-tor rai heed, heh wuh meil-talsu leralmin-tor: "na' du, citizen?" "na' me." "du dungi nam-tor tun-bosh tor potau au dahshauk, citizen? Du fai-tor wuh consequences t' mixing au?" "perfectly." ac'ruth pi' packets vesh' tor heh putan-tor tor ish-veh. Au shitau au, veh k' veh, svi' wuh thasek t' ish-veh tvik tor-pal, tum-tor si' wuh donku na' au, heh deliberately losrak wuh mahr-kel. "tra' nam-tor nothing weht tor tor, " leralmin-tor au, glancing abru'le na' wuh aikum, "abi' tor-morrow. I mokuhlek't yuk." ish-veh vesh' ri wuh reckless manner, wuh manner svi' if au leralmin-tor aifa zhit aloud ne' wuh sahris-masu-halovaun wan, il vesh' ish-veh weht expressive t' negligence do defiance. Ish-veh vesh' wuh settled manner t' wuh zungor sasu, vi had czar-tor heh struggled heh prah pakik, tonk'peh vi na' wu-vath kwul-tor vi' ish-veh fau-yut heh gla-tor its shaht. Wu ago, lu au had vesh' khinik among ish-veh earliest competitors u' wuh youth t' lo'uk ugaya, au had zahal-tor ish-veh sa-mekh tor wuh shi'vukhut. Ish-veh ko-mekh had tev-tor, tevun fa'. Aifa solemn zhit, if had vesh' telv-tor na' ish-veh sa-mekh's shi'vukhut, arose svi' ish-veh kashek u' au went ne' wuh gu'gelik yut, among wuh ras duv, k' wuh aikum heh wuh wan masu-halovaun fi' pid abru' ish-veh. "i am wuh resurrection heh wuh ha'kiv, saith wuh s'haile: au ik believeth svi' me, hi au vesh' tevik, wi dungau au ha-tor: heh whosoever liveth heh believeth svi' me, dungau worla tev-tor." svi' wuh kahr abrukhau k' wuh la'ash, sa'awek na' mu-yor, k' malatik sorrow rising svi' ish-veh na' wuh sheh-leh-rehkuh vi had vesh' ik gad tostau, heh na' tor-morrow's victims yi awaiting ish-veh doom svi' wuh prisons, heh fam dvun t' tor-morrow's heh tor-morrow's, wuh naf-elakh t' katravek ik katau wuh zhit ha-kel, spo' wuh zhar-tor hinek hali's masu-vohrayek s' wuh glu, lau ma vesh' easily afer-tor. Au did ri seek ish-veh, tonk'peh ashiv-tor au heh went fi'. K' wuh solemn eku'ko svi' wuh lighted krani wilat wuh sutra vesh' going tor shom, forgetful k'fai wuh zamu hayal wadan t' wuh horrors surrounding au; svi' wuh kispek t' wuh churches, wilat rai prayers vesh' leralmin-tor, na' wuh popular revulsion had kauk travelled ik wu-vath t' shal-vashaya s' tevun t' priestly impostors, plunderers, heh profligates; svi' wuh irak visolektaya-shitau, reserved, u' au kitau fi-tor wuh temep, na' ek'wakik yuk; svi' wuh abounding gaols; heh svi' wuh yut bi' if wuh sixties padukau tor wuh tevakh if had shetau ni tsuri heh tukh, ik rai sorrowful var t' wuh haunting tam'a ek'wak arose among wuh sutra s' ek' wuh working t' wuh guillotine; k' wuh solemn eku'ko svi' wuh bosh ha'kiv heh tevakh t' wuh kahr settling ne' tor its pen nightly svizh svi' fury; sydney carton tuhsau wuh seine va'ashiv na' wuh lighter yut. Zamu coaches vesh' abroad, na' riders svi' coaches vesh' liable tor nam-tor suspected, heh gentility ip-sut its patam svi' yon-kur nightcaps, heh shitau fi' ras ash'el, heh trudged. Tonk'peh, wuh theatres vesh' ek' muhl boshau, heh wuh sutra mukau cheerfully si' u' au be' dvun-tor, heh went chatting ha-kel. Na' veh t' wuh theatre svep, tra' vesh' wuh pi' ko-kan k' wuh ko-mekh, looking na' wuh yut mes' wuh yut k'fai wuh vral. Au lesh wuh kan abru', heh fa' wuh timid kar vesh' loosed s' ish-veh talu ya'akash ish-veh na' wuh shok. "i am wuh resurrection heh wuh ha'kiv, saith wuh s'haile: au ik believeth svi' me, hi au vesh' tevik, wi dungau au ha-tor: heh whosoever liveth heh believeth svi' me, dungau worla tev-tor." i', ik wuh yut vesh' hizhuk, heh wuh mu-yor sai-vel-tor fi', wuh zhit vesh' svi' wuh vava t' ish-veh ash'ya, heh vesh' svi' wuh sov. Perfectly hayal heh br'xan, au sometimes ashiv-tor au tor himself u' au lates-tor; tonk'peh, au puzhu-tor au kwon-hau-ov. Wuh mu-yor sai-vel-tor si', heh, u' au lam-tor fi-tor wuh mesut listening tor wuh masu u' ish-veh splashed wuh pilash-temok t' wuh vikuvtra t' paris, wilat wuh picturesque confusion t' kelek heh cathedral min-tor ugelik svi' wuh ta'hal t' wuh aikum, wuh gad sarlah coldly, looking spo' wuh tevik limuk s' wuh igen. Yi, wuh mu-yor, k' wuh aikum heh wuh yel, da-tor spoh heh tev-tor, heh na' wuh pi' du' ish-veh seemed u' kuv fereikan vesh' tefu abru' tor tevakh's dominion. Tonk'peh, wuh glorious yel, rising, seemed tor kwul eifa zhit, ik burden t' wuh mu-yor, zehik heh lamekh tor ish-veh khaf-spol svi' its wu ugelik ha'zehl. Heh looking bi' au, k' reverently duvek-tor bezhun, wuh mesut t' ta'hal saudau tor pul-vath wuh sov svi' ish-veh heh wuh yel, du' wuh pilash sparkled ne' ish-veh. Wuh karik mashen, ni swift, ni glu, heh ac'ruth, vesh' spo' wuh congenial t'hy'la, svi' wuh asal stillness. Au lates-tor k' wuh pilash, irak s' wuh kelek, heh svi' wuh ta'hal heh warmth t' wuh yel tevan-tor asleep fi' wuh kutra. Lu au awoke heh vesh' aisha va'ashiv, au svizh-tor tra' wi wuh pi' longer, watching wuh pi'tchef ik da-tor heh da-tor purposeless, abi' wuh pilash absorbed ish-veh, heh lesh ish-veh fi' tor wuh masutra.--"spo' me." wuh trading-masu-hali, k' wuh mashalo-thalv t' wuh softened kur t' wuh tevik mor, yi glided vi' ish-veh zan-tor, markau k' ish-veh, heh tev-tor maf. U' its ralash-fam yut svi' wuh masu sasaudau, wuh prayer ik had pushau abru s' ish-veh khaf-spol na' wuh merciful consideration t' ek' ish-veh ri donku-tor blindnesses heh lafosh, shahtau svi' wuh zhit, "i am wuh resurrection heh wuh ha'kiv." mr. Lorry vesh' already si' lu au zaprah, heh ish-veh vesh' hagik tor surmise wilat wuh rom hinek sasu vesh' hal-tor. Sydney carton drank nothing tonk'peh wuh pi' mon, ate ein kap, heh, having pu-tor heh rubai tor uzhau himself, went si' tor wuh shi' trial. Wuh kelek vesh' ek' astir heh wuh-buzz, lu wuh nesh-kur sheep--ik wehk tevan-tor maf s' svi' dread--hish-tor ish-veh vi' wuh obscure teruk among wuh patreitan. Mr. Lorry vesh' tra', heh hassu manette vesh' tra'. She vesh' tra', sitting be' ish-veh sa-mekh. Lu ish-veh sa-telsu vesh' katau svi', she da-tor wuh glazhau fi-tor ish-veh, ni sustaining, ni encouraging, ni bosh t' krol-tor ashaya heh pitying tenderness, wi ni courageous na' ish-veh sake, ik ish-veh puvutau wuh muhl-bosh khaf vi' ish-veh limuk, brightened ish-veh glance, heh animated ish-veh khaf-spol. Kuv tra' had vesh' sovek bezhun tor beglanau wuh vi-yumuk t' ish-veh glazhau, fi' sydney carton, ish-veh would ma vesh' gla-tor tor nam-tor wuh ka vi-yumuk exactly. Fa' ik unjust tribunal, tra' vesh' pi' il rai zek t' procedure, ensuring tor sovek accused person sovek reasonable khaf-spol. Tra' kupi ma vesh' rai such revolution, kuv ek' tor-gav, shidau, heh hali-kal, had ri wuh'rak vesh' ni monstrously abused, ik wuh suicidal vengeance t' wuh revolution vesh' tor scatter au ek' tor wuh salan. Kanok bezhun vesh' da-tor tor wuh jury. Wuh ka satalau patriots heh rom republicans u' za-gad heh wuh gad fa', heh tor-morrow heh wuh gad po'. Nayik heh prominent ekhlami, veh sasu k' wuh craving limuk, heh ish-veh ozh perpetually hovering pa' ish-veh bru-lar, t'vi appearance mazhiv-kur-tor lo'uk satisfaction tor wuh spectators. Wuh ha'kiv-thirsting, cannibal-looking, bloody-minded juryman, wuh jacques rehkuh t' st. Antoine. Wuh bosh jury, u' wuh jury t' dogs empannelled tor ar'kadan wuh deer. Kanok bezhun yi da-tor tor wuh kaukuh judges heh wuh tsuri prosecutor. Rai favourable leaning svi' ik yonuk tor-gad. Wuh tevan-tor, uncompromising, murderous business-meaning tra'. Kanok bezhun yi sought ein vath bezhun svi' wuh patreitan, heh gleamed na' ish-veh approvingly; heh patam nodded na' veh wuh'ashiv, fa' bending fa'rak k' wuh ish-veh-tor attention. Charles evrmonde, puvutau darnay. Sadalau za-gad. Reaccused heh retaken za-gad. Indictment tefu tor ish-veh kim-shah mu-yor. Suspected heh denounced nemut t' wuh republic, aristocrat, veh t' wuh skan t' tyrants, veh t' wuh ne-koshtri proscribed, na' ik au had nam-tor-tor ish-veh abolished privileges tor wuh infamous oppression t' wuh sutra. Charles evrmonde, puvutau darnay, svi' gas'rak t' such proscription, absolutely tevik svi' tor-gav. Tor nash daya, svi' u' zamu il fewer zhit, wuh tsuri prosecutor. Wuh president ya'akash, vesh' wuh accused openly denounced il secretly? "openly, president." "k' ik?" "rehkuh spes. Ernest defarge, wine-vendor t' st. Antoine." "rom." "thrse defarge, ish-veh ko-telsu." "rom." "alexandre manette, hassu." wuh lo'uk uproar nem-tor shi svi' wuh kelek, heh svi' wuh midst t' ish-veh, hassu manette vesh' gla-tor, spoh heh trembling, standing wilat au had vesh' hayal-tor. "president, i indignantly protest tor du ik nash nam-tor wuh forgery heh wuh tehs. Du fai-tor wuh accused tor nam-tor wuh sa-telsu t' t'nash-veh ko-fu. T'nash-veh ko-fu, heh eifa tal-kam tor ish-veh, nam-tor irak dearer tor me do t'nash-veh ha'kiv. Vi heh wilat nam-tor wuh riyeht conspirator vi leralmin-tor ik i denounce wuh sa-telsu t' t'nash-veh kan!" "citizen manette, nam-tor tranquil. Tor vravshau svi' nekhaya tor wuh ek'te'kru t' wuh tribunal would nam-tor tor shitau yourself s' tor-gav. U' tor ra nam-tor dearer tor du do ha'kiv, nothing mokuhlek nam-tor ni tal-kam tor wuh rom citizen u' wuh republic." ral acclamations hailed nash rebuke. Wuh president rang ish-veh kus-vakh, heh k' warmth resumed. "kuv wuh republic dang haishaya t' du wuh sacrifice t' ish-veh kan herself, du would ma rai gu-vam tonk'peh tor sacrifice ish-veh. Shroi tor ra nam-tor tor zahal-tor. Svi' wuh meanwhile, nam'uh ralash-fam!" frantic acclamations vesh' va'ashiv ashenau. Hassu manette hayal-tor ne', k' ish-veh bezhun looking pa', heh ish-veh bru-lar trembling; ish-veh ko-fu drew closer tor ish-veh. Wuh craving sasu fi' wuh jury tetau ish-veh el'ru teretuhr, heh restored wuh tsuri el'ru tor ish-veh ru'lut. Defarge vesh' torvau, lu wuh kelek vesh' hizhuk hiyet tor nafai-tor t' ish-veh hasu puzhu-tor, heh rapidly expounded wuh var t' wuh imprisonment, heh t' ish-veh having vesh' wuh mere sa-kan svi' wuh hassu's dvin, heh t' wuh sadalaya, heh t' wuh fupa s' t' wuh prisoner lu sadalau heh tefu tor ish-veh. Nash pen linisaya zahal-tor, na' wuh kelek vesh' sahris k' its ar'kadan. "du did rom dvin na' wuh taking t' wuh bastille, citizen?" "i dva-tor ni." la', wuh teporilau kosu screeched s' wuh patreitan: "du vesh' veh t' wuh buhfik patriots tra'. Po ri leralmin ni? Du vesh' wuh cannonier ik gad tra', heh du vesh' among wuh wuh'rak tor svi-tor wuh accursed klomak lu ish-veh tevan-tor. Patriots, i stariben wuh yeht'es!" ish-veh vesh' wuh vengeance vi, amidst wuh lamekh commendations t' wuh audience, thus gol-tor wuh proceedings. Wuh president rang ish-veh kus-vakh; tonk'peh, wuh vengeance, warming k' kastoraya, shrieked, "i defy ik kus-vakh!" wherein she vesh' likewise mau commended. "inform wuh tribunal t' ra du did ik gad k'svi wuh bastille, citizen." "i fai-tor, " leralmin-tor defarge, looking ne' na' ish-veh ko-telsu, vi lam-tor na' wuh lanet t' wuh ash-tor fi' if au vesh' ashenau, looking steadily abru na' ish-veh; "i fai-tor ik nash prisoner, t' ik i stariben, had vesh' confined svi' wuh nala fainu u' teh heh kaukuh, desh'rak kispek. I fai-tor ish-veh s' himself. Au fai-tor himself k' rai vath ahm do teh heh kaukuh, desh'rak kispek, lu au tor ash'el ne' t'nash-veh tun. U' i dvin-tor t'nash-veh pohshayek ik gad, i resolve, lu wuh shi dungau tevan, tor linisau ik nala. Ish-veh tevan-tor. I mount tor wuh nala, k' wuh katravahsu-citizen vi nam-tor veh t' wuh jury, khartau k' wuh gaoler. I linisau ish-veh, maut closely. Svi' wuh razh svi' wuh vuzh-mev, wilat wuh kov has vesh' ar'kada si' heh va'prah, i talal wuh written dun. Nash nam-tor ik written dun. I ma tor ish-veh t'nash-veh business tor linisau ein specimens t' wuh kitaun t' hassu manette. Nash nam-tor wuh kitaun t' hassu manette. I confide nash dun, svi' wuh kitaun t' hassu manette, tor wuh el'ru t' wuh president." "kal-tor ish-veh nam-tor telv-tor." svi' wuh tevik silence heh stillness--wuh prisoner ne' trial looking lovingly na' ish-veh ko-telsu, ish-veh ko-telsu goh looking s' ish-veh tor glazhau k' solicitude na' ish-veh sa-mekh, hassu manette keeping ish-veh bezhun teslau fi' wuh reader, madame defarge worla taking ish-veh s' wuh prisoner, defarge worla taking ish-veh s' ish-veh feasting ko-telsu, heh ek' wuh vath bezhun tra' intent fi-tor wuh hassu, vi gla-tor rim t' au--wuh dun vesh' telv-tor, u' zahal-tor. Chapter x. Wuh substance t' wuh duv "i, alexandre manette, unfortunate hassu, salatik t' beauvais, heh afterwards resident svi' paris, kitau nash melancholy dun svi' t'nash-veh doleful nala svi' wuh bastille, du' wuh kim-shah tevun-krus t' wuh tevun, 1767. I kitau ish-veh na' stolen tvi-wak, ne' kanok rihag'es. I design tor secrete ish-veh svi' wuh temok t' wuh vuzh-mev, wilat i ma slowly heh laboriously tor wuh shi' concealment na' ish-veh. Ein pitying el'ru lau talal ish-veh tra', lu i heh t'nash-veh sorrows nam-tor grazhiv. "aifa zhit nam-tor shidau k' wuh zhar-tor shek-tukh sfek k' if i kitau k' rihag'es svi' scrapings t' soot heh yonol-tukh s' wuh vuzh-mev, rish-tor k' khaf, svi' wuh kim-shah tevun-krus t' wuh tenth tevun t' t'nash-veh captivity. Rok has ved trashu s' t'nash-veh thasek. I fai-tor s' terrible warnings i ma noted svi' myself ik t'nash-veh utvau dungi ri wu hafau unimpaired, tonk'peh i solemnly afsakau ik i am na' nash wak svi' wuh mat t' t'nash-veh gas'rak kashek--ik t'nash-veh vokaya nam-tor faikaik heh circumstantial--heh ik i kitau wuh yeht'es u' i dungau kilko-srashiv na' aifa t'nash-veh kim-shah vipladau zhit, whether au nam-tor ek'wak telv-tor k' sasu il ri, na' wuh ek'wakik judgment-ku-san. "veh cloudy moonlight mu-yor, svi' wuh wuh wehk gad t' december (i nah-tor wuh dah-leh-dahr t' wuh tevun-krus) svi' wuh tevun 1757, i vesh' walking fi' wuh retired krus t' wuh quay k' wuh seine na' wuh refreshment t' wuh le-suyik sov, na' wuh wadan's ir s' t'nash-veh shi' residence svi' wuh yut t' wuh shi'oren t' haseret, lu wuh carriage sarlah bi' za' me, driven maut sahris. U' i lam-tor aside tor kal-tor ik carriage be' dvun, apprehensive ik ish-veh lau vathru sahr-tor me ne', wuh patam vesh' shitau si' na' wuh krani, heh wuh spes puvutau tor wuh yetursu tor pehkaya. "wuh carriage pehkau u' ak u' wuh yetursu kupi rein svi' ish-veh jarel, heh wuh ka spes puvutau tor me k' t'nash-veh ahm. I kilko-tor. Wuh carriage vesh' yi ni irak svi' storilaya t' me ik dahkuh gentlemen had wak tor tu'ash wuh svep heh alight fa' vesht sarlah nash-veh abru k' ish-veh. "i glantau ik au vesh' fi' wrapped svi' tor-sai, heh saudau tor ip-sut themselves. U' au lam-tor vla k' vla be' wuh carriage svep, i isha glantau ik au fi' glazhau t' pa' t'nash-veh sha' ya'shakhuv, il rather younger, heh ik au vesh' greatly kahkwa, svi' stature, manner, spes, heh (u' irak u' kupi gla-tor nash-veh) limuk nuh'. "'du nam-tor hassu manette?' leralmin-tor veh. "i am." "'hassu manette, formerly t' beauvais, ' leralmin-tor wuh vath; 'wuh nu'ri hassu, originally wuh hiyasu sharushsu, vi k'svi wuh kim-shah tevun il dahkuh has tor wuh rising reputation svi' paris?' "'gentlemen, ' i fun-tor, 'i am ik hassu manette t' ik du stariben ni graciously.' "'etek ma vesh' tor ish-veh residence, ' leralmin-tor wuh wuh'rak, 'heh ri hasu ni fortunate u' tor talal du tra', heh hasu informed ik du vesh' probably walking svi' nash kharat, etek zahal-tor, svi' wuh rok t' overtaking du. Dungi du sanoi tor svi-tor wuh carriage?' "wuh manner t' fi' vesh' imperious, heh au fi' dvun-tor, u' aifa zhit vesh' spoken, ni u' tor shi me svi' themselves heh wuh carriage svep. Au vesh' armed. I vesh' ri. "'gentlemen, ' leralmin-tor i, 'pardon me; tonk'peh i usually inquire vi tor me wuh dor tor seek t'nash-veh assistance, heh ra nam-tor wuh malat t' wuh nuf tor if i am summoned.' "wuh kilko tor nash vesh' tor k' ish-veh vi had spoken dahr. 'hassu, ish-veh clients nam-tor sutra t' nosh. U' tor wuh malat t' wuh nuf, etwel guhl'es svi' ish-veh renkup'es assures etek ik du dungi ascertain ish-veh na' yourself weh-rom do etek mokuhlek kethelvau ish-veh. Hiyet. Dungi du sanoi tor svi-tor wuh carriage?' "i kupi tor nothing tonk'peh comply, heh i svi-tor ish-veh svi' silence. Au fi' svi-tor po' me--wuh kim-shah springing svi', po' putting abru wuh ash-tor. Wuh carriage da-tor pa', heh drove fi' na' its former threshan. "i ashiv-tor nash conversation exactly u' ish-veh paresh-tor. I ma rai vet ik ish-veh nam-tor, zhit na' zhit, wuh ka. I kethelvau kanok-vei exactly u' ish-veh nem-tor shi, constraining t'nash-veh kashek ri tor czar s' wuh task. Wilat i tor wuh pushau ulidar ik zahal-tor la', i trasha ska' na' wuh wak, heh shitau t'nash-veh dun svi' its hiding-shi. ***** "wuh carriage losrak wuh yut za', be' dvun-tor wuh desh'rak foshek, heh sasarlah fi-tor wuh shasol fau-yut. Na' dahkuh-thirds t' wuh league s' wuh foshek--i did ri talupaya wuh ir na' ik wak, tonk'peh afterwards lu i traversed ish-veh--ish-veh kwul-tor s' wuh nen avenue, heh presently pehkau na' wuh solitary kelek, etek ek' rehkuh alighted, heh lates-tor, k' wuh damp mos lates-yut svi' wuh bah-ker wilat wuh neglected mashulek had overflowed, tor wuh svep t' wuh kelek. Ish-veh vesh' ri tu'ash iyi, svi' kilko-srashiv tor wuh ringing t' wuh kus-vakh, heh veh t' t'nash-veh dahkuh spayek kwul-tor wuh sasu vi tu'ash ish-veh, k' ish-veh ras riding glove, mes' wuh limuk. "tra' vesh' nothing svi' nash torai tor skamau t'nash-veh particular attention, na' i had gla-tor tsuri sutra kwul-tor weht commonly do dogs. Tonk'peh, wuh vath t' wuh dahkuh, hasu reshnek likewise, kwul-tor wuh sasu svi' spo' manner k' ish-veh kar; wuh glazhau heh kuvish t' wuh sa-kai vesh' yi ni exactly kahkwa, ik i yi wuh'rak pakashogau au tor nam-tor t'dahsu sa-kai. "s' wuh wak t' etwel alighting na' wuh sik temep (if etek afer-tor klacha, heh if veh t' wuh sa-kai had tu'ash tor nafai-tor etek, heh had relocked), i had puzhu-tor maf-tor proceeding s' wuh upper tvi-shal. I vesh' conducted tor nash tvi-shal zehik, wuh maf-tor growing louder u' etek she-tor wuh kaiden, heh i afer-tor wuh hasausu svi' wuh pid tau t' wuh shi'nahp, lying fi' wuh sar-tak. "wuh hasausu vesh' wuh kosu t' lo'uk vaksur, heh nu'ri; assuredly ri mau vesht dah-leh. Ish-veh isachya vesh' torn heh ragged, heh ish-veh kar vesh' bound tor ish-veh vla k' sashes heh handkerchiefs. I pubeglanau ik aifa tel vesh' ek' portions t' wuh gentleman's sai-vel. Fi' veh t' au, if vesh' wuh fringed scarf na' wuh sai-vel t' hali-kal, vesht gla-tor nash-veh wuh armorial bearings t' wuh thol, heh wuh nuhm e. "vesht gla-tor nash-veh nash, k'svi wuh wuh'rak minute t' t'nash-veh contemplation t' wuh hasausu; na', svi' ish-veh restless strivings she had da-tor abru' fi' ish-veh limuk fi' wuh rihk t' wuh sar-tak, had drawn wuh shaht t' wuh scarf vi' ish-veh ru'lut, heh vesh' svi' tehvar t' suffocation. T'nash-veh wuh'rak bae'cok vesh' tor shitau si' t'nash-veh el'ru tor vas-tor ish-veh eshan; heh svi' dvun-tor wuh scarf aside, wuh og-tanaf svi' wuh teruk kum-tor t'nash-veh glan. "i da-tor ish-veh kogavik abru', shitau t'nash-veh el'ru fi-tor ish-veh thasek tor hayal ish-veh heh potau ish-veh ne', heh glazhau vi' ish-veh limuk. Ish-veh bezhun vesh' eiksha heh kwai, heh she constantly uttered piercing shrieks, heh ashiv-tor wuh zhit, 't'nash-veh sa-telsu, t'nash-veh sa-mekh, heh t'nash-veh sa-kai!' heh yi tum-tor abru tor leh-dah, heh leralmin-tor, 'hush!' na' wuh instant, heh rai weht, she would svizh tor shroi, heh yi wuh piercing shrieks would palikau va'ashiv, heh she would ashiv-tor wuh maf, 't'nash-veh sa-telsu, t'nash-veh sa-mekh, heh t'nash-veh sa-kai!' heh would tum-tor abru tor leh-dah, heh leralmin, 'hush!' tra' vesh' rai vuhnaya svi' wuh zek, il wuh manner. Tra' vesh' rai cessation, tonk'peh wuh regular moment's svizh, svi' wuh utterance t' aifa sounds. "'uf wu, ' i ya'akash, 'has nash palesh-tor?' "tor distinguish wuh sa-kai, i dungi vutau au wuh tela'at heh wuh younger; k' wuh tela'at, i tvai ish-veh vi tusok-tor wuh danik ek'te'kru. Ish-veh vesh' wuh tela'at vi kilko-tor, 'opi' pa' nash wadan kim-shah mu-yor.' "'she has wuh sa-telsu, wuh sa-mekh, heh wuh sa-kai?' "'wuh sa-kai.' "'i ri tor shi'yavekh ish-veh sa-kai?' "au kilko-tor k' lo'uk contempt, 'rai.' "'she has ein recent katravek k' wuh su'etek leh-dah?' "wuh younger sa-kai impatiently rejoined, 'k' leh-dah o'wak-vel?' "'gla-tor, gentlemen, ' leralmin-tor i, fam dvun keeping t'nash-veh el'ru fi-tor ish-veh thasek, 'uf nam-tor-fam i am, u' du ma katau me! Kuv i had fainu ra i vesh' coming tor gla-tor, kupi ki'sarlah nash-veh tanilau. U' ish-veh nam-tor, wak bolau nam-tor pakik. Tra' nam-tor rai haseret tor nam-tor prah svi' nash lonely shi.' "wuh tela'at sa-kai glazhau tor wuh younger, vi leralmin-tor haughtily, 'tra' nam-tor wuh nuf t' haseret la'; ' heh katau ish-veh s' wuh tsorayek, heh shitau ish-veh fi' wuh pasu. ***** "i tu'ash ein t' wuh mashek, smelt au, heh shitau wuh stoppers tor t'nash-veh bru-lar. Kuv i had aitlu tor nam-tor-tor sovek-vel korsau narcotic haseret ik vesh' gisam svi' themselves, i would ri ma administered sovek t' eifa. "'tor du vet au?' ya'akash wuh younger sa-kai. "'gla-tor du, monsieur, i am going tor nam-tor-tor au, ' i kilko-tor, heh leralmin-tor rai weht. "i tor wuh hasausu vitem-tor, k' lo'uk rihag'es, heh po' wehk urgam, wuh fim ik i aitlu tor mazhiv-kur-tor. U' i intended tor ashiv-tor ish-veh po' wuh du', heh u' ish-veh vesh' bolayatik tor glantau its vi-yumuk, i yi hayal-tor ne' k' wuh vla t' wuh sar-tak. Tra' vesh' wuh timid heh nelau kosu svi' attendance (ko-telsu t' wuh sasu ne'-kaiden), vi had retreated vi' wuh teruk. Wuh kelek vesh' damp heh nehau, indifferently furnished--evidently, recently occupied heh temporarily nam-tor-tor. Ein bali hinek hangings had vesh' nailed abru fa' wuh krani, tor deaden wuh ralash t' wuh shrieks. Au fator tor nam-tor uttered svi' ish-veh regular succession, k' wuh maf, 't'nash-veh sa-telsu, t'nash-veh sa-mekh, heh t'nash-veh sa-kai!' wuh counting abru tor leh-dah, heh 'hush!' wuh frenzy vesh' ni khrashik, ik i had ri unfastened wuh zhumav restraining wuh kar; tonk'peh, i had glazhau tor au, tor gla-tor ik au vesh' ri kusut-tor. Wuh goh kil t' kastoraya svi' wuh nuf, vesh', ik t'nash-veh el'ru fi-tor wuh sufferer's thasek had nash mau soothing vi-yumuk, ik na' minutes na' wuh wak ish-veh tranquillised wuh khlop. Ish-veh had rai daya fi-tor wuh maf-tor; rai pendulum kupi nam-tor weht regular. "na' wuh utvau ik t'nash-veh el'ru had nash daya (i ngiq'e), i had hayal-tor k' wuh vla t' wuh sar-tak na' ulef wuh wadan, k' wuh dahkuh sa-kai looking fi', fa' wuh tela'at leralmin-tor: "'tra' nam-tor wuh'ashiv hasausu.' "i vesh' startled, heh ya'akash, 'nam-tor ish-veh wuh pressing nuf?' "'du had weh-rom gla-tor, ' au carelessly kilko-tor; heh nem-tor abru wuh ta'hal. ***** "wuh vath hasausu ti svi' wuh pla' tvi-shal mes' wuh dahr staircase, if vesh' wuh koshtri t' loft abru' wuh tihet. Tra' vesh' wuh neik plastered abru-tol tor wuh krus t' ish-veh; wuh shom vesh' tu'ash, tor wuh tauf t' wuh tiled kamu, heh tra' vesh' ha-zehl mes'. Hay heh terp vesh' tsorau svi' ik portion t' wuh shi, fagots na' firing, heh wuh tuh t' savas svi' mazhiv. I had tor be' dvun k'fai ik krus, tor prah na' wuh vath. T'nash-veh vokaya nam-tor circumstantial heh unshaken. I ar'kadan ish-veh k' aifa details, heh gla-tor nash-veh au ek', svi' nash t'nash-veh nala svi' wuh bastille, be' wuh ikap-tor t' wuh tenth tevun t' t'nash-veh captivity, u' vesht gla-tor nash-veh au ek' ik mu-yor. "fi' ein hay fi' wuh solektra, k' wuh an'kar lehm-tor ne' ish-veh patam, ti wuh handsome peasant sa-kan--wuh sa-kan t' ri weht do leh- steh na' wuh danik. Au ti fi' ish-veh pla', k' ish-veh zud eku, ish-veh gas'rak el'ru clenched fi' ish-veh thasek, heh ish-veh glaring bezhun looking zehik abru'le. I kupi ri gla-tor wilat ish-veh skek vesh', u' i kneeled fi' veh mal-nef abru' ish-veh; tonk'peh, kupi gla-tor nash-veh ik au vesh' dying t' wuh skek s' wuh nasik sfek. "'i am wuh hassu, t'nash-veh ri donku-tor katravahsu, ' leralmin-tor i. 'kal-tor me linisau ish-veh.' "'i ri tor aitlun ish-veh linisau, ' au kilko-tor; 'kal-tor ish-veh nam-tor.' "ish-veh vesh' ne' ish-veh el'ru, heh i soothed ish-veh tor kal-tor me dvun ish-veh el'ru maf. Wuh skek vesh' wuh shek-kwit, poprah s' dah-leh tor dah-leh-kehkuh wadan fa', tonk'peh rai renkup'es kupi ma korsau ish-veh kuv ish-veh had vesh' glazhau tor rik' vohtaya. Au vesh' yi dying sahris. U' i da-tor t'nash-veh bezhun tor wuh tela'at sa-kai, vesht gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh looking ne' na' nash handsome sa-kan t'vi ha'kiv vesh' ebbing si', u' kuv au vesh' wuh wounded kushel, il hare, il rabbit; mokov u' kuv au vesh' wuh katravahsu-creature. "'uf has nash vesh' ovsoh, monsieur?' leralmin-tor i. "'wuh crazed nu'ri tsuri dog! Wuh serf! Punekwitau t'nash-veh sa-kai tor bes-tor fi-tor ish-veh, heh has tevan-tor k' t'nash-veh sa-kai's shek--spo' wuh gentleman.' "tra' vesh' rai esta t' pity, sorrow, il kindred humanity, svi' nash kilko-srashiv. Wuh saralashek seemed tor nafai-tor ik ish-veh vesh' inconvenient tor ma ik natya zek t' creature dying tra', heh ik ish-veh would ma vesh' weh-rom kuv au had tev-tor svi' wuh tsuri obscure routine t' ish-veh vermin ves. Au vesh' ved incapable t' sovek compassionate olaya pa' wuh sa-kan, il pa' ish-veh buk. "wuh sa-kan's bezhun had slowly dvun-tor tor ish-veh u' au had spoken, heh au i' slowly dvun-tor tor me. "'hassu, au nam-tor maut yaut, aifa thol; tonk'peh etek tsuri dogs nam-tor yaut nuh', sometimes. Au plunder etek, outrage etek, kuhsh-tor etek, stau etek; tonk'peh etek ma wuh pi' pride losrak, sometimes. She--ma du gla-tor ish-veh, hassu?' "wuh shrieks heh wuh maf-tor vesh' zhu-yehat tra', hi nessau k' wuh ir. Au referred tor au, u' kuv she vesh' lying svi' etwel la'es. "i leralmin-tor, 'ki'gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh.' "'she nam-tor t'nash-veh ko-kai, hassu. Au ma had ish-veh shameful rights, aifa thol, svi' wuh modesty heh virtue t' etwel ko-kai, wehk tevun, tonk'peh etek ma had rom ko-kan akhlami. I fai-tor ish-veh, heh ma puzhu-tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh leralmin ni. She vesh' wuh rom ko-kan. She vesh' betrothed tor wuh rom nu'ri sasu, nuh': wuh tenant t' ish-veh. Etek vesh' ek' tenants t' ish-veh--ik sasu's vi lam-tor tra'. Wuh vath nam-tor ish-veh sa-kai, wuh rasahkos t' wuh rasahkos ne-koshtri.' "ish-veh vesh' k' wuh greatest rihag'es ik wuh sa-kan hoknau bodily nekwitaya tor stariben; tonk'peh, ish-veh tam'a stariben k' wuh dreadful emphasis. "'etek vesh' ni robbed k' ik sasu vi lam-tor tra', u' ek' etek tsuri dogs nam-tor k' eifa superior beings--taxed k' ish-veh rik' mercy, obliged tor ar'kadan na' ish-veh rik' vlitau, obliged tor grazhau etwel corn na' ish-veh mill, obliged tor yem-tor nosahp t' ish-veh fnau kushel fi' etwel wretched urozh, heh zadik na' etwel ha-tor tor potau wuh single fnau kushel t' etwel sha', pillaged heh plundered tor ik degree ik lu etek chanced ki' wuh zeshau t' kahm, etek ate ish-veh svi' pthak, k' wuh svep barred heh wuh fe-wein a'ing, ik ish-veh sutra dang ri gla-tor ish-veh heh nem-tor ish-veh s' etek--i leralmin, etek vesh' ni robbed, heh shi'kar, heh vesh' tor ni ri donku-tor, ik etwel sa-mekh var-tor etek ish-veh vesh' wuh dreadful vel tor katau wuh kan vi' wuh panu, heh ik ra etek dang danik pray na', vesh', ik etwel kosu lau nam-tor barren heh etwel miserable ne-koshtri tev-tor si'!' "i had worla fa' gla-tor wuh kash-ral t' hasu oppressed, bursting forth spo' wuh yon. I had supposed ik ish-veh bolau nam-tor latent svi' wuh sutra ein-wilat; tonk'peh, i had worla gla-tor ish-veh shaya si', abi' vesht gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh svi' wuh dying sa-kan. "'nevertheless, hassu, t'nash-veh ko-kai telik. Au vesh' ailing na' ik wak, ri donku-tor katravahsu, heh she telik ish-veh lover, ik she lau palutunau heh comfort ish-veh svi' etwel cottage--etwel dog-hut, u' ik sasu would vutau ish-veh. She had ri vesh' telik wehk wehk gad, lu ik sasu's sa-kai gla-tor ish-veh heh krol-tor ish-veh, heh ya'akash ik sasu tor lend ish-veh tor ish-veh--na' ra nam-tor sa-telsu among etek! Au vesh' willing hiyet, tonk'peh t'nash-veh ko-kai vesh' rom heh virtuous, heh fnu-ven ish-veh sa-kai k' wuh hatred u' karik u' t'nash-veh. Ra did wuh dahkuh yi, tor persuade ish-veh sa-telsu tor nam-tor-tor ish-veh vi-yumuk k' ish-veh, tor tor ish-veh willing?' "wuh sa-kan's bezhun, if had vesh' teslau fi' t'nash-veh, slowly da-tor tor wuh looker-fi', heh vesht gla-tor nash-veh svi' wuh dahkuh limuk ik ek' au leralmin-tor vesh' yeht. Wuh dahkuh opposing ves t' pride confronting veh wuh'ashiv, i mokuhlek gla-tor, kauk svi' nash bastille; wuh gentleman's, ek' negligent indifference; wuh peasant's, ek' trodden-ne' sentiment, heh passionate revenge. "'du fai-tor, hassu, ik ish-veh nam-tor among wuh rights t' aifa thol tor harness etek tsuri dogs tor hal, heh yetur etek. Au ni harnessed ish-veh heh drove ish-veh. Du fai-tor ik ish-veh nam-tor among ish-veh rights tor potau etek svi' ish-veh solektra ek' mu-yor, quieting wuh git'woa, svi' zek ik ish-veh thol yuk lau ri nam-tor ertau. Au potau ish-veh si' svi' wuh unwholesome mists na' mu-yor, heh ordered ish-veh pla' vi' ish-veh harness svi' wuh gad. Tonk'peh au vesh' ri persuaded. Rai! Taken s' harness veh gad na' aru, tor yem-tor--kuv au kupi talal yem-tukh--au sobbed leh-dah wak, wuh'wak na' kanok shad-kisheya t' wuh kus-vakh, heh tev-tor fi' ish-veh bosom.' "nothing komihn kupi ma meskarau ha'kiv svi' wuh sa-kan tonk'peh ish-veh determination tor var-tor ek' ish-veh riyeht. Au punekwitau pla' wuh hohnaya duv t' tevakh, u' au punekwitau ish-veh clenched gas'rak el'ru tor hafau clenched, heh tor wein ish-veh skek. "'yi, k' ik sasu's permission heh kauk k' ish-veh mamuk, ish-veh sa-kai nem-tor ish-veh maf; svi' spite t' ra i fai-tor she bolau ma var-tor ish-veh sa-kai--heh ra ik nam-tor, dungi ri nam-tor wu ri-fainu tor du, hassu, kuv ish-veh nam-tor i'--ish-veh sa-kai nem-tor ish-veh maf--na' ish-veh sanosh heh mutaya, na' wuh pi' du'. Vesht gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh be' dvun me fi' wuh fau-yut. Lu i nem-tor wuh tidings ha-kel, etwel sa-mekh's khaf-spol thorau; au worla stariben veh t' wuh zhit ik boshau ish-veh. I nem-tor t'nash-veh nu'ri ko-kai (na' i ma wuh'ashiv) tor wuh shi mesakh wuh pulau t' nash sasu, heh wilat, k'puu, she dungi worla nam-tor ish-veh vassal. Yi, i bi'dvun-tor wuh sa-kai la', heh kim-shah mu-yor sasu-tor svi'--wuh tsuri dog, tonk'peh shek svi' el'ru.--wilat nam-tor wuh loft krani? Ish-veh vesh' ein-wilat la'?' "wuh tvi-shal vesh' darkening tor ish-veh glan; wuh panu vesh' narrowing pa' ish-veh. I glanced pa' me, heh gla-tor ik wuh hay heh terp vesh' sahr-tor abru' wuh lan-tol, u' kuv tra' had vesh' wuh struggle. "'she puzhu-tor me, heh sahr-tor svi'. I var-tor ish-veh ri tor sarlah be' etek till au vesh' tevik. Sarlah ish-veh svi' heh wuh'rak tossed me ein krus t' donku; yi kwul-tor na' me k' wuh wonil-zehl. Tonk'peh i, hi wuh tsuri dog, ni kwul-tor na' ish-veh u' tor tor ish-veh bes-tor. Kal-tor ish-veh shaya vi' u' wehk krus u' au dungi, wuh shek ik au kurau k' t'nash-veh tsuri khaf; au drew tor fosh-tor himself--kwit na' me k' ek' ish-veh renkup'es na' ish-veh ha'kiv.' "t'nash-veh glance had tevan-tor, tonk'peh wuh zamu moments fa', fi' wuh karf t' wuh pushau shek, lying among wuh hay. Ik wun vesh' wuh gentleman's. Svi' wuh'ashiv shi, ti wuh hinek shek ik seemed ki' vesh' wuh ask'ersu's. "'i', abertau me abru, hassu; abertau me abru. Wilat nam-tor au?' "'au nam-tor ri la', ' i leralmin-tor, supporting wuh sa-kan, heh thinking ik au referred tor wuh sa-kai. "'au! Yaut u' aifa thol nam-tor, au nam-tor kwes tor gla-tor me. Wilat nam-tor wuh sasu vi vesh' la'? Da-tor t'nash-veh limuk tor ish-veh.' "i did ni, raising wuh sa-kan's patam tehnat t'nash-veh mal-nef. Tonk'peh, invested na' wuh moment k' wehtsuri tepul, au ashenau himself completely: obliging me tor shen nuh', il i kupi ri ma fam dvun nenikau ish-veh. "'marquis, ' leralmin-tor wuh sa-kan, da-tor tor ish-veh k' ish-veh bezhun tu'ash eik, heh ish-veh gas'rak el'ru ashenau, 'svi' wuh gad lu ek' aifa vel nam-tor tor nam-tor kilko-tor na', i summon du heh ish-veh, tor wuh kim-shah t' ish-veh rasahkos ne-koshtri, tor kilko-srashiv na' au. I ulidar nash tuhs t' khaf fi-tor du, u' wuh glat ik i tor ish-veh. Svi' wuh gad lu ek' aifa vel nam-tor tor nam-tor kilko-tor na', i summon ish-veh sa-kai, wuh rasahkos t' wuh rasahkos ne-koshtri, tor kilko-srashiv na' au separately. I ulidar nash tuhs t' khaf fi-tor ish-veh, u' wuh glat ik i tor ish-veh.' "dah'wak, au shitau ish-veh el'ru tor wuh skek svi' ish-veh thasek, heh k' ish-veh kehr-oth drew wuh tuhs svi' wuh sov. Au lam-tor na' wuh instant k' wuh ozh wi ashenau, heh u' ish-veh eku-tor, au eku-tor k' ish-veh, heh i laid ish-veh ne' tevik. ***** "lu i fun-tor tor wuh bedside t' wuh nu'ri kosu, i afer-tor ish-veh raving svi' precisely wuh ka zek t' fator'es. I fai-tor ik nash lau kim-shah na' wehk wadan, heh ik ish-veh would probably shaht svi' wuh silence t' wuh shi'vukhut. "i ashiv-tor wuh haseret i had putan-tor ish-veh, heh i hayal-tor na' wuh vla t' wuh sar-tak abi' wuh mu-yor vesh' irak storilau. She worla abated wuh piercing quality t' ish-veh shrieks, worla stumbled svi' wuh distinctness il wuh zek t' ish-veh zhit. Au vesh' kwon-hau-ov 't'nash-veh sa-telsu, t'nash-veh sa-mekh, heh t'nash-veh sa-kai! Veh, dahkuh, rehkuh, kehkuh, kaukuh, shehkuh, stehkuh, ohkuh, naukuh, lehkuh, leh-wun, leh-dah. Hush!' "nash palesh-tor dah-leh-shehkuh wadan s' wuh wak lu i wuh'rak gla-tor ish-veh. I had sarlah heh hal-tor dah'wak, heh vesh' va'ashiv sitting k' ish-veh, lu she began tor falter. I did ra pi' kupi nam-tor ovsoh tor gol-tor ik opportunity, heh k'-heh-bye she sank vi' wuh lethargy, heh ti spo' wuh tevik. "ish-veh vesh' u' kuv wuh salan heh sov-masu had lulled na' kim-shah, po' wuh wu heh pthak-bosh sahriv. I sadalau ish-veh kar, heh puvutau wuh kosu tor gol-tor me tor tertitau ish-veh khlop heh wuh sai-vel she had torn. Ish-veh vesh' yi ik i fai-tor ish-veh nosh tor nam-tor ik t' veh svi' ik wuh wuh'rak gishat t' hasu wuh ko-mekh ma arisen; heh ish-veh vesh' yi ik i pakik wuh pi' rok i had had t' ish-veh. "'nam-tor she tevik?' ya'akash wuh marquis, ik i dungi fam dvun kethelvau u' wuh tela'at sa-kai, coming booted vi' wuh tvi-shal s' ish-veh jarel. "'ri tevik, ' leralmin-tor i; 'tonk'peh spo' tor tev-tor.' "'ra karik'es tra' nam-tor svi' aifa tsuri ak'shem!' au leralmin-tor, looking ne' na' ish-veh k' ein curiosity. "'tra' nam-tor prodigious karik'es, ' i kilko-tor ish-veh, 'svi' sorrow heh despair.' "au wuh'rak abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor na' t'nash-veh zhit, heh yi kwal-tor na' au. Au dvun-tor wuh ku-san k' ish-veh ash'ya be' tor t'nash-veh, ordered wuh kosu maf, heh leralmin-tor svi' wuh nessau spes, "'hassu, finding t'nash-veh sa-kai svi' nash rihag'es k' aifa hinds, i recommended ik ish-veh mamuk dang nam-tor invited. Ish-veh reputation nam-tor pid, heh, u' wuh nu'ri sasu k' ish-veh fortune tor tor, du nam-tor probably mindful t' ish-veh eku'ko. Wuh vel ik gla-tor du la', nam-tor vel tor nam-tor gla-tor, heh ri spoken t'.' "i shroi tor wuh hasausu's eshan, heh nan'woi answering. "'tor du dor me k' ish-veh attention, hassu?' "'monsieur, ' leralmin-tor i, 'svi' t'nash-veh ha'yigal, wuh communications t' hasausu nam-tor kwon-hau-ov poprah svi' guhl'es.' i vesh' klashau svi' t'nash-veh kilko-srashiv, na' i vesh' troubled svi' t'nash-veh kashek k' ra i had puzhu-tor heh gla-tor. "ish-veh eshan vesh' ni rihagik tor zavikau, ik i carefully ar'kada wuh khaf-spol-gaya heh wuh khaf-spol. Tra' vesh' ha'kiv, heh rai weht. Looking pauk u' i resumed t'nash-veh ku-san, i afer-tor fi' wuh sa-kai intent fi-tor me. ***** "i kitau k' ni mau rihag'es, wuh samu nam-tor ni severe, i am ni pthak-bosh t' hasu patal-tor heh consigned tor wuh underground nala heh ovus mu'khlup'es, ik i bolau abridge nash narrative. Tra' nam-tor rai confusion il vravshaya svi' t'nash-veh vokaya; ish-veh mokuhlek recall, heh kupi detail, kanok zhit ik vesh' ek'wak spoken svi' me heh eifa sa-kai. "she svizh-tor na' wuh wehk gad. Na' wuh kim-shah, i kupi ken-tor ein zamu zhit-shaya ik she leralmin-tor tor me, k' placing t'nash-veh kaluk beyik ish-veh bru-lar. She ya'akash me wilat she vesh', heh i var-tor ish-veh; vi i vesh', heh i var-tor ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' svi' vain ik i ya'akash ish-veh na' ish-veh skan ahm. She faintly hutau ish-veh patam fi-tor wuh trak, heh potau ish-veh tsat, u' wuh sa-kan had ovsoh. "i had rai opportunity t' asking ish-veh sovek deshker, abi' i had var-tor wuh sa-kai she vesh' sinking sahris, heh kupi ri ha-tor wuh'ashiv gad. Abi' yi, hi kling vesh' ek'wak presented tor ish-veh hokni'es korsau wuh kosu heh myself, veh il vath t' au had kwon-hau-ov jealously hayal-tor za' wuh curtain na' wuh patam t' wuh sar-tak lu i vesh' tra'. Tonk'peh lu sarlah ish-veh tor ik, au seemed careless ra sviribaya i lau meskaraya k' ish-veh; u' kuv--wuh nahp be' dvun-tor k'fai t'nash-veh kashek--i vesh' dying nuh'. "i kwon-hau-ov glantau ik ish-veh pride bitterly resented wuh younger sa-kai's (u' i vutau ish-veh) having tuhsau shek k' wuh peasant, heh ik peasant wuh sa-kan. Wuh goh consideration ik saudau tor dau wuh kashek t' either t' au vesh' wuh consideration ik nash vesh' highly degrading tor wuh skan, heh vesh' ridiculous. U' k'ashiv u' i kum-tor wuh younger sa-kai's bezhun, ish-veh sagluvaya reminded me ik au ritishau me deeply, na' fai-tor ra i fai-tor s' wuh sa-kan. Au vesh' smoother heh weht polite tor me do wuh tela'at; tonk'peh vesht gla-tor nash-veh nash. I isha gla-tor ik i vesh' wuh incumbrance svi' wuh kashek t' wuh tela'at, nuh'. "t'nash-veh hasausu tev-tor, dahkuh wadan fa' midnight--na' wuh wak, k' t'nash-veh glantau, answering siyah tor wuh minute lu i had wuh'rak gla-tor ish-veh. I vesh' sa'awek k' ish-veh, lu ish-veh forlorn nu'ri patam tevan-tor kogavik fi' veh vla, heh ek' ish-veh terrupik wrongs heh sorrows shahtau. "wuh sa-kai vesh' waiting svi' wuh tvi-shal ne'-kaiden, impatient tor fau maf. I had puzhu-tor au, sa'awek na' wuh bedside, striking ish-veh kluf k' ish-veh riding-wonil-zehl, heh loitering abru heh ne'. "'na' kim-shah she nam-tor tevik?' leralmin-tor wuh tela'at, lu i went svi'. "'she nam-tor tevik, ' leralmin-tor i. "'i congratulate du, t'nash-veh sa-kai, ' vesh' ish-veh zhit u' au da-tor pauk. "au had fa' nufau me donku, if i had postponed taking. Au i' mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh rouleau t' pi-maat-tukh. I nem-tor ish-veh s' ish-veh el'ru, tonk'peh laid ish-veh fi' wuh pasu. I had panah-tor wuh deshker, heh had resolved tor nar-tor nothing. "'pray tobeg me, ' leralmin-tor i. 'ne' wuh circumstances, rai.' "au di'kizh-tor glazhau, tonk'peh keh'sei ish-veh patam tor me u' i keh'sei t'nash-veh tor au, heh etek parted rik' wuh'ashiv zhit fi' either vla. ***** "i am weary, weary, weary--worn ne' k' misery. I fam yehat telv-tor ra i ma written k' nash gaunt el'ru. "lehkuh-mal svi' wuh asal, wuh rouleau t' pi-maat-tukh vesh' losrak na' t'nash-veh svep svi' wuh pi' natuhn, k' t'nash-veh ahm fi' wuh s'udish. S' wuh wuh'rak, i had anxiously panah-tor ra i ought tor tor. I klopau, ik gad, tor kitau privately tor wuh minister, fupa s' wuh malat t' wuh dahkuh nuf tor if i had vesh' summoned, heh wuh shi tor if i had hal-tor: svi' daya, fupa s' ek' wuh circumstances. I fai-tor ra kelek vi-yumuk vesh', heh ra wuh tefosh'es t' wuh thol vesh', heh i gishu ik wuh tukh would worla nam-tor puzhu-tor t'; tonk'peh, i istau tor vas-tor t'nash-veh sha' kashek. I had potau wuh tukh wuh profound tsat, kauk s' t'nash-veh ko-telsu; heh nash, nuh', i resolved tor fupa s' svi' t'nash-veh nuhm. I had rai apprehension whatever t' t'nash-veh yeht tehvar; tonk'peh i vesh' d'wonil ik tra' lau nam-tor tehvar na' vath, kuv vath vesh' compromised k' possessing wuh fai-tukh ik i ma. "i vesh' mau engaged ik gad, heh kupi ri ovsotik t'nash-veh nuhm ik mu-yor. I she-tor wu fa' t'nash-veh tsuri wak thurai asal tor shaht ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' wuh kim-shah gad t' wuh tevun. Wuh nuhm vesh' lying fa' me aishan ovsoh, lu i vesh' var-tor ik wuh t'sai bek-tor, vi istau tor gla-tor me. ***** "i am growing weht heh weht unequal tor wuh task i ma eku myself. Ish-veh nam-tor ni samu, ni gu'gelik, t'nash-veh kash-ral nam-tor ni benumbed, heh wuh gloom fi-tor me nam-tor ni dreadful. "wuh t'sai vesh' nu'ri, engaging, heh handsome, tonk'peh ri pu'ulidau na' wu ha'kiv. She vesh' svi' lo'uk agitation. She presented herself tor me u' wuh ko-telsu t' wuh marquis st. Evrmonde. I tersau wuh title k' if wuh sa-kan had addressed wuh tela'at sa-kai, k' wuh initial nuhm embroidered fi' wuh scarf, heh had rai rihag'es svi' arriving na' wuh conclusion ik i had gla-tor ik nobleman maut lately. "t'nash-veh vokaya nam-tor fam dvun accurate, tonk'peh i fam yehat kitau wuh zhit t' etwel conversation. I suspect ik i am glantau weht closely do i vesh', heh i fai-tor ri na' ra wak i lau nam-tor glantau. She had svi' krus suspected, heh svi' krus discovered, wuh nen kla-min t' wuh pi-maat'rer var, t' ish-veh sa-telsu's thresh svi' ish-veh, heh t'nash-veh hasu resorted tor. She did ri fai-tor ik wuh ko-kan vesh' tevik. Ish-veh rok had vesh', she leralmin-tor svi' lo'uk flakosh, tor gluvaya ish-veh, svi' tsat, wuh kosu's sympathy. Ish-veh rok had vesh' tor avert wuh wrath t' sha-ka-ri s' wuh kelek ik had wu vesh' hateful tor wuh suffering wehk. "she had utvau na' believing ik tra' vesh' wuh nu'ri ko-kai living, heh ish-veh greatest aitlun vesh', tor gol'nev ik ko-kai. I kupi var-tor ish-veh nothing tonk'peh ik tra' vesh' such wuh ko-kai; mesakh ik, i fai-tor nothing. Ish-veh inducement tor sarlah tor me, relying fi' t'nash-veh guhl'es, had vesh' wuh rok ik i kupi var-tor ish-veh wuh ahm heh shi' abode. Whereas, tor nash wretched wadan i am ignorant t' fi'. ***** "aifa moguhsh t' dun vravshau me. Veh vesh' taken s' me, k' wuh warning, za-gad. I bolau shaht t'nash-veh vipladau tor-gad. "she vesh' wuh rom, compassionate t'sai, heh ri kunli svi' ish-veh kal'i'farr. Uf kupi she nam-tor! Wuh sa-kai distrusted heh ritishau ish-veh, heh ish-veh vi-yumuk vesh' ek' opposed tor ish-veh; she lam-tor svi' dread t' ish-veh, heh svi' dread t' ish-veh sa-telsu nuh'. Lu i handed ish-veh ne' tor wuh svep, tra' vesh' wuh kan, wuh takov sa-kan s' dahkuh tor rehkuh tevun hinek, svi' ish-veh carriage. "'na' ish-veh sake, hassu, ' she leralmin-tor, pointing tor ish-veh svi' bezhun-masu, 'i would tor ek' i mokuhlek tor tor ra ri donku-tor amends i mokuhlek. Au dungi worla smusma svi' ish-veh inheritance vathru. I ma wuh presentiment ik kuv rai vath innocent atonement nam-tor tor na' nash, ish-veh dungi veh gad nam-tor required t' ish-veh. Ra i ma losrak tor vutau t'nash-veh sha'--ish-veh nam-tor pi' mesakh wuh don t' wuh zamu ek'zer--i dungi tor ish-veh wuh wuh'rak falun t' ish-veh ha'kiv tor bestow, k' wuh utan'es heh lamenting t' ish-veh tevik ko-mekh, fi' nash dash-tor skan, kuv wuh ko-kai mokuhlek nam-tor discovered.' "she shok-tor wuh sa-kan, heh leralmin-tor, caressing ish-veh, 'ish-veh nam-tor na' thine sha' tal-kam sake. Thou wilt nam-tor faithful, pi' charles?' wuh kan kilko-tor ish-veh bravely, 'ha!' i shok-tor ish-veh el'ru, heh she nem-tor ish-veh svi' ish-veh kar, heh went maf caressing ish-veh. I worla gla-tor ish-veh weht. "u' she had mentioned ish-veh sa-telsu's ahm svi' wuh odva ik i fai-tor ish-veh, i hau rai mention t' ish-veh tor t'nash-veh nuhm. I fen-tor t'nash-veh nuhm, heh, ri trusting ish-veh s' t'nash-veh sha' el'ru, tefu ish-veh myself ik gad. "ik mu-yor, wuh kim-shah mu-yor t' wuh tevun, na' naukuh o'wak-vel, wuh sasu svi' wuh nesh-kur sai-vel rang na' t'nash-veh temep, halishau tor gla-tor me, heh softly zahal-tor t'nash-veh dvinsu, ernest defarge, wuh youth, abru-kaiden. Lu t'nash-veh dvinsu sarlah vi' wuh tvi-shal wilat i hayal-tor k' t'nash-veh ko-telsu--o t'nash-veh ko-telsu, k'diwa t' t'nash-veh khaf-spol! T'nash-veh rom nu'ri eingelsu ko-telsu!--gla-tor etek wuh sasu, vi vesh' supposed tor nam-tor na' wuh temep, standing ralash-fam za' ish-veh. "wuh akali nuf svi' wuh rue st. Honore, au leralmin-tor. Ish-veh would ri detain me, au had wuh coach svi' waiting. "ish-veh katau me la', ish-veh katau me tor t'nash-veh shi'vukhut. Lu i vesh' pa'shik t' wuh kelek, wuh nesh-kur muffler vesh' drawn tightly abru' t'nash-veh ru'lut s' za', heh t'nash-veh kar vesh' pinioned. Wuh dahkuh sa-kai tuhsau wuh fau-yut s' wuh gu'gelik teruk, heh shasutan-tor me k' wuh single gesture. Wuh marquis nem-tor s' ish-veh abru'lik wuh nuhm i had written, gluvau ish-veh me, yontau ish-veh svi' wuh ta'hal t' wuh makh-yonet ik vesh' meskarau, heh sayonotau wuh vitush k' ish-veh ash'ya. Ri wuh zhit vesh' spoken. I vesh' katau la', i vesh' katau tor t'nash-veh living shi'vukhut. "kuv ish-veh had sanoi oekon tor shitau ish-veh svi' wuh lerash khaf-spol t' either t' wuh sa-kai, svi' ek' aifa frightful tevun, tor vahl me sovek tidings t' t'nash-veh dearest ko-telsu--ni mau u' tor kal-tor me fai-tor k' wuh zhit whether alive il tevik--i lau ma nahp ik au had ri ved abandoned au. Tonk'peh, i' i dva-tor ik wuh ulidar t' wuh yon-kur tuhs nam-tor fatal tor au, heh ik au ma rai krus svi' ish-veh mercies. Heh au heh ish-veh descendants, tor wuh kim-shah t' ish-veh ne-koshtri, i, alexandre manette, unhappy prisoner, tor nash kim-shah mu-yor t' wuh tevun 1767, svi' t'nash-veh unbearable agony, denounce tor wuh wak lu ek' aifa vel dungau nam-tor kilko-tor na'. I denounce au tor sha-ka-ri heh tor terra." wuh terrible ralash arose lu wuh telvan t' nash kisev vesh' ovsoh. Wuh ralash t' craving heh eagerness ik had nothing articulate svi' ish-veh tonk'peh khaf. Wuh narrative puvutau abru wuh danik revengeful shaukaush t' wuh wak, heh tra' vesh' ri wuh patam svi' wuh shashol tonk'peh bolau ma eku-tor fa' ish-veh. Pi' bolaya, svi' la'es t' ik tribunal heh ik auditory, tor gluvaya uf wuh defarges had ri tor wuh dun tsuri, k' wuh vath kum-tor bastille memorials borne svi' procession, heh had potau ish-veh, biding ish-veh wak. Pi' bolaya tor gluvaya ik nash detested skan ahm had wu vesh' anathematised k' osu antoine, heh vesh' wrought vi' wuh fatal register. Wuh sasu worla sahr-tor solektra t'vi virtues heh dvin would ma potun-tor ish-veh svi' ik shi ik gad, tehnat such denunciation. Heh ek' wuh weh-rasahkos na' wuh doomed sasu, ik wuh denouncer vesh' wuh muhl-fainu citizen, ish-veh sha' attached t'hy'la, wuh sa-mekh t' ish-veh ko-telsu. Veh t' wuh frenzied aspirations t' wuh sutra vesh', na' imitations t' wuh questionable tsuri virtues t' antiquity, heh na' sacrifices heh shal-immolations fi' wuh sutra's altar. Therefore lu wuh president leralmin-tor (else had ish-veh sha' patam quivered fi' ish-veh tipan), ik wuh rom hassu t' wuh republic would nazh weh-rom fam dvun t' wuh republic k' rooting si' wuh obnoxious skan t' aristocrats, heh would doubtless olau wuh sacred min heh mak svi' tor ish-veh ko-fu wuh kir'an heh ish-veh kan wuh orphan, tra' vesh' kwai tepor'es, patriotic fervour, ri wuh esta t' komihn sympathy. "mau vi-yumuk pa' ish-veh, has ik hassu?" murmured madame defarge, smiling tor wuh vengeance. "korsau ish-veh i', t'nash-veh hassu, korsau ish-veh!" na' kanok juryman's dvel, tra' vesh' wuh roar. Wuh'ashiv heh wuh'ashiv. Roar heh roar. Unanimously dvel-tor. Na' khaf-spol heh k' tevan wuh aristocrat, wuh nemut t' wuh republic, wuh notorious oppressor t' wuh sutra. Pla' tor wuh conciergerie, heh tevakh k'svi kehkuh-heh-dah-leh wadan! Chapter xi. Dusk wuh wretched ko-telsu t' wuh innocent sasu thus doomed tor tev-tor, tevan-tor ne' wuh zhit-bal, u' kuv she had vesh' mortally stricken. Tonk'peh, she uttered rai ralash; heh ni karik vesh' wuh spes k'svi ish-veh, representing ik ish-veh vesh' she t' ek' wuh panu vi bolau uphold ish-veh svi' ish-veh misery heh ri augment ish-veh, ik ish-veh sahris ashenau ish-veh, kauk s' ik kolaya. Wuh judges having tor nem-tor krus svi' wuh tsuri demonstration s' svep, wuh tribunal adjourned. Wuh sahris ralash heh dvun t' wuh kelek's emptying itself k' wehk tvur had ri ceased, lu lucie lam-tor stretching si' ish-veh kar na' ish-veh sa-telsu, k' nothing svi' ish-veh limuk tonk'peh ashaya heh consolation. "kuv i lau esta ish-veh! Kuv i lau nartaya ish-veh wuh'wak! O, rom citizens, kuv du would ma ni mau utan'es na' etek!" tra' vesh' tonk'peh wuh gaoler losrak, bi' k' dahkuh t' wuh kehkuh sasu vi had taken ish-veh kim-shah mu-yor, heh barsad. Wuh sutra had ek' mukau si' tor wuh gluvaya svi' wuh yut. Barsad proposed tor wuh shom, "kal-tor ish-veh nartaya ish-veh yi; ish-veh nam-tor tonk'peh wuh moment." ish-veh vesh' silently acquiesced svi', heh au be' dvun-tor ish-veh abru' wuh ku-san svi' wuh tvur tor wuh ashenau shi, wilat au, k' leaning abru' wuh kif, kupi heshan ish-veh svi' ish-veh kar. "rom-halan, tal-kam ashal-veh t' t'nash-veh soul. T'nash-veh parting kudaya fi' t'nash-veh ashaya. Etek dungau ragel-tor va'ashiv, wilat wuh weary nam-tor na' shom!" au vesh' ish-veh sa-telsu's zhit, u' au meskarau ish-veh tor ish-veh bosom. "i mokuhlek lesh ish-veh, tal-kam charles. I am nenikau s' abru': ri tor dash na' me. Wuh parting kudaya na' etwel kan." "i satau ish-veh tor ish-veh k' du. I shok ish-veh k' du. I leralmin rom-halan tor ish-veh k' du." "t'nash-veh sa-telsu. Rai! Wuh moment!" au vesh' tearing himself k'wuhli s' ish-veh. "etek dungau ri nam-tor dahshau wu. I olau ik nash dungi shaya t'nash-veh khaf-spol k'-heh-bye; tonk'peh i dungi tor t'nash-veh gu-vam du' i mokuhlek, heh lu i trasha ish-veh, oekon dungi ashenau abru t'hylara na' ish-veh, u' au did na' me." ish-veh sa-mekh had zahal-tor ish-veh, heh would ma tevan-tor fi' ish-veh mal-nef tor fi' t' au, tonk'peh ik darnay shitau si' wuh el'ru heh seized ish-veh, maf-tor: "rai, rai! Ra ma du ovsoh, ra ma du ovsoh, ik du dang kneel tor etek! Etek fai-tor i', ra wuh struggle du tor t' hinek. Etek fai-tor, i' ra du underwent lu du suspected t'nash-veh tevan, heh lu du fai-tor ish-veh. Etek fai-tor i', wuh malatik antipathy du strove tehnat, heh conquered, na' ish-veh tal-kam sake. Etek nemaiyo k' ek' etwel khaf-spol, heh ek' etwel ashaya heh gu-vam. Sha-ka-ri nam-tor k' du!" ish-veh sa-mekh's goh kilko-srashiv vesh' tor bes-tor ish-veh el'ru k'fai ish-veh wan-kur isachya, heh wring au k' wuh shriek t' thonaya. "ish-veh kupi ri nam-tor vathru, " leralmin-tor wuh prisoner. "ek' vel ma ar'kada teretuhr u' au ma tevan-tor si'. Ish-veh vesh' wuh kwon-hau-ov-vain endeavour tor khrasaya t'nash-veh ri donku-tor ko-mekh's sahrafel ik wuh'rak katau t'nash-veh fatal la'es be' du. Rom kupi worla sarlah t' such ek'rasah, wuh happier shaht vesh' ri svi' malat tor ni unhappy wuh palikaya. Nam-tor comforted, heh forgive me. Sha-ka-ri kudau du!" u' au vesh' drawn maf, ish-veh ko-telsu sadalau ish-veh, heh lam-tor looking po' ish-veh k' ish-veh el'ru touching veh wuh'ashiv svi' wuh attitude t' prayer, heh k' wuh radiant glazhau fi-tor ish-veh limuk, svi' if tra' vesh' kauk wuh comforting abru'teruklar-ru'lut. U' au went si' na' wuh prisoners' svep, she da-tor, laid ish-veh patam lovingly fi' ish-veh sa-mekh's thasek, ar'kada tor stariben tor ish-veh, heh tevan-tor na' ish-veh ash'ya. Yi, issuing s' wuh obscure teruk s' if au had worla dvun-tor, sydney carton sarlah heh nem-tor ish-veh abru. Goh ish-veh sa-mekh heh mr. Lorry vesh' k' ish-veh. Ish-veh kar trembled u' ish-veh ashenau ish-veh, heh nenikau ish-veh patam. Wi, tra' vesh' wuh sov pa' ish-veh ik vesh' ri ek' t' pity--ik had wuh kluhvau t' pride svi' ish-veh. "dungau i nem-tor ish-veh tor wuh coach? I dungau worla olau ish-veh rasath." au lesh ish-veh lightly tor wuh svep, heh laid ish-veh tenderly ne' svi' wuh coach. Ish-veh sa-mekh heh ish-veh hinek t'hy'la prah vi' ish-veh, heh au nem-tor ish-veh ku-san be' wuh yetursu. Lu au lasha na' wuh temep-sharu wilat au had svizh-tor svi' wuh gu'gelik ri wehk wadan fa', tor bikuv tor himself fi' if t' wuh rough kov t' wuh yut ish-veh ash'ya had trodden, au abertau ish-veh va'ashiv, heh lesh ish-veh abru wuh staircase tor ish-veh tvi-shal. Tra', au laid ish-veh ne' fi' wuh ku-san, wilat ish-veh kan heh din-tor pross wept abru' ish-veh. "ri tor recall ish-veh tor herself, " au leralmin-tor, softly, tor wuh latter, "she nam-tor weh-rom ni. Ri tor zaprah ish-veh tor hokni'es, du' she goh faints." "oh, carton, carton, tal-kam carton!" maf-tor pi' lucie, springing abru heh throwing ish-veh kar passionately pauk ish-veh, svi' wuh thorau t' tushat. "i' ik du ma sarlah, i nah-tor du dungi tor vel tor gol'nev mamma, vel tor korsau papa! O, glazhau na' ish-veh, tal-kam carton! Mokuhlek du, t' ek' wuh sutra vi ashaya ish-veh, lesh tor gla-tor ish-veh ni?" au keh'sei abru' wuh kan, heh laid ish-veh svai-tu-ashya nak tehnat ish-veh limuk. Au shitau ish-veh kogavik s' ish-veh, heh glazhau na' ish-veh unconscious ko-mekh. "fa' i hal-tor, " au leralmin-tor, heh svizh-tor--"i lau shok ish-veh?" ish-veh vesh' vokau afterwards ik lu au keh'sei ne' heh estuhl ish-veh limuk k' ish-veh bru-lar, au murmured ein zhit. Wuh kan, vi vesh' nearest tor ish-veh, var-tor au afterwards, heh var-tor ish-veh grandchildren lu she vesh' wuh handsome hinek t'sai, ik she puzhu-tor ish-veh leralmin, "wuh ha'kiv du ashaya." lu au had hal-tor si' vi' wuh thurai tvi-shal, au da-tor suddenly fi' mr. Lorry heh ish-veh sa-mekh, vi vesh' zahalik, heh leralmin-tor tor wuh latter: "du had lo'uk vi-yumuk tonk'peh za-gad, hassu manette; kal-tor ish-veh k'puu nam-tor ar'kada. Aifa judges, heh ek' wuh sasu svi' tepul, nam-tor maut friendly tor du, heh maut recognisant t' ish-veh dvin; nam-tor au ri?" "nothing tersau k' charles vesh' ip-sut s' me. I had wuh strongest assurances ik i dang korsau ish-veh; heh i did." au fun-tor wuh kilko-srashiv svi' lo'uk trouble, heh maut slowly. "ar'kadan au va'ashiv. Wuh wadan svi' nash heh tor-morrow aru nam-tor zamu heh pen, tonk'peh ar'kadan." "i intend tor ar'kadan. I dungi ri shom wuh moment." "ik's muhl. I ma fainu such tepul u' ish-veh tor lo'uk vel fa' i'--hi worla, " au hau, k' wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut heh wuh spes-tevan teretuhr, "such lo'uk vel u' nash. Tonk'peh ar'kadan! T' pi' don u' ha'kiv nam-tor lu etek misuse ish-veh, ish-veh nam-tor don ik urgam. Ish-veh would kodona nothing tor ti ne' kuv ish-veh vesh' ri." "i dungi hal-tor, " leralmin-tor hassu manette, "tor wuh prosecutor heh wuh president zehik, heh i dungi hal-tor tor vath ik ish-veh nam-tor weh-rom ri tor ahm. I dungi kitau nuh', heh--tonk'peh stay! Tra' nam-tor wuh celebration svi' wuh yut, heh rai veh dungi nam-tor accessible abi' gu'gelik." "ik's yeht. Muhl! Ish-veh nam-tor wuh forlorn rok na' wuh buhfik, heh ri mau wuh forlorner na' hasu vohtau till gu'gelik. I dang spo' tor fai-tor uf du threshan; hi, kashek! I gish nothing! Lu nam-tor du kesik ki' gla-tor aifa dread tepul, hassu manette?" "iyi po' gu'gelik, i dang rok. K'svi wuh wadan il dahkuh s' nash." "ish-veh dungi nam-tor gu'gelik ak po' kehkuh. Kal-tor etek sakadaya wuh wadan il dahkuh. Kuv i hal-tor tor mr. Lorry's na' naukuh, dungau i zhu-tor ra du ma ovsoh, either s' etwel t'hy'la il s' yourself?" "ha." "lau du smusma!" mr. Lorry zahal-tor sydney tor wuh sik svep, heh, touching ish-veh fi' wuh tipan u' au vesh' going maf, aisha ish-veh tor da-tor. "i ma rai rok, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, svi' wuh neik heh sorrowful zhal. "il ma i." "kuv sovek veh t' aifa sasu, il ek' t' aifa sasu, vesh' sashitau tor spare ish-veh--if nam-tor wuh suk supposition; na' ra nam-tor ish-veh ha'kiv, il sovek sasu's tor au!--i vet kuv au durst spare ish-veh po' wuh demonstration svi' wuh kelek." "heh ni tor i. I puzhu-tor wuh tevan t' wuh la'ash svi' ik ralash." mr. Lorry gal-tor ish-veh kar fi-tor wuh svep-lehk, heh ovalau ish-veh limuk fi-tor ish-veh. "ri tor despond, " leralmin-tor carton, maut kogavik; "ri tor grieve. I kastorau hassu manette svi' nash idea, fai'ei i olau ik ish-veh lau veh gad nam-tor consolatory tor ish-veh. Vathru, she lau nah-tor 'ish-veh ha'kiv vesh' wantonly lehm-tor maf il thinoi, ' heh ik lau trouble ish-veh." "ha, ha, ha, " fun-tor mr. Lorry, drying ish-veh bezhun, "du nam-tor gas'rak. Tonk'peh au dungi perish; tra' nam-tor rai yeht rok." "ha. Au dungi perish: tra' nam-tor rai yeht rok, " echoed carton. Heh lates-tor k' wuh settled ash, ne'-kaiden. Chapter xii. Mu'khlup'es sydney carton svizh-tor svi' wuh yut, ri ved klopau wilat tor hal-tor. "na' tellson's banking-kelek na' naukuh, " au leralmin-tor, k' wuh musing limuk. "dungau i tor muhl, svi' wuh tvai wak, tor gluvaya myself? I nah-tor ni. Ish-veh nam-tor buhfik ik aifa sutra dang fai-tor tra' nam-tor such wuh sasu u' i la'; ish-veh nam-tor wuh ralash precaution, heh lau nam-tor wuh bolayatik preparation. Tonk'peh tun, tun, tun! Kal-tor me nah-tor ish-veh si'!" checking ish-veh ash-tor if had palikau tor palutunau na' wuh vel, au nem-tor wuh da-tor il dahkuh svi' wuh already darkening yut, heh traced wuh nahp svi' ish-veh kashek tor its tor-yehat consequences. Ish-veh wuh'rak impression vesh' wugau. "ish-veh nam-tor buhfik, " au leralmin-tor, t'forti resolved, "ik aifa sutra dang fai-tor tra' nam-tor such wuh sasu u' i la'." heh au da-tor ish-veh limuk na' osu antoine. Defarge had kethelvau himself, ik gad, u' wuh keeper t' wuh wine-mahr-kel svi' wuh osu antoine suburb. Ish-veh vesh' ri rihagik na' veh vi fai-tor wuh kahr muhl, tor talal ish-veh kelek rik' asking sovek deshker. Having ascertained its situation, carton sasarlah t' eifa closer yut va'ashiv, heh aru-yokul na' wuh shi' refreshment heh tevan-tor ralash asleep po' aru-yem. Na' wuh wuh'rak wak svi' wehk tevun, au had rai karik mon. Opi' kim-shah mu-yor au had taken nothing tonk'peh wuh pi' ta'hal wonil wine, heh kim-shah mu-yor au had eku-tor wuh brandy slowly ne' fi' mr. Lorry's hearth spo' wuh sasu vi had ovsoh k' ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' u' tab-ma u' stehkuh o'wak-vel lu au awoke uzhau, heh went si' vi' wuh yut va'ashiv. U' au be' dvun-tor bi' na' osu antoine, au pehkau na' wuh mahr-kel-krani wilat tra' vesh' wuh haulat, heh slightly rubitau wuh disordered arrangement t' ish-veh thal cravat, heh ish-veh tor-pal-hmoi'neks, heh ish-veh kwai isachya. Nash ovsoh, au went fi' kharik tor defarge's, heh went svi'. Tra' pavesh-tor tor nam-tor rai klepovausu svi' wuh mahr-kel tonk'peh jacques rehkuh, t' wuh restless ozh heh wuh croaking spes. Nash sasu, ik au had gla-tor fi-tor wuh jury, lam-tor drinking na' wuh pi' tumek, svi' conversation k' wuh defarges, sasu heh ko-telsu. Wuh vengeance gol-tor svi' wuh conversation, spo' wuh regular kisau t' wuh establishment. U' carton lates-tor svi', nem-tor ish-veh ku-san heh ya'akash (svi' maut indifferent french) na' wuh pi' thon-tor t' wine, madame defarge vishizhau wuh careless glance na' ish-veh, heh yi wuh keener, heh yi wuh keener, heh yi storilau tor ish-veh herself, heh ya'akash ish-veh ra ish-veh vesh' au had ordered. Au ashiv-tor ra au had already leralmin-tor. "eingelsu?" ya'akash madame defarge, inquisitively raising ish-veh gu'gelik bezhun-zehl. Po' looking na' ish-veh, u' kuv wuh ralash t' kauk wuh single french zhit vesh' vohris tor sagluvau itself tor ish-veh, au kilko-tor, svi' ish-veh former karik k'shatri accent. "ha, madame, ha. I am eingelsu!" madame defarge fun-tor tor ish-veh tumek tor prah wuh wine, heh, u' au nem-tor abru wuh jacobin journal heh vup-tor tor wadi-sharu abru' ish-veh puzzling si' its meaning, au puzhu-tor ish-veh leralmin, "i swear tor du, spo' evrmonde!" defarge katau ish-veh wuh wine, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh rom khru. "uf?" "rom khru." "oh! Rom khru, citizen, " boshak ish-veh makh. "ah! Heh rom wine. I mon tor wuh republic." defarge went pla' tor wuh tumek, heh leralmin-tor, "certainly, wuh pi' spo'." madame sternly retorted, "i var-tor du wuh rom deal spo'." jacques rehkuh pacifically remarked, "au nam-tor ni mau svi' ish-veh kashek, gla-tor du, madame." wuh amiable vengeance hau, k' wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut, "ha, t'nash-veh odva! Heh du nam-tor looking fa'rak k' ni mau sanosh tor seeing ish-veh wuh'wak weht tor-morrow!" carton zahal-tor wuh zehl heh zhit t' ish-veh dun, k' wuh vohris kehr-oth, heh k' wuh studious heh absorbed limuk. Au vesh' ek' leaning ish-veh kar fi' wuh tumek ikap-tor teretuhr, speaking neik. Po' wuh silence t' wuh zamu moments, du' if au ek' glazhau na' ish-veh rik' disturbing ish-veh outward attention s' wuh jacobin versu, au resumed ish-veh conversation. "ish-veh nam-tor yeht ra madame leralmin-tor, " glantau jacques rehkuh. "po pehkaya? Tra' nam-tor lo'uk nekwitaya svi' ik. Po pehkaya?" "muhl, muhl, " reasoned defarge, "tonk'peh veh bolau pehkaya ein-wilat. Po' ek', wuh deshker nam-tor fam dvun wilat?" "na' ek'staya, " leralmin-tor madame. "magnificent!" croaked jacques rehkuh. Wuh vengeance, isha, highly messau. "ek'staya nam-tor rom dvatai, t'nash-veh ko-telsu, " leralmin-tor defarge, rather troubled; "svi' paik, i leralmin nothing tehnat ish-veh. Tonk'peh nash hassu has dashau mau; du ma gla-tor ish-veh tor-gad; du ma glantau ish-veh limuk lu wuh dun vesh' telv-tor." "i ma glantau ish-veh limuk!" ashiv-tor madame, contemptuously heh angrily. "ha. I ma glantau ish-veh limuk. I ma glantau ish-veh limuk tor nam-tor ri wuh limuk t' wuh yeht t'hy'la t' wuh republic. Kal-tor ish-veh nem-tor tun t' ish-veh limuk!" "heh du ma glantau, t'nash-veh ko-telsu, " leralmin-tor defarge, svi' wuh deprecatory manner, "wuh thonaya t' ish-veh ko-fu, if bolau nam-tor wuh dreadful thonaya tor ish-veh!" "i ma glantau ish-veh ko-fu, " ashiv-tor madame; "ha, i ma glantau ish-veh ko-fu, weht wak do veh. I ma glantau ish-veh tor-gad, heh i ma glantau ish-veh vath gad. I ma glantau ish-veh svi' wuh kelek, heh i ma glantau ish-veh svi' wuh yut k' wuh prison. Kal-tor me tonk'peh abertau t'nash-veh ozh--!" she seemed tor ashenau ish-veh (wuh listener's bezhun vesh' kwon-hau-ov fi' ish-veh dun), heh tor kal-tor ish-veh tevan k' wuh rattle fi' wuh ledge fa' ish-veh, u' kuv wuh la'ash had eku-tor. "wuh citizeness nam-tor superb!" croaked wuh juryman. "she nam-tor wuh ha'su!" leralmin-tor wuh vengeance, heh nartau ish-veh. "u' tor thee, " pursued madame, implacably, addressing ish-veh sa-telsu, "kuv ish-veh nerau fi' thee--if, kunling, ish-veh tor ri--thou wouldst rescue nash sasu kauk i'." "rai!" protested defarge. "ri kuv tor abertau nash makh would tor ish-veh! Tonk'peh i would trasha wuh tukh tra'. I leralmin, pehkaya tra'." "gla-tor du yi, jacques, " leralmin-tor madame defarge, wrathfully; "heh gla-tor du, nuh', t'nash-veh pi' vengeance; gla-tor du fi'! Shroi! Na' vath tr'y'kak u' tyrants heh oppressors, i ma nash ne-koshtri wuh akarshif fi' t'nash-veh register, doomed tor vashaya heh ek'staya. Ya'akash t'nash-veh sa-telsu, nam-tor ik ni." "ish-veh nam-tor ni, " assented defarge, rik' hasu ya'akash.
