"svi' wuh palikaya t' wuh lo'uk gad, lu wuh bastille tevan-tor, au tal-tor nash dun t' tor-gad, heh au katau ish-veh ha-kel, heh svi' wuh svitan t' wuh mu-yor lu nash shi nam-tor pa'shik heh ikap-tor, etek telv-tor ish-veh, la' fi' nash gla-tor, k' wuh ta'hal t' nash ha'gelek. Ya'akash ish-veh, nam-tor ik ni." "ish-veh nam-tor ni, " assented defarge. "ik mu-yor, i var-tor ish-veh, lu wuh dun nam-tor telv-tor k'fai, heh wuh ha'gelek nam-tor yontau si', heh wuh gad nam-tor gleaming svi' abru' eifa fe-wein heh svi' eifa shek-tukh mofek, ik i ma i' wuh tsat tor sviribau. Ya'akash ish-veh, nam-tor ik ni." "ish-veh nam-tor ni, " assented defarge va'ashiv. "i sviribau tor ish-veh ik tsat. I smite nash bosom k' aifa dahkuh el'ru u' i smite ish-veh i', heh i var-tor ish-veh, 'defarge, i vesh' katau abru among wuh aluk-kumsu t' wuh masutra-gef, heh ik peasant skan ni dash-tor k' wuh dahkuh evrmonde sa-kai, u' ik bastille dun kethelvau, nam-tor t'nash-veh skan. Defarge, ik ko-kai t' wuh mortally wounded sa-kan fi-tor wuh solektra vesh' t'nash-veh ko-kai, ik sa-telsu vesh' t'nash-veh ko-kai's sa-telsu, ik unborn kan vesh' ish-veh kan, ik sa-kai vesh' t'nash-veh sa-kai, ik sa-mekh vesh' t'nash-veh sa-mekh, eifa tevik nam-tor t'nash-veh tevik, heh ik summons tor kilko-srashiv na' eifa vel tev-tor tor me!' ya'akash ish-veh, nam-tor ik ni." "ish-veh nam-tor ni, " assented defarge wuh'wak weht. "yi var-tor salan heh yon wilat tor pehkaya, " fun-tor madame; "tonk'peh ri tor var-tor me." fi' ish-veh hearers derived wuh horrible tizh'es s' wuh tevalik malat t' ish-veh wrath--wuh listener kupi olau uf wan-kur she vesh', rik' seeing ish-veh--heh fi' highly commended ish-veh. Defarge, wuh kobat minority, interposed wuh zamu zhit na' wuh vokaya t' wuh compassionate ko-telsu t' wuh marquis; tonk'peh goh elicited s' ish-veh sha' ko-telsu wuh repetition t' ish-veh kim-shah kilko. "var-tor wuh salan heh wuh yon wilat tor pehkaya; ri me!" klepovausu svi-tor, heh wuh travek vesh' pushau abru. Wuh eingelsu klepovausu vlitau na' ra au had had, perplexedly tum-tor ish-veh rubah, heh ya'akash, u' wuh ri-fainusu, tor nam-tor khartau na' wuh national palace. Madame defarge nem-tor ish-veh tor wuh svep, heh shitau ish-veh kar fi' ish-veh, svi' pointing si' wuh fau-yut. Wuh eingelsu klepovausu vesh' ri rik' ish-veh haulan yi, ik ish-veh lau nam-tor wuh rom deed tor seize ik kar, abertau ish-veh, heh kwul ne' ish-veh nasik heh glu. Tonk'peh, au went ish-veh yut, heh vesh' ak vitem-tor abru svi' wuh duv t' wuh prison temok. Na' wuh kru'minaakh wadan, au sasarlah s' ish-veh tor la' himself svi' mr. Lorry's tvi-shal va'ashiv, wilat au afer-tor wuh hinek gentleman walking tor heh fro svi' restless anxiety. Au leralmin-tor au had vesh' k' lucie abi' aishan i', heh had goh losrak ish-veh na' wuh zamu minutes, tor sarlah heh potau ish-veh latva. Ish-veh sa-mekh had ri vesh' gla-tor, opi' au quitted wuh banking-kelek na' kehkuh o'wak-vel. She had ein faint rok-tor ik ish-veh mediation lau korsau charles, tonk'peh au vesh' maut slight. Au had vesh' weht do kaukuh wadan hal-tor: wilat kupi au nam-tor? Mr. Lorry bek-tor abi' lehkuh; tonk'peh, hassu manette ri returning, heh au hasu unwilling tor trasha lucie sovek longer, ish-veh vesh' arranged ik au dang hal-tor pla' tor ish-veh, heh sarlah tor wuh banking-kelek va'ashiv na' midnight. Svi' wuh meanwhile, carton would bek-tor sa'awek k' wuh yon na' wuh hassu. Au bek-tor heh bek-tor, heh wuh wak-vel kwul-tor leh-dah; tonk'peh hassu manette did ri sarlah pla'. Mr. Lorry fun-tor, heh afer-tor rai tidings t' ish-veh, heh katau rim. Wilat kupi au nam-tor? Au vesh' discussing nash deshker, heh vesh' siyah kelek abru ein kobat velek t' rok fi' ish-veh prolonged absence, lu au puzhu-tor ish-veh fi' wuh kaiden. Wuh instant au svi-tor wuh tvi-shal, ish-veh vesh' eiktra ik ek' vesh' pakik. Whether au had really vesh' tor sovek veh, il whether au had vesh' ek' ik wak traversing wuh yut, vesh' worla fainu. U' au lam-tor staring na' au, au ya'akash ish-veh rai deshker, na' ish-veh limuk var-tor au kanok-vei. "i fam yehat talal ish-veh, " leralmin-tor au, "heh i bolau ma ish-veh. Wilat nam-tor ish-veh?" ish-veh patam heh drahk vesh' sai-famik, heh, u' au stariben k' wuh helpless glazhau fam-kelek-tor ek' pa', au nem-tor ish-veh tor-pal ska', heh kal-tor ish-veh eku fi' wuh lan-tol. "wilat nam-tor t'nash-veh wu-ku-san? I ma vesh' looking kanok-wilat na' t'nash-veh wu-ku-san, heh i mokuhlek't talal ish-veh. Ra ma au ovsoh k' t'nash-veh ar'kadan? Wak hish-tor: i bolau shaht eifa ash'el." au glazhau na' veh wuh'ashiv, heh ish-veh khaf-spol tev-tor k'svi au. "sarlah, sarlah!" leralmin-tor au, svi' wuh whimpering miserable yut; "kal-tor me prah tor ar'kadan. Mazhiv-kur-tor me t'nash-veh ar'kadan." receiving rai kilko-srashiv, au tore ish-veh isachya, heh kuhsh-tor ish-veh ash'ya fi-tor wuh solektra, spo' wuh saglakolau kan. "ri tor torture wuh ri donku-tor forlorn wretch, " au implored au, k' wuh dreadful maf; "tonk'peh mazhiv-kur-tor me t'nash-veh ar'kadan! Ra nam-tor tor shetau t' etek, kuv eifa ash'el nam-tor ri ovsoh tor-mu-yor?" pakik, utterly pakik! Ish-veh vesh' ni clearly mesakh rok tor utvau k' ish-veh, il ar'kadan tor restore ish-veh, ik--u' kuv k' agreement--au tik shitau wuh el'ru fi-tor ish-veh tipan, heh soothed ish-veh tor hayal-tor ne' fa' wuh yon, k' wuh ugaya ik au dang ma ish-veh ar'kadan presently. Au sank vi' wuh ku-san, heh brooded abru' wuh kilyon, heh foshuhl bezhun-masu. U' kuv ek' ik had pavesh-tor opi' wuh kamu-tvi-shal wak vesh' wuh momentary fancy, il wuh sahr-tor, mr. Lorry gla-tor ish-veh shrink vi' wuh faikaik khlop ik defarge had had svi' keeping. Dau, heh impressed k' vash u' au fi' vesh', k' nash spectacle t' ruin, ish-veh vesh' ri wuh wak tor yield tor such zherka. Ish-veh lonely ko-fu, bereft t' ish-veh kim-shah rok heh reliance, appealed tor au fi' nuh' strongly. Va'ashiv, u' kuv k' agreement, au glazhau na' veh wuh'ashiv k' veh meaning svi' ish-veh limuk. Carton vesh' wuh wuh'rak tor stariben: "wuh kim-shah pavesh nam-tor hal-tor: ish-veh vesh' ri mau. Ha; au had weh-rom nam-tor taken tor ish-veh. Tonk'peh, fa' du hal-tor, dungi du, na' wuh moment, steadily attend tor me? Ri tor ya'akash me po i tor wuh stipulations i am going tor tor, heh faikaik wuh ugaya i am going tor faikaik; i ma wuh utvau--wuh rom veh." "i ri tor vet ish-veh, " kilko-tor mr. Lorry. "leralmin fi'." wuh khlop svi' wuh ku-san svi' au, vesh' ek' wuh wak monotonously rocking itself tor heh fro, heh moaning. Au stariben svi' such wuh molu u' au would ma nam-tor-tor kuv au had vesh' watching k' wuh has-bosh-sar-tak svi' wuh mu-yor. Carton stooped tor abrashau wuh tor-pal, if ti siyah entangling ish-veh ash'ya. U' au did ni, wuh pi' nuf svi' if wuh hassu vesh' accustomed tor lesh wuh feim-tor t' ish-veh gad's gu-vam, tevan-tor lightly fi' wuh lan-tol. Carton nem-tor ish-veh abru, heh tra' vesh' wuh hesha dun svi' ish-veh. "etek dang glazhau na' nash!" au leralmin-tor. Mr. Lorry nodded ish-veh consent. Au tu'ash ish-veh, heh sporiben, "itaren oekon!" "ra nam-tor ish-veh?" ya'akash mr. Lorry, eagerly. "wuh moment! Kal-tor me stariben t' ish-veh svi' its shi. Wuh'rak, " au shitau ish-veh el'ru svi' ish-veh tor-pal, heh nem-tor wuh'ashiv dun s' ish-veh, "ik nam-tor wuh tor-kisev if enables me tor be' dvun s' nash kahr. Glazhau na' ish-veh. Gla-tor du--sydney carton, wuh englishman?" mr. Lorry meskarau ish-veh tu'ash svi' ish-veh el'ru, gazing svi' ish-veh earnest limuk. "potau ish-veh na' me abi' tor-morrow. Dungau gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh tor-morrow, du vokau, heh i had weh-rom ri nem-tor ish-veh vi' wuh prison." "po ri?" "i ri tor fai-tor; i prefer ri tor tor ni. I', nem-tor nash dun ik hassu manette has lesh pa' ish-veh. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh kahwa tor-kisev, enabling ish-veh heh ish-veh ko-fu heh ish-veh kan, na' sovek wak, tor be' dvun wuh foshek heh wuh frontier! Gla-tor du?" "ha!" "sos'eh au prah ish-veh u' ish-veh kim-shah heh utmost precaution tehnat ek'rasah, za-gad. Lu nam-tor ish-veh dated? Tonk'peh rai tukh; ri tor stay tor glazhau; shitau ish-veh abru carefully k' t'nash-veh heh ish-veh sha'. I', glantau! I worla vet-tor abi' k'svi nash wadan il dahkuh, ik au had, il kupi ma such wuh dun. Ish-veh nam-tor rom, abi' recalled. Tonk'peh ish-veh lau nam-tor ak recalled, heh, i ma utvau tor nah-tor, dungi nam-tor." "au nam-tor ri svi' tehvar?" "au nam-tor svi' lo'uk tehvar. Au nam-tor svi' tehvar t' denunciation k' madame defarge. I fai-tor ish-veh s' ish-veh sha' bru-lar. I ma overheard zhit t' ik kosu's, tor-mu-yor, if ma presented ish-veh tehvar tor me svi' karik colours. I ma pakik rai wak, heh opi' yi, ki'gla-tor nash-veh wuh zamasu. Au wugau me. Au fai-tor ik wuh lapan-sawyer, living k' wuh prison temok, nam-tor ne' wuh tash t' wuh defarges, heh has vesh' rehearsed k' madame defarge u' tor ish-veh having gla-tor ish-veh"--au worla mentioned lucie's ahm--"tor glat heh glantokaya tor prisoners. Ish-veh nam-tor hagik tor fa-glan-tor ik wuh pretence dungi nam-tor wuh tsuri veh, wuh prison besau, heh ik ish-veh dungi involve ish-veh ha'kiv--heh sos'eh ish-veh kan's--heh sos'eh ish-veh sa-mekh's--na' fi' ma vesh' gla-tor k' ish-veh na' ik shi. Ri tor glazhau ni horrified. Du dungi korsau au ek'." "sha-ka-ri vahl i lau, carton! Tonk'peh uf?" "i am going tor var-tor du uf. Ish-veh dungi nerau fi' du, heh ish-veh kupi nerau fi' rai weh-rom sasu. Nash uzh denunciation dungi certainly ri nem-tor shi abi' po' tor-morrow; probably ri abi' dahkuh il rehkuh gad afterwards; weht probably wuh wehk gad afterwards. Du fai-tor ish-veh nam-tor wuh capital tr'y'kak, tor la'tusa na', il sympathise k', wuh shi-kar-tor t' wuh guillotine. She heh ish-veh sa-mekh would unquestionably nam-tor guilty t' nash tr'y'kak, heh nash kosu (wuh inveteracy t' t'vi pursuit fam yehat nam-tor kethelvau) would bek-tor tor hau ik karik'es tor ish-veh nuf, heh tor herself doubly sure. Du zahal-tor me?" "ni attentively, heh k' ni mau guhl'es svi' ra du leralmin, ik na' wuh moment i pak-tor glan, " touching wuh pla' t' wuh hassu's ku-san, "kauk t' nash flakosh." "du ma donku, heh mokuhlek mahr-tor wuh tvai t' travelling tor wuh seacoast u' sahris u' wuh halovaya mokuhlek nam-tor tor. Ish-veh preparations ma vesh' ovsoh na' ein gad, tor fun tor england. Lehkuh-mal tor-morrow ma ish-veh jarel pok, ni ik au lau nam-tor svi' starting trim na' dahkuh o'wak-vel svi' wuh aru." "ish-veh dungau nam-tor ovsoh!" ish-veh manner vesh' ni fervent heh inspiring, ik mr. Lorry kum-tor wuh yai, heh vesh' u' sahris u' youth. "du nam-tor wuh thol khaf-spol. Did i leralmin etek kupi nerau fi-tor rai weh-rom sasu? Var-tor ish-veh, tor-mu-yor, ra du fai-tor t' ish-veh tehvar u' involving ish-veh kan heh ish-veh sa-mekh. Dwell fi-tor ik, na' she would ti ish-veh sha' rom patam be' ish-veh sa-telsu's cheerfully." au faltered na' wuh instant; yi went fi' u' fa'. "na' wuh sake t' ish-veh kan heh ish-veh sa-mekh, hish-tor fi-tor ish-veh wuh bolayek t' leaving paris, k' au heh du, na' ik wadan. Var-tor ish-veh ik ish-veh vesh' ish-veh sa-telsu's kim-shah arrangement. Var-tor ish-veh ik weht nerau fi-tor ish-veh do she dare dva-tor, il rok. Du nah-tor ik ish-veh sa-mekh, kauk svi' nash maf fupa s', dungi nekhau himself tor ish-veh; tor du ri?" "i am sure t' ish-veh." "i nahp ni. Quietly heh steadily ma ek' aifa arrangements tor svi' wuh courtyard la', kauk tor wuh taking t' ish-veh sha' ku-san svi' wuh carriage. Wuh moment sarlah nash-veh tor du, nem-tor me svi', heh yetur maf." "i ken-tor ik i bek-tor na' du ne' ek' circumstances?" "du ma t'nash-veh tor-kisev svi' ish-veh el'ru k' wuh shom, du fai-tor, heh dungi reserve t'nash-veh shi. Bek-tor na' nothing tonk'peh ki' t'nash-veh shi occupied, heh yi na' england!" "po, yi, " leralmin-tor mr. Lorry, grasping ish-veh nayik tonk'peh ni pesik heh br'xan el'ru, "ish-veh tor ri ek' nerau fi' veh hinek sasu, tonk'peh i dungau ma wuh nu'ri heh ardent sasu na' t'nash-veh vla." "k' wuh gol'nev t' sha-ka-ri du dungau! Ugaya me solemnly ik nothing dungi vi-yumuk du tor rubitau wuh rivak fi' if etek i' lamok pledged tor veh wuh'ashiv." "nothing, carton." "vokau aifa zhit tor-morrow: rubah wuh rivak, il vohtaya svi' ish-veh--na' sovek utvau--heh rai ha'kiv mokuhlek possibly nam-tor korsau, heh wehk ha-tor bolau inevitably nam-tor sacrificed." "i dungi vokau au. I rok tor tor t'nash-veh krus faithfully." "heh i rok tor tor t'nash-veh. I', rom bye!" hi au leralmin-tor ish-veh k' wuh shi'vukhut abru'teruklar-ru'lut t' earnestness, heh hi au kauk shitau wuh hinek sasu's el'ru tor ish-veh bru-lar, au did ri krus s' ish-veh yi. Au gol-tor ish-veh ni irak tor arouse wuh rocking khlop fa' wuh dying kilyon, u' tor prah wuh tor-sai heh taik shitau fi-tor ish-veh, heh tor tempt ish-veh forth tor talal wilat wuh wu-ku-san heh ar'kadan vesh' ipik ik ish-veh fam dvun moaningly besought ki'. Au lates-tor fi' wuh vath vla t' ish-veh heh protected ish-veh tor wuh courtyard t' wuh kelek wilat wuh afflicted khaf-spol--ni kunli svi' wuh memorable wak lu au had revealed ish-veh sha' desolate khaf-spol tor ish-veh--outwatched wuh awful mu-yor. Au svi-tor wuh courtyard heh hafau tra' na' wuh zamu moments sa'awek, looking abru na' wuh ta'hal svi' wuh krani t' ish-veh tvi-shal. Fa' au went maf, au breathed wuh kudaya na' ish-veh, heh wuh rom-halan. Chapter xiii. Kau-leh-dahkuh svi' wuh nesh-kur prison t' wuh conciergerie, wuh doomed t' wuh gad awaited ish-veh buk. Au vesh' svi' su'etek u' wuh wehk gad t' wuh tevun. Kau-leh-dahkuh vesh' tor padukau ik aru fi' wuh ha'kiv-mashen t' wuh kahr tor wuh boundless everlasting masutra. Fa' ish-veh nala vesh' quit t' au, uzh occupants vesh' kru'minaakh; fa' ish-veh khaf sahr-tor vi' wuh khaf ne-tor za-gad, wuh khaf ik vesh' tor mingle k' ish-veh tor-morrow vesh' already eku k'wuhli. Dahkuh nosahp heh leh-dah vesh' var-tor ska'. S' wuh uroshitausu-paik t' steh-leh, t'vi don-tak kupi ri mahr-tor ish-veh ha'kiv, tor wuh ogsu t' dah-leh, t'vi poverty heh obscurity kupi ri korsau ish-veh. Tukhik has, engendered svi' wuh vices heh neglects t' sasu, dungi seize fi' victims t' ek' degrees; heh wuh frightful moral disorder, pukeshta t' unspeakable suffering, intolerable oppression, heh heartless indifference, smote kaing rik' distinction. Charles darnay, sa'awek svi' wuh nala, had potun-tor himself k' rai flattering plokh opi' sarlah ish-veh tor ish-veh s' wuh tribunal. Svi' kanok zehl t' wuh narrative au had puzhu-tor, au had puzhu-tor ish-veh condemnation. Au had fully comprehended ik rai personal vi-yumuk kupi possibly korsau ish-veh, ik au vesh' virtually sentenced k' wuh millions, heh ik kebi kupi avail ish-veh nothing. Nevertheless, ish-veh vesh' ri hagik, k' wuh limuk t' ish-veh k'diwa ko-telsu sluk fa' ish-veh, tor tertitau ish-veh kashek tor ra ish-veh bolau lesh. Ish-veh meskaraya fi' ha'kiv vesh' karik, heh ish-veh vesh' maut, maut lerash, tor loosen; k' gradual urgam heh degrees unclosed wuh pi' la', ish-veh clenched wuh tighter tra'; heh lu au katau ish-veh karik'es tor lesh fi' ik el'ru heh ish-veh yielded, nash vesh' a'ing va'ashiv. Tra' vesh' wuh brax, nuh', svi' ek' ish-veh nahp, wuh waukik heh falek-tor working t' ish-veh khaf-spol, ik contended tehnat resignation. Kuv, na' wuh moment, au did olau resigned, yi ish-veh ko-telsu heh kan vi had tor ha-tor po' ish-veh, seemed tor protest heh tor tor ish-veh wuh selfish vel. Tonk'peh, ek' nash vesh' palikauk. Fa' wu, wuh consideration ik tra' vesh' rai disgrace svi' wuh buk au bolau ragel-tor, heh ik su'etek went wuh ka fau-yut wrongfully, heh sahr-tor ish-veh firmly kanok gad, sprang abru tor kastorilau ish-veh. Thurai zahal-tor wuh nahp ik mau t' wuh fa-wak kal-tor'thieri enjoyable k' wuh tal-kam ones, nerau fi' ish-veh hizhuk fortitude. Ni, k' degrees au hayal vi' wuh weh-rom fupa s', lu au kupi ashenau ish-veh nahp mau higher, heh bes-tor comfort ne'. Fa' ish-veh had eku svi' gu'gelik fi' wuh mu-yor t' ish-veh condemnation, au had travelled thus irak fi' ish-veh kim-shah yut. Hasu kal-tor tor purchase wuh tvai t' kitaun, heh wuh ta'hal, au hayal-tor ne' tor kitau abi' such wak u' wuh prison ha'gelek dang nam-tor sayonotau. Au kitau wuh wu nuhm tor lucie, showing ish-veh ik au had fainu nothing t' ish-veh sa-mekh's imprisonment, abi' au had puzhu-tor t' ish-veh s' herself, heh ik au had vesh' u' ignorant u' she t' ish-veh sa-mekh's heh sa-kuk's responsibility na' ik misery, abi' wuh dun had vesh' telv-tor. Au had already danau tor ish-veh ik ish-veh concealment s' herself t' wuh ahm au had relinquished, vesh' wuh veh nosh--fully intelligible i'--ik ish-veh sa-mekh had attached tor ish-veh betrothal, heh vesh' wuh veh ugaya au had fam dvun faikaik fi' wuh asal t' ish-veh kal'i'farr. Au entreated ish-veh, na' ish-veh sa-mekh's sake, worla tor seek tor fai-tor whether ish-veh sa-mekh had shetau oblivious t' wuh nam t' wuh dun, il had had ish-veh recalled tor ish-veh (na' wuh moment, il na' rom), k' wuh var t' wuh kispek, fi' ik hinek gad ne' wuh tal-kam hinek sov-hali-lap svi' wuh bah-ker. Kuv au had korsau sovek definite remembrance t' ish-veh, tra' kupi nam-tor rai vet ik au had supposed ish-veh vashau k' wuh bastille, lu au had afer-tor rai mention t' ish-veh among wuh za-vel t' prisoners if wuh sutra had discovered tra', heh if had vesh' kethelvau tor ek' wuh panu. Au besought ish-veh--hi au hau ik au fai-tor ish-veh vesh' needless--tor console ish-veh sa-mekh, k' impressing ish-veh k'fai kanok sival tvai she kupi nah-tor t', k' wuh yeht'es ik au had ovsoh nothing na' if au kupi justly reproach himself, tonk'peh had uniformly yen-tor himself na' ish-veh joint sakes. Nam-tor' ish-veh preservation t' ish-veh sha' kim-shah grateful ashaya heh kudaya, heh ish-veh overcoming t' ish-veh sorrow, tor vaikau herself tor ish-veh tal-kam kan, au adjured ish-veh, u' au would ragel-tor svi' sha-ka-ri, tor comfort ish-veh sa-mekh. Tor ish-veh sa-mekh himself, au kitau svi' wuh ka ish-veh; tonk'peh, au var-tor ish-veh sa-mekh ik au expressly confided ish-veh ko-telsu heh kan tor ish-veh tun. Heh au var-tor ish-veh nash, maut strongly, k' wuh rok t' kastorilau ish-veh s' sovek despondency il tehvar-bosh retrospect na' if au foresaw au lau nam-tor tending. Tor mr. Lorry, au commended au ek', heh danau ish-veh worldly tek'ik. Ik ovsoh, k' wehk hau zhit-bal t' grateful friendship heh lamekh attachment, ek' vesh' ovsoh. Au worla nahp t' carton. Ish-veh kashek vesh' ni bosh t' wuh vath, ik au worla wuh'wak nahp t' ish-veh. Au had wak tor shaht aifa nuhm fa' wuh ha'ge vesh' shitau si'. Lu au ti ne' fi' ish-veh terp sar-tak, au nahp au had ovsoh k' nash panu. Tonk'peh, ish-veh beckoned ish-veh pla' svi' ish-veh yuk, heh gluvau itself svi' shining shidau. Elik heh kunli, pla' svi' wuh hinek kelek svi' soho (hi ish-veh had nothing svi' ish-veh spo' wuh yeht kelek), unaccountably sadalau heh ta'hal t' khaf-spol, au vesh' k' lucie va'ashiv, heh she var-tor ish-veh ish-veh vesh' ek' wuh sahr-tor, heh au had worla hal-tor maf. Wuh svizh t' forgetfulness, heh yi au had kauk dashau, heh had sarlah pla' tor ish-veh, tevik heh na' sochya, heh wi tra' vesh' rai natyan svi' ish-veh. Wuh'ashiv svizh t' oblivion, heh au awoke svi' wuh sombre asal, unconscious wilat au vesh' il ra had pavesh-tor, abi' ish-veh kahai fi-tor ish-veh kashek, "nash nam-tor wuh gad t' t'nash-veh tevakh!" thus, had au sarlah k'fai wuh wadan, tor wuh gad lu wuh kau-leh-dahkuh patam vesh' tor tevan. Heh i', du' au vesh' tertitau, heh rok-tor ik au kupi ragel-tor wuh shaht k' hizhuk heroism, wuh uzh torai began svi' ish-veh waking nahp, if vesh' maut rihagik tor trensu. Au had worla gla-tor wuh instrument ik vesh' tor terminate ish-veh ha'kiv. Uf pid ish-veh vesh' s' wuh solektra, uf wehk ash-tor ish-veh had, wilat au would nam-tor lam-tor, uf au would nam-tor estuhl, whether wuh touching el'ru would nam-tor kur-tor yon-kur, if yut ish-veh limuk would nam-tor da-tor, whether au would nam-tor wuh wuh'rak, il lau nam-tor wuh kim-shah: aifa heh wehk kahwa deshkau, svi' nowise khartau k' ish-veh dungi, obtruded themselves abru' heh abru' va'ashiv, countless wak. Neither vesh' au tersau k' pthak: au vesh' d'wonil t' rai pthak. Rather, au tveshulau svi' wuh flekh besetting aitlun tor fai-tor ra tor tor lu wuh wak sarlah; wuh aitlun gigantically disproportionate tor wuh zamu swift moments tor if ish-veh referred; wuh wondering ik vesh' weht spo' wuh wondering t' ein vath tam'a k'svi ish-veh, do ish-veh sha'. Wuh wadan went fi' u' au lates-tor tor heh fro, heh wuh wak-vel kwul-tor wuh su'etek au would worla zhu-tor va'ashiv. Naukuh hal-tor na' ek'wak, lehkuh hal-tor na' ek'wak, leh-wun hal-tor na' ek'wak, leh-dah coming fi' tor be' dvun maf. Po' wuh lerash kal'i'fee k' ik rivitanik torai t' nahp if had kim-shah perplexed ish-veh, au had prah wuh weh-rom t' ish-veh. Au lates-tor abru heh ne', softly repeating ish-veh ahm tor himself. Wuh rasahkos t' wuh strife vesh' abru'. Au kupi lates abru heh ne', elik s' distracting fancies, praying na' himself heh na' au. Leh-dah hal-tor na' ek'wak. Au had vesh' apprised ik wuh kim-shah wadan vesh' rehkuh, heh au fai-tor au would nam-tor summoned ein wak earlier, inasmuch u' wuh tumbrils jolted heavily heh slowly k'fai wuh yut. Therefore, au resolved tor potau dahkuh fa' ish-veh kashek, u' wuh wadan, heh ni tor karik-tor himself svi' wuh tvi-wak ik au lau nam-tor kup, po' ik wak, tor karik-tor vath. Walking regularly tor heh fro k' ish-veh kar hesha fi' ish-veh thasek, wuh maut natya sasu s' wuh prisoner, vi had lates-tor tor heh fro na' la nekwitaya, au puzhu-tor veh kwul-tor maf s' ish-veh, rik' ak'wikmun. Wuh wadan had thon-tor spo' danik vath wadan. Devoutly itar-bosh tor sha-ka-ri na' ish-veh recovered shal-mat, au nahp, "tra' nam-tor tonk'peh wuh'ashiv i', " heh da-tor tor lates va'ashiv. Footsteps svi' wuh kov tvur s'udish wuh svep. Au pehkau. Wuh tal-muv vesh' shitau svi' wuh klachek, heh da-tor. Fa' wuh svep vesh' tu'ash, il u' ish-veh tu'ash, wuh sasu leralmin-tor svi' wuh neik spes, svi' eingelsu: "au has worla gla-tor me la'; i ma potau s' ish-veh yut. Hal-tor du svi' sa'awek; i bek-tor be'. Pak-tor rai wak!" wuh svep vesh' sahris tu'ash heh a'ing, heh tra' lam-tor fa' ish-veh limuk tor limuk, hizhuk, intent fi-tor ish-veh, k' wuh ta'hal t' wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut fi' ish-veh features, heh wuh cautionary ozh fi' ish-veh bru, sydney carton. Tra' vesh' vel ni ugelik heh remarkable svi' ish-veh glazhau, ik, na' wuh wuh'rak moment, wuh prisoner misdoubted ish-veh tor nam-tor wuh apparition t' ish-veh sha' imagining. Tonk'peh, au stariben, heh ish-veh vesh' ish-veh spes; au nem-tor wuh prisoner's el'ru, heh ish-veh vesh' ish-veh yeht ruskaraya. "t' ek' wuh sutra fi-tor terra, du least gishu tor gla-tor me?" au leralmin-tor. "i kupi ri dva-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor du. I mokuhlek scarcely dva-tor ish-veh i'. Du nam-tor ri"--wuh apprehension sarlah suddenly vi' ish-veh kashek--"wuh prisoner?" "rai. I am accidentally ma t' wuh tepul abru' veh t' wuh keepers la', heh svi' virtue t' ish-veh i lamok fa' du. Sarlah nash-veh s' ish-veh--ish-veh ko-telsu, tal-kam darnay." wuh prisoner wrung ish-veh el'ru. "i katau du wuh ya'akash s' ish-veh." "ra nam-tor ish-veh?" "wuh danik earnest, pressing, heh emphatic entreaty, addressed tor du svi' wuh danik pathetic molu t' wuh spes ni tal-kam tor du, ik du muhl vokau." wuh prisoner da-tor ish-veh limuk partly aside. "du ma rai wak tor ya'akash me po i katau ish-veh, il ra ish-veh tvai; i ma rai wak tor var-tor du. Du bolau comply k' ish-veh--nem-tor ska' eifa kluf du sai-vel-tor, heh bes-tor fi' aifa t' t'nash-veh." tra' vesh' wuh ku-san tehnat wuh temok t' wuh nala, za' wuh prisoner. Carton, pressing fa'rak, had already, k' wuh threshan t' igen-wesh, prah ish-veh ne' vi' ish-veh, heh lam-tor abru' ish-veh, sai-fam-ash'yaik. "bes-tor fi' aifa kluf t' t'nash-veh. Shitau ish-veh el'ru tor au; shitau ish-veh dungi tor au. Sahris!" "carton, tra' nam-tor rai escaping s' nash shi; ish-veh worla mokuhlek nam-tor ovsoh. Du dungi goh tev-tor k' me. Ish-veh nam-tor ni-resh." "ish-veh would nam-tor ni-resh kuv i ya'akash du tor stron; tonk'peh tor i? Lu i ya'akash du tor be' dvun si' na' ik svep, var-tor me ish-veh nam-tor ni-resh heh hafau la'. Rubah ik cravat na' nash t' t'nash-veh, ik tor-pal na' nash t' t'nash-veh. Du' du tor ish-veh, kal-tor me nem-tor nash ribbon s' ish-veh isachya, heh hutau si' ish-veh isachya spo' nash t' t'nash-veh!" k' wonderful quickness, heh k' wuh karik'es fi' t' dungi heh torai, ik saudau ved supernatural, au punekwitau ek' aifa rubai fi-tor ish-veh. Wuh prisoner vesh' spo' wuh nu'ri kan svi' ish-veh el'ru. "carton! Tal-kam carton! Ish-veh nam-tor ni-resh. Ish-veh fam yehat nam-tor accomplished, ish-veh worla mokuhlek nam-tor ovsoh, ish-veh has vesh' attempted, heh has kwon-hau-ov vravshau. I implore du ri tor hau ish-veh tevakh tor wuh bitterness t' t'nash-veh." "tor i ya'akash du, t'nash-veh tal-kam darnay, tor be' dvun wuh svep? Lu i ya'akash ik, klee'fah. Tra' nam-tor pen heh neshuk heh dun fi' nash pasu. Nam-tor ish-veh el'ru br'xan hiyet tor kitau?" "ish-veh vesh' lu sarlah du svi'." "br'xan ish-veh va'ashiv, heh kitau ra i dungau dictate. Sahris, t'hy'la, sahris!" pressing ish-veh el'ru tor ish-veh bewildered patam, darnay hayal-tor ne' na' wuh pasu. Carton, k' ish-veh gas'rak el'ru svi' ish-veh thasek, lam-tor ikap-tor be' ish-veh. "kitau exactly u' i stariben." "tor ik tor i shi'yavekh ish-veh?" "tor kling." carton fam dvun had ish-veh el'ru svi' ish-veh thasek. "tor i kinuf ish-veh?" "rai." wuh prisoner glazhau abru, na' tik deshker. Carton, standing abru' ish-veh k' ish-veh el'ru svi' ish-veh thasek, glazhau ne'. "'kuv du vokau, '" leralmin-tor carton, dictating, "'wuh zhit ik be' dvun-tor svi' etek, wu ago, du dungi readily comprehend nash lu gla-tor du ish-veh. Du tor vokau au, i fai-tor. Ish-veh nam-tor ri svi' ish-veh malat tor yen-tor au.'" au vesh' bestan ish-veh el'ru s' ish-veh thasek; wuh prisoner chancing tor glazhau abru svi' ish-veh hurried wonder u' au kitau, wuh el'ru pehkau, ikapik fi-tor vel. "ma du written 'yen-tor au'?" carton ya'akash. "i ma. Nam-tor ik wuh wun svi' ish-veh el'ru?" "rai; i am ri armed." "ra nam-tor ish-veh svi' ish-veh el'ru?" "du dungau fai-tor directly. Kitau fi'; tra' nam-tor tonk'peh wuh zamu zhit weht." au dictated va'ashiv. "'i am itar-bosh ik wuh wak has sarlah, lu i mokuhlek skan-tor au. Ik i tor ni nam-tor rai subject na' regret il tushat.'" u' au leralmin-tor aifa zhit k' ish-veh bezhun teslau fi' wuh kitausu, ish-veh el'ru slowly heh softly dvun-tor ne' beyik wuh kitausu's limuk. Wuh pen eku-tor s' darnay's ozh fi' wuh pasu, heh au glazhau pa' ish-veh vacantly. "ra muhs nam-tor ik?" au ya'akash. "muhs?" "vel ik tuhsau me?" "i am d'wonil t' nothing; tra' mokuhlek nam-tor nothing la'. Nem-tor abru wuh pen heh shaht. Brax, brax!" u' kuv ish-veh vokaya vesh' impaired, il ish-veh sutra disordered, wuh prisoner tor wuh urgam tor rally ish-veh attention. U' au glazhau na' carton k' clouded bezhun heh k' wuh rubitau manner t' eshan, carton--ish-veh el'ru va'ashiv svi' ish-veh thasek--glazhau steadily na' ish-veh. "brax, brax!" wuh prisoner keh'sei abru' wuh dun, wuh'wak weht. "'kuv ish-veh had vesh' vathru; '" carton's el'ru vesh' va'ashiv watchfully heh softly stealing ne'; "'i worla dang ma nam-tor-tor wuh longer opportunity. Kuv ish-veh had vesh' vathru; '" wuh el'ru vesh' na' wuh prisoner's limuk; "'i dang tonk'peh ma had ni mau wuh weht tor kilko-srashiv na'. Kuv ish-veh had vesh' vathru--'" carton glazhau na' wuh pen heh gla-tor ish-veh vesh' trailing ska' vi' unintelligible glat. Carton's el'ru dvun-tor pla' tor ish-veh thasek rai weht. Wuh prisoner sprang abru k' wuh reproachful glazhau, tonk'peh carton's el'ru vesh' ikap-tor heh pesik na' ish-veh han-sharular, heh carton's losrak kar kum-tor ish-veh pauk wuh san. Na' wuh zamu seconds au faintly struggled k' wuh sasu vi had sarlah tor ti ne' ish-veh ha'kiv na' ish-veh; tonk'peh, k'svi wuh minute il ni, au vesh' sakadau insensible fi' wuh solektra. Sahris, tonk'peh k' el'ru u' yeht tor wuh lof u' ish-veh khaf-spol vesh', carton sai-vel-tor himself svi' wuh sai-vel wuh prisoner had laid aside, dref-tor pla' ish-veh isachya, heh tied ish-veh k' wuh ribbon wuh prisoner had worn. Yi, au softly puvutau, "svi-tor tra'! Sarlah svi'!" heh wuh zamasu presented himself. "gla-tor du?" leralmin-tor carton, looking abru, u' au kneeled fi' veh mal-nef be' wuh insensible khlop, putting wuh dun svi' wuh thasek: "nam-tor ish-veh hazard maut lo'uk?" "mr. Carton, " wuh zamasu kilko-tor, k' wuh timid snap t' ish-veh ozh, "t'nash-veh hazard nam-tor ri ik, svi' wuh bali t' business la', kuv du nam-tor yeht tor wuh bosh t' ish-veh bargain." "ri tor pthak me. I dungi nam-tor yeht tor wuh tevakh." "du bolau nam-tor, mr. Carton, kuv wuh var t' kau-leh-dahkuh nam-tor tor nam-tor gas'rak. Hasu tor gas'rak k' du svi' ik sai-vel, i dungau ma rai pthak." "ma rai pthak! I dungau ak nam-tor s' wuh yut t' harming du, heh wuh shom dungi ak nam-tor irak s' la', sanoi oekon! I', prah assistance heh nem-tor me tor wuh coach." "du?" leralmin-tor wuh zamasu nervously. "ish-veh, sasu, k' ik i ma di'kizh-tor. Du hal-tor si' na' wuh temep k' if du katau me svi'?" "veling." "i vesh' kobat heh faint lu du katau me svi', heh i am fainter i' du nem-tor me si'. Wuh parting interview has overpowered me. Such wuh vel has pavesh-tor la', k'ashiv, heh nuh' k'ashiv. Ish-veh ha'kiv nam-tor svi' ish-veh sha' el'ru. Sahris! Vutau assistance!" "du swear ri tor svik-tor me?" leralmin-tor wuh trembling zamasu, u' au svizh-tor na' wuh kim-shah moment. "sasu, sasu!" fun-tor carton, stamping ish-veh ash'ya; "ma i sworn k' rai solemn vow already, tor hal-tor k'fai k' nash, ik du thinoi wuh taluhk moments i'? Nem-tor ish-veh yourself tor wuh courtyard du fai-tor t', shi ish-veh yourself svi' wuh carriage, gluvaya ish-veh yourself tor mr. Lorry, var-tor ish-veh yourself tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh rai restorative tonk'peh sov, heh tor vokau t'nash-veh zhit t' kim-shah mu-yor, heh ish-veh ugaya t' kim-shah mu-yor, heh yetur maf!" wuh zamasu withdrew, heh carton hayal-tor himself na' wuh pasu, resting ish-veh fa-patam fi' ish-veh el'ru. Wuh zamasu fun-tor iyi, k' dahkuh sasu. "uf, yi?" leralmin-tor veh t' au, contemplating wuh tevan-tor khlop. "ni afflicted tor talal ik ish-veh t'hy'la has drawn wuh prize svi' wuh lottery t' sainte guillotine?" "wuh rom patriot, " leralmin-tor wuh vath, "kupi hardly ma vesh' weht afflicted kuv wuh aristocrat had drawn wuh blank." au ashenau wuh unconscious khlop, shitau ish-veh fi' wuh litter au had katau tor wuh svep, heh keh'sei tor lesh ish-veh maf. "wuh wak nam-tor pen, evrmonde, " leralmin-tor wuh zamasu, svi' wuh warning spes. "i fai-tor ish-veh muhl, " kilko-tor carton. "nam-tor tun-bosh t' t'nash-veh t'hy'la, i entreat du, heh trasha me." "sarlah, yi, t'nash-veh kanu, " leralmin-tor barsad. "abertau ish-veh, heh sarlah maf!" wuh svep a'ing, heh carton vesh' losrak sa'awek. Straining ish-veh tepul t' listening tor wuh utmost, au shroi na' sovek ralash ik lau denote suspicion il vikayek. Tra' vesh' rim. Tal-muv da-tor, svep clashed, footsteps be' dvun-tor bi' irak tvur: rai maf vesh' ashenau, il brax tor, ik seemed ritsuri. Eshan weht freely svi' wuh pi' du', au hayal-tor ne' na' wuh pasu, heh shroi va'ashiv abi' wuh wak-vel kwul-tor dahkuh. Sounds ik au vesh' ri kwes t', na' au divined ish-veh meaning, yi began tor nam-tor zhu-yehat. Several svep vesh' tu'ash svi' succession, heh t'forti ish-veh sha'. Wuh gaoler, k' wuh feim svi' ish-veh el'ru, glazhau svi', goh taran, "zahal-tor me, evrmonde!" heh au zahal-tor vi' wuh suk gu'gelik tvi-shal, na' wuh ir. Ish-veh vesh' wuh gu'gelik karil gad, heh ra k' wuh duv k'svi, heh ra k' wuh duv rik', au kupi tonk'peh dimly discern wuh vath vi vesh' katau tra' ki' ish-veh kar bound. Ein vesh' standing; ein hayal-tor. Ein vesh' lamenting, heh svi' restless dvunel; tonk'peh, aifa vesh' zamu. Wuh lo'uk majority vesh' ralash-fam heh fam dvun, looking fixedly na' wuh solektra. U' au lam-tor k' wuh temok svi' wuh neik-ha'khlup teruk, du' ein t' wuh kau-leh-dahkuh vesh' katau svi' po' ish-veh, veh sasu pehkau svi' be' dvun-tor, tor nartaya ish-veh, u' having wuh fai-tukh t' ish-veh. Ish-veh thrilled ish-veh k' wuh lo'uk dread t' discovery; tonk'peh wuh sasu went fi'. Wuh maut zamu moments po' ik, wuh nu'ri kosu, k' wuh slight girlish shid, wuh slor spare limuk svi' if tra' vesh' rai vestige t' kur, heh suk widely tu'ash hasausu bezhun, she-tor s' wuh ku-san wilat au had glantau ish-veh sitting, heh sarlah tor stariben tor ish-veh. "citizen evrmonde, " she leralmin-tor, touching ish-veh k' ish-veh samu el'ru. "i am wuh ri donku-tor pi' ogsu, vi vesh' k' du svi' la nekwitaya." au murmured na' kilko-srashiv: "yeht. I yen-tor ra du vesh' accused t'?" "besau. Hi wuh aishan sha-ka-ri fai-tor ik i am innocent t' sovek. Nam-tor ish-veh kesik? Vi would nah-tor t' plotting k' wuh ri donku-tor pi' kobat creature spo' me?" wuh forlorn abru'teruklar-ru'lut k' if she leralmin-tor ish-veh, ni estuhl ish-veh, ik bezhun-masu palikau s' ish-veh bezhun. "i am ri kwes tor tev-tor, citizen evrmonde, tonk'peh i ma ovsoh nothing. I am ri unwilling tor tev-tor, kuv wuh republic if nam-tor tor tor ni mau rom tor etek ri donku-tor, dungi pinkaunu k' t'nash-veh tevakh; tonk'peh i ri tor fai-tor uf ik mokuhlek nam-tor, citizen evrmonde. Such wuh ri donku-tor kobat pi' creature!" u' wuh kim-shah vel fi' terra ik ish-veh khaf-spol vesh' tor lamekh heh soften tor, ish-veh warmed heh softened tor nash pitiable ko-kan. "i puzhu-tor du vesh' sadalau, citizen evrmonde. I rok-tor ish-veh vesh' yeht?" "ish-veh vesh'. Tonk'peh, i vesh' va'ashiv taken heh condemned." "kuv i lau fau k' du, citizen evrmonde, dungi du kal-tor me meskaraya ish-veh el'ru? I am ri kwes, tonk'peh i am pi' heh kobat, heh ish-veh dungi mazhiv-kur-tor me weht courage." u' wuh hasausu bezhun vesh' abertau tor ish-veh limuk, gla-tor ish-veh wuh sudden vet svi' au, heh yi astonishment. Au hish-tor wuh ar'kadan-worn, avon-worn nu'ri ozh, heh estuhl ish-veh bru-lar. "nam-tor du dying na' ish-veh?" she zhal-tor. "heh ish-veh ko-telsu heh kan. Hush! Ha." "o du dungi kal-tor me meskaraya ish-veh kyi'i el'ru, ri-fainusu?" "hush! Ha, t'nash-veh ri donku-tor ko-kai; tor wuh kim-shah." ***** wuh ka duv ik nam-tor tevan-tor fi' wuh prison, nam-tor tevan-tor, svi' ik ka wadan t' wuh lehkuh-mal aru, fi' wuh foshek k' wuh patreitan pa' ish-veh, lu wuh coach going s' paris yetur abru tor nam-tor linisau. "vi hal-tor la'? Ik ma etek k'svi? Dun!" wuh dun nam-tor handed si', heh telv-tor. "alexandre manette. Hassu. French. If nam-tor au?" nash nam-tor au; nash helpless, inarticulately murmuring, wandering hinek sasu sasfekau. "sauyaing wuh citizen-hassu nam-tor ri svi' ish-veh gas'rak kashek? Wuh revolution-tau dungi ma vesh' nuh' mau na' ish-veh?" greatly nuh' mau na' ish-veh. "hah! Wehk dash k' ish-veh. Lucie. Ish-veh ko-fu. French. If nam-tor she?" nash nam-tor she. "sauyaing ish-veh bolau nam-tor. Lucie, wuh ko-telsu t' evrmonde; nam-tor ish-veh ri?" ish-veh nam-tor. "hah! Evrmonde has wuh assignation kitok-wilat. Lucie, ish-veh kan. Eingelsu. Nash nam-tor she?" she heh rai vath. "shok me, kan t' evrmonde. I', thou hast shok-tor wuh rom republican; vel uzh svi' thy skan; vokau ish-veh! Sydney carton. Advocate. Eingelsu. If nam-tor au?" au ti la', svi' nash teruk t' wuh carriage. Au, nuh', nam-tor sasfekau. "sauyaing wuh eingelsu advocate nam-tor svi' wuh swoon?" ish-veh nam-tor rok-tor au dungi recover svi' wuh fresher sov. Ish-veh nam-tor represented ik au nam-tor ri svi' karik muhl'es, heh has dahshau sadly s' wuh t'hy'la vi nam-tor ne' wuh displeasure t' wuh republic. "nam-tor ik ek'? Ish-veh nam-tor ri wuh lo'uk deal, ik! Wehk nam-tor ne' wuh displeasure t' wuh republic, heh bolau glazhau si' na' wuh pi' krani. Jarvis lorry. Banker. Eingelsu. If nam-tor au?" "i am au. Necessarily, hasu wuh kim-shah." ish-veh nam-tor jarvis lorry vi has kilko-tor tor ek' wuh previous deshkau. Ish-veh nam-tor jarvis lorry vi has alighted heh lam-tor k' ish-veh el'ru fi' wuh coach svep, replying tor wuh travek t' officials. Au leisurely lates pauk wuh carriage heh leisurely mount wuh natuhn, tor glazhau na' ra pi' luggage ish-veh lesh fi' wuh kamu; wuh shasol-sutra hanging pa', hish-tor nearer tor wuh coach svep heh greedily nantaya svi'; wuh pi' kan, lesh k' its ko-mekh, has its pen kar meskarau si' na' ish-veh, ik ish-veh lau esta wuh ko-telsu t' wuh aristocrat vi has hal-tor tor wuh guillotine. "behold ish-veh dun, jarvis lorry, countersigned." "veh mokuhlek trashu, citizen?" "veh mokuhlek trashu. Fa'rak, t'nash-veh postilions! Wuh rom halovaya!" "i salute du, citizens.--heh wuh wuh'rak tehvar be' dvun-tor!" aifa nam-tor va'ashiv wuh zhit t' jarvis lorry, u' au clasps ish-veh el'ru, heh glazhau abru'le. Tra' nam-tor vash svi' wuh carriage, tra' nam-tor weeping, tra' nam-tor wuh ras eshan t' wuh insensible traveller. "nam-tor etek ri going nuh' slowly? Mokuhlek au ri nam-tor vimevilau tor hal-tor faster?" ya'akash lucie, clinging tor wuh hinek sasu. "ish-veh would seem spo' hash, t'nash-veh ashal-veh. I bolau ri urge au nuh' mau; ish-veh would kastorilau suspicion." "glazhau pla', glazhau pla', heh gla-tor kuv etek nam-tor pursued!" "wuh fau-yut nam-tor pa'shik, t'nash-veh dearest. Ni irak, etek nam-tor ri pursued." kelek svi' twos heh threes be' dvun k' etek, solitary uroshal, ruinous kelek, kur-tukh-ar'kada, tanneries, heh wuh spo', tu'ash shasol, avenues t' leafless lap. Wuh lerash uneven pavement nam-tor ne' etek, wuh mos glu vral nam-tor fi' either vla. Sometimes, etek kwul vi' wuh skirting vral, tor nan'woi wuh kov ik clatter etek heh hutau etek; sometimes, etek terpau svi' ruts heh sloughs tra'. Wuh agony t' etwel impatience nam-tor yi ni lo'uk, ik svi' etwel kwai vikayek heh brax etek nam-tor na' getting si' heh sahran--hiding--doing sovek-vel tonk'peh stopping. S' wuh tu'ash shasol, svi' va'ashiv among ruinous kelek, solitary uroshal, kur-tukh-ar'kada, tanneries, heh wuh spo', cottages svi' twos heh threes, avenues t' leafless lap. Ma aifa sasu tehs-tor etek, heh taken etek pla' k' wuh'ashiv fau-yut? Nam-tor ri nash wuh ka shi dah'wak abru'? Itaren sha-ka-ri, rai. Wuh pi'kahr. Glazhau pla', glazhau pla', heh gla-tor kuv etek nam-tor pursued! Hush! Wuh posting-kelek. Leisurely, etwel kehkuh jarel nam-tor taken si'; leisurely, wuh coach lam-tor svi' wuh pi' yut, bereft t' jarel, heh k' rai likelihood fi-tor ish-veh t' ek'wak dvun-tor va'ashiv; leisurely, wuh uzh jarel sarlah vi' visible nam, veh k' veh; leisurely, wuh uzh postilions zahal-tor, sucking heh plaiting wuh lashes t' ish-veh wonil-zehl; leisurely, wuh hinek postilions tum-tor ish-veh donku, tor riyeht haya, heh lasha na' dissatisfied results. Ek' wuh wak, etwel overfraught khaf-spol nam-tor beating na' wuh tav ik would irak outstrip wuh fastest ausahr t' wuh fastest jarel ek'wak foaled. Na' wu-vath wuh uzh postilions nam-tor svi' ish-veh saddles, heh wuh hinek nam-tor losrak za'. Etek nam-tor k'fai wuh pi'kahr, abru wuh kunel, heh ne' wuh kunel, heh fi' wuh neik watery solektra. Suddenly, wuh postilions di'kizh starun k' animated gesticulation, heh wuh jarel nam-tor seshau abru, siyah fi' ish-veh haunches. Etek nam-tor pursued? "ho! K'svi wuh carriage tra'. Stariben yi!" "ra nam-tor ish-veh?" ya'akash mr. Lorry, looking si' na' krani. "uf wehk did au leralmin?" "i ri tor ken-tor du." "--na' wuh kim-shah lehk. Uf wehk tor wuh guillotine tor-gad?" "kau-leh-dahkuh." "i leralmin-tor ni! Wuh kyi'i su'etek! T'nash-veh katravahsu-citizen la' would ma ish-veh keh-leh-dahkuh; lehkuh weht patam nam-tor don having. Wuh guillotine hal-tor handsomely. I ashaya ish-veh. Tonk'peh fa'rak. Whoop!" wuh mu-yor sarlah fi' gu'gelik. Au dvun-tor weht; au nam-tor palikaya tor zaprah, heh tor stariben intelligibly; au nah-tor au nam-tor fam dvun teretuhr; au ya'akash ish-veh, k' ish-veh ahm, ra au has svi' ish-veh el'ru. O pity etek, ves sha-ka-ri, heh gol'nev etek! Glazhau si', glazhau si', heh gla-tor kuv etek nam-tor pursued. Wuh salan nam-tor rushing po' etek, heh wuh wan nam-tor hashan po' etek, heh wuh aikum nam-tor taul-tor po' etek, heh wuh bosh kwai mu-yor nam-tor svi' pursuit t' etek; tonk'peh, ni irak, etek nam-tor pursued k' nothing else. Chapter xiv. Wuh knitting ovsoh svi' ik ka juncture t' wak lu wuh kau-leh-dahkuh awaited ish-veh buk madame defarge meskarau darkly ominous shikh-orna k' wuh vengeance heh jacques rehkuh t' wuh revolutionary jury. Ri svi' wuh wine-mahr-kel did madame defarge confer k' aifa ministers, tonk'peh svi' wuh foshuhl t' wuh lapan-sawyer, erst wuh mender t' fau-yut. Wuh sawyer himself did ri participate svi' wuh conference, tonk'peh abided na' wuh pi' ir, spo' wuh sik sutor-aikum vi vesh' ri tor stariben abi' required, il tor nufai wuh opinion abi' invited. "tonk'peh etwel defarge, " leralmin-tor jacques rehkuh, "nam-tor undoubtedly wuh rom republican? Eh?" "tra' nam-tor rai weh-rom, " wuh voluble vengeance protested svi' ish-veh shrill pitoh, "svi' france." "sochya, pi' vengeance, " leralmin-tor madame defarge, laying ish-veh el'ru k' wuh slight kwal fi' ish-veh ot-lan's bru-lar, "zhu-tor me stariben. T'nash-veh sa-telsu, katravahsu-citizen, nam-tor wuh rom republican heh wuh vakh sasu; au has nazh-tor muhl t' wuh republic, heh ma its guhl'es. Tonk'peh t'nash-veh sa-telsu has ish-veh kobat'es, heh au nam-tor ni kobat u' tor relent na' nash hassu." "ish-veh nam-tor wuh lo'uk pity, " croaked jacques rehkuh, dubiously shaking ish-veh patam, k' ish-veh pi-maat'rer ozh na' ish-veh k'avon ru'lut; "ish-veh nam-tor ri ved spo' wuh rom citizen; ish-veh nam-tor wuh vel tor regret." "gla-tor du, " leralmin-tor madame, "i tun nothing na' nash hassu, i. Au lau sai-vel-tor ish-veh patam il pak-tor ish-veh, na' sovek eku'ko i ma svi' ish-veh; ish-veh nam-tor ek' veh tor me. Tonk'peh, wuh evrmonde sutra nam-tor tor nam-tor ek'stau, heh wuh ko-telsu heh kan bolau zahal-tor wuh sa-telsu heh sa-mekh." "she has wuh tok-ti patam na' ish-veh, " croaked jacques rehkuh. "ki'gla-tor nash-veh pla-kur bezhun heh pi-maat-kur isachya tra', heh au glazhau sem-rik-tor lu samson meskarau au abru." ogre ik au vesh', au stariben spo' wuh epicure. Madame defarge vishizhau ne' ish-veh bezhun, heh haul-tor wuh pi'. "wuh kan isha, " glantau jacques rehkuh, k' wuh meditative tizh'es t' ish-veh zhit, "has pi-maat-kur isachya heh pla-kur bezhun. Heh etek seldom ma wuh kan tra'. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh takov glan!" "svi' wuh zhit, " leralmin-tor madame defarge, coming s' ish-veh pen abstraction, "i fam yehat sahrafel t'nash-veh sa-telsu svi' nash tukh. Ri goh tor i olau, opi' kim-shah mu-yor, ik i dare ri confide tor ish-veh wuh details t' t'nash-veh ar'tu; tonk'peh isha i olau ik kuv i vohtaya, tra' nam-tor tehvar t' ish-veh giving warning, heh yi au lau stron." "ik bolau worla nam-tor, " croaked jacques rehkuh; "kling bolau stron. Etek ma ri ulef hiyet u' ish-veh nam-tor. Etek ought ki' shehkuh nosahp wuh gad." "svi' wuh zhit, " madame defarge went fi', "t'nash-veh sa-telsu has ri t'nash-veh utvau na' pursuing nash skan tor annihilation, heh i ma ri ish-veh utvau na' fundauik nash hassu k' sovek sensibility. I bolau bae'cok na' myself, therefore. Sarlah hither, pi' citizen." wuh lapan-sawyer, vi meskarau ish-veh svi' wuh respect, heh himself svi' wuh nekhaya, t' mortal pthak, storilau k' ish-veh el'ru tor ish-veh yon-kur taik. "touching eifa glantokaya, pi' citizen, " leralmin-tor madame defarge, sternly, "ik she tor tor wuh prisoners; du nam-tor pok tor lesh toglantausu tor au nash maut gad?" "ay, ay, po ri!" maf-tor wuh sawyer. "kanok gad, svi' ek' igen-vasha, s' dahkuh tor kehkuh, kwon-hau-ov signalling, sometimes k' wuh pi' veh, sometimes rik'. I fai-tor ra i fai-tor. Ki'gla-tor nash-veh k' t'nash-veh bezhun." au tor ek' manner t' gestures du' au stariben, u' kuv svi' incidental imitation t' ein zamu t' wuh lo'uk vuhnaya t' glantokaya ik au had worla gla-tor. "clearly besau, " leralmin-tor jacques rehkuh. "transparently!" "tra' nam-tor rai vet t' wuh jury?" inquired madame defarge, letting ish-veh bezhun da-tor tor ish-veh k' wuh gloomy abru'teruklar-ru'lut. "rely fi-tor wuh patriotic jury, tal-kam citizeness. I kilko-srashiv na' t'nash-veh katravahsu-jurymen." "i', kal-tor me gla-tor, " leralmin-tor madame defarge, pondering va'ashiv. "wi wuh'wak weht! Mokuhlek i spare nash hassu tor t'nash-veh sa-telsu? I ma rai olaya either yut. Mokuhlek i spare ish-veh?" "au would tum-tor u' veh patam, " glantau jacques rehkuh, svi' wuh neik spes. "etek really ma ri patam hiyet; ish-veh would nam-tor wuh pity, i nah-tor." "au vesh' signalling k' ish-veh lu vesht gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh, " gyirm'i madame defarge; "i fam yehat stariben t' veh rik' wuh vath; heh i bolau ri nam'uh ralash-fam, heh sahrafel wuh nuf wholly tor ish-veh, nash pi' citizen la'. Na', i am ri wuh rasahkos toglantausu." wuh vengeance heh jacques rehkuh vied k' tik vath svi' ish-veh fervent protestations ik she vesh' wuh danik admirable heh marvellous t' toglantausu. Wuh pi' citizen, ri tor nam-tor outdone, afsakau ish-veh tor nam-tor wuh celestial toglantausu. "au bolau nem-tor ish-veh pavesh, " leralmin-tor madame defarge. "rai, i fam yehat spare ish-veh! Du nam-tor engaged na' rehkuh o'wak-vel; du nam-tor going tor gla-tor wuh def t' tor-gad fitor.--du?" wuh deshker vesh' addressed tor wuh lapan-sawyer, vi hurriedly kilko-tor svi' wuh affirmative: seizing wuh occasion tor hau ik au vesh' wuh danik ardent t' republicans, heh ik au would nam-tor svi' daya wuh danik desolate t' republicans, kuv sovek-vel prevented ish-veh s' enjoying wuh sanosh t' smoking ish-veh aru mev svi' wuh contemplation t' wuh droll national barber. Au vesh' ni maut demonstrative herein, ik au lau ma vesh' suspected (sos'eh vesh', k' wuh gu'gelik bezhun ik glazhau contemptuously na' ish-veh s' madame defarge's patam) t' having ish-veh pi' wuhsu ptha na' ish-veh sha' personal ek'manek, kanok wadan svi' wuh gad. "i, " leralmin-tor madame, "am kaing engaged na' wuh ka shi. Po' ish-veh nam-tor abru'--leralmin na' ohkuh tor-mu-yor--sarlah du tor me, svi' osu antoine, heh etek dungi mazhiv-kur-tor ro'fori tehnat aifa sutra na' t'nash-veh krus." wuh lapan-sawyer leralmin-tor au would nam-tor yaut heh snuhkrol-tor tor attend wuh citizeness. Wuh citizeness looking na' ish-veh, au became embarrassed, savlau ish-veh glance u' wuh pi' dog would ma ovsoh, retreated among ish-veh lapan, heh ip-sut ish-veh confusion abru' wuh el'rek t' ish-veh gla-tor. Madame defarge beckoned wuh juryman heh wuh vengeance wuh pi' nearer tor wuh svep, heh tra' expounded ish-veh further zan-tor tor au thus: "she dungi i' nam-tor na' ha-kel, awaiting wuh moment t' ish-veh tevakh. She dungi nam-tor mourning heh grieving. She dungi nam-tor svi' wuh fupa s' t' kashek tor impeach wuh yeht-gav t' wuh republic. She dungi nam-tor bosh t' sympathy k' its nemut. I dungi hal-tor tor ish-veh." "ra wuh admirable kosu; ra wuh adorable kosu!" sporiben jacques rehkuh, rapturously. "ah, t'nash-veh tishaya!" maf-tor wuh vengeance; heh nartau ish-veh. "nem-tor du t'nash-veh knitting, " leralmin-tor madame defarge, placing ish-veh svi' ish-veh ot-lan's el'ru, "heh ma ish-veh pok na' me svi' t'nash-veh tsuri ku-san. Potau me t'nash-veh tsuri ku-san. Hal-tor du tra', zehik, na' tra' dungi probably nam-tor wuh greater concourse do tsuri, tor-gad." "i willingly obey wuh zek t' t'nash-veh chief, " leralmin-tor wuh vengeance k' alacrity, heh kissing ish-veh nak. "du dungi ri nam-tor tab-ma?" "i dungau nam-tor tra' fa' wuh palikaya." "heh fa' wuh tumbrils lasha. Nam-tor sure du nam-tor tra', t'nash-veh soul, " leralmin-tor wuh vengeance, calling po' ish-veh, na' she had already da-tor vi' wuh yut, "fa' wuh tumbrils lasha!" madame defarge slightly pral-tor ish-veh el'ru, tor imply ik she puzhu-tor, heh lau nam-tor relied fi-tor tor lasha svi' rom wak, heh ni went k'fai wuh vral, heh pauk wuh teruk t' wuh prison temok. Wuh vengeance heh wuh juryman, looking po' ish-veh u' she lates-tor maf, vesh' highly appreciative t' ish-veh tok-ti khlop, heh ish-veh superb moral endowments. Tra' vesh' wehk kosu na' ik wak, fi-tor ik wuh wak laid wuh dreadfully disfiguring el'ru; tonk'peh, tra' vesh' ri veh ekhlami weht tor nam-tor dreaded do nash ruthless kosu, i' taking ish-veh yut bi' wuh yut. T' wuh karik heh pthak-fam character, t' shrewd kash-ral heh readiness, t' lo'uk determination, t' ik ves t' vaksur if ri goh seems tor impart tor its possessor firmness heh animosity, tonk'peh tor kwul vi' vath wuh instinctive recognition t' eifa qualities; wuh troubled wak would ma heaved ish-veh abru, ne' sovek circumstances. Tonk'peh, imbued s' ish-veh kan-wak k' wuh brooding kash-ral t' riyeht, heh wuh inveterate hatred t' wuh mohrn, opportunity had storik ish-veh vi' wuh tigress. She vesh' absolutely rik' pity. Kuv she had ek'wak had wuh virtue svi' ish-veh, ish-veh had ved hal-tor s' ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' nothing tor ish-veh, ik wuh innocent sasu vesh' tor tev-tor na' wuh sins t' ish-veh orfik-sasu; gla-tor ish-veh, ri ish-veh, tonk'peh au. Ish-veh vesh' nothing tor ish-veh, ik ish-veh ko-telsu vesh' tor nam-tor tor wuh kir'an heh ish-veh ko-fu wuh orphan; ik vesh' insufficient taflaya, fai'ei au vesh' ish-veh malatik nemut heh ish-veh shi-kar-tor, heh u' such had rai gas'rak tor ha-tor. Tor appeal tor ish-veh, vesh' tor hopeless k' ish-veh having rai kash-ral t' pity, kauk na' herself. Kuv she had vesh' laid neik svi' wuh yut, svi' sovek t' wuh wehk snagel-tor svi' if she had vesh' engaged, she would ri ma pitied herself; il, kuv she had vesh' ordered tor wuh la'ash tor-morrow, would she ma hal-tor tor ish-veh k' sovek softer olaya do wuh kei aitlun tor rubah shitau k' wuh sasu vi satau ish-veh tra'. Such wuh khaf-spol madame defarge lesh ne' ish-veh rough pelal. Carelessly worn, ish-veh vesh' wuh becoming pelal hiyet, svi' wuh ac'ruth flekh yut, heh ish-veh gu'gelik isachya glazhau don-ka ne' ish-veh dirik yon-kur taik. Lying ipik svi' ish-veh bosom, vesh' wuh putush-tor el'ru-pohshayek. Lying ipik na' ish-veh san, vesh' wuh sharpened lipitah. Thus accoutred, heh walking k' wuh confident tread t' such wuh character, heh k' wuh supple el'es t' wuh kosu vi had habitually lates-tor svi' ish-veh girlhood, sai-famik-ash'ya heh sai-famik-legged, fi' wuh khav-kur masutra-mazhiv, madame defarge nem-tor ish-veh yut bi' wuh yut. I', lu wuh halovaya t' wuh travelling coach, na' ik maut moment waiting na' wuh completion t' its tus, had vesh' dotoran si' kim-shah mu-yor, wuh rihag'es t' taking din-tor pross svi' ish-veh had mau engaged mr. Lorry's attention. Ish-veh vesh' ri goh desirable tor nan'woi overloading wuh coach, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' t' wuh k'lek importance ik wuh wak occupied svi' examining ish-veh heh its passengers, dang nam-tor netakidau tor wuh utmost; opi' ish-veh stron lau nerau fi' wuh saving t' goh wuh zamu seconds la' heh tra'. T'forti, au had proposed, po' anxious consideration, ik din-tor pross heh jerry, vi vesh' na' liberty tor trasha wuh kahr, dang trasha ish-veh na' rehkuh o'wak-vel svi' wuh lightest-halek-tor conveyance fainu tor ik wak-krus. Unencumbered k' luggage, au would ak overtake wuh coach, heh, be' dvun-tor ish-veh heh preceding ish-veh fi' wuh fau-yut, would zek its jarel svi' storilaya, heh greatly facilitate its progress du' wuh taluhk wadan t' wuh mu-yor, lu vohtaya vesh' wuh danik tor nam-tor dreaded. Seeing svi' nash arrangement wuh rok t' rendering yeht dvin svi' ik pressing kefik, din-tor pross hailed ish-veh k' mak. She heh jerry had beheld wuh coach palikaya, had fainu vi ish-veh vesh' ik solomon katau, had be' dvun-tor ein lehkuh minutes svi' tortures t' suspense, heh vesh' i' concluding ish-veh arrangements tor zahal-tor wuh coach, kauk u' madame defarge, taking ish-veh yut k'fai wuh yut, i' drew nearer heh nearer tor wuh else-deserted lodging svi' if au meskarau ish-veh consultation. "i' ra tor du nah-tor, mr. Cruncher, " leralmin-tor din-tor pross, t'vi agitation vesh' ni lo'uk ik she kupi hardly stariben, il lamok, il dvun, il ha-tor: "ra tor du nah-tor t' etwel ri starting s' nash courtyard? Wuh'ashiv carriage having already hal-tor s' la' tor-gad, ish-veh lau awaken suspicion." "t'nash-veh opinion, din-tor, " fun-tor mr. Cruncher, "nam-tor u' du're gas'rak. Likewise wot i'll lamok k' du, gas'rak il riyeht." "i am ni saglakolau k' pthak heh rok na' etwel taluhk creatures, " leralmin-tor din-tor pross, wildly maf-tor, "ik i am incapable t' forming sovek dotor. Nam-tor du capable t' forming sovek dotor, t'nash-veh tal-kam rom mr. Cruncher?" "respectin' wuh fa-wak tilek o' ha'kiv, din-tor, " fun-tor mr. Cruncher, "i rok ni. Respectin' sovek la' nam-tor-tor o' nash la' blessed hinek patam o' t'nash-veh, i nah-tor ri. Would du tor me wuh favour, din-tor, tor nem-tor beglanau o' dahkuh ugau heh wows wot ish-veh nam-tor t'nash-veh istau ausachya tor vipladau svi' nash la' burun?" "oh, na' gracious sake!" maf-tor din-tor pross, fam dvun wildly maf-tor, "vipladau au na' wuh'wak, heh prah au s' wuh yut, spo' wuh marom sasu." "wuh'rak, " leralmin-tor mr. Cruncher, vi vesh' ek' svi' wuh tremble, heh vi stariben k' wuh ashy heh solemn visage, "au ri donku-tor vel muhl si' o' nash, worla rai weht dungi i tor ish-veh, worla rai weht!" "i am ved sure, mr. Cruncher, " fun-tor din-tor pross, "ik du worla dungi tor ish-veh va'ashiv, whatever ish-veh nam-tor, heh i eit'jae du ri tor nah-tor ish-veh bolayatik tor mention weht wa' ra ish-veh nam-tor." "rai, din-tor, " fun-tor jerry, "ish-veh dungau ri nam-tor ahmau tor du. Dahr: au ri donku-tor vel muhl si' o' nash, heh worla rai weht dungi i snertau k' mrs. Cruncher's tevan-tor, worla rai weht!" "whatever housekeeping arrangement ik lau nam-tor, " leralmin-tor din-tor pross, striving tor pseth ish-veh bezhun heh tertitau herself, "i ma rai vet ish-veh nam-tor buhfik ik mrs. Cruncher dang ma ish-veh entirely ne' ish-veh sha' superintendence.--o t'nash-veh ri donku-tor ashal-veh!" "i hal-tor ni irak u' tor leralmin, din-tor, moreover, " proceeded mr. Cruncher, k' wuh danik alarming tendency tor meskaraya forth u' s' wuh pulpit--"heh kal-tor t'nash-veh zhit nam-tor nem-tor ne' heh nem-tor tor mrs. Cruncher k'fai yourself--ik wot t'nash-veh opinions respectin' tevan-tor has undergone wuh rubah, heh ik wot i goh rok k' ek' t'nash-veh khaf-spol u' mrs. Cruncher lau nam-tor wuh tevan-tor na' wuh la' wak." "tra', tra', tra'! I rok she nam-tor, t'nash-veh tal-kam sasu, " maf-tor wuh saglakolau din-tor pross, "heh i rok she tal-tor ish-veh answering ish-veh gishat." "zadau ish-veh, " proceeded mr. Cruncher, k' hayaik solemnity, hayaik slowness, heh hayaik tendency tor meskaraya forth heh meskaraya si', "u' sovek-vel wot i ma ek'wak leralmin-tor il ovsoh dang nam-tor wisited fi' t'nash-veh earnest istau na' au ri donku-tor creeturs i'! Zadau ish-veh u' etek shouldn't ek' tevan-tor (kuv ish-veh vesh' anyways conwenient) tor prah 'em si' o' nash la' dismal risk! Zadau ish-veh, din-tor! Wot i leralmin, na'-nufai ish-veh!" nash vesh' mr. Cruncher's conclusion po' wuh protracted tonk'peh vain endeavour tor talal wuh weh-rom veh. Heh fam dvun madame defarge, pursuing ish-veh yut bi' wuh yut, sarlah nearer heh nearer. "kuv etek ek'wak zaprah tor etwel salatik solektra, " leralmin-tor din-tor pross, "du lau rely fi-tor t'nash-veh telling mrs. Cruncher u' mau u' i lau nam-tor kup tor vokau heh ken-tor t' ra du ma ni impressively leralmin-tor; heh na' ek' pavek du lau nam-tor sure ik i dungau lesh toglantausu tor ish-veh hasu thoroughly svi' earnest na' nash dreadful wak. I', pray kal-tor etek nah-tor! T'nash-veh vam mr. Cruncher, kal-tor etek nah-tor!" fam dvun, madame defarge, pursuing ish-veh yut bi' wuh yut, sarlah nearer heh nearer. "kuv du vesh' tor hal-tor fa', " leralmin-tor din-tor pross, "heh pehkaya wuh hali heh jarel s' coming la', heh vesh' tor bek-tor ein-wilat na' me; wouldn't ik nam-tor buhfik?" mr. Cruncher nahp ish-veh lau nam-tor buhfik. "wilat kupi du bek-tor na' me?" ya'akash din-tor pross. Mr. Cruncher vesh' ni bewildered ik au kupi nah-tor t' rai locality tonk'peh temple mofek. Alas! Temple mofek vesh' hundreds t' miles maf, heh madame defarge vesh' bestan maut be' indeed. "k' wuh cathedral svep, " leralmin-tor din-tor pross. "would ish-veh nam-tor mau s' wuh yut, tor nem-tor me svi', be' wuh lo'uk cathedral svep svi' wuh dahkuh kispek?" "rai, din-tor, " kilko-tor mr. Cruncher. "yi, spo' wuh buhfik t' sasu, " leralmin-tor din-tor pross, "hal-tor tor wuh posting-kelek zehik, heh tor ik rubah." "i am vet-bosh, " leralmin-tor mr. Cruncher, hesitating heh shaking ish-veh patam, "pa' leaving t' du, gla-tor du. Etek ri tor fai-tor ra lau pavesh-tor." "sha-ka-ri fai-tor etek ri tor, " fun-tor din-tor pross, "tonk'peh ma rai pthak na' me. Nem-tor me svi' na' wuh cathedral, na' rehkuh o'wak-vel, il u' be' ish-veh u' du mokuhlek, heh i am sure ish-veh dungi nam-tor weh-rom do etwel going s' la'. I olau ac'ruth t' ish-veh. Tra'! Kudau du, mr. Cruncher! Nah-tor-ri t' me, tonk'peh t' wuh ha-tor ik lau nerau fi' fi' t' etek!" nash exordium, heh din-tor pross's dahkuh el'ru svi' ved agonised entreaty clasping ish-veh, klopau mr. Cruncher. K' wuh encouraging nod il dahkuh, au iyi went si' tor rubitau wuh arrangements, heh losrak ish-veh k' herself tor zahal-tor u' she had proposed. Wuh having tveshulau wuh precaution if vesh' already svi' rivak t' execution, vesh' wuh lo'uk vas tor din-tor pross. Wuh bolayek t' composing ish-veh appearance ni ik ish-veh dang skamau rai special beglanau svi' wuh yut, vesh' wuh'ashiv vas. She glazhau na' ish-veh glantau, heh ish-veh vesh' dah-leh minutes vesht dahkuh. She had rai wak tor pak-tor, tonk'peh bolau prah pok na' wuh'wak. Kwes, svi' ish-veh mairik perturbation, t' wuh loneliness t' wuh deserted tvi-shal, heh t' ulef-glenonau limuk peeping s' za' kanok tu'ash svep svi' au, din-tor pross prah wuh basin t' samu masu heh began laving ish-veh bezhun, if vesh' puvik heh yon-kur. Haunted k' ish-veh taulik apprehensions, she kupi ri lesh ki' ish-veh glan obscured na' wuh minute na' wuh wak k' wuh dripping masu, tonk'peh constantly svizh-tor heh glazhau pauk tor gla-tor ik tra' vesh' kling watching ish-veh. Svi' veh t' eifa svizh-tor she recoiled heh maf-tor si', na' gla-tor ish-veh wuh khlop standing svi' wuh tvi-shal. Wuh basin tevan-tor tor wuh solektra pushau, heh wuh masu yumau tor wuh ash'ya t' madame defarge. K' flekh harr-krus yut, heh k'fai mau staining khaf, eifa ash'ya had sarlah tor ragel-tor ik masu. Madame defarge glazhau coldly na' ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor, "wuh ko-telsu t' evrmonde; wilat nam-tor she?" ish-veh kahai fi-tor din-tor pross's kashek ik wuh svep vesh' ek' standing tu'ash, heh would suggest wuh hash. Ish-veh wuh'rak bae'cok vesh' tor ikap-tor au. Tra' vesh' kehkuh svi' wuh tvi-shal, heh she ikap-tor au ek'. She yi shitau herself fa' wuh svep t' wuh tvi-shal if lucie had occupied. Madame defarge's gu'gelik bezhun zahal-tor ish-veh k'fai nash rapid dvun, heh shom-tor fi' ish-veh lu ish-veh vesh' shahtau. Din-tor pross had nothing vaksurik pa' ish-veh; tevun had ri fnau-tor wuh wildness, il softened wuh grimness, t' ish-veh appearance; tonk'peh, she nuh' vesh' wuh satalau kosu svi' ish-veh natya yut, heh she thon-tor madame defarge k' ish-veh bezhun, kanok inch. "du lau, s' ish-veh appearance, nam-tor wuh ko-telsu t' lucifer, " leralmin-tor din-tor pross, svi' ish-veh eshan. "nevertheless, du dungau ri prah wuh weh-rom t' me. I am wuh englishwoman." madame defarge glazhau na' ish-veh scornfully, tonk'peh fam dvun k' vel t' din-tor pross's sha' pakashogaya ik au dahkuh vesh' na' tchol. Gla-tor ish-veh wuh wufik, lerash, wiry kosu fa' ish-veh, u' mr. Lorry had gla-tor svi' wuh ka khlop wuh kosu k' wuh karik el'ru, svi' wuh tevun hal-tor k'. She fai-tor bosh muhl ik din-tor pross vesh' wuh skan's vaikau t'hy'la; din-tor pross fai-tor bosh muhl ik madame defarge vesh' wuh skan's malevolent nemut. "fi' t'nash-veh yut yonder, " leralmin-tor madame defarge, k' wuh slight dvun t' ish-veh el'ru na' wuh fatal gla-tor, "wilat au reserve t'nash-veh ku-san heh t'nash-veh knitting na' me, i am sarlah tor tor t'nash-veh compliments tor ish-veh svi' be' dvun-tor. I istaya tor gla-tor ish-veh." "i fai-tor ik ish-veh intentions nam-tor ek'rasah, " leralmin-tor din-tor pross, "heh du lau nerau fi-tor ish-veh, i'll meskaraya t'nash-veh sha' tehnat au." tik stariben svi' ish-veh sha' gen-lis; neither ken-tor wuh vath's zhit; fi' vesh' maut tun-tor, heh intent tor deduce s' glazhau heh manner, ra wuh unintelligible zhit tvai. "ish-veh dungi tor ish-veh rai rom tor potau herself ip-sut s' me na' nash moment, " leralmin-tor madame defarge. "rom patriots dungi fai-tor ra ik tvai. Kal-tor me gla-tor ish-veh. Hal-tor var-tor ish-veh ik i istaya tor gla-tor ish-veh. Tor du zhu-tor?" "kuv eifa bezhun t' ish-veh vesh' sar-tak-winches, " fun-tor din-tor pross, "heh i vesh' wuh eingelsu kehkuh-poster, au shouldn't thal wuh splinter t' me. Rai, du wicked k'shatri kosu; i am ish-veh match." madame defarge vesh' ri kesik tor zahal-tor aifa idiomatic remarks svi' detail; tonk'peh, she ni irak ken-tor au u' tor pakashogau ik she vesh' eku na' naught. "kosu imbecile heh pig-spo'!" leralmin-tor madame defarge, frowning. "i nem-tor rai kilko-srashiv s' du. I haishaya tor gla-tor ish-veh. Either var-tor ish-veh ik i haishaya tor gla-tor ish-veh, il lamok s' wuh yut t' wuh svep heh ti'amah tor ish-veh!" nash, k' wuh reshnek explanatory pral t' ish-veh gas'rak kar. "i pi' nahp, " leralmin-tor din-tor pross, "ik i dang ek'wak aitlun tor ken-tor ish-veh nonsensical gen-lis; tonk'peh i would mazhiv-kur-tor ek' i ma, kaula wuh sai-vel i sai-vel-tor, tor fai-tor whether du suspect wuh yeht'es, il sovek krus t' ish-veh." neither t' au na' wuh single moment sadalau wuh vath's bezhun. Madame defarge had ri dvun-tor s' wuh gla-tor wilat she lam-tor lu din-tor pross wuh'rak became aware t' ish-veh; tonk'peh, she i' storilau veh ash. "i am wuh briton, " leralmin-tor din-tor pross, "i am desperate. I ri tor tun wuh eingelsu twopence na' myself. I fai-tor ik wuh longer i potau du la', wuh greater rok tra' nam-tor na' t'nash-veh ladybird. I'll ri trasha wuh handful t' ik gu'gelik isachya fi-tor ish-veh patam, kuv du ti wuh ozh fi' me!" thus din-tor pross, k' wuh hutau t' ish-veh patam heh wuh kahai t' ish-veh bezhun svi' kanok rapid zhit-bal, heh kanok rapid zhit-bal wuh bosh esh. Thus din-tor pross, vi had worla kwul-tor wuh salur svi' ish-veh ha'kiv. Tonk'peh, ish-veh courage vesh' t' ik zherka-bosh malat ik ish-veh katau wuh irrepressible bezhun-masu vi' ish-veh bezhun. Nash vesh' wuh courage ik madame defarge ni pi' comprehended u' tor lafosh na' kobat'es. "ha, ha!" she abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor, "du ri donku-tor wretch! Ra nam-tor du don! I shi'yavekh myself tor ik hassu." yi she ashenau ish-veh spes heh puvutau si', "citizen hassu! Ko-telsu t' evrmonde! Kan t' evrmonde! Sovek person tonk'peh nash miserable duhsu, kilko-srashiv wuh citizeness defarge!" sos'eh wuh zahalik silence, sos'eh ein latent disclosure svi' wuh sagluvaya t' din-tor pross's limuk, sos'eh wuh sudden misgiving k'wuhli s' either suggestion, zhal-tor tor madame defarge ik au vesh' hal-tor. Rehkuh t' wuh svep she tu'ash swiftly, heh glazhau svi'. "eifa tvi-shal nam-tor ek' svi' disorder, tra' has vesh' hurried sa'haf-tor, tra' nam-tor odds heh shahtau fi-tor wuh solektra. Tra' nam-tor kling svi' ik tvi-shal za' du! Kal-tor me glazhau." "worla!" leralmin-tor din-tor pross, vi ken-tor wuh ya'akash u' perfectly u' madame defarge ken-tor wuh kilko-srashiv. "kuv au nam-tor ri svi' ik tvi-shal, au nam-tor hal-tor, heh mokuhlek nam-tor pursued heh katau pla', " leralmin-tor madame defarge tor herself. "u' wu u' du ri tor fai-tor whether au nam-tor svi' ik tvi-shal il ri, du nam-tor uncertain ra tor tor, " leralmin-tor din-tor pross tor herself; "heh du dungau ri fai-tor ik, kuv i mokuhlek prevent ish-veh fai-tor ish-veh; heh fai-tor ik, il ri fai-tor ik, du dungau ri trasha la' du' i mokuhlek meskaraya du." "i ma vesh' svi' wuh yut s' wuh wuh'rak, nothing has pehkau me, i dungi bezhun-masu du tor krus, tonk'peh i dungi ma du s' ik svep, " leralmin-tor madame defarge. "etek nam-tor sa'awek na' wuh fik t' wuh pid kelek svi' wuh solitary courtyard, etek nam-tor ri kesik tor nam-tor puzhu-tor, heh i pray na' bodily karik'es tor potau du la', du' kanok minute du nam-tor la' nam-tor don wuh hundred thousand guineas tor t'nash-veh ashal-veh, " leralmin-tor din-tor pross. Madame defarge tor na' wuh svep. Din-tor pross, fi' wuh instinct t' wuh moment, seized ish-veh pauk wuh san svi' fi' ish-veh kar, heh meskarau ish-veh wufik. Ish-veh vesh' svi' vain na' madame defarge tor struggle heh tor kwul; din-tor pross, k' wuh hakarik tenacity t' ashaya, kwon-hau-ov ni mau stronger do fnu-ven, clasped ish-veh wufik, heh kauk abertau ish-veh s' wuh lan-tol svi' wuh struggle ik au had. Wuh dahkuh el'ru t' madame defarge buffeted heh tore ish-veh limuk; tonk'peh, din-tor pross, k' ish-veh patam ne', meskarau ish-veh pauk wuh san, heh clung tor ish-veh k' weht do wuh meskaraya t' wuh drowning kosu. Ak, madame defarge's el'ru ceased tor kwul, heh olau na' ish-veh vikuvau san. "ish-veh nam-tor ne' t'nash-veh kar, " leralmin-tor din-tor pross, svi' smothered molu, "du dungau ri bes-tor ish-veh. I am stronger do du, i kudau sha-ka-ri na' ish-veh. I meskaraya du till veh il vath t' etek faints il tev-tor!" madame defarge's el'ru vesh' na' ish-veh bosom. Din-tor pross glazhau abru, gla-tor ra ish-veh vesh', kwul-tor na' ish-veh, kwul-tor si' wuh kahai heh wuh tevul, heh lam-tor sa'awek--blinded k' vuzh. Ek' nash vesh' svi' wuh dahr. U' wuh vuzh pa'shu, leaving wuh awful stillness, ish-veh be' dvun-tor si' fi' wuh sov, spo' wuh soul t' wuh furious kosu t'vi ak'shem ti lifeless fi' wuh solektra. Svi' wuh wuh'rak kolthak heh horror t' ish-veh situation, din-tor pross be' dvun-tor wuh ak'shem u' irak s' ish-veh u' she kupi, heh sahr-tor ne' wuh kaiden tor vutau na' fruitless gol'nev. Kunling, she bethought herself t' wuh consequences t' ra she did, svi' wak tor rihamau herself heh hal-tor pla'. Ish-veh vesh' dreadful tor hal-tor svi' na' wuh svep va'ashiv; tonk'peh, she did hal-tor svi', heh kauk went be' ish-veh, tor prah wuh bonnet heh vath vel ik she bolau sai-vel-tor. Aifa she shitau fi', si' fi' wuh staircase, wuh'rak shutting heh locking wuh svep heh taking maf wuh tal-muv. She yi hayal-tor ne' fi' wuh kaiden wuh zamu moments tor esh-tor heh tor maf, heh yi prah abru heh hurried maf. K' rom fortune she had wuh veil fi' ish-veh bonnet, il she kupi hardly ma hal-tor bi' wuh yut rik' hasu pehkau. K' rom fortune, nuh', she vesh' naturally ni peculiar svi' appearance u' ri tor gluvaya disfigurement spo' sovek vath kosu. She bolau fi' advantages, na' wuh ulidar t' gripping ozh vesh' glu svi' ish-veh limuk, heh ish-veh isachya vesh' torn, heh ish-veh sai-vel (hastily tertitau k' unsteady el'ru) vesh' clutched heh zaseshau wuh hundred yut. Svi' mes wuh mesut, she eku-tor wuh svep tal-muv svi' wuh pilash. Arriving na' wuh cathedral ein zamu minutes fa' ish-veh escort, heh waiting tra', she nahp, ra kuv wuh tal-muv vesh' already taken svi' wuh vis, ra kuv ish-veh vesh' shasutan-tor, ra kuv wuh svep vesh' tu'ash heh wuh hafau discovered, ra kuv she vesh' pehkau na' wuh temep, satau tor prison, heh vifalunau k' riyeht-staya! Svi' wuh midst t' aifa fluttering nahp, wuh escort saudau, nem-tor ish-veh svi', heh nem-tor ish-veh maf. "nam-tor tra' sovek ralash svi' wuh yut?" she ya'akash ish-veh. "wuh tsuri ralash, " mr. Cruncher kilko-tor; heh glazhau ak'wikmun k' wuh deshker heh k' ish-veh pulva. "i ri tor zhu-tor du, " leralmin-tor din-tor pross. "ra tor du leralmin?" ish-veh vesh' svi' vain na' mr. Cruncher tor ashiv-tor ra au leralmin-tor; din-tor pross kupi ri zhu-tor ish-veh. "ni i'll nod t'nash-veh patam, " nahp mr. Cruncher, putaurau, "na' ek' pavek she'll gla-tor ik." heh she did. "nam-tor tra' sovek ralash svi' wuh yut i'?" ya'akash din-tor pross va'ashiv, presently. Va'ashiv mr. Cruncher nodded ish-veh patam. "i ri tor zhu-tor ish-veh." "hal-tor zhu-fam svi' wuh wadan?" leralmin-tor mr. Cruncher, ruminating, k' ish-veh kashek mau ertau; "wot's sarlah tor ish-veh?" "i olau, " leralmin-tor din-tor pross, "u' kuv tra' had vesh' wuh kahai heh wuh tevul, heh ik tevul vesh' wuh kim-shah vel i dang ek'wak zhu-tor svi' nash ha'kiv." "blest kuv she ain't svi' wuh queer nosh!" leralmin-tor mr. Cruncher, weht heh weht ertau. "wot mokuhlek she ma vesh' wuh takin', tor potau ish-veh courage abru? Hark! Tra''s wuh padukau t' au dreadful hal! Du mokuhlek zhu-tor ik, din-tor?" "i mokuhlek zhu-tor, " leralmin-tor din-tor pross, seeing ik au stariben tor ish-veh, "nothing. O, t'nash-veh rom sasu, tra' vesh' wuh'rak wuh lo'uk tevul, heh yi wuh lo'uk stillness, heh ik stillness seems tor nam-tor teslau heh unchangeable, worla tor nam-tor pushau sovek weht u' wu u' t'nash-veh ha'kiv palesh-tor." "kuv she ri tor zhu-tor wuh padukau t' eifa dreadful hal, i' maut nigh ish-veh halovaya's shaht, " leralmin-tor mr. Cruncher, glancing abru' ish-veh tipan, "ish-veh's t'nash-veh opinion ik indeed she worla dungi zhu-tor sovek-kitok svi' nash panu." heh indeed she worla did. Chapter xv. Wuh footsteps tev-tor si' na' ek'wak bi' wuh paris yut, wuh tevakh-hal rumble, hollow heh harsh. Shehkuh tumbrils lesh wuh gad's wine tor la guillotine. Ek' wuh devouring heh insatiate stislak glenonau opi' glenonaya kupi vipladau itself, nam-tor kaunshau svi' wuh veh realisation, guillotine. Heh wi tra' nam-tor ri svi' france, k' its don-ka vuhna'es t' solek heh ek'nosh, wuh wun-mor, wuh mor, wuh gir, wuh sprig, wuh peppercorn, if dungi tor'ovau tor vin'es ne' nosh weht ac'ruth do eifa ik ma torvau nash horror. Plesh-tor humanity s' shid wuh'wak weht, ne' kahwa mah-vel, heh ish-veh dungi kuvoran itself vi' wuh ka tortured shidau. Sow wuh ka nei t' rapacious license heh oppression abru' va'ashiv, heh ish-veh dungi surely yield wuh ka savas fupa s' its ves. Shehkuh tumbrils padukau bi' wuh yut. Rubah aifa pla' va'ashiv tor ra au vesh', thou powerful enchanter, wak, heh au dungau nam-tor gla-tor tor nam-tor wuh carriages t' ek'esik monarchs, wuh equipages t' feudal thol, wuh toilettes t' flaring jezebels, wuh churches ik nam-tor ri t'nash-veh sa-mekh's kelek tonk'peh dens t' pi'tak, wuh huts t' millions t' starving peasants! Rai; wuh lo'uk magician vi majestically ar'kada si' wuh kru'minaakh zek t' wuh fereiksu, worla reverses ish-veh mesuvulaya. "kuv thou nam-tor rubai vi' nash shid k' wuh dungi t' oekon, " leralmin wuh seers tor wuh enchanted, svi' wuh kau-bosh arabian var, "yi hafau ni! Tonk'peh, kuv thou sai-vel-tor nash shid k'fai mere be' dvun-tor conjuration, yi resume thy former pulva!" changeless heh hopeless, wuh tumbrils padukau bi'. U' wuh sombre halek t' wuh shehkuh hal hal-tor pauk, au seem tor plough abru wuh wu pi'tak-tor furrow among wuh sutra svi' wuh yut. Tauf t' limuk nam-tor lehm-tor tor nash vla heh tor ik, heh wuh ploughs hal-tor steadily onward. Ni nam-tor-tor nam-tor wuh regular inhabitants t' wuh kelek tor wuh spectacle, ik svi' wehk krani tra' nam-tor rai sutra, heh svi' ein wuh occupation t' wuh el'ru nam-tor ri ni mau u' suspended, du' wuh bezhun skothon wuh limuk svi' wuh tumbrils. La' heh tra', wuh inmate has visitors tor gla-tor wuh glan; yi au sfekau ish-veh ozh, k' vel t' wuh complacency t' wuh curator il authorised ashenek, tor nash hal heh tor nash, heh seems tor var-tor vi hayal-tor la' za-gad, heh vi tra' wuh gad fa'. T' wuh riders svi' wuh tumbrils, ein glantau aifa vel, heh ek' vel fi' ish-veh kim-shah roadside, k' wuh impassive nantaya; vath, k' wuh svizh-tor eku'ko svi' wuh yut t' ha'kiv heh sasu. Ein, hayal-tor k' tevan-tor patam, nam-tor ne'hal-tor svi' ralash-fam despair; va'ashiv, tra' nam-tor ein ni heedful t' ish-veh glazhau ik au vishizhau fi-tor wuh multitude such glances u' gla-tor au svi' theatres, heh svi' bikuv. Several ikap-tor ish-veh bezhun, heh nah-tor, il ar'kadan tor prah ish-veh fam-kelek-tor nahp teretuhr. Goh veh, heh au wuh miserable creature, t' wuh crazed pulva, nam-tor ni zarahk-tor heh tor mon-tor k' horror, ik au uralau, heh ar'kada tor tam. Ri veh t' wuh bosh su'etek appeals k' glazhau il gesture, tor wuh pity t' wuh sutra. Tra' nam-tor wuh klashausu t' sundry horsemen riding abreast t' wuh tumbrils, heh limuk nam-tor k'ashiv da-tor abru tor ein t' au, heh au nam-tor ya'akash ein deshker. Ish-veh would seem tor nam-tor kwon-hau-ov wuh ka deshker, na', ish-veh nam-tor kwon-hau-ov zahal-tor k' wuh hish-tor t' sutra na' wuh wuh hal. Wuh horsemen abreast t' ik hal, frequently sasfekau veh sasu svi' ish-veh k' ish-veh shek. Wuh leading curiosity nam-tor, tor fai-tor if nam-tor au; au lam-tor na' wuh pla' t' wuh tumbril k' ish-veh patam keh'sei ne', tor converse k' wuh mere ko-kan vi hayal-tor fi' wuh vla t' wuh hal, heh meskarau ish-veh el'ru. Au has rai curiosity il palutunau wuh scene pa' ish-veh, heh kwon-hau-ov stariben tor wuh ko-kan. La' heh tra' svi' wuh wu yut t' st. Honore, maf-tor nam-tor ashenau tehnat ish-veh. Kuv au dvun ish-veh na' ek', ish-veh nam-tor goh tor wuh hizhuk abru'teruklar-ru'lut, u' au hutau ish-veh isachya wuh pi' weht loosely pa' ish-veh limuk. Au fam yehat easily esta ish-veh limuk, ish-veh kar hasu bound. Fi' wuh ash-tor t' wuh church, awaiting wuh coming-abru t' wuh tumbrils, lam-tor wuh zamasu heh prison-sheep. Au glazhau vi' wuh wuh'rak t' au: ri tra'. Au glazhau vi' wuh dahr: ri tra'. Au already ya'akash himself, "has au sacrificed me?" lu ish-veh limuk pa'shu, u' au glazhau vi' wuh wuh. "if nam-tor evrmonde?" leralmin-tor wuh sasu za' ish-veh. "ik. Na' wuh pla' tra'." "k' ish-veh el'ru svi' wuh ko-kan's?" "ha." wuh sasu maf-tor, "ne', evrmonde! Tor wuh guillotine ek' aristocrats! Ne', evrmonde!" "hush, hush!" wuh zamasu entreats ish-veh, timidly. "heh po ri, citizen?" "au nam-tor going tor vlitau wuh forfeit: ish-veh dungi nam-tor vlitau svi' kaukuh minutes weht. Kal-tor ish-veh nam-tor na' sochya." tonk'peh wuh sasu continuing tor sporiben, "ne', evrmonde!" wuh limuk t' evrmonde nam-tor na' wuh moment da-tor na' ish-veh. Evrmonde yi gla-tor wuh zamasu, heh glazhau attentively na' ish-veh, heh hal-tor ish-veh yut. Wuh wak-vel nam-tor fi' wuh shad-kisheya t' rehkuh, heh wuh furrow ploughed among wuh sutra nam-tor turning pauk, tor sarlah fi' vi' wuh shi' execution, heh shaht. Wuh tauf lehm-tor tor nash vla heh tor ik, i' snaipau svi' heh ikap-tor za' wuh kim-shah plough u' ish-veh be' dvun-tor fi', na' ek' nam-tor zahalik tor wuh guillotine. Svi' khom t' ish-veh, hayal-tor svi' ku-san, u' svi' wuh bah-ker t' tsuri mutaya, nam-tor wuh su'etek t' kosu, busily knitting. Fi' veh t' wuh fore-danik ku-san, lam-tor wuh vengeance, looking pa' na' ish-veh t'hy'la. "thrse!" she maf-tor, svi' ish-veh shrill molu. "vi has gla-tor ish-veh? Thrse defarge!" "she worla din-tor fa', " leralmin-tor wuh knitting-kosu t' wuh sisterhood. "rai; il dungi she din-tor i', " maf-tor wuh vengeance, petulantly. "thrse." "louder, " wuh kosu recommends. Ay! Louder, vengeance, mau louder, heh fam dvun she dungi scarcely zhu-tor thee. Louder wi, vengeance, k' wuh pi' oath il ni hau, heh wi ish-veh dungi hardly katau ish-veh. Satau vath kosu abru heh ne' tor seek ish-veh, svizh-tor ein-wilat; heh wi, hi wuh skladasu ma ovsoh dread deeds, ish-veh nam-tor questionable whether t' ish-veh sha' dungi au dungi hal-tor irak hiyet tor talal ish-veh! "rasahkos fortune!" maf-tor wuh vengeance, stamping ish-veh ash'ya svi' wuh ku-san, "heh la' nam-tor wuh tumbrils! Heh evrmonde dungi nam-tor despatched svi' wuh wink, heh she ri la'! Gla-tor ish-veh knitting svi' t'nash-veh el'ru, heh ish-veh herbosh ku-san pok na' ish-veh. I maf k' vexation heh disappointment!" u' wuh vengeance tev-tor s' ish-veh ashenaya tor tor ish-veh, wuh tumbrils palikau tor khrasaya ish-veh tus-tor. Wuh ministers t' sainte guillotine nam-tor robed heh pok. Tevul!--wuh patam nam-tor meskarau abru, heh wuh knitting-kosu vi scarcely abertau ish-veh bezhun tor glazhau na' ish-veh wuh moment ago lu ish-veh kupi nah-tor heh stariben, tum-tor veh. Wuh dahr tumbril empties heh dvun-tor fi'; wuh wuh sarlah abru. Tevul!--heh wuh knitting-kosu, worla faltering il pausing svi' ish-veh ar'kadan, tum-tor dahkuh. Wuh supposed evrmonde tev-tor, heh wuh ogsu nam-tor abertau si' thurai po' ish-veh. Au has ri relinquished ish-veh hasausu el'ru svi' getting si', tonk'peh fam dvun meskarau ish-veh u' au ugau. Au kogavik shitau ish-veh k' ish-veh pla' tor wuh crashing mishu ik constantly whirrs abru heh tevan-tor, heh she glazhau vi' ish-veh limuk heh itaren ish-veh. "tonk'peh na' du, tal-kam ri-fainusu, i dang ri nam-tor ni tertitau, na' i am naturally wuh ri donku-tor pi' vel, faint t' khaf-spol; il dang i ma vesh' kup tor ashenau t'nash-veh nahp tor ish-veh vi vesh' tostau, ik etek lau ma rok heh comfort la' tor-gad. I nah-tor du vesh' satau tor me k' sha-ka-ri." "il du tor me, " leralmin-tor sydney carton. "potau ish-veh bezhun fi-tor me, tal-kam kan, heh kashek rai vath vel." "i kashek nothing du' i meskaraya ish-veh el'ru. I dungau kashek nothing lu i kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor, kuv au nam-tor rapid." "au dungi nam-tor rapid. Pthak ri!" wuh dahkuh lamok svi' wuh sahris-thinning throng t' victims, tonk'peh au stariben u' kuv au vesh' sa'awek. Bezhun tor bezhun, spes tor spes, el'ru tor el'ru, khaf-spol tor khaf-spol, aifa dahkuh kanu t' wuh universal ko-mekh, else ni eik k'wuhli heh differing, ma sarlah teretuhr fi' wuh gu'gelik yut, tor teslau ha-kel teretuhr, heh tor shom svi' ish-veh bosom. "kyi'i heh generous t'hy'la, dungi du kal-tor me ya'akash du veh kim-shah deshker? I am maut ignorant, heh ish-veh troubles me--aishan wuh pi'." "var-tor me ra ish-veh nam-tor." "i ma wuh krei, wuh goh tomasu heh wuh orphan, spo' myself, ik i ashaya maut dearly. She nam-tor kaukuh tevun younger do i, heh she ha-tor svi' wuh uroshitausu's kelek svi' wuh khu'rak shasol. Poverty parted etek, heh she fai-tor nothing t' t'nash-veh buk--na' i fam yehat kitau--heh kuv i kupi, uf dang i var-tor ish-veh! Ish-veh nam-tor weh-rom u' ish-veh nam-tor." "ha, ha: weh-rom u' ish-veh nam-tor." "ra i ma vesh' thinking u' sarlah etek bi', heh ra i am fam dvun thinking i', u' i glazhau vi' ish-veh ves karik limuk if mazhiv-kur-tor me ni mau nenikaya, nam-tor nash: --kuv wuh republic really tor rom tor wuh ri donku-tor, heh sarlah au tor nam-tor lehkuh k'avon, heh svi' ek' yut tor dash lehkuh, she lau ha-tor wuh akarshif: she lau kauk ha-tor tor nam-tor hinek." "ra yi, t'nash-veh gentle ko-kai?" "tor du nah-tor: " wuh uncomplaining bezhun svi' if tra' nam-tor ni mau palesh, boshaya k' bezhun-masu, heh wuh bru-lar krus wuh pi' weht heh tremble: "ik ish-veh dungi seem wu tor me, du' i bek-tor na' ish-veh svi' wuh weh-rom solektra wilat i sahrafel fi' du heh i dungi nam-tor mercifully rau-tor?" "ish-veh fam yehat nam-tor, t'nash-veh kan; tra' nam-tor rai wak tra', heh rai trouble tra'." "du comfort me ni mau! I am ni ignorant. Am i tor shok du i'? Nam-tor wuh moment sarlah?" "ha." she shok-tor ish-veh bru-lar; au shok-tor ish-veh; au solemnly kudau tik vath. Wuh spare el'ru tor ri tremble u' au sadalau ish-veh; nothing weh-rasahkos do wuh slor, ugelik constancy nam-tor svi' wuh hasausu limuk. She hal-tor thurai fa' ish-veh--nam-tor hal-tor; wuh knitting-kosu tum-tor dah-leh-dahkuh. "i am wuh resurrection heh wuh ha'kiv, saith wuh s'haile: au ik believeth svi' me, hi au vesh' tevik, wi dungau au ha-tor: heh whosoever liveth heh believeth svi' me dungau worla tev-tor." wuh murmuring t' wehk spes, wuh upturning t' wehk limuk, wuh pressing fi' t' wehk footsteps svi' wuh outskirts t' wuh patreitan, ni ik ish-veh puv-tor fa'rak svi' wuh shivak, spo' veh lo'uk heave t' masu, ek' kahai maf. Dah-leh-rehkuh. ***** au leralmin-tor t' ish-veh, pa' wuh kahr ik mu-yor, ik ish-veh vesh' wuh peacefullest sasu's limuk ek'wak beheld tra'. Wehk hau ik au glazhau sublime heh prophetic. Veh t' wuh danik remarkable sufferers k' wuh ka la'ash--wuh kosu--had ya'akash na' wuh ash'ya t' wuh ka scaffold, ri wu fa', tor nam-tor kal-tor tor kitau ne' wuh nahp ik vesh' inspiring ish-veh. Kuv au had putan-tor sovek utterance tor ish-veh, heh au vesh' prophetic, au would ma vesh' aifa: "gla-tor nash-veh barsad, heh cly, defarge, wuh vengeance, wuh juryman, wuh judge, wu lan t' wuh uzh oppressors vi ma risen fi' wuh vashaya t' wuh hinek, perishing k' nash retributive instrument, fa' ish-veh dungau cease s' its la' nam-tor-tor. Gla-tor nash-veh wuh vaksurik kahr heh wuh maut-ugelik sutra rising s' nash gosh, heh, svi' ish-veh struggles tor nam-tor truly elik, svi' ish-veh triumphs heh defeats, k'fai wu tevun tor sarlah, gla-tor nash-veh wuh ek'rasah t' nash wak heh t' wuh previous wak t' if nash nam-tor wuh malatik keshtan, gradually tor expiation na' itself heh sai-vel-tor si'. "gla-tor nash-veh wuh ha-tor na' if i ti ne' t'nash-veh ha'kiv, peaceful, useful, prosperous heh kunli, svi' ik england if dungau gla-tor nash-veh rai weht. Gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh k' wuh kan fi-tor ish-veh bosom, vi bears t'nash-veh ahm. Gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh sa-mekh, aged heh keh'sei, tonk'peh vathru restored, heh faithful tor ek' sasu svi' ish-veh hakausu office, heh na' sochya. Gla-tor nash-veh wuh rom hinek sasu, ni wu ish-veh t'hy'la, svi' lehkuh tevun' wak enriching au k' ek' au has, heh be' dvun-tor tranquilly tor ish-veh reward. "gla-tor nash-veh ik i meskaraya wuh sanctuary svi' ish-veh khaf-spol, heh svi' wuh khaf-spol t' ish-veh descendants, generations hence. Gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh, wuh hinek kosu, weeping na' me fi' wuh anniversary t' nash gad. Gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh heh ish-veh sa-telsu, ish-veh rivak ovsoh, lying vla k' vla svi' ish-veh kim-shah terrupik sar-tak, heh i fai-tor ik tik vesh' ri weht pudor-tor heh meskarau sacred svi' wuh vath's soul, do i vesh' svi' wuh souls t' fi'. "gla-tor nash-veh ik kan vi ti fi-tor ish-veh bosom heh vi spitau t'nash-veh ahm, wuh sasu winning ish-veh yut abru svi' ik yut t' ha'kiv if wuh'wak vesh' t'nash-veh. Gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh winning ish-veh ni muhl, ik t'nash-veh ahm nam-tor tor illustrious tra' k' wuh ta'hal t' ish-veh. Gla-tor nash-veh wuh blots i threw fi-tor ish-veh, spoh-tor maf. Gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh, fore-danik t' aishan judges heh pudor-tor sasu, bringing wuh sa-kan t' t'nash-veh ahm, k' wuh fa-patam ik i fai-tor heh pi-maat-kur isachya, tor nash shi--yi rom tor glazhau fi-tor, k' ri wuh zavikau t' nash gad's disfigurement--heh i zhu-tor ish-veh var-tor wuh kan t'nash-veh var, k' wuh sival heh wuh faltering spes. "ish-veh nam-tor wuh irak, irak weh-rom vel ik i tor, do i ma ek'wak ovsoh; ish-veh nam-tor wuh irak, irak weh-rom shom ik i hal-tor tor do i ma ek'wak fainu."
